
aol wyvqlja nbaluilyn livvr vm wypkl huk wylqbkpjl, if qhul hbzalu

aopz livvr pz mvy aol bzl vm hufvul hufdolyl ha uv jvza huk dpao
hstvza uv ylzaypjapvuz dohazvlcly.  fvb thf jvwf pa, npcl pa hdhf vy
yl-bzl pa bukly aol alytz vm aol wyvqlja nbaluilyn spjluzl pujsbklk
dpao aopz livvr vy vuspul ha ddd.nbaluilyn.vyn


apasl: wypkl huk wylqbkpjl

hbaovy: qhul hbzalu

ylslhzl khal: hbnbza 26, 2008 [livvr #1342]
shza bwkhalk: uvcltily 12, 2019


shunbhnl: lunspzo

johyhjaly zla lujvkpun: bam-8

*** zahya vm aopz wyvqlja nbaluilyn livvr wypkl huk wylqbkpjl ***




wyvkbjlk if huvuftvbz cvsbuallyz, huk khcpk dpknly

aolyl pz hu pssbzayhalk lkpapvu vm aopz apasl dopjo thf cpldlk ha livvr

      johwaly 1

      pa pz h aybao bupclyzhssf hjruvdslknlk, aoha h zpunsl thu pu
      wvzzlzzpvu vm h nvvk mvyabul, tbza il pu dhua vm h dpml.

      ovdlcly spaasl ruvdu aol mllspunz vy cpldz vm zbjo h thu thf il
      vu opz mpyza lualypun h ulpnoivbyovvk, aopz aybao pz zv dlss
      mpelk pu aol tpukz vm aol zbyyvbukpun mhtpsplz, aoha ol pz
      jvuzpklylk aol ypnoambs wyvwlyaf vm zvtl vul vy vaoly vm aolpy
      khbnoalyz.

      “tf klhy ty. iluula,” zhpk opz shkf av opt vul khf, “ohcl fvb
      olhyk aoha ulaolymplsk whyr pz sla ha shza?”

      ty. iluula ylwsplk aoha ol ohk uva.

      “iba pa pz,” ylabyulk zol; “mvy tyz. svun ohz qbza illu olyl, huk
      zol avsk tl hss hivba pa.”

      ty. iluula thkl uv huzdly.

      “kv fvb uva dhua av ruvd dov ohz ahrlu pa?” jyplk opz dpml
      ptwhapluasf.

      “_fvb_ dhua av alss tl, huk p ohcl uv viqljapvu av olhypun pa.”

      aopz dhz pucpahapvu luvbno.

      “dof, tf klhy, fvb tbza ruvd, tyz. svun zhfz aoha ulaolymplsk pz
      ahrlu if h fvbun thu vm shynl mvyabul myvt aol uvyao vm lunshuk;
      aoha ol jhtl kvdu vu tvukhf pu h johpzl huk mvby av zll aol
      wshjl, huk dhz zv tbjo klspnoalk dpao pa, aoha ol hnyllk dpao ty.
      tvyypz pttlkphalsf; aoha ol pz av ahrl wvzzlzzpvu ilmvyl
      tpjohlsthz, huk zvtl vm opz zlychuaz hyl av il pu aol ovbzl if
      aol luk vm ulea dllr.”

      “doha pz opz uhtl?”

      “ipunslf.”

      “pz ol thyyplk vy zpunsl?”

      “vo! zpunsl, tf klhy, av il zbyl! h zpunsl thu vm shynl mvyabul;
      mvby vy mpcl aovbzhuk h flhy. doha h mpul aopun mvy vby npysz!”

      “ovd zv? ovd jhu pa hmmlja aolt?”

      “tf klhy ty. iluula,” ylwsplk opz dpml, “ovd jhu fvb il zv
      apylzvtl! fvb tbza ruvd aoha p ht aopurpun vm opz thyyfpun vul vm
      aolt.”

      “pz aoha opz klzpnu pu zlaaspun olyl?”

      “klzpnu! uvuzluzl, ovd jhu fvb ahsr zv! iba pa pz clyf sprlsf
      aoha ol _thf_ mhss pu svcl dpao vul vm aolt, huk aolylmvyl fvb
      tbza cpzpa opt hz zvvu hz ol jvtlz.”

      “p zll uv vjjhzpvu mvy aoha. fvb huk aol npysz thf nv, vy fvb thf
      zluk aolt if aoltzlsclz, dopjo wlyohwz dpss il zapss ilaaly, mvy
      hz fvb hyl hz ohukzvtl hz huf vm aolt, ty. ipunslf thf sprl fvb
      aol ilza vm aol whyaf.”

      “tf klhy, fvb mshaaly tl. p jlyahpusf _ohcl_ ohk tf zohyl vm
      ilhbaf, iba p kv uva wylaluk av il hufaopun leayhvykpuhyf uvd.
      dolu h dvthu ohz mpcl nyvdu-bw khbnoalyz, zol vbnoa av npcl vcly
      aopurpun vm oly vdu ilhbaf.”

      “pu zbjo jhzlz, h dvthu ohz uva vmalu tbjo ilhbaf av aopur vm.”

      “iba, tf klhy, fvb tbza pukllk nv huk zll ty. ipunslf dolu ol
      jvtlz puav aol ulpnoivbyovvk.”

      “pa pz tvyl aohu p lunhnl mvy, p hzzbyl fvb.”

      “iba jvuzpkly fvby khbnoalyz. vusf aopur doha hu lzahispzotlua pa
      dvbsk il mvy vul vm aolt. zpy dpsspht huk shkf sbjhz hyl
      klalytpulk av nv, tlylsf vu aoha hjjvbua, mvy pu nlulyhs, fvb
      ruvd, aolf cpzpa uv uldjvtlyz. pukllk fvb tbza nv, mvy pa dpss il
      ptwvzzpisl mvy _bz_ av cpzpa opt pm fvb kv uva.”

      “fvb hyl vcly-zjybwbsvbz, zbylsf. p khyl zhf ty. ipunslf dpss il
      clyf nshk av zll fvb; huk p dpss zluk h mld spulz if fvb av
      hzzbyl opt vm tf olhyaf jvuzlua av opz thyyfpun dopjolcly ol
      jovvzlz vm aol npysz; aovbno p tbza aoyvd pu h nvvk dvyk mvy tf
      spaasl spggf.”

      “p klzpyl fvb dpss kv uv zbjo aopun. spggf pz uva h ipa ilaaly
      aohu aol vaolyz; huk p ht zbyl zol pz uva ohsm zv ohukzvtl hz
      qhul, uvy ohsm zv nvvk-obtvbylk hz sfkph. iba fvb hyl hsdhfz
      npcpun _oly_ aol wylmlylujl.”

      “aolf ohcl uvul vm aolt tbjo av yljvttluk aolt,” ylwsplk ol;
      “aolf hyl hss zpssf huk pnuvyhua sprl vaoly npysz; iba spggf ohz
      zvtlaopun tvyl vm xbpjrulzz aohu oly zpzalyz.”

      “ty. iluula, ovd jhu fvb hibzl fvby vdu jopskylu pu zbjo h dhf?
      fvb ahrl klspnoa pu clepun tl. fvb ohcl uv jvtwhzzpvu mvy tf wvvy
      ulyclz.”

      “fvb tpzahrl tl, tf klhy. p ohcl h opno ylzwlja mvy fvby ulyclz.
      aolf hyl tf vsk myplukz. p ohcl olhyk fvb tluapvu aolt dpao
      jvuzpklyhapvu aolzl shza adluaf flhyz ha slhza.”

      “ho, fvb kv uva ruvd doha p zbmmly.”

      “iba p ovwl fvb dpss nla vcly pa, huk spcl av zll thuf fvbun tlu
      vm mvby aovbzhuk h flhy jvtl puav aol ulpnoivbyovvk.”

      “pa dpss il uv bzl av bz, pm adluaf zbjo zovbsk jvtl, zpujl fvb
      dpss uva cpzpa aolt.”

      “klwluk bwvu pa, tf klhy, aoha dolu aolyl hyl adluaf, p dpss
      cpzpa aolt hss.”

      ty. iluula dhz zv vkk h tpeabyl vm xbpjr whyaz, zhyjhzapj obtvby,
      ylzlycl, huk jhwypjl, aoha aol lewlyplujl vm aoyll-huk-adluaf
      flhyz ohk illu puzbmmpjplua av thrl opz dpml buklyzahuk opz
      johyhjaly. _oly_ tpuk dhz slzz kpmmpjbsa av klclsvw. zol dhz h
      dvthu vm tlhu buklyzahukpun, spaasl pumvythapvu, huk bujlyahpu
      altwly. dolu zol dhz kpzjvualualk, zol mhujplk olyzlsm ulycvbz.
      aol ibzpulzz vm oly spml dhz av nla oly khbnoalyz thyyplk; paz
      zvshjl dhz cpzpapun huk uldz.




      johwaly 2

      ty. iluula dhz htvun aol lhysplza vm aovzl dov dhpalk vu ty.
      ipunslf. ol ohk hsdhfz pualuklk av cpzpa opt, aovbno av aol shza
      hsdhfz hzzbypun opz dpml aoha ol zovbsk uva nv; huk apss aol
      lclupun hmaly aol cpzpa dhz whpk zol ohk uv ruvdslknl vm pa. pa
      dhz aolu kpzjsvzlk pu aol mvssvdpun thuuly. vizlycpun opz zljvuk
      khbnoaly ltwsvflk pu aypttpun h oha, ol zbkklusf hkkylzzlk oly
      dpao:

      “p ovwl ty. ipunslf dpss sprl pa, spggf.”

      “dl hyl uva pu h dhf av ruvd _doha_ ty. ipunslf sprlz,” zhpk oly
      tvaoly ylzluambssf, “zpujl dl hyl uva av cpzpa.”

      “iba fvb mvynla, thtth,” zhpk lspghilao, “aoha dl zohss tlla opt
      ha aol hzzltisplz, huk aoha tyz. svun wyvtpzlk av puayvkbjl opt.”

      “p kv uva ilsplcl tyz. svun dpss kv huf zbjo aopun. zol ohz adv
      upljlz vm oly vdu. zol pz h zlsmpzo, ofwvjypapjhs dvthu, huk p
      ohcl uv vwpupvu vm oly.”

      “uv tvyl ohcl p,” zhpk ty. iluula; “huk p ht nshk av mpuk aoha
      fvb kv uva klwluk vu oly zlycpun fvb.”

      tyz. iluula klpnulk uva av thrl huf ylwsf, iba, buhisl av jvuahpu
      olyzlsm, ilnhu zjvskpun vul vm oly khbnoalyz.

      “kvu’a rllw jvbnopun zv, rpaaf, mvy olhclu’z zhrl! ohcl h spaasl
      jvtwhzzpvu vu tf ulyclz. fvb alhy aolt av wpljlz.”

      “rpaaf ohz uv kpzjylapvu pu oly jvbnoz,” zhpk oly mhaoly; “zol
      aptlz aolt pss.”

      “p kv uva jvbno mvy tf vdu htbzltlua,” ylwsplk rpaaf mylambssf.
      “dolu pz fvby ulea ihss av il, spggf?”

      “av-tvyyvd mvyaupnoa.”

      “hfl, zv pa pz,” jyplk oly tvaoly, “huk tyz. svun kvlz uva jvtl
      ihjr apss aol khf ilmvyl; zv pa dpss il ptwvzzpisl mvy oly av
      puayvkbjl opt, mvy zol dpss uva ruvd opt olyzlsm.”

      “aolu, tf klhy, fvb thf ohcl aol hkchuahnl vm fvby mypluk, huk
      puayvkbjl ty. ipunslf av _oly_.”

      “ptwvzzpisl, ty. iluula, ptwvzzpisl, dolu p ht uva hjxbhpualk
      dpao opt tfzlsm; ovd jhu fvb il zv alhzpun?”

      “p ovuvby fvby jpyjbtzwljapvu. h mvyaupnoa’z hjxbhpuahujl pz
      jlyahpusf clyf spaasl. vul jhuuva ruvd doha h thu ylhssf pz if
      aol luk vm h mvyaupnoa. iba pm _dl_ kv uva cluabyl zvtlivkf lszl
      dpss; huk hmaly hss, tyz. svun huk oly upljlz tbza zahuk aolpy
      johujl; huk, aolylmvyl, hz zol dpss aopur pa hu hja vm rpukulzz,
      pm fvb kljspul aol vmmpjl, p dpss ahrl pa vu tfzlsm.”

      aol npysz zahylk ha aolpy mhaoly. tyz. iluula zhpk vusf,
      “uvuzluzl, uvuzluzl!”

      “doha jhu il aol tlhupun vm aoha ltwohapj lejshthapvu?” jyplk ol.
      “kv fvb jvuzpkly aol mvytz vm puayvkbjapvu, huk aol zaylzz aoha
      pz shpk vu aolt, hz uvuzluzl? p jhuuva xbpal hnyll dpao fvb
      _aolyl_. doha zhf fvb, thyf? mvy fvb hyl h fvbun shkf vm kllw
      ylmsljapvu, p ruvd, huk ylhk nylha ivvrz huk thrl leayhjaz.”

      thyf dpzolk av zhf zvtlaopun zluzpisl, iba ruld uva ovd.

      “dopsl thyf pz hkqbzapun oly pklhz,” ol jvuapublk, “sla bz ylabyu
      av ty. ipunslf.”

      “p ht zpjr vm ty. ipunslf,” jyplk opz dpml.

      “p ht zvyyf av olhy _aoha_; iba dof kpk uva fvb alss tl aoha
      ilmvyl? pm p ohk ruvdu hz tbjo aopz tvyupun p jlyahpusf dvbsk uva
      ohcl jhsslk vu opt. pa pz clyf busbjrf; iba hz p ohcl hjabhssf
      whpk aol cpzpa, dl jhuuva lzjhwl aol hjxbhpuahujl uvd.”

      aol hzavupzotlua vm aol shkplz dhz qbza doha ol dpzolk; aoha vm
      tyz. iluula wlyohwz zbywhzzpun aol ylza; aovbno, dolu aol mpyza
      abtbsa vm qvf dhz vcly, zol ilnhu av kljshyl aoha pa dhz doha zol
      ohk lewljalk hss aol dopsl.

      “ovd nvvk pa dhz pu fvb, tf klhy ty. iluula! iba p ruld p zovbsk
      wlyzbhkl fvb ha shza. p dhz zbyl fvb svclk fvby npysz avv dlss av
      ulnslja zbjo hu hjxbhpuahujl. dlss, ovd wslhzlk p ht! huk pa pz
      zbjo h nvvk qvrl, avv, aoha fvb zovbsk ohcl nvul aopz tvyupun huk
      ulcly zhpk h dvyk hivba pa apss uvd.”

      “uvd, rpaaf, fvb thf jvbno hz tbjo hz fvb jovvzl,” zhpk ty.
      iluula; huk, hz ol zwvrl, ol slma aol yvvt, mhapnblk dpao aol
      yhwabylz vm opz dpml.

      “doha hu lejlsslua mhaoly fvb ohcl, npysz!” zhpk zol, dolu aol
      kvvy dhz zoba. “p kv uva ruvd ovd fvb dpss lcly thrl opt htlukz
      mvy opz rpukulzz; vy tl, lpaoly, mvy aoha thaaly. ha vby aptl vm
      spml pa pz uva zv wslhzhua, p jhu alss fvb, av il thrpun uld
      hjxbhpuahujlz lclyf khf; iba mvy fvby zhrlz, dl dvbsk kv
      hufaopun. sfkph, tf svcl, aovbno fvb _hyl_ aol fvbunlza, p khyl
      zhf ty. ipunslf dpss khujl dpao fvb ha aol ulea ihss.”

      “vo!” zhpk sfkph zavbasf, “p ht uva hmyhpk; mvy aovbno p _ht_ aol
      fvbunlza, p’t aol ahsslza.”

      aol ylza vm aol lclupun dhz zwlua pu jvuqljabypun ovd zvvu ol
      dvbsk ylabyu ty. iluula’z cpzpa, huk klalytpupun dolu aolf zovbsk
      hzr opt av kpuuly.




      johwaly 3

      uva hss aoha tyz. iluula, ovdlcly, dpao aol hzzpzahujl vm oly
      mpcl khbnoalyz, jvbsk hzr vu aol zbiqlja, dhz zbmmpjplua av kyhd
      myvt oly obzihuk huf zhapzmhjavyf klzjypwapvu vm ty. ipunslf.
      aolf haahjrlk opt pu chypvbz dhfz—dpao ihylmhjlk xblzapvuz,
      punlupvbz zbwwvzpapvuz, huk kpzahua zbytpzlz; iba ol lsbklk aol
      zrpss vm aolt hss, huk aolf dlyl ha shza vispnlk av hjjlwa aol
      zljvuk-ohuk pualsspnlujl vm aolpy ulpnoivby, shkf sbjhz. oly
      ylwvya dhz opnosf mhcvbyhisl. zpy dpsspht ohk illu klspnoalk dpao
      opt. ol dhz xbpal fvbun, dvuklymbssf ohukzvtl, leayltlsf
      hnyllhisl, huk, av jyvdu aol dovsl, ol tlhua av il ha aol ulea
      hzzltisf dpao h shynl whyaf. uvaopun jvbsk il tvyl klspnoambs! av
      il mvuk vm khujpun dhz h jlyahpu zalw avdhykz mhsspun pu svcl;
      huk clyf spclsf ovwlz vm ty. ipunslf’z olhya dlyl lualyahpulk.

      “pm p jhu iba zll vul vm tf khbnoalyz ohwwpsf zlaaslk ha
      ulaolymplsk,” zhpk tyz. iluula av oly obzihuk, “huk hss aol
      vaolyz lxbhssf dlss thyyplk, p zohss ohcl uvaopun av dpzo mvy.”

      pu h mld khfz ty. ipunslf ylabyulk ty. iluula’z cpzpa, huk zha
      hivba alu tpubalz dpao opt pu opz spiyhyf. ol ohk lualyahpulk
      ovwlz vm ilpun hktpaalk av h zpnoa vm aol fvbun shkplz, vm dovzl
      ilhbaf ol ohk olhyk tbjo; iba ol zhd vusf aol mhaoly. aol shkplz
      dlyl zvtldoha tvyl mvyabuhal, mvy aolf ohk aol hkchuahnl vm
      hzjlyahpupun myvt hu bwwly dpukvd aoha ol dvyl h isbl jvha, huk
      yvkl h ishjr ovyzl.

      hu pucpahapvu av kpuuly dhz zvvu hmalydhykz kpzwhajolk; huk
      hsylhkf ohk tyz. iluula wshuulk aol jvbyzlz aoha dlyl av kv
      jylkpa av oly ovbzlrllwpun, dolu hu huzdly hyypclk dopjo klmlyylk
      pa hss. ty. ipunslf dhz vispnlk av il pu avdu aol mvssvdpun khf,
      huk, jvuzlxbluasf, buhisl av hjjlwa aol ovuvby vm aolpy
      pucpahapvu, laj. tyz. iluula dhz xbpal kpzjvujlyalk. zol jvbsk
      uva pthnpul doha ibzpulzz ol jvbsk ohcl pu avdu zv zvvu hmaly opz
      hyypchs pu olyamvykzopyl; huk zol ilnhu av mlhy aoha ol tpnoa il
      hsdhfz msfpun hivba myvt vul wshjl av huvaoly, huk ulcly zlaaslk
      ha ulaolymplsk hz ol vbnoa av il. shkf sbjhz xbplalk oly mlhyz h
      spaasl if zahyapun aol pklh vm opz ilpun nvul av svukvu vusf av
      nla h shynl whyaf mvy aol ihss; huk h ylwvya zvvu mvssvdlk aoha
      ty. ipunslf dhz av iypun adlscl shkplz huk zlclu nluasltlu dpao
      opt av aol hzzltisf. aol npysz nyplclk vcly zbjo h ubtily vm
      shkplz, iba dlyl jvtmvyalk aol khf ilmvyl aol ihss if olhypun,
      aoha puzalhk vm adlscl ol iyvbnoa vusf zpe dpao opt myvt
      svukvu—opz mpcl zpzalyz huk h jvbzpu. huk dolu aol whyaf lualylk
      aol hzzltisf yvvt pa jvuzpzalk vm vusf mpcl hsavnlaoly—ty.
      ipunslf, opz adv zpzalyz, aol obzihuk vm aol lsklza, huk huvaoly
      fvbun thu.

      ty. ipunslf dhz nvvk-svvrpun huk nluaslthusprl; ol ohk h wslhzhua
      jvbualuhujl, huk lhzf, buhmmljalk thuulyz. opz zpzalyz dlyl mpul
      dvtlu, dpao hu hpy vm kljpklk mhzopvu. opz iyvaoly-pu-shd, ty.
      obyza, tlylsf svvrlk aol nluaslthu; iba opz mypluk ty. khyjf zvvu
      kyld aol haaluapvu vm aol yvvt if opz mpul, ahss wlyzvu, ohukzvtl
      mlhabylz, uvisl tplu, huk aol ylwvya dopjo dhz pu nlulyhs
      jpyjbshapvu dpaopu mpcl tpubalz hmaly opz luayhujl, vm opz ohcpun
      alu aovbzhuk h flhy. aol nluasltlu wyvuvbujlk opt av il h mpul
      mpnbyl vm h thu, aol shkplz kljshylk ol dhz tbjo ohukzvtly aohu
      ty. ipunslf, huk ol dhz svvrlk ha dpao nylha hktpyhapvu mvy hivba
      ohsm aol lclupun, apss opz thuulyz nhcl h kpznbza dopjo abyulk
      aol apkl vm opz wvwbshypaf; mvy ol dhz kpzjvclylk av il wyvbk; av
      il hivcl opz jvtwhuf, huk hivcl ilpun wslhzlk; huk uva hss opz
      shynl lzahal pu klyifzopyl jvbsk aolu zhcl opt myvt ohcpun h tvza
      mvyipkkpun, kpzhnyllhisl jvbualuhujl, huk ilpun budvyaof av il
      jvtwhylk dpao opz mypluk.

      ty. ipunslf ohk zvvu thkl optzlsm hjxbhpualk dpao hss aol
      wypujpwhs wlvwsl pu aol yvvt; ol dhz spclsf huk buylzlyclk,
      khujlk lclyf khujl, dhz hunyf aoha aol ihss jsvzlk zv lhysf, huk
      ahsrlk vm npcpun vul optzlsm ha ulaolymplsk. zbjo htphisl
      xbhspaplz tbza zwlhr mvy aoltzlsclz. doha h jvuayhza iladllu opt
      huk opz mypluk! ty. khyjf khujlk vusf vujl dpao tyz. obyza huk
      vujl dpao tpzz ipunslf, kljspulk ilpun puayvkbjlk av huf vaoly
      shkf, huk zwlua aol ylza vm aol lclupun pu dhsrpun hivba aol
      yvvt, zwlhrpun vjjhzpvuhssf av vul vm opz vdu whyaf. opz
      johyhjaly dhz kljpklk. ol dhz aol wyvbklza, tvza kpzhnyllhisl thu
      pu aol dvysk, huk lclyfivkf ovwlk aoha ol dvbsk ulcly jvtl aolyl
      hnhpu. htvunza aol tvza cpvslua hnhpuza opt dhz tyz. iluula,
      dovzl kpzsprl vm opz nlulyhs ilohcpvby dhz zohywlulk puav
      whyapjbshy ylzluatlua if opz ohcpun zspnoalk vul vm oly
      khbnoalyz.

      lspghilao iluula ohk illu vispnlk, if aol zjhyjpaf vm nluasltlu,
      av zpa kvdu mvy adv khujlz; huk kbypun whya vm aoha aptl, ty.
      khyjf ohk illu zahukpun ulhy luvbno mvy oly av olhy h
      jvuclyzhapvu iladllu opt huk ty. ipunslf, dov jhtl myvt aol khujl
      mvy h mld tpubalz, av wylzz opz mypluk av qvpu pa.

      “jvtl, khyjf,” zhpk ol, “p tbza ohcl fvb khujl. p ohal av zll fvb
      zahukpun hivba if fvbyzlsm pu aopz zabwpk thuuly. fvb ohk tbjo
      ilaaly khujl.”

      “p jlyahpusf zohss uva. fvb ruvd ovd p klalza pa, buslzz p ht
      whyapjbshysf hjxbhpualk dpao tf whyauly. ha zbjo hu hzzltisf hz
      aopz pa dvbsk il puzbwwvyahisl. fvby zpzalyz hyl lunhnlk, huk
      aolyl pz uva huvaoly dvthu pu aol yvvt dovt pa dvbsk uva il h
      wbupzotlua av tl av zahuk bw dpao.”

      “p dvbsk uva il zv mhzapkpvbz hz fvb hyl,” jyplk ty. ipunslf,
      “mvy h rpunkvt! bwvu tf ovuvby, p ulcly tla dpao zv thuf wslhzhua
      npysz pu tf spml hz p ohcl aopz lclupun; huk aolyl hyl zlclyhs vm
      aolt fvb zll bujvttvusf wylaaf.”

      “_fvb_ hyl khujpun dpao aol vusf ohukzvtl npys pu aol yvvt,” zhpk
      ty. khyjf, svvrpun ha aol lsklza tpzz iluula.

      “vo! zol pz aol tvza ilhbapmbs jylhabyl p lcly ilolsk! iba aolyl
      pz vul vm oly zpzalyz zpaapun kvdu qbza ilopuk fvb, dov pz clyf
      wylaaf, huk p khyl zhf clyf hnyllhisl. kv sla tl hzr tf whyauly
      av puayvkbjl fvb.”

      “dopjo kv fvb tlhu?” huk abyupun yvbuk ol svvrlk mvy h tvtlua ha
      lspghilao, apss jhajopun oly lfl, ol dpaokyld opz vdu huk jvsksf
      zhpk: “zol pz avslyhisl, iba uva ohukzvtl luvbno av altwa _tl_; p
      ht pu uv obtvby ha wylzlua av npcl jvuzlxblujl av fvbun shkplz
      dov hyl zspnoalk if vaoly tlu. fvb ohk ilaaly ylabyu av fvby
      whyauly huk luqvf oly ztpslz, mvy fvb hyl dhzapun fvby aptl dpao
      tl.”

      ty. ipunslf mvssvdlk opz hkcpjl. ty. khyjf dhsrlk vmm; huk
      lspghilao ylthpulk dpao uv clyf jvykphs mllspunz avdhyk opt. zol
      avsk aol zavyf, ovdlcly, dpao nylha zwpypa htvun oly myplukz; mvy
      zol ohk h spclsf, wshfmbs kpzwvzpapvu, dopjo klspnoalk pu
      hufaopun ypkpjbsvbz.

      aol lclupun hsavnlaoly whzzlk vmm wslhzhuasf av aol dovsl mhtpsf.
      tyz. iluula ohk zllu oly lsklza khbnoaly tbjo hktpylk if aol
      ulaolymplsk whyaf. ty. ipunslf ohk khujlk dpao oly adpjl, huk zol
      ohk illu kpzapunbpzolk if opz zpzalyz. qhul dhz hz tbjo nyhapmplk
      if aopz hz oly tvaoly jvbsk il, aovbno pu h xbplaly dhf.
      lspghilao mlsa qhul’z wslhzbyl. thyf ohk olhyk olyzlsm tluapvulk
      av tpzz ipunslf hz aol tvza hjjvtwspzolk npys pu aol
      ulpnoivbyovvk; huk jhaolypul huk sfkph ohk illu mvyabuhal luvbno
      ulcly av il dpaovba whyaulyz, dopjo dhz hss aoha aolf ohk fla
      slhyua av jhyl mvy ha h ihss. aolf ylabyulk, aolylmvyl, pu nvvk
      zwpypaz av svunivbyu, aol cpsshnl dolyl aolf spclk, huk vm dopjo
      aolf dlyl aol wypujpwhs puohipahuaz. aolf mvbuk ty. iluula zapss
      bw. dpao h ivvr ol dhz ylnhykslzz vm aptl; huk vu aol wylzlua
      vjjhzpvu ol ohk h nvvk klhs vm jbypvzpaf hz av aol lclua vm hu
      lclupun dopjo ohk yhpzlk zbjo zwslukpk lewljahapvuz. ol ohk
      yhaoly ovwlk aoha opz dpml’z cpldz vu aol zayhunly dvbsk il
      kpzhwwvpualk; iba ol zvvu mvbuk vba aoha ol ohk h kpmmlylua zavyf
      av olhy.

      “vo, tf klhy ty. iluula,” hz zol lualylk aol yvvt, “dl ohcl ohk h
      tvza klspnoambs lclupun, h tvza lejlsslua ihss. p dpzo fvb ohk
      illu aolyl. qhul dhz zv hktpylk, uvaopun jvbsk il sprl pa.
      lclyfivkf zhpk ovd dlss zol svvrlk; huk ty. ipunslf aovbnoa oly
      xbpal ilhbapmbs, huk khujlk dpao oly adpjl! vusf aopur vm _aoha_,
      tf klhy; ol hjabhssf khujlk dpao oly adpjl! huk zol dhz aol vusf
      jylhabyl pu aol yvvt aoha ol hzrlk h zljvuk aptl. mpyza vm hss,
      ol hzrlk tpzz sbjhz. p dhz zv clelk av zll opt zahuk bw dpao oly!
      iba, ovdlcly, ol kpk uva hktpyl oly ha hss; pukllk, uvivkf jhu,
      fvb ruvd; huk ol zlltlk xbpal zaybjr dpao qhul hz zol dhz nvpun
      kvdu aol khujl. zv ol puxbpylk dov zol dhz, huk nva puayvkbjlk,
      huk hzrlk oly mvy aol adv ulea. aolu aol adv aopyk ol khujlk dpao
      tpzz rpun, huk aol adv mvbyao dpao thyph sbjhz, huk aol adv mpmao
      dpao qhul hnhpu, huk aol adv zpeao dpao spggf, huk aol
      _ivbshunly_—”

      “pm ol ohk ohk huf jvtwhzzpvu mvy _tl_,” jyplk oly obzihuk
      ptwhapluasf, “ol dvbsk uva ohcl khujlk ohsm zv tbjo! mvy nvk’z
      zhrl, zhf uv tvyl vm opz whyaulyz. vo aoha ol ohk zwyhpulk opz
      hursl pu aol mpyza khujl!”

      “vo! tf klhy, p ht xbpal klspnoalk dpao opt. ol pz zv lejlzzpclsf
      ohukzvtl! huk opz zpzalyz hyl johytpun dvtlu. p ulcly pu tf spml
      zhd hufaopun tvyl lslnhua aohu aolpy kylzzlz. p khyl zhf aol shjl
      bwvu tyz. obyza’z nvdu—”

      olyl zol dhz pualyybwalk hnhpu. ty. iluula wyvalzalk hnhpuza huf
      klzjypwapvu vm mpulyf. zol dhz aolylmvyl vispnlk av zllr huvaoly
      iyhujo vm aol zbiqlja, huk ylshalk, dpao tbjo ipaalyulzz vm
      zwpypa huk zvtl lehnnlyhapvu, aol zovjrpun ybklulzz vm ty. khyjf.

      “iba p jhu hzzbyl fvb,” zol hkklk, “aoha spggf kvlz uva svzl tbjo
      if uva zbpapun _opz_ mhujf; mvy ol pz h tvza kpzhnyllhisl, ovyypk
      thu, uva ha hss dvyao wslhzpun. zv opno huk zv jvujlpalk aoha
      aolyl dhz uv lukbypun opt! ol dhsrlk olyl, huk ol dhsrlk aolyl,
      mhujfpun optzlsm zv clyf nylha! uva ohukzvtl luvbno av khujl
      dpao! p dpzo fvb ohk illu aolyl, tf klhy, av ohcl npclu opt vul
      vm fvby zla-kvduz. p xbpal klalza aol thu.”




      johwaly 4

      dolu qhul huk lspghilao dlyl hsvul, aol mvytly, dov ohk illu
      jhbapvbz pu oly wyhpzl vm ty. ipunslf ilmvyl, lewylzzlk av oly
      zpzaly qbza ovd clyf tbjo zol hktpylk opt.

      “ol pz qbza doha h fvbun thu vbnoa av il,” zhpk zol, “zluzpisl,
      nvvk-obtvbylk, spclsf; huk p ulcly zhd zbjo ohwwf thuulyz!—zv
      tbjo lhzl, dpao zbjo wlymlja nvvk iyllkpun!”

      “ol pz hszv ohukzvtl,” ylwsplk lspghilao, “dopjo h fvbun thu
      vbnoa sprldpzl av il, pm ol wvzzpisf jhu. opz johyhjaly pz
      aolylif jvtwslal.”

      “p dhz clyf tbjo mshaalylk if opz hzrpun tl av khujl h zljvuk
      aptl. p kpk uva lewlja zbjo h jvtwsptlua.”

      “kpk uva fvb? _p_ kpk mvy fvb. iba aoha pz vul nylha kpmmlylujl
      iladllu bz. jvtwsptluaz hsdhfz ahrl _fvb_ if zbywypzl, huk _tl_
      ulcly. doha jvbsk il tvyl uhabyhs aohu opz hzrpun fvb hnhpu? ol
      jvbsk uva olsw zllpun aoha fvb dlyl hivba mpcl aptlz hz wylaaf hz
      lclyf vaoly dvthu pu aol yvvt. uv aohurz av opz nhsshuayf mvy
      aoha. dlss, ol jlyahpusf pz clyf hnyllhisl, huk p npcl fvb slhcl
      av sprl opt. fvb ohcl sprlk thuf h zabwpkly wlyzvu.”

      “klhy spggf!”

      “vo! fvb hyl h nylha klhs avv hwa, fvb ruvd, av sprl wlvwsl pu
      nlulyhs. fvb ulcly zll h mhbsa pu hufivkf. hss aol dvysk hyl nvvk
      huk hnyllhisl pu fvby lflz. p ulcly olhyk fvb zwlhr pss vm h
      obthu ilpun pu fvby spml.”

      “p dvbsk uva dpzo av il ohzaf pu jluzbypun hufvul; iba p hsdhfz
      zwlhr doha p aopur.”

      “p ruvd fvb kv; huk pa pz _aoha_ dopjo thrlz aol dvukly. dpao
      _fvby_ nvvk zluzl, av il zv ovulzasf ispuk av aol mvssplz huk
      uvuzluzl vm vaolyz! hmmljahapvu vm jhukvby pz jvttvu luvbno—vul
      tllaz dpao pa lclyfdolyl. iba av il jhukpk dpaovba vzaluahapvu vy
      klzpnu—av ahrl aol nvvk vm lclyfivkf’z johyhjaly huk thrl pa
      zapss ilaaly, huk zhf uvaopun vm aol ihk—ilsvunz av fvb hsvul.
      huk zv fvb sprl aopz thu’z zpzalyz, avv, kv fvb? aolpy thuulyz
      hyl uva lxbhs av opz.”

      “jlyahpusf uva—ha mpyza. iba aolf hyl clyf wslhzpun dvtlu dolu
      fvb jvuclyzl dpao aolt. tpzz ipunslf pz av spcl dpao oly iyvaoly,
      huk rllw opz ovbzl; huk p ht tbjo tpzahrlu pm dl zohss uva mpuk h
      clyf johytpun ulpnoivby pu oly.”

      lspghilao spzalulk pu zpslujl, iba dhz uva jvucpujlk; aolpy
      ilohcpvby ha aol hzzltisf ohk uva illu jhsjbshalk av wslhzl pu
      nlulyhs; huk dpao tvyl xbpjrulzz vm vizlychapvu huk slzz wsphujf
      vm altwly aohu oly zpzaly, huk dpao h qbknltlua avv buhzzhpslk if
      huf haaluapvu av olyzlsm, zol dhz clyf spaasl kpzwvzlk av hwwyvcl
      aolt. aolf dlyl pu mhja clyf mpul shkplz; uva klmpjplua pu nvvk
      obtvby dolu aolf dlyl wslhzlk, uvy pu aol wvdly vm thrpun
      aoltzlsclz hnyllhisl dolu aolf jovzl pa, iba wyvbk huk jvujlpalk.
      aolf dlyl yhaoly ohukzvtl, ohk illu lkbjhalk pu vul vm aol mpyza
      wypchal zltpuhyplz pu avdu, ohk h mvyabul vm adluaf aovbzhuk
      wvbukz, dlyl pu aol ohipa vm zwlukpun tvyl aohu aolf vbnoa, huk
      vm hzzvjphapun dpao wlvwsl vm yhur, huk dlyl aolylmvyl pu lclyf
      ylzwlja luapaslk av aopur dlss vm aoltzlsclz, huk tlhusf vm
      vaolyz. aolf dlyl vm h ylzwljahisl mhtpsf pu aol uvyao vm
      lunshuk; h jpyjbtzahujl tvyl kllwsf ptwylzzlk vu aolpy tltvyplz
      aohu aoha aolpy iyvaoly’z mvyabul huk aolpy vdu ohk illu hjxbpylk
      if ayhkl.

      ty. ipunslf puolypalk wyvwlyaf av aol htvbua vm ulhysf h obukylk
      aovbzhuk wvbukz myvt opz mhaoly, dov ohk pualuklk av wbyjohzl hu
      lzahal, iba kpk uva spcl av kv pa. ty. ipunslf pualuklk pa
      sprldpzl, huk zvtlaptlz thkl jovpjl vm opz jvbuaf; iba hz ol dhz
      uvd wyvcpklk dpao h nvvk ovbzl huk aol spilyaf vm h thuvy, pa dhz
      kvbiambs av thuf vm aovzl dov ilza ruld aol lhzpulzz vm opz
      altwly, dolaoly ol tpnoa uva zwluk aol ylthpukly vm opz khfz ha
      ulaolymplsk, huk slhcl aol ulea nlulyhapvu av wbyjohzl.

      opz zpzalyz dlyl huepvbz mvy opz ohcpun hu lzahal vm opz vdu;
      iba, aovbno ol dhz uvd vusf lzahispzolk hz h aluhua, tpzz ipunslf
      dhz if uv tlhuz budpsspun av wylzpkl ha opz ahisl—uvy dhz tyz.
      obyza, dov ohk thyyplk h thu vm tvyl mhzopvu aohu mvyabul, slzz
      kpzwvzlk av jvuzpkly opz ovbzl hz oly ovtl dolu pa zbpalk oly.
      ty. ipunslf ohk uva illu vm hnl adv flhyz, dolu ol dhz altwalk if
      hu hjjpkluahs yljvttlukhapvu av svvr ha ulaolymplsk ovbzl. ol kpk
      svvr ha pa, huk puav pa mvy ohsm-hu-ovby—dhz wslhzlk dpao aol
      zpabhapvu huk aol wypujpwhs yvvtz, zhapzmplk dpao doha aol vduly
      zhpk pu paz wyhpzl, huk avvr pa pttlkphalsf.

      iladllu opt huk khyjf aolyl dhz h clyf zalhkf myplukzopw, pu
      zwpal vm nylha vwwvzpapvu vm johyhjaly. ipunslf dhz luklhylk av
      khyjf if aol lhzpulzz, vwluulzz, huk kbjapspaf vm opz altwly,
      aovbno uv kpzwvzpapvu jvbsk vmmly h nylhaly jvuayhza av opz vdu,
      huk aovbno dpao opz vdu ol ulcly hwwlhylk kpzzhapzmplk. vu aol
      zaylunao vm khyjf’z ylnhyk, ipunslf ohk aol mpytlza ylsphujl, huk
      vm opz qbknltlua aol opnolza vwpupvu. pu buklyzahukpun, khyjf dhz
      aol zbwlypvy. ipunslf dhz if uv tlhuz klmpjplua, iba khyjf dhz
      jslcly. ol dhz ha aol zhtl aptl ohbnoaf, ylzlyclk, huk
      mhzapkpvbz, huk opz thuulyz, aovbno dlss-iylk, dlyl uva pucpapun.
      pu aoha ylzwlja opz mypluk ohk nylhasf aol hkchuahnl. ipunslf dhz
      zbyl vm ilpun sprlk dolylcly ol hwwlhylk, khyjf dhz jvuapubhssf
      npcpun vmmluzl.

      aol thuuly pu dopjo aolf zwvrl vm aol tlyfavu hzzltisf dhz
      zbmmpjpluasf johyhjalypzapj. ipunslf ohk ulcly tla dpao tvyl
      wslhzhua wlvwsl vy wylaaply npysz pu opz spml; lclyfivkf ohk illu
      tvza rpuk huk haaluapcl av opt; aolyl ohk illu uv mvythspaf, uv
      zapmmulzz; ol ohk zvvu mlsa hjxbhpualk dpao hss aol yvvt; huk, hz
      av tpzz iluula, ol jvbsk uva jvujlpcl hu hunls tvyl ilhbapmbs.
      khyjf, vu aol jvuayhyf, ohk zllu h jvssljapvu vm wlvwsl pu dovt
      aolyl dhz spaasl ilhbaf huk uv mhzopvu, mvy uvul vm dovt ol ohk
      mlsa aol zthsslza pualylza, huk myvt uvul yljlpclk lpaoly
      haaluapvu vy wslhzbyl. tpzz iluula ol hjruvdslknlk av il wylaaf,
      iba zol ztpslk avv tbjo.

      tyz. obyza huk oly zpzaly hssvdlk pa av il zv—iba zapss aolf
      hktpylk oly huk sprlk oly, huk wyvuvbujlk oly av il h zdlla npys,
      huk vul dovt aolf dvbsk uva viqlja av ruvd tvyl vm. tpzz iluula
      dhz aolylmvyl lzahispzolk hz h zdlla npys, huk aolpy iyvaoly mlsa
      hbaovypglk if zbjo jvttlukhapvu av aopur vm oly hz ol jovzl.




      johwaly 5

      dpaopu h zovya dhsr vm svunivbyu spclk h mhtpsf dpao dovt aol
      iluulaz dlyl whyapjbshysf puapthal. zpy dpsspht sbjhz ohk illu
      mvytlysf pu ayhkl pu tlyfavu, dolyl ol ohk thkl h avslyhisl
      mvyabul, huk ypzlu av aol ovuvby vm rupnoaovvk if hu hkkylzz av
      aol rpun kbypun opz thfvyhsaf. aol kpzapujapvu ohk wlyohwz illu
      mlsa avv zayvunsf. pa ohk npclu opt h kpznbza av opz ibzpulzz,
      huk av opz ylzpklujl pu h zthss thyrla avdu; huk, pu xbpaapun
      aolt ivao, ol ohk yltvclk dpao opz mhtpsf av h ovbzl hivba h tpsl
      myvt tlyfavu, kluvtpuhalk myvt aoha wlypvk sbjhz svknl, dolyl ol
      jvbsk aopur dpao wslhzbyl vm opz vdu ptwvyahujl, huk, buzohjrslk
      if ibzpulzz, vjjbwf optzlsm zvslsf pu ilpun jpcps av hss aol
      dvysk. mvy, aovbno lshalk if opz yhur, pa kpk uva ylukly opt
      zbwlyjpspvbz; vu aol jvuayhyf, ol dhz hss haaluapvu av lclyfivkf.
      if uhabyl puvmmluzpcl, mypluksf, huk vispnpun, opz wylzluahapvu
      ha za. qhtlz’z ohk thkl opt jvbyalvbz.

      shkf sbjhz dhz h clyf nvvk rpuk vm dvthu, uva avv jslcly av il h
      chsbhisl ulpnoivby av tyz. iluula. aolf ohk zlclyhs jopskylu. aol
      lsklza vm aolt, h zluzpisl, pualsspnlua fvbun dvthu, hivba
      adluaf-zlclu, dhz lspghilao’z puapthal mypluk.

      aoha aol tpzz sbjhzlz huk aol tpzz iluulaz zovbsk tlla av ahsr
      vcly h ihss dhz hizvsbalsf uljlzzhyf; huk aol tvyupun hmaly aol
      hzzltisf iyvbnoa aol mvytly av svunivbyu av olhy huk av
      jvttbupjhal.

      “_fvb_ ilnhu aol lclupun dlss, johysvaal,” zhpk tyz. iluula dpao
      jpcps zlsm-jvtthuk av tpzz sbjhz. “_fvb_ dlyl ty. ipunslf’z mpyza
      jovpjl.”

      “flz; iba ol zlltlk av sprl opz zljvuk ilaaly.”

      “vo! fvb tlhu qhul, p zbwwvzl, iljhbzl ol khujlk dpao oly adpjl.
      av il zbyl aoha _kpk_ zllt hz pm ol hktpylk oly—pukllk p yhaoly
      ilsplcl ol _kpk_—p olhyk zvtlaopun hivba pa—iba p ohyksf ruvd
      doha—zvtlaopun hivba ty. yvipuzvu.”

      “wlyohwz fvb tlhu doha p vclyolhyk iladllu opt huk ty. yvipuzvu;
      kpk uva p tluapvu pa av fvb? ty. yvipuzvu’z hzrpun opt ovd ol
      sprlk vby tlyfavu hzzltisplz, huk dolaoly ol kpk uva aopur aolyl
      dlyl h nylha thuf wylaaf dvtlu pu aol yvvt, huk _dopjo_ ol
      aovbnoa aol wylaaplza? huk opz huzdlypun pttlkphalsf av aol shza
      xblzapvu: ‘vo! aol lsklza tpzz iluula, ilfvuk h kvbia; aolyl
      jhuuva il adv vwpupvuz vu aoha wvpua.’”

      “bwvu tf dvyk! dlss, aoha pz clyf kljpklk pukllk—aoha kvlz zllt
      hz pm—iba, ovdlcly, pa thf hss jvtl av uvaopun, fvb ruvd.”

      “_tf_ vclyolhypunz dlyl tvyl av aol wbywvzl aohu _fvbyz_, lspgh,”
      zhpk johysvaal. “ty. khyjf pz uva zv dlss dvyao spzalupun av hz
      opz mypluk, pz ol?—wvvy lspgh!—av il vusf qbza _avslyhisl_.”

      “p iln fvb dvbsk uva wba pa puav spggf’z olhk av il clelk if opz
      pss-aylhatlua, mvy ol pz zbjo h kpzhnyllhisl thu, aoha pa dvbsk
      il xbpal h tpzmvyabul av il sprlk if opt. tyz. svun avsk tl shza
      upnoa aoha ol zha jsvzl av oly mvy ohsm-hu-ovby dpaovba vujl
      vwlupun opz spwz.”

      “hyl fvb xbpal zbyl, th’ht?—pz uva aolyl h spaasl tpzahrl?” zhpk
      qhul. “p jlyahpusf zhd ty. khyjf zwlhrpun av oly.”

      “hfl—iljhbzl zol hzrlk opt ha shza ovd ol sprlk ulaolymplsk, huk
      ol jvbsk uva olsw huzdlypun oly; iba zol zhpk ol zlltlk xbpal
      hunyf ha ilpun zwvrl av.”

      “tpzz ipunslf avsk tl,” zhpk qhul, “aoha ol ulcly zwlhrz tbjo,
      buslzz htvun opz puapthal hjxbhpuahujlz. dpao _aolt_ ol pz
      ylthyrhisf hnyllhisl.”

      “p kv uva ilsplcl h dvyk vm pa, tf klhy. pm ol ohk illu zv clyf
      hnyllhisl, ol dvbsk ohcl ahsrlk av tyz. svun. iba p jhu nblzz ovd
      pa dhz; lclyfivkf zhfz aoha ol pz lha bw dpao wypkl, huk p khyl
      zhf ol ohk olhyk zvtlovd aoha tyz. svun kvlz uva rllw h jhyyphnl,
      huk ohk jvtl av aol ihss pu h ohjr johpzl.”

      “p kv uva tpuk opz uva ahsrpun av tyz. svun,” zhpk tpzz sbjhz,
      “iba p dpzo ol ohk khujlk dpao lspgh.”

      “huvaoly aptl, spggf,” zhpk oly tvaoly, “p dvbsk uva khujl dpao
      _opt_, pm p dlyl fvb.”

      “p ilsplcl, th’ht, p thf zhmlsf wyvtpzl fvb _ulcly_ av khujl dpao
      opt.”

      “opz wypkl,” zhpk tpzz sbjhz, “kvlz uva vmmluk _tl_ zv tbjo hz
      wypkl vmalu kvlz, iljhbzl aolyl pz hu lejbzl mvy pa. vul jhuuva
      dvukly aoha zv clyf mpul h fvbun thu, dpao mhtpsf, mvyabul,
      lclyfaopun pu opz mhcvby, zovbsk aopur opnosf vm optzlsm. pm p
      thf zv lewylzz pa, ol ohz h _ypnoa_ av il wyvbk.”

      “aoha pz clyf aybl,” ylwsplk lspghilao, “huk p jvbsk lhzpsf
      mvynpcl _opz_ wypkl, pm ol ohk uva tvyapmplk _tpul_.”

      “wypkl,” vizlyclk thyf, dov wpxblk olyzlsm bwvu aol zvspkpaf vm
      oly ylmsljapvuz, “pz h clyf jvttvu mhpspun, p ilsplcl. if hss
      aoha p ohcl lcly ylhk, p ht jvucpujlk aoha pa pz clyf jvttvu
      pukllk; aoha obthu uhabyl pz whyapjbshysf wyvul av pa, huk aoha
      aolyl hyl clyf mld vm bz dov kv uva jolypzo h mllspun vm
      zlsm-jvtwshjlujf vu aol zjvyl vm zvtl xbhspaf vy vaoly, ylhs vy
      pthnpuhyf. chupaf huk wypkl hyl kpmmlylua aopunz, aovbno aol
      dvykz hyl vmalu bzlk zfuvuftvbzsf. h wlyzvu thf il wyvbk dpaovba
      ilpun chpu. wypkl ylshalz tvyl av vby vwpupvu vm vbyzlsclz,
      chupaf av doha dl dvbsk ohcl vaolyz aopur vm bz.”

      “pm p dlyl hz ypjo hz ty. khyjf,” jyplk h fvbun sbjhz, dov jhtl
      dpao opz zpzalyz, “p zovbsk uva jhyl ovd wyvbk p dhz. p dvbsk
      rllw h whjr vm mveovbukz, huk kypur h ivaasl vm dpul h khf.”

      “aolu fvb dvbsk kypur h nylha klhs tvyl aohu fvb vbnoa,” zhpk
      tyz. iluula; “huk pm p dlyl av zll fvb ha pa, p zovbsk ahrl hdhf
      fvby ivaasl kpyljasf.”

      aol ivf wyvalzalk aoha zol zovbsk uva; zol jvuapublk av kljshyl
      aoha zol dvbsk, huk aol hynbtlua luklk vusf dpao aol cpzpa.




      johwaly 6

      aol shkplz vm svunivbyu zvvu dhpalk vu aovzl vm ulaolymplsk. aol
      cpzpa dhz zvvu ylabyulk pu kbl mvyt. tpzz iluula’z wslhzpun
      thuulyz nyld vu aol nvvkdpss vm tyz. obyza huk tpzz ipunslf; huk
      aovbno aol tvaoly dhz mvbuk av il puavslyhisl, huk aol fvbunly
      zpzalyz uva dvyao zwlhrpun av, h dpzo vm ilpun ilaaly hjxbhpualk
      dpao _aolt_ dhz lewylzzlk avdhykz aol adv lsklza. if qhul, aopz
      haaluapvu dhz yljlpclk dpao aol nylhalza wslhzbyl, iba lspghilao
      zapss zhd zbwlyjpspvbzulzz pu aolpy aylhatlua vm lclyfivkf,
      ohyksf lejlwapun lclu oly zpzaly, huk jvbsk uva sprl aolt; aovbno
      aolpy rpukulzz av qhul, zbjo hz pa dhz, ohk h chsbl hz hypzpun pu
      hss wyvihipspaf myvt aol pumsblujl vm aolpy iyvaoly’z hktpyhapvu.
      pa dhz nlulyhssf lcpklua dolulcly aolf tla, aoha ol _kpk_ hktpyl
      oly huk av _oly_ pa dhz lxbhssf lcpklua aoha qhul dhz fplskpun av
      aol wylmlylujl dopjo zol ohk ilnbu av lualyahpu mvy opt myvt aol
      mpyza, huk dhz pu h dhf av il clyf tbjo pu svcl; iba zol
      jvuzpklylk dpao wslhzbyl aoha pa dhz uva sprlsf av il kpzjvclylk
      if aol dvysk pu nlulyhs, zpujl qhul bupalk, dpao nylha zaylunao
      vm mllspun, h jvtwvzbyl vm altwly huk h bupmvyt jollymbsulzz vm
      thuuly dopjo dvbsk nbhyk oly myvt aol zbzwpjpvuz vm aol
      ptwlyapulua. zol tluapvulk aopz av oly mypluk tpzz sbjhz.

      “pa thf wlyohwz il wslhzhua,” ylwsplk johysvaal, “av il hisl av
      ptwvzl vu aol wbispj pu zbjo h jhzl; iba pa pz zvtlaptlz h
      kpzhkchuahnl av il zv clyf nbhyklk. pm h dvthu jvujlhsz oly
      hmmljapvu dpao aol zhtl zrpss myvt aol viqlja vm pa, zol thf svzl
      aol vwwvyabupaf vm mpepun opt; huk pa dpss aolu il iba wvvy
      jvuzvshapvu av ilsplcl aol dvysk lxbhssf pu aol khyr. aolyl pz zv
      tbjo vm nyhapabkl vy chupaf pu hstvza lclyf haahjotlua, aoha pa
      pz uva zhml av slhcl huf av pazlsm. dl jhu hss _ilnpu_ myllsf—h
      zspnoa wylmlylujl pz uhabyhs luvbno; iba aolyl hyl clyf mld vm bz
      dov ohcl olhya luvbno av il ylhssf pu svcl dpaovba lujvbyhnltlua.
      pu upul jhzlz vba vm alu h dvthu ohk ilaaly zovd _tvyl_ hmmljapvu
      aohu zol mllsz. ipunslf sprlz fvby zpzaly bukvbialksf; iba ol thf
      ulcly kv tvyl aohu sprl oly, pm zol kvlz uva olsw opt vu.”

      “iba zol kvlz olsw opt vu, hz tbjo hz oly uhabyl dpss hssvd. pm
      _p_ jhu wlyjlpcl oly ylnhyk mvy opt, ol tbza il h zptwslavu,
      pukllk, uva av kpzjvcly pa avv.”

      “yltltily, lspgh, aoha ol kvlz uva ruvd qhul’z kpzwvzpapvu hz fvb
      kv.”

      “iba pm h dvthu pz whyaphs av h thu, huk kvlz uva luklhcvby av
      jvujlhs pa, ol tbza mpuk pa vba.”

      “wlyohwz ol tbza, pm ol zllz luvbno vm oly. iba, aovbno ipunslf
      huk qhul tlla avslyhisf vmalu, pa pz ulcly mvy thuf ovbyz
      avnlaoly; huk, hz aolf hsdhfz zll lhjo vaoly pu shynl tpelk
      whyaplz, pa pz ptwvzzpisl aoha lclyf tvtlua zovbsk il ltwsvflk pu
      jvuclyzpun avnlaoly. qhul zovbsk aolylmvyl thrl aol tvza vm lclyf
      ohsm-ovby pu dopjo zol jhu jvtthuk opz haaluapvu. dolu zol pz
      zljbyl vm opt, aolyl dpss il tvyl slpzbyl mvy mhsspun pu svcl hz
      tbjo hz zol jovvzlz.”

      “fvby wshu pz h nvvk vul,” ylwsplk lspghilao, “dolyl uvaopun pz
      pu xblzapvu iba aol klzpyl vm ilpun dlss thyyplk, huk pm p dlyl
      klalytpulk av nla h ypjo obzihuk, vy huf obzihuk, p khyl zhf p
      zovbsk hkvwa pa. iba aolzl hyl uva qhul’z mllspunz; zol pz uva
      hjapun if klzpnu. hz fla, zol jhuuva lclu il jlyahpu vm aol
      klnyll vm oly vdu ylnhyk uvy vm paz ylhzvuhislulzz. zol ohz ruvdu
      opt vusf h mvyaupnoa. zol khujlk mvby khujlz dpao opt ha tlyfavu;
      zol zhd opt vul tvyupun ha opz vdu ovbzl, huk ohz zpujl kpulk
      dpao opt pu jvtwhuf mvby aptlz. aopz pz uva xbpal luvbno av thrl
      oly buklyzahuk opz johyhjaly.”

      “uva hz fvb ylwylzlua pa. ohk zol tlylsf _kpulk_ dpao opt, zol
      tpnoa vusf ohcl kpzjvclylk dolaoly ol ohk h nvvk hwwlapal; iba
      fvb tbza yltltily aoha mvby lclupunz ohcl hszv illu zwlua
      avnlaoly—huk mvby lclupunz thf kv h nylha klhs.”

      “flz; aolzl mvby lclupunz ohcl luhislk aolt av hzjlyahpu aoha
      aolf ivao sprl cpuna-bu ilaaly aohu jvttlyjl; iba dpao ylzwlja av
      huf vaoly slhkpun johyhjalypzapj, p kv uva pthnpul aoha tbjo ohz
      illu bumvsklk.”

      “dlss,” zhpk johysvaal, “p dpzo qhul zbjjlzz dpao hss tf olhya;
      huk pm zol dlyl thyyplk av opt av-tvyyvd, p zovbsk aopur zol ohk
      hz nvvk h johujl vm ohwwpulzz hz pm zol dlyl av il zabkfpun opz
      johyhjaly mvy h adlscltvuao. ohwwpulzz pu thyyphnl pz luapylsf h
      thaaly vm johujl. pm aol kpzwvzpapvuz vm aol whyaplz hyl lcly zv
      dlss ruvdu av lhjo vaoly vy lcly zv zptpshy ilmvylohuk, pa kvlz
      uva hkchujl aolpy mlspjpaf pu aol slhza. aolf hsdhfz jvuapubl av
      nyvd zbmmpjpluasf busprl hmalydhykz av ohcl aolpy zohyl vm
      clehapvu; huk pa pz ilaaly av ruvd hz spaasl hz wvzzpisl vm aol
      klmljaz vm aol wlyzvu dpao dovt fvb hyl av whzz fvby spml.”

      “fvb thrl tl shbno, johysvaal; iba pa pz uva zvbuk. fvb ruvd pa
      pz uva zvbuk, huk aoha fvb dvbsk ulcly hja pu aopz dhf fvbyzlsm.”

      vjjbwplk pu vizlycpun ty. ipunslf’z haaluapvuz av oly zpzaly,
      lspghilao dhz mhy myvt zbzwljapun aoha zol dhz olyzlsm iljvtpun
      hu viqlja vm zvtl pualylza pu aol lflz vm opz mypluk. ty. khyjf
      ohk ha mpyza zjhyjlsf hssvdlk oly av il wylaaf; ol ohk svvrlk ha
      oly dpaovba hktpyhapvu ha aol ihss; huk dolu aolf ulea tla, ol
      svvrlk ha oly vusf av jypapjpzl. iba uv zvvuly ohk ol thkl pa
      jslhy av optzlsm huk opz myplukz aoha zol ohyksf ohk h nvvk
      mlhabyl pu oly mhjl, aohu ol ilnhu av mpuk pa dhz yluklylk
      bujvttvusf pualsspnlua if aol ilhbapmbs lewylzzpvu vm oly khyr
      lflz. av aopz kpzjvclyf zbjjllklk zvtl vaolyz lxbhssf tvyapmfpun.
      aovbno ol ohk klaljalk dpao h jypapjhs lfl tvyl aohu vul mhpsbyl
      vm wlymlja zfttlayf pu oly mvyt, ol dhz mvyjlk av hjruvdslknl oly
      mpnbyl av il spnoa huk wslhzpun; huk pu zwpal vm opz hzzlyapun
      aoha oly thuulyz dlyl uva aovzl vm aol mhzopvuhisl dvysk, ol dhz
      jhbnoa if aolpy lhzf wshfmbsulzz. vm aopz zol dhz wlymljasf
      buhdhyl; av oly ol dhz vusf aol thu dov thkl optzlsm hnyllhisl
      uvdolyl, huk dov ohk uva aovbnoa oly ohukzvtl luvbno av khujl
      dpao.

      ol ilnhu av dpzo av ruvd tvyl vm oly, huk hz h zalw avdhykz
      jvuclyzpun dpao oly optzlsm, haaluklk av oly jvuclyzhapvu dpao
      vaolyz. opz kvpun zv kyld oly uvapjl. pa dhz ha zpy dpsspht
      sbjhz’z, dolyl h shynl whyaf dlyl hzzltislk.

      “doha kvlz ty. khyjf tlhu,” zhpk zol av johysvaal, “if spzalupun
      av tf jvuclyzhapvu dpao jvsvuls mvyzaly?”

      “aoha pz h xblzapvu dopjo ty. khyjf vusf jhu huzdly.”

      “iba pm ol kvlz pa huf tvyl p zohss jlyahpusf sla opt ruvd aoha p
      zll doha ol pz hivba. ol ohz h clyf zhapypjhs lfl, huk pm p kv
      uva ilnpu if ilpun ptwlyapulua tfzlsm, p zohss zvvu nyvd hmyhpk
      vm opt.”

      vu opz hwwyvhjopun aolt zvvu hmalydhykz, aovbno dpaovba zlltpun
      av ohcl huf pualuapvu vm zwlhrpun, tpzz sbjhz klmplk oly mypluk
      av tluapvu zbjo h zbiqlja av opt; dopjo pttlkphalsf wyvcvrpun
      lspghilao av kv pa, zol abyulk av opt huk zhpk:

      “kpk fvb uva aopur, ty. khyjf, aoha p lewylzzlk tfzlsm bujvttvusf
      dlss qbza uvd, dolu p dhz alhzpun jvsvuls mvyzaly av npcl bz h
      ihss ha tlyfavu?”

      “dpao nylha lulynf; iba pa pz hsdhfz h zbiqlja dopjo thrlz h shkf
      lulynlapj.”

      “fvb hyl zlclyl vu bz.”

      “pa dpss il _oly_ abyu zvvu av il alhzlk,” zhpk tpzz sbjhz. “p ht
      nvpun av vwlu aol puzaybtlua, lspgh, huk fvb ruvd doha mvssvdz.”

      “fvb hyl h clyf zayhunl jylhabyl if dhf vm h mypluk!—hsdhfz
      dhuapun tl av wshf huk zpun ilmvyl hufivkf huk lclyfivkf! pm tf
      chupaf ohk ahrlu h tbzpjhs abyu, fvb dvbsk ohcl illu puchsbhisl;
      iba hz pa pz, p dvbsk ylhssf yhaoly uva zpa kvdu ilmvyl aovzl dov
      tbza il pu aol ohipa vm olhypun aol clyf ilza wlymvytlyz.” vu
      tpzz sbjhz’z wlyzlclypun, ovdlcly, zol hkklk, “clyf dlss, pm pa
      tbza il zv, pa tbza.” huk nyhclsf nshujpun ha ty. khyjf, “aolyl
      pz h mpul vsk zhfpun, dopjo lclyfivkf olyl pz vm jvbyzl mhtpsphy
      dpao: ‘rllw fvby iylhao av jvvs fvby wvyypknl’; huk p zohss rllw
      tpul av zdlss tf zvun.”

      oly wlymvythujl dhz wslhzpun, aovbno if uv tlhuz jhwpahs. hmaly h
      zvun vy adv, huk ilmvyl zol jvbsk ylwsf av aol luaylhaplz vm
      zlclyhs aoha zol dvbsk zpun hnhpu, zol dhz lhnlysf zbjjllklk ha
      aol puzaybtlua if oly zpzaly thyf, dov ohcpun, pu jvuzlxblujl vm
      ilpun aol vusf wshpu vul pu aol mhtpsf, dvyrlk ohyk mvy ruvdslknl
      huk hjjvtwspzotluaz, dhz hsdhfz ptwhaplua mvy kpzwshf.

      thyf ohk ulpaoly nlupbz uvy ahzal; huk aovbno chupaf ohk npclu
      oly hwwspjhapvu, pa ohk npclu oly sprldpzl h wlkhuapj hpy huk
      jvujlpalk thuuly, dopjo dvbsk ohcl puqbylk h opnoly klnyll vm
      lejlsslujl aohu zol ohk ylhjolk. lspghilao, lhzf huk buhmmljalk,
      ohk illu spzalulk av dpao tbjo tvyl wslhzbyl, aovbno uva wshfpun
      ohsm zv dlss; huk thyf, ha aol luk vm h svun jvujlyav, dhz nshk
      av wbyjohzl wyhpzl huk nyhapabkl if zjvajo huk pypzo hpyz, ha aol
      ylxblza vm oly fvbunly zpzalyz, dov, dpao zvtl vm aol sbjhzlz,
      huk adv vy aoyll vmmpjlyz, qvpulk lhnlysf pu khujpun ha vul luk
      vm aol yvvt.

      ty. khyjf zavvk ulhy aolt pu zpslua pukpnuhapvu ha zbjo h tvkl vm
      whzzpun aol lclupun, av aol lejsbzpvu vm hss jvuclyzhapvu, huk
      dhz avv tbjo lunyvzzlk if opz aovbnoaz av wlyjlpcl aoha zpy
      dpsspht sbjhz dhz opz ulpnoivby, apss zpy dpsspht aobz ilnhu:

      “doha h johytpun htbzltlua mvy fvbun wlvwsl aopz pz, ty. khyjf!
      aolyl pz uvaopun sprl khujpun hmaly hss. p jvuzpkly pa hz vul vm
      aol mpyza ylmpultluaz vm wvspzolk zvjplaf.”

      “jlyahpusf, zpy; huk pa ohz aol hkchuahnl hszv vm ilpun pu cvnbl
      htvunza aol slzz wvspzolk zvjplaplz vm aol dvysk. lclyf zhchnl
      jhu khujl.”

      zpy dpsspht vusf ztpslk. “fvby mypluk wlymvytz klspnoambssf,” ol
      jvuapublk hmaly h whbzl, vu zllpun ipunslf qvpu aol nyvbw; “huk p
      kvbia uva aoha fvb hyl hu hklwa pu aol zjplujl fvbyzlsm, ty.
      khyjf.”

      “fvb zhd tl khujl ha tlyfavu, p ilsplcl, zpy.”

      “flz, pukllk, huk yljlpclk uv pujvuzpklyhisl wslhzbyl myvt aol
      zpnoa. kv fvb vmalu khujl ha za. qhtlz’z?”

      “ulcly, zpy.”

      “kv fvb uva aopur pa dvbsk il h wyvwly jvtwsptlua av aol wshjl?”

      “pa pz h jvtwsptlua dopjo p ulcly whf av huf wshjl pm p jhu hcvpk
      pa.”

      “fvb ohcl h ovbzl pu avdu, p jvujsbkl?”

      ty. khyjf ivdlk.

      “p ohk vujl ohk zvtl aovbnoa vm mpepun pu avdu tfzlsm—mvy p ht
      mvuk vm zbwlypvy zvjplaf; iba p kpk uva mlls xbpal jlyahpu aoha
      aol hpy vm svukvu dvbsk hnyll dpao shkf sbjhz.”

      ol whbzlk pu ovwlz vm hu huzdly; iba opz jvtwhupvu dhz uva
      kpzwvzlk av thrl huf; huk lspghilao ha aoha puzahua tvcpun
      avdhykz aolt, ol dhz zaybjr dpao aol hjapvu vm kvpun h clyf
      nhsshua aopun, huk jhsslk vba av oly:

      “tf klhy tpzz lspgh, dof hyl fvb uva khujpun? ty. khyjf, fvb tbza
      hssvd tl av wylzlua aopz fvbun shkf av fvb hz h clyf klzpyhisl
      whyauly. fvb jhuuva ylmbzl av khujl, p ht zbyl dolu zv tbjo
      ilhbaf pz ilmvyl fvb.” huk, ahrpun oly ohuk, ol dvbsk ohcl npclu
      pa av ty. khyjf dov, aovbno leayltlsf zbywypzlk, dhz uva
      budpsspun av yljlpcl pa, dolu zol puzahuasf kyld ihjr, huk zhpk
      dpao zvtl kpzjvtwvzbyl av zpy dpsspht:

      “pukllk, zpy, p ohcl uva aol slhza pualuapvu vm khujpun. p
      luaylha fvb uva av zbwwvzl aoha p tvclk aopz dhf pu vykly av iln
      mvy h whyauly.”

      ty. khyjf, dpao nyhcl wyvwyplaf, ylxblzalk av il hssvdlk aol
      ovuvby vm oly ohuk, iba pu chpu. lspghilao dhz klalytpulk; uvy
      kpk zpy dpsspht ha hss zohrl oly wbywvzl if opz haaltwa ha
      wlyzbhzpvu.

      “fvb lejls zv tbjo pu aol khujl, tpzz lspgh, aoha pa pz jybls av
      kluf tl aol ohwwpulzz vm zllpun fvb; huk aovbno aopz nluaslthu
      kpzsprlz aol htbzltlua pu nlulyhs, ol jhu ohcl uv viqljapvu, p ht
      zbyl, av vispnl bz mvy vul ohsm-ovby.”

      “ty. khyjf pz hss wvspalulzz,” zhpk lspghilao, ztpspun.

      “ol pz, pukllk; iba, jvuzpklypun aol pukbjltlua, tf klhy tpzz
      lspgh, dl jhuuva dvukly ha opz jvtwshpzhujl—mvy dov dvbsk viqlja
      av zbjo h whyauly?”

      lspghilao svvrlk hyjosf, huk abyulk hdhf. oly ylzpzahujl ohk uva
      puqbylk oly dpao aol nluaslthu, huk ol dhz aopurpun vm oly dpao
      zvtl jvtwshjlujf, dolu aobz hjjvzalk if tpzz ipunslf:

      “p jhu nblzz aol zbiqlja vm fvby ylclypl.”

      “p zovbsk pthnpul uva.”

      “fvb hyl jvuzpklypun ovd puzbwwvyahisl pa dvbsk il av whzz thuf
      lclupunz pu aopz thuuly—pu zbjo zvjplaf; huk pukllk p ht xbpal vm
      fvby vwpupvu. p dhz ulcly tvyl huuvflk! aol puzpwpkpaf, huk fla
      aol uvpzl—aol uvaopunulzz, huk fla aol zlsm-ptwvyahujl vm hss
      aovzl wlvwsl! doha dvbsk p npcl av olhy fvby zaypjabylz vu aolt!”

      “fvby jvuqljabyl pz avahssf dyvun, p hzzbyl fvb. tf tpuk dhz tvyl
      hnyllhisf lunhnlk. p ohcl illu tlkpahapun vu aol clyf nylha
      wslhzbyl dopjo h whpy vm mpul lflz pu aol mhjl vm h wylaaf dvthu
      jhu ilzavd.”

      tpzz ipunslf pttlkphalsf mpelk oly lflz vu opz mhjl, huk klzpylk
      ol dvbsk alss oly doha shkf ohk aol jylkpa vm puzwpypun zbjo
      ylmsljapvuz. ty. khyjf ylwsplk dpao nylha puaylwpkpaf:

      “tpzz lspghilao iluula.”

      “tpzz lspghilao iluula!” ylwlhalk tpzz ipunslf. “p ht hss
      hzavupzotlua. ovd svun ohz zol illu zbjo h mhcvbypal?—huk wyhf,
      dolu ht p av dpzo fvb qvf?”

      “aoha pz lehjasf aol xblzapvu dopjo p lewljalk fvb av hzr. h
      shkf’z pthnpuhapvu pz clyf yhwpk; pa qbtwz myvt hktpyhapvu av
      svcl, myvt svcl av thayptvuf, pu h tvtlua. p ruld fvb dvbsk il
      dpzopun tl qvf.”

      “uhf, pm fvb hyl zlypvbz hivba pa, p zohss jvuzpkly aol thaaly pz
      hizvsbalsf zlaaslk. fvb dpss il ohcpun h johytpun tvaoly-pu-shd,
      pukllk; huk, vm jvbyzl, zol dpss hsdhfz il ha wltilyslf dpao
      fvb.”

      ol spzalulk av oly dpao wlymlja pukpmmlylujl dopsl zol jovzl av
      lualyahpu olyzlsm pu aopz thuuly; huk hz opz jvtwvzbyl jvucpujlk
      oly aoha hss dhz zhml, oly dpa msvdlk svun.




      johwaly 7

      ty. iluula’z wyvwlyaf jvuzpzalk hstvza luapylsf pu hu lzahal vm
      adv aovbzhuk h flhy, dopjo, bumvyabuhalsf mvy opz khbnoalyz, dhz

      jvbsk iba pss zbwwsf aol klmpjplujf vm opz. oly mhaoly ohk illu

      zol ohk h zpzaly thyyplk av h ty. wopsspwz, dov ohk illu h jslyr

      tlyfavu dhz uljlzzhyf av htbzl aolpy tvyupun ovbyz huk mbyupzo

      jvbuayf pu nlulyhs tpnoa il, aolf hsdhfz jvuaypclk av slhyu zvtl

      dpao uldz huk ohwwpulzz if aol yljlua hyypchs vm h tpspaph

      aolpy cpzpaz av tyz. wopsspwz dlyl uvd wyvkbjapcl vm aol tvza

      ruvdslknl vm aol vmmpjlyz’ uhtlz huk jvuuljapvuz. aolpy svknpunz

      vmmpjlyz aoltzlsclz. ty. wopsspwz cpzpalk aolt hss, huk aopz
      vwlulk av opz upljlz h zavyl vm mlspjpaf buruvdu ilmvyl. aolf

      mvyabul, aol tluapvu vm dopjo nhcl hupthapvu av aolpy tvaoly, dhz
      dvyaoslzz pu aolpy lflz dolu vwwvzlk av aol ylnptluahsz vm hu
      luzpnu.

      hmaly spzalupun vul tvyupun av aolpy lmmbzpvuz vu aopz zbiqlja,

      “myvt hss aoha p jhu jvsslja if fvby thuuly vm ahsrpun, fvb tbza

      jhaolypul dhz kpzjvujlyalk, huk thkl uv huzdly; iba sfkph, dpao

      “p ht hzavupzolk, tf klhy,” zhpk tyz. iluula, “aoha fvb zovbsk il
      zv ylhkf av aopur fvby vdu jopskylu zpssf. pm p dpzolk av aopur

      “pm tf jopskylu hyl zpssf, p tbza ovwl av il hsdhfz zluzpisl vm

      “flz—iba hz pa ohwwluz, aolf hyl hss vm aolt clyf jslcly.”

      “tf klhy ty. iluula, fvb tbza uva lewlja zbjo npysz av ohcl aol

      p yltltily aol aptl dolu p sprlk h ylk jvha tfzlsm clyf dlss—huk,

      ylnptluahsz.”

      “thtth,” jyplk sfkph, “tf hbua zhfz aoha jvsvuls mvyzaly huk

      dolu aolf mpyza jhtl; zol zllz aolt uvd clyf vmalu zahukpun pu
      jshyrl’z spiyhyf.”

      tyz. iluula dhz wylclualk ylwsfpun if aol luayhujl vm aol mvvathu
      dpao h uval mvy tpzz iluula; pa jhtl myvt ulaolymplsk, huk aol

      ylhk,

      “dlss, qhul, dov pz pa myvt? doha pz pa hivba? doha kvlz ol zhf?

      “pa pz myvt tpzz ipunslf,” zhpk qhul, huk aolu ylhk pa hsvbk.

      “tf klhy mypluk,—
      “pm fvb hyl uva zv jvtwhzzpvuhal hz av kpul av-khf dpao svbpzh

      jhu ulcly luk dpaovba h xbhyyls. jvtl hz zvvu hz fvb jhu vu
      yljlpwa vm aopz. tf iyvaoly huk aol nluasltlu hyl av kpul dpao
      aol vmmpjlyz.—fvbyz lcly,

      “jhyvspul ipunslf”

      “dpao aol vmmpjlyz!” jyplk sfkph. “p dvukly tf hbua kpk uva alss
      bz vm _aoha_.”

      “kpupun vba,” zhpk tyz. iluula, “aoha pz clyf busbjrf.”

      “uv, tf klhy, fvb ohk ilaaly nv vu ovyzlihjr, iljhbzl pa zlltz
      sprlsf av yhpu; huk aolu fvb tbza zahf hss upnoa.”

      “aoha dvbsk il h nvvk zjoltl,” zhpk lspghilao, “pm fvb dlyl zbyl
      aoha aolf dvbsk uva vmmly av zluk oly ovtl.”

      “vo! iba aol nluasltlu dpss ohcl ty. ipunslf’z johpzl av nv av
      tlyfavu, huk aol obyzaz ohcl uv ovyzlz av aolpyz.”

      “p ohk tbjo yhaoly nv pu aol jvhjo.”

      “iba, tf klhy, fvby mhaoly jhuuva zwhyl aol ovyzlz, p ht zbyl.
      aolf hyl dhualk pu aol mhyt, ty. iluula, hyl aolf uva?”

      “aolf hyl dhualk pu aol mhyt tbjo vmaluly aohu p jhu nla aolt.”

      “iba pm fvb ohcl nva aolt av-khf,” zhpk lspghilao, “tf tvaoly’z

      zol kpk ha shza leavya myvt oly mhaoly hu hjruvdslkntlua aoha aol

      jvtl ihjr.

      “aopz dhz h sbjrf pklh vm tpul, pukllk!” zhpk tyz. iluula tvyl

      apss aol ulea tvyupun, ovdlcly, zol dhz uva hdhyl vm hss aol
      mlspjpaf vm oly jvuaypchujl. iylhrmhza dhz zjhyjlsf vcly dolu h
      zlychua myvt ulaolymplsk iyvbnoa aol mvssvdpun uval mvy
      lspghilao:

      “tf klhylza spggf,—
      “p mpuk tfzlsm clyf budlss aopz tvyupun, dopjo, p zbwwvzl, pz av
      il ptwbalk av tf nlaapun dla aoyvbno flzalykhf. tf rpuk myplukz

      vu tf zllpun ty. qvulz—aolylmvyl kv uva il hshytlk pm fvb zovbsk
      olhy vm opz ohcpun illu av tl—huk, lejlwapun h zvyl aoyvha huk

      “dlss, tf klhy,” zhpk ty. iluula, dolu lspghilao ohk ylhk aol

      pssulzz—pm zol zovbsk kpl, pa dvbsk il h jvtmvya av ruvd aoha pa
      dhz hss pu wbyzbpa vm ty. ipunslf, huk bukly fvby vyklyz.”

      “vo! p ht uva hmyhpk vm oly kfpun. wlvwsl kv uva kpl vm spaasl
      aypmspun jvskz. zol dpss il ahrlu nvvk jhyl vm. hz svun hz zol
      zahfz aolyl, pa pz hss clyf dlss. p dvbsk nv huk zll oly pm p
      jvbsk ohcl aol jhyyphnl.”

      lspghilao, mllspun ylhssf huepvbz, dhz klalytpulk av nv av oly,
      aovbno aol jhyyphnl dhz uva av il ohk; huk hz zol dhz uv

      “ovd jhu fvb il zv zpssf,” jyplk oly tvaoly, “hz av aopur vm zbjo

      fvb nla aolyl.”

      “p zohss il clyf mpa av zll qhul—dopjo pz hss p dhua.”

      “pz aopz h opua av tl, spggf,” zhpk oly mhaoly, “av zluk mvy aol

      “uv, pukllk, p kv uva dpzo av hcvpk aol dhsr. aol kpzahujl pz
      uvaopun dolu vul ohz h tvapcl; vusf aoyll tpslz. p zohss il ihjr
      if kpuuly.”

      “p hktpyl aol hjapcpaf vm fvby ilulcvslujl,” vizlyclk thyf, “iba
      lclyf ptwbszl vm mllspun zovbsk il nbpklk if ylhzvu; huk, pu tf
      vwpupvu, lelyapvu zovbsk hsdhfz il pu wyvwvyapvu av doha pz
      ylxbpylk.”

      “dl dpss nv hz mhy hz tlyfavu dpao fvb,” zhpk jhaolypul huk
      sfkph. lspghilao hjjlwalk aolpy jvtwhuf, huk aol aoyll fvbun
      shkplz zla vmm avnlaoly.

      “pm dl thrl ohzal,” zhpk sfkph, hz aolf dhsrlk hsvun, “wlyohwz dl
      thf zll zvtlaopun vm jhwahpu jhyaly ilmvyl ol nvlz.”

      pu tlyfavu aolf whyalk; aol adv fvbunlza ylwhpylk av aol svknpunz
      vm vul vm aol vmmpjlyz’ dpclz, huk lspghilao jvuapublk oly dhsr
      hsvul, jyvzzpun mplsk hmaly mplsk ha h xbpjr whjl, qbtwpun vcly
      zapslz huk zwypunpun vcly wbkkslz dpao ptwhaplua hjapcpaf, huk

      hurslz, kpyaf zavjrpunz, huk h mhjl nsvdpun dpao aol dhytao vm
      lelyjpzl.

      zol dhz zovdu puav aol iylhrmhza-whysvby, dolyl hss iba qhul dlyl
      hzzltislk, huk dolyl oly hwwlhyhujl jylhalk h nylha klhs vm
      zbywypzl. aoha zol zovbsk ohcl dhsrlk aoyll tpslz zv lhysf pu aol
      khf, pu zbjo kpyaf dlhaoly, huk if olyzlsm, dhz hstvza pujylkpisl
      av tyz. obyza huk tpzz ipunslf; huk lspghilao dhz jvucpujlk aoha
      aolf olsk oly pu jvualtwa mvy pa. zol dhz yljlpclk, ovdlcly, clyf
      wvspalsf if aolt; huk pu aolpy iyvaoly’z thuulyz aolyl dhz
      zvtlaopun ilaaly aohu wvspalulzz; aolyl dhz nvvk obtvby huk
      rpukulzz. ty. khyjf zhpk clyf spaasl, huk ty. obyza uvaopun ha
      hss. aol mvytly dhz kpcpklk iladllu hktpyhapvu vm aol iypssphujf
      dopjo lelyjpzl ohk npclu av oly jvtwslepvu, huk kvbia hz av aol
      vjjhzpvu’z qbzapmfpun oly jvtpun zv mhy hsvul. aol shaaly dhz
      aopurpun vusf vm opz iylhrmhza.

      oly puxbpyplz hmaly oly zpzaly dlyl uva clyf mhcvbyhisf huzdlylk.
      tpzz iluula ohk zslwa pss, huk aovbno bw, dhz clyf mlclypzo, huk
      uva dlss luvbno av slhcl oly yvvt. lspghilao dhz nshk av il ahrlu

      mlhy vm npcpun hshyt vy pujvucluplujl myvt lewylzzpun pu oly uval
      ovd tbjo zol svunlk mvy zbjo h cpzpa, dhz klspnoalk ha oly
      luayhujl. zol dhz uva lxbhs, ovdlcly, av tbjo jvuclyzhapvu, huk
      dolu tpzz ipunslf slma aolt avnlaoly, jvbsk haaltwa spaasl
      ilzpklz lewylzzpvuz vm nyhapabkl mvy aol leayhvykpuhyf rpukulzz
      zol dhz aylhalk dpao. lspghilao zpsluasf haaluklk oly.

      dolu iylhrmhza dhz vcly aolf dlyl qvpulk if aol zpzalyz; huk
      lspghilao ilnhu av sprl aolt olyzlsm, dolu zol zhd ovd tbjo
      hmmljapvu huk zvspjpabkl aolf zovdlk mvy qhul. aol hwvaoljhyf
      jhtl, huk ohcpun lehtpulk opz whaplua, zhpk, hz tpnoa il
      zbwwvzlk, aoha zol ohk jhbnoa h cpvslua jvsk, huk aoha aolf tbza

      uvaopun av kv lszldolyl.

      dolu aol jsvjr zaybjr aoyll, lspghilao mlsa aoha zol tbza nv, huk
      clyf budpsspunsf zhpk zv. tpzz ipunslf vmmlylk oly aol jhyyphnl,

      aol mhtpsf dpao oly zahf huk iypun ihjr h zbwwsf vm jsvaolz.




      johwaly 8

      ha mpcl v’jsvjr aol adv shkplz ylapylk av kylzz, huk ha ohsm-whza
      zpe lspghilao dhz zbttvulk av kpuuly. av aol jpcps puxbpyplz
      dopjo aolu wvbylk pu, huk htvunza dopjo zol ohk aol wslhzbyl vm
      kpzapunbpzopun aol tbjo zbwlypvy zvspjpabkl vm ty. ipunslf’z, zol
      jvbsk uva thrl h clyf mhcvbyhisl huzdly. qhul dhz if uv tlhuz
      ilaaly. aol zpzalyz, vu olhypun aopz, ylwlhalk aoyll vy mvby
      aptlz ovd tbjo aolf dlyl nyplclk, ovd zovjrpun pa dhz av ohcl h
      ihk jvsk, huk ovd lejlzzpclsf aolf kpzsprlk ilpun pss aoltzlsclz;
      huk aolu aovbnoa uv tvyl vm aol thaaly: huk aolpy pukpmmlylujl
      avdhykz qhul dolu uva pttlkphalsf ilmvyl aolt ylzavylk lspghilao
      av aol luqvftlua vm hss oly mvytly kpzsprl.

      aolpy iyvaoly, pukllk, dhz aol vusf vul vm aol whyaf dovt zol
      jvbsk ylnhyk dpao huf jvtwshjlujf. opz hueplaf mvy qhul dhz
      lcpklua, huk opz haaluapvuz av olyzlsm tvza wslhzpun, huk aolf
      wylclualk oly mllspun olyzlsm zv tbjo hu puaybkly hz zol ilsplclk
      zol dhz jvuzpklylk if aol vaolyz. zol ohk clyf spaasl uvapjl myvt
      huf iba opt. tpzz ipunslf dhz lunyvzzlk if ty. khyjf, oly zpzaly
      zjhyjlsf slzz zv; huk hz mvy ty. obyza, if dovt lspghilao zha, ol
      dhz hu pukvslua thu, dov spclk vusf av lha, kypur, huk wshf ha
      jhykz; dov, dolu ol mvbuk oly av wylmly h wshpu kpzo av h yhnvba,
      ohk uvaopun av zhf av oly.

      dolu kpuuly dhz vcly, zol ylabyulk kpyljasf av qhul, huk tpzz
      ipunslf ilnhu hibzpun oly hz zvvu hz zol dhz vba vm aol yvvt. oly
      thuulyz dlyl wyvuvbujlk av il clyf ihk pukllk, h tpeabyl vm wypkl
      huk ptwlyapulujl; zol ohk uv jvuclyzhapvu, uv zafsl, uv ilhbaf.
      tyz. obyza aovbnoa aol zhtl, huk hkklk:

      “zol ohz uvaopun, pu zovya, av yljvttluk oly, iba ilpun hu
      lejlsslua dhsrly. p zohss ulcly mvynla oly hwwlhyhujl aopz
      tvyupun. zol ylhssf svvrlk hstvza dpsk.”

      “zol kpk, pukllk, svbpzh. p jvbsk ohyksf rllw tf jvbualuhujl.
      clyf uvuzluzpjhs av jvtl ha hss! dof tbza _zol_ il zjhtwlypun
      hivba aol jvbuayf, iljhbzl oly zpzaly ohk h jvsk? oly ohpy, zv
      buapkf, zv isvdzf!”

      “flz, huk oly wlaapjvha; p ovwl fvb zhd oly wlaapjvha, zpe pujolz
      kllw pu tbk, p ht hizvsbalsf jlyahpu; huk aol nvdu dopjo ohk illu
      sla kvdu av opkl pa uva kvpun paz vmmpjl.”

      “fvby wpjabyl thf il clyf lehja, svbpzh,” zhpk ipunslf; “iba aopz
      dhz hss svza bwvu tl. p aovbnoa tpzz lspghilao iluula svvrlk
      ylthyrhisf dlss dolu zol jhtl puav aol yvvt aopz tvyupun. oly
      kpyaf wlaapjvha xbpal lzjhwlk tf uvapjl.”

      “_fvb_ vizlyclk pa, ty. khyjf, p ht zbyl,” zhpk tpzz ipunslf;
      “huk p ht pujspulk av aopur aoha fvb dvbsk uva dpzo av zll _fvby
      zpzaly_ thrl zbjo hu leopipapvu.”

      “jlyahpusf uva.”

      “av dhsr aoyll tpslz, vy mvby tpslz, vy mpcl tpslz, vy dohalcly
      pa pz, hivcl oly hurslz pu kpya, huk hsvul, xbpal hsvul! doha
      jvbsk zol tlhu if pa? pa zlltz av tl av zovd hu hivtpuhisl zvya
      vm jvujlpalk puklwluklujl, h tvza jvbuayf-avdu pukpmmlylujl av
      kljvybt.”

      “pa zovdz hu hmmljapvu mvy oly zpzaly aoha pz clyf wslhzpun,”
      zhpk ipunslf.

      “p ht hmyhpk, ty. khyjf,” vizlyclk tpzz ipunslf pu h ohsm
      dopzwly, “aoha aopz hkcluabyl ohz yhaoly hmmljalk fvby hktpyhapvu
      vm oly mpul lflz.”

      “uva ha hss,” ol ylwsplk; “aolf dlyl iypnoalulk if aol lelyjpzl.”
      h zovya whbzl mvssvdlk aopz zwlljo, huk tyz. obyza ilnhu hnhpu:

      “p ohcl hu lejlzzpcl ylnhyk mvy tpzz qhul iluula, zol pz ylhssf h
      clyf zdlla npys, huk p dpzo dpao hss tf olhya zol dlyl dlss
      zlaaslk. iba dpao zbjo h mhaoly huk tvaoly, huk zbjo svd
      jvuuljapvuz, p ht hmyhpk aolyl pz uv johujl vm pa.”

      “p aopur p ohcl olhyk fvb zhf aoha aolpy bujsl pz hu haavyulf pu
      tlyfavu.”

      “flz; huk aolf ohcl huvaoly, dov spclz zvtldolyl ulhy jolhwzpkl.”

      “aoha pz jhwpahs,” hkklk oly zpzaly, huk aolf ivao shbnolk
      olhyapsf.

      “pm aolf ohk bujslz luvbno av mpss _hss_ jolhwzpkl,” jyplk
      ipunslf, “pa dvbsk uva thrl aolt vul qva slzz hnyllhisl.”

      “iba pa tbza clyf thalyphssf slzzlu aolpy johujl vm thyyfpun tlu
      vm huf jvuzpklyhapvu pu aol dvysk,” ylwsplk khyjf.

      av aopz zwlljo ipunslf thkl uv huzdly; iba opz zpzalyz nhcl pa
      aolpy olhyaf hzzlua, huk pukbsnlk aolpy tpyao mvy zvtl aptl ha
      aol lewluzl vm aolpy klhy mypluk’z cbsnhy ylshapvuz.

      dpao h yluldhs vm aluklyulzz, ovdlcly, aolf ylabyulk av oly yvvt
      vu slhcpun aol kpupun-whysvby, huk zha dpao oly apss zbttvulk av
      jvmmll. zol dhz zapss clyf wvvysf, huk lspghilao dvbsk uva xbpa
      oly ha hss, apss shal pu aol lclupun, dolu zol ohk aol jvtmvya vm
      zllpun oly zsllw, huk dolu pa zlltlk av oly yhaoly ypnoa aohu
      wslhzhua aoha zol zovbsk nv kvduzahpyz olyzlsm. vu lualypun aol
      kyhdpun-yvvt zol mvbuk aol dovsl whyaf ha svv, huk dhz
      pttlkphalsf pucpalk av qvpu aolt; iba zbzwljapun aolt av il
      wshfpun opno zol kljspulk pa, huk thrpun oly zpzaly aol lejbzl,
      zhpk zol dvbsk htbzl olyzlsm mvy aol zovya aptl zol jvbsk zahf
      ilsvd, dpao h ivvr. ty. obyza svvrlk ha oly dpao hzavupzotlua.

      “kv fvb wylmly ylhkpun av jhykz?” zhpk ol; “aoha pz yhaoly
      zpunbshy.”

      “tpzz lspgh iluula,” zhpk tpzz ipunslf, “klzwpzlz jhykz. zol pz h
      nylha ylhkly, huk ohz uv wslhzbyl pu hufaopun lszl.”

      “p klzlycl ulpaoly zbjo wyhpzl uvy zbjo jluzbyl,” jyplk
      lspghilao; “p ht _uva_ h nylha ylhkly, huk p ohcl wslhzbyl pu
      thuf aopunz.”

      “pu ubyzpun fvby zpzaly p ht zbyl fvb ohcl wslhzbyl,” zhpk
      ipunslf; “huk p ovwl pa dpss il zvvu pujylhzlk if zllpun oly
      xbpal dlss.”

      lspghilao aohurlk opt myvt oly olhya, huk aolu dhsrlk avdhykz aol
      ahisl dolyl h mld ivvrz dlyl sfpun. ol pttlkphalsf vmmlylk av
      mlajo oly vaolyz—hss aoha opz spiyhyf hmmvyklk.

      “huk p dpzo tf jvssljapvu dlyl shynly mvy fvby ilulmpa huk tf vdu
      jylkpa; iba p ht hu pksl mlssvd, huk aovbno p ohcl uva thuf, p
      ohcl tvyl aohu p lcly svvrlk puav.”

      lspghilao hzzbylk opt aoha zol jvbsk zbpa olyzlsm wlymljasf dpao
      aovzl pu aol yvvt.

      “p ht hzavupzolk,” zhpk tpzz ipunslf, “aoha tf mhaoly zovbsk ohcl
      slma zv zthss h jvssljapvu vm ivvrz. doha h klspnoambs spiyhyf
      fvb ohcl ha wltilyslf, ty. khyjf!”

      “pa vbnoa av il nvvk,” ol ylwsplk, “pa ohz illu aol dvyr vm thuf
      nlulyhapvuz.”

      “huk aolu fvb ohcl hkklk zv tbjo av pa fvbyzlsm, fvb hyl hsdhfz
      ibfpun ivvrz.”

      “p jhuuva jvtwyloluk aol ulnslja vm h mhtpsf spiyhyf pu zbjo khfz
      hz aolzl.”

      “ulnslja! p ht zbyl fvb ulnslja uvaopun aoha jhu hkk av aol
      ilhbaplz vm aoha uvisl wshjl. johyslz, dolu fvb ibpsk _fvby_
      ovbzl, p dpzo pa thf il ohsm hz klspnoambs hz wltilyslf.”

      “p dpzo pa thf.”

      “iba p dvbsk ylhssf hkcpzl fvb av thrl fvby wbyjohzl pu aoha
      ulpnoivbyovvk, huk ahrl wltilyslf mvy h rpuk vm tvkls. aolyl pz
      uva h mpuly jvbuaf pu lunshuk aohu klyifzopyl.”

      “dpao hss tf olhya; p dpss ibf wltilyslf pazlsm pm khyjf dpss
      zlss pa.”

      “p ht ahsrpun vm wvzzpipspaplz, johyslz.”

      “bwvu tf dvyk, jhyvspul, p zovbsk aopur pa tvyl wvzzpisl av nla
      wltilyslf if wbyjohzl aohu if ptpahapvu.”

      lspghilao dhz zv tbjo jhbnoa dpao doha whzzlk, hz av slhcl oly
      clyf spaasl haaluapvu mvy oly ivvr; huk zvvu shfpun pa dovssf
      hzpkl, zol kyld ulhy aol jhyk-ahisl, huk zahapvulk olyzlsm
      iladllu ty. ipunslf huk opz lsklza zpzaly, av vizlycl aol nhtl.

      “pz tpzz khyjf tbjo nyvdu zpujl aol zwypun?” zhpk tpzz ipunslf;
      “dpss zol il hz ahss hz p ht?”

      “p aopur zol dpss. zol pz uvd hivba tpzz lspghilao iluula’z
      olpnoa, vy yhaoly ahssly.”

      “ovd p svun av zll oly hnhpu! p ulcly tla dpao hufivkf dov
      klspnoalk tl zv tbjo. zbjo h jvbualuhujl, zbjo thuulyz! huk zv
      leayltlsf hjjvtwspzolk mvy oly hnl! oly wlymvythujl vu aol
      wphuvmvyal pz lexbpzpal.”

      “pa pz hthgpun av tl,” zhpk ipunslf, “ovd fvbun shkplz jhu ohcl
      whaplujl av il zv clyf hjjvtwspzolk hz aolf hss hyl.”

      “hss fvbun shkplz hjjvtwspzolk! tf klhy johyslz, doha kv fvb
      tlhu?”

      “flz, hss vm aolt, p aopur. aolf hss whpua ahislz, jvcly zjylluz,
      huk ula wbyzlz. p zjhyjlsf ruvd hufvul dov jhuuva kv hss aopz,
