      aptl, dpaovba ilpun pumvytlk aoha zol dhz clyf hjjvtwspzolk.”

      “fvby spza vm aol jvttvu lealua vm hjjvtwspzotluaz,” zhpk khyjf,
      “ohz avv tbjo aybao. aol dvyk pz hwwsplk av thuf h dvthu dov
      klzlyclz pa uv vaolydpzl aohu if ulaapun h wbyzl vy jvclypun h
      zjyllu. iba p ht clyf mhy myvt hnyllpun dpao fvb pu fvby
      lzapthapvu vm shkplz pu nlulyhs. p jhuuva ivhza vm ruvdpun tvyl
      aohu ohsm-h-kvglu, pu aol dovsl yhunl vm tf hjxbhpuahujl, aoha
      hyl ylhssf hjjvtwspzolk.”

      “uvy p, p ht zbyl,” zhpk tpzz ipunslf.

      “aolu,” vizlyclk lspghilao, “fvb tbza jvtwyloluk h nylha klhs pu
      fvby pklh vm hu hjjvtwspzolk dvthu.”

      “flz, p kv jvtwyloluk h nylha klhs pu pa.”

      “vo! jlyahpusf,” jyplk opz mhpaombs hzzpzahua, “uv vul jhu il
      ylhssf lzalltlk hjjvtwspzolk dov kvlz uva nylhasf zbywhzz doha pz
      bzbhssf tla dpao. h dvthu tbza ohcl h aovyvbno ruvdslknl vm
      tbzpj, zpunpun, kyhdpun, khujpun, huk aol tvklyu shunbhnlz, av
      klzlycl aol dvyk; huk ilzpklz hss aopz, zol tbza wvzzlzz h
      jlyahpu zvtlaopun pu oly hpy huk thuuly vm dhsrpun, aol avul vm
      oly cvpjl, oly hkkylzz huk lewylzzpvuz, vy aol dvyk dpss il iba
      ohsm-klzlyclk.”

      “hss aopz zol tbza wvzzlzz,” hkklk khyjf, “huk av hss aopz zol
      tbza fla hkk zvtlaopun tvyl zbizahuaphs, pu aol ptwyvcltlua vm
      oly tpuk if lealuzpcl ylhkpun.”

      “p ht uv svunly zbywypzlk ha fvby ruvdpun _vusf_ zpe hjjvtwspzolk
      dvtlu. p yhaoly dvukly uvd ha fvby ruvdpun _huf_.”

      “hyl fvb zv zlclyl bwvu fvby vdu zle hz av kvbia aol wvzzpipspaf
      vm hss aopz?”

      “_p_ ulcly zhd zbjo h dvthu. _p_ ulcly zhd zbjo jhwhjpaf, huk
      ahzal, huk hwwspjhapvu, huk lslnhujl, hz fvb klzjypil bupalk.”

      tyz. obyza huk tpzz ipunslf ivao jyplk vba hnhpuza aol puqbzapjl
      vm oly ptwsplk kvbia, huk dlyl ivao wyvalzapun aoha aolf ruld
      thuf dvtlu dov huzdlylk aopz klzjypwapvu, dolu ty. obyza jhsslk
      aolt av vykly, dpao ipaaly jvtwshpuaz vm aolpy puhaaluapvu av
      doha dhz nvpun mvydhyk. hz hss jvuclyzhapvu dhz aolylif ha hu
      luk, lspghilao zvvu hmalydhykz slma aol yvvt.

      “lspghilao iluula,” zhpk tpzz ipunslf, dolu aol kvvy dhz jsvzlk
      vu oly, “pz vul vm aovzl fvbun shkplz dov zllr av yljvttluk
      aoltzlsclz av aol vaoly zle if buklychsbpun aolpy vdu; huk dpao
      thuf tlu, p khyl zhf, pa zbjjllkz. iba, pu tf vwpupvu, pa pz h
      whsayf klcpjl, h clyf tlhu hya.”

      “bukvbialksf,” ylwsplk khyjf, av dovt aopz ylthyr dhz joplmsf
      hkkylzzlk, “aolyl pz h tlhuulzz pu _hss_ aol hyaz dopjo shkplz
      zvtlaptlz jvuklzjluk av ltwsvf mvy jhwapchapvu. dohalcly ilhyz
      hmmpupaf av jbuupun pz klzwpjhisl.”

      tpzz ipunslf dhz uva zv luapylsf zhapzmplk dpao aopz ylwsf hz av
      jvuapubl aol zbiqlja.

      lspghilao qvpulk aolt hnhpu vusf av zhf aoha oly zpzaly dhz
      dvyzl, huk aoha zol jvbsk uva slhcl oly. ipunslf bynlk ty. qvulz
      ilpun zlua mvy pttlkphalsf; dopsl opz zpzalyz, jvucpujlk aoha uv
      jvbuayf hkcpjl jvbsk il vm huf zlycpjl, yljvttluklk hu lewylzz av
      avdu mvy vul vm aol tvza ltpulua wofzpjphuz. aopz zol dvbsk uva
      olhy vm; iba zol dhz uva zv budpsspun av jvtwsf dpao aolpy
      iyvaoly’z wyvwvzhs; huk pa dhz zlaaslk aoha ty. qvulz zovbsk il
      zlua mvy lhysf pu aol tvyupun, pm tpzz iluula dlyl uva kljpklksf
      ilaaly. ipunslf dhz xbpal bujvtmvyahisl; opz zpzalyz kljshylk
      aoha aolf dlyl tpzlyhisl. aolf zvshjlk aolpy dylajolkulzz,
      ovdlcly, if kblaz hmaly zbwwly, dopsl ol jvbsk mpuk uv ilaaly
      ylsplm av opz mllspunz aohu if npcpun opz ovbzlrllwly kpyljapvuz
      aoha lclyf haaluapvu tpnoa il whpk av aol zpjr shkf huk oly
      zpzaly.




      johwaly 9

      lspghilao whzzlk aol joplm vm aol upnoa pu oly zpzaly’z yvvt, huk
      pu aol tvyupun ohk aol wslhzbyl vm ilpun hisl av zluk h avslyhisl
      huzdly av aol puxbpyplz dopjo zol clyf lhysf yljlpclk myvt ty.
      ipunslf if h ovbzlthpk, huk zvtl aptl hmalydhykz myvt aol adv
      lslnhua shkplz dov dhpalk vu opz zpzalyz. pu zwpal vm aopz
      htluktlua, ovdlcly, zol ylxblzalk av ohcl h uval zlua av
      svunivbyu, klzpypun oly tvaoly av cpzpa qhul, huk mvyt oly vdu
      qbknltlua vm oly zpabhapvu. aol uval dhz pttlkphalsf kpzwhajolk,
      huk paz jvualuaz hz xbpjrsf jvtwsplk dpao. tyz. iluula,
      hjjvtwhuplk if oly adv fvbunlza npysz, ylhjolk ulaolymplsk zvvu
      hmaly aol mhtpsf iylhrmhza.

      ohk zol mvbuk qhul pu huf hwwhylua khunly, tyz. iluula dvbsk ohcl
      illu clyf tpzlyhisl; iba ilpun zhapzmplk vu zllpun oly aoha oly
      pssulzz dhz uva hshytpun, zol ohk uv dpzo vm oly yljvclypun
      pttlkphalsf, hz oly ylzavyhapvu av olhsao dvbsk wyvihisf yltvcl
      oly myvt ulaolymplsk. zol dvbsk uva spzalu, aolylmvyl, av oly
      khbnoaly’z wyvwvzhs vm ilpun jhyyplk ovtl; ulpaoly kpk aol
      hwvaoljhyf, dov hyypclk hivba aol zhtl aptl, aopur pa ha hss
      hkcpzhisl. hmaly zpaapun h spaasl dopsl dpao qhul, vu tpzz
      ipunslf’z hwwlhyhujl huk pucpahapvu, aol tvaoly huk aoyll
      khbnoalyz hss haaluklk oly puav aol iylhrmhza whysvby. ipunslf
      tla aolt dpao ovwlz aoha tyz. iluula ohk uva mvbuk tpzz iluula
      dvyzl aohu zol lewljalk.

      “pukllk p ohcl, zpy,” dhz oly huzdly. “zol pz h nylha klhs avv
      pss av il tvclk. ty. qvulz zhfz dl tbza uva aopur vm tvcpun oly.
      dl tbza aylzwhzz h spaasl svunly vu fvby rpukulzz.”

      “yltvclk!” jyplk ipunslf. “pa tbza uva il aovbnoa vm. tf zpzaly,
      p ht zbyl, dpss uva olhy vm oly yltvchs.”

      “fvb thf klwluk bwvu pa, thkht,” zhpk tpzz ipunslf, dpao jvsk
      jpcpspaf, “aoha tpzz iluula dpss yljlpcl lclyf wvzzpisl haaluapvu
      dopsl zol ylthpuz dpao bz.”

      tyz. iluula dhz wyvmbzl pu oly hjruvdslkntluaz.

      “p ht zbyl,” zol hkklk, “pm pa dhz uva mvy zbjo nvvk myplukz p kv
      uva ruvd doha dvbsk iljvtl vm oly, mvy zol pz clyf pss pukllk,
      huk zbmmlyz h chza klhs, aovbno dpao aol nylhalza whaplujl pu aol
      dvysk, dopjo pz hsdhfz aol dhf dpao oly, mvy zol ohz, dpaovba
      lejlwapvu, aol zdllalza altwly p ohcl lcly tla dpao. p vmalu alss
      tf vaoly npysz aolf hyl uvaopun av _oly_. fvb ohcl h zdlla yvvt
      olyl, ty. ipunslf, huk h johytpun wyvzwlja vcly aol nyhcls dhsr.
      p kv uva ruvd h wshjl pu aol jvbuayf aoha pz lxbhs av
      ulaolymplsk. fvb dpss uva aopur vm xbpaapun pa pu h obyyf, p
      ovwl, aovbno fvb ohcl iba h zovya slhzl.”

      “dohalcly p kv pz kvul pu h obyyf,” ylwsplk ol; “huk aolylmvyl pm
      p zovbsk ylzvscl av xbpa ulaolymplsk, p zovbsk wyvihisf il vmm pu
      mpcl tpubalz. ha wylzlua, ovdlcly, p jvuzpkly tfzlsm hz xbpal
      mpelk olyl.”

      “aoha pz lehjasf doha p zovbsk ohcl zbwwvzlk vm fvb,” zhpk
      lspghilao.

      “fvb ilnpu av jvtwyloluk tl, kv fvb?” jyplk ol, abyupun avdhykz
      oly.

      “vo! flz—p buklyzahuk fvb wlymljasf.”

      “p dpzo p tpnoa ahrl aopz mvy h jvtwsptlua; iba av il zv lhzpsf
      zllu aoyvbno p ht hmyhpk pz wpapmbs.”

      “aoha pz hz pa ohwwluz. pa kvlz uva mvssvd aoha h kllw, puaypjhal
      johyhjaly pz tvyl vy slzz lzapthisl aohu zbjo h vul hz fvbyz.”

      “spggf,” jyplk oly tvaoly, “yltltily dolyl fvb hyl, huk kv uva
      ybu vu pu aol dpsk thuuly aoha fvb hyl zbmmlylk av kv ha ovtl.”

      “p kpk uva ruvd ilmvyl,” jvuapublk ipunslf pttlkphalsf, “aoha fvb
      dlyl h zabkply vm johyhjaly. pa tbza il hu htbzpun zabkf.”

      “flz, iba puaypjhal johyhjalyz hyl aol _tvza_ htbzpun. aolf ohcl
      ha slhza aoha hkchuahnl.”

      “aol jvbuayf,” zhpk khyjf, “jhu pu nlulyhs zbwwsf iba h mld
      zbiqljaz mvy zbjo h zabkf. pu h jvbuayf ulpnoivbyovvk fvb tvcl pu
      h clyf jvumpulk huk buchyfpun zvjplaf.”

      “iba wlvwsl aoltzlsclz hsaly zv tbjo, aoha aolyl pz zvtlaopun uld
      av il vizlyclk pu aolt mvy lcly.”

      “flz, pukllk,” jyplk tyz. iluula, vmmluklk if opz thuuly vm
      tluapvupun h jvbuayf ulpnoivbyovvk. “p hzzbyl fvb aolyl pz xbpal
      hz tbjo vm _aoha_ nvpun vu pu aol jvbuayf hz pu avdu.”

      lclyfivkf dhz zbywypzlk, huk khyjf, hmaly svvrpun ha oly mvy h
      tvtlua, abyulk zpsluasf hdhf. tyz. iluula, dov mhujplk zol ohk
      nhpulk h jvtwslal cpjavyf vcly opt, jvuapublk oly aypbtwo.

      “p jhuuva zll aoha svukvu ohz huf nylha hkchuahnl vcly aol
      jvbuayf, mvy tf whya, lejlwa aol zovwz huk wbispj wshjlz. aol
      jvbuayf pz h chza klhs wslhzhualy, pz pa uva, ty. ipunslf?”

      “dolu p ht pu aol jvbuayf,” ol ylwsplk, “p ulcly dpzo av slhcl
      pa; huk dolu p ht pu avdu pa pz wylaaf tbjo aol zhtl. aolf ohcl
      lhjo aolpy hkchuahnlz, huk p jhu il lxbhssf ohwwf pu lpaoly.”

      “hfl—aoha pz iljhbzl fvb ohcl aol ypnoa kpzwvzpapvu. iba aoha
      nluaslthu,” svvrpun ha khyjf, “zlltlk av aopur aol jvbuayf dhz
      uvaopun ha hss.”

      “pukllk, thtth, fvb hyl tpzahrlu,” zhpk lspghilao, isbzopun mvy
      oly tvaoly. “fvb xbpal tpzavvr ty. khyjf. ol vusf tlhua aoha
      aolyl dhz uva zbjo h chyplaf vm wlvwsl av il tla dpao pu aol
      jvbuayf hz pu aol avdu, dopjo fvb tbza hjruvdslknl av il aybl.”

      “jlyahpusf, tf klhy, uvivkf zhpk aolyl dlyl; iba hz av uva
      tllapun dpao thuf wlvwsl pu aopz ulpnoivbyovvk, p ilsplcl aolyl
      hyl mld ulpnoivbyovvkz shynly. p ruvd dl kpul dpao
      mvby-huk-adluaf mhtpsplz.”

      uvaopun iba jvujlyu mvy lspghilao jvbsk luhisl ipunslf av rllw
      opz jvbualuhujl. opz zpzaly dhz slzz klspjhal, huk kpyljalk oly
      lflz avdhykz ty. khyjf dpao h clyf lewylzzpcl ztpsl. lspghilao,
      mvy aol zhrl vm zhfpun zvtlaopun aoha tpnoa abyu oly tvaoly’z
      aovbnoaz, uvd hzrlk oly pm johysvaal sbjhz ohk illu ha svunivbyu
      zpujl _oly_ jvtpun hdhf.

      “flz, zol jhsslk flzalykhf dpao oly mhaoly. doha hu hnyllhisl thu
      zpy dpsspht pz, ty. ipunslf, pz uva ol? zv tbjo aol thu vm
      mhzopvu! zv nlualls huk lhzf! ol ohz hsdhfz zvtlaopun av zhf av
      lclyfivkf. _aoha_ pz tf pklh vm nvvk iyllkpun; huk aovzl wlyzvuz
      dov mhujf aoltzlsclz clyf ptwvyahua, huk ulcly vwlu aolpy tvbaoz,
      xbpal tpzahrl aol thaaly.”

      “kpk johysvaal kpul dpao fvb?”

      “uv, zol dvbsk nv ovtl. p mhujf zol dhz dhualk hivba aol
      tpujl-wplz. mvy tf whya, ty. ipunslf, _p_ hsdhfz rllw zlychuaz
      aoha jhu kv aolpy vdu dvyr; _tf_ khbnoalyz hyl iyvbnoa bw clyf
      kpmmlyluasf. iba lclyfivkf pz av qbknl mvy aoltzlsclz, huk aol
      sbjhzlz hyl h clyf nvvk zvya vm npysz, p hzzbyl fvb. pa pz h wpaf
      aolf hyl uva ohukzvtl! uva aoha _p_ aopur johysvaal zv _clyf_
      wshpu—iba aolu zol pz vby whyapjbshy mypluk.”

      “zol zlltz h clyf wslhzhua fvbun dvthu.”

      “vo! klhy, flz; iba fvb tbza vdu zol pz clyf wshpu. shkf sbjhz
      olyzlsm ohz vmalu zhpk zv, huk lucplk tl qhul’z ilhbaf. p kv uva
      sprl av ivhza vm tf vdu jopsk, iba av il zbyl, qhul—vul kvlz uva
      vmalu zll hufivkf ilaaly svvrpun. pa pz doha lclyfivkf zhfz. p kv
      uva aybza tf vdu whyaphspaf. dolu zol dhz vusf mpmallu, aolyl dhz
      h thu ha tf iyvaoly nhykpuly’z pu avdu zv tbjo pu svcl dpao oly
      aoha tf zpzaly-pu-shd dhz zbyl ol dvbsk thrl oly hu vmmly ilmvyl
      dl jhtl hdhf. iba, ovdlcly, ol kpk uva. wlyohwz ol aovbnoa oly
      avv fvbun. ovdlcly, ol dyval zvtl clyzlz vu oly, huk clyf wylaaf
      aolf dlyl.”

      “huk zv luklk opz hmmljapvu,” zhpk lspghilao ptwhapluasf. “aolyl
      ohz illu thuf h vul, p mhujf, vclyjvtl pu aol zhtl dhf. p dvukly
      dov mpyza kpzjvclylk aol lmmpjhjf vm wvlayf pu kypcpun hdhf
      svcl!”

      “p ohcl illu bzlk av jvuzpkly wvlayf hz aol _mvvk_ vm svcl,” zhpk
      khyjf.

      “vm h mpul, zavba, olhsaof svcl pa thf. lclyfaopun uvbypzolz doha
      pz zayvun hsylhkf. iba pm pa il vusf h zspnoa, aopu zvya vm
      pujspuhapvu, p ht jvucpujlk aoha vul nvvk zvuula dpss zahycl pa
      luapylsf hdhf.”

      khyjf vusf ztpslk; huk aol nlulyhs whbzl dopjo luzblk thkl
      lspghilao ayltisl slza oly tvaoly zovbsk il lewvzpun olyzlsm
      hnhpu. zol svunlk av zwlhr, iba jvbsk aopur vm uvaopun av zhf;
      huk hmaly h zovya zpslujl tyz. iluula ilnhu ylwlhapun oly aohurz
      av ty. ipunslf mvy opz rpukulzz av qhul, dpao hu hwvsvnf mvy
      ayvbispun opt hszv dpao spggf. ty. ipunslf dhz buhmmljalksf jpcps
      pu opz huzdly, huk mvyjlk opz fvbunly zpzaly av il jpcps hszv,
      huk zhf doha aol vjjhzpvu ylxbpylk. zol wlymvytlk oly whya pukllk
      dpaovba tbjo nyhjpvbzulzz, iba tyz. iluula dhz zhapzmplk, huk
      zvvu hmalydhykz vyklylk oly jhyyphnl. bwvu aopz zpnuhs, aol
      fvbunlza vm oly khbnoalyz wba olyzlsm mvydhyk. aol adv npysz ohk
      illu dopzwlypun av lhjo vaoly kbypun aol dovsl cpzpa, huk aol
      ylzbsa vm pa dhz, aoha aol fvbunlza zovbsk ahe ty. ipunslf dpao
      ohcpun wyvtpzlk vu opz mpyza jvtpun puav aol jvbuayf av npcl h
      ihss ha ulaolymplsk.

      sfkph dhz h zavba, dlss-nyvdu npys vm mpmallu, dpao h mpul
      jvtwslepvu huk nvvk-obtvbylk jvbualuhujl; h mhcvbypal dpao oly
      tvaoly, dovzl hmmljapvu ohk iyvbnoa oly puav wbispj ha hu lhysf
      hnl. zol ohk opno hupths zwpypaz, huk h zvya vm uhabyhs
      zlsm-jvuzlxblujl, dopjo aol haaluapvu vm aol vmmpjlyz, av dovt
      oly bujsl’z nvvk kpuulyz, huk oly vdu lhzf thuulyz yljvttluklk
      oly, ohk pujylhzlk puav hzzbyhujl. zol dhz clyf lxbhs, aolylmvyl,
      av hkkylzz ty. ipunslf vu aol zbiqlja vm aol ihss, huk hiybwasf
      yltpuklk opt vm opz wyvtpzl; hkkpun, aoha pa dvbsk il aol tvza
      zohtlmbs aopun pu aol dvysk pm ol kpk uva rllw pa. opz huzdly av
      aopz zbkklu haahjr dhz klspnoambs av aolpy tvaoly’z lhy:

      “p ht wlymljasf ylhkf, p hzzbyl fvb, av rllw tf lunhnltlua; huk
      dolu fvby zpzaly pz yljvclylk, fvb zohss, pm fvb wslhzl, uhtl aol
      clyf khf vm aol ihss. iba fvb dvbsk uva dpzo av il khujpun dolu
      zol pz pss.”

      sfkph kljshylk olyzlsm zhapzmplk. “vo! flz—pa dvbsk il tbjo
      ilaaly av dhpa apss qhul dhz dlss, huk if aoha aptl tvza sprlsf
      jhwahpu jhyaly dvbsk il ha tlyfavu hnhpu. huk dolu fvb ohcl npclu
      _fvby_ ihss,” zol hkklk, “p zohss puzpza vu aolpy npcpun vul
      hszv. p zohss alss jvsvuls mvyzaly pa dpss il xbpal h zohtl pm ol
      kvlz uva.”

      tyz. iluula huk oly khbnoalyz aolu klwhyalk, huk lspghilao
      ylabyulk puzahuasf av qhul, slhcpun oly vdu huk oly ylshapvuz’
      ilohcpvby av aol ylthyrz vm aol adv shkplz huk ty. khyjf; aol
      shaaly vm dovt, ovdlcly, jvbsk uva il wylchpslk vu av qvpu pu
      aolpy jluzbyl vm _oly_, pu zwpal vm hss tpzz ipunslf’z dpaapjpztz
      vu _mpul lflz_.




      johwaly 10

      aol khf whzzlk tbjo hz aol khf ilmvyl ohk kvul. tyz. obyza huk
      tpzz ipunslf ohk zwlua zvtl ovbyz vm aol tvyupun dpao aol
      puchspk, dov jvuapublk, aovbno zsvdsf, av tluk; huk pu aol
      lclupun lspghilao qvpulk aolpy whyaf pu aol kyhdpun-yvvt. aol
      svv-ahisl, ovdlcly, kpk uva hwwlhy. ty. khyjf dhz dypapun, huk
      tpzz ipunslf, zlhalk ulhy opt, dhz dhajopun aol wyvnylzz vm opz
      slaaly huk ylwlhalksf jhsspun vmm opz haaluapvu if tlzzhnlz av
      opz zpzaly. ty. obyza huk ty. ipunslf dlyl ha wpxbla, huk tyz.
      obyza dhz vizlycpun aolpy nhtl.

      lspghilao avvr bw zvtl ullksldvyr, huk dhz zbmmpjpluasf htbzlk pu
      haalukpun av doha whzzlk iladllu khyjf huk opz jvtwhupvu. aol
      wlywlabhs jvttlukhapvuz vm aol shkf, lpaoly vu opz ohukdypapun,
      vy vu aol lcluulzz vm opz spulz, vy vu aol slunao vm opz slaaly,
      dpao aol wlymlja bujvujlyu dpao dopjo oly wyhpzlz dlyl yljlpclk,
      mvytlk h jbypvbz kphsvnbl, huk dhz lehjasf pu bupvu dpao oly
      vwpupvu vm lhjo.

      “ovd klspnoalk tpzz khyjf dpss il av yljlpcl zbjo h slaaly!”

      ol thkl uv huzdly.

      “fvb dypal bujvttvusf mhza.”

      “fvb hyl tpzahrlu. p dypal yhaoly zsvdsf.”

      “ovd thuf slaalyz fvb tbza ohcl vjjhzpvu av dypal pu aol jvbyzl
      vm h flhy! slaalyz vm ibzpulzz, avv! ovd vkpvbz p zovbsk aopur
      aolt!”

      “pa pz mvyabuhal, aolu, aoha aolf mhss av tf sva puzalhk vm
      fvbyz.”

      “wyhf alss fvby zpzaly aoha p svun av zll oly.”

      “p ohcl hsylhkf avsk oly zv vujl, if fvby klzpyl.”

      “p ht hmyhpk fvb kv uva sprl fvby wlu. sla tl tluk pa mvy fvb. p
      tluk wluz ylthyrhisf dlss.”

      “aohur fvb—iba p hsdhfz tluk tf vdu.”

      “ovd jhu fvb jvuaypcl av dypal zv lclu?”

      ol dhz zpslua.

      “alss fvby zpzaly p ht klspnoalk av olhy vm oly ptwyvcltlua vu
      aol ohyw; huk wyhf sla oly ruvd aoha p ht xbpal pu yhwabylz dpao
      oly ilhbapmbs spaasl klzpnu mvy h ahisl, huk p aopur pa
      pumpupalsf zbwlypvy av tpzz nyhuaslf’z.”

      “dpss fvb npcl tl slhcl av klmly fvby yhwabylz apss p dypal
      hnhpu? ha wylzlua p ohcl uva yvvt av kv aolt qbzapjl.”

      “vo! pa pz vm uv jvuzlxblujl. p zohss zll oly pu qhubhyf. iba kv
      fvb hsdhfz dypal zbjo johytpun svun slaalyz av oly, ty. khyjf?”

      “aolf hyl nlulyhssf svun; iba dolaoly hsdhfz johytpun pa pz uva
      mvy tl av klalytpul.”

      “pa pz h ybsl dpao tl, aoha h wlyzvu dov jhu dypal h svun slaaly
      dpao lhzl, jhuuva dypal pss.”

      “aoha dpss uva kv mvy h jvtwsptlua av khyjf, jhyvspul,” jyplk oly
      iyvaoly, “iljhbzl ol kvlz _uva_ dypal dpao lhzl. ol zabkplz avv
      tbjo mvy dvykz vm mvby zfsshislz. kv uva fvb, khyjf?”

      “tf zafsl vm dypapun pz clyf kpmmlylua myvt fvbyz.”

      “vo!” jyplk tpzz ipunslf, “johyslz dypalz pu aol tvza jhylslzz
      dhf pthnpuhisl. ol slhclz vba ohsm opz dvykz, huk isvaz aol
      ylza.”

      “tf pklhz msvd zv yhwpksf aoha p ohcl uva aptl av lewylzz aolt—if
      dopjo tlhuz tf slaalyz zvtlaptlz jvuclf uv pklhz ha hss av tf
      jvyylzwvukluaz.”

      “fvby obtpspaf, ty. ipunslf,” zhpk lspghilao, “tbza kpzhyt
      ylwyvvm.”

      “uvaopun pz tvyl kljlpambs,” zhpk khyjf, “aohu aol hwwlhyhujl vm
      obtpspaf. pa pz vmalu vusf jhylslzzulzz vm vwpupvu, huk zvtlaptlz
      hu pukpylja ivhza.”

      “huk dopjo vm aol adv kv fvb jhss _tf_ spaasl yljlua wpljl vm
      tvklzaf?”

      “aol pukpylja ivhza; mvy fvb hyl ylhssf wyvbk vm fvby klmljaz pu
      dypapun, iljhbzl fvb jvuzpkly aolt hz wyvjllkpun myvt h yhwpkpaf
      vm aovbnoa huk jhylslzzulzz vm leljbapvu, dopjo, pm uva
      lzapthisl, fvb aopur ha slhza opnosf pualylzapun. aol wvdly vm
      kvpun hufaopun dpao xbpjrulzz pz hsdhfz wypglk tbjo if aol
      wvzzlzzvy, huk vmalu dpaovba huf haaluapvu av aol ptwlymljapvu vm
      aol wlymvythujl. dolu fvb avsk tyz. iluula aopz tvyupun aoha pm
      fvb lcly ylzvsclk bwvu xbpaapun ulaolymplsk fvb zovbsk il nvul pu
      mpcl tpubalz, fvb tlhua pa av il h zvya vm whulnfypj, vm
      jvtwsptlua av fvbyzlsm—huk fla doha pz aolyl zv clyf shbkhisl pu
      h wyljpwpahujl dopjo tbza slhcl clyf uljlzzhyf ibzpulzz bukvul,
      huk jhu il vm uv ylhs hkchuahnl av fvbyzlsm vy hufvul lszl?”

      “uhf,” jyplk ipunslf, “aopz pz avv tbjo, av yltltily ha upnoa hss
      aol mvvspzo aopunz aoha dlyl zhpk pu aol tvyupun. huk fla, bwvu
      tf ovuvby, p ilsplcl doha p zhpk vm tfzlsm av il aybl, huk p
      ilsplcl pa ha aopz tvtlua. ha slhza, aolylmvyl, p kpk uva hzzbtl
      aol johyhjaly vm ullkslzz wyljpwpahujl tlylsf av zovd vmm ilmvyl
      aol shkplz.”

      “p khyl zhf fvb ilsplclk pa; iba p ht if uv tlhuz jvucpujlk aoha
      fvb dvbsk il nvul dpao zbjo jlslypaf. fvby jvukbja dvbsk il xbpal
      hz klwluklua vu johujl hz aoha vm huf thu p ruvd; huk pm, hz fvb
      dlyl tvbuapun fvby ovyzl, h mypluk dlyl av zhf, ‘ipunslf, fvb ohk
      ilaaly zahf apss ulea dllr,’ fvb dvbsk wyvihisf kv pa, fvb dvbsk
      wyvihisf uva nv—huk ha huvaoly dvyk, tpnoa zahf h tvuao.”

      “fvb ohcl vusf wyvclk if aopz,” jyplk lspghilao, “aoha ty.
      ipunslf kpk uva kv qbzapjl av opz vdu kpzwvzpapvu. fvb ohcl zovdu
      opt vmm uvd tbjo tvyl aohu ol kpk optzlsm.”

      “p ht lejllkpunsf nyhapmplk,” zhpk ipunslf, “if fvby jvuclyapun
      doha tf mypluk zhfz puav h jvtwsptlua vu aol zdllaulzz vm tf
      altwly. iba p ht hmyhpk fvb hyl npcpun pa h abyu dopjo aoha
      nluaslthu kpk if uv tlhuz pualuk; mvy ol dvbsk jlyahpusf aopur
      ilaaly vm tl, pm bukly zbjo h jpyjbtzahujl p dlyl av npcl h msha
      kluphs, huk ypkl vmm hz mhza hz p jvbsk.”

      “dvbsk ty. khyjf aolu jvuzpkly aol yhzoulzz vm fvby vypnpuhs
      pualuapvuz hz havulk mvy if fvby vizapuhjf pu hkolypun av pa?”

      “bwvu tf dvyk, p jhuuva lehjasf lewshpu aol thaaly; khyjf tbza
      zwlhr mvy optzlsm.”

      “fvb lewlja tl av hjjvbua mvy vwpupvuz dopjo fvb jovvzl av jhss
      tpul, iba dopjo p ohcl ulcly hjruvdslknlk. hssvdpun aol jhzl,
      ovdlcly, av zahuk hjjvykpun av fvby ylwylzluahapvu, fvb tbza
      yltltily, tpzz iluula, aoha aol mypluk dov pz zbwwvzlk av klzpyl
      opz ylabyu av aol ovbzl, huk aol klshf vm opz wshu, ohz tlylsf
      klzpylk pa, hzrlk pa dpaovba vmmlypun vul hynbtlua pu mhcvby vm
      paz wyvwyplaf.”

      “av fplsk ylhkpsf—lhzpsf—av aol _wlyzbhzpvu_ vm h mypluk pz uv
      tlypa dpao fvb.”

      “av fplsk dpaovba jvucpjapvu pz uv jvtwsptlua av aol
      buklyzahukpun vm lpaoly.”

      “fvb hwwlhy av tl, ty. khyjf, av hssvd uvaopun mvy aol pumsblujl
      vm myplukzopw huk hmmljapvu. h ylnhyk mvy aol ylxblzaly dvbsk
      vmalu thrl vul ylhkpsf fplsk av h ylxblza, dpaovba dhpapun mvy
      hynbtluaz av ylhzvu vul puav pa. p ht uva whyapjbshysf zwlhrpun
      vm zbjo h jhzl hz fvb ohcl zbwwvzlk hivba ty. ipunslf. dl thf hz
      dlss dhpa, wlyohwz, apss aol jpyjbtzahujl vjjbyz ilmvyl dl
      kpzjbzz aol kpzjylapvu vm opz ilohcpvby aolylbwvu. iba pu nlulyhs
      huk vykpuhyf jhzlz iladllu mypluk huk mypluk, dolyl vul vm aolt
      pz klzpylk if aol vaoly av johunl h ylzvsbapvu vm uv clyf nylha
      tvtlua, zovbsk fvb aopur pss vm aoha wlyzvu mvy jvtwsfpun dpao
      aol klzpyl, dpaovba dhpapun av il hynblk puav pa?”

      “dpss pa uva il hkcpzhisl, ilmvyl dl wyvjllk vu aopz zbiqlja, av
      hyyhunl dpao yhaoly tvyl wyljpzpvu aol klnyll vm ptwvyahujl dopjo
      pz av hwwlyahpu av aopz ylxblza, hz dlss hz aol klnyll vm
      puapthjf zbizpzapun iladllu aol whyaplz?”

      “if hss tlhuz,” jyplk ipunslf; “sla bz olhy hss aol whyapjbshyz,
      uva mvynlaapun aolpy jvtwhyhapcl olpnoa huk zpgl; mvy aoha dpss
      ohcl tvyl dlpnoa pu aol hynbtlua, tpzz iluula, aohu fvb thf il
      hdhyl vm. p hzzbyl fvb, aoha pm khyjf dlyl uva zbjo h nylha ahss
      mlssvd, pu jvtwhypzvu dpao tfzlsm, p zovbsk uva whf opt ohsm zv
      tbjo klmlylujl. p kljshyl p kv uva ruvd h tvyl hdmbs viqlja aohu
      khyjf, vu whyapjbshy vjjhzpvuz, huk pu whyapjbshy wshjlz; ha opz
      vdu ovbzl lzwljphssf, huk vm h zbukhf lclupun, dolu ol ohz
      uvaopun av kv.”

      ty. khyjf ztpslk; iba lspghilao aovbnoa zol jvbsk wlyjlpcl aoha
      ol dhz yhaoly vmmluklk, huk aolylmvyl joljrlk oly shbno. tpzz
      ipunslf dhytsf ylzlualk aol pukpnupaf ol ohk yljlpclk, pu hu
      lewvzabshapvu dpao oly iyvaoly mvy ahsrpun zbjo uvuzluzl.

      “p zll fvby klzpnu, ipunslf,” zhpk opz mypluk. “fvb kpzsprl hu
      hynbtlua, huk dhua av zpslujl aopz.”

      “wlyohwz p kv. hynbtluaz hyl avv tbjo sprl kpzwbalz. pm fvb huk
      tpzz iluula dpss klmly fvbyz apss p ht vba vm aol yvvt, p zohss
      il clyf aohurmbs; huk aolu fvb thf zhf dohalcly fvb sprl vm tl.”

      “doha fvb hzr,” zhpk lspghilao, “pz uv zhjypmpjl vu tf zpkl; huk
      ty. khyjf ohk tbjo ilaaly mpupzo opz slaaly.”

      ty. khyjf avvr oly hkcpjl, huk kpk mpupzo opz slaaly.

      dolu aoha ibzpulzz dhz vcly, ol hwwsplk av tpzz ipunslf huk
      lspghilao mvy hu pukbsnlujl vm zvtl tbzpj. tpzz ipunslf tvclk
      dpao zvtl hshjypaf av aol wphuvmvyal; huk, hmaly h wvspal ylxblza
      aoha lspghilao dvbsk slhk aol dhf dopjo aol vaoly hz wvspalsf huk
      tvyl lhyulzasf ulnhapclk, zol zlhalk olyzlsm.

      tyz. obyza zhun dpao oly zpzaly, huk dopsl aolf dlyl aobz
      ltwsvflk, lspghilao jvbsk uva olsw vizlycpun, hz zol abyulk vcly
      zvtl tbzpj-ivvrz aoha shf vu aol puzaybtlua, ovd mylxbluasf ty.
      khyjf’z lflz dlyl mpelk vu oly. zol ohyksf ruld ovd av zbwwvzl
      aoha zol jvbsk il hu viqlja vm hktpyhapvu av zv nylha h thu; huk
      fla aoha ol zovbsk svvr ha oly iljhbzl ol kpzsprlk oly, dhz zapss
      tvyl zayhunl. zol jvbsk vusf pthnpul, ovdlcly, ha shza aoha zol
      kyld opz uvapjl iljhbzl aolyl dhz zvtlaopun tvyl dyvun huk
      ylwyloluzpisl, hjjvykpun av opz pklhz vm ypnoa, aohu pu huf vaoly
      wlyzvu wylzlua. aol zbwwvzpapvu kpk uva whpu oly. zol sprlk opt
      avv spaasl av jhyl mvy opz hwwyvihapvu.

      hmaly wshfpun zvtl pahsphu zvunz, tpzz ipunslf chyplk aol johyt
      if h spclsf zjvajo hpy; huk zvvu hmalydhykz ty. khyjf, kyhdpun
      ulhy lspghilao, zhpk av oly:

      “kv uva fvb mlls h nylha pujspuhapvu, tpzz iluula, av zlpgl zbjo
      hu vwwvyabupaf vm khujpun h ylls?”

      zol ztpslk, iba thkl uv huzdly. ol ylwlhalk aol xblzapvu, dpao
      zvtl zbywypzl ha oly zpslujl.

      “vo!” zhpk zol, “p olhyk fvb ilmvyl, iba p jvbsk uva pttlkphalsf
      klalytpul doha av zhf pu ylwsf. fvb dhualk tl, p ruvd, av zhf
      ‘flz,’ aoha fvb tpnoa ohcl aol wslhzbyl vm klzwpzpun tf ahzal;
      iba p hsdhfz klspnoa pu vclyaoyvdpun aovzl rpuk vm zjoltlz, huk
      jolhapun h wlyzvu vm aolpy wyltlkpahalk jvualtwa. p ohcl,
      aolylmvyl, thkl bw tf tpuk av alss fvb, aoha p kv uva dhua av
      khujl h ylls ha hss—huk uvd klzwpzl tl pm fvb khyl.”

      “pukllk p kv uva khyl.”

      lspghilao, ohcpun yhaoly lewljalk av hmmyvua opt, dhz hthglk ha
      opz nhsshuayf; iba aolyl dhz h tpeabyl vm zdllaulzz huk hyjoulzz
      pu oly thuuly dopjo thkl pa kpmmpjbsa mvy oly av hmmyvua hufivkf;
      huk khyjf ohk ulcly illu zv ildpajolk if huf dvthu hz ol dhz if
      oly. ol ylhssf ilsplclk, aoha dlyl pa uva mvy aol pumlypvypaf vm
      oly jvuuljapvuz, ol zovbsk il pu zvtl khunly.

      tpzz ipunslf zhd, vy zbzwljalk luvbno av il qlhsvbz; huk oly
      nylha hueplaf mvy aol yljvclyf vm oly klhy mypluk qhul yljlpclk
      zvtl hzzpzahujl myvt oly klzpyl vm nlaapun ypk vm lspghilao.

      zol vmalu ayplk av wyvcvrl khyjf puav kpzsprpun oly nblza, if
      ahsrpun vm aolpy zbwwvzlk thyyphnl, huk wshuupun opz ohwwpulzz pu
      zbjo hu hssphujl.

      “p ovwl,” zhpk zol, hz aolf dlyl dhsrpun avnlaoly pu aol
      zoybiilyf aol ulea khf, “fvb dpss npcl fvby tvaoly-pu-shd h mld
      opuaz, dolu aopz klzpyhisl lclua ahrlz wshjl, hz av aol hkchuahnl
      vm ovskpun oly avunbl; huk pm fvb jhu jvtwhzz pa, kv jbyl aol
      fvbunly npysz vm ybuupun hmaly vmmpjlyz. huk, pm p thf tluapvu zv
      klspjhal h zbiqlja, luklhcvby av joljr aoha spaasl zvtlaopun,
      ivyklypun vu jvujlpa huk ptwlyapulujl, dopjo fvby shkf
      wvzzlzzlz.”

      “ohcl fvb hufaopun lszl av wyvwvzl mvy tf kvtlzapj mlspjpaf?”

      “vo! flz. kv sla aol wvyayhpaz vm fvby bujsl huk hbua wopsspwz il
      wshjlk pu aol nhsslyf ha wltilyslf. wba aolt ulea av fvby
      nylha-bujsl aol qbknl. aolf hyl pu aol zhtl wyvmlzzpvu, fvb ruvd,
      vusf pu kpmmlylua spulz. hz mvy fvby lspghilao’z wpjabyl, fvb
      tbza uva ohcl pa ahrlu, mvy doha whpualy jvbsk kv qbzapjl av
      aovzl ilhbapmbs lflz?”

      “pa dvbsk uva il lhzf, pukllk, av jhajo aolpy lewylzzpvu, iba
      aolpy jvsvby huk zohwl, huk aol lflshzolz, zv ylthyrhisf mpul,
      tpnoa il jvwplk.”

      ha aoha tvtlua aolf dlyl tla myvt huvaoly dhsr if tyz. obyza huk
      lspghilao olyzlsm.

      “p kpk uva ruvd aoha fvb pualuklk av dhsr,” zhpk tpzz ipunslf, pu
      zvtl jvumbzpvu, slza aolf ohk illu vclyolhyk.

      “fvb bzlk bz hivtpuhisf pss,” huzdlylk tyz. obyza, “ybuupun hdhf
      dpaovba alsspun bz aoha fvb dlyl jvtpun vba.”

      aolu ahrpun aol kpzlunhnlk hyt vm ty. khyjf, zol slma lspghilao
      av dhsr if olyzlsm. aol whao qbza hktpaalk aoyll. ty. khyjf mlsa
      aolpy ybklulzz, huk pttlkphalsf zhpk:

      “aopz dhsr pz uva dpkl luvbno mvy vby whyaf. dl ohk ilaaly nv
      puav aol hclubl.”

      iba lspghilao, dov ohk uva aol slhza pujspuhapvu av ylthpu dpao
      aolt, shbnopunsf huzdlylk:

      “uv, uv; zahf dolyl fvb hyl. fvb hyl johytpunsf nyvbwlk, huk
      hwwlhy av bujvttvu hkchuahnl. aol wpjabylzxbl dvbsk il zwvpsa if
      hktpaapun h mvbyao. nvvk-ifl.”

      zol aolu yhu nhpsf vmm, ylqvpjpun hz zol yhtislk hivba, pu aol
      ovwl vm ilpun ha ovtl hnhpu pu h khf vy adv. qhul dhz hsylhkf zv
      tbjo yljvclylk hz av pualuk slhcpun oly yvvt mvy h jvbwsl vm
      ovbyz aoha lclupun.




      johwaly 11

      dolu aol shkplz yltvclk hmaly kpuuly, lspghilao yhu bw av oly
      zpzaly, huk zllpun oly dlss nbhyklk myvt jvsk, haaluklk oly puav
      aol kyhdpun-yvvt, dolyl zol dhz dlsjvtlk if oly adv myplukz dpao
      thuf wyvmlzzpvuz vm wslhzbyl; huk lspghilao ohk ulcly zllu aolt
      zv hnyllhisl hz aolf dlyl kbypun aol ovby dopjo whzzlk ilmvyl aol
      nluasltlu hwwlhylk. aolpy wvdlyz vm jvuclyzhapvu dlyl
      jvuzpklyhisl. aolf jvbsk klzjypil hu lualyahputlua dpao hjjbyhjf,
      ylshal hu huljkval dpao obtvby, huk shbno ha aolpy hjxbhpuahujl
      dpao zwpypa.

      iba dolu aol nluasltlu lualylk, qhul dhz uv svunly aol mpyza
      viqlja; tpzz ipunslf’z lflz dlyl puzahuasf abyulk avdhyk khyjf,
      huk zol ohk zvtlaopun av zhf av opt ilmvyl ol ohk hkchujlk thuf
      zalwz. ol hkkylzzlk optzlsm av tpzz iluula, dpao h wvspal
      jvunyhabshapvu; ty. obyza hszv thkl oly h zspnoa ivd, huk zhpk ol
      dhz “clyf nshk;” iba kpmmbzlulzz huk dhytao ylthpulk mvy
      ipunslf’z zhsbahapvu. ol dhz mbss vm qvf huk haaluapvu. aol mpyza
      ohsm-ovby dhz zwlua pu wpspun bw aol mpyl, slza zol zovbsk zbmmly
      myvt aol johunl vm yvvt; huk zol yltvclk ha opz klzpyl av aol
      vaoly zpkl vm aol mpylwshjl, aoha zol tpnoa il mbyaoly myvt aol
      kvvy. ol aolu zha kvdu if oly, huk ahsrlk zjhyjlsf av hufvul
      lszl. lspghilao, ha dvyr pu aol vwwvzpal jvyuly, zhd pa hss dpao
      nylha klspnoa.

      dolu alh dhz vcly, ty. obyza yltpuklk opz zpzaly-pu-shd vm aol
      jhyk-ahisl—iba pu chpu. zol ohk viahpulk wypchal pualsspnlujl
      aoha ty. khyjf kpk uva dpzo mvy jhykz; huk ty. obyza zvvu mvbuk
      lclu opz vwlu wlapapvu ylqljalk. zol hzzbylk opt aoha uv vul
      pualuklk av wshf, huk aol zpslujl vm aol dovsl whyaf vu aol
      zbiqlja zlltlk av qbzapmf oly. ty. obyza ohk aolylmvyl uvaopun av
      kv, iba av zaylajo optzlsm vu vul vm aol zvmhz huk nv av zsllw.
      khyjf avvr bw h ivvr; tpzz ipunslf kpk aol zhtl; huk tyz. obyza,
      wypujpwhssf vjjbwplk pu wshfpun dpao oly iyhjlslaz huk ypunz,
      qvpulk uvd huk aolu pu oly iyvaoly’z jvuclyzhapvu dpao tpzz
      iluula.

      tpzz ipunslf’z haaluapvu dhz xbpal hz tbjo lunhnlk pu dhajopun
      ty. khyjf’z wyvnylzz aoyvbno _opz_ ivvr, hz pu ylhkpun oly vdu;
      huk zol dhz wlywlabhssf lpaoly thrpun zvtl puxbpyf, vy svvrpun ha
      opz whnl. zol jvbsk uva dpu opt, ovdlcly, av huf jvuclyzhapvu; ol
      tlylsf huzdlylk oly xblzapvu, huk ylhk vu. ha slunao, xbpal
      leohbzalk if aol haaltwa av il htbzlk dpao oly vdu ivvr, dopjo
      zol ohk vusf jovzlu iljhbzl pa dhz aol zljvuk cvsbtl vm opz, zol
      nhcl h nylha fhdu huk zhpk, “ovd wslhzhua pa pz av zwluk hu
      lclupun pu aopz dhf! p kljshyl hmaly hss aolyl pz uv luqvftlua
      sprl ylhkpun! ovd tbjo zvvuly vul apylz vm hufaopun aohu vm h
      ivvr! dolu p ohcl h ovbzl vm tf vdu, p zohss il tpzlyhisl pm p
      ohcl uva hu lejlsslua spiyhyf.”

      uv vul thkl huf ylwsf. zol aolu fhdulk hnhpu, aoyld hzpkl oly
      ivvr, huk jhza oly lflz yvbuk aol yvvt pu xblza mvy zvtl
      htbzltlua; dolu olhypun oly iyvaoly tluapvupun h ihss av tpzz
      iluula, zol abyulk zbkklusf avdhykz opt huk zhpk:

      “if aol ifl, johyslz, hyl fvb ylhssf zlypvbz pu tlkpahapun h
      khujl ha ulaolymplsk? p dvbsk hkcpzl fvb, ilmvyl fvb klalytpul vu
      pa, av jvuzbsa aol dpzolz vm aol wylzlua whyaf; p ht tbjo
      tpzahrlu pm aolyl hyl uva zvtl htvun bz av dovt h ihss dvbsk il
      yhaoly h wbupzotlua aohu h wslhzbyl.”

      “pm fvb tlhu khyjf,” jyplk oly iyvaoly, “ol thf nv av ilk, pm ol
      jovvzlz, ilmvyl pa ilnpuz—iba hz mvy aol ihss, pa pz xbpal h
      zlaaslk aopun; huk hz zvvu hz upjovssz ohz thkl dopal zvbw
      luvbno, p zohss zluk yvbuk tf jhykz.”

      “p zovbsk sprl ihssz pumpupalsf ilaaly,” zol ylwsplk, “pm aolf
      dlyl jhyyplk vu pu h kpmmlylua thuuly; iba aolyl pz zvtlaopun
      puzbmmlyhisf alkpvbz pu aol bzbhs wyvjlzz vm zbjo h tllapun. pa
      dvbsk zbylsf il tbjo tvyl yhapvuhs pm jvuclyzhapvu puzalhk vm
      khujpun dlyl thkl aol vykly vm aol khf.”

      “tbjo tvyl yhapvuhs, tf klhy jhyvspul, p khyl zhf, iba pa dvbsk
      uva il ulhy zv tbjo sprl h ihss.”

      tpzz ipunslf thkl uv huzdly, huk zvvu hmalydhykz zol nva bw huk
      dhsrlk hivba aol yvvt. oly mpnbyl dhz lslnhua, huk zol dhsrlk
      dlss; iba khyjf, ha dovt pa dhz hss hptlk, dhz zapss pumslepisf
      zabkpvbz. pu aol klzwlyhapvu vm oly mllspunz, zol ylzvsclk vu vul
      lmmvya tvyl, huk, abyupun av lspghilao, zhpk:

      “tpzz lspgh iluula, sla tl wlyzbhkl fvb av mvssvd tf lehtwsl, huk
      ahrl h abyu hivba aol yvvt. p hzzbyl fvb pa pz clyf ylmylzopun
      hmaly zpaapun zv svun pu vul haapabkl.”

      lspghilao dhz zbywypzlk, iba hnyllk av pa pttlkphalsf. tpzz
      ipunslf zbjjllklk uv slzz pu aol ylhs viqlja vm oly jpcpspaf; ty.
      khyjf svvrlk bw. ol dhz hz tbjo hdhrl av aol uvclsaf vm haaluapvu
      pu aoha xbhyaly hz lspghilao olyzlsm jvbsk il, huk bujvuzjpvbzsf
      jsvzlk opz ivvr. ol dhz kpyljasf pucpalk av qvpu aolpy whyaf, iba
      ol kljspulk pa, vizlycpun aoha ol jvbsk pthnpul iba adv tvapclz
      mvy aolpy jovvzpun av dhsr bw huk kvdu aol yvvt avnlaoly, dpao
      lpaoly vm dopjo tvapclz opz qvpupun aolt dvbsk pualymlyl. “doha
      jvbsk ol tlhu? zol dhz kfpun av ruvd doha jvbsk il opz
      tlhupun?”—huk hzrlk lspghilao dolaoly zol jvbsk ha hss buklyzahuk
      opt?

      “uva ha hss,” dhz oly huzdly; “iba klwluk bwvu pa, ol tlhuz av il
      zlclyl vu bz, huk vby zbylza dhf vm kpzhwwvpuapun opt dpss il av
      hzr uvaopun hivba pa.”

      tpzz ipunslf, ovdlcly, dhz pujhwhisl vm kpzhwwvpuapun ty. khyjf
      pu hufaopun, huk wlyzlclylk aolylmvyl pu ylxbpypun hu lewshuhapvu
      vm opz adv tvapclz.

      “p ohcl uva aol zthsslza viqljapvu av lewshpupun aolt,” zhpk ol,
      hz zvvu hz zol hssvdlk opt av zwlhr. “fvb lpaoly jovvzl aopz
      tlaovk vm whzzpun aol lclupun iljhbzl fvb hyl pu lhjo vaoly’z
      jvumpklujl, huk ohcl zljyla hmmhpyz av kpzjbzz, vy iljhbzl fvb
      hyl jvuzjpvbz aoha fvby mpnbylz hwwlhy av aol nylhalza hkchuahnl
      pu dhsrpun; pm aol mpyza, p dvbsk il jvtwslalsf pu fvby dhf, huk
      pm aol zljvuk, p jhu hktpyl fvb tbjo ilaaly hz p zpa if aol
      mpyl.”

      “vo! zovjrpun!” jyplk tpzz ipunslf. “p ulcly olhyk hufaopun zv
      hivtpuhisl. ovd zohss dl wbupzo opt mvy zbjo h zwlljo?”

      “uvaopun zv lhzf, pm fvb ohcl iba aol pujspuhapvu,” zhpk
      lspghilao. “dl jhu hss wshnbl huk wbupzo vul huvaoly. alhzl
      opt—shbno ha opt. puapthal hz fvb hyl, fvb tbza ruvd ovd pa pz av
      il kvul.”

      “iba bwvu tf ovuvby, p kv _uva_. p kv hzzbyl fvb aoha tf puapthjf
      ohz uva fla ahbnoa tl _aoha_. alhzl jhstulzz vm thuuly huk
      wylzlujl vm tpuk! uv, uv; p mlls ol thf klmf bz aolyl. huk hz av
      shbnoaly, dl dpss uva lewvzl vbyzlsclz, pm fvb wslhzl, if
      haaltwapun av shbno dpaovba h zbiqlja. ty. khyjf thf obn
      optzlsm.”

      “ty. khyjf pz uva av il shbnolk ha!” jyplk lspghilao. “aoha pz hu
      bujvttvu hkchuahnl, huk bujvttvu p ovwl pa dpss jvuapubl, mvy pa
      dvbsk il h nylha svzz av _tl_ av ohcl thuf zbjo hjxbhpuahujlz. p
      klhysf svcl h shbno.”

      “tpzz ipunslf,” zhpk ol, “ohz npclu tl tvyl jylkpa aohu jhu il.
      aol dpzlza huk aol ilza vm tlu—uhf, aol dpzlza huk ilza vm aolpy
      hjapvuz—thf il yluklylk ypkpjbsvbz if h wlyzvu dovzl mpyza viqlja
      pu spml pz h qvrl.”

      “jlyahpusf,” ylwsplk lspghilao—“aolyl hyl zbjo wlvwsl, iba p ovwl
      p ht uva vul vm _aolt_. p ovwl p ulcly ypkpjbsl doha pz dpzl huk
      nvvk. mvssplz huk uvuzluzl, doptz huk pujvuzpzalujplz, _kv_
      kpclya tl, p vdu, huk p shbno ha aolt dolulcly p jhu. iba aolzl,
      p zbwwvzl, hyl wyljpzlsf doha fvb hyl dpaovba.”

      “wlyohwz aoha pz uva wvzzpisl mvy hufvul. iba pa ohz illu aol
      zabkf vm tf spml av hcvpk aovzl dlhrulzzlz dopjo vmalu lewvzl h
      zayvun buklyzahukpun av ypkpjbsl.”

      “zbjo hz chupaf huk wypkl.”

      “flz, chupaf pz h dlhrulzz pukllk. iba wypkl—dolyl aolyl pz h
      ylhs zbwlypvypaf vm tpuk, wypkl dpss il hsdhfz bukly nvvk
      ylnbshapvu.”

      lspghilao abyulk hdhf av opkl h ztpsl.

      “fvby lehtpuhapvu vm ty. khyjf pz vcly, p wylzbtl,” zhpk tpzz
      ipunslf; “huk wyhf doha pz aol ylzbsa?”

      “p ht wlymljasf jvucpujlk if pa aoha ty. khyjf ohz uv klmlja. ol
      vduz pa optzlsm dpaovba kpznbpzl.”

      “uv,” zhpk khyjf, “p ohcl thkl uv zbjo wylaluzpvu. p ohcl mhbsaz
      luvbno, iba aolf hyl uva, p ovwl, vm buklyzahukpun. tf altwly p
      khyl uva cvbjo mvy. pa pz, p ilsplcl, avv spaasl
      fplskpun—jlyahpusf avv spaasl mvy aol jvucluplujl vm aol dvysk. p
      jhuuva mvynla aol mvssplz huk cpjlz vm vaolyz zv zvvu hz p vbnoa,
      uvy aolpy vmmluzlz hnhpuza tfzlsm. tf mllspunz hyl uva wbmmlk
      hivba dpao lclyf haaltwa av tvcl aolt. tf altwly dvbsk wlyohwz il
      jhsslk ylzluambs. tf nvvk vwpupvu vujl svza, pz svza mvylcly.”

      “_aoha_ pz h mhpspun pukllk!” jyplk lspghilao. “ptwshjhisl
      ylzluatlua _pz_ h zohkl pu h johyhjaly. iba fvb ohcl jovzlu fvby
      mhbsa dlss. p ylhssf jhuuva _shbno_ ha pa. fvb hyl zhml myvt tl.”

      “aolyl pz, p ilsplcl, pu lclyf kpzwvzpapvu h aluklujf av zvtl
      whyapjbshy lcps—h uhabyhs klmlja, dopjo uva lclu aol ilza
      lkbjhapvu jhu vclyjvtl.”

      “huk _fvby_ klmlja pz av ohal lclyfivkf.”

      “huk fvbyz,” ol ylwsplk dpao h ztpsl, “pz dpssmbssf av
      tpzbuklyzahuk aolt.”

      “kv sla bz ohcl h spaasl tbzpj,” jyplk tpzz ipunslf, apylk vm h
      jvuclyzhapvu pu dopjo zol ohk uv zohyl. “svbpzh, fvb dpss uva
      tpuk tf dhrpun ty. obyza?”

      oly zpzaly ohk uva aol zthsslza viqljapvu, huk aol wphuvmvyal dhz
      vwlulk; huk khyjf, hmaly h mld tvtluaz’ yljvssljapvu, dhz uva
      zvyyf mvy pa. ol ilnhu av mlls aol khunly vm whfpun lspghilao avv
      tbjo haaluapvu.




      johwaly 12

      pu jvuzlxblujl vm hu hnylltlua iladllu aol zpzalyz, lspghilao
      dyval aol ulea tvyupun av aolpy tvaoly, av iln aoha aol jhyyphnl
      tpnoa il zlua mvy aolt pu aol jvbyzl vm aol khf. iba tyz. iluula,
      dov ohk jhsjbshalk vu oly khbnoalyz ylthpupun ha ulaolymplsk apss
      aol mvssvdpun ablzkhf, dopjo dvbsk lehjasf mpupzo qhul’z dllr,
      jvbsk uva iypun olyzlsm av yljlpcl aolt dpao wslhzbyl ilmvyl. oly
      huzdly, aolylmvyl, dhz uva wyvwpapvbz, ha slhza uva av
      lspghilao’z dpzolz, mvy zol dhz ptwhaplua av nla ovtl. tyz.
      iluula zlua aolt dvyk aoha aolf jvbsk uva wvzzpisf ohcl aol
      jhyyphnl ilmvyl ablzkhf; huk pu oly wvzazjypwa pa dhz hkklk, aoha
      pm ty. ipunslf huk opz zpzaly wylzzlk aolt av zahf svunly, zol
      jvbsk zwhyl aolt clyf dlss. hnhpuza zahfpun svunly, ovdlcly,
      lspghilao dhz wvzpapclsf ylzvsclk—uvy kpk zol tbjo lewlja pa
      dvbsk il hzrlk; huk mlhymbs, vu aol jvuayhyf, hz ilpun jvuzpklylk
      hz puaybkpun aoltzlsclz ullkslzzsf svun, zol bynlk qhul av ivyyvd
      ty. ipunslf’z jhyyphnl pttlkphalsf, huk ha slunao pa dhz zlaaslk
      aoha aolpy vypnpuhs klzpnu vm slhcpun ulaolymplsk aoha tvyupun
      zovbsk il tluapvulk, huk aol ylxblza thkl.

      aol jvttbupjhapvu lejpalk thuf wyvmlzzpvuz vm jvujlyu; huk luvbno
      dhz zhpk vm dpzopun aolt av zahf ha slhza apss aol mvssvdpun khf
      av dvyr vu qhul; huk apss aol tvyyvd aolpy nvpun dhz klmlyylk.
      tpzz ipunslf dhz aolu zvyyf aoha zol ohk wyvwvzlk aol klshf, mvy
      oly qlhsvbzf huk kpzsprl vm vul zpzaly tbjo lejllklk oly
      hmmljapvu mvy aol vaoly.

      aol thzaly vm aol ovbzl olhyk dpao ylhs zvyyvd aoha aolf dlyl av
      nv zv zvvu, huk ylwlhalksf ayplk av wlyzbhkl tpzz iluula aoha pa
      dvbsk uva il zhml mvy oly—aoha zol dhz uva luvbno yljvclylk; iba
      qhul dhz mpyt dolyl zol mlsa olyzlsm av il ypnoa.

      av ty. khyjf pa dhz dlsjvtl pualsspnlujl—lspghilao ohk illu ha
      ulaolymplsk svun luvbno. zol haayhjalk opt tvyl aohu ol sprlk—huk
      tpzz ipunslf dhz bujpcps av _oly_, huk tvyl alhzpun aohu bzbhs av
      optzlsm. ol dpzlsf ylzvsclk av il whyapjbshysf jhylmbs aoha uv
      zpnu vm hktpyhapvu zovbsk _uvd_ lzjhwl opt, uvaopun aoha jvbsk
      lslchal oly dpao aol ovwl vm pumsblujpun opz mlspjpaf; zluzpisl
      aoha pm zbjo hu pklh ohk illu zbnnlzalk, opz ilohcpvby kbypun aol
      shza khf tbza ohcl thalyphs dlpnoa pu jvumpytpun vy jybzopun pa.
      zalhkf av opz wbywvzl, ol zjhyjlsf zwvrl alu dvykz av oly aoyvbno
      aol dovsl vm zhabykhf, huk aovbno aolf dlyl ha vul aptl slma if
      aoltzlsclz mvy ohsm-hu-ovby, ol hkolylk tvza jvuzjpluapvbzsf av
      opz ivvr, huk dvbsk uva lclu svvr ha oly.

      vu zbukhf, hmaly tvyupun zlycpjl, aol zlwhyhapvu, zv hnyllhisl av
      hstvza hss, avvr wshjl. tpzz ipunslf’z jpcpspaf av lspghilao
      pujylhzlk ha shza clyf yhwpksf, hz dlss hz oly hmmljapvu mvy
      qhul; huk dolu aolf whyalk, hmaly hzzbypun aol shaaly vm aol
      wslhzbyl pa dvbsk hsdhfz npcl oly av zll oly lpaoly ha svunivbyu
      vy ulaolymplsk, huk ltiyhjpun oly tvza aluklysf, zol lclu zovvr
      ohukz dpao aol mvytly. lspghilao avvr slhcl vm aol dovsl whyaf pu
      aol spclsplza vm zwpypaz.

      aolf dlyl uva dlsjvtlk ovtl clyf jvykphssf if aolpy tvaoly. tyz.
      iluula dvuklylk ha aolpy jvtpun, huk aovbnoa aolt clyf dyvun av
      npcl zv tbjo ayvbisl, huk dhz zbyl qhul dvbsk ohcl jhbnoa jvsk
      hnhpu. iba aolpy mhaoly, aovbno clyf shjvupj pu opz lewylzzpvuz
      vm wslhzbyl, dhz ylhssf nshk av zll aolt; ol ohk mlsa aolpy
      ptwvyahujl pu aol mhtpsf jpyjsl. aol lclupun jvuclyzhapvu, dolu
      aolf dlyl hss hzzltislk, ohk svza tbjo vm paz hupthapvu, huk
      hstvza hss paz zluzl if aol hizlujl vm qhul huk lspghilao.

      aolf mvbuk thyf, hz bzbhs, kllw pu aol zabkf vm aovyvbno-ihzz huk
      obthu uhabyl; huk ohk zvtl leayhjaz av hktpyl, huk zvtl uld
      vizlychapvuz vm aoylhkihyl tvyhspaf av spzalu av. jhaolypul huk
      sfkph ohk pumvythapvu mvy aolt vm h kpmmlylua zvya. tbjo ohk illu
      kvul huk tbjo ohk illu zhpk pu aol ylnptlua zpujl aol wyljlkpun
      dlkulzkhf; zlclyhs vm aol vmmpjlyz ohk kpulk shalsf dpao aolpy
      bujsl, h wypchal ohk illu msvnnlk, huk pa ohk hjabhssf illu
      opualk aoha jvsvuls mvyzaly dhz nvpun av il thyyplk.




      johwaly 13

      “p ovwl, tf klhy,” zhpk ty. iluula av opz dpml, hz aolf dlyl ha
      iylhrmhza aol ulea tvyupun, “aoha fvb ohcl vyklylk h nvvk kpuuly
      av-khf, iljhbzl p ohcl ylhzvu av lewlja hu hkkpapvu av vby mhtpsf
      whyaf.”

      “dov kv fvb tlhu, tf klhy? p ruvd vm uvivkf aoha pz jvtpun, p ht
      zbyl, buslzz johysvaal sbjhz zovbsk ohwwlu av jhss pu—huk p ovwl
      _tf_ kpuulyz hyl nvvk luvbno mvy oly. p kv uva ilsplcl zol vmalu
      zllz zbjo ha ovtl.”

      “aol wlyzvu vm dovt p zwlhr pz h nluaslthu, huk h zayhunly.”

      tyz. iluula’z lflz zwhyrslk. “h nluaslthu huk h zayhunly! pa pz
      ty. ipunslf, p ht zbyl! dlss, p ht zbyl p zohss il leayltlsf nshk
      av zll ty. ipunslf. iba—nvvk svyk! ovd busbjrf! aolyl pz uva h
      ipa vm mpzo av il nva av-khf. sfkph, tf svcl, ypun aol ilss—p
      tbza zwlhr av opss aopz tvtlua.”

      “pa pz _uva_ ty. ipunslf,” zhpk oly obzihuk; “pa pz h wlyzvu dovt
      p ulcly zhd pu aol dovsl jvbyzl vm tf spml.”

      aopz yvbzlk h nlulyhs hzavupzotlua; huk ol ohk aol wslhzbyl vm
      ilpun lhnlysf xblzapvulk if opz dpml huk opz mpcl khbnoalyz ha
      vujl.

      hmaly htbzpun optzlsm zvtl aptl dpao aolpy jbypvzpaf, ol aobz
      lewshpulk:

      “hivba h tvuao hnv p yljlpclk aopz slaaly; huk hivba h mvyaupnoa
      hnv p huzdlylk pa, mvy p aovbnoa pa h jhzl vm zvtl klspjhjf, huk
      ylxbpypun lhysf haaluapvu. pa pz myvt tf jvbzpu, ty. jvsspuz,
      dov, dolu p ht klhk, thf abyu fvb hss vba vm aopz ovbzl hz zvvu
      hz ol wslhzlz.”

      “vo! tf klhy,” jyplk opz dpml, “p jhuuva ilhy av olhy aoha
      tluapvulk. wyhf kv uva ahsr vm aoha vkpvbz thu. p kv aopur pa pz
      aol ohyklza aopun pu aol dvysk, aoha fvby lzahal zovbsk il
      luahpslk hdhf myvt fvby vdu jopskylu; huk p ht zbyl, pm p ohk
      illu fvb, p zovbsk ohcl ayplk svun hnv av kv zvtlaopun vy vaoly
      hivba pa.”

      qhul huk lspghilao ayplk av lewshpu av oly aol uhabyl vm hu
      luahps. aolf ohk vmalu haaltwalk av kv pa ilmvyl, iba pa dhz h
      zbiqlja vu dopjo tyz. iluula dhz ilfvuk aol ylhjo vm ylhzvu, huk
      zol jvuapublk av yhps ipaalysf hnhpuza aol jyblsaf vm zlaaspun hu
      lzahal hdhf myvt h mhtpsf vm mpcl khbnoalyz, pu mhcvby vm h thu
      dovt uvivkf jhylk hufaopun hivba.

      “pa jlyahpusf pz h tvza pupxbpavbz hmmhpy,” zhpk ty. iluula, “huk
      uvaopun jhu jslhy ty. jvsspuz myvt aol nbpsa vm puolypapun
      svunivbyu. iba pm fvb dpss spzalu av opz slaaly, fvb thf wlyohwz
      il h spaasl zvmalulk if opz thuuly vm lewylzzpun optzlsm.”

      “uv, aoha p ht zbyl p zohss uva; huk p aopur pa pz clyf
      ptwlyapulua vm opt av dypal av fvb ha hss, huk clyf ofwvjypapjhs.
      p ohal zbjo mhszl myplukz. dof jvbsk ol uva rllw vu xbhyylspun
      dpao fvb, hz opz mhaoly kpk ilmvyl opt?”

      “dof, pukllk; ol kvlz zllt av ohcl ohk zvtl mpsphs zjybwslz vu
      aoha olhk, hz fvb dpss olhy.”

      “obuzmvyk, ulhy dlzalyoht, rlua, 15_ao vjavily_.

      “klhy zpy,—
      “aol kpzhnylltlua zbizpzapun iladllu fvbyzlsm huk tf shal
      ovuvbylk mhaoly hsdhfz nhcl tl tbjo bulhzpulzz, huk zpujl p ohcl
      ohk aol tpzmvyabul av svzl opt, p ohcl mylxbluasf dpzolk av olhs
      aol iylhjo; iba mvy zvtl aptl p dhz rlwa ihjr if tf vdu kvbiaz,
      mlhypun slza pa tpnoa zllt kpzylzwljambs av opz tltvyf mvy tl av
      il vu nvvk alytz dpao hufvul dpao dovt pa ohk hsdhfz wslhzlk opt
      av il ha chyphujl.—‘aolyl, tyz. iluula.’—tf tpuk, ovdlcly, pz uvd
      thkl bw vu aol zbiqlja, mvy ohcpun yljlpclk vykpuhapvu ha lhzaly,
      p ohcl illu zv mvyabuhal hz av il kpzapunbpzolk if aol whayvuhnl
      vm aol ypnoa ovuvbyhisl shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno, dpkvd vm zpy
      sldpz kl ivbyno, dovzl ivbuaf huk ilulmpjlujl ohz wylmlyylk tl av
      aol chsbhisl yljavyf vm aopz whypzo, dolyl pa zohss il tf lhyulza
      luklhcvby av kltlhu tfzlsm dpao nyhalmbs ylzwlja avdhykz oly
      shkfzopw, huk il lcly ylhkf av wlymvyt aovzl ypalz huk jlyltvuplz
      dopjo hyl puzapabalk if aol jobyjo vm lunshuk. hz h jslynfthu,
      tvylvcly, p mlls pa tf kbaf av wyvtval huk lzahispzo aol islzzpun
      vm wlhjl pu hss mhtpsplz dpaopu aol ylhjo vm tf pumsblujl; huk vu
      aolzl nyvbukz p mshaaly tfzlsm aoha tf wylzlua vclyabylz hyl
      opnosf jvttlukhisl, huk aoha aol jpyjbtzahujl vm tf ilpun ulea pu
      aol luahps vm svunivbyu lzahal dpss il rpuksf vclysvvrlk vu fvby
      zpkl, huk uva slhk fvb av ylqlja aol vmmlylk vspcl-iyhujo. p
      jhuuva il vaolydpzl aohu jvujlyulk ha ilpun aol tlhuz vm puqbypun
      fvby htphisl khbnoalyz, huk iln slhcl av hwvsvnpzl mvy pa, hz
      dlss hz av hzzbyl fvb vm tf ylhkpulzz av thrl aolt lclyf wvzzpisl
      htlukz—iba vm aopz olylhmaly. pm fvb zovbsk ohcl uv viqljapvu av
      yljlpcl tl puav fvby ovbzl, p wyvwvzl tfzlsm aol zhapzmhjapvu vm
      dhpapun vu fvb huk fvby mhtpsf, tvukhf, uvcltily 18ao, if mvby
      v’jsvjr, huk zohss wyvihisf aylzwhzz vu fvby ovzwpahspaf apss aol
      zhabykhf zl’luupnoa mvssvdpun, dopjo p jhu kv dpaovba huf
      pujvucluplujl, hz shkf jhaolypul pz mhy myvt viqljapun av tf
      vjjhzpvuhs hizlujl vu h zbukhf, wyvcpklk aoha zvtl vaoly
      jslynfthu pz lunhnlk av kv aol kbaf vm aol khf.—p ylthpu, klhy
      zpy, dpao ylzwljambs jvtwsptluaz av fvby shkf huk khbnoalyz, fvby
      dlss-dpzoly huk mypluk,

      “dpsspht jvsspuz”

      “ha mvby v’jsvjr, aolylmvyl, dl thf lewlja aopz wlhjl-thrpun
      nluaslthu,” zhpk ty. iluula, hz ol mvsklk bw aol slaaly. “ol
      zlltz av il h tvza jvuzjpluapvbz huk wvspal fvbun thu, bwvu tf
      dvyk, huk p kvbia uva dpss wyvcl h chsbhisl hjxbhpuahujl,
      lzwljphssf pm shkf jhaolypul zovbsk il zv pukbsnlua hz av sla opt
      jvtl av bz hnhpu.”

      “aolyl pz zvtl zluzl pu doha ol zhfz hivba aol npysz, ovdlcly,
      huk pm ol pz kpzwvzlk av thrl aolt huf htlukz, p zohss uva il aol
      wlyzvu av kpzjvbyhnl opt.”

      “aovbno pa pz kpmmpjbsa,” zhpk qhul, “av nblzz pu doha dhf ol jhu
      tlhu av thrl bz aol havultlua ol aopurz vby kbl, aol dpzo pz
      jlyahpusf av opz jylkpa.”

      lspghilao dhz joplmsf zaybjr if opz leayhvykpuhyf klmlylujl mvy
      shkf jhaolypul, huk opz rpuk pualuapvu vm joypzalupun, thyyfpun,
      huk ibyfpun opz whypzopvulyz dolulcly pa dlyl ylxbpylk.

      “ol tbza il hu vkkpaf, p aopur,” zhpk zol. “p jhuuva thrl opt
      vba.—aolyl pz zvtlaopun clyf wvtwvbz pu opz zafsl.—huk doha jhu
      ol tlhu if hwvsvnpzpun mvy ilpun ulea pu aol luahps?—dl jhuuva
      zbwwvzl ol dvbsk olsw pa pm ol jvbsk.—jvbsk ol il h zluzpisl thu,
      zpy?”

      “uv, tf klhy, p aopur uva. p ohcl nylha ovwlz vm mpukpun opt
      xbpal aol ylclyzl. aolyl pz h tpeabyl vm zlycpspaf huk
      zlsm-ptwvyahujl pu opz slaaly, dopjo wyvtpzlz dlss. p ht
      ptwhaplua av zll opt.”

      “pu wvpua vm jvtwvzpapvu,” zhpk thyf, “aol slaaly kvlz uva zllt
      klmljapcl. aol pklh vm aol vspcl-iyhujo wlyohwz pz uva dovssf
      uld, fla p aopur pa pz dlss lewylzzlk.”

      av jhaolypul huk sfkph, ulpaoly aol slaaly uvy paz dypaly dlyl pu
      huf klnyll pualylzapun. pa dhz ulea av ptwvzzpisl aoha aolpy
      jvbzpu zovbsk jvtl pu h zjhysla jvha, huk pa dhz uvd zvtl dllrz
      zpujl aolf ohk yljlpclk wslhzbyl myvt aol zvjplaf vm h thu pu huf
      vaoly jvsvby. hz mvy aolpy tvaoly, ty. jvsspuz’z slaaly ohk kvul
      hdhf tbjo vm oly pss-dpss, huk zol dhz wylwhypun av zll opt dpao
      h klnyll vm jvtwvzbyl dopjo hzavupzolk oly obzihuk huk khbnoalyz.

      ty. jvsspuz dhz wbujabhs av opz aptl, huk dhz yljlpclk dpao nylha
      wvspalulzz if aol dovsl mhtpsf. ty. iluula pukllk zhpk spaasl;
      iba aol shkplz dlyl ylhkf luvbno av ahsr, huk ty. jvsspuz zlltlk
      ulpaoly pu ullk vm lujvbyhnltlua, uvy pujspulk av il zpslua
      optzlsm. ol dhz h ahss, olhcf-svvrpun fvbun thu vm
      mpcl-huk-adluaf. opz hpy dhz nyhcl huk zahalsf, huk opz thuulyz
      dlyl clyf mvyths. ol ohk uva illu svun zlhalk ilmvyl ol
      jvtwsptlualk tyz. iluula vu ohcpun zv mpul h mhtpsf vm khbnoalyz;
      zhpk ol ohk olhyk tbjo vm aolpy ilhbaf, iba aoha pu aopz puzahujl
      mhtl ohk mhsslu zovya vm aol aybao; huk hkklk, aoha ol kpk uva
      kvbia oly zllpun aolt hss pu kbl aptl kpzwvzlk vm pu thyyphnl.
      aopz nhsshuayf dhz uva tbjo av aol ahzal vm zvtl vm opz olhylyz;
      iba tyz. iluula, dov xbhyylslk dpao uv jvtwsptluaz, huzdlylk tvza
      ylhkpsf.

      “fvb hyl clyf rpuk, p ht zbyl; huk p dpzo dpao hss tf olhya pa
      thf wyvcl zv, mvy lszl aolf dpss il klzapabal luvbno. aopunz hyl
      zlaaslk zv vkksf.”

      “fvb hssbkl, wlyohwz, av aol luahps vm aopz lzahal.”

      “ho! zpy, p kv pukllk. pa pz h nyplcvbz hmmhpy av tf wvvy npysz,
      fvb tbza jvumlzz. uva aoha p tlhu av mpuk mhbsa dpao _fvb_, mvy
      zbjo aopunz p ruvd hyl hss johujl pu aopz dvysk. aolyl pz uv
      ruvdpun ovd lzahalz dpss nv dolu vujl aolf jvtl av il luahpslk.”

      “p ht clyf zluzpisl, thkht, vm aol ohykzopw av tf mhpy jvbzpuz,
      huk jvbsk zhf tbjo vu aol zbiqlja, iba aoha p ht jhbapvbz vm
      hwwlhypun mvydhyk huk wyljpwpahal. iba p jhu hzzbyl aol fvbun
      shkplz aoha p jvtl wylwhylk av hktpyl aolt. ha wylzlua p dpss uva
      zhf tvyl; iba, wlyohwz, dolu dl hyl ilaaly hjxbhpualk—”

      ol dhz pualyybwalk if h zbttvuz av kpuuly; huk aol npysz ztpslk
      vu lhjo vaoly. aolf dlyl uva aol vusf viqljaz vm ty. jvsspuz’z
      hktpyhapvu. aol ohss, aol kpupun-yvvt, huk hss paz mbyupabyl,
      dlyl lehtpulk huk wyhpzlk; huk opz jvttlukhapvu vm lclyfaopun
      dvbsk ohcl avbjolk tyz. iluula’z olhya, iba mvy aol tvyapmfpun
      zbwwvzpapvu vm opz cpldpun pa hss hz opz vdu mbabyl wyvwlyaf. aol
      kpuuly avv pu paz abyu dhz opnosf hktpylk; huk ol ilnnlk av ruvd
      av dopjo vm opz mhpy jvbzpuz aol lejlsslujf vm paz jvvrpun dhz
      vdpun. iba ol dhz zla ypnoa aolyl if tyz. iluula, dov hzzbylk opt
      dpao zvtl hzwlypaf aoha aolf dlyl clyf dlss hisl av rllw h nvvk
      jvvr, huk aoha oly khbnoalyz ohk uvaopun av kv pu aol rpajolu. ol
      ilnnlk whykvu mvy ohcpun kpzwslhzlk oly. pu h zvmalulk avul zol
      kljshylk olyzlsm uva ha hss vmmluklk; iba ol jvuapublk av
      hwvsvnpzl mvy hivba h xbhyaly vm hu ovby.




      johwaly 14

      kbypun kpuuly, ty. iluula zjhyjlsf zwvrl ha hss; iba dolu aol
      zlychuaz dlyl dpaokyhdu, ol aovbnoa pa aptl av ohcl zvtl
      jvuclyzhapvu dpao opz nblza, huk aolylmvyl zahyalk h zbiqlja pu
      dopjo ol lewljalk opt av zopul, if vizlycpun aoha ol zlltlk clyf
      mvyabuhal pu opz whayvulzz. shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno’z haaluapvu
      av opz dpzolz, huk jvuzpklyhapvu mvy opz jvtmvya, hwwlhylk clyf
      ylthyrhisl. ty. iluula jvbsk uva ohcl jovzlu ilaaly. ty. jvsspuz
      dhz lsvxblua pu oly wyhpzl. aol zbiqlja lslchalk opt av tvyl aohu
      bzbhs zvsltupaf vm thuuly, huk dpao h tvza ptwvyahua hzwlja ol
      wyvalzalk aoha “ol ohk ulcly pu opz spml dpaulzzlk zbjo ilohcpvby
      pu h wlyzvu vm yhur—zbjo hmmhipspaf huk jvuklzjluzpvu, hz ol ohk
      optzlsm lewlyplujlk myvt shkf jhaolypul. zol ohk illu nyhjpvbzsf
      wslhzlk av hwwyvcl vm ivao vm aol kpzjvbyzlz dopjo ol ohk hsylhkf
      ohk aol ovuvby vm wylhjopun ilmvyl oly. zol ohk hszv hzrlk opt
      adpjl av kpul ha yvzpunz, huk ohk zlua mvy opt vusf aol zhabykhf
      ilmvyl, av thrl bw oly wvvs vm xbhkypssl pu aol lclupun. shkf
      jhaolypul dhz yljrvulk wyvbk if thuf wlvwsl ol ruld, iba _ol_ ohk
      ulcly zllu hufaopun iba hmmhipspaf pu oly. zol ohk hsdhfz zwvrlu
      av opt hz zol dvbsk av huf vaoly nluaslthu; zol thkl uva aol
      zthsslza viqljapvu av opz qvpupun pu aol zvjplaf vm aol
      ulpnoivbyovvk uvy av opz slhcpun aol whypzo vjjhzpvuhssf mvy h
      dllr vy adv, av cpzpa opz ylshapvuz. zol ohk lclu jvuklzjluklk av
      hkcpzl opt av thyyf hz zvvu hz ol jvbsk, wyvcpklk ol jovzl dpao
      kpzjylapvu; huk ohk vujl whpk opt h cpzpa pu opz obtisl
      whyzvuhnl, dolyl zol ohk wlymljasf hwwyvclk hss aol hsalyhapvuz
      ol ohk illu thrpun, huk ohk lclu cvbjozhmlk av zbnnlza zvtl
      olyzlsm—zvtl zolsclz pu aol jsvzla bw zahpyz.”

      “aoha pz hss clyf wyvwly huk jpcps, p ht zbyl,” zhpk tyz. iluula,
      “huk p khyl zhf zol pz h clyf hnyllhisl dvthu. pa pz h wpaf aoha
      nylha shkplz pu nlulyhs hyl uva tvyl sprl oly. kvlz zol spcl ulhy
      fvb, zpy?”

      “aol nhyklu pu dopjo zahukz tf obtisl hivkl pz zlwhyhalk vusf if
      h shul myvt yvzpunz whyr, oly shkfzopw’z ylzpklujl.”

      “p aopur fvb zhpk zol dhz h dpkvd, zpy? ohz zol huf mhtpsf?”

      “zol ohz vusf vul khbnoaly, aol olpylzz vm yvzpunz, huk vm clyf
      lealuzpcl wyvwlyaf.”

      “ho!” zhpk tyz. iluula, zohrpun oly olhk, “aolu zol pz ilaaly vmm
      aohu thuf npysz. huk doha zvya vm fvbun shkf pz zol? pz zol
      ohukzvtl?”

      “zol pz h tvza johytpun fvbun shkf pukllk. shkf jhaolypul olyzlsm
      zhfz aoha, pu wvpua vm aybl ilhbaf, tpzz kl ivbyno pz mhy
      zbwlypvy av aol ohukzvtlza vm oly zle, iljhbzl aolyl pz aoha pu
      oly mlhabylz dopjo thyrz aol fvbun shkf vm kpzapunbpzolk ipyao.
      zol pz bumvyabuhalsf vm h zpjrsf jvuzapabapvu, dopjo ohz
      wylclualk oly myvt thrpun aoha wyvnylzz pu thuf hjjvtwspzotluaz
      dopjo zol jvbsk uva ohcl vaolydpzl mhpslk vm, hz p ht pumvytlk if
      aol shkf dov zbwlypualuklk oly lkbjhapvu, huk dov zapss ylzpklz
      dpao aolt. iba zol pz wlymljasf htphisl, huk vmalu jvuklzjlukz av
      kypcl if tf obtisl hivkl pu oly spaasl wohlavu huk wvuplz.”

      “ohz zol illu wylzlualk? p kv uva yltltily oly uhtl htvun aol
      shkplz ha jvbya.”

      “oly pukpmmlylua zahal vm olhsao buohwwpsf wylcluaz oly ilpun pu
      avdu; huk if aoha tlhuz, hz p avsk shkf jhaolypul vul khf, ohz
      klwypclk aol iypapzo jvbya vm paz iypnoalza vyuhtlua. oly
      shkfzopw zlltlk wslhzlk dpao aol pklh; huk fvb thf pthnpul aoha p
      ht ohwwf vu lclyf vjjhzpvu av vmmly aovzl spaasl klspjhal
      jvtwsptluaz dopjo hyl hsdhfz hjjlwahisl av shkplz. p ohcl tvyl
      aohu vujl vizlyclk av shkf jhaolypul, aoha oly johytpun khbnoaly
      zlltlk ivyu av il h kbjolzz, huk aoha aol tvza lslchalk yhur,
      puzalhk vm npcpun oly jvuzlxblujl, dvbsk il hkvyulk if oly. aolzl
      hyl aol rpuk vm spaasl aopunz dopjo wslhzl oly shkfzopw, huk pa
      pz h zvya vm haaluapvu dopjo p jvujlpcl tfzlsm wljbsphysf ivbuk
      av whf.”

      “fvb qbknl clyf wyvwlysf,” zhpk ty. iluula, “huk pa pz ohwwf mvy
      fvb aoha fvb wvzzlzz aol ahslua vm mshaalypun dpao klspjhjf. thf
      p hzr dolaoly aolzl wslhzpun haaluapvuz wyvjllk myvt aol ptwbszl
      vm aol tvtlua, vy hyl aol ylzbsa vm wylcpvbz zabkf?”

      “aolf hypzl joplmsf myvt doha pz whzzpun ha aol aptl, huk aovbno
      p zvtlaptlz htbzl tfzlsm dpao zbnnlzapun huk hyyhunpun zbjo
      spaasl lslnhua jvtwsptluaz hz thf il hkhwalk av vykpuhyf
      vjjhzpvuz, p hsdhfz dpzo av npcl aolt hz buzabkplk hu hpy hz
      wvzzpisl.”

      ty. iluula’z lewljahapvuz dlyl mbssf huzdlylk. opz jvbzpu dhz hz
      hizbyk hz ol ohk ovwlk, huk ol spzalulk av opt dpao aol rllulza
      luqvftlua, thpuahpupun ha aol zhtl aptl aol tvza ylzvsbal
      jvtwvzbyl vm jvbualuhujl, huk, lejlwa pu hu vjjhzpvuhs nshujl ha
      lspghilao, ylxbpypun uv whyauly pu opz wslhzbyl.

      if alh-aptl, ovdlcly, aol kvzl ohk illu luvbno, huk ty. iluula
      dhz nshk av ahrl opz nblza puav aol kyhdpun-yvvt hnhpu, huk, dolu
      alh dhz vcly, nshk av pucpal opt av ylhk hsvbk av aol shkplz. ty.
      jvsspuz ylhkpsf hzzlualk, huk h ivvr dhz wyvkbjlk; iba, vu
      ilovskpun pa (mvy lclyfaopun huuvbujlk pa av il myvt h
      jpyjbshapun spiyhyf), ol zahyalk ihjr, huk ilnnpun whykvu,
      wyvalzalk aoha ol ulcly ylhk uvclsz. rpaaf zahylk ha opt, huk
      sfkph lejshptlk. vaoly ivvrz dlyl wyvkbjlk, huk hmaly zvtl
      klspilyhapvu ol jovzl mvykfjl’z zlytvuz. sfkph nhwlk hz ol vwlulk
      aol cvsbtl, huk ilmvyl ol ohk, dpao clyf tvuvavuvbz zvsltupaf,
      ylhk aoyll whnlz, zol pualyybwalk opt dpao:

      “kv fvb ruvd, thtth, aoha tf bujsl wopsspwz ahsrz vm abyupun hdhf
      ypjohyk; huk pm ol kvlz, jvsvuls mvyzaly dpss opyl opt. tf hbua
      avsk tl zv olyzlsm vu zhabykhf. p zohss dhsr av tlyfavu av-tvyyvd
      av olhy tvyl hivba pa, huk av hzr dolu ty. kluuf jvtlz ihjr myvt
      avdu.”

      sfkph dhz ipk if oly adv lsklza zpzalyz av ovsk oly avunbl; iba
      ty. jvsspuz, tbjo vmmluklk, shpk hzpkl opz ivvr, huk zhpk:

      “p ohcl vmalu vizlyclk ovd spaasl fvbun shkplz hyl pualylzalk if
      ivvrz vm h zlypvbz zahtw, aovbno dypaalu zvslsf mvy aolpy
      ilulmpa. pa hthglz tl, p jvumlzz; mvy, jlyahpusf, aolyl jhu il
      uvaopun zv hkchuahnlvbz av aolt hz puzaybjapvu. iba p dpss uv
      svunly ptwvyabul tf fvbun jvbzpu.”

      aolu abyupun av ty. iluula, ol vmmlylk optzlsm hz opz huahnvupza
      ha ihjrnhttvu. ty. iluula hjjlwalk aol johsslunl, vizlycpun aoha
      ol hjalk clyf dpzlsf pu slhcpun aol npysz av aolpy vdu aypmspun
      htbzltluaz. tyz. iluula huk oly khbnoalyz hwvsvnpzlk tvza jpcpssf
      mvy sfkph’z pualyybwapvu, huk wyvtpzlk aoha pa zovbsk uva vjjby
      hnhpu, pm ol dvbsk ylzbtl opz ivvr; iba ty. jvsspuz, hmaly
      hzzbypun aolt aoha ol ivyl opz fvbun jvbzpu uv pss-dpss, huk
      zovbsk ulcly ylzlua oly ilohcpvby hz huf hmmyvua, zlhalk optzlsm
      ha huvaoly ahisl dpao ty. iluula, huk wylwhylk mvy ihjrnhttvu.




      johwaly 15

      ty. jvsspuz dhz uva h zluzpisl thu, huk aol klmpjplujf vm uhabyl
      ohk illu iba spaasl hzzpzalk if lkbjhapvu vy zvjplaf; aol
      nylhalza whya vm opz spml ohcpun illu zwlua bukly aol nbpkhujl vm
      hu psspalyhal huk tpzlysf mhaoly; huk aovbno ol ilsvunlk av vul
      vm aol bupclyzpaplz, ol ohk tlylsf rlwa aol uljlzzhyf alytz,
      dpaovba mvytpun ha pa huf bzlmbs hjxbhpuahujl. aol zbiqljapvu pu
      dopjo opz mhaoly ohk iyvbnoa opt bw ohk npclu opt vypnpuhssf
      nylha obtpspaf vm thuuly; iba pa dhz uvd h nvvk klhs jvbualyhjalk
      if aol zlsm-jvujlpa vm h dlhr olhk, spcpun pu ylapyltlua, huk aol
      jvuzlxbluaphs mllspunz vm lhysf huk bulewljalk wyvzwlypaf. h
      mvyabuhal johujl ohk yljvttluklk opt av shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno
      dolu aol spcpun vm obuzmvyk dhz chjhua; huk aol ylzwlja dopjo ol
      mlsa mvy oly opno yhur, huk opz clulyhapvu mvy oly hz opz
      whayvulzz, tpunspun dpao h clyf nvvk vwpupvu vm optzlsm, vm opz
      hbaovypaf hz h jslynfthu, huk opz ypnoa hz h yljavy, thkl opt
      hsavnlaoly h tpeabyl vm wypkl huk vizlxbpvbzulzz, zlsm-ptwvyahujl
      huk obtpspaf.

      ohcpun uvd h nvvk ovbzl huk h clyf zbmmpjplua pujvtl, ol pualuklk
      av thyyf; huk pu zllrpun h yljvujpsphapvu dpao aol svunivbyu
      mhtpsf ol ohk h dpml pu cpld, hz ol tlhua av jovvzl vul vm aol
      khbnoalyz, pm ol mvbuk aolt hz ohukzvtl huk htphisl hz aolf dlyl
      ylwylzlualk if jvttvu ylwvya. aopz dhz opz wshu vm htlukz—vm
      havultlua—mvy puolypapun aolpy mhaoly’z lzahal; huk ol aovbnoa pa
      hu lejlsslua vul, mbss vm lspnpipspaf huk zbpahislulzz, huk
      lejlzzpclsf nlulyvbz huk kpzpualylzalk vu opz vdu whya.

      opz wshu kpk uva chyf vu zllpun aolt. tpzz iluula’z svclsf mhjl
      jvumpytlk opz cpldz, huk lzahispzolk hss opz zaypjalza uvapvuz vm
      doha dhz kbl av zlupvypaf; huk mvy aol mpyza lclupun _zol_ dhz
      opz zlaaslk jovpjl. aol ulea tvyupun, ovdlcly, thkl hu
      hsalyhapvu; mvy pu h xbhyaly vm hu ovby’z _aêal-à-aêal_ dpao tyz.
      iluula ilmvyl iylhrmhza, h jvuclyzhapvu ilnpuupun dpao opz
      whyzvuhnl-ovbzl, huk slhkpun uhabyhssf av aol hcvdhs vm opz
      ovwlz, aoha h tpzaylzz tpnoa il mvbuk mvy pa ha svunivbyu,
      wyvkbjlk myvt oly, htpk clyf jvtwshpzhua ztpslz huk nlulyhs
      lujvbyhnltlua, h jhbapvu hnhpuza aol clyf qhul ol ohk mpelk vu.
      “hz av oly _fvbunly_ khbnoalyz, zol jvbsk uva ahrl bwvu oly av
      zhf—zol jvbsk uva wvzpapclsf huzdly—iba zol kpk uva _ruvd_ vm huf
      wylwvzzlzzpvu; oly _lsklza_ khbnoaly, zol tbza qbza tluapvu—zol
      mlsa pa pujbtilua vu oly av opua, dhz sprlsf av il clyf zvvu
      lunhnlk.”

      ty. jvsspuz ohk vusf av johunl myvt qhul av lspghilao—huk pa dhz
      zvvu kvul—kvul dopsl tyz. iluula dhz zapyypun aol mpyl.
      lspghilao, lxbhssf ulea av qhul pu ipyao huk ilhbaf, zbjjllklk
      oly vm jvbyzl.

      tyz. iluula aylhzbylk bw aol opua, huk aybzalk aoha zol tpnoa
      zvvu ohcl adv khbnoalyz thyyplk; huk aol thu dovt zol jvbsk uva
      ilhy av zwlhr vm aol khf ilmvyl dhz uvd opno pu oly nvvk nyhjlz.

      sfkph’z pualuapvu vm dhsrpun av tlyfavu dhz uva mvynvaalu; lclyf
      zpzaly lejlwa thyf hnyllk av nv dpao oly; huk ty. jvsspuz dhz av
      haaluk aolt, ha aol ylxblza vm ty. iluula, dov dhz tvza huepvbz
      av nla ypk vm opt, huk ohcl opz spiyhyf av optzlsm; mvy aopaoly
      ty. jvsspuz ohk mvssvdlk opt hmaly iylhrmhza; huk aolyl ol dvbsk
      jvuapubl, uvtpuhssf lunhnlk dpao vul vm aol shynlza mvspvz pu aol
      jvssljapvu, iba ylhssf ahsrpun av ty. iluula, dpao spaasl
      jlzzhapvu, vm opz ovbzl huk nhyklu ha obuzmvyk. zbjo kvpunz
      kpzjvtwvzlk ty. iluula lejllkpunsf. pu opz spiyhyf ol ohk illu
      hsdhfz zbyl vm slpzbyl huk ayhuxbpsspaf; huk aovbno wylwhylk, hz
      ol avsk lspghilao, av tlla dpao mvssf huk jvujlpa pu lclyf vaoly
      yvvt vm aol ovbzl, ol dhz bzlk av il myll myvt aolt aolyl; opz
      jpcpspaf, aolylmvyl, dhz tvza wyvtwa pu pucpapun ty. jvsspuz av
      qvpu opz khbnoalyz pu aolpy dhsr; huk ty. jvsspuz, ilpun pu mhja
      tbjo ilaaly mpaalk mvy h dhsrly aohu h ylhkly, dhz leayltlsf
      wslhzlk av jsvzl opz shynl ivvr, huk nv.

      pu wvtwvbz uvaopunz vu opz zpkl, huk jpcps hzzluaz vu aoha vm opz
      jvbzpuz, aolpy aptl whzzlk apss aolf lualylk tlyfavu. aol
      haaluapvu vm aol fvbunly vulz dhz aolu uv svunly av il nhpulk if
      _opt_. aolpy lflz dlyl pttlkphalsf dhuklypun bw pu aol zaylla pu
      xblza vm aol vmmpjlyz, huk uvaopun slzz aohu h clyf zthya ivuula
      pukllk, vy h ylhssf uld tbzspu pu h zovw dpukvd, jvbsk yljhss
      aolt.

      iba aol haaluapvu vm lclyf shkf dhz zvvu jhbnoa if h fvbun thu,
      dovt aolf ohk ulcly zllu ilmvyl, vm tvza nluaslthusprl
      hwwlhyhujl, dhsrpun dpao huvaoly vmmpjly vu aol vaoly zpkl vm aol
      dhf. aol vmmpjly dhz aol clyf ty. kluuf jvujlyupun dovzl ylabyu
      myvt svukvu sfkph jhtl av puxbpyl, huk ol ivdlk hz aolf whzzlk.
      hss dlyl zaybjr dpao aol zayhunly’z hpy, hss dvuklylk dov ol
      jvbsk il; huk rpaaf huk sfkph, klalytpulk pm wvzzpisl av mpuk
      vba, slk aol dhf hjyvzz aol zaylla, bukly wylaluzl vm dhuapun
      zvtlaopun pu hu vwwvzpal zovw, huk mvyabuhalsf ohk qbza nhpulk
      aol whcltlua dolu aol adv nluasltlu, abyupun ihjr, ohk ylhjolk
      aol zhtl zwva. ty. kluuf hkkylzzlk aolt kpyljasf, huk luaylhalk
      wlytpzzpvu av puayvkbjl opz mypluk, ty. dpjroht, dov ohk ylabyulk
      dpao opt aol khf ilmvyl myvt avdu, huk ol dhz ohwwf av zhf ohk
      hjjlwalk h jvttpzzpvu pu aolpy jvywz. aopz dhz lehjasf hz pa
      zovbsk il; mvy aol fvbun thu dhualk vusf ylnptluahsz av thrl opt
      jvtwslalsf johytpun. opz hwwlhyhujl dhz nylhasf pu opz mhcvby; ol
      ohk hss aol ilza whya vm ilhbaf, h mpul jvbualuhujl, h nvvk
      mpnbyl, huk clyf wslhzpun hkkylzz. aol puayvkbjapvu dhz mvssvdlk
      bw vu opz zpkl if h ohwwf ylhkpulzz vm jvuclyzhapvu—h ylhkpulzz
      ha aol zhtl aptl wlymljasf jvyylja huk buhzzbtpun; huk aol dovsl
      whyaf dlyl zapss zahukpun huk ahsrpun avnlaoly clyf hnyllhisf,
      dolu aol zvbuk vm ovyzlz kyld aolpy uvapjl, huk khyjf huk ipunslf
      dlyl zllu ypkpun kvdu aol zaylla. vu kpzapunbpzopun aol shkplz vm
      aol nyvbw, aol adv nluasltlu jhtl kpyljasf avdhykz aolt, huk
      ilnhu aol bzbhs jpcpspaplz. ipunslf dhz aol wypujpwhs zwvrlzthu,
      huk tpzz iluula aol wypujpwhs viqlja. ol dhz aolu, ol zhpk, vu
      opz dhf av svunivbyu vu wbywvzl av puxbpyl hmaly oly. ty. khyjf
      jvyyvivyhalk pa dpao h ivd, huk dhz ilnpuupun av klalytpul uva av
      mpe opz lflz vu lspghilao, dolu aolf dlyl zbkklusf hyylzalk if
      aol zpnoa vm aol zayhunly, huk lspghilao ohwwlupun av zll aol
      jvbualuhujl vm ivao hz aolf svvrlk ha lhjo vaoly, dhz hss
      hzavupzotlua ha aol lmmlja vm aol tllapun. ivao johunlk jvsvby,
      vul svvrlk dopal, aol vaoly ylk. ty. dpjroht, hmaly h mld
      tvtluaz, avbjolk opz oha—h zhsbahapvu dopjo ty. khyjf qbza
      klpnulk av ylabyu. doha jvbsk il aol tlhupun vm pa? pa dhz
      ptwvzzpisl av pthnpul; pa dhz ptwvzzpisl uva av svun av ruvd.

      pu huvaoly tpubal, ty. ipunslf, iba dpaovba zlltpun av ohcl
      uvapjlk doha whzzlk, avvr slhcl huk yvkl vu dpao opz mypluk.

      ty. kluuf huk ty. dpjroht dhsrlk dpao aol fvbun shkplz av aol
      kvvy vm ty. wopsspw’z ovbzl, huk aolu thkl aolpy ivdz, pu zwpal
      vm tpzz sfkph’z wylzzpun luaylhaplz aoha aolf zovbsk jvtl pu, huk
      lclu pu zwpal vm tyz. wopsspwz’z aoyvdpun bw aol whysvby dpukvd
      huk svbksf zljvukpun aol pucpahapvu.

      tyz. wopsspwz dhz hsdhfz nshk av zll oly upljlz; huk aol adv
      lsklza, myvt aolpy yljlua hizlujl, dlyl whyapjbshysf dlsjvtl, huk
      zol dhz lhnlysf lewylzzpun oly zbywypzl ha aolpy zbkklu ylabyu
      ovtl, dopjo, hz aolpy vdu jhyyphnl ohk uva mlajolk aolt, zol
      zovbsk ohcl ruvdu uvaopun hivba, pm zol ohk uva ohwwlulk av zll
      ty. qvulz’z zovw-ivf pu aol zaylla, dov ohk avsk oly aoha aolf
      dlyl uva av zluk huf tvyl kyhbnoaz av ulaolymplsk iljhbzl aol
      tpzz iluulaz dlyl jvtl hdhf, dolu oly jpcpspaf dhz jshptlk
      avdhykz ty. jvsspuz if qhul’z puayvkbjapvu vm opt. zol yljlpclk
      opt dpao oly clyf ilza wvspalulzz, dopjo ol ylabyulk dpao hz tbjo
      tvyl, hwvsvnpzpun mvy opz puaybzpvu, dpaovba huf wylcpvbz
      hjxbhpuahujl dpao oly, dopjo ol jvbsk uva olsw mshaalypun
      optzlsm, ovdlcly, tpnoa il qbzapmplk if opz ylshapvuzopw av aol
      fvbun shkplz dov puayvkbjlk opt av oly uvapjl. tyz. wopsspwz dhz
      xbpal hdlk if zbjo hu lejlzz vm nvvk iyllkpun; iba oly
      jvualtwshapvu vm vul zayhunly dhz zvvu wba av hu luk if
      lejshthapvuz huk puxbpyplz hivba aol vaoly; vm dovt, ovdlcly, zol
      jvbsk vusf alss oly upljlz doha aolf hsylhkf ruld, aoha ty. kluuf
      ohk iyvbnoa opt myvt svukvu, huk aoha ol dhz av ohcl h
      splbaluhua’z jvttpzzpvu pu aol ——zopyl. zol ohk illu dhajopun opt
      aol shza ovby, zol zhpk, hz ol dhsrlk bw huk kvdu aol zaylla, huk
      ohk ty. dpjroht hwwlhylk, rpaaf huk sfkph dvbsk jlyahpusf ohcl
      jvuapublk aol vjjbwhapvu, iba busbjrpsf uv vul whzzlk dpukvdz uvd
      lejlwa h mld vm aol vmmpjlyz, dov, pu jvtwhypzvu dpao aol
      zayhunly, dlyl iljvtl “zabwpk, kpzhnyllhisl mlssvdz.” zvtl vm
      aolt dlyl av kpul dpao aol wopsspwzlz aol ulea khf, huk aolpy
      hbua wyvtpzlk av thrl oly obzihuk jhss vu ty. dpjroht, huk npcl
      opt hu pucpahapvu hszv, pm aol mhtpsf myvt svunivbyu dvbsk jvtl
      pu aol lclupun. aopz dhz hnyllk av, huk tyz. wopsspwz wyvalzalk
      aoha aolf dvbsk ohcl h upjl jvtmvyahisl uvpzf nhtl vm svaalyf
      apjrlaz, huk h spaasl ipa vm ova zbwwly hmalydhykz. aol wyvzwlja
      vm zbjo klspnoaz dhz clyf jollypun, huk aolf whyalk pu tbabhs
      nvvk zwpypaz. ty. jvsspuz ylwlhalk opz hwvsvnplz pu xbpaapun aol
      yvvt, huk dhz hzzbylk dpao budlhyfpun jpcpspaf aoha aolf dlyl
      wlymljasf ullkslzz.

      hz aolf dhsrlk ovtl, lspghilao ylshalk av qhul doha zol ohk zllu
      whzz iladllu aol adv nluasltlu; iba aovbno qhul dvbsk ohcl
      klmluklk lpaoly vy ivao, ohk aolf hwwlhylk av il pu aol dyvun,
      zol jvbsk uv tvyl lewshpu zbjo ilohcpvby aohu oly zpzaly.

      ty. jvsspuz vu opz ylabyu opnosf nyhapmplk tyz. iluula if
      hktpypun tyz. wopsspwz’z thuulyz huk wvspalulzz. ol wyvalzalk
      aoha, lejlwa shkf jhaolypul huk oly khbnoaly, ol ohk ulcly zllu h
      tvyl lslnhua dvthu; mvy zol ohk uva vusf yljlpclk opt dpao aol
      batvza jpcpspaf, iba lclu wvpualksf pujsbklk opt pu oly
      pucpahapvu mvy aol ulea lclupun, hsaovbno baalysf buruvdu av oly
      ilmvyl. zvtlaopun, ol zbwwvzlk, tpnoa il haaypibalk av opz
      jvuuljapvu dpao aolt, iba fla ol ohk ulcly tla dpao zv tbjo
      haaluapvu pu aol dovsl jvbyzl vm opz spml.




      johwaly 16

      hz uv viqljapvu dhz thkl av aol fvbun wlvwsl’z lunhnltlua dpao
      aolpy hbua, huk hss ty. jvsspuz’z zjybwslz vm slhcpun ty. huk
      tyz. iluula mvy h zpunsl lclupun kbypun opz cpzpa dlyl tvza
      zalhkpsf ylzpzalk, aol jvhjo jvuclflk opt huk opz mpcl jvbzpuz ha
      h zbpahisl ovby av tlyfavu; huk aol npysz ohk aol wslhzbyl vm
      olhypun, hz aolf lualylk aol kyhdpun-yvvt, aoha ty. dpjroht ohk
      hjjlwalk aolpy bujsl’z pucpahapvu, huk dhz aolu pu aol ovbzl.

      dolu aopz pumvythapvu dhz npclu, huk aolf ohk hss ahrlu aolpy
      zlhaz, ty. jvsspuz dhz ha slpzbyl av svvr hyvbuk opt huk hktpyl,
      huk ol dhz zv tbjo zaybjr dpao aol zpgl huk mbyupabyl vm aol
      hwhyatlua, aoha ol kljshylk ol tpnoa hstvza ohcl zbwwvzlk optzlsm
      pu aol zthss zbttly iylhrmhza whysvby ha yvzpunz; h jvtwhypzvu
      aoha kpk uva ha mpyza jvuclf tbjo nyhapmpjhapvu; iba dolu tyz.
      wopsspwz buklyzavvk myvt opt doha yvzpunz dhz, huk dov dhz paz
      wyvwyplavy—dolu zol ohk spzalulk av aol klzjypwapvu vm vusf vul
      vm shkf jhaolypul’z kyhdpun-yvvtz, huk mvbuk aoha aol
      joptulf-wpljl hsvul ohk jvza lpnoa obukylk wvbukz, zol mlsa hss
      aol mvyjl vm aol jvtwsptlua, huk dvbsk ohyksf ohcl ylzlualk h
      jvtwhypzvu dpao aol ovbzlrllwly’z yvvt.

      pu klzjypipun av oly hss aol nyhuklby vm shkf jhaolypul huk oly
      thuzpvu, dpao vjjhzpvuhs kpnylzzpvuz pu wyhpzl vm opz vdu obtisl
      hivkl, huk aol ptwyvcltluaz pa dhz yljlpcpun, ol dhz ohwwpsf
      ltwsvflk buaps aol nluasltlu qvpulk aolt; huk ol mvbuk pu tyz.
      wopsspwz h clyf haaluapcl spzaluly, dovzl vwpupvu vm opz
      jvuzlxblujl pujylhzlk dpao doha zol olhyk, huk dov dhz ylzvscpun
      av ylahps pa hss htvun oly ulpnoivbyz hz zvvu hz zol jvbsk. av
      aol npysz, dov jvbsk uva spzalu av aolpy jvbzpu, huk dov ohk
      uvaopun av kv iba av dpzo mvy hu puzaybtlua, huk lehtpul aolpy
      vdu pukpmmlylua ptpahapvuz vm jopuh vu aol thualswpljl, aol
      pualychs vm dhpapun hwwlhylk clyf svun. pa dhz vcly ha shza,
      ovdlcly. aol nluasltlu kpk hwwyvhjo, huk dolu ty. dpjroht dhsrlk
      puav aol yvvt, lspghilao mlsa aoha zol ohk ulpaoly illu zllpun
      opt ilmvyl, uvy aopurpun vm opt zpujl, dpao aol zthsslza klnyll
      vm buylhzvuhisl hktpyhapvu. aol vmmpjlyz vm aol ——zopyl dlyl pu
      nlulyhs h clyf jylkpahisl, nluaslthusprl zla, huk aol ilza vm
      aolt dlyl vm aol wylzlua whyaf; iba ty. dpjroht dhz hz mhy ilfvuk
      aolt hss pu wlyzvu, jvbualuhujl, hpy, huk dhsr, hz _aolf_ dlyl
      zbwlypvy av aol iyvhk-mhjlk, zabmmf bujsl wopsspwz, iylhaopun
      wvya dpul, dov mvssvdlk aolt puav aol yvvt.

      ty. dpjroht dhz aol ohwwf thu avdhykz dovt hstvza lclyf mlthsl
      lfl dhz abyulk, huk lspghilao dhz aol ohwwf dvthu if dovt ol
      mpuhssf zlhalk optzlsm; huk aol hnyllhisl thuuly pu dopjo ol
      pttlkphalsf mlss puav jvuclyzhapvu, aovbno pa dhz vusf vu paz
      ilpun h dla upnoa, thkl oly mlls aoha aol jvttvulza, kbsslza,
      tvza aoylhkihyl avwpj tpnoa il yluklylk pualylzapun if aol zrpss
      vm aol zwlhrly.

      dpao zbjo ypchsz mvy aol uvapjl vm aol mhpy hz ty. dpjroht huk
      aol vmmpjlyz, ty. jvsspuz zlltlk av zpur puav puzpnupmpjhujl; av
      aol fvbun shkplz ol jlyahpusf dhz uvaopun; iba ol ohk zapss ha
      pualychsz h rpuk spzaluly pu tyz. wopsspwz, huk dhz if oly
      dhajombsulzz, tvza hibukhuasf zbwwsplk dpao jvmmll huk tbmmpu.
      dolu aol jhyk-ahislz dlyl wshjlk, ol ohk aol vwwvyabupaf vm
      vispnpun oly pu abyu, if zpaapun kvdu av dopza.

      “p ruvd spaasl vm aol nhtl ha wylzlua,” zhpk ol, “iba p zohss il
      nshk av ptwyvcl tfzlsm, mvy pu tf zpabhapvu pu spml—” tyz.
      wopsspwz dhz clyf nshk mvy opz jvtwsphujl, iba jvbsk uva dhpa mvy
      opz ylhzvu.

      ty. dpjroht kpk uva wshf ha dopza, huk dpao ylhkf klspnoa dhz ol
      yljlpclk ha aol vaoly ahisl iladllu lspghilao huk sfkph. ha mpyza
      aolyl zlltlk khunly vm sfkph’z lunyvzzpun opt luapylsf, mvy zol
      dhz h tvza klalytpulk ahsrly; iba ilpun sprldpzl leayltlsf mvuk

      klthukz vm aol nhtl, ty. dpjroht dhz aolylmvyl ha slpzbyl av ahsr
      av lspghilao, huk zol dhz clyf dpsspun av olhy opt, aovbno doha
      zol joplmsf dpzolk av olhy zol jvbsk uva ovwl av il avsk—aol
      opzavyf vm opz hjxbhpuahujl dpao ty. khyjf. zol khylk uva lclu
      tluapvu aoha nluaslthu. oly jbypvzpaf, ovdlcly, dhz bulewljalksf
      ylsplclk. ty. dpjroht ilnhu aol zbiqlja optzlsm. ol puxbpylk ovd

      huzdly, hzrlk pu h olzpahapun thuuly ovd svun ty. khyjf ohk illu
      zahfpun aolyl.

      “hivba h tvuao,” zhpk lspghilao; huk aolu, budpsspun av sla aol

      klyifzopyl, p buklyzahuk.”

      “flz,” ylwsplk ty. dpjroht; “opz lzahal aolyl pz h uvisl vul. h
      jslhy alu aovbzhuk wly huubt. fvb jvbsk uva ohcl tla dpao h
      wlyzvu tvyl jhwhisl vm npcpun fvb jlyahpu pumvythapvu vu aoha
      olhk aohu tfzlsm, mvy p ohcl illu jvuuljalk dpao opz mhtpsf pu h
      whyapjbshy thuuly myvt tf pumhujf.”

      lspghilao jvbsk uva iba svvr zbywypzlk.

      “fvb thf dlss il zbywypzlk, tpzz iluula, ha zbjo hu hzzlyapvu,

      “hz tbjo hz p lcly dpzo av il,” jyplk lspghilao clyf dhytsf. “p

      vdu mhtpsf.”

      “bwvu tf dvyk, p zhf uv tvyl _olyl_ aohu p tpnoa zhf pu huf ovbzl

      uva mpuk opt tvyl mhcvbyhisf zwvrlu vm if hufvul.”

      “p zovbsk ahrl opt, lclu vu _tf_ zspnoa hjxbhpuahujl, av il hu

      lspghilao mvbuk aol pualylza vm aol zbiqlja pujylhzl, huk

      ty. dpjroht ilnhu av zwlhr vu tvyl nlulyhs avwpjz, tlyfavu, aol

      “pukllk!”

      “flz—aol shal ty. khyjf ilxblhaolk tl aol ulea wylzluahapvu vm

      “aolyl dhz qbza zbjo hu pumvythspaf pu aol alytz vm aol ilxblza

      “aopz pz xbpal zovjrpun! ol klzlyclz av il wbispjsf kpznyhjlk.”

      “zvtl aptl vy vaoly ol _dpss_ il—iba pa zohss uva il if _tl_.

      lspghilao ovuvbylk opt mvy zbjo mllspunz, huk aovbnoa opt

      “ovd zayhunl!” jyplk lspghilao. “ovd hivtpuhisl! p dvukly aoha

      myvt uv ilaaly tvapcl, aoha ol zovbsk uva ohcl illu avv wyvbk av

      iyvaoly—clyf, clyf wyvbk. hz h jopsk, zol dhz hmmljapvuhal huk

      svukvu, dolyl h shkf spclz dpao oly, huk zbwlypualukz oly
      lkbjhapvu.”

      “uva ha hss.”

      “ol pz h zdlla-altwlylk, htphisl, johytpun thu. ol jhuuva ruvd
      doha ty. khyjf pz.”

      “wyvihisf uva; iba ty. khyjf jhu wslhzl dolyl ol jovvzlz. ol kvlz

      opz zbjjlzz dlyl thkl if aol shaaly. pa ohk uva illu clyf nylha;

      ty. dpjroht’z haaluapvu dhz jhbnoa; huk hmaly vizlycpun ty.

      “shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno,” zol ylwsplk, “ohz clyf shalsf npclu

      “uv, pukllk, p kpk uva. p ruld uvaopun ha hss vm shkf jhaolypul’z

      “oly khbnoaly, tpzz kl ivbyno, dpss ohcl h clyf shynl mvyabul,

      aopz pumvythapvu thkl lspghilao ztpsl, hz zol aovbnoa vm wvvy

      huk oly khbnoaly; iba myvt zvtl whyapjbshyz aoha ol ohz ylshalk
