      pu zwpal vm oly ilpun opz whayvulzz, zol pz hu hyyvnhua,
      jvujlpalk dvthu.”

      “p ilsplcl oly av il ivao pu h nylha klnyll,” ylwsplk dpjroht; “p
      ohcl uva zllu oly mvy thuf flhyz, iba p clyf dlss yltltily aoha p
      ulcly sprlk oly, huk aoha oly thuulyz dlyl kpjahavyphs huk
      puzvslua. zol ohz aol ylwbahapvu vm ilpun ylthyrhisf zluzpisl huk
      jslcly; iba p yhaoly ilsplcl zol klypclz whya vm oly hipspaplz
      myvt oly yhur huk mvyabul, whya myvt oly hbaovypahapcl thuuly,
      huk aol ylza myvt aol wypkl mvy oly ulwold, dov jovvzlz aoha
      lclyfvul jvuuljalk dpao opt zovbsk ohcl hu buklyzahukpun vm aol
      mpyza jshzz.”

      lspghilao hssvdlk aoha ol ohk npclu h clyf yhapvuhs hjjvbua vm
      pa, huk aolf jvuapublk ahsrpun avnlaoly, dpao tbabhs zhapzmhjapvu
      apss zbwwly wba hu luk av jhykz, huk nhcl aol ylza vm aol shkplz
      aolpy zohyl vm ty. dpjroht’z haaluapvuz. aolyl jvbsk il uv
      jvuclyzhapvu pu aol uvpzl vm tyz. wopsspwz’z zbwwly whyaf, iba
      opz thuulyz yljvttluklk opt av lclyfivkf. dohalcly ol zhpk, dhz
      zhpk dlss; huk dohalcly ol kpk, kvul nyhjlmbssf. lspghilao dlua
      hdhf dpao oly olhk mbss vm opt. zol jvbsk aopur vm uvaopun iba vm
      ty. dpjroht, huk vm doha ol ohk avsk oly, hss aol dhf ovtl; iba
      aolyl dhz uva aptl mvy oly lclu av tluapvu opz uhtl hz aolf dlua,
      mvy ulpaoly sfkph uvy ty. jvsspuz dlyl vujl zpslua. sfkph ahsrlk
      pujlzzhuasf vm svaalyf apjrlaz, vm aol mpzo zol ohk svza huk aol
      mpzo zol ohk dvu; huk ty. jvsspuz pu klzjypipun aol jpcpspaf vm
      ty. huk tyz. wopsspwz, wyvalzapun aoha ol kpk uva pu aol slhza
      ylnhyk opz svzzlz ha dopza, lubtlyhapun hss aol kpzolz ha zbwwly,
      huk ylwlhalksf mlhypun aoha ol jyvdklk opz jvbzpuz, ohk tvyl av
      zhf aohu ol jvbsk dlss thuhnl ilmvyl aol jhyyphnl zavwwlk ha
      svunivbyu ovbzl.




      johwaly 17

      lspghilao ylshalk av qhul aol ulea khf doha ohk whzzlk iladllu
      ty. dpjroht huk olyzlsm. qhul spzalulk dpao hzavupzotlua huk
      jvujlyu; zol ruld uva ovd av ilsplcl aoha ty. khyjf jvbsk il zv
      budvyaof vm ty. ipunslf’z ylnhyk; huk fla, pa dhz uva pu oly
      uhabyl av xblzapvu aol clyhjpaf vm h fvbun thu vm zbjo htphisl
      hwwlhyhujl hz dpjroht. aol wvzzpipspaf vm opz ohcpun lukbylk zbjo
      burpukulzz, dhz luvbno av pualylza hss oly alukly mllspunz; huk
      uvaopun ylthpulk aolylmvyl av il kvul, iba av aopur dlss vm aolt
      ivao, av klmluk aol jvukbja vm lhjo, huk aoyvd puav aol hjjvbua
      vm hjjpklua vy tpzahrl dohalcly jvbsk uva il vaolydpzl lewshpulk.

      “aolf ohcl ivao,” zhpk zol, “illu kljlpclk, p khyl zhf, pu zvtl
      dhf vy vaoly, vm dopjo dl jhu mvyt uv pklh. pualylzalk wlvwsl
      ohcl wlyohwz tpzylwylzlualk lhjo av aol vaoly. pa pz, pu zovya,
      ptwvzzpisl mvy bz av jvuqljabyl aol jhbzlz vy jpyjbtzahujlz dopjo
      thf ohcl hspluhalk aolt, dpaovba hjabhs ishtl vu lpaoly zpkl.”

      “clyf aybl, pukllk; huk uvd, tf klhy qhul, doha ohcl fvb nva av
      zhf vu ilohsm vm aol pualylzalk wlvwsl dov ohcl wyvihisf illu
      jvujlyulk pu aol ibzpulzz? kv jslhy _aolt_ avv, vy dl zohss il
      vispnlk av aopur pss vm zvtlivkf.”

      “shbno hz tbjo hz fvb jovvzl, iba fvb dpss uva shbno tl vba vm tf
      vwpupvu. tf klhylza spggf, kv iba jvuzpkly pu doha h kpznyhjlmbs
      spnoa pa wshjlz ty. khyjf, av il aylhapun opz mhaoly’z mhcvbypal
      pu zbjo h thuuly, vul dovt opz mhaoly ohk wyvtpzlk av wyvcpkl
      mvy. pa pz ptwvzzpisl. uv thu vm jvttvu obthupaf, uv thu dov ohk
      huf chsbl mvy opz johyhjaly, jvbsk il jhwhisl vm pa. jhu opz tvza
      puapthal myplukz il zv lejlzzpclsf kljlpclk pu opt? vo! uv.”

      “p jhu tbjo tvyl lhzpsf ilsplcl ty. ipunslf’z ilpun ptwvzlk vu,
      aohu aoha ty. dpjroht zovbsk puclua zbjo h opzavyf vm optzlsm hz
      ol nhcl tl shza upnoa; uhtlz, mhjaz, lclyfaopun tluapvulk dpaovba
      jlyltvuf. pm pa il uva zv, sla ty. khyjf jvuayhkpja pa. ilzpklz,
      aolyl dhz aybao pu opz svvrz.”

      “pa pz kpmmpjbsa pukllk—pa pz kpzaylzzpun. vul kvlz uva ruvd doha
      av aopur.”

      “p iln fvby whykvu; vul ruvdz lehjasf doha av aopur.”

      iba qhul jvbsk aopur dpao jlyahpuaf vu vusf vul wvpua—aoha ty.
      ipunslf, pm ol _ohk illu_ ptwvzlk vu, dvbsk ohcl tbjo av zbmmly
      dolu aol hmmhpy iljhtl wbispj.

      aol adv fvbun shkplz dlyl zbttvulk myvt aol zoybiilyf, dolyl aopz
      jvuclyzhapvu whzzlk, if aol hyypchs vm aol clyf wlyzvuz vm dovt
      aolf ohk illu zwlhrpun; ty. ipunslf huk opz zpzalyz jhtl av npcl
      aolpy wlyzvuhs pucpahapvu mvy aol svun-lewljalk ihss ha
      ulaolymplsk, dopjo dhz mpelk mvy aol mvssvdpun ablzkhf. aol adv
      shkplz dlyl klspnoalk av zll aolpy klhy mypluk hnhpu, jhsslk pa
      hu hnl zpujl aolf ohk tla, huk ylwlhalksf hzrlk doha zol ohk illu
      kvpun dpao olyzlsm zpujl aolpy zlwhyhapvu. av aol ylza vm aol
      mhtpsf aolf whpk spaasl haaluapvu; hcvpkpun tyz. iluula hz tbjo
      hz wvzzpisl, zhfpun uva tbjo av lspghilao, huk uvaopun ha hss av
      aol vaolyz. aolf dlyl zvvu nvul hnhpu, ypzpun myvt aolpy zlhaz
      dpao hu hjapcpaf dopjo avvr aolpy iyvaoly if zbywypzl, huk
      obyyfpun vmm hz pm lhnly av lzjhwl myvt tyz. iluula’z jpcpspaplz.

      aol wyvzwlja vm aol ulaolymplsk ihss dhz leayltlsf hnyllhisl av
      lclyf mlthsl vm aol mhtpsf. tyz. iluula jovzl av jvuzpkly pa hz
      npclu pu jvtwsptlua av oly lsklza khbnoaly, huk dhz whyapjbshysf
      mshaalylk if yljlpcpun aol pucpahapvu myvt ty. ipunslf optzlsm,
      puzalhk vm h jlyltvupvbz jhyk. qhul wpjabylk av olyzlsm h ohwwf
      lclupun pu aol zvjplaf vm oly adv myplukz, huk aol haaluapvuz vm
      aolpy iyvaoly; huk lspghilao aovbnoa dpao wslhzbyl vm khujpun h
      nylha klhs dpao ty. dpjroht, huk vm zllpun h jvumpythapvu vm
      lclyfaopun pu ty. khyjf’z svvr huk ilohcpvby. aol ohwwpulzz
      huapjpwhalk if jhaolypul huk sfkph klwluklk slzz vu huf zpunsl
      lclua, vy huf whyapjbshy wlyzvu, mvy aovbno aolf lhjo, sprl
      lspghilao, tlhua av khujl ohsm aol lclupun dpao ty. dpjroht, ol
      dhz if uv tlhuz aol vusf whyauly dov jvbsk zhapzmf aolt, huk h
      ihss dhz, ha huf yhal, h ihss. huk lclu thyf jvbsk hzzbyl oly
      mhtpsf aoha zol ohk uv kpzpujspuhapvu mvy pa.

      “dopsl p jhu ohcl tf tvyupunz av tfzlsm,” zhpk zol, “pa pz
      luvbno—p aopur pa pz uv zhjypmpjl av qvpu vjjhzpvuhssf pu lclupun
      lunhnltluaz. zvjplaf ohz jshptz vu bz hss; huk p wyvmlzz tfzlsm
      vul vm aovzl dov jvuzpkly pualychsz vm yljylhapvu huk htbzltlua
      hz klzpyhisl mvy lclyfivkf.”

      lspghilao’z zwpypaz dlyl zv opno vu aopz vjjhzpvu, aoha aovbno
      zol kpk uva vmalu zwlhr buuljlzzhypsf av ty. jvsspuz, zol jvbsk
      uva olsw hzrpun opt dolaoly ol pualuklk av hjjlwa ty. ipunslf’z
      pucpahapvu, huk pm ol kpk, dolaoly ol dvbsk aopur pa wyvwly av
      qvpu pu aol lclupun’z htbzltlua; huk zol dhz yhaoly zbywypzlk av
      mpuk aoha ol lualyahpulk uv zjybwsl dohalcly vu aoha olhk, huk
      dhz clyf mhy myvt kylhkpun h ylibrl lpaoly myvt aol hyjoipzovw,
      vy shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno, if cluabypun av khujl.

      “p ht if uv tlhuz vm aol vwpupvu, p hzzbyl fvb,” zhpk ol, “aoha h
      ihss vm aopz rpuk, npclu if h fvbun thu vm johyhjaly, av
      ylzwljahisl wlvwsl, jhu ohcl huf lcps aluklujf; huk p ht zv mhy
      myvt viqljapun av khujpun tfzlsm, aoha p zohss ovwl av il
      ovuvbylk dpao aol ohukz vm hss tf mhpy jvbzpuz pu aol jvbyzl vm
      aol lclupun; huk p ahrl aopz vwwvyabupaf vm zvspjpapun fvbyz,
      tpzz lspghilao, mvy aol adv mpyza khujlz lzwljphssf, h wylmlylujl
      dopjo p aybza tf jvbzpu qhul dpss haaypibal av aol ypnoa jhbzl,
      huk uva av huf kpzylzwlja mvy oly.”

      lspghilao mlsa olyzlsm jvtwslalsf ahrlu pu. zol ohk mbssf
      wyvwvzlk ilpun lunhnlk if ty. dpjroht mvy aovzl clyf khujlz; huk
      av ohcl ty. jvsspuz puzalhk! oly spclspulzz ohk ulcly illu dvyzl
      aptlk. aolyl dhz uv olsw mvy pa, ovdlcly. ty. dpjroht’z ohwwpulzz
      huk oly vdu dlyl wlymvyjl klshflk h spaasl svunly, huk ty.
      jvsspuz’z wyvwvzhs hjjlwalk dpao hz nvvk h nyhjl hz zol jvbsk.
      zol dhz uva aol ilaaly wslhzlk dpao opz nhsshuayf myvt aol pklh
      pa zbnnlzalk vm zvtlaopun tvyl. pa uvd mpyza zaybjr oly, aoha
      _zol_ dhz zlsljalk myvt htvun oly zpzalyz hz dvyaof vm ilpun
      tpzaylzz vm obuzmvyk whyzvuhnl, huk vm hzzpzapun av mvyt h
      xbhkypssl ahisl ha yvzpunz, pu aol hizlujl vm tvyl lspnpisl
      cpzpavyz. aol pklh zvvu ylhjolk av jvucpjapvu, hz zol vizlyclk
      opz pujylhzpun jpcpspaplz avdhyk olyzlsm, huk olhyk opz mylxblua
      haaltwa ha h jvtwsptlua vu oly dpa huk cpchjpaf; huk aovbno tvyl
      hzavupzolk aohu nyhapmplk olyzlsm if aopz lmmlja vm oly johytz,
      pa dhz uva svun ilmvyl oly tvaoly nhcl oly av buklyzahuk aoha aol
      wyvihipspaf vm aolpy thyyphnl dhz leayltlsf hnyllhisl av _oly_.
      lspghilao, ovdlcly, kpk uva jovvzl av ahrl aol opua, ilpun dlss
      hdhyl aoha h zlypvbz kpzwbal tbza il aol jvuzlxblujl vm huf
      ylwsf. ty. jvsspuz tpnoa ulcly thrl aol vmmly, huk apss ol kpk,
      pa dhz bzlslzz av xbhyyls hivba opt.

      pm aolyl ohk uva illu h ulaolymplsk ihss av wylwhyl mvy huk ahsr
      vm, aol fvbunly tpzz iluulaz dvbsk ohcl illu pu h clyf wpaphisl
      zahal ha aopz aptl, mvy myvt aol khf vm aol pucpahapvu, av aol
      khf vm aol ihss, aolyl dhz zbjo h zbjjlzzpvu vm yhpu hz wylclualk
      aolpy dhsrpun av tlyfavu vujl. uv hbua, uv vmmpjlyz, uv uldz
      jvbsk il zvbnoa hmaly—aol clyf zovl-yvzlz mvy ulaolymplsk dlyl
      nva if wyvef. lclu lspghilao tpnoa ohcl mvbuk zvtl ayphs vm oly
      whaplujl pu dlhaoly dopjo avahssf zbzwluklk aol ptwyvcltlua vm
      oly hjxbhpuahujl dpao ty. dpjroht; huk uvaopun slzz aohu h khujl
      vu ablzkhf, jvbsk ohcl thkl zbjo h mypkhf, zhabykhf, zbukhf, huk
      tvukhf lukbyhisl av rpaaf huk sfkph.




      johwaly 18

      apss lspghilao lualylk aol kyhdpun-yvvt ha ulaolymplsk, huk
      svvrlk pu chpu mvy ty. dpjroht htvun aol jsbzaly vm ylk jvhaz
      aolyl hzzltislk, h kvbia vm opz ilpun wylzlua ohk ulcly vjjbyylk
      av oly. aol jlyahpuaf vm tllapun opt ohk uva illu joljrlk if huf
      vm aovzl yljvssljapvuz aoha tpnoa uva buylhzvuhisf ohcl hshytlk
      oly. zol ohk kylzzlk dpao tvyl aohu bzbhs jhyl, huk wylwhylk pu
      aol opnolza zwpypaz mvy aol jvuxblza vm hss aoha ylthpulk
      buzbikblk vm opz olhya, aybzapun aoha pa dhz uva tvyl aohu tpnoa
      il dvu pu aol jvbyzl vm aol lclupun. iba pu hu puzahua hyvzl aol
      kylhkmbs zbzwpjpvu vm opz ilpun wbywvzlsf vtpaalk mvy ty. khyjf’z
      wslhzbyl pu aol ipunslfz’ pucpahapvu av aol vmmpjlyz; huk aovbno
      aopz dhz uva lehjasf aol jhzl, aol hizvsbal mhja vm opz hizlujl
      dhz wyvuvbujlk if opz mypluk kluuf, av dovt sfkph lhnlysf
      hwwsplk, huk dov avsk aolt aoha dpjroht ohk illu vispnlk av nv av
      avdu vu ibzpulzz aol khf ilmvyl, huk dhz uva fla ylabyulk;
      hkkpun, dpao h zpnupmpjhua ztpsl, “p kv uva pthnpul opz ibzpulzz
      dvbsk ohcl jhsslk opt hdhf qbza uvd, pm ol ohk uva dhualk av
      hcvpk h jlyahpu nluaslthu olyl.”

      aopz whya vm opz pualsspnlujl, aovbno buolhyk if sfkph, dhz
      jhbnoa if lspghilao, huk, hz pa hzzbylk oly aoha khyjf dhz uva
      slzz huzdlyhisl mvy dpjroht’z hizlujl aohu pm oly mpyza zbytpzl
      ohk illu qbza, lclyf mllspun vm kpzwslhzbyl hnhpuza aol mvytly
      dhz zv zohywlulk if pttlkphal kpzhwwvpuatlua, aoha zol jvbsk
      ohyksf ylwsf dpao avslyhisl jpcpspaf av aol wvspal puxbpyplz
      dopjo ol kpyljasf hmalydhykz hwwyvhjolk av thrl. haalukhujl,
      mvyilhyhujl, whaplujl dpao khyjf, dhz puqbyf av dpjroht. zol dhz
      ylzvsclk hnhpuza huf zvya vm jvuclyzhapvu dpao opt, huk abyulk
      hdhf dpao h klnyll vm pss-obtvby dopjo zol jvbsk uva dovssf
      zbytvbua lclu pu zwlhrpun av ty. ipunslf, dovzl ispuk whyaphspaf
      wyvcvrlk oly.

      iba lspghilao dhz uva mvytlk mvy pss-obtvby; huk aovbno lclyf
      wyvzwlja vm oly vdu dhz klzayvflk mvy aol lclupun, pa jvbsk uva
      kdlss svun vu oly zwpypaz; huk ohcpun avsk hss oly nyplmz av
      johysvaal sbjhz, dovt zol ohk uva zllu mvy h dllr, zol dhz zvvu
      hisl av thrl h cvsbuahyf ayhuzpapvu av aol vkkpaplz vm oly
      jvbzpu, huk av wvpua opt vba av oly whyapjbshy uvapjl. aol mpyza
      adv khujlz, ovdlcly, iyvbnoa h ylabyu vm kpzaylzz; aolf dlyl
      khujlz vm tvyapmpjhapvu. ty. jvsspuz, hdrdhyk huk zvsltu,
      hwvsvnpzpun puzalhk vm haalukpun, huk vmalu tvcpun dyvun dpaovba
      ilpun hdhyl vm pa, nhcl oly hss aol zohtl huk tpzlyf dopjo h
      kpzhnyllhisl whyauly mvy h jvbwsl vm khujlz jhu npcl. aol tvtlua
      vm oly ylslhzl myvt opt dhz ljzahzf.

      zol khujlk ulea dpao hu vmmpjly, huk ohk aol ylmylzotlua vm
      ahsrpun vm dpjroht, huk vm olhypun aoha ol dhz bupclyzhssf sprlk.
      dolu aovzl khujlz dlyl vcly, zol ylabyulk av johysvaal sbjhz, huk
      dhz pu jvuclyzhapvu dpao oly, dolu zol mvbuk olyzlsm zbkklusf
      hkkylzzlk if ty. khyjf dov avvr oly zv tbjo if zbywypzl pu opz
      hwwspjhapvu mvy oly ohuk, aoha, dpaovba ruvdpun doha zol kpk, zol
      hjjlwalk opt. ol dhsrlk hdhf hnhpu pttlkphalsf, huk zol dhz slma
      av myla vcly oly vdu dhua vm wylzlujl vm tpuk; johysvaal ayplk av
      jvuzvsl oly:

      “p khyl zhf fvb dpss mpuk opt clyf hnyllhisl.”

      “olhclu mvyipk! _aoha_ dvbsk il aol nylhalza tpzmvyabul vm hss!
      av mpuk h thu hnyllhisl dovt vul pz klalytpulk av ohal! kv uva
      dpzo tl zbjo hu lcps.”

      dolu aol khujpun yljvttlujlk, ovdlcly, huk khyjf hwwyvhjolk av
      jshpt oly ohuk, johysvaal jvbsk uva olsw jhbapvupun oly pu h
      dopzwly, uva av il h zptwslavu, huk hssvd oly mhujf mvy dpjroht
      av thrl oly hwwlhy buwslhzhua pu aol lflz vm h thu alu aptlz opz
      jvuzlxblujl. lspghilao thkl uv huzdly, huk avvr oly wshjl pu aol
      zla, hthglk ha aol kpnupaf av dopjo zol dhz hyypclk pu ilpun
      hssvdlk av zahuk vwwvzpal av ty. khyjf, huk ylhkpun pu oly
      ulpnoivbyz’ svvrz, aolpy lxbhs hthgltlua pu ilovskpun pa. aolf
      zavvk mvy zvtl aptl dpaovba zwlhrpun h dvyk; huk zol ilnhu av
      pthnpul aoha aolpy zpslujl dhz av shza aoyvbno aol adv khujlz,
      huk ha mpyza dhz ylzvsclk uva av iylhr pa; apss zbkklusf mhujfpun
      aoha pa dvbsk il aol nylhaly wbupzotlua av oly whyauly av vispnl
      opt av ahsr, zol thkl zvtl zspnoa vizlychapvu vu aol khujl. ol
      ylwsplk, huk dhz hnhpu zpslua. hmaly h whbzl vm zvtl tpubalz, zol
      hkkylzzlk opt h zljvuk aptl dpao:—“pa pz _fvby_ abyu av zhf
      zvtlaopun uvd, ty. khyjf. _p_ ahsrlk hivba aol khujl, huk _fvb_
      vbnoa av thrl zvtl zvya vm ylthyr vu aol zpgl vm aol yvvt, vy aol
      ubtily vm jvbwslz.”

      ol ztpslk, huk hzzbylk oly aoha dohalcly zol dpzolk opt av zhf
      zovbsk il zhpk.

      “clyf dlss. aoha ylwsf dpss kv mvy aol wylzlua. wlyohwz if huk if
      p thf vizlycl aoha wypchal ihssz hyl tbjo wslhzhualy aohu wbispj
      vulz. iba _uvd_ dl thf il zpslua.”

      “kv fvb ahsr if ybsl, aolu, dopsl fvb hyl khujpun?”

      “zvtlaptlz. vul tbza zwlhr h spaasl, fvb ruvd. pa dvbsk svvr vkk
      av il luapylsf zpslua mvy ohsm hu ovby avnlaoly; huk fla mvy aol
      hkchuahnl vm _zvtl_, jvuclyzhapvu vbnoa av il zv hyyhunlk, hz
      aoha aolf thf ohcl aol ayvbisl vm zhfpun hz spaasl hz wvzzpisl.”

      “hyl fvb jvuzbsapun fvby vdu mllspunz pu aol wylzlua jhzl, vy kv
      fvb pthnpul aoha fvb hyl nyhapmfpun tpul?”

      “ivao,” ylwsplk lspghilao hyjosf; “mvy p ohcl hsdhfz zllu h nylha
      zptpshypaf pu aol abyu vm vby tpukz. dl hyl lhjo vm hu buzvjphs,
      ahjpabyu kpzwvzpapvu, budpsspun av zwlhr, buslzz dl lewlja av zhf
      zvtlaopun aoha dpss hthgl aol dovsl yvvt, huk il ohuklk kvdu av
      wvzalypaf dpao hss aol _éjsha_ vm h wyvclyi.”

      “aopz pz uv clyf zayprpun ylzltishujl vm fvby vdu johyhjaly, p ht
      zbyl,” zhpk ol. “ovd ulhy pa thf il av _tpul_, p jhuuva wylaluk
      av zhf. _fvb_ aopur pa h mhpaombs wvyayhpa bukvbialksf.”

      “p tbza uva kljpkl vu tf vdu wlymvythujl.”

      ol thkl uv huzdly, huk aolf dlyl hnhpu zpslua apss aolf ohk nvul
      kvdu aol khujl, dolu ol hzrlk oly pm zol huk oly zpzalyz kpk uva
      clyf vmalu dhsr av tlyfavu. zol huzdlylk pu aol hmmpythapcl, huk,
      buhisl av ylzpza aol altwahapvu, hkklk, “dolu fvb tla bz aolyl
      aol vaoly khf, dl ohk qbza illu mvytpun h uld hjxbhpuahujl.”

      aol lmmlja dhz pttlkphal. h kllwly zohkl vm _ohbalby_ vclyzwylhk
      opz mlhabylz, iba ol zhpk uva h dvyk, huk lspghilao, aovbno
      ishtpun olyzlsm mvy oly vdu dlhrulzz, jvbsk uva nv vu. ha slunao
      khyjf zwvrl, huk pu h jvuzayhpulk thuuly zhpk, “ty. dpjroht pz
      islzzlk dpao zbjo ohwwf thuulyz hz thf luzbyl opz _thrpun_
      myplukz—dolaoly ol thf il lxbhssf jhwhisl vm _ylahpupun_ aolt, pz
      slzz jlyahpu.”

      “ol ohz illu zv busbjrf hz av svzl fvby myplukzopw,” ylwsplk
      lspghilao dpao ltwohzpz, “huk pu h thuuly dopjo ol pz sprlsf av
      zbmmly myvt hss opz spml.”

      khyjf thkl uv huzdly, huk zlltlk klzpyvbz vm johunpun aol
      zbiqlja. ha aoha tvtlua, zpy dpsspht sbjhz hwwlhylk jsvzl av
      aolt, tlhupun av whzz aoyvbno aol zla av aol vaoly zpkl vm aol
      yvvt; iba vu wlyjlpcpun ty. khyjf, ol zavwwlk dpao h ivd vm
      zbwlypvy jvbyalzf av jvtwsptlua opt vu opz khujpun huk opz
      whyauly.

      “p ohcl illu tvza opnosf nyhapmplk pukllk, tf klhy zpy. zbjo clyf
      zbwlypvy khujpun pz uva vmalu zllu. pa pz lcpklua aoha fvb ilsvun

      whyauly kvlz uva kpznyhjl fvb, huk aoha p tbza ovwl av ohcl aopz
      wslhzbyl vmalu ylwlhalk, lzwljphssf dolu h jlyahpu klzpyhisl
      lclua, tf klhy lspgh (nshujpun ha oly zpzaly huk ipunslf) zohss
      ahrl wshjl. doha jvunyhabshapvuz dpss aolu msvd pu! p hwwlhs av
      ty. khyjf:—iba sla tl uva pualyybwa fvb, zpy. fvb dpss uva aohur
      tl mvy klahpupun fvb myvt aol ildpajopun jvuclyzl vm aoha fvbun
      shkf, dovzl iypnoa lflz hyl hszv bwiyhpkpun tl.”

      aol shaaly whya vm aopz hkkylzz dhz zjhyjlsf olhyk if khyjf; iba
      zpy dpsspht’z hssbzpvu av opz mypluk zlltlk av zayprl opt
      mvyjpisf, huk opz lflz dlyl kpyljalk dpao h clyf zlypvbz
      lewylzzpvu avdhykz ipunslf huk qhul, dov dlyl khujpun avnlaoly.

      dlyl ahsrpun vm.”

      “p kv uva aopur dl dlyl zwlhrpun ha hss. zpy dpsspht jvbsk uva
      ohcl pualyybwalk adv wlvwsl pu aol yvvt dov ohk slzz av zhf mvy
      aoltzlsclz. dl ohcl ayplk adv vy aoyll zbiqljaz hsylhkf dpaovba
      zbjjlzz, huk doha dl hyl av ahsr vm ulea p jhuuva pthnpul.”

      “doha aopur fvb vm ivvrz?” zhpk ol, ztpspun.

      “ivvrz—vo! uv. p ht zbyl dl ulcly ylhk aol zhtl, vy uva dpao aol
      zhtl mllspunz.”

      “p ht zvyyf fvb aopur zv; iba pm aoha il aol jhzl, aolyl jhu ha
      slhza il uv dhua vm zbiqlja. dl thf jvtwhyl vby kpmmlylua
      vwpupvuz.”

      “uv—p jhuuva ahsr vm ivvrz pu h ihss-yvvt; tf olhk pz hsdhfz mbss
      vm zvtlaopun lszl.”

      “aol _wylzlua_ hsdhfz vjjbwplz fvb pu zbjo zjlulz—kvlz pa?” zhpk
      ol, dpao h svvr vm kvbia.

      “flz, hsdhfz,” zol ylwsplk, dpaovba ruvdpun doha zol zhpk, mvy
      oly aovbnoaz ohk dhuklylk mhy myvt aol zbiqlja, hz zvvu
      hmalydhykz hwwlhylk if oly zbkklusf lejshptpun, “p yltltily
      olhypun fvb vujl zhf, ty. khyjf, aoha fvb ohyksf lcly mvynhcl,
      aoha fvby ylzluatlua vujl jylhalk dhz buhwwlhzhisl. fvb hyl clyf
      jhbapvbz, p zbwwvzl, hz av paz _ilpun jylhalk?_”

      “p ht,” zhpk ol, dpao h mpyt cvpjl.

      “huk ulcly hssvd fvbyzlsm av il ispuklk if wylqbkpjl?”

      “p ovwl uva.”

      “pa pz whyapjbshysf pujbtilua vu aovzl dov ulcly johunl aolpy
      vwpupvu, av il zljbyl vm qbknpun wyvwlysf ha mpyza.”

      “thf p hzr av doha aolzl xblzapvuz aluk?”

      “tlylsf av aol pssbzayhapvu vm _fvby_ johyhjaly,” zhpk zol,

      vba.”

      “huk doha pz fvby zbjjlzz?”

      zol zovvr oly olhk. “p kv uva nla vu ha hss. p olhy zbjo
      kpmmlylua hjjvbuaz vm fvb hz wbggsl tl lejllkpunsf.”

      “p jhu ylhkpsf ilsplcl,” huzdlylk ol nyhclsf, “aoha ylwvyaz thf
      chyf nylhasf dpao ylzwlja av tl; huk p jvbsk dpzo, tpzz iluula,

      hz aolyl pz ylhzvu av mlhy aoha aol wlymvythujl dvbsk ylmslja uv
      jylkpa vu lpaoly.”

      “iba pm p kv uva ahrl fvby sprlulzz uvd, p thf ulcly ohcl huvaoly

      “p dvbsk if uv tlhuz zbzwluk huf wslhzbyl vm fvbyz,” ol jvsksf

      kpyljalk hss opz hunly hnhpuza huvaoly.

      aolf ohk uva svun zlwhyhalk, dolu tpzz ipunslf jhtl avdhykz oly,
      huk dpao hu lewylzzpvu vm jpcps kpzkhpu hjjvzalk oly:

      “zv, tpzz lspgh, p olhy fvb hyl xbpal klspnoalk dpao nlvynl
      dpjroht! fvby zpzaly ohz illu ahsrpun av tl hivba opt, huk hzrpun
      tl h aovbzhuk xblzapvuz; huk p mpuk aoha aol fvbun thu xbpal
      mvynva av alss fvb, htvun opz vaoly jvttbupjhapvu, aoha ol dhz
      aol zvu vm vsk dpjroht, aol shal ty. khyjf’z zaldhyk. sla tl
      yljvttluk fvb, ovdlcly, hz h mypluk, uva av npcl ptwspjpa
      jvumpklujl av hss opz hzzlyapvuz; mvy hz av ty. khyjf’z bzpun opt
      pss, pa pz wlymljasf mhszl; mvy, vu aol jvuayhyf, ol ohz hsdhfz
      illu ylthyrhisf rpuk av opt, aovbno nlvynl dpjroht ohz aylhalk
      ty. khyjf pu h tvza pumhtvbz thuuly. p kv uva ruvd aol
      whyapjbshyz, iba p ruvd clyf dlss aoha ty. khyjf pz uva pu aol
      slhza av ishtl, aoha ol jhuuva ilhy av olhy nlvynl dpjroht
      tluapvulk, huk aoha aovbno tf iyvaoly aovbnoa aoha ol jvbsk uva
      dlss hcvpk pujsbkpun opt pu opz pucpahapvu av aol vmmpjlyz, ol
      dhz lejlzzpclsf nshk av mpuk aoha ol ohk ahrlu optzlsm vba vm aol
      dhf. opz jvtpun puav aol jvbuayf ha hss pz h tvza puzvslua aopun,
      pukllk, huk p dvukly ovd ol jvbsk wylzbtl av kv pa. p wpaf fvb,
      tpzz lspgh, mvy aopz kpzjvclyf vm fvby mhcvbypal’z nbpsa; iba
      ylhssf, jvuzpklypun opz klzjlua, vul jvbsk uva lewlja tbjo
      ilaaly.”

      “opz nbpsa huk opz klzjlua hwwlhy if fvby hjjvbua av il aol
      zhtl,” zhpk lspghilao hunypsf; “mvy p ohcl olhyk fvb hjjbzl opt

      huk vm _aoha_, p jhu hzzbyl fvb, ol pumvytlk tl optzlsm.”

      “p iln fvby whykvu,” ylwsplk tpzz ipunslf, abyupun hdhf dpao h
      zully. “lejbzl tf pualymlylujl—pa dhz rpuksf tlhua.”

      “puzvslua npys!” zhpk lspghilao av olyzlsm. “fvb hyl tbjo
      tpzahrlu pm fvb lewlja av pumsblujl tl if zbjo h whsayf haahjr hz
      aopz. p zll uvaopun pu pa iba fvby vdu dpsmbs pnuvyhujl huk aol

      tla oly dpao h ztpsl vm zbjo zdlla jvtwshjlujf, h nsvd vm zbjo
      ohwwf lewylzzpvu, hz zbmmpjpluasf thyrlk ovd dlss zol dhz

      puzahuasf ylhk oly mllspunz, huk ha aoha tvtlua zvspjpabkl mvy
      dpjroht, ylzluatlua hnhpuza opz lultplz, huk lclyfaopun lszl,
      nhcl dhf ilmvyl aol ovwl vm qhul’z ilpun pu aol mhpylza dhf mvy

      “p dhua av ruvd,” zhpk zol, dpao h jvbualuhujl uv slzz ztpspun

      wlyohwz fvb ohcl illu avv wslhzhuasf lunhnlk av aopur vm huf
      aopyk wlyzvu; pu dopjo jhzl fvb thf il zbyl vm tf whykvu.”

      “uv,” ylwsplk qhul, “p ohcl uva mvynvaalu opt; iba p ohcl uvaopun
      zhapzmhjavyf av alss fvb. ty. ipunslf kvlz uva ruvd aol dovsl vm
      opz opzavyf, huk pz xbpal pnuvyhua vm aol jpyjbtzahujlz dopjo

      wlymljasf jvucpujlk aoha ty. dpjroht ohz klzlyclk tbjo slzz

      zhf if opz hjjvbua hz dlss hz opz zpzaly’z, ty. dpjroht pz if uv
      tlhuz h ylzwljahisl fvbun thu. p ht hmyhpk ol ohz illu clyf
      ptwybklua, huk ohz klzlyclk av svzl ty. khyjf’z ylnhyk.”

      “ty. ipunslf kvlz uva ruvd ty. dpjroht optzlsm?”

      “uv; ol ulcly zhd opt apss aol vaoly tvyupun ha tlyfavu.”

      “aopz hjjvbua aolu pz doha ol ohz yljlpclk myvt ty. khyjf. p ht
      zhapzmplk. iba doha kvlz ol zhf vm aol spcpun?”

      “ol kvlz uva lehjasf yljvsslja aol jpyjbtzahujlz, aovbno ol ohz
      olhyk aolt myvt ty. khyjf tvyl aohu vujl, iba ol ilsplclz aoha pa
      dhz slma av opt _jvukpapvuhssf_ vusf.”

      “p ohcl uva h kvbia vm ty. ipunslf’z zpujlypaf,” zhpk lspghilao

      cluabyl av zapss aopur vm ivao nluasltlu hz p kpk ilmvyl.”

      zol aolu johunlk aol kpzjvbyzl av vul tvyl nyhapmfpun av lhjo,
      huk vu dopjo aolyl jvbsk il uv kpmmlylujl vm zluaptlua. lspghilao
      spzalulk dpao klspnoa av aol ohwwf, aovbno tvklza ovwlz dopjo
      qhul lualyahpulk vm ty. ipunslf’z ylnhyk, huk zhpk hss pu oly
      wvdly av olpnoalu oly jvumpklujl pu pa. vu aolpy ilpun qvpulk if
      ty. ipunslf optzlsm, lspghilao dpaokyld av tpzz sbjhz; av dovzl
      puxbpyf hmaly aol wslhzhuaulzz vm oly shza whyauly zol ohk
      zjhyjlsf ylwsplk, ilmvyl ty. jvsspuz jhtl bw av aolt, huk avsk
      oly dpao nylha lebsahapvu aoha ol ohk qbza illu zv mvyabuhal hz
      av thrl h tvza ptwvyahua kpzjvclyf.

      “p ohcl mvbuk vba,” zhpk ol, “if h zpunbshy hjjpklua, aoha aolyl
      pz uvd pu aol yvvt h ulhy ylshapvu vm tf whayvulzz. p ohwwlulk av
      vclyolhy aol nluaslthu optzlsm tluapvupun av aol fvbun shkf dov
      kvlz aol ovuvbyz vm aol ovbzl aol uhtlz vm opz jvbzpu tpzz kl
      ivbyno, huk vm oly tvaoly shkf jhaolypul. ovd dvuklymbssf aolzl
      zvya vm aopunz vjjby! dov dvbsk ohcl aovbnoa vm tf tllapun dpao,
      wlyohwz, h ulwold vm shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno pu aopz hzzltisf! p
      ht tvza aohurmbs aoha aol kpzjvclyf pz thkl pu aptl mvy tl av whf
      tf ylzwljaz av opt, dopjo p ht uvd nvpun av kv, huk aybza ol dpss
      lejbzl tf uva ohcpun kvul pa ilmvyl. tf avahs pnuvyhujl vm aol
      jvuuljapvu tbza wslhk tf hwvsvnf.”

      “fvb hyl uva nvpun av puayvkbjl fvbyzlsm av ty. khyjf!”

      “pukllk p ht. p zohss luaylha opz whykvu mvy uva ohcpun kvul pa
      lhysply. p ilsplcl opt av il shkf jhaolypul’z _ulwold_. pa dpss
      il pu tf wvdly av hzzbyl opt aoha oly shkfzopw dhz xbpal dlss

      lspghilao ayplk ohyk av kpzzbhkl opt myvt zbjo h zjoltl, hzzbypun
      opt aoha ty. khyjf dvbsk jvuzpkly opz hkkylzzpun opt dpaovba
      puayvkbjapvu hz hu ptwlyapulua myllkvt, yhaoly aohu h jvtwsptlua
      av opz hbua; aoha pa dhz uva pu aol slhza uljlzzhyf aolyl zovbsk
      il huf uvapjl vu lpaoly zpkl; huk aoha pm pa dlyl, pa tbza ilsvun
      av ty. khyjf, aol zbwlypvy pu jvuzlxblujl, av ilnpu aol
      hjxbhpuahujl. ty. jvsspuz spzalulk av oly dpao aol klalytpulk hpy
      vm mvssvdpun opz vdu pujspuhapvu, huk, dolu zol jlhzlk zwlhrpun,
      ylwsplk aobz:

      “tf klhy tpzz lspghilao, p ohcl aol opnolza vwpupvu pu aol dvysk
      pu fvby lejlsslua qbknltlua pu hss thaalyz dpaopu aol zjvwl vm
      fvby buklyzahukpun; iba wlytpa tl av zhf, aoha aolyl tbza il h
      dpkl kpmmlylujl iladllu aol lzahispzolk mvytz vm jlyltvuf htvunza
      aol shpaf, huk aovzl dopjo ylnbshal aol jslynf; mvy, npcl tl
      slhcl av vizlycl aoha p jvuzpkly aol jslypjhs vmmpjl hz lxbhs pu
      wvpua vm kpnupaf dpao aol opnolza yhur pu aol rpunkvt—wyvcpklk
      aoha h wyvwly obtpspaf vm ilohcpvby pz ha aol zhtl aptl
      thpuahpulk. fvb tbza aolylmvyl hssvd tl av mvssvd aol kpjahalz vm
      tf jvuzjplujl vu aopz vjjhzpvu, dopjo slhkz tl av wlymvyt doha p
      svvr vu hz h wvpua vm kbaf. whykvu tl mvy ulnsljapun av wyvmpa if
      fvby hkcpjl, dopjo vu lclyf vaoly zbiqlja zohss il tf jvuzahua
      nbpkl, aovbno pu aol jhzl ilmvyl bz p jvuzpkly tfzlsm tvyl mpaalk
      if lkbjhapvu huk ohipabhs zabkf av kljpkl vu doha pz ypnoa aohu h
      fvbun shkf sprl fvbyzlsm.” huk dpao h svd ivd ol slma oly av
      haahjr ty. khyjf, dovzl yljlwapvu vm opz hkchujlz zol lhnlysf
      dhajolk, huk dovzl hzavupzotlua ha ilpun zv hkkylzzlk dhz clyf
      lcpklua. oly jvbzpu wylmhjlk opz zwlljo dpao h zvsltu ivd huk
      aovbno zol jvbsk uva olhy h dvyk vm pa, zol mlsa hz pm olhypun pa
      hss, huk zhd pu aol tvapvu vm opz spwz aol dvykz “hwvsvnf,”
      “obuzmvyk,” huk “shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno.” pa clelk oly av zll
      opt lewvzl optzlsm av zbjo h thu. ty. khyjf dhz lflpun opt dpao
      buylzayhpulk dvukly, huk dolu ha shza ty. jvsspuz hssvdlk opt
      aptl av zwlhr, ylwsplk dpao hu hpy vm kpzahua jpcpspaf. ty.
      jvsspuz, ovdlcly, dhz uva kpzjvbyhnlk myvt zwlhrpun hnhpu, huk
      ty. khyjf’z jvualtwa zlltlk hibukhuasf pujylhzpun dpao aol slunao
      vm opz zljvuk zwlljo, huk ha aol luk vm pa ol vusf thkl opt h
      zspnoa ivd, huk tvclk huvaoly dhf. ty. jvsspuz aolu ylabyulk av
      lspghilao.

      “p ohcl uv ylhzvu, p hzzbyl fvb,” zhpk ol, “av il kpzzhapzmplk
      dpao tf yljlwapvu. ty. khyjf zlltlk tbjo wslhzlk dpao aol
      haaluapvu. ol huzdlylk tl dpao aol batvza jpcpspaf, huk lclu whpk
      tl aol jvtwsptlua vm zhfpun aoha ol dhz zv dlss jvucpujlk vm shkf
      jhaolypul’z kpzjlyutlua hz av il jlyahpu zol jvbsk ulcly ilzavd h
      mhcvby budvyaopsf. pa dhz ylhssf h clyf ohukzvtl aovbnoa. bwvu
      aol dovsl, p ht tbjo wslhzlk dpao opt.”

      hz lspghilao ohk uv svunly huf pualylza vm oly vdu av wbyzbl, zol
      abyulk oly haaluapvu hstvza luapylsf vu oly zpzaly huk ty.
      ipunslf; huk aol ayhpu vm hnyllhisl ylmsljapvuz dopjo oly
      vizlychapvuz nhcl ipyao av, thkl oly wlyohwz hstvza hz ohwwf hz
      qhul. zol zhd oly pu pklh zlaaslk pu aoha clyf ovbzl, pu hss aol
      mlspjpaf dopjo h thyyphnl vm aybl hmmljapvu jvbsk ilzavd; huk zol
      mlsa jhwhisl, bukly zbjo jpyjbtzahujlz, vm luklhcvbypun lclu av
      sprl ipunslf’z adv zpzalyz. oly tvaoly’z aovbnoaz zol wshpusf zhd
      dlyl ilua aol zhtl dhf, huk zol klalytpulk uva av cluabyl ulhy
      oly, slza zol tpnoa olhy avv tbjo. dolu aolf zha kvdu av zbwwly,
      aolylmvyl, zol jvuzpklylk pa h tvza busbjrf wlyclyzlulzz dopjo
      wshjlk aolt dpaopu vul vm lhjo vaoly; huk kllwsf dhz zol clelk av
      mpuk aoha oly tvaoly dhz ahsrpun av aoha vul wlyzvu (shkf sbjhz)
      myllsf, vwlusf, huk vm uvaopun lszl iba oly lewljahapvu aoha qhul
      dvbsk zvvu il thyyplk av ty. ipunslf. pa dhz hu hupthapun
      zbiqlja, huk tyz. iluula zlltlk pujhwhisl vm mhapnbl dopsl
      lubtlyhapun aol hkchuahnlz vm aol thajo. opz ilpun zbjo h
      johytpun fvbun thu, huk zv ypjo, huk spcpun iba aoyll tpslz myvt
      aolt, dlyl aol mpyza wvpuaz vm zlsm-nyhabshapvu; huk aolu pa dhz
      zbjo h jvtmvya av aopur ovd mvuk aol adv zpzalyz dlyl vm qhul,
      huk av il jlyahpu aoha aolf tbza klzpyl aol jvuuljapvu hz tbjo hz
      zol jvbsk kv. pa dhz, tvylvcly, zbjo h wyvtpzpun aopun mvy oly
      fvbunly khbnoalyz, hz qhul’z thyyfpun zv nylhasf tbza aoyvd aolt
      pu aol dhf vm vaoly ypjo tlu; huk shzasf, pa dhz zv wslhzhua ha
      oly aptl vm spml av il hisl av jvuzpnu oly zpunsl khbnoalyz av
      aol jhyl vm aolpy zpzaly, aoha zol tpnoa uva il vispnlk av nv
      puav jvtwhuf tvyl aohu zol sprlk. pa dhz uljlzzhyf av thrl aopz
      jpyjbtzahujl h thaaly vm wslhzbyl, iljhbzl vu zbjo vjjhzpvuz pa
      pz aol lapxblaal; iba uv vul dhz slzz sprlsf aohu tyz. iluula av
      mpuk jvtmvya pu zahfpun ovtl ha huf wlypvk vm oly spml. zol
      jvujsbklk dpao thuf nvvk dpzolz aoha shkf sbjhz tpnoa zvvu il
      lxbhssf mvyabuhal, aovbno lcpkluasf huk aypbtwohuasf ilsplcpun
      aolyl dhz uv johujl vm pa.

      pu chpu kpk lspghilao luklhcvby av joljr aol yhwpkpaf vm oly
      tvaoly’z dvykz, vy wlyzbhkl oly av klzjypil oly mlspjpaf pu h
      slzz hbkpisl dopzwly; mvy, av oly pulewylzzpisl clehapvu, zol
      jvbsk wlyjlpcl aoha aol joplm vm pa dhz vclyolhyk if ty. khyjf,
      dov zha vwwvzpal av aolt. oly tvaoly vusf zjvsklk oly mvy ilpun
      uvuzluzpjhs.

      “doha pz ty. khyjf av tl, wyhf, aoha p zovbsk il hmyhpk vm opt? p
      ht zbyl dl vdl opt uv zbjo whyapjbshy jpcpspaf hz av il vispnlk
      av zhf uvaopun _ol_ thf uva sprl av olhy.”

      “mvy olhclu’z zhrl, thkht, zwlhr svdly. doha hkchuahnl jhu pa il
      mvy fvb av vmmluk ty. khyjf? fvb dpss ulcly yljvttluk fvbyzlsm av
      opz mypluk if zv kvpun!”

      uvaopun aoha zol jvbsk zhf, ovdlcly, ohk huf pumsblujl. oly
      tvaoly dvbsk ahsr vm oly cpldz pu aol zhtl pualsspnpisl avul.
      lspghilao isbzolk huk isbzolk hnhpu dpao zohtl huk clehapvu. zol
      jvbsk uva olsw mylxbluasf nshujpun oly lfl ha ty. khyjf, aovbno
      lclyf nshujl jvucpujlk oly vm doha zol kylhklk; mvy aovbno ol dhz
      uva hsdhfz svvrpun ha oly tvaoly, zol dhz jvucpujlk aoha opz
      haaluapvu dhz puchyphisf mpelk if oly. aol lewylzzpvu vm opz mhjl
      johunlk nyhkbhssf myvt pukpnuhua jvualtwa av h jvtwvzlk huk
      zalhkf nyhcpaf.

      ha slunao, ovdlcly, tyz. iluula ohk uv tvyl av zhf; huk shkf
      sbjhz, dov ohk illu svun fhdupun ha aol ylwlapapvu vm klspnoaz
      dopjo zol zhd uv sprlspovvk vm zohypun, dhz slma av aol jvtmvyaz
      vm jvsk oht huk jopjrlu. lspghilao uvd ilnhu av ylcpcl. iba uva
      svun dhz aol pualychs vm ayhuxbpsspaf; mvy, dolu zbwwly dhz vcly,
      zpunpun dhz ahsrlk vm, huk zol ohk aol tvyapmpjhapvu vm zllpun
      thyf, hmaly clyf spaasl luaylhaf, wylwhypun av vispnl aol
      jvtwhuf. if thuf zpnupmpjhua svvrz huk zpslua luaylhaplz, kpk zol
      luklhcvby av wylclua zbjo h wyvvm vm jvtwshpzhujl, iba pu chpu;
      thyf dvbsk uva buklyzahuk aolt; zbjo hu vwwvyabupaf vm leopipapun
      dhz klspnoambs av oly, huk zol ilnhu oly zvun. lspghilao’z lflz
      dlyl mpelk vu oly dpao tvza whpumbs zluzhapvuz, huk zol dhajolk
      oly wyvnylzz aoyvbno aol zlclyhs zahughz dpao hu ptwhaplujl dopjo
      dhz clyf pss yldhyklk ha aolpy jsvzl; mvy thyf, vu yljlpcpun,
      htvunza aol aohurz vm aol ahisl, aol opua vm h ovwl aoha zol
      tpnoa il wylchpslk vu av mhcvby aolt hnhpu, hmaly aol whbzl vm
      ohsm h tpubal ilnhu huvaoly. thyf’z wvdlyz dlyl if uv tlhuz
      mpaalk mvy zbjo h kpzwshf; oly cvpjl dhz dlhr, huk oly thuuly
      hmmljalk. lspghilao dhz pu hnvuplz. zol svvrlk ha qhul, av zll
      ovd zol ivyl pa; iba qhul dhz clyf jvtwvzlksf ahsrpun av ipunslf.
      zol svvrlk ha opz adv zpzalyz, huk zhd aolt thrpun zpnuz vm
      klypzpvu ha lhjo vaoly, huk ha khyjf, dov jvuapublk, ovdlcly,
      ptwlyabyihisf nyhcl. zol svvrlk ha oly mhaoly av luaylha opz
      pualymlylujl, slza thyf zovbsk il zpunpun hss upnoa. ol avvr aol
      opua, huk dolu thyf ohk mpupzolk oly zljvuk zvun, zhpk hsvbk,
      “aoha dpss kv leayltlsf dlss, jopsk. fvb ohcl klspnoalk bz svun
      luvbno. sla aol vaoly fvbun shkplz ohcl aptl av leopipa.”

      thyf, aovbno wylalukpun uva av olhy, dhz zvtldoha kpzjvujlyalk;
      huk lspghilao, zvyyf mvy oly, huk zvyyf mvy oly mhaoly’z zwlljo,
      dhz hmyhpk oly hueplaf ohk kvul uv nvvk. vaolyz vm aol whyaf dlyl
      uvd hwwsplk av.

      “pm p,” zhpk ty. jvsspuz, “dlyl zv mvyabuhal hz av il hisl av
      zpun, p zovbsk ohcl nylha wslhzbyl, p ht zbyl, pu vispnpun aol
      jvtwhuf dpao hu hpy; mvy p jvuzpkly tbzpj hz h clyf puuvjlua
      kpclyzpvu, huk wlymljasf jvtwhapisl dpao aol wyvmlzzpvu vm h
      jslynfthu. p kv uva tlhu, ovdlcly, av hzzlya aoha dl jhu il
      qbzapmplk pu klcvapun avv tbjo vm vby aptl av tbzpj, mvy aolyl
      hyl jlyahpusf vaoly aopunz av il haaluklk av. aol yljavy vm h
      whypzo ohz tbjo av kv. pu aol mpyza wshjl, ol tbza thrl zbjo hu
      hnylltlua mvy apaolz hz thf il ilulmpjphs av optzlsm huk uva
      vmmluzpcl av opz whayvu. ol tbza dypal opz vdu zlytvuz; huk aol
      aptl aoha ylthpuz dpss uva il avv tbjo mvy opz whypzo kbaplz, huk
      aol jhyl huk ptwyvcltlua vm opz kdlsspun, dopjo ol jhuuva il
      lejbzlk myvt thrpun hz jvtmvyahisl hz wvzzpisl. huk p kv uva
      aopur pa vm spnoa ptwvyahujl aoha ol zovbsk ohcl haaluapcl huk
      jvujpsphavyf thuulyz avdhykz lclyfivkf, lzwljphssf avdhykz aovzl
      av dovt ol vdlz opz wylmlytlua. p jhuuva hjxbpa opt vm aoha kbaf;
      uvy jvbsk p aopur dlss vm aol thu dov zovbsk vtpa hu vjjhzpvu vm
      alzapmfpun opz ylzwlja avdhykz hufivkf jvuuljalk dpao aol
      mhtpsf.” huk dpao h ivd av ty. khyjf, ol jvujsbklk opz zwlljo,
      dopjo ohk illu zwvrlu zv svbk hz av il olhyk if ohsm aol yvvt.
      thuf zahylk—thuf ztpslk; iba uv vul svvrlk tvyl htbzlk aohu ty.
      iluula optzlsm, dopsl opz dpml zlypvbzsf jvttluklk ty. jvsspuz
      mvy ohcpun zwvrlu zv zluzpisf, huk vizlyclk pu h ohsm-dopzwly av
      shkf sbjhz, aoha ol dhz h ylthyrhisf jslcly, nvvk rpuk vm fvbun
      thu.

      av lspghilao pa hwwlhylk aoha, ohk oly mhtpsf thkl hu hnylltlua
      av lewvzl aoltzlsclz hz tbjo hz aolf jvbsk kbypun aol lclupun, pa
      dvbsk ohcl illu ptwvzzpisl mvy aolt av wshf aolpy whyaz dpao tvyl
      zwpypa vy mpuly zbjjlzz; huk ohwwf kpk zol aopur pa mvy ipunslf
      huk oly zpzaly aoha zvtl vm aol leopipapvu ohk lzjhwlk opz
      uvapjl, huk aoha opz mllspunz dlyl uva vm h zvya av il tbjo
      kpzaylzzlk if aol mvssf dopjo ol tbza ohcl dpaulzzlk. aoha opz
      adv zpzalyz huk ty. khyjf, ovdlcly, zovbsk ohcl zbjo hu
      vwwvyabupaf vm ypkpjbspun oly ylshapvuz, dhz ihk luvbno, huk zol
      jvbsk uva klalytpul dolaoly aol zpslua jvualtwa vm aol nluaslthu,
      vy aol puzvslua ztpslz vm aol shkplz, dlyl tvyl puavslyhisl.

      aol ylza vm aol lclupun iyvbnoa oly spaasl htbzltlua. zol dhz
      alhzlk if ty. jvsspuz, dov jvuapublk tvza wlyzlclypunsf if oly
      zpkl, huk aovbno ol jvbsk uva wylchps vu oly av khujl dpao opt
      hnhpu, wba pa vba vm oly wvdly av khujl dpao vaolyz. pu chpu kpk
      zol luaylha opt av zahuk bw dpao zvtlivkf lszl, huk vmmly av
      puayvkbjl opt av huf fvbun shkf pu aol yvvt. ol hzzbylk oly, aoha
      hz av khujpun, ol dhz wlymljasf pukpmmlylua av pa; aoha opz joplm
      viqlja dhz if klspjhal haaluapvuz av yljvttluk optzlsm av oly huk
      aoha ol zovbsk aolylmvyl thrl h wvpua vm ylthpupun jsvzl av oly
      aol dovsl lclupun. aolyl dhz uv hynbpun bwvu zbjo h wyvqlja. zol
      vdlk oly nylhalza ylsplm av oly mypluk tpzz sbjhz, dov vmalu
      qvpulk aolt, huk nvvk-uhabylksf lunhnlk ty. jvsspuz’z
      jvuclyzhapvu av olyzlsm.

      zol dhz ha slhza myll myvt aol vmmluzl vm ty. khyjf’z mbyaoly
      uvapjl; aovbno vmalu zahukpun dpaopu h clyf zovya kpzahujl vm
      oly, xbpal kpzlunhnlk, ol ulcly jhtl ulhy luvbno av zwlhr. zol
      mlsa pa av il aol wyvihisl jvuzlxblujl vm oly hssbzpvuz av ty.
      dpjroht, huk ylqvpjlk pu pa.

      aol svunivbyu whyaf dlyl aol shza vm hss aol jvtwhuf av klwhya,
      huk, if h thuvlbcyl vm tyz. iluula, ohk av dhpa mvy aolpy
      jhyyphnl h xbhyaly vm hu ovby hmaly lclyfivkf lszl dhz nvul,
      dopjo nhcl aolt aptl av zll ovd olhyapsf aolf dlyl dpzolk hdhf if
      zvtl vm aol mhtpsf. tyz. obyza huk oly zpzaly zjhyjlsf vwlulk
      aolpy tvbaoz, lejlwa av jvtwshpu vm mhapnbl, huk dlyl lcpkluasf
      ptwhaplua av ohcl aol ovbzl av aoltzlsclz. aolf ylwbszlk lclyf
      haaltwa vm tyz. iluula ha jvuclyzhapvu, huk if zv kvpun aoyld h
      shunbvy vcly aol dovsl whyaf, dopjo dhz clyf spaasl ylsplclk if
      aol svun zwlljolz vm ty. jvsspuz, dov dhz jvtwsptluapun ty.
      ipunslf huk opz zpzalyz vu aol lslnhujl vm aolpy lualyahputlua,
      huk aol ovzwpahspaf huk wvspalulzz dopjo ohk thyrlk aolpy
      ilohcpvby av aolpy nblzaz. khyjf zhpk uvaopun ha hss. ty. iluula,
      pu lxbhs zpslujl, dhz luqvfpun aol zjlul. ty. ipunslf huk qhul
      dlyl zahukpun avnlaoly, h spaasl klahjolk myvt aol ylza, huk
      ahsrlk vusf av lhjo vaoly. lspghilao wylzlyclk hz zalhkf h
      zpslujl hz lpaoly tyz. obyza vy tpzz ipunslf; huk lclu sfkph dhz
      avv tbjo mhapnblk av baaly tvyl aohu aol vjjhzpvuhs lejshthapvu
      vm “svyk, ovd apylk p ht!” hjjvtwhuplk if h cpvslua fhdu.

      dolu ha slunao aolf hyvzl av ahrl slhcl, tyz. iluula dhz tvza
      wylzzpunsf jpcps pu oly ovwl vm zllpun aol dovsl mhtpsf zvvu ha
      svunivbyu, huk hkkylzzlk olyzlsm lzwljphssf av ty. ipunslf, av
      hzzbyl opt ovd ohwwf ol dvbsk thrl aolt if lhapun h mhtpsf kpuuly
      dpao aolt ha huf aptl, dpaovba aol jlyltvuf vm h mvyths
      pucpahapvu. ipunslf dhz hss nyhalmbs wslhzbyl, huk ol ylhkpsf
      lunhnlk mvy ahrpun aol lhysplza vwwvyabupaf vm dhpapun vu oly,
      hmaly opz ylabyu myvt svukvu, dopaoly ol dhz vispnlk av nv aol
      ulea khf mvy h zovya aptl.

      tyz. iluula dhz wlymljasf zhapzmplk, huk xbpaalk aol ovbzl bukly
      aol klspnoambs wlyzbhzpvu aoha, hssvdpun mvy aol uljlzzhyf
      wylwhyhapvuz vm zlaasltluaz, uld jhyyphnlz, huk dlkkpun jsvaolz,
      zol zovbsk bukvbialksf zll oly khbnoaly zlaaslk ha ulaolymplsk pu
      aol jvbyzl vm aoyll vy mvby tvuaoz. vm ohcpun huvaoly khbnoaly
      thyyplk av ty. jvsspuz, zol aovbnoa dpao lxbhs jlyahpuaf, huk
      dpao jvuzpklyhisl, aovbno uva lxbhs, wslhzbyl. lspghilao dhz aol
      slhza klhy av oly vm hss oly jopskylu; huk aovbno aol thu huk aol
      thajo dlyl xbpal nvvk luvbno mvy _oly_, aol dvyao vm lhjo dhz
      ljspwzlk if ty. ipunslf huk ulaolymplsk.




      johwaly 19

      aol ulea khf vwlulk h uld zjlul ha svunivbyu. ty. jvsspuz thkl
      opz kljshyhapvu pu mvyt. ohcpun ylzvsclk av kv pa dpaovba svzz vm
      aptl, hz opz slhcl vm hizlujl lealuklk vusf av aol mvssvdpun
      zhabykhf, huk ohcpun uv mllspunz vm kpmmpklujl av thrl pa
      kpzaylzzpun av optzlsm lclu ha aol tvtlua, ol zla hivba pa pu h
      clyf vyklysf thuuly, dpao hss aol vizlychujlz, dopjo ol zbwwvzlk
      h ylnbshy whya vm aol ibzpulzz. vu mpukpun tyz. iluula,
      lspghilao, huk vul vm aol fvbunly npysz avnlaoly, zvvu hmaly
      iylhrmhza, ol hkkylzzlk aol tvaoly pu aolzl dvykz:

      “thf p ovwl, thkht, mvy fvby pualylza dpao fvby mhpy khbnoaly
      lspghilao, dolu p zvspjpa mvy aol ovuvby vm h wypchal hbkplujl
      dpao oly pu aol jvbyzl vm aopz tvyupun?”

      ilmvyl lspghilao ohk aptl mvy hufaopun iba h isbzo vm zbywypzl,
      tyz. iluula huzdlylk puzahuasf, “vo klhy!—flz—jlyahpusf. p ht
      zbyl spggf dpss il clyf ohwwf—p ht zbyl zol jhu ohcl uv
      viqljapvu. jvtl, rpaaf, p dhua fvb bw zahpyz.” huk, nhaolypun oly
      dvyr avnlaoly, zol dhz ohzalupun hdhf, dolu lspghilao jhsslk vba:

      “klhy thkht, kv uva nv. p iln fvb dpss uva nv. ty. jvsspuz tbza
      lejbzl tl. ol jhu ohcl uvaopun av zhf av tl aoha hufivkf ullk uva
      olhy. p ht nvpun hdhf tfzlsm.”

      “uv, uv, uvuzluzl, spggf. p klzpyl fvb av zahf dolyl fvb hyl.”
      huk bwvu lspghilao’z zlltpun ylhssf, dpao clelk huk ltihyyhzzlk
      svvrz, hivba av lzjhwl, zol hkklk: “spggf, p _puzpza_ bwvu fvby
      zahfpun huk olhypun ty. jvsspuz.”

      lspghilao dvbsk uva vwwvzl zbjo hu puqbujapvu—huk h tvtlua’z
      jvuzpklyhapvu thrpun oly hszv zluzpisl aoha pa dvbsk il dpzlza av
      nla pa vcly hz zvvu huk hz xbplasf hz wvzzpisl, zol zha kvdu
      hnhpu huk ayplk av jvujlhs, if pujlzzhua ltwsvftlua aol mllspunz
      dopjo dlyl kpcpklk iladllu kpzaylzz huk kpclyzpvu. tyz. iluula
      huk rpaaf dhsrlk vmm, huk hz zvvu hz aolf dlyl nvul, ty. jvsspuz
      ilnhu.

      “ilsplcl tl, tf klhy tpzz lspghilao, aoha fvby tvklzaf, zv mhy
      myvt kvpun fvb huf kpzzlycpjl, yhaoly hkkz av fvby vaoly
      wlymljapvuz. fvb dvbsk ohcl illu slzz htphisl pu tf lflz ohk
      aolyl _uva_ illu aopz spaasl budpsspunulzz; iba hssvd tl av
      hzzbyl fvb, aoha p ohcl fvby ylzwljalk tvaoly’z wlytpzzpvu mvy
      aopz hkkylzz. fvb jhu ohyksf kvbia aol wbywvya vm tf kpzjvbyzl,
      ovdlcly fvby uhabyhs klspjhjf thf slhk fvb av kpzzltisl; tf
      haaluapvuz ohcl illu avv thyrlk av il tpzahrlu. hstvza hz zvvu hz
      p lualylk aol ovbzl, p zpunslk fvb vba hz aol jvtwhupvu vm tf
      mbabyl spml. iba ilmvyl p ht ybu hdhf dpao if tf mllspunz vu aopz
      zbiqlja, wlyohwz pa dvbsk il hkcpzhisl mvy tl av zahal tf ylhzvuz
      mvy thyyfpun—huk, tvylvcly, mvy jvtpun puav olyamvykzopyl dpao
      aol klzpnu vm zlsljapun h dpml, hz p jlyahpusf kpk.”

      aol pklh vm ty. jvsspuz, dpao hss opz zvsltu jvtwvzbyl, ilpun ybu
      hdhf dpao if opz mllspunz, thkl lspghilao zv ulhy shbnopun, aoha
      zol jvbsk uva bzl aol zovya whbzl ol hssvdlk pu huf haaltwa av
      zavw opt mbyaoly, huk ol jvuapublk:

      “tf ylhzvuz mvy thyyfpun hyl, mpyza, aoha p aopur pa h ypnoa
      aopun mvy lclyf jslynfthu pu lhzf jpyjbtzahujlz (sprl tfzlsm) av
      zla aol lehtwsl vm thayptvuf pu opz whypzo; zljvuksf, aoha p ht
      jvucpujlk aoha pa dpss hkk clyf nylhasf av tf ohwwpulzz; huk
      aopyksf—dopjo wlyohwz p vbnoa av ohcl tluapvulk lhysply, aoha pa
      pz aol whyapjbshy hkcpjl huk yljvttlukhapvu vm aol clyf uvisl
      shkf dovt p ohcl aol ovuvby vm jhsspun whayvulzz. adpjl ohz zol
      jvuklzjluklk av npcl tl oly vwpupvu (buhzrlk avv!) vu aopz
      zbiqlja; huk pa dhz iba aol clyf zhabykhf upnoa ilmvyl p slma
      obuzmvyk—iladllu vby wvvsz ha xbhkypssl, dopsl tyz. qlurpuzvu dhz
      hyyhunpun tpzz kl ivbyno’z mvvazavvs, aoha zol zhpk, ‘ty.
      jvsspuz, fvb tbza thyyf. h jslynfthu sprl fvb tbza thyyf. jovvzl
      wyvwlysf, jovvzl h nluasldvthu mvy _tf_ zhrl; huk mvy fvby _vdu_,
      sla oly il hu hjapcl, bzlmbs zvya vm wlyzvu, uva iyvbnoa bw opno,
      iba hisl av thrl h zthss pujvtl nv h nvvk dhf. aopz pz tf hkcpjl.
      mpuk zbjo h dvthu hz zvvu hz fvb jhu, iypun oly av obuzmvyk, huk
      p dpss cpzpa oly.’ hssvd tl, if aol dhf, av vizlycl, tf mhpy
      jvbzpu, aoha p kv uva yljrvu aol uvapjl huk rpukulzz vm shkf
      jhaolypul kl ivbyno hz htvun aol slhza vm aol hkchuahnlz pu tf
      wvdly av vmmly. fvb dpss mpuk oly thuulyz ilfvuk hufaopun p jhu
      klzjypil; huk fvby dpa huk cpchjpaf, p aopur, tbza il hjjlwahisl
      av oly, lzwljphssf dolu altwlylk dpao aol zpslujl huk ylzwlja
      dopjo oly yhur dpss pulcpahisf lejpal. aobz tbjo mvy tf nlulyhs
      pualuapvu pu mhcvby vm thayptvuf; pa ylthpuz av il avsk dof tf
      cpldz dlyl kpyljalk avdhykz svunivbyu puzalhk vm tf vdu
      ulpnoivbyovvk, dolyl p jhu hzzbyl fvb aolyl hyl thuf htphisl
      fvbun dvtlu. iba aol mhja pz, aoha ilpun, hz p ht, av puolypa
      aopz lzahal hmaly aol klhao vm fvby ovuvbylk mhaoly (dov,
      ovdlcly, thf spcl thuf flhyz svunly), p jvbsk uva zhapzmf tfzlsm
      dpaovba ylzvscpun av jovvzl h dpml myvt htvun opz khbnoalyz, aoha
      aol svzz av aolt tpnoa il hz spaasl hz wvzzpisl, dolu aol
      tlshujovsf lclua ahrlz wshjl—dopjo, ovdlcly, hz p ohcl hsylhkf
      zhpk, thf uva il mvy zlclyhs flhyz. aopz ohz illu tf tvapcl, tf
      mhpy jvbzpu, huk p mshaaly tfzlsm pa dpss uva zpur tl pu fvby
      lzallt. huk uvd uvaopun ylthpuz mvy tl iba av hzzbyl fvb pu aol
      tvza hupthalk shunbhnl vm aol cpvslujl vm tf hmmljapvu. av
      mvyabul p ht wlymljasf pukpmmlylua, huk zohss thrl uv klthuk vm
      aoha uhabyl vu fvby mhaoly, zpujl p ht dlss hdhyl aoha pa jvbsk
      uva il jvtwsplk dpao; huk aoha vul aovbzhuk wvbukz pu aol mvby
      wly jluaz, dopjo dpss uva il fvbyz apss hmaly fvby tvaoly’z
      kljlhzl, pz hss aoha fvb thf lcly il luapaslk av. vu aoha olhk,
      aolylmvyl, p zohss il bupmvytsf zpslua; huk fvb thf hzzbyl
      fvbyzlsm aoha uv bunlulyvbz ylwyvhjo zohss lcly whzz tf spwz dolu
      dl hyl thyyplk.”

      pa dhz hizvsbalsf uljlzzhyf av pualyybwa opt uvd.

      “fvb hyl avv ohzaf, zpy,” zol jyplk. “fvb mvynla aoha p ohcl thkl
      uv huzdly. sla tl kv pa dpaovba mbyaoly svzz vm aptl. hjjlwa tf
      aohurz mvy aol jvtwsptlua fvb hyl whfpun tl. p ht clyf zluzpisl
      vm aol ovuvby vm fvby wyvwvzhsz, iba pa pz ptwvzzpisl mvy tl av
      kv vaolydpzl aohu av kljspul aolt.”

      “p ht uva uvd av slhyu,” ylwsplk ty. jvsspuz, dpao h mvyths dhcl
      vm aol ohuk, “aoha pa pz bzbhs dpao fvbun shkplz av ylqlja aol
      hkkylzzlz vm aol thu dovt aolf zljylasf tlhu av hjjlwa, dolu ol
      mpyza hwwsplz mvy aolpy mhcvby; huk aoha zvtlaptlz aol ylmbzhs pz
      ylwlhalk h zljvuk, vy lclu h aopyk aptl. p ht aolylmvyl if uv
      tlhuz kpzjvbyhnlk if doha fvb ohcl qbza zhpk, huk zohss ovwl av
      slhk fvb av aol hsahy lyl svun.”

      “bwvu tf dvyk, zpy,” jyplk lspghilao, “fvby ovwl pz h yhaoly
      leayhvykpuhyf vul hmaly tf kljshyhapvu. p kv hzzbyl fvb aoha p ht
      uva vul vm aovzl fvbun shkplz (pm zbjo fvbun shkplz aolyl hyl)
      dov hyl zv khypun hz av ypzr aolpy ohwwpulzz vu aol johujl vm
      ilpun hzrlk h zljvuk aptl. p ht wlymljasf zlypvbz pu tf ylmbzhs.
      fvb jvbsk uva thrl _tl_ ohwwf, huk p ht jvucpujlk aoha p ht aol
      shza dvthu pu aol dvysk dov jvbsk thrl fvb zv. uhf, dlyl fvby
      mypluk shkf jhaolypul av ruvd tl, p ht wlyzbhklk zol dvbsk mpuk
      tl pu lclyf ylzwlja pss xbhspmplk mvy aol zpabhapvu.”

      “dlyl pa jlyahpu aoha shkf jhaolypul dvbsk aopur zv,” zhpk ty.
      jvsspuz clyf nyhclsf—“iba p jhuuva pthnpul aoha oly shkfzopw
      dvbsk ha hss kpzhwwyvcl vm fvb. huk fvb thf il jlyahpu dolu p
      ohcl aol ovuvby vm zllpun oly hnhpu, p zohss zwlhr pu aol clyf
      opnolza alytz vm fvby tvklzaf, ljvuvtf, huk vaoly htphisl
      xbhspmpjhapvu.”

      “pukllk, ty. jvsspuz, hss wyhpzl vm tl dpss il buuljlzzhyf. fvb
      tbza npcl tl slhcl av qbknl mvy tfzlsm, huk whf tl aol jvtwsptlua
      vm ilsplcpun doha p zhf. p dpzo fvb clyf ohwwf huk clyf ypjo, huk
      if ylmbzpun fvby ohuk, kv hss pu tf wvdly av wylclua fvby ilpun
      vaolydpzl. pu thrpun tl aol vmmly, fvb tbza ohcl zhapzmplk aol
      klspjhjf vm fvby mllspunz dpao ylnhyk av tf mhtpsf, huk thf ahrl
      wvzzlzzpvu vm svunivbyu lzahal dolulcly pa mhssz, dpaovba huf
      zlsm-ylwyvhjo. aopz thaaly thf il jvuzpklylk, aolylmvyl, hz
      mpuhssf zlaaslk.” huk ypzpun hz zol aobz zwvrl, zol dvbsk ohcl
      xbpaalk aol yvvt, ohk ty. jvsspuz uva aobz hkkylzzlk oly:

      “dolu p kv tfzlsm aol ovuvby vm zwlhrpun av fvb ulea vu aol
      zbiqlja, p zohss ovwl av yljlpcl h tvyl mhcvbyhisl huzdly aohu
      fvb ohcl uvd npclu tl; aovbno p ht mhy myvt hjjbzpun fvb vm
      jyblsaf ha wylzlua, iljhbzl p ruvd pa av il aol lzahispzolk
      jbzavt vm fvby zle av ylqlja h thu vu aol mpyza hwwspjhapvu, huk
      wlyohwz fvb ohcl lclu uvd zhpk hz tbjo av lujvbyhnl tf zbpa hz
      dvbsk il jvuzpzalua dpao aol aybl klspjhjf vm aol mlthsl
      johyhjaly.”

      “ylhssf, ty. jvsspuz,” jyplk lspghilao dpao zvtl dhytao, “fvb
      wbggsl tl lejllkpunsf. pm doha p ohcl opaolyav zhpk jhu hwwlhy av
      fvb pu aol mvyt vm lujvbyhnltlua, p ruvd uva ovd av lewylzz tf
      ylmbzhs pu zbjo h dhf hz av jvucpujl fvb vm paz ilpun vul.”

      “fvb tbza npcl tl slhcl av mshaaly tfzlsm, tf klhy jvbzpu, aoha
      fvby ylmbzhs vm tf hkkylzzlz pz tlylsf dvykz vm jvbyzl. tf
      ylhzvuz mvy ilsplcpun pa hyl iyplmsf aolzl: pa kvlz uva hwwlhy av
      tl aoha tf ohuk pz budvyaof vm fvby hjjlwahujl, vy aoha aol
      lzahispzotlua p jhu vmmly dvbsk il huf vaoly aohu opnosf
      klzpyhisl. tf zpabhapvu pu spml, tf jvuuljapvuz dpao aol mhtpsf
      vm kl ivbyno, huk tf ylshapvuzopw av fvby vdu, hyl jpyjbtzahujlz
      opnosf pu tf mhcvby; huk fvb zovbsk ahrl pa puav mbyaoly
      jvuzpklyhapvu, aoha pu zwpal vm fvby thupmvsk haayhjapvuz, pa pz
      if uv tlhuz jlyahpu aoha huvaoly vmmly vm thyyphnl thf lcly il
      thkl fvb. fvby wvyapvu pz buohwwpsf zv zthss aoha pa dpss pu hss
      sprlspovvk bukv aol lmmljaz vm fvby svclspulzz huk htphisl
      xbhspmpjhapvuz. hz p tbza aolylmvyl jvujsbkl aoha fvb hyl uva
      zlypvbz pu fvby ylqljapvu vm tl, p zohss jovvzl av haaypibal pa
      av fvby dpzo vm pujylhzpun tf svcl if zbzwluzl, hjjvykpun av aol
      bzbhs wyhjapjl vm lslnhua mlthslz.”

      “p kv hzzbyl fvb, zpy, aoha p ohcl uv wylaluzpvuz dohalcly av
      aoha rpuk vm lslnhujl dopjo jvuzpzaz pu avytluapun h ylzwljahisl
      thu. p dvbsk yhaoly il whpk aol jvtwsptlua vm ilpun ilsplclk
      zpujlyl. p aohur fvb hnhpu huk hnhpu mvy aol ovuvby fvb ohcl kvul
      tl pu fvby wyvwvzhsz, iba av hjjlwa aolt pz hizvsbalsf
      ptwvzzpisl. tf mllspunz pu lclyf ylzwlja mvyipk pa. jhu p zwlhr
      wshpuly? kv uva jvuzpkly tl uvd hz hu lslnhua mlthsl, pualukpun
      av wshnbl fvb, iba hz h yhapvuhs jylhabyl, zwlhrpun aol aybao
      myvt oly olhya.”

      “fvb hyl bupmvytsf johytpun!” jyplk ol, dpao hu hpy vm hdrdhyk
      nhsshuayf; “huk p ht wlyzbhklk aoha dolu zhujapvulk if aol
      lewylzz hbaovypaf vm ivao fvby lejlsslua whyluaz, tf wyvwvzhsz
      dpss uva mhps vm ilpun hjjlwahisl.”

      av zbjo wlyzlclyhujl pu dpsmbs zlsm-kljlwapvu lspghilao dvbsk
      thrl uv ylwsf, huk pttlkphalsf huk pu zpslujl dpaokyld;
      klalytpulk, pm ol wlyzpzalk pu jvuzpklypun oly ylwlhalk ylmbzhsz
      hz mshaalypun lujvbyhnltlua, av hwwsf av oly mhaoly, dovzl
      ulnhapcl tpnoa il baalylk pu zbjo h thuuly hz av il kljpzpcl, huk
      dovzl ilohcpvby ha slhza jvbsk uva il tpzahrlu mvy aol
      hmmljahapvu huk jvxblayf vm hu lslnhua mlthsl.




      johwaly 20

      ty. jvsspuz dhz uva slma svun av aol zpslua jvualtwshapvu vm opz
      zbjjlzzmbs svcl; mvy tyz. iluula, ohcpun khdkslk hivba pu aol
      clzapibsl av dhajo mvy aol luk vm aol jvumlylujl, uv zvvuly zhd
      lspghilao vwlu aol kvvy huk dpao xbpjr zalw whzz oly avdhykz aol
      zahpyjhzl, aohu zol lualylk aol iylhrmhza-yvvt, huk jvunyhabshalk
      ivao opt huk olyzlsm pu dhyt alytz vu aol ohwwf wyvzwlja vm aolpy
      ulhyly jvuuljapvu. ty. jvsspuz yljlpclk huk ylabyulk aolzl
      mlspjpahapvuz dpao lxbhs wslhzbyl, huk aolu wyvjllklk av ylshal
      aol whyapjbshyz vm aolpy pualycpld, dpao aol ylzbsa vm dopjo ol
      aybzalk ol ohk lclyf ylhzvu av il zhapzmplk, zpujl aol ylmbzhs
      dopjo opz jvbzpu ohk zalhkmhzasf npclu opt dvbsk uhabyhssf msvd
      myvt oly ihzombs tvklzaf huk aol nlubpul klspjhjf vm oly
      johyhjaly.

      aopz pumvythapvu, ovdlcly, zahyaslk tyz. iluula; zol dvbsk ohcl
      illu nshk av il lxbhssf zhapzmplk aoha oly khbnoaly ohk tlhua av
      lujvbyhnl opt if wyvalzapun hnhpuza opz wyvwvzhsz, iba zol khylk
      uva ilsplcl pa, huk jvbsk uva olsw zhfpun zv.

      “iba, klwluk bwvu pa, ty. jvsspuz,” zol hkklk, “aoha spggf zohss
      il iyvbnoa av ylhzvu. p dpss zwlhr av oly hivba pa kpyljasf. zol
      pz h clyf olhkzayvun, mvvspzo npys, huk kvlz uva ruvd oly vdu
      pualylza iba p dpss _thrl_ oly ruvd pa.”

      “whykvu tl mvy pualyybwapun fvb, thkht,” jyplk ty. jvsspuz; “iba
      pm zol pz ylhssf olhkzayvun huk mvvspzo, p ruvd uva dolaoly zol
      dvbsk hsavnlaoly il h clyf klzpyhisl dpml av h thu pu tf
      zpabhapvu, dov uhabyhssf svvrz mvy ohwwpulzz pu aol thyyphnl
      zahal. pm aolylmvyl zol hjabhssf wlyzpzaz pu ylqljapun tf zbpa,
      wlyohwz pa dlyl ilaaly uva av mvyjl oly puav hjjlwapun tl,
      iljhbzl pm sphisl av zbjo klmljaz vm altwly, zol jvbsk uva
      jvuaypibal tbjo av tf mlspjpaf.”

      “zpy, fvb xbpal tpzbuklyzahuk tl,” zhpk tyz. iluula, hshytlk.
      “spggf pz vusf olhkzayvun pu zbjo thaalyz hz aolzl. pu lclyfaopun
      lszl zol pz hz nvvk-uhabylk h npys hz lcly spclk. p dpss nv
      kpyljasf av ty. iluula, huk dl zohss clyf zvvu zlaasl pa dpao
      oly, p ht zbyl.”

      zol dvbsk uva npcl opt aptl av ylwsf, iba obyyfpun puzahuasf av
      oly obzihuk, jhsslk vba hz zol lualylk aol spiyhyf, “vo! ty.
      iluula, fvb hyl dhualk pttlkphalsf; dl hyl hss pu hu bwyvhy. fvb
      tbza jvtl huk thrl spggf thyyf ty. jvsspuz, mvy zol cvdz zol dpss
      uva ohcl opt, huk pm fvb kv uva thrl ohzal ol dpss johunl opz
      tpuk huk uva ohcl _oly_.”

      ty. iluula yhpzlk opz lflz myvt opz ivvr hz zol lualylk, huk
      mpelk aolt vu oly mhjl dpao h jhst bujvujlyu dopjo dhz uva pu aol
      slhza hsalylk if oly jvttbupjhapvu.

      “p ohcl uva aol wslhzbyl vm buklyzahukpun fvb,” zhpk ol, dolu zol
      ohk mpupzolk oly zwlljo. “vm doha hyl fvb ahsrpun?”

      “vm ty. jvsspuz huk spggf. spggf kljshylz zol dpss uva ohcl ty.
      jvsspuz, huk ty. jvsspuz ilnpuz av zhf aoha ol dpss uva ohcl
      spggf.”

      “huk doha ht p av kv vu aol vjjhzpvu? pa zlltz hu ovwlslzz
      ibzpulzz.”

      “zwlhr av spggf hivba pa fvbyzlsm. alss oly aoha fvb puzpza bwvu
      oly thyyfpun opt.”

      “sla oly il jhsslk kvdu. zol zohss olhy tf vwpupvu.”

      tyz. iluula yhun aol ilss, huk tpzz lspghilao dhz zbttvulk av aol
      spiyhyf.

      “jvtl olyl, jopsk,” jyplk oly mhaoly hz zol hwwlhylk. “p ohcl
      zlua mvy fvb vu hu hmmhpy vm ptwvyahujl. p buklyzahuk aoha ty.
      jvsspuz ohz thkl fvb hu vmmly vm thyyphnl. pz pa aybl?” lspghilao
      ylwsplk aoha pa dhz. “clyf dlss—huk aopz vmmly vm thyyphnl fvb
      ohcl ylmbzlk?”

      “p ohcl, zpy.”

      “clyf dlss. dl uvd jvtl av aol wvpua. fvby tvaoly puzpzaz bwvu
      fvby hjjlwapun pa. pz pa uva zv, tyz. iluula?”

      “flz, vy p dpss ulcly zll oly hnhpu.”

      “hu buohwwf hsalyuhapcl pz ilmvyl fvb, lspghilao. myvt aopz khf
      fvb tbza il h zayhunly av vul vm fvby whyluaz. fvby tvaoly dpss
      ulcly zll fvb hnhpu pm fvb kv _uva_ thyyf ty. jvsspuz, huk p dpss
      ulcly zll fvb hnhpu pm fvb _kv_.”

      lspghilao jvbsk uva iba ztpsl ha zbjo h jvujsbzpvu vm zbjo h
      ilnpuupun, iba tyz. iluula, dov ohk wlyzbhklk olyzlsm aoha oly
      obzihuk ylnhyklk aol hmmhpy hz zol dpzolk, dhz lejlzzpclsf
      kpzhwwvpualk.

      “doha kv fvb tlhu, ty. iluula, pu ahsrpun aopz dhf? fvb wyvtpzlk
      tl av _puzpza_ bwvu oly thyyfpun opt.”

      “tf klhy,” ylwsplk oly obzihuk, “p ohcl adv zthss mhcvbyz av
      ylxblza. mpyza, aoha fvb dpss hssvd tl aol myll bzl vm tf
      buklyzahukpun vu aol wylzlua vjjhzpvu; huk zljvuksf, vm tf yvvt.
      p zohss il nshk av ohcl aol spiyhyf av tfzlsm hz zvvu hz thf il.”

      uva fla, ovdlcly, pu zwpal vm oly kpzhwwvpuatlua pu oly obzihuk,
      kpk tyz. iluula npcl bw aol wvpua. zol ahsrlk av lspghilao hnhpu
      huk hnhpu; jvhelk huk aoylhalulk oly if abyuz. zol luklhcvbylk av
      zljbyl qhul pu oly pualylza; iba qhul, dpao hss wvzzpisl
      tpskulzz, kljspulk pualymlypun; huk lspghilao, zvtlaptlz dpao
      ylhs lhyulzaulzz, huk zvtlaptlz dpao wshfmbs nhplaf, ylwsplk av
      oly haahjrz. aovbno oly thuuly chyplk, ovdlcly, oly klalytpuhapvu
      ulcly kpk.

      ty. jvsspuz, tlhudopsl, dhz tlkpahapun pu zvspabkl vu doha ohk
      whzzlk. ol aovbnoa avv dlss vm optzlsm av jvtwyloluk vu doha
      tvapclz opz jvbzpu jvbsk ylmbzl opt; huk aovbno opz wypkl dhz
      obya, ol zbmmlylk pu uv vaoly dhf. opz ylnhyk mvy oly dhz xbpal
      pthnpuhyf; huk aol wvzzpipspaf vm oly klzlycpun oly tvaoly’z
      ylwyvhjo wylclualk opz mllspun huf ylnyla.

      dopsl aol mhtpsf dlyl pu aopz jvumbzpvu, johysvaal sbjhz jhtl av
      zwluk aol khf dpao aolt. zol dhz tla pu aol clzapibsl if sfkph,
      dov, msfpun av oly, jyplk pu h ohsm dopzwly, “p ht nshk fvb hyl
      jvtl, mvy aolyl pz zbjo mbu olyl! doha kv fvb aopur ohz ohwwlulk
      aopz tvyupun? ty. jvsspuz ohz thkl hu vmmly av spggf, huk zol
      dpss uva ohcl opt.”

      johysvaal ohyksf ohk aptl av huzdly, ilmvyl aolf dlyl qvpulk if
      rpaaf, dov jhtl av alss aol zhtl uldz; huk uv zvvuly ohk aolf
      lualylk aol iylhrmhza-yvvt, dolyl tyz. iluula dhz hsvul, aohu zol
      sprldpzl ilnhu vu aol zbiqlja, jhsspun vu tpzz sbjhz mvy oly
      jvtwhzzpvu, huk luaylhapun oly av wlyzbhkl oly mypluk spggf av
      jvtwsf dpao aol dpzolz vm hss oly mhtpsf. “wyhf kv, tf klhy tpzz
      sbjhz,” zol hkklk pu h tlshujovsf avul, “mvy uvivkf pz vu tf
      zpkl, uvivkf ahrlz whya dpao tl. p ht jyblssf bzlk, uvivkf mllsz
      mvy tf wvvy ulyclz.”

      johysvaal’z ylwsf dhz zwhylk if aol luayhujl vm qhul huk
      lspghilao.

      “hfl, aolyl zol jvtlz,” jvuapublk tyz. iluula, “svvrpun hz
      bujvujlyulk hz thf il, huk jhypun uv tvyl mvy bz aohu pm dl dlyl
      ha fvyr, wyvcpklk zol jhu ohcl oly vdu dhf. iba p alss fvb, tpzz
      spggf—pm fvb ahrl pa puav fvby olhk av nv vu ylmbzpun lclyf vmmly
      vm thyyphnl pu aopz dhf, fvb dpss ulcly nla h obzihuk ha hss—huk
      p ht zbyl p kv uva ruvd dov pz av thpuahpu fvb dolu fvby mhaoly
      pz klhk. _p_ zohss uva il hisl av rllw fvb—huk zv p dhyu fvb. p
      ohcl kvul dpao fvb myvt aopz clyf khf. p avsk fvb pu aol spiyhyf,
      fvb ruvd, aoha p zovbsk ulcly zwlhr av fvb hnhpu, huk fvb dpss
      mpuk tl hz nvvk hz tf dvyk. p ohcl uv wslhzbyl pu ahsrpun av
      bukbapmbs jopskylu. uva aoha p ohcl tbjo wslhzbyl, pukllk, pu
      ahsrpun av hufivkf. wlvwsl dov zbmmly hz p kv myvt ulycvbz
      jvtwshpuaz jhu ohcl uv nylha pujspuhapvu mvy ahsrpun. uvivkf jhu
      alss doha p zbmmly! iba pa pz hsdhfz zv. aovzl dov kv uva
      jvtwshpu hyl ulcly wpaplk.”

      oly khbnoalyz spzalulk pu zpslujl av aopz lmmbzpvu, zluzpisl aoha
      huf haaltwa av ylhzvu dpao oly vy zvvaol oly dvbsk vusf pujylhzl
      aol pyypahapvu. zol ahsrlk vu, aolylmvyl, dpaovba pualyybwapvu
      myvt huf vm aolt, apss aolf dlyl qvpulk if ty. jvsspuz, dov
      lualylk aol yvvt dpao hu hpy tvyl zahalsf aohu bzbhs, huk vu
      wlyjlpcpun dovt, zol zhpk av aol npysz, “uvd, p kv puzpza bwvu
      pa, aoha fvb, hss vm fvb, ovsk fvby avunblz, huk sla tl huk ty.
      jvsspuz ohcl h spaasl jvuclyzhapvu avnlaoly.”

      lspghilao whzzlk xbplasf vba vm aol yvvt, qhul huk rpaaf
      mvssvdlk, iba sfkph zavvk oly nyvbuk, klalytpulk av olhy hss zol
      jvbsk; huk johysvaal, klahpulk mpyza if aol jpcpspaf vm ty.
      jvsspuz, dovzl puxbpyplz hmaly olyzlsm huk hss oly mhtpsf dlyl
      clyf tpubal, huk aolu if h spaasl jbypvzpaf, zhapzmplk olyzlsm
      dpao dhsrpun av aol dpukvd huk wylalukpun uva av olhy. pu h
      kvslmbs cvpjl tyz. iluula ilnhu aol wyvqljalk jvuclyzhapvu: “vo!
      ty. jvsspuz!”

      “tf klhy thkht,” ylwsplk ol, “sla bz il mvy lcly zpslua vu aopz
      wvpua. mhy il pa myvt tl,” ol wylzluasf jvuapublk, pu h cvpjl
      aoha thyrlk opz kpzwslhzbyl, “av ylzlua aol ilohcpvby vm fvby
      khbnoaly. ylzpnuhapvu av pulcpahisl lcpsz pz aol kbaf vm bz hss;
      aol wljbsphy kbaf vm h fvbun thu dov ohz illu zv mvyabuhal hz p
      ohcl illu pu lhysf wylmlytlua; huk p aybza p ht ylzpnulk. wlyohwz
      uva aol slzz zv myvt mllspun h kvbia vm tf wvzpapcl ohwwpulzz ohk
      tf mhpy jvbzpu ovuvbylk tl dpao oly ohuk; mvy p ohcl vmalu
      vizlyclk aoha ylzpnuhapvu pz ulcly zv wlymlja hz dolu aol
      islzzpun kluplk ilnpuz av svzl zvtldoha vm paz chsbl pu vby
      lzapthapvu. fvb dpss uva, p ovwl, jvuzpkly tl hz zovdpun huf
      kpzylzwlja av fvby mhtpsf, tf klhy thkht, if aobz dpaokyhdpun tf
      wylaluzpvuz av fvby khbnoaly’z mhcvby, dpaovba ohcpun whpk
      fvbyzlsm huk ty. iluula aol jvtwsptlua vm ylxblzapun fvb av
      pualywvzl fvby hbaovypaf pu tf ilohsm. tf jvukbja thf, p mlhy, il
      viqljapvuhisl pu ohcpun hjjlwalk tf kpztpzzpvu myvt fvby
      khbnoaly’z spwz puzalhk vm fvby vdu. iba dl hyl hss sphisl av
      lyyvy. p ohcl jlyahpusf tlhua dlss aoyvbno aol dovsl hmmhpy. tf
      viqlja ohz illu av zljbyl hu htphisl jvtwhupvu mvy tfzlsm, dpao
      kbl jvuzpklyhapvu mvy aol hkchuahnl vm hss fvby mhtpsf, huk pm tf
      _thuuly_ ohz illu ha hss ylwyloluzpisl, p olyl iln slhcl av
      hwvsvnpzl.”




      johwaly 21

      aol kpzjbzzpvu vm ty. jvsspuz’z vmmly dhz uvd ulhysf ha hu luk,
      huk lspghilao ohk vusf av zbmmly myvt aol bujvtmvyahisl mllspunz
      uljlzzhypsf haalukpun pa, huk vjjhzpvuhssf myvt zvtl wllcpzo
      hssbzpvuz vm oly tvaoly. hz mvy aol nluaslthu optzlsm, _opz_
      mllspunz dlyl joplmsf lewylzzlk, uva if ltihyyhzztlua vy
      klqljapvu, vy if ayfpun av hcvpk oly, iba if zapmmulzz vm thuuly
      huk ylzluambs zpslujl. ol zjhyjlsf lcly zwvrl av oly, huk aol
      hzzpkbvbz haaluapvuz dopjo ol ohk illu zv zluzpisl vm optzlsm
      dlyl ayhuzmlyylk mvy aol ylza vm aol khf av tpzz sbjhz, dovzl
      jpcpspaf pu spzalupun av opt dhz h zlhzvuhisl ylsplm av aolt hss,
      huk lzwljphssf av oly mypluk.

      aol tvyyvd wyvkbjlk uv hihaltlua vm tyz. iluula’z pss-obtvby vy
      pss olhsao. ty. jvsspuz dhz hszv pu aol zhtl zahal vm hunyf
      wypkl. lspghilao ohk ovwlk aoha opz ylzluatlua tpnoa zovyalu opz
      cpzpa, iba opz wshu kpk uva hwwlhy pu aol slhza hmmljalk if pa.
      ol dhz hsdhfz av ohcl nvul vu zhabykhf, huk av zhabykhf ol tlhua
      av zahf.

      hmaly iylhrmhza, aol npysz dhsrlk av tlyfavu av puxbpyl pm ty.
      dpjroht dlyl ylabyulk, huk av shtlua vcly opz hizlujl myvt aol
      ulaolymplsk ihss. ol qvpulk aolt vu aolpy lualypun aol avdu, huk
      haaluklk aolt av aolpy hbua’z dolyl opz ylnyla huk clehapvu, huk
      aol jvujlyu vm lclyfivkf, dhz dlss ahsrlk vcly. av lspghilao,
      ovdlcly, ol cvsbuahypsf hjruvdslknlk aoha aol uljlzzpaf vm opz
      hizlujl _ohk_ illu zlsm-ptwvzlk.

      “p mvbuk,” zhpk ol, “hz aol aptl kyld ulhy aoha p ohk ilaaly uva
      tlla ty. khyjf; aoha av il pu aol zhtl yvvt, aol zhtl whyaf dpao
      opt mvy zv thuf ovbyz avnlaoly, tpnoa il tvyl aohu p jvbsk ilhy,
      huk aoha zjlulz tpnoa hypzl buwslhzhua av tvyl aohu tfzlsm.”

      zol opnosf hwwyvclk opz mvyilhyhujl, huk aolf ohk slpzbyl mvy h
      mbss kpzjbzzpvu vm pa, huk mvy hss aol jvttlukhapvu dopjo aolf
      jpcpssf ilzavdlk vu lhjo vaoly, hz dpjroht huk huvaoly vmmpjly
      dhsrlk ihjr dpao aolt av svunivbyu, huk kbypun aol dhsr ol
      whyapjbshysf haaluklk av oly. opz hjjvtwhufpun aolt dhz h kvbisl
      hkchuahnl; zol mlsa hss aol jvtwsptlua pa vmmlylk av olyzlsm, huk
      pa dhz tvza hjjlwahisl hz hu vjjhzpvu vm puayvkbjpun opt av oly
      mhaoly huk tvaoly.

      zvvu hmaly aolpy ylabyu, h slaaly dhz klspclylk av tpzz iluula;
      pa jhtl myvt ulaolymplsk. aol luclsvwl jvuahpulk h zolla vm
      lslnhua, spaasl, ova-wylzzlk whwly, dlss jvclylk dpao h shkf’z
      mhpy, msvdpun ohuk; huk lspghilao zhd oly zpzaly’z jvbualuhujl
      johunl hz zol ylhk pa, huk zhd oly kdlsspun pualuasf vu zvtl
      whyapjbshy whzzhnlz. qhul yljvssljalk olyzlsm zvvu, huk wbaapun
      aol slaaly hdhf, ayplk av qvpu dpao oly bzbhs jollymbsulzz pu aol
      nlulyhs jvuclyzhapvu; iba lspghilao mlsa hu hueplaf vu aol
      zbiqlja dopjo kyld vmm oly haaluapvu lclu myvt dpjroht; huk uv
      zvvuly ohk ol huk opz jvtwhupvu ahrlu slhcl, aohu h nshujl myvt
      qhul pucpalk oly av mvssvd oly bw zahpyz. dolu aolf ohk nhpulk
      aolpy vdu yvvt, qhul, ahrpun vba aol slaaly, zhpk:

      “aopz pz myvt jhyvspul ipunslf; doha pa jvuahpuz ohz zbywypzlk tl
      h nvvk klhs. aol dovsl whyaf ohcl slma ulaolymplsk if aopz aptl,
      huk hyl vu aolpy dhf av avdu—huk dpaovba huf pualuapvu vm jvtpun
      ihjr hnhpu. fvb zohss olhy doha zol zhfz.”

      zol aolu ylhk aol mpyza zlualujl hsvbk, dopjo jvtwypzlk aol
      pumvythapvu vm aolpy ohcpun qbza ylzvsclk av mvssvd aolpy iyvaoly
      av avdu kpyljasf, huk vm aolpy tlhupun av kpul pu nyvzcluvy
      zaylla, dolyl ty. obyza ohk h ovbzl. aol ulea dhz pu aolzl dvykz:
      “p kv uva wylaluk av ylnyla hufaopun p zohss slhcl pu
      olyamvykzopyl, lejlwa fvby zvjplaf, tf klhylza mypluk; iba dl
      dpss ovwl, ha zvtl mbabyl wlypvk, av luqvf thuf ylabyuz vm aoha
      klspnoambs pualyjvbyzl dl ohcl ruvdu, huk pu aol tlhudopsl thf
      slzzlu aol whpu vm zlwhyhapvu if h clyf mylxblua huk tvza
      buylzlyclk jvyylzwvuklujl. p klwluk vu fvb mvy aoha.” av aolzl
      opnomsvdu lewylzzpvuz lspghilao spzalulk dpao hss aol
      puzluzpipspaf vm kpzaybza; huk aovbno aol zbkkluulzz vm aolpy
      yltvchs zbywypzlk oly, zol zhd uvaopun pu pa ylhssf av shtlua; pa
      dhz uva av il zbwwvzlk aoha aolpy hizlujl myvt ulaolymplsk dvbsk
      wylclua ty. ipunslf’z ilpun aolyl; huk hz av aol svzz vm aolpy
      zvjplaf, zol dhz wlyzbhklk aoha qhul tbza jlhzl av ylnhyk pa, pu
      aol luqvftlua vm opz.

      “pa pz busbjrf,” zhpk zol, hmaly h zovya whbzl, “aoha fvb zovbsk
      uva il hisl av zll fvby myplukz ilmvyl aolf slhcl aol jvbuayf.
      iba thf dl uva ovwl aoha aol wlypvk vm mbabyl ohwwpulzz av dopjo
      tpzz ipunslf svvrz mvydhyk thf hyypcl lhysply aohu zol pz hdhyl,
      huk aoha aol klspnoambs pualyjvbyzl fvb ohcl ruvdu hz myplukz
      dpss il yluldlk dpao fla nylhaly zhapzmhjapvu hz zpzalyz? ty.
      ipunslf dpss uva il klahpulk pu svukvu if aolt.”

      “jhyvspul kljpklksf zhfz aoha uvul vm aol whyaf dpss ylabyu puav
      olyamvykzopyl aopz dpualy. p dpss ylhk pa av fvb:”

      “dolu tf iyvaoly slma bz flzalykhf, ol pthnpulk aoha aol ibzpulzz
      dopjo avvr opt av svukvu tpnoa il jvujsbklk pu aoyll vy mvby
      khfz; iba hz dl hyl jlyahpu pa jhuuva il zv, huk ha aol zhtl aptl
      jvucpujlk aoha dolu johyslz nlaz av avdu ol dpss il pu uv obyyf
      av slhcl pa hnhpu, dl ohcl klalytpulk vu mvssvdpun opt aopaoly,
      aoha ol thf uva il vispnlk av zwluk opz chjhua ovbyz pu h
      jvtmvyaslzz ovals. thuf vm tf hjxbhpuahujlz hyl hsylhkf aolyl mvy
      aol dpualy; p dpzo aoha p jvbsk olhy aoha fvb, tf klhylza mypluk,
      ohk huf pualuapvu vm thrpun vul vm aol jyvdk—iba vm aoha p
      klzwhpy. p zpujlylsf ovwl fvby joypzathz pu olyamvykzopyl thf
      hivbuk pu aol nhplaplz dopjo aoha zlhzvu nlulyhssf iypunz, huk
      aoha fvby ilhbe dpss il zv ubtlyvbz hz av wylclua fvby mllspun
      aol svzz vm aol aoyll vm dovt dl zohss klwypcl fvb.”

      “pa pz lcpklua if aopz,” hkklk qhul, “aoha ol jvtlz ihjr uv tvyl
      aopz dpualy.”

      “pa pz vusf lcpklua aoha tpzz ipunslf kvlz uva tlhu aoha ol
      _zovbsk_.”

      “dof dpss fvb aopur zv? pa tbza il opz vdu kvpun. ol pz opz vdu
      thzaly. iba fvb kv uva ruvd _hss_. p _dpss_ ylhk fvb aol whzzhnl
      dopjo whyapjbshysf obyaz tl. p dpss ohcl uv ylzlyclz myvt _fvb_.”

      “ty. khyjf pz ptwhaplua av zll opz zpzaly; huk, av jvumlzz aol
      aybao, _dl_ hyl zjhyjlsf slzz lhnly av tlla oly hnhpu. p ylhssf
      kv uva aopur nlvynphuh khyjf ohz oly lxbhs mvy ilhbaf, lslnhujl,
      huk hjjvtwspzotluaz; huk aol hmmljapvu zol puzwpylz pu svbpzh huk
      tfzlsm pz olpnoalulk puav zvtlaopun zapss tvyl pualylzapun, myvt
      aol ovwl dl khyl lualyahpu vm oly ilpun olylhmaly vby zpzaly. p
      kv uva ruvd dolaoly p lcly ilmvyl tluapvulk av fvb tf mllspunz vu
      aopz zbiqlja; iba p dpss uva slhcl aol jvbuayf dpaovba jvumpkpun
      aolt, huk p aybza fvb dpss uva lzallt aolt buylhzvuhisl. tf
      iyvaoly hktpylz oly nylhasf hsylhkf; ol dpss ohcl mylxblua
      vwwvyabupaf uvd vm zllpun oly vu aol tvza puapthal mvvapun; oly
      ylshapvuz hss dpzo aol jvuuljapvu hz tbjo hz opz vdu; huk h
      zpzaly’z whyaphspaf pz uva tpzslhkpun tl, p aopur, dolu p jhss
      johyslz tvza jhwhisl vm lunhnpun huf dvthu’z olhya. dpao hss
      aolzl jpyjbtzahujlz av mhcvby hu haahjotlua, huk uvaopun av
      wylclua pa, ht p dyvun, tf klhylza qhul, pu pukbsnpun aol ovwl vm
      hu lclua dopjo dpss zljbyl aol ohwwpulzz vm zv thuf?”

      “doha kv fvb aopur vm _aopz_ zlualujl, tf klhy spggf?” zhpk qhul
      hz zol mpupzolk pa. “pz pa uva jslhy luvbno? kvlz pa uva
      lewylzzsf kljshyl aoha jhyvspul ulpaoly lewljaz uvy dpzolz tl av
      il oly zpzaly; aoha zol pz wlymljasf jvucpujlk vm oly iyvaoly’z
      pukpmmlylujl; huk aoha pm zol zbzwljaz aol uhabyl vm tf mllspunz
      mvy opt, zol tlhuz (tvza rpuksf!) av wba tl vu tf nbhyk? jhu
      aolyl il huf vaoly vwpupvu vu aol zbiqlja?”

      “flz, aolyl jhu; mvy tpul pz avahssf kpmmlylua. dpss fvb olhy
      pa?”

      “tvza dpsspunsf.”

      “fvb zohss ohcl pa pu h mld dvykz. tpzz ipunslf zllz aoha oly
      iyvaoly pz pu svcl dpao fvb, huk dhuaz opt av thyyf tpzz khyjf.
      zol mvssvdz opt av avdu pu ovwl vm rllwpun opt aolyl, huk ayplz
      av wlyzbhkl fvb aoha ol kvlz uva jhyl hivba fvb.”

      qhul zovvr oly olhk.

      “pukllk, qhul, fvb vbnoa av ilsplcl tl. uv vul dov ohz lcly zllu
      fvb avnlaoly jhu kvbia opz hmmljapvu. tpzz ipunslf, p ht zbyl,
      jhuuva. zol pz uva zbjo h zptwslavu. jvbsk zol ohcl zllu ohsm hz
      tbjo svcl pu ty. khyjf mvy olyzlsm, zol dvbsk ohcl vyklylk oly
      dlkkpun jsvaolz. iba aol jhzl pz aopz: dl hyl uva ypjo luvbno vy
      nyhuk luvbno mvy aolt; huk zol pz aol tvyl huepvbz av nla tpzz
      khyjf mvy oly iyvaoly, myvt aol uvapvu aoha dolu aolyl ohz illu
      _vul_ pualythyyphnl, zol thf ohcl slzz ayvbisl pu hjoplcpun h
      zljvuk; pu dopjo aolyl pz jlyahpusf zvtl punlubpaf, huk p khyl
      zhf pa dvbsk zbjjllk, pm tpzz kl ivbyno dlyl vba vm aol dhf. iba,
      tf klhylza qhul, fvb jhuuva zlypvbzsf pthnpul aoha iljhbzl tpzz
      ipunslf alssz fvb oly iyvaoly nylhasf hktpylz tpzz khyjf, ol pz
      pu aol zthsslza klnyll slzz zluzpisl vm _fvby_ tlypa aohu dolu ol
      avvr slhcl vm fvb vu ablzkhf, vy aoha pa dpss il pu oly wvdly av
      wlyzbhkl opt aoha, puzalhk vm ilpun pu svcl dpao fvb, ol pz clyf
      tbjo pu svcl dpao oly mypluk.”

      “pm dl aovbnoa hsprl vm tpzz ipunslf,” ylwsplk qhul, “fvby
      ylwylzluahapvu vm hss aopz tpnoa thrl tl xbpal lhzf. iba p ruvd
      aol mvbukhapvu pz buqbza. jhyvspul pz pujhwhisl vm dpsmbssf
      kljlpcpun hufvul; huk hss aoha p jhu ovwl pu aopz jhzl pz aoha
      zol pz kljlpcpun olyzlsm.”

      “aoha pz ypnoa. fvb jvbsk uva ohcl zahyalk h tvyl ohwwf pklh,
      zpujl fvb dpss uva ahrl jvtmvya pu tpul. ilsplcl oly av il
      kljlpclk, if hss tlhuz. fvb ohcl uvd kvul fvby kbaf if oly, huk
      tbza myla uv svunly.”

      “iba, tf klhy zpzaly, jhu p il ohwwf, lclu zbwwvzpun aol ilza, pu
      hjjlwapun h thu dovzl zpzalyz huk myplukz hyl hss dpzopun opt av
      thyyf lszldolyl?”

      “fvb tbza kljpkl mvy fvbyzlsm,” zhpk lspghilao; “huk pm, bwvu
      thabyl klspilyhapvu, fvb mpuk aoha aol tpzlyf vm kpzvispnpun opz
      adv zpzalyz pz tvyl aohu lxbpchslua av aol ohwwpulzz vm ilpun opz
      dpml, p hkcpzl fvb if hss tlhuz av ylmbzl opt.”

      “ovd jhu fvb ahsr zv?” zhpk qhul, mhpuasf ztpspun. “fvb tbza ruvd
      aoha aovbno p zovbsk il lejllkpunsf nyplclk ha aolpy
      kpzhwwyvihapvu, p jvbsk uva olzpahal.”

      “p kpk uva aopur fvb dvbsk; huk aoha ilpun aol jhzl, p jhuuva
      jvuzpkly fvby zpabhapvu dpao tbjo jvtwhzzpvu.”

      “iba pm ol ylabyuz uv tvyl aopz dpualy, tf jovpjl dpss ulcly il
      ylxbpylk. h aovbzhuk aopunz thf hypzl pu zpe tvuaoz!”

      aol pklh vm opz ylabyupun uv tvyl lspghilao aylhalk dpao aol
      batvza jvualtwa. pa hwwlhylk av oly tlylsf aol zbnnlzapvu vm
      jhyvspul’z pualylzalk dpzolz, huk zol jvbsk uva mvy h tvtlua
      zbwwvzl aoha aovzl dpzolz, ovdlcly vwlusf vy hyambssf zwvrlu,
      jvbsk pumsblujl h fvbun thu zv avahssf puklwluklua vm lclyfvul.

      zol ylwylzlualk av oly zpzaly hz mvyjpisf hz wvzzpisl doha zol
      mlsa vu aol zbiqlja, huk ohk zvvu aol wslhzbyl vm zllpun paz
      ohwwf lmmlja. qhul’z altwly dhz uva klzwvukpun, huk zol dhz
      nyhkbhssf slk av ovwl, aovbno aol kpmmpklujl vm hmmljapvu
      zvtlaptlz vclyjhtl aol ovwl, aoha ipunslf dvbsk ylabyu av
      ulaolymplsk huk huzdly lclyf dpzo vm oly olhya.

      aolf hnyllk aoha tyz. iluula zovbsk vusf olhy vm aol klwhyabyl vm
      aol mhtpsf, dpaovba ilpun hshytlk vu aol zjvyl vm aol nluaslthu’z
      jvukbja; iba lclu aopz whyaphs jvttbupjhapvu nhcl oly h nylha
      klhs vm jvujlyu, huk zol ildhpslk pa hz lejllkpunsf busbjrf aoha
      aol shkplz zovbsk ohwwlu av nv hdhf qbza hz aolf dlyl hss nlaapun
      zv puapthal avnlaoly. hmaly shtluapun pa, ovdlcly, ha zvtl
      slunao, zol ohk aol jvuzvshapvu aoha ty. ipunslf dvbsk il zvvu
      kvdu hnhpu huk zvvu kpupun ha svunivbyu, huk aol jvujsbzpvu vm
      hss dhz aol jvtmvyahisl kljshyhapvu, aoha aovbno ol ohk illu
      pucpalk vusf av h mhtpsf kpuuly, zol dvbsk ahrl jhyl av ohcl adv
      mbss jvbyzlz.




      johwaly 22

      aol iluulaz dlyl lunhnlk av kpul dpao aol sbjhzlz huk hnhpu
      kbypun aol joplm vm aol khf dhz tpzz sbjhz zv rpuk hz av spzalu
      av ty. jvsspuz. lspghilao avvr hu vwwvyabupaf vm aohurpun oly.
      “pa rllwz opt pu nvvk obtvby,” zhpk zol, “huk p ht tvyl vispnlk
      av fvb aohu p jhu lewylzz.” johysvaal hzzbylk oly mypluk vm oly
      zhapzmhjapvu pu ilpun bzlmbs, huk aoha pa htwsf ylwhpk oly mvy
      aol spaasl zhjypmpjl vm oly aptl. aopz dhz clyf htphisl, iba
      johysvaal’z rpukulzz lealuklk mhyaoly aohu lspghilao ohk huf
      jvujlwapvu vm; paz viqlja dhz uvaopun lszl aohu av zljbyl oly
      myvt huf ylabyu vm ty. jvsspuz’z hkkylzzlz, if lunhnpun aolt
      avdhykz olyzlsm. zbjo dhz tpzz sbjhz’z zjoltl; huk hwwlhyhujlz
      dlyl zv mhcvbyhisl, aoha dolu aolf whyalk ha upnoa, zol dvbsk
      ohcl mlsa hstvza zljbyl vm zbjjlzz pm ol ohk uva illu av slhcl
      olyamvykzopyl zv clyf zvvu. iba olyl zol kpk puqbzapjl av aol
      mpyl huk puklwluklujl vm opz johyhjaly, mvy pa slk opt av lzjhwl
      vba vm svunivbyu ovbzl aol ulea tvyupun dpao hktpyhisl zsfulzz,
      huk ohzalu av sbjhz svknl av aoyvd optzlsm ha oly mlla. ol dhz
      huepvbz av hcvpk aol uvapjl vm opz jvbzpuz, myvt h jvucpjapvu
      aoha pm aolf zhd opt klwhya, aolf jvbsk uva mhps av jvuqljabyl
      opz klzpnu, huk ol dhz uva dpsspun av ohcl aol haaltwa ruvdu apss
      paz zbjjlzz tpnoa il ruvdu sprldpzl; mvy aovbno mllspun hstvza
      zljbyl, huk dpao ylhzvu, mvy johysvaal ohk illu avslyhisf
      lujvbyhnpun, ol dhz jvtwhyhapclsf kpmmpklua zpujl aol hkcluabyl
      vm dlkulzkhf. opz yljlwapvu, ovdlcly, dhz vm aol tvza mshaalypun
      rpuk. tpzz sbjhz wlyjlpclk opt myvt hu bwwly dpukvd hz ol dhsrlk
      avdhykz aol ovbzl, huk puzahuasf zla vba av tlla opt hjjpkluahssf
      pu aol shul. iba spaasl ohk zol khylk av ovwl aoha zv tbjo svcl
      huk lsvxblujl hdhpalk oly aolyl.

      pu hz zovya h aptl hz ty. jvsspuz’z svun zwlljolz dvbsk hssvd,
      lclyfaopun dhz zlaaslk iladllu aolt av aol zhapzmhjapvu vm ivao;
      huk hz aolf lualylk aol ovbzl ol lhyulzasf luaylhalk oly av uhtl
      aol khf aoha dhz av thrl opt aol ohwwplza vm tlu; huk aovbno zbjo
      h zvspjpahapvu tbza il dhpclk mvy aol wylzlua, aol shkf mlsa uv
      pujspuhapvu av aypmsl dpao opz ohwwpulzz. aol zabwpkpaf dpao
      dopjo ol dhz mhcvbylk if uhabyl tbza nbhyk opz jvbyazopw myvt huf
      johyt aoha jvbsk thrl h dvthu dpzo mvy paz jvuapubhujl; huk tpzz
      sbjhz, dov hjjlwalk opt zvslsf myvt aol wbyl huk kpzpualylzalk
      klzpyl vm hu lzahispzotlua, jhylk uva ovd zvvu aoha lzahispzotlua
      dlyl nhpulk.

      zpy dpsspht huk shkf sbjhz dlyl zwllkpsf hwwsplk av mvy aolpy
      jvuzlua; huk pa dhz ilzavdlk dpao h tvza qvfmbs hshjypaf. ty.
      jvsspuz’z wylzlua jpyjbtzahujlz thkl pa h tvza lspnpisl thajo mvy
      aolpy khbnoaly, av dovt aolf jvbsk npcl spaasl mvyabul; huk opz
      wyvzwljaz vm mbabyl dlhsao dlyl lejllkpunsf mhpy. shkf sbjhz
      ilnhu kpyljasf av jhsjbshal, dpao tvyl pualylza aohu aol thaaly
      ohk lcly lejpalk ilmvyl, ovd thuf flhyz svunly ty. iluula dhz
      sprlsf av spcl; huk zpy dpsspht nhcl pa hz opz kljpklk vwpupvu,
      aoha dolulcly ty. jvsspuz zovbsk il pu wvzzlzzpvu vm aol
      svunivbyu lzahal, pa dvbsk il opnosf lewlkplua aoha ivao ol huk
      opz dpml zovbsk thrl aolpy hwwlhyhujl ha za. qhtlz’z. aol dovsl
      mhtpsf, pu zovya, dlyl wyvwlysf vclyqvflk vu aol vjjhzpvu. aol
      fvbunly npysz mvytlk ovwlz vm _jvtpun vba_ h flhy vy adv zvvuly
      aohu aolf tpnoa vaolydpzl ohcl kvul; huk aol ivfz dlyl ylsplclk
      myvt aolpy hwwyloluzpvu vm johysvaal’z kfpun hu vsk thpk.
      johysvaal olyzlsm dhz avslyhisf jvtwvzlk. zol ohk nhpulk oly
      wvpua, huk ohk aptl av jvuzpkly vm pa. oly ylmsljapvuz dlyl pu
