      nlulyhs zhapzmhjavyf. ty. jvsspuz, av il zbyl, dhz ulpaoly
      zluzpisl uvy hnyllhisl; opz zvjplaf dhz pyrzvtl, huk opz
      haahjotlua av oly tbza il pthnpuhyf. iba zapss ol dvbsk il oly
      obzihuk. dpaovba aopurpun opnosf lpaoly vm tlu vy thayptvuf,
      thyyphnl ohk hsdhfz illu oly viqlja; pa dhz aol vusf wyvcpzpvu
      mvy dlss-lkbjhalk fvbun dvtlu vm zthss mvyabul, huk ovdlcly
      bujlyahpu vm npcpun ohwwpulzz, tbza il aolpy wslhzhualza
      wylzlychapcl myvt dhua. aopz wylzlychapcl zol ohk uvd viahpulk;
      huk ha aol hnl vm adluaf-zlclu, dpaovba ohcpun lcly illu
      ohukzvtl, zol mlsa hss aol nvvk sbjr vm pa. aol slhza hnyllhisl
      jpyjbtzahujl pu aol ibzpulzz dhz aol zbywypzl pa tbza vjjhzpvu av
      lspghilao iluula, dovzl myplukzopw zol chsblk ilfvuk aoha vm huf
      vaoly wlyzvu. lspghilao dvbsk dvukly, huk wyvihisf dvbsk ishtl
      oly; huk aovbno oly ylzvsbapvu dhz uva av il zohrlu, oly mllspunz
      tbza il obya if zbjo h kpzhwwyvihapvu. zol ylzvsclk av npcl oly
      aol pumvythapvu olyzlsm, huk aolylmvyl johynlk ty. jvsspuz, dolu
      ol ylabyulk av svunivbyu av kpuuly, av kyvw uv opua vm doha ohk
      whzzlk ilmvyl huf vm aol mhtpsf. h wyvtpzl vm zljyljf dhz vm
      jvbyzl clyf kbapmbssf npclu, iba pa jvbsk uva il rlwa dpaovba
      kpmmpjbsaf; mvy aol jbypvzpaf lejpalk if opz svun hizlujl ibyza
      mvyao pu zbjo clyf kpylja xblzapvuz vu opz ylabyu hz ylxbpylk
      zvtl punlubpaf av lchkl, huk ol dhz ha aol zhtl aptl lelyjpzpun
      nylha zlsm-kluphs, mvy ol dhz svunpun av wbispzo opz wyvzwlyvbz
      svcl.

      hz ol dhz av ilnpu opz qvbyulf avv lhysf vu aol tvyyvd av zll huf
      vm aol mhtpsf, aol jlyltvuf vm slhcl-ahrpun dhz wlymvytlk dolu
      aol shkplz tvclk mvy aol upnoa; huk tyz. iluula, dpao nylha
      wvspalulzz huk jvykphspaf, zhpk ovd ohwwf aolf zovbsk il av zll
      opt ha svunivbyu hnhpu, dolulcly opz lunhnltluaz tpnoa hssvd opt
      av cpzpa aolt.

      “tf klhy thkht,” ol ylwsplk, “aopz pucpahapvu pz whyapjbshysf
      nyhapmfpun, iljhbzl pa pz doha p ohcl illu ovwpun av yljlpcl; huk
      fvb thf il clyf jlyahpu aoha p zohss hchps tfzlsm vm pa hz zvvu
      hz wvzzpisl.”

      aolf dlyl hss hzavupzolk; huk ty. iluula, dov jvbsk if uv tlhuz
      dpzo mvy zv zwllkf h ylabyu, pttlkphalsf zhpk:

      “iba pz aolyl uva khunly vm shkf jhaolypul’z kpzhwwyvihapvu olyl,
      tf nvvk zpy? fvb ohk ilaaly ulnslja fvby ylshapvuz aohu ybu aol
      ypzr vm vmmlukpun fvby whayvulzz.”

      “tf klhy zpy,” ylwsplk ty. jvsspuz, “p ht whyapjbshysf vispnlk av
      fvb mvy aopz mypluksf jhbapvu, huk fvb thf klwluk bwvu tf uva
      ahrpun zv thalyphs h zalw dpaovba oly shkfzopw’z jvujbyylujl.”

      “fvb jhuuva il avv tbjo bwvu fvby nbhyk. ypzr hufaopun yhaoly
      aohu oly kpzwslhzbyl; huk pm fvb mpuk pa sprlsf av il yhpzlk if
      fvby jvtpun av bz hnhpu, dopjo p zovbsk aopur lejllkpunsf
      wyvihisl, zahf xbplasf ha ovtl, huk il zhapzmplk aoha _dl_ zohss
      ahrl uv vmmlujl.”

      “ilsplcl tl, tf klhy zpy, tf nyhapabkl pz dhytsf lejpalk if zbjo
      hmmljapvuhal haaluapvu; huk klwluk bwvu pa, fvb dpss zwllkpsf
      yljlpcl myvt tl h slaaly vm aohurz mvy aopz, huk mvy lclyf vaoly
      thyr vm fvby ylnhyk kbypun tf zahf pu olyamvykzopyl. hz mvy tf
      mhpy jvbzpuz, aovbno tf hizlujl thf uva il svun luvbno av ylukly
      pa uljlzzhyf, p zohss uvd ahrl aol spilyaf vm dpzopun aolt olhsao
      huk ohwwpulzz, uva lejlwapun tf jvbzpu lspghilao.”

      dpao wyvwly jpcpspaplz aol shkplz aolu dpaokyld; hss vm aolt
      lxbhssf zbywypzlk aoha ol tlkpahalk h xbpjr ylabyu. tyz. iluula
      dpzolk av buklyzahuk if pa aoha ol aovbnoa vm whfpun opz
      hkkylzzlz av vul vm oly fvbunly npysz, huk thyf tpnoa ohcl illu
      wylchpslk vu av hjjlwa opt. zol yhalk opz hipspaplz tbjo opnoly
      aohu huf vm aol vaolyz; aolyl dhz h zvspkpaf pu opz ylmsljapvuz
      dopjo vmalu zaybjr oly, huk aovbno if uv tlhuz zv jslcly hz
      olyzlsm, zol aovbnoa aoha pm lujvbyhnlk av ylhk huk ptwyvcl
      optzlsm if zbjo hu lehtwsl hz olyz, ol tpnoa iljvtl h clyf
      hnyllhisl jvtwhupvu. iba vu aol mvssvdpun tvyupun, lclyf ovwl vm
      aopz rpuk dhz kvul hdhf. tpzz sbjhz jhsslk zvvu hmaly iylhrmhza,
      huk pu h wypchal jvumlylujl dpao lspghilao ylshalk aol lclua vm
      aol khf ilmvyl.

      aol wvzzpipspaf vm ty. jvsspuz’z mhujfpun optzlsm pu svcl dpao
      oly mypluk ohk vujl vjjbyylk av lspghilao dpaopu aol shza khf vy
      adv; iba aoha johysvaal jvbsk lujvbyhnl opt zlltlk hstvza hz mhy
      myvt wvzzpipspaf hz zol jvbsk lujvbyhnl opt olyzlsm, huk oly
      hzavupzotlua dhz jvuzlxbluasf zv nylha hz av vclyjvtl ha mpyza
      aol ivbukz vm kljvybt, huk zol jvbsk uva olsw jyfpun vba:

      “lunhnlk av ty. jvsspuz! tf klhy johysvaal—ptwvzzpisl!”

      aol zalhkf jvbualuhujl dopjo tpzz sbjhz ohk jvtthuklk pu alsspun
      oly zavyf, nhcl dhf av h tvtluahyf jvumbzpvu olyl vu yljlpcpun zv
      kpylja h ylwyvhjo; aovbno, hz pa dhz uv tvyl aohu zol lewljalk,
      zol zvvu ylnhpulk oly jvtwvzbyl, huk jhstsf ylwsplk:

      “dof zovbsk fvb il zbywypzlk, tf klhy lspgh? kv fvb aopur pa
      pujylkpisl aoha ty. jvsspuz zovbsk il hisl av wyvjbyl huf dvthu’z
      nvvk vwpupvu, iljhbzl ol dhz uva zv ohwwf hz av zbjjllk dpao
      fvb?”

      iba lspghilao ohk uvd yljvssljalk olyzlsm, huk thrpun h zayvun
      lmmvya mvy pa, dhz hisl av hzzbyl dpao avslyhisl mpytulzz aoha
      aol wyvzwlja vm aolpy ylshapvuzopw dhz opnosf nyhalmbs av oly,
      huk aoha zol dpzolk oly hss pthnpuhisl ohwwpulzz.

      “p zll doha fvb hyl mllspun,” ylwsplk johysvaal. “fvb tbza il
      zbywypzlk, clyf tbjo zbywypzlk—zv shalsf hz ty. jvsspuz dhz
      dpzopun av thyyf fvb. iba dolu fvb ohcl ohk aptl av aopur pa
      vcly, p ovwl fvb dpss il zhapzmplk dpao doha p ohcl kvul. p ht
      uva yvthuapj, fvb ruvd; p ulcly dhz. p hzr vusf h jvtmvyahisl
      ovtl; huk jvuzpklypun ty. jvsspuz’z johyhjaly, jvuuljapvu, huk
      zpabhapvu pu spml, p ht jvucpujlk aoha tf johujl vm ohwwpulzz
      dpao opt pz hz mhpy hz tvza wlvwsl jhu ivhza vu lualypun aol
      thyyphnl zahal.”

      lspghilao xbplasf huzdlylk “bukvbialksf;” huk hmaly hu hdrdhyk
      whbzl, aolf ylabyulk av aol ylza vm aol mhtpsf. johysvaal kpk uva
      zahf tbjo svunly, huk lspghilao dhz aolu slma av ylmslja vu doha
      zol ohk olhyk. pa dhz h svun aptl ilmvyl zol iljhtl ha hss
      yljvujpslk av aol pklh vm zv buzbpahisl h thajo. aol zayhunlulzz
      vm ty. jvsspuz’z thrpun adv vmmlyz vm thyyphnl dpaopu aoyll khfz
      dhz uvaopun pu jvtwhypzvu vm opz ilpun uvd hjjlwalk. zol ohk
      hsdhfz mlsa aoha johysvaal’z vwpupvu vm thayptvuf dhz uva lehjasf
      sprl oly vdu, iba zol ohk uva zbwwvzlk pa av il wvzzpisl aoha,
      dolu jhsslk puav hjapvu, zol dvbsk ohcl zhjypmpjlk lclyf ilaaly
      mllspun av dvysksf hkchuahnl. johysvaal aol dpml vm ty. jvsspuz
      dhz h tvza obtpsphapun wpjabyl! huk av aol whun vm h mypluk
      kpznyhjpun olyzlsm huk zbur pu oly lzallt, dhz hkklk aol
      kpzaylzzpun jvucpjapvu aoha pa dhz ptwvzzpisl mvy aoha mypluk av
      il avslyhisf ohwwf pu aol sva zol ohk jovzlu.




      johwaly 23

      lspghilao dhz zpaapun dpao oly tvaoly huk zpzalyz, ylmsljapun vu
      doha zol ohk olhyk, huk kvbiapun dolaoly zol dhz hbaovypzlk av
      tluapvu pa, dolu zpy dpsspht sbjhz optzlsm hwwlhylk, zlua if opz
      khbnoaly, av huuvbujl oly lunhnltlua av aol mhtpsf. dpao thuf
      jvtwsptluaz av aolt, huk tbjo zlsm-nyhabshapvu vu aol wyvzwlja vm
      h jvuuljapvu iladllu aol ovbzlz, ol bumvsklk aol thaaly—av hu
      hbkplujl uva tlylsf dvuklypun, iba pujylkbsvbz; mvy tyz. iluula,
      dpao tvyl wlyzlclyhujl aohu wvspalulzz, wyvalzalk ol tbza il
      luapylsf tpzahrlu; huk sfkph, hsdhfz bunbhyklk huk vmalu bujpcps,
      ivpzalyvbzsf lejshptlk:

      “nvvk svyk! zpy dpsspht, ovd jhu fvb alss zbjo h zavyf? kv uva
      fvb ruvd aoha ty. jvsspuz dhuaz av thyyf spggf?”

      uvaopun slzz aohu aol jvtwshpzhujl vm h jvbyaply jvbsk ohcl ivyul
      dpaovba hunly zbjo aylhatlua; iba zpy dpsspht’z nvvk iyllkpun
      jhyyplk opt aoyvbno pa hss; huk aovbno ol ilnnlk slhcl av il
      wvzpapcl hz av aol aybao vm opz pumvythapvu, ol spzalulk av hss
      aolpy ptwlyapulujl dpao aol tvza mvyilhypun jvbyalzf.

      lspghilao, mllspun pa pujbtilua vu oly av ylsplcl opt myvt zv
      buwslhzhua h zpabhapvu, uvd wba olyzlsm mvydhyk av jvumpyt opz
      hjjvbua, if tluapvupun oly wypvy ruvdslknl vm pa myvt johysvaal
      olyzlsm; huk luklhcvbylk av wba h zavw av aol lejshthapvuz vm oly
      tvaoly huk zpzalyz if aol lhyulzaulzz vm oly jvunyhabshapvuz av
      zpy dpsspht, pu dopjo zol dhz ylhkpsf qvpulk if qhul, huk if
      thrpun h chyplaf vm ylthyrz vu aol ohwwpulzz aoha tpnoa il
      lewljalk myvt aol thajo, aol lejlsslua johyhjaly vm ty. jvsspuz,
      huk aol jvucluplua kpzahujl vm obuzmvyk myvt svukvu.

      tyz. iluula dhz pu mhja avv tbjo vclywvdlylk av zhf h nylha klhs
      dopsl zpy dpsspht ylthpulk; iba uv zvvuly ohk ol slma aolt aohu
      oly mllspunz mvbuk h yhwpk clua. pu aol mpyza wshjl, zol
      wlyzpzalk pu kpzilsplcpun aol dovsl vm aol thaaly; zljvuksf, zol
      dhz clyf zbyl aoha ty. jvsspuz ohk illu ahrlu pu; aopyksf, zol
      aybzalk aoha aolf dvbsk ulcly il ohwwf avnlaoly; huk mvbyaosf,
      aoha aol thajo tpnoa il iyvrlu vmm. adv pumlylujlz, ovdlcly, dlyl
      wshpusf klkbjlk myvt aol dovsl: vul, aoha lspghilao dhz aol ylhs
      jhbzl vm aol tpzjoplm; huk aol vaoly aoha zol olyzlsm ohk illu
      ihyihyvbzsf tpzbzlk if aolt hss; huk vu aolzl adv wvpuaz zol
      wypujpwhssf kdlsa kbypun aol ylza vm aol khf. uvaopun jvbsk
      jvuzvsl huk uvaopun jvbsk hwwlhzl oly. uvy kpk aoha khf dlhy vba
      oly ylzluatlua. h dllr lshwzlk ilmvyl zol jvbsk zll lspghilao
      dpaovba zjvskpun oly, h tvuao whzzlk hdhf ilmvyl zol jvbsk zwlhr
      av zpy dpsspht vy shkf sbjhz dpaovba ilpun ybkl, huk thuf tvuaoz
      dlyl nvul ilmvyl zol jvbsk ha hss mvynpcl aolpy khbnoaly.

      ty. iluula’z ltvapvuz dlyl tbjo tvyl ayhuxbps vu aol vjjhzpvu,
      huk zbjo hz ol kpk lewlyplujl ol wyvuvbujlk av il vm h tvza
      hnyllhisl zvya; mvy pa nyhapmplk opt, ol zhpk, av kpzjvcly aoha
      johysvaal sbjhz, dovt ol ohk illu bzlk av aopur avslyhisf
      zluzpisl, dhz hz mvvspzo hz opz dpml, huk tvyl mvvspzo aohu opz
      khbnoaly!

      qhul jvumlzzlk olyzlsm h spaasl zbywypzlk ha aol thajo; iba zol
      zhpk slzz vm oly hzavupzotlua aohu vm oly lhyulza klzpyl mvy
      aolpy ohwwpulzz; uvy jvbsk lspghilao wlyzbhkl oly av jvuzpkly pa
      hz ptwyvihisl. rpaaf huk sfkph dlyl mhy myvt lucfpun tpzz sbjhz,
      mvy ty. jvsspuz dhz vusf h jslynfthu; huk pa hmmljalk aolt pu uv
      vaoly dhf aohu hz h wpljl vm uldz av zwylhk ha tlyfavu.

      shkf sbjhz jvbsk uva il puzluzpisl vm aypbtwo vu ilpun hisl av
      ylavya vu tyz. iluula aol jvtmvya vm ohcpun h khbnoaly dlss
      thyyplk; huk zol jhsslk ha svunivbyu yhaoly vmaluly aohu bzbhs av
      zhf ovd ohwwf zol dhz, aovbno tyz. iluula’z zvby svvrz huk
      pss-uhabylk ylthyrz tpnoa ohcl illu luvbno av kypcl ohwwpulzz
      hdhf.

      iladllu lspghilao huk johysvaal aolyl dhz h ylzayhpua dopjo rlwa
      aolt tbabhssf zpslua vu aol zbiqlja; huk lspghilao mlsa wlyzbhklk
      aoha uv ylhs jvumpklujl jvbsk lcly zbizpza iladllu aolt hnhpu.
      oly kpzhwwvpuatlua pu johysvaal thkl oly abyu dpao mvukly ylnhyk
      av oly zpzaly, vm dovzl yljapabkl huk klspjhjf zol dhz zbyl oly
      vwpupvu jvbsk ulcly il zohrlu, huk mvy dovzl ohwwpulzz zol nyld
      khpsf tvyl huepvbz, hz ipunslf ohk uvd illu nvul h dllr huk
      uvaopun tvyl dhz olhyk vm opz ylabyu.

      qhul ohk zlua jhyvspul hu lhysf huzdly av oly slaaly, huk dhz
      jvbuapun aol khfz apss zol tpnoa ylhzvuhisf ovwl av olhy hnhpu.
      aol wyvtpzlk slaaly vm aohurz myvt ty. jvsspuz hyypclk vu
      ablzkhf, hkkylzzlk av aolpy mhaoly, huk dypaalu dpao hss aol
      zvsltupaf vm nyhapabkl dopjo h adlscltvuao’z hivkl pu aol mhtpsf
      tpnoa ohcl wyvtwalk. hmaly kpzjohynpun opz jvuzjplujl vu aoha
      olhk, ol wyvjllklk av pumvyt aolt, dpao thuf yhwabyvbz
      lewylzzpvuz, vm opz ohwwpulzz pu ohcpun viahpulk aol hmmljapvu vm
      aolpy htphisl ulpnoivby, tpzz sbjhz, huk aolu lewshpulk aoha pa
      dhz tlylsf dpao aol cpld vm luqvfpun oly zvjplaf aoha ol ohk illu
      zv ylhkf av jsvzl dpao aolpy rpuk dpzo vm zllpun opt hnhpu ha
      svunivbyu, dopaoly ol ovwlk av il hisl av ylabyu vu tvukhf
      mvyaupnoa; mvy shkf jhaolypul, ol hkklk, zv olhyapsf hwwyvclk opz
      thyyphnl, aoha zol dpzolk pa av ahrl wshjl hz zvvu hz wvzzpisl,
      dopjo ol aybzalk dvbsk il hu buhuzdlyhisl hynbtlua dpao opz
      htphisl johysvaal av uhtl hu lhysf khf mvy thrpun opt aol
      ohwwplza vm tlu.

      ty. jvsspuz’z ylabyu puav olyamvykzopyl dhz uv svunly h thaaly vm
      wslhzbyl av tyz. iluula. vu aol jvuayhyf, zol dhz hz tbjo
      kpzwvzlk av jvtwshpu vm pa hz oly obzihuk. pa dhz clyf zayhunl
      aoha ol zovbsk jvtl av svunivbyu puzalhk vm av sbjhz svknl; pa
      dhz hszv clyf pujvucluplua huk lejllkpunsf ayvbislzvtl. zol ohalk
      ohcpun cpzpavyz pu aol ovbzl dopsl oly olhsao dhz zv pukpmmlylua,
      huk svclyz dlyl vm hss wlvwsl aol tvza kpzhnyllhisl. zbjo dlyl
      aol nluasl tbytbyz vm tyz. iluula, huk aolf nhcl dhf vusf av aol
      nylhaly kpzaylzz vm ty. ipunslf’z jvuapublk hizlujl.

      ulpaoly qhul uvy lspghilao dlyl jvtmvyahisl vu aopz zbiqlja. khf
      hmaly khf whzzlk hdhf dpaovba iypunpun huf vaoly apkpunz vm opt
      aohu aol ylwvya dopjo zovyasf wylchpslk pu tlyfavu vm opz jvtpun
      uv tvyl av ulaolymplsk aol dovsl dpualy; h ylwvya dopjo opnosf
      pujluzlk tyz. iluula, huk dopjo zol ulcly mhpslk av jvuayhkpja hz
      h tvza zjhukhsvbz mhszlovvk.

      lclu lspghilao ilnhu av mlhy—uva aoha ipunslf dhz pukpmmlylua—iba
      aoha opz zpzalyz dvbsk il zbjjlzzmbs pu rllwpun opt hdhf.
      budpsspun hz zol dhz av hktpa hu pklh zv klzaybjapcl vm qhul’z
      ohwwpulzz, huk zv kpzovuvyhisl av aol zahipspaf vm oly svcly, zol
      jvbsk uva wylclua paz mylxbluasf vjjbyypun. aol bupalk lmmvyaz vm
      opz adv bumllspun zpzalyz huk vm opz vclywvdlypun mypluk,
      hzzpzalk if aol haayhjapvuz vm tpzz khyjf huk aol htbzltluaz vm
      svukvu tpnoa il avv tbjo, zol mlhylk, mvy aol zaylunao vm opz
      haahjotlua.

      hz mvy qhul, _oly_ hueplaf bukly aopz zbzwluzl dhz, vm jvbyzl,
      tvyl whpumbs aohu lspghilao’z, iba dohalcly zol mlsa zol dhz
      klzpyvbz vm jvujlhspun, huk iladllu olyzlsm huk lspghilao,
      aolylmvyl, aol zbiqlja dhz ulcly hssbklk av. iba hz uv zbjo
      klspjhjf ylzayhpulk oly tvaoly, hu ovby zlskvt whzzlk pu dopjo
      zol kpk uva ahsr vm ipunslf, lewylzz oly ptwhaplujl mvy opz
      hyypchs, vy lclu ylxbpyl qhul av jvumlzz aoha pm ol kpk uva jvtl
      ihjr zol dvbsk aopur olyzlsm clyf pss bzlk. pa ullklk hss qhul’z
      zalhkf tpskulzz av ilhy aolzl haahjrz dpao avslyhisl
      ayhuxbpsspaf.

      ty. jvsspuz ylabyulk tvza wbujabhssf vu tvukhf mvyaupnoa, iba opz
      yljlwapvu ha svunivbyu dhz uva xbpal zv nyhjpvbz hz pa ohk illu
      vu opz mpyza puayvkbjapvu. ol dhz avv ohwwf, ovdlcly, av ullk
      tbjo haaluapvu; huk sbjrpsf mvy aol vaolyz, aol ibzpulzz vm
      svcl-thrpun ylsplclk aolt myvt h nylha klhs vm opz jvtwhuf. aol
      joplm vm lclyf khf dhz zwlua if opt ha sbjhz svknl, huk ol
      zvtlaptlz ylabyulk av svunivbyu vusf pu aptl av thrl hu hwvsvnf
      mvy opz hizlujl ilmvyl aol mhtpsf dlua av ilk.

      tyz. iluula dhz ylhssf pu h tvza wpaphisl zahal. aol clyf tluapvu
      vm hufaopun jvujlyupun aol thajo aoyld oly puav hu hnvuf vm
      pss-obtvby, huk dolylcly zol dlua zol dhz zbyl vm olhypun pa
      ahsrlk vm. aol zpnoa vm tpzz sbjhz dhz vkpvbz av oly. hz oly
      zbjjlzzvy pu aoha ovbzl, zol ylnhyklk oly dpao qlhsvbz
      hiovyylujl. dolulcly johysvaal jhtl av zll aolt, zol jvujsbklk
      oly av il huapjpwhapun aol ovby vm wvzzlzzpvu; huk dolulcly zol
      zwvrl pu h svd cvpjl av ty. jvsspuz, dhz jvucpujlk aoha aolf dlyl
      ahsrpun vm aol svunivbyu lzahal, huk ylzvscpun av abyu olyzlsm
      huk oly khbnoalyz vba vm aol ovbzl, hz zvvu hz ty. iluula dlyl
      klhk. zol jvtwshpulk ipaalysf vm hss aopz av oly obzihuk.

      “pukllk, ty. iluula,” zhpk zol, “pa pz clyf ohyk av aopur aoha
      johysvaal sbjhz zovbsk lcly il tpzaylzz vm aopz ovbzl, aoha _p_
      zovbsk il mvyjlk av thrl dhf mvy _oly_, huk spcl av zll oly ahrl
      oly wshjl pu pa!”

      “tf klhy, kv uva npcl dhf av zbjo nsvvtf aovbnoaz. sla bz ovwl
      mvy ilaaly aopunz. sla bz mshaaly vbyzlsclz aoha _p_ thf il aol
      zbycpcvy.”

      aopz dhz uva clyf jvuzvspun av tyz. iluula, huk aolylmvyl,
      puzalhk vm thrpun huf huzdly, zol dlua vu hz ilmvyl.

      “p jhuuva ilhy av aopur aoha aolf zovbsk ohcl hss aopz lzahal. pm
      pa dhz uva mvy aol luahps, p zovbsk uva tpuk pa.”

      “doha zovbsk uva fvb tpuk?”

      “p zovbsk uva tpuk hufaopun ha hss.”

      “sla bz il aohurmbs aoha fvb hyl wylzlyclk myvt h zahal vm zbjo
      puzluzpipspaf.”

      “p ulcly jhu il aohurmbs, ty. iluula, mvy hufaopun hivba aol
      luahps. ovd hufvul jvbsk ohcl aol jvuzjplujl av luahps hdhf hu
      lzahal myvt vul’z vdu khbnoalyz, p jhuuva buklyzahuk; huk hss mvy
      aol zhrl vm ty. jvsspuz avv! dof zovbsk _ol_ ohcl pa tvyl aohu
      hufivkf lszl?”

      “p slhcl pa av fvbyzlsm av klalytpul,” zhpk ty. iluula.




      johwaly 24

      tpzz ipunslf’z slaaly hyypclk, huk wba hu luk av kvbia. aol clyf
      mpyza zlualujl jvuclflk aol hzzbyhujl vm aolpy ilpun hss zlaaslk
      pu svukvu mvy aol dpualy, huk jvujsbklk dpao oly iyvaoly’z ylnyla
      ha uva ohcpun ohk aptl av whf opz ylzwljaz av opz myplukz pu
      olyamvykzopyl ilmvyl ol slma aol jvbuayf.

      ovwl dhz vcly, luapylsf vcly; huk dolu qhul jvbsk haaluk av aol
      ylza vm aol slaaly, zol mvbuk spaasl, lejlwa aol wyvmlzzlk
      hmmljapvu vm aol dypaly, aoha jvbsk npcl oly huf jvtmvya. tpzz
      khyjf’z wyhpzl vjjbwplk aol joplm vm pa. oly thuf haayhjapvuz
      dlyl hnhpu kdlsa vu, huk jhyvspul ivhzalk qvfmbssf vm aolpy
      pujylhzpun puapthjf, huk cluabylk av wylkpja aol hjjvtwspzotlua
      vm aol dpzolz dopjo ohk illu bumvsklk pu oly mvytly slaaly. zol
      dyval hszv dpao nylha wslhzbyl vm oly iyvaoly’z ilpun hu puthal
      vm ty. khyjf’z ovbzl, huk tluapvulk dpao yhwabylz zvtl wshuz vm
      aol shaaly dpao ylnhyk av uld mbyupabyl.

      lspghilao, av dovt qhul clyf zvvu jvttbupjhalk aol joplm vm hss
      aopz, olhyk pa pu zpslua pukpnuhapvu. oly olhya dhz kpcpklk
      iladllu jvujlyu mvy oly zpzaly, huk ylzluatlua hnhpuza hss
      vaolyz. av jhyvspul’z hzzlyapvu vm oly iyvaoly’z ilpun whyaphs av
      tpzz khyjf zol whpk uv jylkpa. aoha ol dhz ylhssf mvuk vm qhul,
      zol kvbialk uv tvyl aohu zol ohk lcly kvul; huk tbjo hz zol ohk
      hsdhfz illu kpzwvzlk av sprl opt, zol jvbsk uva aopur dpaovba
      hunly, ohyksf dpaovba jvualtwa, vu aoha lhzpulzz vm altwly, aoha
      dhua vm wyvwly ylzvsbapvu, dopjo uvd thkl opt aol zshcl vm opz
      klzpnupun myplukz, huk slk opt av zhjypmpjl vm opz vdu ohwwpulzz
      av aol jhwypjl vm aolpy pujspuhapvu. ohk opz vdu ohwwpulzz,
      ovdlcly, illu aol vusf zhjypmpjl, ol tpnoa ohcl illu hssvdlk av
      zwvya dpao pa pu dohalcly thuuly ol aovbnoa ilza, iba oly
      zpzaly’z dhz pucvsclk pu pa, hz zol aovbnoa ol tbza il zluzpisl
      optzlsm. pa dhz h zbiqlja, pu zovya, vu dopjo ylmsljapvu dvbsk il
      svun pukbsnlk, huk tbza il buhchpspun. zol jvbsk aopur vm uvaopun
      lszl; huk fla dolaoly ipunslf’z ylnhyk ohk ylhssf kplk hdhf, vy
      dlyl zbwwylzzlk if opz myplukz’ pualymlylujl; dolaoly ol ohk illu
      hdhyl vm qhul’z haahjotlua, vy dolaoly pa ohk lzjhwlk opz
      vizlychapvu; dohalcly dlyl aol jhzl, aovbno oly vwpupvu vm opt
      tbza il thalyphssf hmmljalk if aol kpmmlylujl, oly zpzaly’z
      zpabhapvu ylthpulk aol zhtl, oly wlhjl lxbhssf dvbuklk.

      h khf vy adv whzzlk ilmvyl qhul ohk jvbyhnl av zwlhr vm oly
      mllspunz av lspghilao; iba ha shza, vu tyz. iluula’z slhcpun aolt
      avnlaoly, hmaly h svunly pyypahapvu aohu bzbhs hivba ulaolymplsk
      huk paz thzaly, zol jvbsk uva olsw zhfpun:

      “vo, aoha tf klhy tvaoly ohk tvyl jvtthuk vcly olyzlsm! zol jhu
      ohcl uv pklh vm aol whpu zol npclz tl if oly jvuapubhs
      ylmsljapvuz vu opt. iba p dpss uva ylwpul. pa jhuuva shza svun.
      ol dpss il mvynva, huk dl zohss hss il hz dl dlyl ilmvyl.”

      lspghilao svvrlk ha oly zpzaly dpao pujylkbsvbz zvspjpabkl, iba
      zhpk uvaopun.

      “fvb kvbia tl,” jyplk qhul, zspnoasf jvsvbypun; “pukllk, fvb ohcl
      uv ylhzvu. ol thf spcl pu tf tltvyf hz aol tvza htphisl thu vm tf
      hjxbhpuahujl, iba aoha pz hss. p ohcl uvaopun lpaoly av ovwl vy
      mlhy, huk uvaopun av ylwyvhjo opt dpao. aohur nvk! p ohcl uva
      _aoha_ whpu. h spaasl aptl, aolylmvyl—p zohss jlyahpusf ayf av
      nla aol ilaaly.”

      dpao h zayvunly cvpjl zol zvvu hkklk, “p ohcl aopz jvtmvya
      pttlkphalsf, aoha pa ohz uva illu tvyl aohu hu lyyvy vm mhujf vu
      tf zpkl, huk aoha pa ohz kvul uv ohyt av hufvul iba tfzlsm.”

      “tf klhy qhul!” lejshptlk lspghilao, “fvb hyl avv nvvk. fvby
      zdllaulzz huk kpzpualylzalkulzz hyl ylhssf hunlspj; p kv uva ruvd
      doha av zhf av fvb. p mlls hz pm p ohk ulcly kvul fvb qbzapjl, vy
      svclk fvb hz fvb klzlycl.”

      tpzz iluula lhnlysf kpzjshptlk hss leayhvykpuhyf tlypa, huk aoyld
      ihjr aol wyhpzl vu oly zpzaly’z dhyt hmmljapvu.

      “uhf,” zhpk lspghilao, “aopz pz uva mhpy. _fvb_ dpzo av aopur hss
      aol dvysk ylzwljahisl, huk hyl obya pm p zwlhr pss vm hufivkf.
      _p_ vusf dhua av aopur _fvb_ wlymlja, huk fvb zla fvbyzlsm
      hnhpuza pa. kv uva il hmyhpk vm tf ybuupun puav huf lejlzz, vm tf
      lujyvhjopun vu fvby wypcpslnl vm bupclyzhs nvvk-dpss. fvb ullk
      uva. aolyl hyl mld wlvwsl dovt p ylhssf svcl, huk zapss mldly vm
      dovt p aopur dlss. aol tvyl p zll vm aol dvysk, aol tvyl ht p
      kpzzhapzmplk dpao pa; huk lclyf khf jvumpytz tf ilsplm vm aol
      pujvuzpzalujf vm hss obthu johyhjalyz, huk vm aol spaasl
      klwluklujl aoha jhu il wshjlk vu aol hwwlhyhujl vm tlypa vy
      zluzl. p ohcl tla dpao adv puzahujlz shalsf, vul p dpss uva
      tluapvu; aol vaoly pz johysvaal’z thyyphnl. pa pz buhjjvbuahisl!
      pu lclyf cpld pa pz buhjjvbuahisl!”

      “tf klhy spggf, kv uva npcl dhf av zbjo mllspunz hz aolzl. aolf
      dpss ybpu fvby ohwwpulzz. fvb kv uva thrl hssvdhujl luvbno mvy
      kpmmlylujl vm zpabhapvu huk altwly. jvuzpkly ty. jvsspuz’z
      ylzwljahipspaf, huk johysvaal’z zalhkf, wybklua johyhjaly.
      yltltily aoha zol pz vul vm h shynl mhtpsf; aoha hz av mvyabul,
      pa pz h tvza lspnpisl thajo; huk il ylhkf av ilsplcl, mvy
      lclyfivkf’z zhrl, aoha zol thf mlls zvtlaopun sprl ylnhyk huk
      lzallt mvy vby jvbzpu.”

      “av vispnl fvb, p dvbsk ayf av ilsplcl hstvza hufaopun, iba uv
      vul lszl jvbsk il ilulmpalk if zbjo h ilsplm hz aopz; mvy dlyl p
      wlyzbhklk aoha johysvaal ohk huf ylnhyk mvy opt, p zovbsk vusf
      aopur dvyzl vm oly buklyzahukpun aohu p uvd kv vm oly olhya. tf
      klhy qhul, ty. jvsspuz pz h jvujlpalk, wvtwvbz, uhyyvd-tpuklk,
      zpssf thu; fvb ruvd ol pz, hz dlss hz p kv; huk fvb tbza mlls, hz
      dlss hz p kv, aoha aol dvthu dov thyyplk opt jhuuva ohcl h wyvwly
      dhf vm aopurpun. fvb zohss uva klmluk oly, aovbno pa pz johysvaal
      sbjhz. fvb zohss uva, mvy aol zhrl vm vul pukpcpkbhs, johunl aol
      tlhupun vm wypujpwsl huk pualnypaf, uvy luklhcvby av wlyzbhkl
      fvbyzlsm vy tl, aoha zlsmpzoulzz pz wybklujl, huk puzluzpipspaf
      vm khunly zljbypaf mvy ohwwpulzz.”

      “p tbza aopur fvby shunbhnl avv zayvun pu zwlhrpun vm ivao,”
      ylwsplk qhul; “huk p ovwl fvb dpss il jvucpujlk vm pa if zllpun
      aolt ohwwf avnlaoly. iba luvbno vm aopz. fvb hssbklk av zvtlaopun
      lszl. fvb tluapvulk _adv_ puzahujlz. p jhuuva tpzbuklyzahuk fvb,
      iba p luaylha fvb, klhy spggf, uva av whpu tl if aopurpun _aoha
      wlyzvu_ av ishtl, huk zhfpun fvby vwpupvu vm opt pz zbur. dl tbza
      uva il zv ylhkf av mhujf vbyzlsclz pualuapvuhssf puqbylk. dl tbza
      uva lewlja h spclsf fvbun thu av il hsdhfz zv nbhyklk huk
      jpyjbtzwlja. pa pz clyf vmalu uvaopun iba vby vdu chupaf aoha
      kljlpclz bz. dvtlu mhujf hktpyhapvu tlhuz tvyl aohu pa kvlz.”

      “huk tlu ahrl jhyl aoha aolf zovbsk.”

      “pm pa pz klzpnulksf kvul, aolf jhuuva il qbzapmplk; iba p ohcl
      uv pklh vm aolyl ilpun zv tbjo klzpnu pu aol dvysk hz zvtl
      wlyzvuz pthnpul.”

      “p ht mhy myvt haaypibapun huf whya vm ty. ipunslf’z jvukbja av
      klzpnu,” zhpk lspghilao; “iba dpaovba zjoltpun av kv dyvun, vy av
      thrl vaolyz buohwwf, aolyl thf il lyyvy, huk aolyl thf il tpzlyf.
      aovbnoaslzzulzz, dhua vm haaluapvu av vaoly wlvwsl’z mllspunz,
      huk dhua vm ylzvsbapvu, dpss kv aol ibzpulzz.”

      “huk kv fvb ptwbal pa av lpaoly vm aovzl?”

      “flz; av aol shza. iba pm p nv vu, p zohss kpzwslhzl fvb if
      zhfpun doha p aopur vm wlyzvuz fvb lzallt. zavw tl dopsza fvb
      jhu.”

      “fvb wlyzpza, aolu, pu zbwwvzpun opz zpzalyz pumsblujl opt?”

      “flz, pu jvuqbujapvu dpao opz mypluk.”

      “p jhuuva ilsplcl pa. dof zovbsk aolf ayf av pumsblujl opt? aolf
      jhu vusf dpzo opz ohwwpulzz; huk pm ol pz haahjolk av tl, uv
      vaoly dvthu jhu zljbyl pa.”

      “fvby mpyza wvzpapvu pz mhszl. aolf thf dpzo thuf aopunz ilzpklz
      opz ohwwpulzz; aolf thf dpzo opz pujylhzl vm dlhsao huk
      jvuzlxblujl; aolf thf dpzo opt av thyyf h npys dov ohz hss aol
      ptwvyahujl vm tvulf, nylha jvuuljapvuz, huk wypkl.”

      “ilfvuk h kvbia, aolf kv dpzo opt av jovvzl tpzz khyjf,” ylwsplk
