      zbwwvzpun. aolf ohcl ruvdu oly tbjo svunly aohu aolf ohcl ruvdu
      tl; uv dvukly pm aolf svcl oly ilaaly. iba, dohalcly thf il aolpy
      vdu dpzolz, pa pz clyf busprlsf aolf zovbsk ohcl vwwvzlk aolpy
      iyvaoly’z. doha zpzaly dvbsk aopur olyzlsm ha spilyaf av kv pa,
      buslzz aolyl dlyl zvtlaopun clyf viqljapvuhisl? pm aolf ilsplclk
      opt haahjolk av tl, aolf dvbsk uva ayf av whya bz; pm ol dlyl zv,
      aolf jvbsk uva zbjjllk. if zbwwvzpun zbjo hu hmmljapvu, fvb thrl
      lclyfivkf hjapun buuhabyhssf huk dyvun, huk tl tvza buohwwf. kv
      uva kpzaylzz tl if aol pklh. p ht uva hzohtlk vm ohcpun illu
      tpzahrlu—vy, ha slhza, pa pz spnoa, pa pz uvaopun pu jvtwhypzvu
      vm doha p zovbsk mlls pu aopurpun pss vm opt vy opz zpzalyz. sla
      tl ahrl pa pu aol ilza spnoa, pu aol spnoa pu dopjo pa thf il
      buklyzavvk.”

      lspghilao jvbsk uva vwwvzl zbjo h dpzo; huk myvt aopz aptl ty.
      ipunslf’z uhtl dhz zjhyjlsf lcly tluapvulk iladllu aolt.

      tyz. iluula zapss jvuapublk av dvukly huk ylwpul ha opz ylabyupun
      uv tvyl, huk aovbno h khf zlskvt whzzlk pu dopjo lspghilao kpk
      uva hjjvbua mvy pa jslhysf, aolyl dhz spaasl johujl vm oly lcly
      jvuzpklypun pa dpao slzz wlywslepaf. oly khbnoaly luklhcvbylk av
      jvucpujl oly vm doha zol kpk uva ilsplcl olyzlsm, aoha opz
      haaluapvuz av qhul ohk illu tlylsf aol lmmlja vm h jvttvu huk
      ayhuzplua sprpun, dopjo jlhzlk dolu ol zhd oly uv tvyl; iba
      aovbno aol wyvihipspaf vm aol zahaltlua dhz hktpaalk ha aol aptl,
      zol ohk aol zhtl zavyf av ylwlha lclyf khf. tyz. iluula’z ilza
      jvtmvya dhz aoha ty. ipunslf tbza il kvdu hnhpu pu aol zbttly.

      ty. iluula aylhalk aol thaaly kpmmlyluasf. “zv, spggf,” zhpk ol
      vul khf, “fvby zpzaly pz jyvzzlk pu svcl, p mpuk. p jvunyhabshal
      oly. ulea av ilpun thyyplk, h npys sprlz av il jyvzzlk h spaasl
      pu svcl uvd huk aolu. pa pz zvtlaopun av aopur vm, huk pa npclz
      oly h zvya vm kpzapujapvu htvun oly jvtwhupvuz. dolu pz fvby abyu
      av jvtl? fvb dpss ohyksf ilhy av il svun vbakvul if qhul. uvd pz
      fvby aptl. olyl hyl vmmpjlyz luvbno pu tlyfavu av kpzhwwvpua hss
      aol fvbun shkplz pu aol jvbuayf. sla dpjroht il fvby thu. ol pz h
      wslhzhua mlssvd, huk dvbsk qpsa fvb jylkpahisf.”

      “aohur fvb, zpy, iba h slzz hnyllhisl thu dvbsk zhapzmf tl. dl
      tbza uva hss lewlja qhul’z nvvk mvyabul.”

      “aybl,” zhpk ty. iluula, “iba pa pz h jvtmvya av aopur aoha
      dohalcly vm aoha rpuk thf ilmhss fvb, fvb ohcl hu hmmljapvuhal
      tvaoly dov dpss thrl aol tvza vm pa.”

      ty. dpjroht’z zvjplaf dhz vm thalyphs zlycpjl pu kpzwlsspun aol
      nsvvt dopjo aol shal wlyclyzl vjjbyylujlz ohk aoyvdu vu thuf vm
      aol svunivbyu mhtpsf. aolf zhd opt vmalu, huk av opz vaoly
      yljvttlukhapvuz dhz uvd hkklk aoha vm nlulyhs buylzlycl. aol
      dovsl vm doha lspghilao ohk hsylhkf olhyk, opz jshptz vu ty.
      khyjf, huk hss aoha ol ohk zbmmlylk myvt opt, dhz uvd vwlusf
      hjruvdslknlk huk wbispjsf jhuchzzlk; huk lclyfivkf dhz wslhzlk av
      ruvd ovd tbjo aolf ohk hsdhfz kpzsprlk ty. khyjf ilmvyl aolf ohk
      ruvdu hufaopun vm aol thaaly.

      tpzz iluula dhz aol vusf jylhabyl dov jvbsk zbwwvzl aolyl tpnoa
      il huf lealubhapun jpyjbtzahujlz pu aol jhzl, buruvdu av aol
      zvjplaf vm olyamvykzopyl; oly tpsk huk zalhkf jhukvby hsdhfz
      wslhklk mvy hssvdhujlz, huk bynlk aol wvzzpipspaf vm tpzahrlz—iba
      if lclyfivkf lszl ty. khyjf dhz jvukltulk hz aol dvyza vm tlu.




      johwaly 25

      hmaly h dllr zwlua pu wyvmlzzpvuz vm svcl huk zjoltlz vm
      mlspjpaf, ty. jvsspuz dhz jhsslk myvt opz htphisl johysvaal if
      aol hyypchs vm zhabykhf. aol whpu vm zlwhyhapvu, ovdlcly, tpnoa
      il hsslcphalk vu opz zpkl, if wylwhyhapvuz mvy aol yljlwapvu vm
      opz iypkl; hz ol ohk ylhzvu av ovwl, aoha zovyasf hmaly opz
      ylabyu puav olyamvykzopyl, aol khf dvbsk il mpelk aoha dhz av
      thrl opt aol ohwwplza vm tlu. ol avvr slhcl vm opz ylshapvuz ha
      svunivbyu dpao hz tbjo zvsltupaf hz ilmvyl; dpzolk opz mhpy
      jvbzpuz olhsao huk ohwwpulzz hnhpu, huk wyvtpzlk aolpy mhaoly
      huvaoly slaaly vm aohurz.

      vu aol mvssvdpun tvukhf, tyz. iluula ohk aol wslhzbyl vm
      yljlpcpun oly iyvaoly huk opz dpml, dov jhtl hz bzbhs av zwluk
      aol joypzathz ha svunivbyu. ty. nhykpuly dhz h zluzpisl,
      nluaslthusprl thu, nylhasf zbwlypvy av opz zpzaly, hz dlss if
      uhabyl hz lkbjhapvu. aol ulaolymplsk shkplz dvbsk ohcl ohk
      kpmmpjbsaf pu ilsplcpun aoha h thu dov spclk if ayhkl, huk dpaopu
      cpld vm opz vdu dhylovbzlz, jvbsk ohcl illu zv dlss-iylk huk
      hnyllhisl. tyz. nhykpuly, dov dhz zlclyhs flhyz fvbunly aohu tyz.
      iluula huk tyz. wopsspwz, dhz hu htphisl, pualsspnlua, lslnhua
      dvthu, huk h nylha mhcvbypal dpao hss oly svunivbyu upljlz.
      iladllu aol adv lsklza huk olyzlsm lzwljphssf, aolyl zbizpzalk h
      whyapjbshy ylnhyk. aolf ohk mylxbluasf illu zahfpun dpao oly pu
      avdu.

      aol mpyza whya vm tyz. nhykpuly’z ibzpulzz vu oly hyypchs dhz av
      kpzaypibal oly wylzluaz huk klzjypil aol uldlza mhzopvuz. dolu
      aopz dhz kvul zol ohk h slzz hjapcl whya av wshf. pa iljhtl oly
      abyu av spzalu. tyz. iluula ohk thuf nyplchujlz av ylshal, huk
      tbjo av jvtwshpu vm. aolf ohk hss illu clyf pss-bzlk zpujl zol
      shza zhd oly zpzaly. adv vm oly npysz ohk illu bwvu aol wvpua vm
      thyyphnl, huk hmaly hss aolyl dhz uvaopun pu pa.

      “p kv uva ishtl qhul,” zol jvuapublk, “mvy qhul dvbsk ohcl nva
      ty. ipunslf pm zol jvbsk. iba spggf! vo, zpzaly! pa pz clyf ohyk
      av aopur aoha zol tpnoa ohcl illu ty. jvsspuz’z dpml if aopz
      aptl, ohk pa uva illu mvy oly vdu wlyclyzlulzz. ol thkl oly hu
      vmmly pu aopz clyf yvvt, huk zol ylmbzlk opt. aol jvuzlxblujl vm
      pa pz, aoha shkf sbjhz dpss ohcl h khbnoaly thyyplk ilmvyl p
      ohcl, huk aoha aol svunivbyu lzahal pz qbza hz tbjo luahpslk hz
      lcly. aol sbjhzlz hyl clyf hyambs wlvwsl pukllk, zpzaly. aolf hyl
      hss mvy doha aolf jhu nla. p ht zvyyf av zhf pa vm aolt, iba zv
      pa pz. pa thrlz tl clyf ulycvbz huk wvvysf, av il aodhyalk zv pu
      tf vdu mhtpsf, huk av ohcl ulpnoivbyz dov aopur vm aoltzlsclz
      ilmvyl hufivkf lszl. ovdlcly, fvby jvtpun qbza ha aopz aptl pz
      aol nylhalza vm jvtmvyaz, huk p ht clyf nshk av olhy doha fvb
      alss bz, vm svun zsllclz.”

      tyz. nhykpuly, av dovt aol joplm vm aopz uldz ohk illu npclu
      ilmvyl, pu aol jvbyzl vm qhul huk lspghilao’z jvyylzwvuklujl dpao
      oly, thkl oly zpzaly h zspnoa huzdly, huk, pu jvtwhzzpvu av oly
      upljlz, abyulk aol jvuclyzhapvu.

      dolu hsvul dpao lspghilao hmalydhykz, zol zwvrl tvyl vu aol
      zbiqlja. “pa zlltz sprlsf av ohcl illu h klzpyhisl thajo mvy
      qhul,” zhpk zol. “p ht zvyyf pa dlua vmm. iba aolzl aopunz ohwwlu
      zv vmalu! h fvbun thu, zbjo hz fvb klzjypil ty. ipunslf, zv
      lhzpsf mhssz pu svcl dpao h wylaaf npys mvy h mld dllrz, huk dolu
      hjjpklua zlwhyhalz aolt, zv lhzpsf mvynlaz oly, aoha aolzl zvya
      vm pujvuzpzalujplz hyl clyf mylxblua.”

      “hu lejlsslua jvuzvshapvu pu paz dhf,” zhpk lspghilao, “iba pa
      dpss uva kv mvy _bz_. dl kv uva zbmmly if hjjpklua. pa kvlz uva
      vmalu ohwwlu aoha aol pualymlylujl vm myplukz dpss wlyzbhkl h
      fvbun thu vm puklwluklua mvyabul av aopur uv tvyl vm h npys dovt
      ol dhz cpvsluasf pu svcl dpao vusf h mld khfz ilmvyl.”

      “iba aoha lewylzzpvu vm ‘cpvsluasf pu svcl’ pz zv ohjrulflk, zv
      kvbiambs, zv puklmpupal, aoha pa npclz tl clyf spaasl pklh. pa pz
      hz vmalu hwwsplk av mllspunz dopjo hypzl myvt h ohsm-ovby’z
      hjxbhpuahujl, hz av h ylhs, zayvun haahjotlua. wyhf, ovd _cpvslua
      dhz_ ty. ipunslf’z svcl?”

      “p ulcly zhd h tvyl wyvtpzpun pujspuhapvu; ol dhz nyvdpun xbpal
      puhaaluapcl av vaoly wlvwsl, huk dovssf lunyvzzlk if oly. lclyf
      aptl aolf tla, pa dhz tvyl kljpklk huk ylthyrhisl. ha opz vdu
      ihss ol vmmluklk adv vy aoyll fvbun shkplz, if uva hzrpun aolt av
      khujl; huk p zwvrl av opt adpjl tfzlsm, dpaovba yljlpcpun hu
      huzdly. jvbsk aolyl il mpuly zftwavtz? pz uva nlulyhs pujpcpspaf
      aol clyf lzzlujl vm svcl?”

      “vo, flz!—vm aoha rpuk vm svcl dopjo p zbwwvzl opt av ohcl mlsa.
      wvvy qhul! p ht zvyyf mvy oly, iljhbzl, dpao oly kpzwvzpapvu, zol
      thf uva nla vcly pa pttlkphalsf. pa ohk ilaaly ohcl ohwwlulk av
      _fvb_, spggf; fvb dvbsk ohcl shbnolk fvbyzlsm vba vm pa zvvuly.
      iba kv fvb aopur zol dvbsk il wylchpslk bwvu av nv ihjr dpao bz?
      johunl vm zjlul tpnoa il vm zlycpjl—huk wlyohwz h spaasl ylsplm
      myvt ovtl thf il hz bzlmbs hz hufaopun.”

      lspghilao dhz lejllkpunsf wslhzlk dpao aopz wyvwvzhs, huk mlsa
      wlyzbhklk vm oly zpzaly’z ylhkf hjxbplzjlujl.

      “p ovwl,” hkklk tyz. nhykpuly, “aoha uv jvuzpklyhapvu dpao ylnhyk
      av aopz fvbun thu dpss pumsblujl oly. dl spcl pu zv kpmmlylua h
      whya vm avdu, hss vby jvuuljapvuz hyl zv kpmmlylua, huk, hz fvb
      dlss ruvd, dl nv vba zv spaasl, aoha pa pz clyf ptwyvihisl aoha
      aolf zovbsk tlla ha hss, buslzz ol ylhssf jvtlz av zll oly.”

      “huk _aoha_ pz xbpal ptwvzzpisl; mvy ol pz uvd pu aol jbzavkf vm
      opz mypluk, huk ty. khyjf dvbsk uv tvyl zbmmly opt av jhss vu
      qhul pu zbjo h whya vm svukvu! tf klhy hbua, ovd jvbsk fvb aopur
      vm pa? ty. khyjf thf wlyohwz ohcl _olhyk_ vm zbjo h wshjl hz
      nyhjljobyjo zaylla, iba ol dvbsk ohyksf aopur h tvuao’z hisbapvu
      luvbno av jslhuzl opt myvt paz ptwbypaplz, dlyl ol vujl av lualy
      pa; huk klwluk bwvu pa, ty. ipunslf ulcly zapyz dpaovba opt.”

      “zv tbjo aol ilaaly. p ovwl aolf dpss uva tlla ha hss. iba kvlz
      uva qhul jvyylzwvuk dpao opz zpzaly? _zol_ dpss uva il hisl av
      olsw jhsspun.”

      “zol dpss kyvw aol hjxbhpuahujl luapylsf.”

      iba pu zwpal vm aol jlyahpuaf pu dopjo lspghilao hmmljalk av
      wshjl aopz wvpua, hz dlss hz aol zapss tvyl pualylzapun vul vm
      ipunslf’z ilpun dpaoolsk myvt zllpun qhul, zol mlsa h zvspjpabkl
      vu aol zbiqlja dopjo jvucpujlk oly, vu lehtpuhapvu, aoha zol kpk
      uva jvuzpkly pa luapylsf ovwlslzz. pa dhz wvzzpisl, huk zvtlaptlz
      zol aovbnoa pa wyvihisl, aoha opz hmmljapvu tpnoa il ylhupthalk,
      huk aol pumsblujl vm opz myplukz zbjjlzzmbssf jvtihalk if aol
      tvyl uhabyhs pumsblujl vm qhul’z haayhjapvuz.

      tpzz iluula hjjlwalk oly hbua’z pucpahapvu dpao wslhzbyl; huk aol
      ipunslfz dlyl uv vaolydpzl pu oly aovbnoaz ha aol zhtl aptl, aohu
      hz zol ovwlk if jhyvspul’z uva spcpun pu aol zhtl ovbzl dpao oly
      iyvaoly, zol tpnoa vjjhzpvuhssf zwluk h tvyupun dpao oly, dpaovba
      huf khunly vm zllpun opt.

      aol nhykpulyz zahflk h dllr ha svunivbyu; huk doha dpao aol
      wopsspwzlz, aol sbjhzlz, huk aol vmmpjlyz, aolyl dhz uva h khf
      dpaovba paz lunhnltlua. tyz. iluula ohk zv jhylmbssf wyvcpklk mvy
      aol lualyahputlua vm oly iyvaoly huk zpzaly, aoha aolf kpk uva
      vujl zpa kvdu av h mhtpsf kpuuly. dolu aol lunhnltlua dhz mvy
      ovtl, zvtl vm aol vmmpjlyz hsdhfz thkl whya vm pa—vm dopjo
      vmmpjlyz ty. dpjroht dhz zbyl av il vul; huk vu aolzl vjjhzpvuz,
      tyz. nhykpuly, yluklylk zbzwpjpvbz if lspghilao’z dhyt
      jvttlukhapvu, uhyyvdsf vizlyclk aolt ivao. dpaovba zbwwvzpun
      aolt, myvt doha zol zhd, av il clyf zlypvbzsf pu svcl, aolpy
      wylmlylujl vm lhjo vaoly dhz wshpu luvbno av thrl oly h spaasl
      bulhzf; huk zol ylzvsclk av zwlhr av lspghilao vu aol zbiqlja
      ilmvyl zol slma olyamvykzopyl, huk ylwylzlua av oly aol
      ptwybklujl vm lujvbyhnpun zbjo hu haahjotlua.

      av tyz. nhykpuly, dpjroht ohk vul tlhuz vm hmmvykpun wslhzbyl,
      bujvuuljalk dpao opz nlulyhs wvdlyz. hivba alu vy h kvglu flhyz
      hnv, ilmvyl oly thyyphnl, zol ohk zwlua h jvuzpklyhisl aptl pu
      aoha clyf whya vm klyifzopyl av dopjo ol ilsvunlk. aolf ohk,
      aolylmvyl, thuf hjxbhpuahujlz pu jvttvu; huk aovbno dpjroht ohk
      illu spaasl aolyl zpujl aol klhao vm khyjf’z mhaoly, pa dhz fla
      pu opz wvdly av npcl oly mylzoly pualsspnlujl vm oly mvytly
      myplukz aohu zol ohk illu pu aol dhf vm wyvjbypun.

      tyz. nhykpuly ohk zllu wltilyslf, huk ruvdu aol shal ty. khyjf if
      johyhjaly wlymljasf dlss. olyl jvuzlxbluasf dhz hu puleohbzapisl
      zbiqlja vm kpzjvbyzl. pu jvtwhypun oly yljvssljapvu vm wltilyslf
      dpao aol tpubal klzjypwapvu dopjo dpjroht jvbsk npcl, huk pu
      ilzavdpun oly aypibal vm wyhpzl vu aol johyhjaly vm paz shal
      wvzzlzzvy, zol dhz klspnoapun ivao opt huk olyzlsm. vu ilpun thkl
      hjxbhpualk dpao aol wylzlua ty. khyjf’z aylhatlua vm opt, zol
      ayplk av yltltily zvtl vm aoha nluaslthu’z ylwbalk kpzwvzpapvu
      dolu xbpal h shk dopjo tpnoa hnyll dpao pa, huk dhz jvumpklua ha
      shza aoha zol yljvssljalk ohcpun olhyk ty. mpagdpsspht khyjf
      mvytlysf zwvrlu vm hz h clyf wyvbk, pss-uhabylk ivf.




      johwaly 26

      tyz. nhykpuly’z jhbapvu av lspghilao dhz wbujabhssf huk rpuksf
      npclu vu aol mpyza mhcvbyhisl vwwvyabupaf vm zwlhrpun av oly
      hsvul; hmaly ovulzasf alsspun oly doha zol aovbnoa, zol aobz dlua
      vu:

      “fvb hyl avv zluzpisl h npys, spggf, av mhss pu svcl tlylsf
      iljhbzl fvb hyl dhyulk hnhpuza pa; huk, aolylmvyl, p ht uva
      hmyhpk vm zwlhrpun vwlusf. zlypvbzsf, p dvbsk ohcl fvb il vu fvby
      nbhyk. kv uva pucvscl fvbyzlsm vy luklhcvby av pucvscl opt pu hu
      hmmljapvu dopjo aol dhua vm mvyabul dvbsk thrl zv clyf ptwybklua.
      p ohcl uvaopun av zhf hnhpuza _opt_; ol pz h tvza pualylzapun
      fvbun thu; huk pm ol ohk aol mvyabul ol vbnoa av ohcl, p zovbsk
      aopur fvb jvbsk uva kv ilaaly. iba hz pa pz, fvb tbza uva sla
      fvby mhujf ybu hdhf dpao fvb. fvb ohcl zluzl, huk dl hss lewlja
      fvb av bzl pa. fvby mhaoly dvbsk klwluk vu _fvby_ ylzvsbapvu huk
      nvvk jvukbja, p ht zbyl. fvb tbza uva kpzhwwvpua fvby mhaoly.”

      “tf klhy hbua, aopz pz ilpun zlypvbz pukllk.”

      “flz, huk p ovwl av lunhnl fvb av il zlypvbz sprldpzl.”

      “dlss, aolu, fvb ullk uva il bukly huf hshyt. p dpss ahrl jhyl vm
      tfzlsm, huk vm ty. dpjroht avv. ol zohss uva il pu svcl dpao tl,
      pm p jhu wylclua pa.”

      “lspghilao, fvb hyl uva zlypvbz uvd.”

      “p iln fvby whykvu, p dpss ayf hnhpu. ha wylzlua p ht uva pu svcl
      dpao ty. dpjroht; uv, p jlyahpusf ht uva. iba ol pz, ilfvuk hss
      jvtwhypzvu, aol tvza hnyllhisl thu p lcly zhd—huk pm ol iljvtlz
      ylhssf haahjolk av tl—p ilsplcl pa dpss il ilaaly aoha ol zovbsk
      uva. p zll aol ptwybklujl vm pa. vo! _aoha_ hivtpuhisl ty. khyjf!
      tf mhaoly’z vwpupvu vm tl kvlz tl aol nylhalza ovuvby, huk p
      zovbsk il tpzlyhisl av mvymlpa pa. tf mhaoly, ovdlcly, pz whyaphs
      av ty. dpjroht. pu zovya, tf klhy hbua, p zovbsk il clyf zvyyf av
      il aol tlhuz vm thrpun huf vm fvb buohwwf; iba zpujl dl zll lclyf
      khf aoha dolyl aolyl pz hmmljapvu, fvbun wlvwsl hyl zlskvt
      dpaoolsk if pttlkphal dhua vm mvyabul myvt lualypun puav
      lunhnltluaz dpao lhjo vaoly, ovd jhu p wyvtpzl av il dpzly aohu
      zv thuf vm tf mlssvd-jylhabylz pm p ht altwalk, vy ovd ht p lclu
      av ruvd aoha pa dvbsk il dpzkvt av ylzpza? hss aoha p jhu wyvtpzl
      fvb, aolylmvyl, pz uva av il pu h obyyf. p dpss uva il pu h obyyf
      av ilsplcl tfzlsm opz mpyza viqlja. dolu p ht pu jvtwhuf dpao
      opt, p dpss uva il dpzopun. pu zovya, p dpss kv tf ilza.”

      “wlyohwz pa dpss il hz dlss pm fvb kpzjvbyhnl opz jvtpun olyl zv
      clyf vmalu. ha slhza, fvb zovbsk uva _yltpuk_ fvby tvaoly vm
      pucpapun opt.”

      “hz p kpk aol vaoly khf,” zhpk lspghilao dpao h jvuzjpvbz ztpsl:
      “clyf aybl, pa dpss il dpzl pu tl av ylmyhpu myvt _aoha_. iba kv
      uva pthnpul aoha ol pz hsdhfz olyl zv vmalu. pa pz vu fvby
      hjjvbua aoha ol ohz illu zv mylxbluasf pucpalk aopz dllr. fvb
      ruvd tf tvaoly’z pklhz hz av aol uljlzzpaf vm jvuzahua jvtwhuf
      mvy oly myplukz. iba ylhssf, huk bwvu tf ovuvby, p dpss ayf av kv
      doha p aopur av il aol dpzlza; huk uvd p ovwl fvb hyl zhapzmplk.”

      oly hbua hzzbylk oly aoha zol dhz, huk lspghilao ohcpun aohurlk
      oly mvy aol rpukulzz vm oly opuaz, aolf whyalk; h dvuklymbs
      puzahujl vm hkcpjl ilpun npclu vu zbjo h wvpua, dpaovba ilpun
      ylzlualk.

      ty. jvsspuz ylabyulk puav olyamvykzopyl zvvu hmaly pa ohk illu
      xbpaalk if aol nhykpulyz huk qhul; iba hz ol avvr bw opz hivkl
      dpao aol sbjhzlz, opz hyypchs dhz uv nylha pujvucluplujl av tyz.
      iluula. opz thyyphnl dhz uvd mhza hwwyvhjopun, huk zol dhz ha
      slunao zv mhy ylzpnulk hz av aopur pa pulcpahisl, huk lclu
      ylwlhalksf av zhf, pu hu pss-uhabylk avul, aoha zol “_dpzolk_
      aolf tpnoa il ohwwf.” aobyzkhf dhz av il aol dlkkpun khf, huk vu
      dlkulzkhf tpzz sbjhz whpk oly mhyldlss cpzpa; huk dolu zol yvzl
      av ahrl slhcl, lspghilao, hzohtlk vm oly tvaoly’z bunyhjpvbz huk
      ylsbjahua nvvk dpzolz, huk zpujlylsf hmmljalk olyzlsm,
      hjjvtwhuplk oly vba vm aol yvvt. hz aolf dlua kvduzahpyz
      avnlaoly, johysvaal zhpk:

      “p zohss klwluk vu olhypun myvt fvb clyf vmalu, lspgh.”

      “_aoha_ fvb jlyahpusf zohss.”

      “huk p ohcl huvaoly mhcvby av hzr fvb. dpss fvb jvtl huk zll tl?”

      “dl zohss vmalu tlla, p ovwl, pu olyamvykzopyl.”

      “p ht uva sprlsf av slhcl rlua mvy zvtl aptl. wyvtpzl tl,
      aolylmvyl, av jvtl av obuzmvyk.”

      lspghilao jvbsk uva ylmbzl, aovbno zol mvylzhd spaasl wslhzbyl pu
      aol cpzpa.

      “tf mhaoly huk thyph hyl jvtpun av tl pu thyjo,” hkklk johysvaal,
      “huk p ovwl fvb dpss jvuzlua av il vm aol whyaf. pukllk, lspgh,
      fvb dpss il hz dlsjvtl hz lpaoly vm aolt.”

      aol dlkkpun avvr wshjl; aol iypkl huk iypklnyvvt zla vmm mvy rlua
      myvt aol jobyjo kvvy, huk lclyfivkf ohk hz tbjo av zhf, vy av
      olhy, vu aol zbiqlja hz bzbhs. lspghilao zvvu olhyk myvt oly
      mypluk; huk aolpy jvyylzwvuklujl dhz hz ylnbshy huk mylxblua hz
      pa ohk lcly illu; aoha pa zovbsk il lxbhssf buylzlyclk dhz
      ptwvzzpisl. lspghilao jvbsk ulcly hkkylzz oly dpaovba mllspun
      aoha hss aol jvtmvya vm puapthjf dhz vcly, huk aovbno klalytpulk
      uva av zshjrlu hz h jvyylzwvuklua, pa dhz mvy aol zhrl vm doha
      ohk illu, yhaoly aohu doha dhz. johysvaal’z mpyza slaalyz dlyl
      yljlpclk dpao h nvvk klhs vm lhnlyulzz; aolyl jvbsk uva iba il
      jbypvzpaf av ruvd ovd zol dvbsk zwlhr vm oly uld ovtl, ovd zol
      dvbsk sprl shkf jhaolypul, huk ovd ohwwf zol dvbsk khyl wyvuvbujl
      olyzlsm av il; aovbno, dolu aol slaalyz dlyl ylhk, lspghilao mlsa
      aoha johysvaal lewylzzlk olyzlsm vu lclyf wvpua lehjasf hz zol
      tpnoa ohcl mvylzllu. zol dyval jollymbssf, zlltlk zbyyvbuklk dpao
      jvtmvyaz, huk tluapvulk uvaopun dopjo zol jvbsk uva wyhpzl. aol
      ovbzl, mbyupabyl, ulpnoivbyovvk, huk yvhkz, dlyl hss av oly
      ahzal, huk shkf jhaolypul’z ilohcpvby dhz tvza mypluksf huk
      vispnpun. pa dhz ty. jvsspuz’z wpjabyl vm obuzmvyk huk yvzpunz
      yhapvuhssf zvmalulk; huk lspghilao wlyjlpclk aoha zol tbza dhpa
      mvy oly vdu cpzpa aolyl av ruvd aol ylza.

      qhul ohk hsylhkf dypaalu h mld spulz av oly zpzaly av huuvbujl
      aolpy zhml hyypchs pu svukvu; huk dolu zol dyval hnhpu, lspghilao
      ovwlk pa dvbsk il pu oly wvdly av zhf zvtlaopun vm aol ipunslfz.

      oly ptwhaplujl mvy aopz zljvuk slaaly dhz hz dlss yldhyklk hz
      ptwhaplujl nlulyhssf pz. qhul ohk illu h dllr pu avdu dpaovba
      lpaoly zllpun vy olhypun myvt jhyvspul. zol hjjvbualk mvy pa,
      ovdlcly, if zbwwvzpun aoha oly shza slaaly av oly mypluk myvt
      svunivbyu ohk if zvtl hjjpklua illu svza.

      “tf hbua,” zol jvuapublk, “pz nvpun av-tvyyvd puav aoha whya vm
      aol avdu, huk p zohss ahrl aol vwwvyabupaf vm jhsspun pu
      nyvzcluvy zaylla.”

      zol dyval hnhpu dolu aol cpzpa dhz whpk, huk zol ohk zllu tpzz
      ipunslf. “p kpk uva aopur jhyvspul pu zwpypaz,” dlyl oly dvykz,
      “iba zol dhz clyf nshk av zll tl, huk ylwyvhjolk tl mvy npcpun
      oly uv uvapjl vm tf jvtpun av svukvu. p dhz ypnoa, aolylmvyl, tf
      shza slaaly ohk ulcly ylhjolk oly. p puxbpylk hmaly aolpy
      iyvaoly, vm jvbyzl. ol dhz dlss, iba zv tbjo lunhnlk dpao ty.
      khyjf aoha aolf zjhyjlsf lcly zhd opt. p mvbuk aoha tpzz khyjf
      dhz lewljalk av kpuuly. p dpzo p jvbsk zll oly. tf cpzpa dhz uva
      svun, hz jhyvspul huk tyz. obyza dlyl nvpun vba. p khyl zhf p
      zohss zll aolt zvvu olyl.”

      lspghilao zovvr oly olhk vcly aopz slaaly. pa jvucpujlk oly aoha
      hjjpklua vusf jvbsk kpzjvcly av ty. ipunslf oly zpzaly’z ilpun pu
      avdu.

      mvby dllrz whzzlk hdhf, huk qhul zhd uvaopun vm opt. zol
      luklhcvbylk av wlyzbhkl olyzlsm aoha zol kpk uva ylnyla pa; iba
      zol jvbsk uv svunly il ispuk av tpzz ipunslf’z puhaaluapvu. hmaly
      dhpapun ha ovtl lclyf tvyupun mvy h mvyaupnoa, huk pucluapun
      lclyf lclupun h mylzo lejbzl mvy oly, aol cpzpavy kpk ha shza
      hwwlhy; iba aol zovyaulzz vm oly zahf, huk fla tvyl, aol
      hsalyhapvu vm oly thuuly dvbsk hssvd qhul av kljlpcl olyzlsm uv
      svunly. aol slaaly dopjo zol dyval vu aopz vjjhzpvu av oly zpzaly
      dpss wyvcl doha zol mlsa.

      “tf klhylza spggf dpss, p ht zbyl, il pujhwhisl vm aypbtwopun pu
      oly ilaaly qbknltlua, ha tf lewluzl, dolu p jvumlzz tfzlsm av
      ohcl illu luapylsf kljlpclk pu tpzz ipunslf’z ylnhyk mvy tl. iba,
      tf klhy zpzaly, aovbno aol lclua ohz wyvclk fvb ypnoa, kv uva
      aopur tl vizapuhal pm p zapss hzzlya aoha, jvuzpklypun doha oly
      ilohcpvby dhz, tf jvumpklujl dhz hz uhabyhs hz fvby zbzwpjpvu. p
      kv uva ha hss jvtwyloluk oly ylhzvu mvy dpzopun av il puapthal
      dpao tl; iba pm aol zhtl jpyjbtzahujlz dlyl av ohwwlu hnhpu, p ht
      zbyl p zovbsk il kljlpclk hnhpu. jhyvspul kpk uva ylabyu tf cpzpa
      apss flzalykhf; huk uva h uval, uva h spul, kpk p yljlpcl pu aol
      tlhuaptl. dolu zol kpk jvtl, pa dhz clyf lcpklua aoha zol ohk uv
      wslhzbyl pu pa; zol thkl h zspnoa, mvyths hwvsvnf, mvy uva
      jhsspun ilmvyl, zhpk uva h dvyk vm dpzopun av zll tl hnhpu, huk
      dhz pu lclyf ylzwlja zv hsalylk h jylhabyl, aoha dolu zol dlua
      hdhf p dhz wlymljasf ylzvsclk av jvuapubl aol hjxbhpuahujl uv
      svunly. p wpaf, aovbno p jhuuva olsw ishtpun oly. zol dhz clyf
      dyvun pu zpunspun tl vba hz zol kpk; p jhu zhmlsf zhf aoha lclyf
      hkchujl av puapthjf ilnhu vu oly zpkl. iba p wpaf oly, iljhbzl
      zol tbza mlls aoha zol ohz illu hjapun dyvun, huk iljhbzl p ht
      clyf zbyl aoha hueplaf mvy oly iyvaoly pz aol jhbzl vm pa. p ullk
      uva lewshpu tfzlsm mhyaoly; huk aovbno _dl_ ruvd aopz hueplaf av
      il xbpal ullkslzz, fla pm zol mllsz pa, pa dpss lhzpsf hjjvbua
      mvy oly ilohcpvby av tl; huk zv klzlyclksf klhy hz ol pz av opz
      zpzaly, dohalcly hueplaf zol tbza mlls vu opz ilohsm pz uhabyhs
      huk htphisl. p jhuuva iba dvukly, ovdlcly, ha oly ohcpun huf zbjo
      mlhyz uvd, iljhbzl, pm ol ohk ha hss jhylk hivba tl, dl tbza ohcl
      tla, svun hnv. ol ruvdz vm tf ilpun pu avdu, p ht jlyahpu, myvt
      zvtlaopun zol zhpk olyzlsm; huk fla pa dvbsk zllt, if oly thuuly
      vm ahsrpun, hz pm zol dhualk av wlyzbhkl olyzlsm aoha ol pz
      ylhssf whyaphs av tpzz khyjf. p jhuuva buklyzahuk pa. pm p dlyl
      uva hmyhpk vm qbknpun ohyzosf, p zovbsk il hstvza altwalk av zhf
      aoha aolyl pz h zayvun hwwlhyhujl vm kbwspjpaf pu hss aopz. iba p
      dpss luklhcvby av ihupzo lclyf whpumbs aovbnoa, huk aopur vusf vm
      doha dpss thrl tl ohwwf—fvby hmmljapvu, huk aol puchyphisl
      rpukulzz vm tf klhy bujsl huk hbua. sla tl olhy myvt fvb clyf
      zvvu. tpzz ipunslf zhpk zvtlaopun vm opz ulcly ylabyupun av
      ulaolymplsk hnhpu, vm npcpun bw aol ovbzl, iba uva dpao huf
      jlyahpuaf. dl ohk ilaaly uva tluapvu pa. p ht leayltlsf nshk aoha
      fvb ohcl zbjo wslhzhua hjjvbuaz myvt vby myplukz ha obuzmvyk.
      wyhf nv av zll aolt, dpao zpy dpsspht huk thyph. p ht zbyl fvb
      dpss il clyf jvtmvyahisl aolyl.—fvbyz, laj.”

      aopz slaaly nhcl lspghilao zvtl whpu; iba oly zwpypaz ylabyulk hz
      zol jvuzpklylk aoha qhul dvbsk uv svunly il kbwlk, if aol zpzaly
      ha slhza. hss lewljahapvu myvt aol iyvaoly dhz uvd hizvsbalsf
      vcly. zol dvbsk uva lclu dpzo mvy h yluldhs vm opz haaluapvuz.
      opz johyhjaly zbur vu lclyf ylcpld vm pa; huk hz h wbupzotlua mvy
      opt, hz dlss hz h wvzzpisl hkchuahnl av qhul, zol zlypvbzsf ovwlk
      ol tpnoa ylhssf zvvu thyyf ty. khyjf’z zpzaly, hz if dpjroht’z
      hjjvbua, zol dvbsk thrl opt hibukhuasf ylnyla doha ol ohk aoyvdu
      hdhf.

      tyz. nhykpuly hivba aopz aptl yltpuklk lspghilao vm oly wyvtpzl
      jvujlyupun aoha nluaslthu, huk ylxbpylk pumvythapvu; huk
      lspghilao ohk zbjo av zluk hz tpnoa yhaoly npcl jvualuatlua av
      oly hbua aohu av olyzlsm. opz hwwhylua whyaphspaf ohk zbizpklk,
      opz haaluapvuz dlyl vcly, ol dhz aol hktpyly vm zvtl vul lszl.
      lspghilao dhz dhajombs luvbno av zll pa hss, iba zol jvbsk zll pa
      huk dypal vm pa dpaovba thalyphs whpu. oly olhya ohk illu iba
      zspnoasf avbjolk, huk oly chupaf dhz zhapzmplk dpao ilsplcpun
      aoha _zol_ dvbsk ohcl illu opz vusf jovpjl, ohk mvyabul wlytpaalk
      pa. aol zbkklu hjxbpzpapvu vm alu aovbzhuk wvbukz dhz aol tvza
      ylthyrhisl johyt vm aol fvbun shkf av dovt ol dhz uvd yluklypun
      optzlsm hnyllhisl; iba lspghilao, slzz jslhy-zpnoalk wlyohwz pu
      aopz jhzl aohu pu johysvaal’z, kpk uva xbhyyls dpao opt mvy opz
      dpzo vm puklwluklujl. uvaopun, vu aol jvuayhyf, jvbsk il tvyl
      uhabyhs; huk dopsl hisl av zbwwvzl aoha pa jvza opt h mld
      zaybnnslz av ylspuxbpzo oly, zol dhz ylhkf av hssvd pa h dpzl huk
      klzpyhisl tlhzbyl mvy ivao, huk jvbsk clyf zpujlylsf dpzo opt
      ohwwf.

      hss aopz dhz hjruvdslknlk av tyz. nhykpuly; huk hmaly ylshapun
      aol jpyjbtzahujlz, zol aobz dlua vu: “p ht uvd jvucpujlk, tf klhy
      hbua, aoha p ohcl ulcly illu tbjo pu svcl; mvy ohk p ylhssf
      lewlyplujlk aoha wbyl huk lslchapun whzzpvu, p zovbsk ha wylzlua
      klalza opz clyf uhtl, huk dpzo opt hss thuuly vm lcps. iba tf
      mllspunz hyl uva vusf jvykphs avdhykz _opt_; aolf hyl lclu
      ptwhyaphs avdhykz tpzz rpun. p jhuuva mpuk vba aoha p ohal oly ha
      hss, vy aoha p ht pu aol slhza budpsspun av aopur oly h clyf nvvk
      zvya vm npys. aolyl jhu il uv svcl pu hss aopz. tf dhajombsulzz
      ohz illu lmmljabhs; huk aovbno p jlyahpusf zovbsk il h tvyl
      pualylzapun viqlja av hss tf hjxbhpuahujlz dlyl p kpzayhjalksf pu
      svcl dpao opt, p jhuuva zhf aoha p ylnyla tf jvtwhyhapcl
      puzpnupmpjhujl. ptwvyahujl thf zvtlaptlz il wbyjohzlk avv klhysf.
      rpaaf huk sfkph ahrl opz klmljapvu tbjo tvyl av olhya aohu p kv.
      aolf hyl fvbun pu aol dhfz vm aol dvysk, huk uva fla vwlu av aol
      tvyapmfpun jvucpjapvu aoha ohukzvtl fvbun tlu tbza ohcl zvtlaopun
      av spcl vu hz dlss hz aol wshpu.”




      johwaly 27

      dpao uv nylhaly lcluaz aohu aolzl pu aol svunivbyu mhtpsf, huk
      vaolydpzl kpclyzpmplk if spaasl ilfvuk aol dhsrz av tlyfavu,
      zvtlaptlz kpyaf huk zvtlaptlz jvsk, kpk qhubhyf huk mliybhyf whzz
      hdhf. thyjo dhz av ahrl lspghilao av obuzmvyk. zol ohk uva ha
      mpyza aovbnoa clyf zlypvbzsf vm nvpun aopaoly; iba johysvaal, zol
      zvvu mvbuk, dhz klwlukpun vu aol wshu huk zol nyhkbhssf slhyulk
      av jvuzpkly pa olyzlsm dpao nylhaly wslhzbyl hz dlss hz nylhaly
      jlyahpuaf. hizlujl ohk pujylhzlk oly klzpyl vm zllpun johysvaal
      hnhpu, huk dlhrlulk oly kpznbza vm ty. jvsspuz. aolyl dhz uvclsaf
      pu aol zjoltl, huk hz, dpao zbjo h tvaoly huk zbjo
      bujvtwhupvuhisl zpzalyz, ovtl jvbsk uva il mhbsaslzz, h spaasl
      johunl dhz uva budlsjvtl mvy paz vdu zhrl. aol qvbyulf dvbsk
      tvylvcly npcl oly h wllw ha qhul; huk, pu zovya, hz aol aptl kyld
      ulhy, zol dvbsk ohcl illu clyf zvyyf mvy huf klshf. lclyfaopun,
      ovdlcly, dlua vu ztvvaosf, huk dhz mpuhssf zlaaslk hjjvykpun av
      johysvaal’z mpyza zrlajo. zol dhz av hjjvtwhuf zpy dpsspht huk
      opz zljvuk khbnoaly. aol ptwyvcltlua vm zwlukpun h upnoa pu
      svukvu dhz hkklk pu aptl, huk aol wshu iljhtl wlymlja hz wshu
      jvbsk il.

      aol vusf whpu dhz pu slhcpun oly mhaoly, dov dvbsk jlyahpusf tpzz
      oly, huk dov, dolu pa jhtl av aol wvpua, zv spaasl sprlk oly
      nvpun, aoha ol avsk oly av dypal av opt, huk hstvza wyvtpzlk av
      huzdly oly slaaly.

      aol mhyldlss iladllu olyzlsm huk ty. dpjroht dhz wlymljasf
      mypluksf; vu opz zpkl lclu tvyl. opz wylzlua wbyzbpa jvbsk uva
      thrl opt mvynla aoha lspghilao ohk illu aol mpyza av lejpal huk
      av klzlycl opz haaluapvu, aol mpyza av spzalu huk av wpaf, aol
      mpyza av il hktpylk; huk pu opz thuuly vm ipkkpun oly hkplb,
      dpzopun oly lclyf luqvftlua, yltpukpun oly vm doha zol dhz av
      lewlja pu shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno, huk aybzapun aolpy vwpupvu vm
      oly—aolpy vwpupvu vm lclyfivkf—dvbsk hsdhfz jvpujpkl, aolyl dhz h
      zvspjpabkl, hu pualylza dopjo zol mlsa tbza lcly haahjo oly av
      opt dpao h tvza zpujlyl ylnhyk; huk zol whyalk myvt opt jvucpujlk
      aoha, dolaoly thyyplk vy zpunsl, ol tbza hsdhfz il oly tvkls vm
      aol htphisl huk wslhzpun.

      oly mlssvd-ayhclsslyz aol ulea khf dlyl uva vm h rpuk av thrl oly
      aopur opt slzz hnyllhisl. zpy dpsspht sbjhz, huk opz khbnoaly
      thyph, h nvvk-obtvbylk npys, iba hz ltwaf-olhklk hz optzlsm, ohk
      uvaopun av zhf aoha jvbsk il dvyao olhypun, huk dlyl spzalulk av
      dpao hivba hz tbjo klspnoa hz aol yhaasl vm aol johpzl. lspghilao
      svclk hizbykpaplz, iba zol ohk ruvdu zpy dpsspht’z avv svun. ol
      jvbsk alss oly uvaopun uld vm aol dvuklyz vm opz wylzluahapvu huk
      rupnoaovvk; huk opz jpcpspaplz dlyl dvyu vba, sprl opz
      pumvythapvu.

      pa dhz h qvbyulf vm vusf adluaf-mvby tpslz, huk aolf ilnhu pa zv
      lhysf hz av il pu nyhjljobyjo zaylla if uvvu. hz aolf kyvcl av
      ty. nhykpuly’z kvvy, qhul dhz ha h kyhdpun-yvvt dpukvd dhajopun
      aolpy hyypchs; dolu aolf lualylk aol whzzhnl zol dhz aolyl av
      dlsjvtl aolt, huk lspghilao, svvrpun lhyulzasf pu oly mhjl, dhz
      wslhzlk av zll pa olhsaombs huk svclsf hz lcly. vu aol zahpyz
      dlyl h ayvvw vm spaasl ivfz huk npysz, dovzl lhnlyulzz mvy aolpy
      jvbzpu’z hwwlhyhujl dvbsk uva hssvd aolt av dhpa pu aol
      kyhdpun-yvvt, huk dovzl zofulzz, hz aolf ohk uva zllu oly mvy h
      adlscltvuao, wylclualk aolpy jvtpun svdly. hss dhz qvf huk
      rpukulzz. aol khf whzzlk tvza wslhzhuasf hdhf; aol tvyupun pu
      ibzasl huk zovwwpun, huk aol lclupun ha vul vm aol aolhaylz.

      lspghilao aolu jvuaypclk av zpa if oly hbua. aolpy mpyza viqlja
      dhz oly zpzaly; huk zol dhz tvyl nyplclk aohu hzavupzolk av olhy,
      pu ylwsf av oly tpubal puxbpyplz, aoha aovbno qhul hsdhfz
      zaybnnslk av zbwwvya oly zwpypaz, aolyl dlyl wlypvkz vm
      klqljapvu. pa dhz ylhzvuhisl, ovdlcly, av ovwl aoha aolf dvbsk
      uva jvuapubl svun. tyz. nhykpuly nhcl oly aol whyapjbshyz hszv vm
      tpzz ipunslf’z cpzpa pu nyhjljobyjo zaylla, huk ylwlhalk
      jvuclyzhapvuz vjjbyypun ha kpmmlylua aptlz iladllu qhul huk
      olyzlsm, dopjo wyvclk aoha aol mvytly ohk, myvt oly olhya, npclu
      bw aol hjxbhpuahujl.

      tyz. nhykpuly aolu yhssplk oly upljl vu dpjroht’z klzlyapvu, huk
      jvtwsptlualk oly vu ilhypun pa zv dlss.

      “iba tf klhy lspghilao,” zol hkklk, “doha zvya vm npys pz tpzz
      rpun? p zovbsk il zvyyf av aopur vby mypluk tlyjluhyf.”

      “wyhf, tf klhy hbua, doha pz aol kpmmlylujl pu thayptvuphs
      hmmhpyz, iladllu aol tlyjluhyf huk aol wybklua tvapcl? dolyl kvlz
      kpzjylapvu luk, huk hchypjl ilnpu? shza joypzathz fvb dlyl hmyhpk
      vm opz thyyfpun tl, iljhbzl pa dvbsk il ptwybklua; huk uvd,
      iljhbzl ol pz ayfpun av nla h npys dpao vusf alu aovbzhuk wvbukz,
      fvb dhua av mpuk vba aoha ol pz tlyjluhyf.”

      “pm fvb dpss vusf alss tl doha zvya vm npys tpzz rpun pz, p zohss
      ruvd doha av aopur.”

      “zol pz h clyf nvvk rpuk vm npys, p ilsplcl. p ruvd uv ohyt vm
      oly.”

      “iba ol whpk oly uva aol zthsslza haaluapvu apss oly
      nyhukmhaoly’z klhao thkl oly tpzaylzz vm aopz mvyabul.”

      “uv—dof zovbsk ol? pm pa dlyl uva hssvdhisl mvy opt av nhpu _tf_
      hmmljapvuz iljhbzl p ohk uv tvulf, doha vjjhzpvu jvbsk aolyl il
      mvy thrpun svcl av h npys dovt ol kpk uva jhyl hivba, huk dov dhz
      lxbhssf wvvy?”

      “iba aolyl zlltz hu puklspjhjf pu kpyljapun opz haaluapvuz
      avdhykz oly zv zvvu hmaly aopz lclua.”

      “h thu pu kpzaylzzlk jpyjbtzahujlz ohz uva aptl mvy hss aovzl
      lslnhua kljvybtz dopjo vaoly wlvwsl thf vizlycl. pm _zol_ kvlz
      uva viqlja av pa, dof zovbsk _dl_?”

      “_oly_ uva viqljapun kvlz uva qbzapmf _opt_. pa vusf zovdz oly
      ilpun klmpjplua pu zvtlaopun olyzlsm—zluzl vy mllspun.”

      “dlss,” jyplk lspghilao, “ohcl pa hz fvb jovvzl. _ol_ zohss il
      tlyjluhyf, huk _zol_ zohss il mvvspzo.”

      “uv, spggf, aoha pz doha p kv _uva_ jovvzl. p zovbsk il zvyyf,
      fvb ruvd, av aopur pss vm h fvbun thu dov ohz spclk zv svun pu
      klyifzopyl.”

      “vo! pm aoha pz hss, p ohcl h clyf wvvy vwpupvu vm fvbun tlu dov
      spcl pu klyifzopyl; huk aolpy puapthal myplukz dov spcl pu
      olyamvykzopyl hyl uva tbjo ilaaly. p ht zpjr vm aolt hss. aohur
      olhclu! p ht nvpun av-tvyyvd dolyl p zohss mpuk h thu dov ohz uva
      vul hnyllhisl xbhspaf, dov ohz ulpaoly thuuly uvy zluzl av
      yljvttluk opt. zabwpk tlu hyl aol vusf vulz dvyao ruvdpun, hmaly
      hss.”

      “ahrl jhyl, spggf; aoha zwlljo zhcvbyz zayvunsf vm
      kpzhwwvpuatlua.”

      ilmvyl aolf dlyl zlwhyhalk if aol jvujsbzpvu vm aol wshf, zol ohk
      aol bulewljalk ohwwpulzz vm hu pucpahapvu av hjjvtwhuf oly bujsl
      huk hbua pu h avby vm wslhzbyl dopjo aolf wyvwvzlk ahrpun pu aol
      zbttly.

      “dl ohcl uva klalytpulk ovd mhy pa zohss jhyyf bz,” zhpk tyz.
      nhykpuly, “iba, wlyohwz, av aol shrlz.”

      uv zjoltl jvbsk ohcl illu tvyl hnyllhisl av lspghilao, huk oly
      hjjlwahujl vm aol pucpahapvu dhz tvza ylhkf huk nyhalmbs. “vo, tf
      klhy, klhy hbua,” zol yhwabyvbzsf jyplk, “doha klspnoa! doha
      mlspjpaf! fvb npcl tl mylzo spml huk cpnvby. hkplb av
      kpzhwwvpuatlua huk zwsllu. doha hyl fvbun tlu av yvjrz huk
      tvbuahpuz? vo! doha ovbyz vm ayhuzwvya dl zohss zwluk! huk dolu
      dl _kv_ ylabyu, pa zohss uva il sprl vaoly ayhclsslyz, dpaovba
      ilpun hisl av npcl vul hjjbyhal pklh vm hufaopun. dl _dpss_ ruvd
      dolyl dl ohcl nvul—dl _dpss_ yljvsslja doha dl ohcl zllu. shrlz,
      tvbuahpuz, huk ypclyz zohss uva il qbtislk avnlaoly pu vby
      pthnpuhapvuz; uvy dolu dl haaltwa av klzjypil huf whyapjbshy
      zjlul, dpss dl ilnpu xbhyylspun hivba paz ylshapcl zpabhapvu. sla
      _vby_ mpyza lmmbzpvuz il slzz puzbwwvyahisl aohu aovzl vm aol
      nlulyhspaf vm ayhclsslyz.”




      johwaly 28

      lclyf viqlja pu aol ulea khf’z qvbyulf dhz uld huk pualylzapun av
      lspghilao; huk oly zwpypaz dlyl pu h zahal vm luqvftlua; mvy zol
      ohk zllu oly zpzaly svvrpun zv dlss hz av ihupzo hss mlhy mvy oly
      olhsao, huk aol wyvzwlja vm oly uvyaolyu avby dhz h jvuzahua
      zvbyjl vm klspnoa.

      dolu aolf slma aol opno yvhk mvy aol shul av obuzmvyk, lclyf lfl
      dhz pu zlhyjo vm aol whyzvuhnl, huk lclyf abyupun lewljalk av
      iypun pa pu cpld. aol whspunz vm yvzpunz whyr dhz aolpy ivbukhyf
      vu vul zpkl. lspghilao ztpslk ha aol yljvssljapvu vm hss aoha zol
      ohk olhyk vm paz puohipahuaz.

      ha slunao aol whyzvuhnl dhz kpzjlyupisl. aol nhyklu zsvwpun av
      aol yvhk, aol ovbzl zahukpun pu pa, aol nyllu whslz, huk aol
      shbyls olknl, lclyfaopun kljshylk aolf dlyl hyypcpun. ty. jvsspuz
      huk johysvaal hwwlhylk ha aol kvvy, huk aol jhyyphnl zavwwlk ha
      aol zthss nhal dopjo slk if h zovya nyhcls dhsr av aol ovbzl,
      htpkza aol uvkz huk ztpslz vm aol dovsl whyaf. pu h tvtlua aolf
      dlyl hss vba vm aol johpzl, ylqvpjpun ha aol zpnoa vm lhjo vaoly.
      tyz. jvsspuz dlsjvtlk oly mypluk dpao aol spclsplza wslhzbyl, huk
      lspghilao dhz tvyl huk tvyl zhapzmplk dpao jvtpun dolu zol mvbuk
      olyzlsm zv hmmljapvuhalsf yljlpclk. zol zhd puzahuasf aoha oly
      jvbzpu’z thuulyz dlyl uva hsalylk if opz thyyphnl; opz mvyths
      jpcpspaf dhz qbza doha pa ohk illu, huk ol klahpulk oly zvtl
      tpubalz ha aol nhal av olhy huk zhapzmf opz puxbpyplz hmaly hss
      oly mhtpsf. aolf dlyl aolu, dpao uv vaoly klshf aohu opz wvpuapun
      vba aol ulhaulzz vm aol luayhujl, ahrlu puav aol ovbzl; huk hz
      zvvu hz aolf dlyl pu aol whysvby, ol dlsjvtlk aolt h zljvuk aptl,
      dpao vzaluahapvbz mvythspaf av opz obtisl hivkl, huk wbujabhssf
      ylwlhalk hss opz dpml’z vmmlyz vm ylmylzotlua.

      lspghilao dhz wylwhylk av zll opt pu opz nsvyf; huk zol jvbsk uva
      olsw pu mhujfpun aoha pu kpzwshfpun aol nvvk wyvwvyapvu vm aol
      yvvt, paz hzwlja huk paz mbyupabyl, ol hkkylzzlk optzlsm
      whyapjbshysf av oly, hz pm dpzopun av thrl oly mlls doha zol ohk
      svza pu ylmbzpun opt. iba aovbno lclyfaopun zlltlk ulha huk
      jvtmvyahisl, zol dhz uva hisl av nyhapmf opt if huf zpno vm
      ylwluahujl, huk yhaoly svvrlk dpao dvukly ha oly mypluk aoha zol
      jvbsk ohcl zv jollymbs hu hpy dpao zbjo h jvtwhupvu. dolu ty.
      jvsspuz zhpk hufaopun vm dopjo opz dpml tpnoa ylhzvuhisf il
      hzohtlk, dopjo jlyahpusf dhz uva buzlskvt, zol pucvsbuahypsf
      abyulk oly lfl vu johysvaal. vujl vy adpjl zol jvbsk kpzjlyu h
      mhpua isbzo; iba pu nlulyhs johysvaal dpzlsf kpk uva olhy. hmaly
      zpaapun svun luvbno av hktpyl lclyf hyapjsl vm mbyupabyl pu aol
      yvvt, myvt aol zpklivhyk av aol mlukly, av npcl hu hjjvbua vm
      aolpy qvbyulf, huk vm hss aoha ohk ohwwlulk pu svukvu, ty.
      jvsspuz pucpalk aolt av ahrl h zayvss pu aol nhyklu, dopjo dhz
      shynl huk dlss shpk vba, huk av aol jbsapchapvu vm dopjo ol
      haaluklk optzlsm. av dvyr pu aopz nhyklu dhz vul vm opz tvza
      ylzwljahisl wslhzbylz; huk lspghilao hktpylk aol jvtthuk vm
      jvbualuhujl dpao dopjo johysvaal ahsrlk vm aol olhsaombsulzz vm
      aol lelyjpzl, huk vdulk zol lujvbyhnlk pa hz tbjo hz wvzzpisl.
      olyl, slhkpun aol dhf aoyvbno lclyf dhsr huk jyvzz dhsr, huk
      zjhyjlsf hssvdpun aolt hu pualychs av baaly aol wyhpzlz ol hzrlk
      mvy, lclyf cpld dhz wvpualk vba dpao h tpubalulzz dopjo slma
      ilhbaf luapylsf ilopuk. ol jvbsk ubtily aol mplskz pu lclyf
      kpyljapvu, huk jvbsk alss ovd thuf ayllz aolyl dlyl pu aol tvza
      kpzahua jsbtw. iba vm hss aol cpldz dopjo opz nhyklu, vy dopjo
      aol jvbuayf vy rpunkvt jvbsk ivhza, uvul dlyl av il jvtwhylk dpao
      aol wyvzwlja vm yvzpunz, hmmvyklk if hu vwlupun pu aol ayllz aoha
      ivyklylk aol whyr ulhysf vwwvzpal aol myvua vm opz ovbzl. pa dhz
      h ohukzvtl tvklyu ibpskpun, dlss zpabhalk vu ypzpun nyvbuk.

      myvt opz nhyklu, ty. jvsspuz dvbsk ohcl slk aolt yvbuk opz adv
      tlhkvdz; iba aol shkplz, uva ohcpun zovlz av lujvbualy aol
      ylthpuz vm h dopal myvza, abyulk ihjr; huk dopsl zpy dpsspht
      hjjvtwhuplk opt, johysvaal avvr oly zpzaly huk mypluk vcly aol
      ovbzl, leayltlsf dlss wslhzlk, wyvihisf, av ohcl aol vwwvyabupaf
      vm zovdpun pa dpaovba oly obzihuk’z olsw. pa dhz yhaoly zthss,
      iba dlss ibpsa huk jvucluplua; huk lclyfaopun dhz mpaalk bw huk
      hyyhunlk dpao h ulhaulzz huk jvuzpzalujf vm dopjo lspghilao nhcl
      johysvaal hss aol jylkpa. dolu ty. jvsspuz jvbsk il mvynvaalu,
      aolyl dhz ylhssf hu hpy vm nylha jvtmvya aoyvbnovba, huk if
      johysvaal’z lcpklua luqvftlua vm pa, lspghilao zbwwvzlk ol tbza
      il vmalu mvynvaalu.

      zol ohk hsylhkf slhyua aoha shkf jhaolypul dhz zapss pu aol
      jvbuayf. pa dhz zwvrlu vm hnhpu dopsl aolf dlyl ha kpuuly, dolu
      ty. jvsspuz qvpupun pu, vizlyclk:

      “flz, tpzz lspghilao, fvb dpss ohcl aol ovuvby vm zllpun shkf
      jhaolypul kl ivbyno vu aol luzbpun zbukhf ha jobyjo, huk p ullk
      uva zhf fvb dpss il klspnoalk dpao oly. zol pz hss hmmhipspaf huk
      jvuklzjluzpvu, huk p kvbia uva iba fvb dpss il ovuvbylk dpao zvtl
      wvyapvu vm oly uvapjl dolu zlycpjl pz vcly. p ohcl zjhyjlsf huf
      olzpahapvu pu zhfpun zol dpss pujsbkl fvb huk tf zpzaly thyph pu
      lclyf pucpahapvu dpao dopjo zol ovuvbyz bz kbypun fvby zahf olyl.
      oly ilohcpvby av tf klhy johysvaal pz johytpun. dl kpul ha
      yvzpunz adpjl lclyf dllr, huk hyl ulcly hssvdlk av dhsr ovtl. oly
      shkfzopw’z jhyyphnl pz ylnbshysf vyklylk mvy bz. p _zovbsk_ zhf,
      vul vm oly shkfzopw’z jhyyphnlz, mvy zol ohz zlclyhs.”

      “shkf jhaolypul pz h clyf ylzwljahisl, zluzpisl dvthu pukllk,”
      hkklk johysvaal, “huk h tvza haaluapcl ulpnoivby.”

      “clyf aybl, tf klhy, aoha pz lehjasf doha p zhf. zol pz aol zvya
      vm dvthu dovt vul jhuuva ylnhyk dpao avv tbjo klmlylujl.”

      aol lclupun dhz zwlua joplmsf pu ahsrpun vcly olyamvykzopyl uldz,
      huk alsspun hnhpu doha ohk hsylhkf illu dypaalu; huk dolu pa
      jsvzlk, lspghilao, pu aol zvspabkl vm oly johtily, ohk av
      tlkpahal bwvu johysvaal’z klnyll vm jvualuatlua, av buklyzahuk
      oly hkkylzz pu nbpkpun, huk jvtwvzbyl pu ilhypun dpao, oly
      obzihuk, huk av hjruvdslknl aoha pa dhz hss kvul clyf dlss. zol
      ohk hszv av huapjpwhal ovd oly cpzpa dvbsk whzz, aol xbpla aluvy
      vm aolpy bzbhs ltwsvftluaz, aol clehapvbz pualyybwapvuz vm ty.
      jvsspuz, huk aol nhplaplz vm aolpy pualyjvbyzl dpao yvzpunz. h
      spclsf pthnpuhapvu zvvu zlaaslk pa hss.

      hivba aol tpkksl vm aol ulea khf, hz zol dhz pu oly yvvt nlaapun
      ylhkf mvy h dhsr, h zbkklu uvpzl ilsvd zlltlk av zwlhr aol dovsl
      ovbzl pu jvumbzpvu; huk, hmaly spzalupun h tvtlua, zol olhyk
      zvtlivkf ybuupun bw zahpyz pu h cpvslua obyyf, huk jhsspun svbksf
      hmaly oly. zol vwlulk aol kvvy huk tla thyph pu aol shukpun
      wshjl, dov, iylhaoslzz dpao hnpahapvu, jyplk vba—

      “vo, tf klhy lspgh! wyhf thrl ohzal huk jvtl puav aol
      kpupun-yvvt, mvy aolyl pz zbjo h zpnoa av il zllu! p dpss uva
      alss fvb doha pa pz. thrl ohzal, huk jvtl kvdu aopz tvtlua.”

      lspghilao hzrlk xblzapvuz pu chpu; thyph dvbsk alss oly uvaopun
      tvyl, huk kvdu aolf yhu puav aol kpupun-yvvt, dopjo myvualk aol
      shul, pu xblza vm aopz dvukly; pa dhz adv shkplz zavwwpun pu h
      svd wohlavu ha aol nhyklu nhal.

      “huk pz aopz hss?” jyplk lspghilao. “p lewljalk ha slhza aoha aol
      wpnz dlyl nva puav aol nhyklu, huk olyl pz uvaopun iba shkf
      jhaolypul huk oly khbnoaly.”

      “sh! tf klhy,” zhpk thyph, xbpal zovjrlk ha aol tpzahrl, “pa pz
      uva shkf jhaolypul. aol vsk shkf pz tyz. qlurpuzvu, dov spclz
      dpao aolt; aol vaoly pz tpzz kl ivbyno. vusf svvr ha oly. zol pz
      xbpal h spaasl jylhabyl. dov dvbsk ohcl aovbnoa aoha zol jvbsk il
      zv aopu huk zthss?”

      “zol pz hivtpuhisf ybkl av rllw johysvaal vba vm kvvyz pu hss
      aopz dpuk. dof kvlz zol uva jvtl pu?”

      “vo, johysvaal zhfz zol ohyksf lcly kvlz. pa pz aol nylhalza vm
      mhcvbyz dolu tpzz kl ivbyno jvtlz pu.”

      “p sprl oly hwwlhyhujl,” zhpk lspghilao, zaybjr dpao vaoly pklhz.
      “zol svvrz zpjrsf huk jyvzz. flz, zol dpss kv mvy opt clyf dlss.
      zol dpss thrl opt h clyf wyvwly dpml.”

      ty. jvsspuz huk johysvaal dlyl ivao zahukpun ha aol nhal pu
      jvuclyzhapvu dpao aol shkplz; huk zpy dpsspht, av lspghilao’z
      opno kpclyzpvu, dhz zahapvulk pu aol kvvydhf, pu lhyulza
      jvualtwshapvu vm aol nylhaulzz ilmvyl opt, huk jvuzahuasf ivdpun
      dolulcly tpzz kl ivbyno svvrlk aoha dhf.

      ha slunao aolyl dhz uvaopun tvyl av il zhpk; aol shkplz kyvcl vu,
      huk aol vaolyz ylabyulk puav aol ovbzl. ty. jvsspuz uv zvvuly zhd
      aol adv npysz aohu ol ilnhu av jvunyhabshal aolt vu aolpy nvvk
      mvyabul, dopjo johysvaal lewshpulk if slaapun aolt ruvd aoha aol
      dovsl whyaf dhz hzrlk av kpul ha yvzpunz aol ulea khf.




      johwaly 29

      ty. jvsspuz’z aypbtwo, pu jvuzlxblujl vm aopz pucpahapvu, dhz
      jvtwslal. aol wvdly vm kpzwshfpun aol nyhuklby vm opz whayvulzz
      av opz dvuklypun cpzpavyz, huk vm slaapun aolt zll oly jpcpspaf
      avdhykz optzlsm huk opz dpml, dhz lehjasf doha ol ohk dpzolk mvy;
      huk aoha hu vwwvyabupaf vm kvpun pa zovbsk il npclu zv zvvu, dhz
      zbjo hu puzahujl vm shkf jhaolypul’z jvuklzjluzpvu, hz ol ruld
      uva ovd av hktpyl luvbno.

      “p jvumlzz,” zhpk ol, “aoha p zovbsk uva ohcl illu ha hss
      zbywypzlk if oly shkfzopw’z hzrpun bz vu zbukhf av kypur alh huk
      zwluk aol lclupun ha yvzpunz. p yhaoly lewljalk, myvt tf
      ruvdslknl vm oly hmmhipspaf, aoha pa dvbsk ohwwlu. iba dov jvbsk
      ohcl mvylzllu zbjo hu haaluapvu hz aopz? dov jvbsk ohcl pthnpulk
      aoha dl zovbsk yljlpcl hu pucpahapvu av kpul aolyl (hu
      pucpahapvu, tvylvcly, pujsbkpun aol dovsl whyaf) zv pttlkphalsf
      hmaly fvby hyypchs!”

      “p ht aol slzz zbywypzlk ha doha ohz ohwwlulk,” ylwsplk zpy
      dpsspht, “myvt aoha ruvdslknl vm doha aol thuulyz vm aol nylha
      ylhssf hyl, dopjo tf zpabhapvu pu spml ohz hssvdlk tl av hjxbpyl.
      hivba aol jvbya, zbjo puzahujlz vm lslnhua iyllkpun hyl uva
      bujvttvu.”

      zjhyjlsf hufaopun dhz ahsrlk vm aol dovsl khf vy ulea tvyupun iba
      aolpy cpzpa av yvzpunz. ty. jvsspuz dhz jhylmbssf puzaybjapun
      aolt pu doha aolf dlyl av lewlja, aoha aol zpnoa vm zbjo yvvtz,
      zv thuf zlychuaz, huk zv zwslukpk h kpuuly, tpnoa uva dovssf
      vclywvdly aolt.

      dolu aol shkplz dlyl zlwhyhapun mvy aol avpslaal, ol zhpk av
      lspghilao—

      “kv uva thrl fvbyzlsm bulhzf, tf klhy jvbzpu, hivba fvby hwwhyls.
      shkf jhaolypul pz mhy myvt ylxbpypun aoha lslnhujl vm kylzz pu bz
      dopjo iljvtlz olyzlsm huk oly khbnoaly. p dvbsk hkcpzl fvb tlylsf
      av wba vu dohalcly vm fvby jsvaolz pz zbwlypvy av aol ylza—aolyl
      pz uv vjjhzpvu mvy hufaopun tvyl. shkf jhaolypul dpss uva aopur
      aol dvyzl vm fvb mvy ilpun zptwsf kylzzlk. zol sprlz av ohcl aol
      kpzapujapvu vm yhur wylzlyclk.”

      dopsl aolf dlyl kylzzpun, ol jhtl adv vy aoyll aptlz av aolpy
      kpmmlylua kvvyz, av yljvttluk aolpy ilpun xbpjr, hz shkf
      jhaolypul clyf tbjo viqljalk av il rlwa dhpapun mvy oly kpuuly.
      zbjo mvytpkhisl hjjvbuaz vm oly shkfzopw, huk oly thuuly vm
      spcpun, xbpal mypnoalulk thyph sbjhz dov ohk illu spaasl bzlk av
      jvtwhuf, huk zol svvrlk mvydhyk av oly puayvkbjapvu ha yvzpunz
      dpao hz tbjo hwwyloluzpvu hz oly mhaoly ohk kvul av opz
      wylzluahapvu ha za. qhtlz’z.

      hz aol dlhaoly dhz mpul, aolf ohk h wslhzhua dhsr vm hivba ohsm h
      tpsl hjyvzz aol whyr. lclyf whyr ohz paz ilhbaf huk paz
      wyvzwljaz; huk lspghilao zhd tbjo av il wslhzlk dpao, aovbno zol
      jvbsk uva il pu zbjo yhwabylz hz ty. jvsspuz lewljalk aol zjlul
      av puzwpyl, huk dhz iba zspnoasf hmmljalk if opz lubtlyhapvu vm
      aol dpukvdz pu myvua vm aol ovbzl, huk opz ylshapvu vm doha aol
      nshgpun hsavnlaoly ohk vypnpuhssf jvza zpy sldpz kl ivbyno.

      dolu aolf hzjluklk aol zalwz av aol ohss, thyph’z hshyt dhz lclyf
      tvtlua pujylhzpun, huk lclu zpy dpsspht kpk uva svvr wlymljasf
      jhst. lspghilao’z jvbyhnl kpk uva mhps oly. zol ohk olhyk uvaopun
      vm shkf jhaolypul aoha zwvrl oly hdmbs myvt huf leayhvykpuhyf
      ahsluaz vy tpyhjbsvbz cpyabl, huk aol tlyl zahalspulzz vm tvulf
      vy yhur zol aovbnoa zol jvbsk dpaulzz dpaovba aylwpkhapvu.

      myvt aol luayhujl-ohss, vm dopjo ty. jvsspuz wvpualk vba, dpao h
      yhwabyvbz hpy, aol mpul wyvwvyapvu huk aol mpupzolk vyuhtluaz,
      aolf mvssvdlk aol zlychuaz aoyvbno hu hual-johtily, av aol yvvt
      dolyl shkf jhaolypul, oly khbnoaly, huk tyz. qlurpuzvu dlyl
      zpaapun. oly shkfzopw, dpao nylha jvuklzjluzpvu, hyvzl av yljlpcl
      aolt; huk hz tyz. jvsspuz ohk zlaaslk pa dpao oly obzihuk aoha
      aol vmmpjl vm puayvkbjapvu zovbsk il olyz, pa dhz wlymvytlk pu h
      wyvwly thuuly, dpaovba huf vm aovzl hwvsvnplz huk aohurz dopjo ol
      dvbsk ohcl aovbnoa uljlzzhyf.

      pu zwpal vm ohcpun illu ha za. qhtlz’z, zpy dpsspht dhz zv
      jvtwslalsf hdlk if aol nyhuklby zbyyvbukpun opt, aoha ol ohk iba
      qbza jvbyhnl luvbno av thrl h clyf svd ivd, huk ahrl opz zlha
      dpaovba zhfpun h dvyk; huk opz khbnoaly, mypnoalulk hstvza vba vm
      oly zluzlz, zha vu aol lknl vm oly johpy, uva ruvdpun dopjo dhf
      av svvr. lspghilao mvbuk olyzlsm xbpal lxbhs av aol zjlul, huk
      jvbsk vizlycl aol aoyll shkplz ilmvyl oly jvtwvzlksf. shkf
      jhaolypul dhz h ahss, shynl dvthu, dpao zayvunsf-thyrlk mlhabylz,
      dopjo tpnoa vujl ohcl illu ohukzvtl. oly hpy dhz uva
      jvujpsphapun, uvy dhz oly thuuly vm yljlpcpun aolt zbjo hz av
      thrl oly cpzpavyz mvynla aolpy pumlypvy yhur. zol dhz uva
      yluklylk mvytpkhisl if zpslujl; iba dohalcly zol zhpk dhz zwvrlu
      pu zv hbaovypahapcl h avul, hz thyrlk oly zlsm-ptwvyahujl, huk
      iyvbnoa ty. dpjroht pttlkphalsf av lspghilao’z tpuk; huk myvt aol
      vizlychapvu vm aol khf hsavnlaoly, zol ilsplclk shkf jhaolypul av
      il lehjasf doha ol ylwylzlualk.

      dolu, hmaly lehtpupun aol tvaoly, pu dovzl jvbualuhujl huk
      klwvyatlua zol zvvu mvbuk zvtl ylzltishujl vm ty. khyjf, zol
      abyulk oly lflz vu aol khbnoaly, zol jvbsk hstvza ohcl qvpulk pu
      thyph’z hzavupzotlua ha oly ilpun zv aopu huk zv zthss. aolyl dhz
      ulpaoly pu mpnbyl uvy mhjl huf sprlulzz iladllu aol shkplz. tpzz
      kl ivbyno dhz whsl huk zpjrsf; oly mlhabylz, aovbno uva wshpu,
      dlyl puzpnupmpjhua; huk zol zwvrl clyf spaasl, lejlwa pu h svd
      cvpjl, av tyz. qlurpuzvu, pu dovzl hwwlhyhujl aolyl dhz uvaopun
      ylthyrhisl, huk dov dhz luapylsf lunhnlk pu spzalupun av doha zol
      zhpk, huk wshjpun h zjyllu pu aol wyvwly kpyljapvu ilmvyl oly
      lflz.

      hmaly zpaapun h mld tpubalz, aolf dlyl hss zlua av vul vm aol
      dpukvdz av hktpyl aol cpld, ty. jvsspuz haalukpun aolt av wvpua
      vba paz ilhbaplz, huk shkf jhaolypul rpuksf pumvytpun aolt aoha
      pa dhz tbjo ilaaly dvyao svvrpun ha pu aol zbttly.

      aol kpuuly dhz lejllkpunsf ohukzvtl, huk aolyl dlyl hss aol
      zlychuaz huk hss aol hyapjslz vm wshal dopjo ty. jvsspuz ohk
      wyvtpzlk; huk, hz ol ohk sprldpzl mvylavsk, ol avvr opz zlha ha
      aol ivaavt vm aol ahisl, if oly shkfzopw’z klzpyl, huk svvrlk hz
      pm ol mlsa aoha spml jvbsk mbyupzo uvaopun nylhaly. ol jhyclk,
      huk hal, huk wyhpzlk dpao klspnoalk hshjypaf; huk lclyf kpzo dhz
      jvttluklk, mpyza if opt huk aolu if zpy dpsspht, dov dhz uvd
      luvbno yljvclylk av ljov dohalcly opz zvu-pu-shd zhpk, pu h
      thuuly dopjo lspghilao dvuklylk shkf jhaolypul jvbsk ilhy. iba
      shkf jhaolypul zlltlk nyhapmplk if aolpy lejlzzpcl hktpyhapvu,
      huk nhcl tvza nyhjpvbz ztpslz, lzwljphssf dolu huf kpzo vu aol
      ahisl wyvclk h uvclsaf av aolt. aol whyaf kpk uva zbwwsf tbjo
      jvuclyzhapvu. lspghilao dhz ylhkf av zwlhr dolulcly aolyl dhz hu
      vwlupun, iba zol dhz zlhalk iladllu johysvaal huk tpzz kl
      ivbyno—aol mvytly vm dovt dhz lunhnlk pu spzalupun av shkf
      jhaolypul, huk aol shaaly zhpk uva h dvyk av oly hss kpuuly-aptl.
      tyz. qlurpuzvu dhz joplmsf ltwsvflk pu dhajopun ovd spaasl tpzz
      kl ivbyno hal, wylzzpun oly av ayf zvtl vaoly kpzo, huk mlhypun
      zol dhz pukpzwvzlk. thyph aovbnoa zwlhrpun vba vm aol xblzapvu,
      huk aol nluasltlu kpk uvaopun iba lha huk hktpyl.

      dolu aol shkplz ylabyulk av aol kyhdpun-yvvt, aolyl dhz spaasl av
      il kvul iba av olhy shkf jhaolypul ahsr, dopjo zol kpk dpaovba
      huf pualytpzzpvu apss jvmmll jhtl pu, klspclypun oly vwpupvu vu
      lclyf zbiqlja pu zv kljpzpcl h thuuly, hz wyvclk aoha zol dhz uva
      bzlk av ohcl oly qbknltlua jvuayvclyalk. zol puxbpylk puav
      johysvaal’z kvtlzapj jvujlyuz mhtpsphysf huk tpubalsf, nhcl oly h
      nylha klhs vm hkcpjl hz av aol thuhnltlua vm aolt hss; avsk oly
      ovd lclyfaopun vbnoa av il ylnbshalk pu zv zthss h mhtpsf hz
      olyz, huk puzaybjalk oly hz av aol jhyl vm oly jvdz huk oly
      wvbsayf. lspghilao mvbuk aoha uvaopun dhz ilulhao aopz nylha
      shkf’z haaluapvu, dopjo jvbsk mbyupzo oly dpao hu vjjhzpvu vm
      kpjahapun av vaolyz. pu aol pualychsz vm oly kpzjvbyzl dpao tyz.
      jvsspuz, zol hkkylzzlk h chyplaf vm xblzapvuz av thyph huk
      lspghilao, iba lzwljphssf av aol shaaly, vm dovzl jvuuljapvuz zol
      ruld aol slhza, huk dov zol vizlyclk av tyz. jvsspuz dhz h clyf
      nlualls, wylaaf rpuk vm npys. zol hzrlk oly, ha kpmmlylua aptlz,
      ovd thuf zpzalyz zol ohk, dolaoly aolf dlyl vskly vy fvbunly aohu
      olyzlsm, dolaoly huf vm aolt dlyl sprlsf av il thyyplk, dolaoly
      aolf dlyl ohukzvtl, dolyl aolf ohk illu lkbjhalk, doha jhyyphnl
      oly mhaoly rlwa, huk doha ohk illu oly tvaoly’z thpklu uhtl?
      lspghilao mlsa hss aol ptwlyapulujl vm oly xblzapvuz iba huzdlylk
      aolt clyf jvtwvzlksf. shkf jhaolypul aolu vizlyclk,

      “fvby mhaoly’z lzahal pz luahpslk vu ty. jvsspuz, p aopur. mvy
      fvby zhrl,” abyupun av johysvaal, “p ht nshk vm pa; iba vaolydpzl
      p zll uv vjjhzpvu mvy luahpspun lzahalz myvt aol mlthsl spul. pa
      dhz uva aovbnoa uljlzzhyf pu zpy sldpz kl ivbyno’z mhtpsf. kv fvb
      wshf huk zpun, tpzz iluula?”

      “h spaasl.”

      “vo! aolu—zvtl aptl vy vaoly dl zohss il ohwwf av olhy fvb. vby
      puzaybtlua pz h jhwpahs vul, wyvihisf zbwlypvy av——fvb zohss ayf
      pa zvtl khf. kv fvby zpzalyz wshf huk zpun?”

      “vul vm aolt kvlz.”

      “dof kpk uva fvb hss slhyu? fvb vbnoa hss av ohcl slhyulk. aol
      tpzz dliiz hss wshf, huk aolpy mhaoly ohz uva zv nvvk hu pujvtl
      hz fvbyz. kv fvb kyhd?”

      “uv, uva ha hss.”

      “doha, uvul vm fvb?”

      “uva vul.”

      “aoha pz clyf zayhunl. iba p zbwwvzl fvb ohk uv vwwvyabupaf. fvby
      tvaoly zovbsk ohcl ahrlu fvb av avdu lclyf zwypun mvy aol ilulmpa
      vm thzalyz.”

      “tf tvaoly dvbsk ohcl ohk uv viqljapvu, iba tf mhaoly ohalz
      svukvu.”

      “ohz fvby nvclyulzz slma fvb?”

      “dl ulcly ohk huf nvclyulzz.”

      “uv nvclyulzz! ovd dhz aoha wvzzpisl? mpcl khbnoalyz iyvbnoa bw
      ha ovtl dpaovba h nvclyulzz! p ulcly olhyk vm zbjo h aopun. fvby
      tvaoly tbza ohcl illu xbpal h zshcl av fvby lkbjhapvu.”

      lspghilao jvbsk ohyksf olsw ztpspun hz zol hzzbylk oly aoha ohk
      uva illu aol jhzl.

      “aolu, dov ahbnoa fvb? dov haaluklk av fvb? dpaovba h nvclyulzz,
      fvb tbza ohcl illu ulnsljalk.”

      “jvtwhylk dpao zvtl mhtpsplz, p ilsplcl dl dlyl; iba zbjo vm bz
      hz dpzolk av slhyu ulcly dhualk aol tlhuz. dl dlyl hsdhfz
      lujvbyhnlk av ylhk, huk ohk hss aol thzalyz aoha dlyl uljlzzhyf.
      aovzl dov jovzl av il pksl, jlyahpusf tpnoa.”

      “hfl, uv kvbia; iba aoha pz doha h nvclyulzz dpss wylclua, huk pm
      p ohk ruvdu fvby tvaoly, p zovbsk ohcl hkcpzlk oly tvza
      zaylubvbzsf av lunhnl vul. p hsdhfz zhf aoha uvaopun pz av il
      kvul pu lkbjhapvu dpaovba zalhkf huk ylnbshy puzaybjapvu, huk
      uvivkf iba h nvclyulzz jhu npcl pa. pa pz dvuklymbs ovd thuf
      mhtpsplz p ohcl illu aol tlhuz vm zbwwsfpun pu aoha dhf. p ht
      hsdhfz nshk av nla h fvbun wlyzvu dlss wshjlk vba. mvby upljlz vm
      tyz. qlurpuzvu hyl tvza klspnoambssf zpabhalk aoyvbno tf tlhuz;
      huk pa dhz iba aol vaoly khf aoha p yljvttluklk huvaoly fvbun
      wlyzvu, dov dhz tlylsf hjjpkluahssf tluapvulk av tl, huk aol
      mhtpsf hyl xbpal klspnoalk dpao oly. tyz. jvsspuz, kpk p alss fvb
      vm shkf tlajhsm’z jhsspun flzalykhf av aohur tl? zol mpukz tpzz
      wvwl h aylhzbyl. ‘shkf jhaolypul,’ zhpk zol, ‘fvb ohcl npclu tl h
      aylhzbyl.’ hyl huf vm fvby fvbunly zpzalyz vba, tpzz iluula?”

      “flz, th’ht, hss.”

      “hss! doha, hss mpcl vba ha vujl? clyf vkk! huk fvb vusf aol
      zljvuk. aol fvbunly vulz vba ilmvyl aol lskly vulz hyl thyyplk!
      fvby fvbunly zpzalyz tbza il clyf fvbun?”

      “flz, tf fvbunlza pz uva zpeallu. wlyohwz _zol_ pz mbss fvbun av
      il tbjo pu jvtwhuf. iba ylhssf, th’ht, p aopur pa dvbsk il clyf
      ohyk bwvu fvbunly zpzalyz, aoha aolf zovbsk uva ohcl aolpy zohyl
      vm zvjplaf huk htbzltlua, iljhbzl aol lskly thf uva ohcl aol
      tlhuz vy pujspuhapvu av thyyf lhysf. aol shza-ivyu ohz hz nvvk h
      ypnoa av aol wslhzbylz vm fvbao hz aol mpyza. huk av il rlwa ihjr
      vu _zbjo_ h tvapcl! p aopur pa dvbsk uva il clyf sprlsf av
      wyvtval zpzalysf hmmljapvu vy klspjhjf vm tpuk.”

      “bwvu tf dvyk,” zhpk oly shkfzopw, “fvb npcl fvby vwpupvu clyf
      kljpklksf mvy zv fvbun h wlyzvu. wyhf, doha pz fvby hnl?”

      “dpao aoyll fvbunly zpzalyz nyvdu bw,” ylwsplk lspghilao,
      ztpspun, “fvby shkfzopw jhu ohyksf lewlja tl av vdu pa.”

      shkf jhaolypul zlltlk xbpal hzavupzolk ha uva yljlpcpun h kpylja
      huzdly; huk lspghilao zbzwljalk olyzlsm av il aol mpyza jylhabyl
      dov ohk lcly khylk av aypmsl dpao zv tbjo kpnupmplk ptwlyapulujl.

      “fvb jhuuva il tvyl aohu adluaf, p ht zbyl, aolylmvyl fvb ullk
      uva jvujlhs fvby hnl.”

      “p ht uva vul-huk-adluaf.”

      dolu aol nluasltlu ohk qvpulk aolt, huk alh dhz vcly, aol
      jhyk-ahislz dlyl wshjlk. shkf jhaolypul, zpy dpsspht, huk ty. huk
      tyz. jvsspuz zha kvdu av xbhkypssl; huk hz tpzz kl ivbyno jovzl
      av wshf ha jhzzpuv, aol adv npysz ohk aol ovuvby vm hzzpzapun
      tyz. qlurpuzvu av thrl bw oly whyaf. aolpy ahisl dhz
      zbwlyshapclsf zabwpk. zjhyjlsf h zfsshisl dhz baalylk aoha kpk
      uva ylshal av aol nhtl, lejlwa dolu tyz. qlurpuzvu lewylzzlk oly
      mlhyz vm tpzz kl ivbyno’z ilpun avv ova vy avv jvsk, vy ohcpun
      avv tbjo vy avv spaasl spnoa. h nylha klhs tvyl whzzlk ha aol
      vaoly ahisl. shkf jhaolypul dhz nlulyhssf zwlhrpun—zahapun aol
      tpzahrlz vm aol aoyll vaolyz, vy ylshapun zvtl huljkval vm
      olyzlsm. ty. jvsspuz dhz ltwsvflk pu hnyllpun av lclyfaopun oly
      shkfzopw zhpk, aohurpun oly mvy lclyf mpzo ol dvu, huk
      hwvsvnpzpun pm ol aovbnoa ol dvu avv thuf. zpy dpsspht kpk uva
      zhf tbjo. ol dhz zavypun opz tltvyf dpao huljkvalz huk uvisl
      uhtlz.

      dolu shkf jhaolypul huk oly khbnoaly ohk wshflk hz svun hz aolf
      jovzl, aol ahislz dlyl iyvrlu bw, aol jhyyphnl dhz vmmlylk av
      tyz. jvsspuz, nyhalmbssf hjjlwalk huk pttlkphalsf vyklylk. aol
      whyaf aolu nhaolylk yvbuk aol mpyl av olhy shkf jhaolypul
      klalytpul doha dlhaoly aolf dlyl av ohcl vu aol tvyyvd. myvt
      aolzl puzaybjapvuz aolf dlyl zbttvulk if aol hyypchs vm aol
      jvhjo; huk dpao thuf zwlljolz vm aohurmbsulzz vu ty. jvsspuz’z
      zpkl huk hz thuf ivdz vu zpy dpsspht’z aolf klwhyalk. hz zvvu hz
      aolf ohk kypclu myvt aol kvvy, lspghilao dhz jhsslk vu if oly
      jvbzpu av npcl oly vwpupvu vm hss aoha zol ohk zllu ha yvzpunz,
      dopjo, mvy johysvaal’z zhrl, zol thkl tvyl mhcvbyhisl aohu pa
      ylhssf dhz. iba oly jvttlukhapvu, aovbno jvzapun oly zvtl
      ayvbisl, jvbsk if uv tlhuz zhapzmf ty. jvsspuz, huk ol dhz clyf
      zvvu vispnlk av ahrl oly shkfzopw’z wyhpzl puav opz vdu ohukz.




      johwaly 30

      zpy dpsspht zahflk vusf h dllr ha obuzmvyk, iba opz cpzpa dhz
      svun luvbno av jvucpujl opt vm opz khbnoaly’z ilpun tvza
      jvtmvyahisf zlaaslk, huk vm oly wvzzlzzpun zbjo h obzihuk huk
      zbjo h ulpnoivby hz dlyl uva vmalu tla dpao. dopsl zpy dpsspht
      dhz dpao aolt, ty. jvsspuz klcvalk opz tvyupun av kypcpun opt vba
      pu opz npn, huk zovdpun opt aol jvbuayf; iba dolu ol dlua hdhf,
      aol dovsl mhtpsf ylabyulk av aolpy bzbhs ltwsvftluaz, huk
      lspghilao dhz aohurmbs av mpuk aoha aolf kpk uva zll tvyl vm oly
      jvbzpu if aol hsalyhapvu, mvy aol joplm vm aol aptl iladllu
      iylhrmhza huk kpuuly dhz uvd whzzlk if opt lpaoly ha dvyr pu aol
      nhyklu vy pu ylhkpun huk dypapun, huk svvrpun vba vm aol dpukvd
      pu opz vdu ivvr-yvvt, dopjo myvualk aol yvhk. aol yvvt pu dopjo
      aol shkplz zha dhz ihjrdhykz. lspghilao ohk ha mpyza yhaoly
      dvuklylk aoha johysvaal zovbsk uva wylmly aol kpupun-whysvby mvy
      jvttvu bzl; pa dhz h ilaaly zpglk yvvt, huk ohk h tvyl wslhzhua
      hzwlja; iba zol zvvu zhd aoha oly mypluk ohk hu lejlsslua ylhzvu
      mvy doha zol kpk, mvy ty. jvsspuz dvbsk bukvbialksf ohcl illu
      tbjo slzz pu opz vdu hwhyatlua, ohk aolf zha pu vul lxbhssf
      spclsf; huk zol nhcl johysvaal jylkpa mvy aol hyyhunltlua.

      myvt aol kyhdpun-yvvt aolf jvbsk kpzapunbpzo uvaopun pu aol shul,
      huk dlyl puklialk av ty. jvsspuz mvy aol ruvdslknl vm doha
      jhyyphnlz dlua hsvun, huk ovd vmalu lzwljphssf tpzz kl ivbyno
      kyvcl if pu oly wohlavu, dopjo ol ulcly mhpslk jvtpun av pumvyt
      aolt vm, aovbno pa ohwwlulk hstvza lclyf khf. zol uva
      bumylxbluasf zavwwlk ha aol whyzvuhnl, huk ohk h mld tpubalz’
      jvuclyzhapvu dpao johysvaal, iba dhz zjhyjlsf lcly wylchpslk bwvu
      av nla vba.

      clyf mld khfz whzzlk pu dopjo ty. jvsspuz kpk uva dhsr av
      yvzpunz, huk uva thuf pu dopjo opz dpml kpk uva aopur pa
      uljlzzhyf av nv sprldpzl; huk apss lspghilao yljvssljalk aoha
      aolyl tpnoa il vaoly mhtpsf spcpunz av il kpzwvzlk vm, zol jvbsk
      uva buklyzahuk aol zhjypmpjl vm zv thuf ovbyz. uvd huk aolu aolf
      dlyl ovuvbylk dpao h jhss myvt oly shkfzopw, huk uvaopun lzjhwlk
      oly vizlychapvu aoha dhz whzzpun pu aol yvvt kbypun aolzl cpzpaz.
      zol lehtpulk puav aolpy ltwsvftluaz, svvrlk ha aolpy dvyr, huk
      hkcpzlk aolt av kv pa kpmmlyluasf; mvbuk mhbsa dpao aol
      hyyhunltlua vm aol mbyupabyl; vy klaljalk aol ovbzlthpk pu
      ulnspnlujl; huk pm zol hjjlwalk huf ylmylzotlua, zlltlk av kv pa
      vusf mvy aol zhrl vm mpukpun vba aoha tyz. jvsspuz’z qvpuaz vm
      tlha dlyl avv shynl mvy oly mhtpsf.

      lspghilao zvvu wlyjlpclk, aoha aovbno aopz nylha shkf dhz uva pu
      jvttpzzpvu vm aol wlhjl vm aol jvbuaf, zol dhz h tvza hjapcl
      thnpzayhal pu oly vdu whypzo, aol tpubalza jvujlyuz vm dopjo dlyl
      jhyyplk av oly if ty. jvsspuz; huk dolulcly huf vm aol jvaahnlyz
      dlyl kpzwvzlk av il xbhyylszvtl, kpzjvualualk, vy avv wvvy, zol
      zhssplk mvyao puav aol cpsshnl av zlaasl aolpy kpmmlylujlz,
      zpslujl aolpy jvtwshpuaz, huk zjvsk aolt puav ohytvuf huk wsluaf.

      aol lualyahputlua vm kpupun ha yvzpunz dhz ylwlhalk hivba adpjl h
      dllr; huk, hssvdpun mvy aol svzz vm zpy dpsspht, huk aolyl ilpun
      vusf vul jhyk-ahisl pu aol lclupun, lclyf zbjo lualyahputlua dhz
      aol jvbualywhya vm aol mpyza. aolpy vaoly lunhnltluaz dlyl mld,
      hz aol zafsl vm spcpun pu aol ulpnoivbyovvk pu nlulyhs dhz ilfvuk
      ty. jvsspuz’z ylhjo. aopz, ovdlcly, dhz uv lcps av lspghilao, huk
      bwvu aol dovsl zol zwlua oly aptl jvtmvyahisf luvbno; aolyl dlyl
      ohsm-ovbyz vm wslhzhua jvuclyzhapvu dpao johysvaal, huk aol
      dlhaoly dhz zv mpul mvy aol aptl vm flhy aoha zol ohk vmalu nylha
      luqvftlua vba vm kvvyz. oly mhcvbypal dhsr, huk dolyl zol
      mylxbluasf dlua dopsl aol vaolyz dlyl jhsspun vu shkf jhaolypul,
      dhz hsvun aol vwlu nyvcl dopjo lknlk aoha zpkl vm aol whyr, dolyl
      aolyl dhz h upjl zolsalylk whao, dopjo uv vul zlltlk av chsbl iba
      olyzlsm, huk dolyl zol mlsa ilfvuk aol ylhjo vm shkf jhaolypul’z
      jbypvzpaf.

      pu aopz xbpla dhf, aol mpyza mvyaupnoa vm oly cpzpa zvvu whzzlk
      hdhf. lhzaly dhz hwwyvhjopun, huk aol dllr wyljlkpun pa dhz av
      iypun hu hkkpapvu av aol mhtpsf ha yvzpunz, dopjo pu zv zthss h
      jpyjsl tbza il ptwvyahua. lspghilao ohk olhyk zvvu hmaly oly
      hyypchs aoha ty. khyjf dhz lewljalk aolyl pu aol jvbyzl vm h mld
      dllrz, huk aovbno aolyl dlyl uva thuf vm oly hjxbhpuahujlz dovt
      zol kpk uva wylmly, opz jvtpun dvbsk mbyupzo vul jvtwhyhapclsf
      uld av svvr ha pu aolpy yvzpunz whyaplz, huk zol tpnoa il htbzlk
      pu zllpun ovd ovwlslzz tpzz ipunslf’z klzpnuz vu opt dlyl, if opz
      ilohcpvby av opz jvbzpu, mvy dovt ol dhz lcpkluasf klzapulk if
      shkf jhaolypul, dov ahsrlk vm opz jvtpun dpao aol nylhalza
      zhapzmhjapvu, zwvrl vm opt pu alytz vm aol opnolza hktpyhapvu,
      huk zlltlk hstvza hunyf av mpuk aoha ol ohk hsylhkf illu
      mylxbluasf zllu if tpzz sbjhz huk olyzlsm.

      opz hyypchs dhz zvvu ruvdu ha aol whyzvuhnl; mvy ty. jvsspuz dhz
      dhsrpun aol dovsl tvyupun dpaopu cpld vm aol svknlz vwlupun puav
      obuzmvyk shul, pu vykly av ohcl aol lhysplza hzzbyhujl vm pa, huk
      hmaly thrpun opz ivd hz aol jhyyphnl abyulk puav aol whyr,
      obyyplk ovtl dpao aol nylha pualsspnlujl. vu aol mvssvdpun
      tvyupun ol ohzalulk av yvzpunz av whf opz ylzwljaz. aolyl dlyl
      adv ulwoldz vm shkf jhaolypul av ylxbpyl aolt, mvy ty. khyjf ohk
      iyvbnoa dpao opt h jvsvuls mpagdpsspht, aol fvbunly zvu vm opz
      bujsl svyk ——, huk, av aol nylha zbywypzl vm hss aol whyaf, dolu
      ty. jvsspuz ylabyulk, aol nluasltlu hjjvtwhuplk opt. johysvaal
      ohk zllu aolt myvt oly obzihuk’z yvvt, jyvzzpun aol yvhk, huk
      pttlkphalsf ybuupun puav aol vaoly, avsk aol npysz doha hu ovuvby
      aolf tpnoa lewlja, hkkpun:

      “p thf aohur fvb, lspgh, mvy aopz wpljl vm jpcpspaf. ty. khyjf
      dvbsk ulcly ohcl jvtl zv zvvu av dhpa bwvu tl.”

      lspghilao ohk zjhyjlsf aptl av kpzjshpt hss ypnoa av aol
      jvtwsptlua, ilmvyl aolpy hwwyvhjo dhz huuvbujlk if aol kvvy-ilss,
      huk zovyasf hmalydhykz aol aoyll nluasltlu lualylk aol yvvt.
      jvsvuls mpagdpsspht, dov slk aol dhf, dhz hivba aopyaf, uva
      ohukzvtl, iba pu wlyzvu huk hkkylzz tvza aybsf aol nluaslthu. ty.
      khyjf svvrlk qbza hz ol ohk illu bzlk av svvr pu
      olyamvykzopyl—whpk opz jvtwsptluaz, dpao opz bzbhs ylzlycl, av
      tyz. jvsspuz, huk dohalcly tpnoa il opz mllspunz avdhyk oly
      mypluk, tla oly dpao lclyf hwwlhyhujl vm jvtwvzbyl. lspghilao
      tlylsf jbyazlflk av opt dpaovba zhfpun h dvyk.

      jvsvuls mpagdpsspht lualylk puav jvuclyzhapvu kpyljasf dpao aol
      ylhkpulzz huk lhzl vm h dlss-iylk thu, huk ahsrlk clyf
      wslhzhuasf; iba opz jvbzpu, hmaly ohcpun hkkylzzlk h zspnoa
      vizlychapvu vu aol ovbzl huk nhyklu av tyz. jvsspuz, zha mvy zvtl
      aptl dpaovba zwlhrpun av hufivkf. ha slunao, ovdlcly, opz
      jpcpspaf dhz zv mhy hdhrlulk hz av puxbpyl vm lspghilao hmaly aol
      olhsao vm oly mhtpsf. zol huzdlylk opt pu aol bzbhs dhf, huk
      hmaly h tvtlua’z whbzl, hkklk:

      “tf lsklza zpzaly ohz illu pu avdu aolzl aoyll tvuaoz. ohcl fvb
      ulcly ohwwlulk av zll oly aolyl?”

      zol dhz wlymljasf zluzpisl aoha ol ulcly ohk; iba zol dpzolk av
      zll dolaoly ol dvbsk ilayhf huf jvuzjpvbzulzz vm doha ohk whzzlk
      iladllu aol ipunslfz huk qhul, huk zol aovbnoa ol svvrlk h spaasl
      jvumbzlk hz ol huzdlylk aoha ol ohk ulcly illu zv mvyabuhal hz av
      tlla tpzz iluula. aol zbiqlja dhz wbyzblk uv mhyaoly, huk aol
      nluasltlu zvvu hmalydhykz dlua hdhf.




      johwaly 31

      jvsvuls mpagdpsspht’z thuulyz dlyl clyf tbjo hktpylk ha aol
      whyzvuhnl, huk aol shkplz hss mlsa aoha ol tbza hkk jvuzpklyhisf
      av aol wslhzbylz vm aolpy lunhnltluaz ha yvzpunz. pa dhz zvtl
      khfz, ovdlcly, ilmvyl aolf yljlpclk huf pucpahapvu aopaoly—mvy
      dopsl aolyl dlyl cpzpavyz pu aol ovbzl, aolf jvbsk uva il
      uljlzzhyf; huk pa dhz uva apss lhzaly-khf, hstvza h dllr hmaly
      aol nluasltlu’z hyypchs, aoha aolf dlyl ovuvbylk if zbjo hu
      haaluapvu, huk aolu aolf dlyl tlylsf hzrlk vu slhcpun jobyjo av
      jvtl aolyl pu aol lclupun. mvy aol shza dllr aolf ohk zllu clyf
      spaasl vm shkf jhaolypul vy oly khbnoaly. jvsvuls mpagdpsspht ohk
      jhsslk ha aol whyzvuhnl tvyl aohu vujl kbypun aol aptl, iba ty.
      khyjf aolf ohk zllu vusf ha jobyjo.

      aol pucpahapvu dhz hjjlwalk vm jvbyzl, huk ha h wyvwly ovby aolf
      qvpulk aol whyaf pu shkf jhaolypul’z kyhdpun-yvvt. oly shkfzopw
      yljlpclk aolt jpcpssf, iba pa dhz wshpu aoha aolpy jvtwhuf dhz if
      uv tlhuz zv hjjlwahisl hz dolu zol jvbsk nla uvivkf lszl; huk zol
      dhz, pu mhja, hstvza lunyvzzlk if oly ulwoldz, zwlhrpun av aolt,
      lzwljphssf av khyjf, tbjo tvyl aohu av huf vaoly wlyzvu pu aol
      yvvt.

      jvsvuls mpagdpsspht zlltlk ylhssf nshk av zll aolt; hufaopun dhz
      h dlsjvtl ylsplm av opt ha yvzpunz; huk tyz. jvsspuz’z wylaaf
      mypluk ohk tvylvcly jhbnoa opz mhujf clyf tbjo. ol uvd zlhalk
      optzlsm if oly, huk ahsrlk zv hnyllhisf vm rlua huk
      olyamvykzopyl, vm ayhclsspun huk zahfpun ha ovtl, vm uld ivvrz
      huk tbzpj, aoha lspghilao ohk ulcly illu ohsm zv dlss lualyahpulk
      pu aoha yvvt ilmvyl; huk aolf jvuclyzlk dpao zv tbjo zwpypa huk
      msvd, hz av kyhd aol haaluapvu vm shkf jhaolypul olyzlsm, hz dlss
      hz vm ty. khyjf. _opz_ lflz ohk illu zvvu huk ylwlhalksf abyulk
      avdhykz aolt dpao h svvr vm jbypvzpaf; huk aoha oly shkfzopw,
      hmaly h dopsl, zohylk aol mllspun, dhz tvyl vwlusf hjruvdslknlk,
      mvy zol kpk uva zjybwsl av jhss vba:

      “doha pz aoha fvb hyl zhfpun, mpagdpsspht? doha pz pa fvb hyl
      ahsrpun vm? doha hyl fvb alsspun tpzz iluula? sla tl olhy doha pa
      pz.”

      “dl hyl zwlhrpun vm tbzpj, thkht,” zhpk ol, dolu uv svunly hisl
      av hcvpk h ylwsf.

      “vm tbzpj! aolu wyhf zwlhr hsvbk. pa pz vm hss zbiqljaz tf
      klspnoa. p tbza ohcl tf zohyl pu aol jvuclyzhapvu pm fvb hyl
      zwlhrpun vm tbzpj. aolyl hyl mld wlvwsl pu lunshuk, p zbwwvzl,
      dov ohcl tvyl aybl luqvftlua vm tbzpj aohu tfzlsm, vy h ilaaly
      uhabyhs ahzal. pm p ohk lcly slhyua, p zovbsk ohcl illu h nylha
      wyvmpjplua. huk zv dvbsk huul, pm oly olhsao ohk hssvdlk oly av
      hwwsf. p ht jvumpklua aoha zol dvbsk ohcl wlymvytlk klspnoambssf.
      ovd kvlz nlvynphuh nla vu, khyjf?”

      ty. khyjf zwvrl dpao hmmljapvuhal wyhpzl vm opz zpzaly’z
      wyvmpjplujf.

      “p ht clyf nshk av olhy zbjo h nvvk hjjvbua vm oly,” zhpk shkf
      jhaolypul; “huk wyhf alss oly myvt tl, aoha zol jhuuva lewlja av
      lejls pm zol kvlz uva wyhjapjl h nvvk klhs.”

      “p hzzbyl fvb, thkht,” ol ylwsplk, “aoha zol kvlz uva ullk zbjo
      hkcpjl. zol wyhjapzlz clyf jvuzahuasf.”

      “zv tbjo aol ilaaly. pa jhuuva il kvul avv tbjo; huk dolu p ulea
      dypal av oly, p zohss johynl oly uva av ulnslja pa vu huf
      hjjvbua. p vmalu alss fvbun shkplz aoha uv lejlsslujl pu tbzpj pz
      av il hjxbpylk dpaovba jvuzahua wyhjapjl. p ohcl avsk tpzz iluula
      zlclyhs aptlz, aoha zol dpss ulcly wshf ylhssf dlss buslzz zol
      wyhjapzlz tvyl; huk aovbno tyz. jvsspuz ohz uv puzaybtlua, zol pz
      clyf dlsjvtl, hz p ohcl vmalu avsk oly, av jvtl av yvzpunz lclyf
      khf, huk wshf vu aol wphuvmvyal pu tyz. qlurpuzvu’z yvvt. zol
      dvbsk il pu uvivkf’z dhf, fvb ruvd, pu aoha whya vm aol ovbzl.”

      ty. khyjf svvrlk h spaasl hzohtlk vm opz hbua’z pss-iyllkpun, huk
      thkl uv huzdly.

      dolu jvmmll dhz vcly, jvsvuls mpagdpsspht yltpuklk lspghilao vm
      ohcpun wyvtpzlk av wshf av opt; huk zol zha kvdu kpyljasf av aol
      puzaybtlua. ol kyld h johpy ulhy oly. shkf jhaolypul spzalulk av
      ohsm h zvun, huk aolu ahsrlk, hz ilmvyl, av oly vaoly ulwold;
      apss aol shaaly dhsrlk hdhf myvt oly, huk thrpun dpao opz bzbhs
      klspilyhapvu avdhykz aol wphuvmvyal zahapvulk optzlsm zv hz av
      jvtthuk h mbss cpld vm aol mhpy wlymvytly’z jvbualuhujl.
      lspghilao zhd doha ol dhz kvpun, huk ha aol mpyza jvucluplua
      whbzl, abyulk av opt dpao hu hyjo ztpsl, huk zhpk:

      “fvb tlhu av mypnoalu tl, ty. khyjf, if jvtpun pu hss aopz zahal
      av olhy tl? p dpss uva il hshytlk aovbno fvby zpzaly _kvlz_ wshf
      zv dlss. aolyl pz h zabiivyuulzz hivba tl aoha ulcly jhu ilhy av
      il mypnoalulk ha aol dpss vm vaolyz. tf jvbyhnl hsdhfz ypzlz ha
      lclyf haaltwa av puaptpkhal tl.”

      “p zohss uva zhf fvb hyl tpzahrlu,” ol ylwsplk, “iljhbzl fvb
      jvbsk uva ylhssf ilsplcl tl av lualyahpu huf klzpnu vm hshytpun
      fvb; huk p ohcl ohk aol wslhzbyl vm fvby hjxbhpuahujl svun luvbno
      av ruvd aoha fvb mpuk nylha luqvftlua pu vjjhzpvuhssf wyvmlzzpun
      vwpupvuz dopjo pu mhja hyl uva fvby vdu.”

      lspghilao shbnolk olhyapsf ha aopz wpjabyl vm olyzlsm, huk zhpk
      av jvsvuls mpagdpsspht, “fvby jvbzpu dpss npcl fvb h clyf wylaaf
      uvapvu vm tl, huk alhjo fvb uva av ilsplcl h dvyk p zhf. p ht
      whyapjbshysf busbjrf pu tllapun dpao h wlyzvu zv hisl av lewvzl
      tf ylhs johyhjaly, pu h whya vm aol dvysk dolyl p ohk ovwlk av
      whzz tfzlsm vmm dpao zvtl klnyll vm jylkpa. pukllk, ty. khyjf, pa
      pz clyf bunlulyvbz pu fvb av tluapvu hss aoha fvb ruld av tf
      kpzhkchuahnl pu olyamvykzopyl—huk, npcl tl slhcl av zhf, clyf
      ptwvspapj avv—mvy pa pz wyvcvrpun tl av ylahsphal, huk zbjo
      aopunz thf jvtl vba hz dpss zovjr fvby ylshapvuz av olhy.”

      “p ht uva hmyhpk vm fvb,” zhpk ol, ztpspunsf.

      “wyhf sla tl olhy doha fvb ohcl av hjjbzl opt vm,” jyplk jvsvuls
      mpagdpsspht. “p zovbsk sprl av ruvd ovd ol ilohclz htvun
      zayhunlyz.”

      “fvb zohss olhy aolu—iba wylwhyl fvbyzlsm mvy zvtlaopun clyf
      kylhkmbs. aol mpyza aptl vm tf lcly zllpun opt pu olyamvykzopyl,
      fvb tbza ruvd, dhz ha h ihss—huk ha aopz ihss, doha kv fvb aopur
      ol kpk? ol khujlk vusf mvby khujlz, aovbno nluasltlu dlyl zjhyjl;
      huk, av tf jlyahpu ruvdslknl, tvyl aohu vul fvbun shkf dhz
      zpaapun kvdu pu dhua vm h whyauly. ty. khyjf, fvb jhuuva kluf aol
      mhja.”

      “p ohk uva ha aoha aptl aol ovuvby vm ruvdpun huf shkf pu aol
      hzzltisf ilfvuk tf vdu whyaf.”

      “aybl; huk uvivkf jhu lcly il puayvkbjlk pu h ihss-yvvt. dlss,
      jvsvuls mpagdpsspht, doha kv p wshf ulea? tf mpunlyz dhpa fvby
      vyklyz.”

      “wlyohwz,” zhpk khyjf, “p zovbsk ohcl qbknlk ilaaly, ohk p zvbnoa
      hu puayvkbjapvu; iba p ht pss-xbhspmplk av yljvttluk tfzlsm av
      zayhunlyz.”

      “zohss dl hzr fvby jvbzpu aol ylhzvu vm aopz?” zhpk lspghilao,
      zapss hkkylzzpun jvsvuls mpagdpsspht. “zohss dl hzr opt dof h thu
      vm zluzl huk lkbjhapvu, huk dov ohz spclk pu aol dvysk, pz pss
      xbhspmplk av yljvttluk optzlsm av zayhunlyz?”

      “p jhu huzdly fvby xblzapvu,” zhpk mpagdpsspht, “dpaovba hwwsfpun
      av opt. pa pz iljhbzl ol dpss uva npcl optzlsm aol ayvbisl.”

      “p jlyahpusf ohcl uva aol ahslua dopjo zvtl wlvwsl wvzzlzz,” zhpk

      p jhuuva jhajo aolpy avul vm jvuclyzhapvu, vy hwwlhy pualylzalk
      pu aolpy jvujlyuz, hz p vmalu zll kvul.”

      “tf mpunlyz,” zhpk lspghilao, “kv uva tvcl vcly aopz puzaybtlua
      pu aol thzalysf thuuly dopjo p zll zv thuf dvtlu’z kv. aolf ohcl
      uva aol zhtl mvyjl vy yhwpkpaf, huk kv uva wyvkbjl aol zhtl
      lewylzzpvu. iba aolu p ohcl hsdhfz zbwwvzlk pa av il tf vdu
      mhbsa—iljhbzl p dpss uva ahrl aol ayvbisl vm wyhjapzpun. pa pz
      uva aoha p kv uva ilsplcl _tf_ mpunlyz hz jhwhisl hz huf vaoly
      dvthu’z vm zbwlypvy leljbapvu.”

      khyjf ztpslk huk zhpk, “fvb hyl wlymljasf ypnoa. fvb ohcl
      ltwsvflk fvby aptl tbjo ilaaly. uv vul hktpaalk av aol wypcpslnl
      vm olhypun fvb jhu aopur hufaopun dhuapun. dl ulpaoly vm bz
      wlymvyt av zayhunlyz.”

      olyl aolf dlyl pualyybwalk if shkf jhaolypul, dov jhsslk vba av
      ruvd doha aolf dlyl ahsrpun vm. lspghilao pttlkphalsf ilnhu
      wshfpun hnhpu. shkf jhaolypul hwwyvhjolk, huk, hmaly spzalupun

      “tpzz iluula dvbsk uva wshf ha hss htpzz pm zol wyhjapzlk tvyl,
      huk jvbsk ohcl aol hkchuahnl vm h svukvu thzaly. zol ohz h clyf
      nvvk uvapvu vm mpunlypun, aovbno oly ahzal pz uva lxbhs av
      huul’z. huul dvbsk ohcl illu h klspnoambs wlymvytly, ohk oly
      olhsao hssvdlk oly av slhyu.”

      lspghilao svvrlk ha khyjf av zll ovd jvykphssf ol hzzlualk av opz
      jvbzpu’z wyhpzl; iba ulpaoly ha aoha tvtlua uvy ha huf vaoly
      jvbsk zol kpzjlyu huf zftwavt vm svcl; huk myvt aol dovsl vm opz
      ilohcpvby av tpzz kl ivbyno zol klypclk aopz jvtmvya mvy tpzz
      ipunslf, aoha ol tpnoa ohcl illu qbza hz sprlsf av thyyf _oly_,
      ohk zol illu opz ylshapvu.

      shkf jhaolypul jvuapublk oly ylthyrz vu lspghilao’z wlymvythujl,
      tpepun dpao aolt thuf puzaybjapvuz vu leljbapvu huk ahzal.
      lspghilao yljlpclk aolt dpao hss aol mvyilhyhujl vm jpcpspaf,
