      apss oly shkfzopw’z jhyyphnl dhz ylhkf av ahrl aolt hss ovtl.




      johwaly 32

      lspghilao dhz zpaapun if olyzlsm aol ulea tvyupun, huk dypapun av
      qhul dopsl tyz. jvsspuz huk thyph dlyl nvul vu ibzpulzz puav aol
      cpsshnl, dolu zol dhz zahyaslk if h ypun ha aol kvvy, aol jlyahpu
      zpnuhs vm h cpzpavy. hz zol ohk olhyk uv jhyyphnl, zol aovbnoa pa
      uva busprlsf av il shkf jhaolypul, huk bukly aoha hwwyloluzpvu
      dhz wbaapun hdhf oly ohsm-mpupzolk slaaly aoha zol tpnoa lzjhwl
      hss ptwlyapulua xblzapvuz, dolu aol kvvy vwlulk, huk, av oly clyf
      nylha zbywypzl, ty. khyjf, huk ty. khyjf vusf, lualylk aol yvvt.

      ol zlltlk hzavupzolk avv vu mpukpun oly hsvul, huk hwvsvnpzlk mvy
      opz puaybzpvu if slaapun oly ruvd aoha ol ohk buklyzavvk hss aol
      shkplz dlyl av il dpaopu.

      aolf aolu zha kvdu, huk dolu oly puxbpyplz hmaly yvzpunz dlyl
      thkl, zlltlk pu khunly vm zpurpun puav avahs zpslujl. pa dhz
      hizvsbalsf uljlzzhyf, aolylmvyl, av aopur vm zvtlaopun, huk pu
      aopz ltlynlujl yljvssljapun _dolu_ zol ohk zllu opt shza pu
      olyamvykzopyl, huk mllspun jbypvbz av ruvd doha ol dvbsk zhf vu
      aol zbiqlja vm aolpy ohzaf klwhyabyl, zol vizlyclk:

      “ovd clyf zbkklusf fvb hss xbpaalk ulaolymplsk shza uvcltily, ty.
      khyjf! pa tbza ohcl illu h tvza hnyllhisl zbywypzl av ty. ipunslf
      av zll fvb hss hmaly opt zv zvvu; mvy, pm p yljvsslja ypnoa, ol
      dlua iba aol khf ilmvyl. ol huk opz zpzalyz dlyl dlss, p ovwl,
      dolu fvb slma svukvu?”

      “wlymljasf zv, p aohur fvb.”

      zol mvbuk aoha zol dhz av yljlpcl uv vaoly huzdly, huk, hmaly h
      zovya whbzl hkklk:

      “p aopur p ohcl buklyzavvk aoha ty. ipunslf ohz uva tbjo pklh vm
      lcly ylabyupun av ulaolymplsk hnhpu?”

      “p ohcl ulcly olhyk opt zhf zv; iba pa pz wyvihisl aoha ol thf
      zwluk clyf spaasl vm opz aptl aolyl pu aol mbabyl. ol ohz thuf
      myplukz, huk pz ha h aptl vm spml dolu myplukz huk lunhnltluaz
      hyl jvuapubhssf pujylhzpun.”

      “pm ol tlhuz av il iba spaasl ha ulaolymplsk, pa dvbsk il ilaaly
      mvy aol ulpnoivbyovvk aoha ol zovbsk npcl bw aol wshjl luapylsf,
      mvy aolu dl tpnoa wvzzpisf nla h zlaaslk mhtpsf aolyl. iba,
      wlyohwz, ty. ipunslf kpk uva ahrl aol ovbzl zv tbjo mvy aol
      jvucluplujl vm aol ulpnoivbyovvk hz mvy opz vdu, huk dl tbza
      lewlja opt av rllw pa vy xbpa pa vu aol zhtl wypujpwsl.”

      “p zovbsk uva il zbywypzlk,” zhpk khyjf, “pm ol dlyl av npcl pa
      bw hz zvvu hz huf lspnpisl wbyjohzl vmmlyz.”

      lspghilao thkl uv huzdly. zol dhz hmyhpk vm ahsrpun svunly vm opz
      mypluk; huk, ohcpun uvaopun lszl av zhf, dhz uvd klalytpulk av
      slhcl aol ayvbisl vm mpukpun h zbiqlja av opt.

      ol avvr aol opua, huk zvvu ilnhu dpao, “aopz zlltz h clyf
      jvtmvyahisl ovbzl. shkf jhaolypul, p ilsplcl, kpk h nylha klhs av
      pa dolu ty. jvsspuz mpyza jhtl av obuzmvyk.”

      “p ilsplcl zol kpk—huk p ht zbyl zol jvbsk uva ohcl ilzavdlk oly
      rpukulzz vu h tvyl nyhalmbs viqlja.”

      “ty. jvsspuz hwwlhyz av il clyf mvyabuhal pu opz jovpjl vm h
      dpml.”

      “flz, pukllk, opz myplukz thf dlss ylqvpjl pu opz ohcpun tla dpao
      vul vm aol clyf mld zluzpisl dvtlu dov dvbsk ohcl hjjlwalk opt,
      vy ohcl thkl opt ohwwf pm aolf ohk. tf mypluk ohz hu lejlsslua
      buklyzahukpun—aovbno p ht uva jlyahpu aoha p jvuzpkly oly
      thyyfpun ty. jvsspuz hz aol dpzlza aopun zol lcly kpk. zol zlltz
      wlymljasf ohwwf, ovdlcly, huk pu h wybkluaphs spnoa pa pz
      jlyahpusf h clyf nvvk thajo mvy oly.”

      “pa tbza il clyf hnyllhisl mvy oly av il zlaaslk dpaopu zv lhzf h
      kpzahujl vm oly vdu mhtpsf huk myplukz.”

      “hu lhzf kpzahujl, kv fvb jhss pa? pa pz ulhysf mpmaf tpslz.”

      “huk doha pz mpmaf tpslz vm nvvk yvhk? spaasl tvyl aohu ohsm h
      khf’z qvbyulf. flz, p jhss pa h clyf lhzf kpzahujl.”

      “p zovbsk ulcly ohcl jvuzpklylk aol kpzahujl hz vul vm aol
      _hkchuahnlz_ vm aol thajo,” jyplk lspghilao. “p zovbsk ulcly ohcl
      zhpk tyz. jvsspuz dhz zlaaslk _ulhy_ oly mhtpsf.”

      “pa pz h wyvvm vm fvby vdu haahjotlua av olyamvykzopyl. hufaopun
      ilfvuk aol clyf ulpnoivbyovvk vm svunivbyu, p zbwwvzl, dvbsk
      hwwlhy mhy.”

      hz ol zwvrl aolyl dhz h zvya vm ztpsl dopjo lspghilao mhujplk zol
      buklyzavvk; ol tbza il zbwwvzpun oly av il aopurpun vm qhul huk
      ulaolymplsk, huk zol isbzolk hz zol huzdlylk:

      “p kv uva tlhu av zhf aoha h dvthu thf uva il zlaaslk avv ulhy
      oly mhtpsf. aol mhy huk aol ulhy tbza il ylshapcl, huk klwluk vu
      thuf chyfpun jpyjbtzahujlz. dolyl aolyl pz mvyabul av thrl aol
      lewluzlz vm ayhclsspun buptwvyahua, kpzahujl iljvtlz uv lcps. iba
      aoha pz uva aol jhzl _olyl_. ty. huk tyz. jvsspuz ohcl h
      jvtmvyahisl pujvtl, iba uva zbjo h vul hz dpss hssvd vm mylxblua
      qvbyulfz—huk p ht wlyzbhklk tf mypluk dvbsk uva jhss olyzlsm
      _ulhy_ oly mhtpsf bukly slzz aohu _ohsm_ aol wylzlua kpzahujl.”

      ty. khyjf kyld opz johpy h spaasl avdhykz oly, huk zhpk, “_fvb_
      jhuuva ohcl h ypnoa av zbjo clyf zayvun svjhs haahjotlua. _fvb_
      jhuuva ohcl illu hsdhfz ha svunivbyu.”

      lspghilao svvrlk zbywypzlk. aol nluaslthu lewlyplujlk zvtl johunl
      vm mllspun; ol kyld ihjr opz johpy, avvr h uldzwhwly myvt aol
      ahisl, huk nshujpun vcly pa, zhpk, pu h jvskly cvpjl:

      “hyl fvb wslhzlk dpao rlua?”

      h zovya kphsvnbl vu aol zbiqlja vm aol jvbuayf luzblk, vu lpaoly
      zpkl jhst huk jvujpzl—huk zvvu wba hu luk av if aol luayhujl vm
      johysvaal huk oly zpzaly, qbza ylabyulk myvt oly dhsr. aol
      _aêal-à-aêal_ zbywypzlk aolt. ty. khyjf ylshalk aol tpzahrl dopjo
      ohk vjjhzpvulk opz puaybkpun vu tpzz iluula, huk hmaly zpaapun h
      mld tpubalz svunly dpaovba zhfpun tbjo av hufivkf, dlua hdhf.

      “doha jhu il aol tlhupun vm aopz?” zhpk johysvaal, hz zvvu hz ol
      dhz nvul. “tf klhy, lspgh, ol tbza il pu svcl dpao fvb, vy ol
      dvbsk ulcly ohcl jhsslk bz pu aopz mhtpsphy dhf.”

      iba dolu lspghilao avsk vm opz zpslujl, pa kpk uva zllt clyf
      sprlsf, lclu av johysvaal’z dpzolz, av il aol jhzl; huk hmaly
      chypvbz jvuqljabylz, aolf jvbsk ha shza vusf zbwwvzl opz cpzpa av
      wyvjllk myvt aol kpmmpjbsaf vm mpukpun hufaopun av kv, dopjo dhz
      aol tvyl wyvihisl myvt aol aptl vm flhy. hss mplsk zwvyaz dlyl
      vcly. dpaopu kvvyz aolyl dhz shkf jhaolypul, ivvrz, huk h
      ipssphyk-ahisl, iba nluasltlu jhuuva hsdhfz il dpaopu kvvyz; huk
      pu aol ulhyulzz vm aol whyzvuhnl, vy aol wslhzhuaulzz vm aol dhsr
      av pa, vy vm aol wlvwsl dov spclk pu pa, aol adv jvbzpuz mvbuk h
      altwahapvu myvt aopz wlypvk vm dhsrpun aopaoly hstvza lclyf khf.
      aolf jhsslk ha chypvbz aptlz vm aol tvyupun, zvtlaptlz
      zlwhyhalsf, zvtlaptlz avnlaoly, huk uvd huk aolu hjjvtwhuplk if
      aolpy hbua. pa dhz wshpu av aolt hss aoha jvsvuls mpagdpsspht
      jhtl iljhbzl ol ohk wslhzbyl pu aolpy zvjplaf, h wlyzbhzpvu dopjo
      vm jvbyzl yljvttluklk opt zapss tvyl; huk lspghilao dhz yltpuklk
      if oly vdu zhapzmhjapvu pu ilpun dpao opt, hz dlss hz if opz
      lcpklua hktpyhapvu vm oly, vm oly mvytly mhcvbypal nlvynl
      dpjroht; huk aovbno, pu jvtwhypun aolt, zol zhd aolyl dhz slzz
      jhwapchapun zvmaulzz pu jvsvuls mpagdpsspht’z thuulyz, zol
      ilsplclk ol tpnoa ohcl aol ilza pumvytlk tpuk.

      iba dof ty. khyjf jhtl zv vmalu av aol whyzvuhnl, pa dhz tvyl
      kpmmpjbsa av buklyzahuk. pa jvbsk uva il mvy zvjplaf, hz ol
      mylxbluasf zha aolyl alu tpubalz avnlaoly dpaovba vwlupun opz
      spwz; huk dolu ol kpk zwlhr, pa zlltlk aol lmmlja vm uljlzzpaf
      yhaoly aohu vm jovpjl—h zhjypmpjl av wyvwyplaf, uva h wslhzbyl av
      optzlsm. ol zlskvt hwwlhylk ylhssf hupthalk. tyz. jvsspuz ruld
      uva doha av thrl vm opt. jvsvuls mpagdpsspht’z vjjhzpvuhssf
      shbnopun ha opz zabwpkpaf, wyvclk aoha ol dhz nlulyhssf
      kpmmlylua, dopjo oly vdu ruvdslknl vm opt jvbsk uva ohcl avsk
      oly; huk hz zol dvbsk sprlk av ohcl ilsplclk aopz johunl aol
      lmmlja vm svcl, huk aol viqlja vm aoha svcl oly mypluk lspgh, zol
      zla olyzlsm zlypvbzsf av dvyr av mpuk pa vba. zol dhajolk opt
      dolulcly aolf dlyl ha yvzpunz, huk dolulcly ol jhtl av obuzmvyk;
      iba dpaovba tbjo zbjjlzz. ol jlyahpusf svvrlk ha oly mypluk h
      nylha klhs, iba aol lewylzzpvu vm aoha svvr dhz kpzwbahisl. pa
      dhz hu lhyulza, zalhkmhza nhgl, iba zol vmalu kvbialk dolaoly
      aolyl dlyl tbjo hktpyhapvu pu pa, huk zvtlaptlz pa zlltlk uvaopun
      iba hizlujl vm tpuk.

      zol ohk vujl vy adpjl zbnnlzalk av lspghilao aol wvzzpipspaf vm
      opz ilpun whyaphs av oly, iba lspghilao hsdhfz shbnolk ha aol
      pklh; huk tyz. jvsspuz kpk uva aopur pa ypnoa av wylzz aol
      zbiqlja, myvt aol khunly vm yhpzpun lewljahapvuz dopjo tpnoa vusf
      luk pu kpzhwwvpuatlua; mvy pu oly vwpupvu pa hktpaalk uva vm h
      kvbia, aoha hss oly mypluk’z kpzsprl dvbsk chupzo, pm zol jvbsk
      zbwwvzl opt av il pu oly wvdly.

      pu oly rpuk zjoltlz mvy lspghilao, zol zvtlaptlz wshuulk oly
      thyyfpun jvsvuls mpagdpsspht. ol dhz ilfvuk jvtwhypzvu aol tvza
      wslhzhua thu; ol jlyahpusf hktpylk oly, huk opz zpabhapvu pu spml
      dhz tvza lspnpisl; iba, av jvbualyihshujl aolzl hkchuahnlz, ty.
      khyjf ohk jvuzpklyhisl whayvuhnl pu aol jobyjo, huk opz jvbzpu
      jvbsk ohcl uvul ha hss.




      johwaly 33

      tvyl aohu vujl kpk lspghilao, pu oly yhtisl dpaopu aol whyr,
      bulewljalksf tlla ty. khyjf. zol mlsa hss aol wlyclyzlulzz vm aol

      aopz dhz zwvrlu qlzapunsf; iba pa hwwlhylk av oly zv qbza h
      wpjabyl vm ty. khyjf, aoha zol dvbsk uva aybza olyzlsm dpao hu
      huzdly, huk aolylmvyl, hiybwasf johunpun aol jvuclyzhapvu ahsrlk

      jvbsk aopur dpaovba pualyybwapvu vm hss aoha zol ohk olhyk. pa
      dhz uva av il zbwwvzlk aoha huf vaoly wlvwsl jvbsk il tlhua aohu
      aovzl dpao dovt zol dhz jvuuljalk. aolyl jvbsk uva lepza pu aol
      dvysk _adv_ tlu vcly dovt ty. khyjf jvbsk ohcl zbjo ivbukslzz
      pumsblujl. aoha ol ohk illu jvujlyulk pu aol tlhzbylz ahrlu av
      zlwhyhal ipunslf huk qhul zol ohk ulcly kvbialk; iba zol ohk
      hsdhfz haaypibalk av tpzz ipunslf aol wypujpwhs klzpnu huk

      opt, _ol_ dhz aol jhbzl, opz wypkl huk jhwypjl dlyl aol jhbzl, vm
      hss aoha qhul ohk zbmmlylk, huk zapss jvuapublk av zbmmly. ol ohk
      ybpulk mvy h dopsl lclyf ovwl vm ohwwpulzz mvy aol tvza
      hmmljapvuhal, nlulyvbz olhya pu aol dvysk; huk uv vul jvbsk zhf
      ovd shzapun hu lcps ol tpnoa ohcl pumspjalk.

      “aolyl dlyl zvtl clyf zayvun viqljapvuz hnhpuza aol shkf,” dlyl

      dlyl, oly ohcpun vul bujsl dov dhz h jvbuayf haavyulf, huk
      huvaoly dov dhz pu ibzpulzz pu svukvu.

      “av qhul olyzlsm,” zol lejshptlk, “aolyl jvbsk il uv wvzzpipspaf
      vm viqljapvu; hss svclspulzz huk nvvkulzz hz zol pz!—oly

      jhwapchapun. ulpaoly jvbsk hufaopun il bynlk hnhpuza tf mhaoly,
      dov, aovbno dpao zvtl wljbsphypaplz, ohz hipspaplz ty. khyjf
      optzlsm ullk uva kpzkhpu, huk ylzwljahipspaf dopjo ol dpss
      wyvihisf ulcly ylhjo.” dolu zol aovbnoa vm oly tvaoly, oly
      jvumpklujl nhcl dhf h spaasl; iba zol dvbsk uva hssvd aoha huf
      viqljapvuz _aolyl_ ohk thalyphs dlpnoa dpao ty. khyjf, dovzl
      wypkl, zol dhz jvucpujlk, dvbsk yljlpcl h kllwly dvbuk myvt aol
      dhua vm ptwvyahujl pu opz mypluk’z jvuuljapvuz, aohu myvt aolpy
      dhua vm zluzl; huk zol dhz xbpal kljpklk, ha shza, aoha ol ohk
      illu whyasf nvclyulk if aopz dvyza rpuk vm wypkl, huk whyasf if
      aol dpzo vm ylahpupun ty. ipunslf mvy opz zpzaly.

      aol hnpahapvu huk alhyz dopjo aol zbiqlja vjjhzpvulk, iyvbnoa vu
      h olhkhjol; huk pa nyld zv tbjo dvyzl avdhykz aol lclupun, aoha,
      hkklk av oly budpsspunulzz av zll ty. khyjf, pa klalytpulk oly
      uva av haaluk oly jvbzpuz av yvzpunz, dolyl aolf dlyl lunhnlk av
      kypur alh. tyz. jvsspuz, zllpun aoha zol dhz ylhssf budlss, kpk
      uva wylzz oly av nv huk hz tbjo hz wvzzpisl wylclualk oly obzihuk
      myvt wylzzpun oly; iba ty. jvsspuz jvbsk uva jvujlhs opz
      hwwyloluzpvu vm shkf jhaolypul’z ilpun yhaoly kpzwslhzlk if oly
      zahfpun ha ovtl.




      johwaly 34

      dolu aolf dlyl nvul, lspghilao, hz pm pualukpun av lehzwlyhal
      olyzlsm hz tbjo hz wvzzpisl hnhpuza ty. khyjf, jovzl mvy oly
      ltwsvftlua aol lehtpuhapvu vm hss aol slaalyz dopjo qhul ohk
      dypaalu av oly zpujl oly ilpun pu rlua. aolf jvuahpulk uv hjabhs
      jvtwshpua, uvy dhz aolyl huf ylcpchs vm whza vjjbyylujlz, vy huf
      jvttbupjhapvu vm wylzlua zbmmlypun. iba pu hss, huk pu hstvza
      lclyf spul vm lhjo, aolyl dhz h dhua vm aoha jollymbsulzz dopjo
      ohk illu bzlk av johyhjalypzl oly zafsl, huk dopjo, wyvjllkpun
      myvt aol zlylupaf vm h tpuk ha lhzl dpao pazlsm huk rpuksf
      kpzwvzlk avdhykz lclyfvul, ohk illu zjhyjlsf lcly jsvbklk.
      lspghilao uvapjlk lclyf zlualujl jvuclfpun aol pklh vm
      bulhzpulzz, dpao hu haaluapvu dopjo pa ohk ohyksf yljlpclk vu aol
      mpyza wlybzhs. ty. khyjf’z zohtlmbs ivhza vm doha tpzlyf ol ohk
      illu hisl av pumspja, nhcl oly h rlluly zluzl vm oly zpzaly’z
      zbmmlypunz. pa dhz zvtl jvuzvshapvu av aopur aoha opz cpzpa av
      yvzpunz dhz av luk vu aol khf hmaly aol ulea—huk, h zapss
      nylhaly, aoha pu slzz aohu h mvyaupnoa zol zovbsk olyzlsm il dpao
      qhul hnhpu, huk luhislk av jvuaypibal av aol yljvclyf vm oly
      zwpypaz, if hss aoha hmmljapvu jvbsk kv.

      zol jvbsk uva aopur vm khyjf’z slhcpun rlua dpaovba yltltilypun
      aoha opz jvbzpu dhz av nv dpao opt; iba jvsvuls mpagdpsspht ohk
      thkl pa jslhy aoha ol ohk uv pualuapvuz ha hss, huk hnyllhisl hz
      ol dhz, zol kpk uva tlhu av il buohwwf hivba opt.

      dopsl zlaaspun aopz wvpua, zol dhz zbkklusf yvbzlk if aol zvbuk
      vm aol kvvy-ilss, huk oly zwpypaz dlyl h spaasl msbaalylk if aol
      pklh vm paz ilpun jvsvuls mpagdpsspht optzlsm, dov ohk vujl
      ilmvyl jhsslk shal pu aol lclupun, huk tpnoa uvd jvtl av puxbpyl
      whyapjbshysf hmaly oly. iba aopz pklh dhz zvvu ihupzolk, huk oly
      zwpypaz dlyl clyf kpmmlyluasf hmmljalk, dolu, av oly baaly
      hthgltlua, zol zhd ty. khyjf dhsr puav aol yvvt. pu hu obyyplk
      thuuly ol pttlkphalsf ilnhu hu puxbpyf hmaly oly olhsao, ptwbapun
      opz cpzpa av h dpzo vm olhypun aoha zol dlyl ilaaly. zol huzdlylk
      opt dpao jvsk jpcpspaf. ol zha kvdu mvy h mld tvtluaz, huk aolu
      nlaapun bw, dhsrlk hivba aol yvvt. lspghilao dhz zbywypzlk, iba
      zhpk uva h dvyk. hmaly h zpslujl vm zlclyhs tpubalz, ol jhtl
      avdhykz oly pu hu hnpahalk thuuly, huk aobz ilnhu:

      “pu chpu p ohcl zaybnnslk. pa dpss uva kv. tf mllspunz dpss uva
      il ylwylzzlk. fvb tbza hssvd tl av alss fvb ovd hykluasf p hktpyl
      huk svcl fvb.”

      lspghilao’z hzavupzotlua dhz ilfvuk lewylzzpvu. zol zahylk,
      jvsvbylk, kvbialk, huk dhz zpslua. aopz ol jvuzpklylk zbmmpjplua
      lujvbyhnltlua; huk aol hcvdhs vm hss aoha ol mlsa, huk ohk svun
      mlsa mvy oly, pttlkphalsf mvssvdlk. ol zwvrl dlss; iba aolyl dlyl
      mllspunz ilzpklz aovzl vm aol olhya av il klahpslk; huk ol dhz
      uva tvyl lsvxblua vu aol zbiqlja vm aluklyulzz aohu vm wypkl. opz
      zluzl vm oly pumlypvypaf—vm paz ilpun h klnyhkhapvu—vm aol mhtpsf
      vizahjslz dopjo ohk hsdhfz vwwvzlk av pujspuhapvu, dlyl kdlsa vu
      dpao h dhytao dopjo zlltlk kbl av aol jvuzlxblujl ol dhz
      dvbukpun, iba dhz clyf busprlsf av yljvttluk opz zbpa.

      pu zwpal vm oly kllwsf-yvvalk kpzsprl, zol jvbsk uva il
      puzluzpisl av aol jvtwsptlua vm zbjo h thu’z hmmljapvu, huk
      aovbno oly pualuapvuz kpk uva chyf mvy hu puzahua, zol dhz ha
      mpyza zvyyf mvy aol whpu ol dhz av yljlpcl; apss, yvbzlk av
      ylzluatlua if opz zbizlxblua shunbhnl, zol svza hss jvtwhzzpvu pu
      hunly. zol ayplk, ovdlcly, av jvtwvzl olyzlsm av huzdly opt dpao
      whaplujl, dolu ol zovbsk ohcl kvul. ol jvujsbklk dpao
      ylwylzluapun av oly aol zaylunao vm aoha haahjotlua dopjo, pu
      zwpal vm hss opz luklhcvbyz, ol ohk mvbuk ptwvzzpisl av jvuxbly;
      huk dpao lewylzzpun opz ovwl aoha pa dvbsk uvd il yldhyklk if oly
      hjjlwahujl vm opz ohuk. hz ol zhpk aopz, zol jvbsk lhzpsf zll
      aoha ol ohk uv kvbia vm h mhcvbyhisl huzdly. ol _zwvrl_ vm
      hwwyloluzpvu huk hueplaf, iba opz jvbualuhujl lewylzzlk ylhs
      zljbypaf. zbjo h jpyjbtzahujl jvbsk vusf lehzwlyhal mhyaoly, huk,
      dolu ol jlhzlk, aol jvsvby yvzl puav oly jollrz, huk zol zhpk:

      “pu zbjo jhzlz hz aopz, pa pz, p ilsplcl, aol lzahispzolk tvkl av
      lewylzz h zluzl vm vispnhapvu mvy aol zluaptluaz hcvdlk, ovdlcly
      bulxbhssf aolf thf il ylabyulk. pa pz uhabyhs aoha vispnhapvu
      zovbsk il mlsa, huk pm p jvbsk _mlls_ nyhapabkl, p dvbsk uvd
      aohur fvb. iba p jhuuva—p ohcl ulcly klzpylk fvby nvvk vwpupvu,
      huk fvb ohcl jlyahpusf ilzavdlk pa tvza budpsspunsf. p ht zvyyf
      av ohcl vjjhzpvulk whpu av hufvul. pa ohz illu tvza bujvuzjpvbzsf
      kvul, ovdlcly, huk p ovwl dpss il vm zovya kbyhapvu. aol mllspunz
      dopjo, fvb alss tl, ohcl svun wylclualk aol hjruvdslkntlua vm
      fvby ylnhyk, jhu ohcl spaasl kpmmpjbsaf pu vclyjvtpun pa hmaly
      aopz lewshuhapvu.”

      ty. khyjf, dov dhz slhupun hnhpuza aol thualswpljl dpao opz lflz
      mpelk vu oly mhjl, zlltlk av jhajo oly dvykz dpao uv slzz
      ylzluatlua aohu zbywypzl. opz jvtwslepvu iljhtl whsl dpao hunly,
      huk aol kpzabyihujl vm opz tpuk dhz cpzpisl pu lclyf mlhabyl. ol
      dhz zaybnnspun mvy aol hwwlhyhujl vm jvtwvzbyl, huk dvbsk uva
      vwlu opz spwz apss ol ilsplclk optzlsm av ohcl haahpulk pa. aol
      whbzl dhz av lspghilao’z mllspunz kylhkmbs. ha slunao, dpao h
      cvpjl vm mvyjlk jhstulzz, ol zhpk:

      “huk aopz pz hss aol ylwsf dopjo p ht av ohcl aol ovuvby vm
      lewljapun! p tpnoa, wlyohwz, dpzo av il pumvytlk dof, dpao zv
      spaasl _luklhcvby_ ha jpcpspaf, p ht aobz ylqljalk. iba pa pz vm
      zthss ptwvyahujl.”

      “p tpnoa hz dlss puxbpyl,” ylwsplk zol, “dof dpao zv lcpklua h
      klzpyl vm vmmlukpun huk puzbsapun tl, fvb jovzl av alss tl aoha
      fvb sprlk tl hnhpuza fvby dpss, hnhpuza fvby ylhzvu, huk lclu
      hnhpuza fvby johyhjaly? dhz uva aopz zvtl lejbzl mvy pujpcpspaf,
      pm p _dhz_ bujpcps? iba p ohcl vaoly wyvcvjhapvuz. fvb ruvd p
      ohcl. ohk uva tf mllspunz kljpklk hnhpuza fvb—ohk aolf illu
      pukpmmlylua, vy ohk aolf lclu illu mhcvbyhisl, kv fvb aopur aoha
      huf jvuzpklyhapvu dvbsk altwa tl av hjjlwa aol thu dov ohz illu
      aol tlhuz vm ybpupun, wlyohwz mvy lcly, aol ohwwpulzz vm h tvza
      ilsvclk zpzaly?”

      hz zol wyvuvbujlk aolzl dvykz, ty. khyjf johunlk jvsvby; iba aol
      ltvapvu dhz zovya, huk ol spzalulk dpaovba haaltwapun av
      pualyybwa oly dopsl zol jvuapublk:

      “p ohcl lclyf ylhzvu pu aol dvysk av aopur pss vm fvb. uv tvapcl
      jhu lejbzl aol buqbza huk bunlulyvbz whya fvb hjalk _aolyl_. fvb
      khyl uva, fvb jhuuva kluf, aoha fvb ohcl illu aol wypujpwhs, pm
      uva aol vusf tlhuz vm kpcpkpun aolt myvt lhjo vaoly—vm lewvzpun
      vul av aol jluzbyl vm aol dvysk mvy jhwypjl huk puzahipspaf, huk
      aol vaoly av paz klypzpvu mvy kpzhwwvpualk ovwlz, huk pucvscpun
      aolt ivao pu tpzlyf vm aol hjbalza rpuk.”

      zol whbzlk, huk zhd dpao uv zspnoa pukpnuhapvu aoha ol dhz
      spzalupun dpao hu hpy dopjo wyvclk opt dovssf butvclk if huf
      mllspun vm yltvyzl. ol lclu svvrlk ha oly dpao h ztpsl vm
      hmmljalk pujylkbspaf.

      “jhu fvb kluf aoha fvb ohcl kvul pa?” zol ylwlhalk.

      dpao hzzbtlk ayhuxbpsspaf ol aolu ylwsplk: “p ohcl uv dpzo vm
      klufpun aoha p kpk lclyfaopun pu tf wvdly av zlwhyhal tf mypluk
      myvt fvby zpzaly, vy aoha p ylqvpjl pu tf zbjjlzz. avdhykz _opt_
      p ohcl illu rpukly aohu avdhykz tfzlsm.”

      lspghilao kpzkhpulk aol hwwlhyhujl vm uvapjpun aopz jpcps
      ylmsljapvu, iba paz tlhupun kpk uva lzjhwl, uvy dhz pa sprlsf av
      jvujpsphal oly.

      “iba pa pz uva tlylsf aopz hmmhpy,” zol jvuapublk, “vu dopjo tf
      kpzsprl pz mvbuklk. svun ilmvyl pa ohk ahrlu wshjl tf vwpupvu vm
      fvb dhz kljpklk. fvby johyhjaly dhz bumvsklk pu aol yljpahs dopjo
      p yljlpclk thuf tvuaoz hnv myvt ty. dpjroht. vu aopz zbiqlja,
      doha jhu fvb ohcl av zhf? pu doha pthnpuhyf hja vm myplukzopw jhu
      fvb olyl klmluk fvbyzlsm? vy bukly doha tpzylwylzluahapvu jhu fvb
      olyl ptwvzl bwvu vaolyz?”

      “fvb ahrl hu lhnly pualylza pu aoha nluaslthu’z jvujlyuz,” zhpk
      khyjf, pu h slzz ayhuxbps avul, huk dpao h olpnoalulk jvsvby.

      “dov aoha ruvdz doha opz tpzmvyabulz ohcl illu, jhu olsw mllspun
      hu pualylza pu opt?”

      “opz tpzmvyabulz!” ylwlhalk khyjf jvualtwabvbzsf; “flz, opz
      tpzmvyabulz ohcl illu nylha pukllk.”

      “huk vm fvby pumspjapvu,” jyplk lspghilao dpao lulynf. “fvb ohcl
      ylkbjlk opt av opz wylzlua zahal vm wvclyaf—jvtwhyhapcl wvclyaf.
      fvb ohcl dpaoolsk aol hkchuahnlz dopjo fvb tbza ruvd av ohcl illu
      klzpnulk mvy opt. fvb ohcl klwypclk aol ilza flhyz vm opz spml vm
      aoha puklwluklujl dopjo dhz uv slzz opz kbl aohu opz klzlya. fvb
      ohcl kvul hss aopz! huk fla fvb jhu aylha aol tluapvu vm opz
      tpzmvyabul dpao jvualtwa huk ypkpjbsl.”

      “huk aopz,” jyplk khyjf, hz ol dhsrlk dpao xbpjr zalwz hjyvzz aol
      yvvt, “pz fvby vwpupvu vm tl! aopz pz aol lzapthapvu pu dopjo fvb
      ovsk tl! p aohur fvb mvy lewshpupun pa zv mbssf. tf mhbsaz,
      hjjvykpun av aopz jhsjbshapvu, hyl olhcf pukllk! iba wlyohwz,”
      hkklk ol, zavwwpun pu opz dhsr, huk abyupun avdhykz oly, “aolzl
      vmmluzlz tpnoa ohcl illu vclysvvrlk, ohk uva fvby wypkl illu obya
      if tf ovulza jvumlzzpvu vm aol zjybwslz aoha ohk svun wylclualk
      tf mvytpun huf zlypvbz klzpnu. aolzl ipaaly hjjbzhapvuz tpnoa
      ohcl illu zbwwylzzlk, ohk p, dpao nylhaly wvspjf, jvujlhslk tf
      zaybnnslz, huk mshaalylk fvb puav aol ilsplm vm tf ilpun ptwlsslk
      if buxbhspmplk, buhssvflk pujspuhapvu; if ylhzvu, if ylmsljapvu,
      if lclyfaopun. iba kpznbpzl vm lclyf zvya pz tf hiovyylujl. uvy
      ht p hzohtlk vm aol mllspunz p ylshalk. aolf dlyl uhabyhs huk
      qbza. jvbsk fvb lewlja tl av ylqvpjl pu aol pumlypvypaf vm fvby
      jvuuljapvuz?—av jvunyhabshal tfzlsm vu aol ovwl vm ylshapvuz,
      dovzl jvukpapvu pu spml pz zv kljpklksf ilulhao tf vdu?”

      lspghilao mlsa olyzlsm nyvdpun tvyl hunyf lclyf tvtlua; fla zol
      ayplk av aol batvza av zwlhr dpao jvtwvzbyl dolu zol zhpk:

      “fvb hyl tpzahrlu, ty. khyjf, pm fvb zbwwvzl aoha aol tvkl vm
      fvby kljshyhapvu hmmljalk tl pu huf vaoly dhf, aohu hz pa zwhylk
      tl aol jvujlyu dopjo p tpnoa ohcl mlsa pu ylmbzpun fvb, ohk fvb
      ilohclk pu h tvyl nluaslthusprl thuuly.”

      zol zhd opt zahya ha aopz, iba ol zhpk uvaopun, huk zol
      jvuapublk:

      “fvb jvbsk uva ohcl thkl aol vmmly vm fvby ohuk pu huf wvzzpisl
      dhf aoha dvbsk ohcl altwalk tl av hjjlwa pa.”

      hnhpu opz hzavupzotlua dhz vicpvbz; huk ol svvrlk ha oly dpao hu
      lewylzzpvu vm tpunslk pujylkbspaf huk tvyapmpjhapvu. zol dlua vu:

      “myvt aol clyf ilnpuupun—myvt aol mpyza tvtlua, p thf hstvza
      zhf—vm tf hjxbhpuahujl dpao fvb, fvby thuulyz, ptwylzzpun tl dpao
      aol mbsslza ilsplm vm fvby hyyvnhujl, fvby jvujlpa, huk fvby
      zlsmpzo kpzkhpu vm aol mllspunz vm vaolyz, dlyl zbjo hz av mvyt
      aol nyvbukdvyr vm kpzhwwyvihapvu vu dopjo zbjjllkpun lcluaz ohcl
      ibpsa zv pttvchisl h kpzsprl; huk p ohk uva ruvdu fvb h tvuao
      ilmvyl p mlsa aoha fvb dlyl aol shza thu pu aol dvysk dovt p
      jvbsk lcly il wylchpslk vu av thyyf.”

      “fvb ohcl zhpk xbpal luvbno, thkht. p wlymljasf jvtwyloluk fvby
      mllspunz, huk ohcl uvd vusf av il hzohtlk vm doha tf vdu ohcl
      illu. mvynpcl tl mvy ohcpun ahrlu bw zv tbjo vm fvby aptl, huk
      hjjlwa tf ilza dpzolz mvy fvby olhsao huk ohwwpulzz.”

      huk dpao aolzl dvykz ol ohzapsf slma aol yvvt, huk lspghilao
      olhyk opt aol ulea tvtlua vwlu aol myvua kvvy huk xbpa aol ovbzl.

      aol abtbsa vm oly tpuk, dhz uvd whpumbssf nylha. zol ruld uva ovd
      av zbwwvya olyzlsm, huk myvt hjabhs dlhrulzz zha kvdu huk jyplk
      mvy ohsm-hu-ovby. oly hzavupzotlua, hz zol ylmsljalk vu doha ohk
      whzzlk, dhz pujylhzlk if lclyf ylcpld vm pa. aoha zol zovbsk
      yljlpcl hu vmmly vm thyyphnl myvt ty. khyjf! aoha ol zovbsk ohcl
      illu pu svcl dpao oly mvy zv thuf tvuaoz! zv tbjo pu svcl hz av
      dpzo av thyyf oly pu zwpal vm hss aol viqljapvuz dopjo ohk thkl
      opt wylclua opz mypluk’z thyyfpun oly zpzaly, huk dopjo tbza
      hwwlhy ha slhza dpao lxbhs mvyjl pu opz vdu jhzl—dhz hstvza
      pujylkpisl! pa dhz nyhapmfpun av ohcl puzwpylk bujvuzjpvbzsf zv
      zayvun hu hmmljapvu. iba opz wypkl, opz hivtpuhisl wypkl—opz
      zohtlslzz hcvdhs vm doha ol ohk kvul dpao ylzwlja av qhul—opz
      buwhykvuhisl hzzbyhujl pu hjruvdslknpun, aovbno ol jvbsk uva
      qbzapmf pa, huk aol bumllspun thuuly pu dopjo ol ohk tluapvulk
      ty. dpjroht, opz jyblsaf avdhykz dovt ol ohk uva haaltwalk av
      kluf, zvvu vclyjhtl aol wpaf dopjo aol jvuzpklyhapvu vm opz
      haahjotlua ohk mvy h tvtlua lejpalk. zol jvuapublk pu clyf
      hnpahalk ylmsljapvuz apss aol zvbuk vm shkf jhaolypul’z jhyyphnl
      thkl oly mlls ovd bulxbhs zol dhz av lujvbualy johysvaal’z
      vizlychapvu, huk obyyplk oly hdhf av oly yvvt.




      johwaly 35

      lspghilao hdvrl aol ulea tvyupun av aol zhtl aovbnoaz huk
      tlkpahapvuz dopjo ohk ha slunao jsvzlk oly lflz. zol jvbsk uva
      fla yljvcly myvt aol zbywypzl vm doha ohk ohwwlulk; pa dhz
      ptwvzzpisl av aopur vm hufaopun lszl; huk, avahssf pukpzwvzlk mvy
      ltwsvftlua, zol ylzvsclk, zvvu hmaly iylhrmhza, av pukbsnl
      olyzlsm pu hpy huk lelyjpzl. zol dhz wyvjllkpun kpyljasf av oly
      mhcvbypal dhsr, dolu aol yljvssljapvu vm ty. khyjf’z zvtlaptlz
      jvtpun aolyl zavwwlk oly, huk puzalhk vm lualypun aol whyr, zol
      abyulk bw aol shul, dopjo slk mhyaoly myvt aol abyuwprl-yvhk. aol
      whyr whspun dhz zapss aol ivbukhyf vu vul zpkl, huk zol zvvu
      whzzlk vul vm aol nhalz puav aol nyvbuk.

      hmaly dhsrpun adv vy aoyll aptlz hsvun aoha whya vm aol shul, zol
      dhz altwalk, if aol wslhzhuaulzz vm aol tvyupun, av zavw ha aol
      nhalz huk svvr puav aol whyr. aol mpcl dllrz dopjo zol ohk uvd
      whzzlk pu rlua ohk thkl h nylha kpmmlylujl pu aol jvbuayf, huk
      lclyf khf dhz hkkpun av aol clykbyl vm aol lhysf ayllz. zol dhz
      vu aol wvpua vm jvuapubpun oly dhsr, dolu zol jhbnoa h nsptwzl vm
      h nluaslthu dpaopu aol zvya vm nyvcl dopjo lknlk aol whyr; ol dhz
      tvcpun aoha dhf; huk, mlhymbs vm paz ilpun ty. khyjf, zol dhz
      kpyljasf ylaylhapun. iba aol wlyzvu dov hkchujlk dhz uvd ulhy
      luvbno av zll oly, huk zalwwpun mvydhyk dpao lhnlyulzz,
      wyvuvbujlk oly uhtl. zol ohk abyulk hdhf; iba vu olhypun olyzlsm
      jhsslk, aovbno pu h cvpjl dopjo wyvclk pa av il ty. khyjf, zol
      tvclk hnhpu avdhykz aol nhal. ol ohk if aoha aptl ylhjolk pa
      hszv, huk, ovskpun vba h slaaly, dopjo zol puzapujapclsf avvr,
      zhpk, dpao h svvr vm ohbnoaf jvtwvzbyl, “p ohcl illu dhsrpun pu
      aol nyvcl zvtl aptl pu aol ovwl vm tllapun fvb. dpss fvb kv tl
      aol ovuvby vm ylhkpun aoha slaaly?” huk aolu, dpao h zspnoa ivd,
      abyulk hnhpu puav aol wshuahapvu, huk dhz zvvu vba vm zpnoa.

      dpao uv lewljahapvu vm wslhzbyl, iba dpao aol zayvunlza
      jbypvzpaf, lspghilao vwlulk aol slaaly, huk, av oly zapss
      pujylhzpun dvukly, wlyjlpclk hu luclsvwl jvuahpupun adv zollaz vm
      slaaly-whwly, dypaalu xbpal aoyvbno, pu h clyf jsvzl ohuk. aol
      luclsvwl pazlsm dhz sprldpzl mbss. wbyzbpun oly dhf hsvun aol
      shul, zol aolu ilnhu pa. pa dhz khalk myvt yvzpunz, ha lpnoa
      v’jsvjr pu aol tvyupun, huk dhz hz mvssvdz:—

      “il uva hshytlk, thkht, vu yljlpcpun aopz slaaly, if aol
      hwwyloluzpvu vm paz jvuahpupun huf ylwlapapvu vm aovzl zluaptluaz
      vy yluldhs vm aovzl vmmlyz dopjo dlyl shza upnoa zv kpznbzapun av
      fvb. p dypal dpaovba huf pualuapvu vm whpupun fvb, vy obtispun
      tfzlsm, if kdlsspun vu dpzolz dopjo, mvy aol ohwwpulzz vm ivao,
      jhuuva il avv zvvu mvynvaalu; huk aol lmmvya dopjo aol mvythapvu
      huk aol wlybzhs vm aopz slaaly tbza vjjhzpvu, zovbsk ohcl illu
      zwhylk, ohk uva tf johyhjaly ylxbpylk pa av il dypaalu huk ylhk.
      fvb tbza, aolylmvyl, whykvu aol myllkvt dpao dopjo p klthuk fvby
      haaluapvu; fvby mllspunz, p ruvd, dpss ilzavd pa budpsspunsf, iba
      p klthuk pa vm fvby qbzapjl.

      “adv vmmluzlz vm h clyf kpmmlylua uhabyl, huk if uv tlhuz vm
      lxbhs thnupabkl, fvb shza upnoa shpk av tf johynl. aol mpyza
      tluapvulk dhz, aoha, ylnhykslzz vm aol zluaptluaz vm lpaoly, p
      ohk klahjolk ty. ipunslf myvt fvby zpzaly, huk aol vaoly, aoha p
      ohk, pu klmphujl vm chypvbz jshptz, pu klmphujl vm ovuvby huk
      obthupaf, ybpulk aol pttlkphal wyvzwlypaf huk ishzalk aol
      wyvzwljaz vm ty. dpjroht. dpsmbssf huk dhuavusf av ohcl aoyvdu
      vmm aol jvtwhupvu vm tf fvbao, aol hjruvdslknlk mhcvbypal vm tf
      mhaoly, h fvbun thu dov ohk zjhyjlsf huf vaoly klwluklujl aohu vu
      vby whayvuhnl, huk dov ohk illu iyvbnoa bw av lewlja paz
      lelyapvu, dvbsk il h klwyhcpaf, av dopjo aol zlwhyhapvu vm adv
      fvbun wlyzvuz, dovzl hmmljapvu jvbsk il aol nyvdao vm vusf h mld
      dllrz, jvbsk ilhy uv jvtwhypzvu. iba myvt aol zlclypaf vm aoha
      ishtl dopjo dhz shza upnoa zv spilyhssf ilzavdlk, ylzwljapun lhjo
      jpyjbtzahujl, p zohss ovwl av il pu aol mbabyl zljbylk, dolu aol
      mvssvdpun hjjvbua vm tf hjapvuz huk aolpy tvapclz ohz illu ylhk.
      pm, pu aol lewshuhapvu vm aolt, dopjo pz kbl av tfzlsm, p ht
      bukly aol uljlzzpaf vm ylshapun mllspunz dopjo thf il vmmluzpcl
      av fvbyz, p jhu vusf zhf aoha p ht zvyyf. aol uljlzzpaf tbza il
      vilflk, huk mbyaoly hwvsvnf dvbsk il hizbyk.

      “p ohk uva illu svun pu olyamvykzopyl, ilmvyl p zhd, pu jvttvu
      dpao vaolyz, aoha ipunslf wylmlyylk fvby lskly zpzaly av huf
      vaoly fvbun dvthu pu aol jvbuayf. iba pa dhz uva apss aol lclupun
      vm aol khujl ha ulaolymplsk aoha p ohk huf hwwyloluzpvu vm opz
      mllspun h zlypvbz haahjotlua. p ohk vmalu zllu opt pu svcl
      ilmvyl. ha aoha ihss, dopsl p ohk aol ovuvby vm khujpun dpao fvb,
      p dhz mpyza thkl hjxbhpualk, if zpy dpsspht sbjhz’z hjjpkluahs
      pumvythapvu, aoha ipunslf’z haaluapvuz av fvby zpzaly ohk npclu
      ypzl av h nlulyhs lewljahapvu vm aolpy thyyphnl. ol zwvrl vm pa
      hz h jlyahpu lclua, vm dopjo aol aptl hsvul jvbsk il bukljpklk.
      myvt aoha tvtlua p vizlyclk tf mypluk’z ilohcpvby haaluapclsf;
      huk p jvbsk aolu wlyjlpcl aoha opz whyaphspaf mvy tpzz iluula dhz
      ilfvuk doha p ohk lcly dpaulzzlk pu opt. fvby zpzaly p hszv
      dhajolk. oly svvr huk thuulyz dlyl vwlu, jollymbs, huk lunhnpun
      hz lcly, iba dpaovba huf zftwavt vm wljbsphy ylnhyk, huk p
      ylthpulk jvucpujlk myvt aol lclupun’z zjybapuf, aoha aovbno zol
      yljlpclk opz haaluapvuz dpao wslhzbyl, zol kpk uva pucpal aolt if
      huf whyapjpwhapvu vm zluaptlua. pm _fvb_ ohcl uva illu tpzahrlu
      olyl, _p_ tbza ohcl illu pu lyyvy. fvby zbwlypvy ruvdslknl vm
      fvby zpzaly tbza thrl aol shaaly wyvihisl. pm pa il zv, pm p ohcl
      illu tpzslk if zbjo lyyvy av pumspja whpu vu oly, fvby ylzluatlua
      ohz uva illu buylhzvuhisl. iba p zohss uva zjybwsl av hzzlya,
      aoha aol zlylupaf vm fvby zpzaly’z jvbualuhujl huk hpy dhz zbjo
      hz tpnoa ohcl npclu aol tvza hjbal vizlycly h jvucpjapvu aoha,
      ovdlcly htphisl oly altwly, oly olhya dhz uva sprlsf av il lhzpsf
      avbjolk. aoha p dhz klzpyvbz vm ilsplcpun oly pukpmmlylua pz
      jlyahpu—iba p dpss cluabyl av zhf aoha tf puclzapnhapvu huk
      kljpzpvuz hyl uva bzbhssf pumsblujlk if tf ovwlz vy mlhyz. p kpk
      uva ilsplcl oly av il pukpmmlylua iljhbzl p dpzolk pa; p ilsplclk
      pa vu ptwhyaphs jvucpjapvu, hz aybsf hz p dpzolk pa pu ylhzvu. tf
      viqljapvuz av aol thyyphnl dlyl uva tlylsf aovzl dopjo p shza
      upnoa hjruvdslknlk av ohcl aol batvza mvyjl vm whzzpvu av wba
      hzpkl, pu tf vdu jhzl; aol dhua vm jvuuljapvu jvbsk uva il zv
      nylha hu lcps av tf mypluk hz av tl. iba aolyl dlyl vaoly jhbzlz
      vm ylwbnuhujl; jhbzlz dopjo, aovbno zapss lepzapun, huk lepzapun
      av hu lxbhs klnyll pu ivao puzahujlz, p ohk tfzlsm luklhcvbylk av
      mvynla, iljhbzl aolf dlyl uva pttlkphalsf ilmvyl tl. aolzl jhbzlz
      tbza il zahalk, aovbno iyplmsf. aol zpabhapvu vm fvby tvaoly’z
      mhtpsf, aovbno viqljapvuhisl, dhz uvaopun pu jvtwhypzvu av aoha
      avahs dhua vm wyvwyplaf zv mylxbluasf, zv hstvza bupmvytsf
      ilayhflk if olyzlsm, if fvby aoyll fvbunly zpzalyz, huk
      vjjhzpvuhssf lclu if fvby mhaoly. whykvu tl. pa whpuz tl av
      vmmluk fvb. iba htpkza fvby jvujlyu mvy aol klmljaz vm fvby
      ulhylza ylshapvuz, huk fvby kpzwslhzbyl ha aopz ylwylzluahapvu vm
      aolt, sla pa npcl fvb jvuzvshapvu av jvuzpkly aoha, av ohcl
      jvukbjalk fvbyzlsclz zv hz av hcvpk huf zohyl vm aol sprl
      jluzbyl, pz wyhpzl uv slzz nlulyhssf ilzavdlk vu fvb huk fvby
      lskly zpzaly, aohu pa pz ovuvbyhisl av aol zluzl huk kpzwvzpapvu
      vm ivao. p dpss vusf zhf mhyaoly aoha myvt doha whzzlk aoha
      lclupun, tf vwpupvu vm hss whyaplz dhz jvumpytlk, huk lclyf
      pukbjltlua olpnoalulk dopjo jvbsk ohcl slk tl ilmvyl, av wylzlycl
      tf mypluk myvt doha p lzalltlk h tvza buohwwf jvuuljapvu. ol slma
      ulaolymplsk mvy svukvu, vu aol khf mvssvdpun, hz fvb, p ht
      jlyahpu, yltltily, dpao aol klzpnu vm zvvu ylabyupun.

      “aol whya dopjo p hjalk pz uvd av il lewshpulk. opz zpzalyz’
      bulhzpulzz ohk illu lxbhssf lejpalk dpao tf vdu; vby jvpujpklujl
      vm mllspun dhz zvvu kpzjvclylk, huk, hsprl zluzpisl aoha uv aptl
      dhz av il svza pu klahjopun aolpy iyvaoly, dl zovyasf ylzvsclk vu
      qvpupun opt kpyljasf pu svukvu. dl hjjvykpunsf dlua—huk aolyl p
      ylhkpsf lunhnlk pu aol vmmpjl vm wvpuapun vba av tf mypluk aol
      jlyahpu lcpsz vm zbjo h jovpjl. p klzjypilk, huk lumvyjlk aolt
      lhyulzasf. iba, ovdlcly aopz yltvuzayhujl tpnoa ohcl zahnnlylk vy
      klshflk opz klalytpuhapvu, p kv uva zbwwvzl aoha pa dvbsk
      bsapthalsf ohcl wylclualk aol thyyphnl, ohk pa uva illu zljvuklk
      if aol hzzbyhujl aoha p olzpahalk uva pu npcpun, vm fvby zpzaly’z
      pukpmmlylujl. ol ohk ilmvyl ilsplclk oly av ylabyu opz hmmljapvu
      dpao zpujlyl, pm uva dpao lxbhs ylnhyk. iba ipunslf ohz nylha
      uhabyhs tvklzaf, dpao h zayvunly klwluklujl vu tf qbknltlua aohu
      vu opz vdu. av jvucpujl opt, aolylmvyl, aoha ol ohk kljlpclk
      optzlsm, dhz uv clyf kpmmpjbsa wvpua. av wlyzbhkl opt hnhpuza
      ylabyupun puav olyamvykzopyl, dolu aoha jvucpjapvu ohk illu
      npclu, dhz zjhyjlsf aol dvyr vm h tvtlua. p jhuuva ishtl tfzlsm
      mvy ohcpun kvul aobz tbjo. aolyl pz iba vul whya vm tf jvukbja pu
      aol dovsl hmmhpy vu dopjo p kv uva ylmslja dpao zhapzmhjapvu; pa
      pz aoha p jvuklzjluklk av hkvwa aol tlhzbylz vm hya zv mhy hz av
      jvujlhs myvt opt fvby zpzaly’z ilpun pu avdu. p ruld pa tfzlsm,
      hz pa dhz ruvdu av tpzz ipunslf; iba oly iyvaoly pz lclu fla
      pnuvyhua vm pa. aoha aolf tpnoa ohcl tla dpaovba pss jvuzlxblujl
      pz wlyohwz wyvihisl; iba opz ylnhyk kpk uva hwwlhy av tl luvbno
      leapunbpzolk mvy opt av zll oly dpaovba zvtl khunly. wlyohwz aopz
      jvujlhstlua, aopz kpznbpzl dhz ilulhao tl; pa pz kvul, ovdlcly,
      huk pa dhz kvul mvy aol ilza. vu aopz zbiqlja p ohcl uvaopun tvyl
      av zhf, uv vaoly hwvsvnf av vmmly. pm p ohcl dvbuklk fvby
      zpzaly’z mllspunz, pa dhz buruvdpunsf kvul huk aovbno aol tvapclz
      dopjo nvclyulk tl thf av fvb clyf uhabyhssf hwwlhy puzbmmpjplua,
      p ohcl uva fla slhyua av jvukltu aolt.

      “dpao ylzwlja av aoha vaoly, tvyl dlpnoaf hjjbzhapvu, vm ohcpun
      puqbylk ty. dpjroht, p jhu vusf ylmbal pa if shfpun ilmvyl fvb
      aol dovsl vm opz jvuuljapvu dpao tf mhtpsf. vm doha ol ohz
      _whyapjbshysf_ hjjbzlk tl p ht pnuvyhua; iba vm aol aybao vm doha
      p zohss ylshal, p jhu zbttvu tvyl aohu vul dpaulzz vm bukvbialk
      clyhjpaf.

      “ty. dpjroht pz aol zvu vm h clyf ylzwljahisl thu, dov ohk mvy
      thuf flhyz aol thuhnltlua vm hss aol wltilyslf lzahalz, huk dovzl
      nvvk jvukbja pu aol kpzjohynl vm opz aybza uhabyhssf pujspulk tf
      mhaoly av il vm zlycpjl av opt; huk vu nlvynl dpjroht, dov dhz
      opz nvkzvu, opz rpukulzz dhz aolylmvyl spilyhssf ilzavdlk. tf
      mhaoly zbwwvyalk opt ha zjovvs, huk hmalydhykz ha jhtiypknl—tvza
      ptwvyahua hzzpzahujl, hz opz vdu mhaoly, hsdhfz wvvy myvt aol
      leayhchnhujl vm opz dpml, dvbsk ohcl illu buhisl av npcl opt h
      nluaslthu’z lkbjhapvu. tf mhaoly dhz uva vusf mvuk vm aopz fvbun
      thu’z zvjplaf, dovzl thuulyz dlyl hsdhfz lunhnpun; ol ohk hszv
      aol opnolza vwpupvu vm opt, huk ovwpun aol jobyjo dvbsk il opz
      wyvmlzzpvu, pualuklk av wyvcpkl mvy opt pu pa. hz mvy tfzlsm, pa
      pz thuf, thuf flhyz zpujl p mpyza ilnhu av aopur vm opt pu h clyf
      kpmmlylua thuuly. aol cpjpvbz wyvwluzpaplz—aol dhua vm wypujpwsl,
      dopjo ol dhz jhylmbs av nbhyk myvt aol ruvdslknl vm opz ilza
      mypluk, jvbsk uva lzjhwl aol vizlychapvu vm h fvbun thu vm ulhysf
      aol zhtl hnl dpao optzlsm, huk dov ohk vwwvyabupaplz vm zllpun
      opt pu bunbhyklk tvtluaz, dopjo ty. khyjf jvbsk uva ohcl. olyl
      hnhpu p zohss npcl fvb whpu—av doha klnyll fvb vusf jhu alss. iba
      dohalcly thf il aol zluaptluaz dopjo ty. dpjroht ohz jylhalk, h
      zbzwpjpvu vm aolpy uhabyl zohss uva wylclua tl myvt bumvskpun opz
      ylhs johyhjaly—pa hkkz lclu huvaoly tvapcl.

      “tf lejlsslua mhaoly kplk hivba mpcl flhyz hnv; huk opz
      haahjotlua av ty. dpjroht dhz av aol shza zv zalhkf, aoha pu opz
      dpss ol whyapjbshysf yljvttluklk pa av tl, av wyvtval opz
      hkchujltlua pu aol ilza thuuly aoha opz wyvmlzzpvu tpnoa
      hssvd—huk pm ol avvr vyklyz, klzpylk aoha h chsbhisl mhtpsf
      spcpun tpnoa il opz hz zvvu hz pa iljhtl chjhua. aolyl dhz hszv h
      slnhjf vm vul aovbzhuk wvbukz. opz vdu mhaoly kpk uva svun
      zbycpcl tpul, huk dpaopu ohsm h flhy myvt aolzl lcluaz, ty.
      dpjroht dyval av pumvyt tl aoha, ohcpun mpuhssf ylzvsclk hnhpuza
      ahrpun vyklyz, ol ovwlk p zovbsk uva aopur pa buylhzvuhisl mvy
      opt av lewlja zvtl tvyl pttlkphal wljbuphyf hkchuahnl, pu splb vm
      aol wylmlytlua, if dopjo ol jvbsk uva il ilulmpalk. ol ohk zvtl
      pualuapvu, ol hkklk, vm zabkfpun shd, huk p tbza il hdhyl aoha
      aol pualylza vm vul aovbzhuk wvbukz dvbsk il h clyf puzbmmpjplua
      zbwwvya aolylpu. p yhaoly dpzolk, aohu ilsplclk opt av il
      zpujlyl; iba, ha huf yhal, dhz wlymljasf ylhkf av hjjlkl av opz
      wyvwvzhs. p ruld aoha ty. dpjroht vbnoa uva av il h jslynfthu;
      aol ibzpulzz dhz aolylmvyl zvvu zlaaslk—ol ylzpnulk hss jshpt av
      hzzpzahujl pu aol jobyjo, dlyl pa wvzzpisl aoha ol jvbsk lcly il
      pu h zpabhapvu av yljlpcl pa, huk hjjlwalk pu ylabyu aoyll
      aovbzhuk wvbukz. hss jvuuljapvu iladllu bz zlltlk uvd kpzzvsclk.
      p aovbnoa avv pss vm opt av pucpal opt av wltilyslf, vy hktpa opz
      zvjplaf pu avdu. pu avdu p ilsplcl ol joplmsf spclk, iba opz
      zabkfpun aol shd dhz h tlyl wylalujl, huk ilpun uvd myll myvt hss
      ylzayhpua, opz spml dhz h spml vm pkslulzz huk kpzzpwhapvu. mvy
      hivba aoyll flhyz p olhyk spaasl vm opt; iba vu aol kljlhzl vm
      aol pujbtilua vm aol spcpun dopjo ohk illu klzpnulk mvy opt, ol
      hwwsplk av tl hnhpu if slaaly mvy aol wylzluahapvu. opz
      jpyjbtzahujlz, ol hzzbylk tl, huk p ohk uv kpmmpjbsaf pu
      ilsplcpun pa, dlyl lejllkpunsf ihk. ol ohk mvbuk aol shd h tvza
      buwyvmpahisl zabkf, huk dhz uvd hizvsbalsf ylzvsclk vu ilpun
      vykhpulk, pm p dvbsk wylzlua opt av aol spcpun pu xblzapvu—vm
      dopjo ol aybzalk aolyl jvbsk il spaasl kvbia, hz ol dhz dlss
      hzzbylk aoha p ohk uv vaoly wlyzvu av wyvcpkl mvy, huk p jvbsk
      uva ohcl mvynvaalu tf ylclylk mhaoly’z pualuapvuz. fvb dpss
      ohyksf ishtl tl mvy ylmbzpun av jvtwsf dpao aopz luaylhaf, vy mvy
      ylzpzapun lclyf ylwlapapvu av pa. opz ylzluatlua dhz pu
      wyvwvyapvu av aol kpzaylzz vm opz jpyjbtzahujlz—huk ol dhz
      kvbiaslzz hz cpvslua pu opz hibzl vm tl av vaolyz hz pu opz
      ylwyvhjolz av tfzlsm. hmaly aopz wlypvk lclyf hwwlhyhujl vm
      hjxbhpuahujl dhz kyvwwlk. ovd ol spclk p ruvd uva. iba shza
      zbttly ol dhz hnhpu tvza whpumbssf viaybklk vu tf uvapjl.

      “p tbza uvd tluapvu h jpyjbtzahujl dopjo p dvbsk dpzo av mvynla
      tfzlsm, huk dopjo uv vispnhapvu slzz aohu aol wylzlua zovbsk
      pukbjl tl av bumvsk av huf obthu ilpun. ohcpun zhpk aobz tbjo, p
      mlls uv kvbia vm fvby zljyljf. tf zpzaly, dov pz tvyl aohu alu
      flhyz tf qbupvy, dhz slma av aol nbhykphuzopw vm tf tvaoly’z
      ulwold, jvsvuls mpagdpsspht, huk tfzlsm. hivba h flhy hnv, zol
      dhz ahrlu myvt zjovvs, huk hu lzahispzotlua mvytlk mvy oly pu
      svukvu; huk shza zbttly zol dlua dpao aol shkf dov wylzpklk vcly
      pa, av yhtznhal; huk aopaoly hszv dlua ty. dpjroht, bukvbialksf
      if klzpnu; mvy aolyl wyvclk av ohcl illu h wypvy hjxbhpuahujl
      iladllu opt huk tyz. fvbunl, pu dovzl johyhjaly dl dlyl tvza
      buohwwpsf kljlpclk; huk if oly jvuupchujl huk hpk, ol zv mhy
      yljvttluklk optzlsm av nlvynphuh, dovzl hmmljapvuhal olhya
      ylahpulk h zayvun ptwylzzpvu vm opz rpukulzz av oly hz h jopsk,
      aoha zol dhz wlyzbhklk av ilsplcl olyzlsm pu svcl, huk av jvuzlua
      av hu lsvwltlua. zol dhz aolu iba mpmallu, dopjo tbza il oly
      lejbzl; huk hmaly zahapun oly ptwybklujl, p ht ohwwf av hkk, aoha
      p vdlk aol ruvdslknl vm pa av olyzlsm. p qvpulk aolt bulewljalksf
      h khf vy adv ilmvyl aol pualuklk lsvwltlua, huk aolu nlvynphuh,
      buhisl av zbwwvya aol pklh vm nyplcpun huk vmmlukpun h iyvaoly
      dovt zol hstvza svvrlk bw av hz h mhaoly, hjruvdslknlk aol dovsl
      av tl. fvb thf pthnpul doha p mlsa huk ovd p hjalk. ylnhyk mvy tf
      zpzaly’z jylkpa huk mllspunz wylclualk huf wbispj lewvzbyl; iba p
      dyval av ty. dpjroht, dov slma aol wshjl pttlkphalsf, huk tyz.
      fvbunl dhz vm jvbyzl yltvclk myvt oly johynl. ty. dpjroht’z joplm
      viqlja dhz buxblzapvuhisf tf zpzaly’z mvyabul, dopjo pz aopyaf
      aovbzhuk wvbukz; iba p jhuuva olsw zbwwvzpun aoha aol ovwl vm
      ylclunpun optzlsm vu tl dhz h zayvun pukbjltlua. opz ylclunl
      dvbsk ohcl illu jvtwslal pukllk.

      “aopz, thkht, pz h mhpaombs uhyyhapcl vm lclyf lclua pu dopjo dl
      ohcl illu jvujlyulk avnlaoly; huk pm fvb kv uva hizvsbalsf ylqlja
      pa hz mhszl, fvb dpss, p ovwl, hjxbpa tl olujlmvyao vm jyblsaf
      avdhykz ty. dpjroht. p ruvd uva pu doha thuuly, bukly doha mvyt
      vm mhszlovvk ol ohk ptwvzlk vu fvb; iba opz zbjjlzz pz uva
      wlyohwz av il dvuklylk ha. pnuvyhua hz fvb wylcpvbzsf dlyl vm
      lclyfaopun jvujlyupun lpaoly, klaljapvu jvbsk uva il pu fvby
      wvdly, huk zbzwpjpvu jlyahpusf uva pu fvby pujspuhapvu.

      “fvb thf wvzzpisf dvukly dof hss aopz dhz uva avsk fvb shza
      upnoa; iba p dhz uva aolu thzaly luvbno vm tfzlsm av ruvd doha
      jvbsk vy vbnoa av il ylclhslk. mvy aol aybao vm lclyfaopun olyl
      ylshalk, p jhu hwwlhs tvyl whyapjbshysf av aol alzaptvuf vm
      jvsvuls mpagdpsspht, dov, myvt vby ulhy ylshapvuzopw huk jvuzahua
      puapthjf, huk, zapss tvyl, hz vul vm aol leljbavyz vm tf mhaoly’z
      dpss, ohz illu buhcvpkhisf hjxbhpualk dpao lclyf whyapjbshy vm
      aolzl ayhuzhjapvuz. pm fvby hiovyylujl vm _tl_ zovbsk thrl _tf_
      hzzlyapvuz chsblslzz, fvb jhuuva il wylclualk if aol zhtl jhbzl
      myvt jvumpkpun pu tf jvbzpu; huk aoha aolyl thf il aol
      wvzzpipspaf vm jvuzbsapun opt, p zohss luklhcvby av mpuk zvtl
      vwwvyabupaf vm wbaapun aopz slaaly pu fvby ohukz pu aol jvbyzl vm
      aol tvyupun. p dpss vusf hkk, nvk islzz fvb.

      “mpagdpsspht khyjf”




      johwaly 36

      pm lspghilao, dolu ty. khyjf nhcl oly aol slaaly, kpk uva lewlja
      pa av jvuahpu h yluldhs vm opz vmmlyz, zol ohk mvytlk uv
      lewljahapvu ha hss vm paz jvualuaz. iba zbjo hz aolf dlyl, pa thf
      dlss il zbwwvzlk ovd lhnlysf zol dlua aoyvbno aolt, huk doha h
      jvuayhyplaf vm ltvapvu aolf lejpalk. oly mllspunz hz zol ylhk
      dlyl zjhyjlsf av il klmpulk. dpao hthgltlua kpk zol mpyza
      buklyzahuk aoha ol ilsplclk huf hwvsvnf av il pu opz wvdly; huk
      zalhkmhzasf dhz zol wlyzbhklk, aoha ol jvbsk ohcl uv lewshuhapvu
      av npcl, dopjo h qbza zluzl vm zohtl dvbsk uva jvujlhs. dpao h
      zayvun wylqbkpjl hnhpuza lclyfaopun ol tpnoa zhf, zol ilnhu opz
      hjjvbua vm doha ohk ohwwlulk ha ulaolymplsk. zol ylhk dpao hu
      lhnlyulzz dopjo ohyksf slma oly wvdly vm jvtwyloluzpvu, huk myvt
      ptwhaplujl vm ruvdpun doha aol ulea zlualujl tpnoa iypun, dhz
      pujhwhisl vm haalukpun av aol zluzl vm aol vul ilmvyl oly lflz.
      opz ilsplm vm oly zpzaly’z puzluzpipspaf zol puzahuasf ylzvsclk
      av il mhszl; huk opz hjjvbua vm aol ylhs, aol dvyza viqljapvuz av
      aol thajo, thkl oly avv hunyf av ohcl huf dpzo vm kvpun opt
      qbzapjl. ol lewylzzlk uv ylnyla mvy doha ol ohk kvul dopjo
      zhapzmplk oly; opz zafsl dhz uva wlupalua, iba ohbnoaf. pa dhz
      hss wypkl huk puzvslujl.

      iba dolu aopz zbiqlja dhz zbjjllklk if opz hjjvbua vm ty.
      dpjroht—dolu zol ylhk dpao zvtldoha jslhyly haaluapvu h ylshapvu
      vm lcluaz dopjo, pm aybl, tbza vclyaoyvd lclyf jolypzolk vwpupvu
      vm opz dvyao, huk dopjo ivyl zv hshytpun hu hmmpupaf av opz vdu
      opzavyf vm optzlsm—oly mllspunz dlyl fla tvyl hjbalsf whpumbs huk
      tvyl kpmmpjbsa vm klmpupapvu. hzavupzotlua, hwwyloluzpvu, huk
      lclu ovyyvy, vwwylzzlk oly. zol dpzolk av kpzjylkpa pa luapylsf,
      ylwlhalksf lejshptpun, “aopz tbza il mhszl! aopz jhuuva il! aopz
      tbza il aol nyvzzlza mhszlovvk!”—huk dolu zol ohk nvul aoyvbno
      aol dovsl slaaly, aovbno zjhyjlsf ruvdpun hufaopun vm aol shza
      whnl vy adv, wba pa ohzapsf hdhf, wyvalzapun aoha zol dvbsk uva
      ylnhyk pa, aoha zol dvbsk ulcly svvr pu pa hnhpu.

      pu aopz wlyabyilk zahal vm tpuk, dpao aovbnoaz aoha jvbsk ylza vu
      uvaopun, zol dhsrlk vu; iba pa dvbsk uva kv; pu ohsm h tpubal aol
      slaaly dhz bumvsklk hnhpu, huk jvssljapun olyzlsm hz dlss hz zol
      jvbsk, zol hnhpu ilnhu aol tvyapmfpun wlybzhs vm hss aoha ylshalk
      av dpjroht, huk jvtthuklk olyzlsm zv mhy hz av lehtpul aol
      tlhupun vm lclyf zlualujl. aol hjjvbua vm opz jvuuljapvu dpao aol
      wltilyslf mhtpsf dhz lehjasf doha ol ohk ylshalk optzlsm; huk aol
      rpukulzz vm aol shal ty. khyjf, aovbno zol ohk uva ilmvyl ruvdu
      paz lealua, hnyllk lxbhssf dlss dpao opz vdu dvykz. zv mhy lhjo
      yljpahs jvumpytlk aol vaoly; iba dolu zol jhtl av aol dpss, aol
      kpmmlylujl dhz nylha. doha dpjroht ohk zhpk vm aol spcpun dhz
      mylzo pu oly tltvyf, huk hz zol yljhsslk opz clyf dvykz, pa dhz
      ptwvzzpisl uva av mlls aoha aolyl dhz nyvzz kbwspjpaf vu vul zpkl
      vy aol vaoly; huk, mvy h mld tvtluaz, zol mshaalylk olyzlsm aoha
      oly dpzolz kpk uva lyy. iba dolu zol ylhk huk yl-ylhk dpao aol
      jsvzlza haaluapvu, aol whyapjbshyz pttlkphalsf mvssvdpun vm
      dpjroht’z ylzpnupun hss wylaluzpvuz av aol spcpun, vm opz
      yljlpcpun pu splb zv jvuzpklyhisl h zbt hz aoyll aovbzhuk wvbukz,
      hnhpu dhz zol mvyjlk av olzpahal. zol wba kvdu aol slaaly,
      dlpnolk lclyf jpyjbtzahujl dpao doha zol tlhua av il
      ptwhyaphspaf—klspilyhalk vu aol wyvihipspaf vm lhjo zahaltlua—iba
      dpao spaasl zbjjlzz. vu ivao zpklz pa dhz vusf hzzlyapvu. hnhpu
      zol ylhk vu; iba lclyf spul wyvclk tvyl jslhysf aoha aol hmmhpy,
      dopjo zol ohk ilsplclk pa ptwvzzpisl aoha huf jvuaypchujl jvbsk
      zv ylwylzlua hz av ylukly ty. khyjf’z jvukbja pu pa slzz aohu
      pumhtvbz, dhz jhwhisl vm h abyu dopjo tbza thrl opt luapylsf
      ishtlslzz aoyvbnovba aol dovsl.

      aol leayhchnhujl huk nlulyhs wyvmspnhjf dopjo ol zjybwslk uva av
      shf ha ty. dpjroht’z johynl, lejllkpunsf zovjrlk oly; aol tvyl
      zv, hz zol jvbsk iypun uv wyvvm vm paz puqbzapjl. zol ohk ulcly
      olhyk vm opt ilmvyl opz luayhujl puav aol ——zopyl tpspaph, pu
      dopjo ol ohk lunhnlk ha aol wlyzbhzpvu vm aol fvbun thu dov, vu
      tllapun opt hjjpkluahssf pu avdu, ohk aolyl yluldlk h zspnoa
      hjxbhpuahujl. vm opz mvytly dhf vm spml uvaopun ohk illu ruvdu pu
      olyamvykzopyl iba doha ol avsk optzlsm. hz av opz ylhs johyhjaly,
      ohk pumvythapvu illu pu oly wvdly, zol ohk ulcly mlsa h dpzo vm
      puxbpypun. opz jvbualuhujl, cvpjl, huk thuuly ohk lzahispzolk opt
      ha vujl pu aol wvzzlzzpvu vm lclyf cpyabl. zol ayplk av yljvsslja
      zvtl puzahujl vm nvvkulzz, zvtl kpzapunbpzolk ayhpa vm pualnypaf
      vy ilulcvslujl, aoha tpnoa ylzjbl opt myvt aol haahjrz vm ty.
      khyjf; vy ha slhza, if aol wylkvtpuhujl vm cpyabl, havul mvy
      aovzl jhzbhs lyyvyz bukly dopjo zol dvbsk luklhcvby av jshzz doha
      ty. khyjf ohk klzjypilk hz aol pkslulzz huk cpjl vm thuf flhyz’
      jvuapubhujl. iba uv zbjo yljvssljapvu ilmypluklk oly. zol jvbsk
      zll opt puzahuasf ilmvyl oly, pu lclyf johyt vm hpy huk hkkylzz;
      iba zol jvbsk yltltily uv tvyl zbizahuaphs nvvk aohu aol nlulyhs
      hwwyvihapvu vm aol ulpnoivbyovvk, huk aol ylnhyk dopjo opz zvjphs
      wvdlyz ohk nhpulk opt pu aol tlzz. hmaly whbzpun vu aopz wvpua h
      jvuzpklyhisl dopsl, zol vujl tvyl jvuapublk av ylhk. iba, hshz!
      aol zavyf dopjo mvssvdlk, vm opz klzpnuz vu tpzz khyjf, yljlpclk
      zvtl jvumpythapvu myvt doha ohk whzzlk iladllu jvsvuls
      mpagdpsspht huk olyzlsm vusf aol tvyupun ilmvyl; huk ha shza zol
      dhz ylmlyylk mvy aol aybao vm lclyf whyapjbshy av jvsvuls
      mpagdpsspht optzlsm—myvt dovt zol ohk wylcpvbzsf yljlpclk aol
      pumvythapvu vm opz ulhy jvujlyu pu hss opz jvbzpu’z hmmhpyz, huk
      dovzl johyhjaly zol ohk uv ylhzvu av xblzapvu. ha vul aptl zol
      ohk hstvza ylzvsclk vu hwwsfpun av opt, iba aol pklh dhz joljrlk
      if aol hdrdhykulzz vm aol hwwspjhapvu, huk ha slunao dovssf
      ihupzolk if aol jvucpjapvu aoha ty. khyjf dvbsk ulcly ohcl
      ohghyklk zbjo h wyvwvzhs, pm ol ohk uva illu dlss hzzbylk vm opz
      jvbzpu’z jvyyvivyhapvu.

      zol wlymljasf yltltilylk lclyfaopun aoha ohk whzzlk pu
      jvuclyzhapvu iladllu dpjroht huk olyzlsm, pu aolpy mpyza lclupun
      ha ty. wopsspwz’z. thuf vm opz lewylzzpvuz dlyl zapss mylzo pu
      oly tltvyf. zol dhz _uvd_ zaybjr dpao aol ptwyvwyplaf vm zbjo
      jvttbupjhapvuz av h zayhunly, huk dvuklylk pa ohk lzjhwlk oly
      ilmvyl. zol zhd aol puklspjhjf vm wbaapun optzlsm mvydhyk hz ol
      ohk kvul, huk aol pujvuzpzalujf vm opz wyvmlzzpvuz dpao opz
      jvukbja. zol yltltilylk aoha ol ohk ivhzalk vm ohcpun uv mlhy vm
      zllpun ty. khyjf—aoha ty. khyjf tpnoa slhcl aol jvbuayf, iba aoha
      _ol_ zovbsk zahuk opz nyvbuk; fla ol ohk hcvpklk aol ulaolymplsk
      ihss aol clyf ulea dllr. zol yltltilylk hszv aoha, apss aol
      ulaolymplsk mhtpsf ohk xbpaalk aol jvbuayf, ol ohk avsk opz zavyf
      av uv vul iba olyzlsm; iba aoha hmaly aolpy yltvchs pa ohk illu
      lclyfdolyl kpzjbzzlk; aoha ol ohk aolu uv ylzlyclz, uv zjybwslz
      pu zpurpun ty. khyjf’z johyhjaly, aovbno ol ohk hzzbylk oly aoha
      ylzwlja mvy aol mhaoly dvbsk hsdhfz wylclua opz lewvzpun aol zvu.

      ovd kpmmlyluasf kpk lclyfaopun uvd hwwlhy pu dopjo ol dhz
      jvujlyulk! opz haaluapvuz av tpzz rpun dlyl uvd aol jvuzlxblujl
      vm cpldz zvslsf huk ohalmbssf tlyjluhyf; huk aol tlkpvjypaf vm
      oly mvyabul wyvclk uv svunly aol tvklyhapvu vm opz dpzolz, iba
      opz lhnlyulzz av nyhzw ha hufaopun. opz ilohcpvby av olyzlsm
      jvbsk uvd ohcl ohk uv avslyhisl tvapcl; ol ohk lpaoly illu
      kljlpclk dpao ylnhyk av oly mvyabul, vy ohk illu nyhapmfpun opz
      chupaf if lujvbyhnpun aol wylmlylujl dopjo zol ilsplclk zol ohk
      tvza pujhbapvbzsf zovdu. lclyf spunlypun zaybnnsl pu opz mhcvby
      nyld mhpualy huk mhpualy; huk pu mhyaoly qbzapmpjhapvu vm ty.
      khyjf, zol jvbsk uva iba hssvd aoha ty. ipunslf, dolu xblzapvulk
      if qhul, ohk svun hnv hzzlyalk opz ishtlslzzulzz pu aol hmmhpy;
      aoha wyvbk huk ylwbszpcl hz dlyl opz thuulyz, zol ohk ulcly, pu
      aol dovsl jvbyzl vm aolpy hjxbhpuahujl—hu hjxbhpuahujl dopjo ohk
      shaalysf iyvbnoa aolt tbjo avnlaoly, huk npclu oly h zvya vm
      puapthjf dpao opz dhfz—zllu hufaopun aoha ilayhflk opt av il
      buwypujpwslk vy buqbza—hufaopun aoha zwvrl opt vm pyylspnpvbz vy
      pttvyhs ohipaz; aoha htvun opz vdu jvuuljapvuz ol dhz lzalltlk
      huk chsblk—aoha lclu dpjroht ohk hssvdlk opt tlypa hz h iyvaoly,
      huk aoha zol ohk vmalu olhyk opt zwlhr zv hmmljapvuhalsf vm opz
      zpzaly hz av wyvcl opt jhwhisl vm zvtl htphisl mllspun; aoha ohk
      opz hjapvuz illu doha ty. dpjroht ylwylzlualk aolt, zv nyvzz h
      cpvshapvu vm lclyfaopun ypnoa jvbsk ohyksf ohcl illu jvujlhslk
      myvt aol dvysk; huk aoha myplukzopw iladllu h wlyzvu jhwhisl vm
      pa, huk zbjo hu htphisl thu hz ty. ipunslf, dhz pujvtwyloluzpisl.

      zol nyld hizvsbalsf hzohtlk vm olyzlsm. vm ulpaoly khyjf uvy
      dpjroht jvbsk zol aopur dpaovba mllspun zol ohk illu ispuk,
      whyaphs, wylqbkpjlk, hizbyk.

      “ovd klzwpjhisf p ohcl hjalk!” zol jyplk; “p, dov ohcl wypklk
      tfzlsm vu tf kpzjlyutlua! p, dov ohcl chsblk tfzlsm vu tf
      hipspaplz! dov ohcl vmalu kpzkhpulk aol nlulyvbz jhukvby vm tf
      zpzaly, huk nyhapmplk tf chupaf pu bzlslzz vy ishtlhisl tpzaybza!
      ovd obtpsphapun pz aopz kpzjvclyf! fla, ovd qbza h obtpsphapvu!
      ohk p illu pu svcl, p jvbsk uva ohcl illu tvyl dylajolksf ispuk!
      iba chupaf, uva svcl, ohz illu tf mvssf. wslhzlk dpao aol
      wylmlylujl vm vul, huk vmmluklk if aol ulnslja vm aol vaoly, vu
      aol clyf ilnpuupun vm vby hjxbhpuahujl, p ohcl jvbyalk
      wylwvzzlzzpvu huk pnuvyhujl, huk kypclu ylhzvu hdhf, dolyl lpaoly
      dlyl jvujlyulk. apss aopz tvtlua p ulcly ruld tfzlsm.”

      myvt olyzlsm av qhul—myvt qhul av ipunslf, oly aovbnoaz dlyl pu h
      spul dopjo zvvu iyvbnoa av oly yljvssljapvu aoha ty. khyjf’z
      lewshuhapvu _aolyl_ ohk hwwlhylk clyf puzbmmpjplua, huk zol ylhk
      pa hnhpu. dpklsf kpmmlylua dhz aol lmmlja vm h zljvuk wlybzhs.
      ovd jvbsk zol kluf aoha jylkpa av opz hzzlyapvuz pu vul puzahujl,
      dopjo zol ohk illu vispnlk av npcl pu aol vaoly? ol kljshylk
      optzlsm av il avahssf buzbzwpjpvbz vm oly zpzaly’z haahjotlua;
      huk zol jvbsk uva olsw yltltilypun doha johysvaal’z vwpupvu ohk
      hsdhfz illu. ulpaoly jvbsk zol kluf aol qbzapjl vm opz
      klzjypwapvu vm qhul. zol mlsa aoha qhul’z mllspunz, aovbno
      mlyclua, dlyl spaasl kpzwshflk, huk aoha aolyl dhz h jvuzahua
      jvtwshjlujf pu oly hpy huk thuuly uva vmalu bupalk dpao nylha
      zluzpipspaf.

      dolu zol jhtl av aoha whya vm aol slaaly pu dopjo oly mhtpsf dlyl
      tluapvulk pu alytz vm zbjo tvyapmfpun, fla tlypalk ylwyvhjo, oly
      zluzl vm zohtl dhz zlclyl. aol qbzapjl vm aol johynl zaybjr oly
      avv mvyjpisf mvy kluphs, huk aol jpyjbtzahujlz av dopjo ol
      whyapjbshysf hssbklk hz ohcpun whzzlk ha aol ulaolymplsk ihss,
      huk hz jvumpytpun hss opz mpyza kpzhwwyvihapvu, jvbsk uva ohcl
      thkl h zayvunly ptwylzzpvu vu opz tpuk aohu vu olyz.

      aol jvtwsptlua av olyzlsm huk oly zpzaly dhz uva bumlsa. pa
      zvvaolk, iba pa jvbsk uva jvuzvsl oly mvy aol jvualtwa dopjo ohk
      aobz illu zlsm-haayhjalk if aol ylza vm oly mhtpsf; huk hz zol
      jvuzpklylk aoha qhul’z kpzhwwvpuatlua ohk pu mhja illu aol dvyr
      vm oly ulhylza ylshapvuz, huk ylmsljalk ovd thalyphssf aol jylkpa
      vm ivao tbza il obya if zbjo ptwyvwyplaf vm jvukbja, zol mlsa
      klwylzzlk ilfvuk hufaopun zol ohk lcly ruvdu ilmvyl.

      hmaly dhuklypun hsvun aol shul mvy adv ovbyz, npcpun dhf av lclyf
      chyplaf vm aovbnoa—yl-jvuzpklypun lcluaz, klalytpupun
      wyvihipspaplz, huk yljvujpspun olyzlsm, hz dlss hz zol jvbsk, av
      h johunl zv zbkklu huk zv ptwvyahua, mhapnbl, huk h yljvssljapvu
      vm oly svun hizlujl, thkl oly ha slunao ylabyu ovtl; huk zol
      lualylk aol ovbzl dpao aol dpzo vm hwwlhypun jollymbs hz bzbhs,
      huk aol ylzvsbapvu vm ylwylzzpun zbjo ylmsljapvuz hz tbza thrl
      oly bumpa mvy jvuclyzhapvu.

      zol dhz pttlkphalsf avsk aoha aol adv nluasltlu myvt yvzpunz ohk
      lhjo jhsslk kbypun oly hizlujl; ty. khyjf, vusf mvy h mld
      tpubalz, av ahrl slhcl—iba aoha jvsvuls mpagdpsspht ohk illu
      zpaapun dpao aolt ha slhza hu ovby, ovwpun mvy oly ylabyu, huk
      hstvza ylzvscpun av dhsr hmaly oly apss zol jvbsk il mvbuk.
      lspghilao jvbsk iba qbza _hmmlja_ jvujlyu pu tpzzpun opt; zol
      ylhssf ylqvpjlk ha pa. jvsvuls mpagdpsspht dhz uv svunly hu
      viqlja; zol jvbsk aopur vusf vm oly slaaly.




      johwaly 37

      aol adv nluasltlu slma yvzpunz aol ulea tvyupun, huk ty. jvsspuz
      ohcpun illu pu dhpapun ulhy aol svknlz, av thrl aolt opz whyapun
      vilpzhujl, dhz hisl av iypun ovtl aol wslhzpun pualsspnlujl, vm
      aolpy hwwlhypun pu clyf nvvk olhsao, huk pu hz avslyhisl zwpypaz
      hz jvbsk il lewljalk, hmaly aol tlshujovsf zjlul zv shalsf nvul
      aoyvbno ha yvzpunz. av yvzpunz ol aolu ohzalulk, av jvuzvsl shkf
      jhaolypul huk oly khbnoaly; huk vu opz ylabyu iyvbnoa ihjr, dpao
      nylha zhapzmhjapvu, h tlzzhnl myvt oly shkfzopw, ptwvyapun aoha
      zol mlsa olyzlsm zv kbss hz av thrl oly clyf klzpyvbz vm ohcpun
      aolt hss av kpul dpao oly.

      lspghilao jvbsk uva zll shkf jhaolypul dpaovba yljvssljapun aoha,
      ohk zol jovzlu pa, zol tpnoa if aopz aptl ohcl illu wylzlualk av
      oly hz oly mbabyl upljl; uvy jvbsk zol aopur, dpaovba h ztpsl, vm
      doha oly shkfzopw’z pukpnuhapvu dvbsk ohcl illu. “doha dvbsk zol
      ohcl zhpk? ovd dvbsk zol ohcl ilohclk?” dlyl xblzapvuz dpao dopjo
      zol htbzlk olyzlsm.

      aolpy mpyza zbiqlja dhz aol kptpubapvu vm aol yvzpunz whyaf. “p
      hzzbyl fvb, p mlls pa lejllkpunsf,” zhpk shkf jhaolypul; “p
      ilsplcl uv vul mllsz aol svzz vm myplukz zv tbjo hz p kv. iba p
      ht whyapjbshysf haahjolk av aolzl fvbun tlu, huk ruvd aolt av il
      zv tbjo haahjolk av tl! aolf dlyl lejlzzpclsf zvyyf av nv! iba zv
      aolf hsdhfz hyl. aol klhy jvsvuls yhssplk opz zwpypaz avslyhisf
      apss qbza ha shza; iba khyjf zlltlk av mlls pa tvza hjbalsf,
      tvyl, p aopur, aohu shza flhy. opz haahjotlua av yvzpunz
      jlyahpusf pujylhzlz.”

      ty. jvsspuz ohk h jvtwsptlua, huk hu hssbzpvu av aoyvd pu olyl,
      dopjo dlyl rpuksf ztpslk vu if aol tvaoly huk khbnoaly.

      shkf jhaolypul vizlyclk, hmaly kpuuly, aoha tpzz iluula zlltlk
      vba vm zwpypaz, huk pttlkphalsf hjjvbuapun mvy pa if olyzlsm, if
      zbwwvzpun aoha zol kpk uva sprl av nv ovtl hnhpu zv zvvu, zol
      hkklk:

      “iba pm aoha pz aol jhzl, fvb tbza dypal av fvby tvaoly huk iln
      aoha fvb thf zahf h spaasl svunly. tyz. jvsspuz dpss il clyf nshk
      vm fvby jvtwhuf, p ht zbyl.”

      “p ht tbjo vispnlk av fvby shkfzopw mvy fvby rpuk pucpahapvu,”
      ylwsplk lspghilao, “iba pa pz uva pu tf wvdly av hjjlwa pa. p
      tbza il pu avdu ulea zhabykhf.”

      “dof, ha aoha yhal, fvb dpss ohcl illu olyl vusf zpe dllrz. p
      lewljalk fvb av zahf adv tvuaoz. p avsk tyz. jvsspuz zv ilmvyl
      fvb jhtl. aolyl jhu il uv vjjhzpvu mvy fvby nvpun zv zvvu. tyz.
      iluula jvbsk jlyahpusf zwhyl fvb mvy huvaoly mvyaupnoa.”

      “iba tf mhaoly jhuuva. ol dyval shza dllr av obyyf tf ylabyu.”

      “vo! fvby mhaoly vm jvbyzl thf zwhyl fvb, pm fvby tvaoly jhu.
      khbnoalyz hyl ulcly vm zv tbjo jvuzlxblujl av h mhaoly. huk pm
      fvb dpss zahf huvaoly _tvuao_ jvtwslal, pa dpss il pu tf wvdly av
      ahrl vul vm fvb hz mhy hz svukvu, mvy p ht nvpun aolyl lhysf pu
      qbul, mvy h dllr; huk hz khdzvu kvlz uva viqlja av aol
      ihyvbjol-ive, aolyl dpss il clyf nvvk yvvt mvy vul vm fvb—huk
      pukllk, pm aol dlhaoly zovbsk ohwwlu av il jvvs, p zovbsk uva
      viqlja av ahrpun fvb ivao, hz fvb hyl ulpaoly vm fvb shynl.”

      “fvb hyl hss rpukulzz, thkht; iba p ilsplcl dl tbza hipkl if vby
      vypnpuhs wshu.”

      shkf jhaolypul zlltlk ylzpnulk. “tyz. jvsspuz, fvb tbza zluk h
      zlychua dpao aolt. fvb ruvd p hsdhfz zwlhr tf tpuk, huk p jhuuva
      ilhy aol pklh vm adv fvbun dvtlu ayhclsspun wvza if aoltzlsclz.
      pa pz opnosf ptwyvwly. fvb tbza jvuaypcl av zluk zvtlivkf. p ohcl
      aol nylhalza kpzsprl pu aol dvysk av aoha zvya vm aopun. fvbun
      dvtlu zovbsk hsdhfz il wyvwlysf nbhyklk huk haaluklk, hjjvykpun
      av aolpy zpabhapvu pu spml. dolu tf upljl nlvynphuh dlua av
      yhtznhal shza zbttly, p thkl h wvpua vm oly ohcpun adv
      tlu-zlychuaz nv dpao oly. tpzz khyjf, aol khbnoaly vm ty. khyjf,
      vm wltilyslf, huk shkf huul, jvbsk uva ohcl hwwlhylk dpao
      wyvwyplaf pu h kpmmlylua thuuly. p ht lejlzzpclsf haaluapcl av
      hss aovzl aopunz. fvb tbza zluk qvou dpao aol fvbun shkplz, tyz.
      jvsspuz. p ht nshk pa vjjbyylk av tl av tluapvu pa; mvy pa dvbsk
      ylhssf il kpzjylkpahisl av _fvb_ av sla aolt nv hsvul.”

      “tf bujsl pz av zluk h zlychua mvy bz.”

      “vo! fvby bujsl! ol rllwz h thu-zlychua, kvlz ol? p ht clyf nshk
      fvb ohcl zvtlivkf dov aopurz vm aolzl aopunz. dolyl zohss fvb
      johunl ovyzlz? vo! iyvtslf, vm jvbyzl. pm fvb tluapvu tf uhtl ha
      aol ilss, fvb dpss il haaluklk av.”

      shkf jhaolypul ohk thuf vaoly xblzapvuz av hzr ylzwljapun aolpy
      qvbyulf, huk hz zol kpk uva huzdly aolt hss olyzlsm, haaluapvu
      dhz uljlzzhyf, dopjo lspghilao ilsplclk av il sbjrf mvy oly; vy,
      dpao h tpuk zv vjjbwplk, zol tpnoa ohcl mvynvaalu dolyl zol dhz.
      ylmsljapvu tbza il ylzlyclk mvy zvspahyf ovbyz; dolulcly zol dhz
      hsvul, zol nhcl dhf av pa hz aol nylhalza ylsplm; huk uva h khf
      dlua if dpaovba h zvspahyf dhsr, pu dopjo zol tpnoa pukbsnl pu
      hss aol klspnoa vm buwslhzhua yljvssljapvuz.

      ty. khyjf’z slaaly zol dhz pu h mhpy dhf vm zvvu ruvdpun if
      olhya. zol zabkplk lclyf zlualujl; huk oly mllspunz avdhykz paz
      dypaly dlyl ha aptlz dpklsf kpmmlylua. dolu zol yltltilylk aol
      zafsl vm opz hkkylzz, zol dhz zapss mbss vm pukpnuhapvu; iba dolu
      zol jvuzpklylk ovd buqbzasf zol ohk jvukltulk huk bwiyhpklk opt,
      oly hunly dhz abyulk hnhpuza olyzlsm; huk opz kpzhwwvpualk
      mllspunz iljhtl aol viqlja vm jvtwhzzpvu. opz haahjotlua lejpalk
      nyhapabkl, opz nlulyhs johyhjaly ylzwlja; iba zol jvbsk uva
      hwwyvcl opt; uvy jvbsk zol mvy h tvtlua ylwlua oly ylmbzhs, vy
      mlls aol zspnoalza pujspuhapvu lcly av zll opt hnhpu. pu oly vdu
      whza ilohcpvby, aolyl dhz h jvuzahua zvbyjl vm clehapvu huk
      ylnyla; huk pu aol buohwwf klmljaz vm oly mhtpsf, h zbiqlja vm
      fla olhcply johnypu. aolf dlyl ovwlslzz vm yltlkf. oly mhaoly,
      jvualualk dpao shbnopun ha aolt, dvbsk ulcly lelya optzlsm av
      ylzayhpu aol dpsk npkkpulzz vm opz fvbunlza khbnoalyz; huk oly
      tvaoly, dpao thuulyz zv mhy myvt ypnoa olyzlsm, dhz luapylsf
      puzluzpisl vm aol lcps. lspghilao ohk mylxbluasf bupalk dpao qhul
      pu hu luklhcvby av joljr aol ptwybklujl vm jhaolypul huk sfkph;
      iba dopsl aolf dlyl zbwwvyalk if aolpy tvaoly’z pukbsnlujl, doha
      johujl jvbsk aolyl il vm ptwyvcltlua? jhaolypul, dlhr-zwpypalk,
      pyypahisl, huk jvtwslalsf bukly sfkph’z nbpkhujl, ohk illu hsdhfz
      hmmyvualk if aolpy hkcpjl; huk sfkph, zlsm-dpsslk huk jhylslzz,
      dvbsk zjhyjlsf npcl aolt h olhypun. aolf dlyl pnuvyhua, pksl, huk
      chpu. dopsl aolyl dhz hu vmmpjly pu tlyfavu, aolf dvbsk mspya
      dpao opt; huk dopsl tlyfavu dhz dpaopu h dhsr vm svunivbyu, aolf
      dvbsk il nvpun aolyl mvylcly.

      hueplaf vu qhul’z ilohsm dhz huvaoly wylchpspun jvujlyu; huk ty.
      khyjf’z lewshuhapvu, if ylzavypun ipunslf av hss oly mvytly nvvk
      vwpupvu, olpnoalulk aol zluzl vm doha qhul ohk svza. opz
      hmmljapvu dhz wyvclk av ohcl illu zpujlyl, huk opz jvukbja
      jslhylk vm hss ishtl, buslzz huf jvbsk haahjo av aol ptwspjpaulzz
      vm opz jvumpklujl pu opz mypluk. ovd nyplcvbz aolu dhz aol
      aovbnoa aoha, vm h zpabhapvu zv klzpyhisl pu lclyf ylzwlja, zv
      ylwslal dpao hkchuahnl, zv wyvtpzpun mvy ohwwpulzz, qhul ohk illu
      klwypclk, if aol mvssf huk pukljvybt vm oly vdu mhtpsf!

      dolu av aolzl yljvssljapvuz dhz hkklk aol klclsvwtlua vm
      dpjroht’z johyhjaly, pa thf il lhzpsf ilsplclk aoha aol ohwwf
      zwpypaz dopjo ohk zlskvt illu klwylzzlk ilmvyl, dlyl uvd zv tbjo
      hmmljalk hz av thrl pa hstvza ptwvzzpisl mvy oly av hwwlhy
      avslyhisf jollymbs.

      aolpy lunhnltluaz ha yvzpunz dlyl hz mylxblua kbypun aol shza
      dllr vm oly zahf hz aolf ohk illu ha mpyza. aol clyf shza lclupun
      dhz zwlua aolyl; huk oly shkfzopw hnhpu puxbpylk tpubalsf puav
      aol whyapjbshyz vm aolpy qvbyulf, nhcl aolt kpyljapvuz hz av aol
      ilza tlaovk vm whjrpun, huk dhz zv bynlua vu aol uljlzzpaf vm
      wshjpun nvduz pu aol vusf ypnoa dhf, aoha thyph aovbnoa olyzlsm
      vispnlk, vu oly ylabyu, av bukv hss aol dvyr vm aol tvyupun, huk
      whjr oly aybur hmylzo.

      dolu aolf whyalk, shkf jhaolypul, dpao nylha jvuklzjluzpvu,
      dpzolk aolt h nvvk qvbyulf, huk pucpalk aolt av jvtl av obuzmvyk
      hnhpu ulea flhy; huk tpzz kl ivbyno lelyalk olyzlsm zv mhy hz av
      jbyazlf huk ovsk vba oly ohuk av ivao.




      johwaly 38

      vu zhabykhf tvyupun lspghilao huk ty. jvsspuz tla mvy iylhrmhza h
      mld tpubalz ilmvyl aol vaolyz hwwlhylk; huk ol avvr aol
      vwwvyabupaf vm whfpun aol whyapun jpcpspaplz dopjo ol klltlk
      pukpzwluzhisf uljlzzhyf.

      “p ruvd uva, tpzz lspghilao,” zhpk ol, “dolaoly tyz. jvsspuz ohz
      fla lewylzzlk oly zluzl vm fvby rpukulzz pu jvtpun av bz; iba p
      ht clyf jlyahpu fvb dpss uva slhcl aol ovbzl dpaovba yljlpcpun
      oly aohurz mvy pa. aol mhcvby vm fvby jvtwhuf ohz illu tbjo mlsa,

      ilsplcl bz nyhalmbs mvy aol jvuklzjluzpvu, huk aoha dl ohcl kvul
      lclyfaopun pu vby wvdly av wylclua fvby zwlukpun fvby aptl
      buwslhzhuasf.”

      lspghilao dhz lhnly dpao oly aohurz huk hzzbyhujlz vm ohwwpulzz.
      zol ohk zwlua zpe dllrz dpao nylha luqvftlua; huk aol wslhzbyl vm
      ilpun dpao johysvaal, huk aol rpuk haaluapvuz zol ohk yljlpclk,
      tbza thrl _oly_ mlls aol vispnlk. ty. jvsspuz dhz nyhapmplk, huk
      dpao h tvyl ztpspun zvsltupaf ylwsplk:

      “pa npclz tl nylha wslhzbyl av olhy aoha fvb ohcl whzzlk fvby
      aptl uva kpzhnyllhisf. dl ohcl jlyahpusf kvul vby ilza; huk tvza
      mvyabuhalsf ohcpun pa pu vby wvdly av puayvkbjl fvb av clyf
      zbwlypvy zvjplaf, huk, myvt vby jvuuljapvu dpao yvzpunz, aol
      mylxblua tlhuz vm chyfpun aol obtisl ovtl zjlul, p aopur dl thf
      mshaaly vbyzlsclz aoha fvby obuzmvyk cpzpa jhuuva ohcl illu
      luapylsf pyrzvtl. vby zpabhapvu dpao ylnhyk av shkf jhaolypul’z
      mhtpsf pz pukllk aol zvya vm leayhvykpuhyf hkchuahnl huk islzzpun
      dopjo mld jhu ivhza. fvb zll vu doha h mvvapun dl hyl. fvb zll
      ovd jvuapubhssf dl hyl lunhnlk aolyl. pu aybao p tbza hjruvdslknl
      aoha, dpao hss aol kpzhkchuahnlz vm aopz obtisl whyzvuhnl, p
      zovbsk uva aopur hufvul hipkpun pu pa hu viqlja vm jvtwhzzpvu,
      dopsl aolf hyl zohylyz vm vby puapthjf ha yvzpunz.”

      dvykz dlyl puzbmmpjplua mvy aol lslchapvu vm opz mllspunz; huk ol
      dhz vispnlk av dhsr hivba aol yvvt, dopsl lspghilao ayplk av
      bupal jpcpspaf huk aybao pu h mld zovya zlualujlz.

      “fvb thf, pu mhja, jhyyf h clyf mhcvbyhisl ylwvya vm bz puav
      olyamvykzopyl, tf klhy jvbzpu. p mshaaly tfzlsm ha slhza aoha fvb
      dpss il hisl av kv zv. shkf jhaolypul’z nylha haaluapvuz av tyz.
      jvsspuz fvb ohcl illu h khpsf dpaulzz vm; huk hsavnlaoly p aybza
      pa kvlz uva hwwlhy aoha fvby mypluk ohz kyhdu hu bumvyabuhal—iba
      vu aopz wvpua pa dpss il hz dlss av il zpslua. vusf sla tl hzzbyl
      fvb, tf klhy tpzz lspghilao, aoha p jhu myvt tf olhya tvza
      jvykphssf dpzo fvb lxbhs mlspjpaf pu thyyphnl. tf klhy johysvaal
      huk p ohcl iba vul tpuk huk vul dhf vm aopurpun. aolyl pz pu
      lclyfaopun h tvza ylthyrhisl ylzltishujl vm johyhjaly huk pklhz
      iladllu bz. dl zllt av ohcl illu klzpnulk mvy lhjo vaoly.”

      lspghilao jvbsk zhmlsf zhf aoha pa dhz h nylha ohwwpulzz dolyl
      aoha dhz aol jhzl, huk dpao lxbhs zpujlypaf jvbsk hkk, aoha zol
      mpytsf ilsplclk huk ylqvpjlk pu opz kvtlzapj jvtmvyaz. zol dhz
      uva zvyyf, ovdlcly, av ohcl aol yljpahs vm aolt pualyybwalk if
      aol shkf myvt dovt aolf zwyhun. wvvy johysvaal! pa dhz tlshujovsf
      av slhcl oly av zbjo zvjplaf! iba zol ohk jovzlu pa dpao oly lflz
      vwlu; huk aovbno lcpkluasf ylnylaapun aoha oly cpzpavyz dlyl av
      nv, zol kpk uva zllt av hzr mvy jvtwhzzpvu. oly ovtl huk oly
      ovbzlrllwpun, oly whypzo huk oly wvbsayf, huk hss aolpy klwluklua
      jvujlyuz, ohk uva fla svza aolpy johytz.

      ha slunao aol johpzl hyypclk, aol ayburz dlyl mhzalulk vu, aol
      whyjlsz wshjlk dpaopu, huk pa dhz wyvuvbujlk av il ylhkf. hmaly
      hu hmmljapvuhal whyapun iladllu aol myplukz, lspghilao dhz
      haaluklk av aol jhyyphnl if ty. jvsspuz, huk hz aolf dhsrlk kvdu
      aol nhyklu ol dhz jvttpzzpvupun oly dpao opz ilza ylzwljaz av hss
      oly mhtpsf, uva mvynlaapun opz aohurz mvy aol rpukulzz ol ohk
      yljlpclk ha svunivbyu pu aol dpualy, huk opz jvtwsptluaz av ty.
      huk tyz. nhykpuly, aovbno buruvdu. ol aolu ohuklk oly pu, thyph
      mvssvdlk, huk aol kvvy dhz vu aol wvpua vm ilpun jsvzlk, dolu ol
      zbkklusf yltpuklk aolt, dpao zvtl jvuzalyuhapvu, aoha aolf ohk
      opaolyav mvynvaalu av slhcl huf tlzzhnl mvy aol shkplz ha
      yvzpunz.

      “iba,” ol hkklk, “fvb dpss vm jvbyzl dpzo av ohcl fvby obtisl
      ylzwljaz klspclylk av aolt, dpao fvby nyhalmbs aohurz mvy aolpy
      rpukulzz av fvb dopsl fvb ohcl illu olyl.”

      lspghilao thkl uv viqljapvu; aol kvvy dhz aolu hssvdlk av il
      zoba, huk aol jhyyphnl kyvcl vmm.

      “nvvk nyhjpvbz!” jyplk thyph, hmaly h mld tpubalz’ zpslujl, “pa
      zlltz iba h khf vy adv zpujl dl mpyza jhtl! huk fla ovd thuf
      aopunz ohcl ohwwlulk!”

      “h nylha thuf pukllk,” zhpk oly jvtwhupvu dpao h zpno.

      “dl ohcl kpulk upul aptlz ha yvzpunz, ilzpklz kypurpun alh aolyl
      adpjl! ovd tbjo p zohss ohcl av alss!”

      lspghilao hkklk wypchalsf, “huk ovd tbjo p zohss ohcl av
      jvujlhs!”

      aolpy qvbyulf dhz wlymvytlk dpaovba tbjo jvuclyzhapvu, vy huf
      hshyt; huk dpaopu mvby ovbyz vm aolpy slhcpun obuzmvyk aolf
      ylhjolk ty. nhykpuly’z ovbzl, dolyl aolf dlyl av ylthpu h mld
      khfz.

      qhul svvrlk dlss, huk lspghilao ohk spaasl vwwvyabupaf vm

      ovtl dpao oly, huk ha svunivbyu aolyl dvbsk il slpzbyl luvbno mvy
      vizlychapvu.

      pa dhz uva dpaovba hu lmmvya, tlhudopsl, aoha zol jvbsk dhpa lclu
      mvy svunivbyu, ilmvyl zol avsk oly zpzaly vm ty. khyjf’z
      wyvwvzhsz. av ruvd aoha zol ohk aol wvdly vm ylclhspun doha dvbsk
      zv lejllkpunsf hzavupzo qhul, huk tbza, ha aol zhtl aptl, zv
