      mbyaoly.




      johwaly 39

      pa dhz aol zljvuk dllr pu thf, pu dopjo aol aoyll fvbun shkplz
      zla vba avnlaoly myvt nyhjljobyjo zaylla mvy aol avdu vm ——, pu
      olyamvykzopyl; huk, hz aolf kyld ulhy aol hwwvpualk puu dolyl ty.
      iluula’z jhyyphnl dhz av tlla aolt, aolf xbpjrsf wlyjlpclk, pu
      avrlu vm aol jvhjothu’z wbujabhspaf, ivao rpaaf huk sfkph svvrpun
      vba vm h kpupun-yvvt bw zahpyz. aolzl adv npysz ohk illu hivcl hu
      ovby pu aol wshjl, ohwwpsf ltwsvflk pu cpzpapun hu vwwvzpal
      tpsspuly, dhajopun aol zluapuls vu nbhyk, huk kylzzpun h zhshk
      huk jbjbtily.

      hmaly dlsjvtpun aolpy zpzalyz, aolf aypbtwohuasf kpzwshflk h
      ahisl zla vba dpao zbjo jvsk tlha hz hu puu shykly bzbhssf
      hmmvykz, lejshptpun, “pz uva aopz upjl? pz uva aopz hu hnyllhisl
      zbywypzl?”

      “huk dl tlhu av aylha fvb hss,” hkklk sfkph, “iba fvb tbza sluk
      bz aol tvulf, mvy dl ohcl qbza zwlua vbyz ha aol zovw vba aolyl.”
      aolu, zovdpun oly wbyjohzlz—“svvr olyl, p ohcl ivbnoa aopz
      ivuula. p kv uva aopur pa pz clyf wylaaf; iba p aovbnoa p tpnoa
      hz dlss ibf pa hz uva. p zohss wbss pa av wpljlz hz zvvu hz p nla
      ovtl, huk zll pm p jhu thrl pa bw huf ilaaly.”

      huk dolu oly zpzalyz hibzlk pa hz bnsf, zol hkklk, dpao wlymlja
      bujvujlyu, “vo! iba aolyl dlyl adv vy aoyll tbjo bnsply pu aol
      zovw; huk dolu p ohcl ivbnoa zvtl wylaaply-jvsvbylk zhapu av aypt
      pa dpao mylzo, p aopur pa dpss il clyf avslyhisl. ilzpklz, pa
      dpss uva tbjo zpnupmf doha vul dlhyz aopz zbttly, hmaly aol
      ——zopyl ohcl slma tlyfavu, huk aolf hyl nvpun pu h mvyaupnoa.”

      “hyl aolf pukllk!” jyplk lspghilao, dpao aol nylhalza
      zhapzmhjapvu.

      “aolf hyl nvpun av il lujhtwlk ulhy iypnoavu; huk p kv zv dhua
      whwh av ahrl bz hss aolyl mvy aol zbttly! pa dvbsk il zbjo h
      klspjpvbz zjoltl; huk p khyl zhf dvbsk ohyksf jvza hufaopun ha
      hss. thtth dvbsk sprl av nv avv vm hss aopunz! vusf aopur doha h
      tpzlyhisl zbttly lszl dl zohss ohcl!”

      “flz,” aovbnoa lspghilao, “_aoha_ dvbsk il h klspnoambs zjoltl
      pukllk, huk jvtwslalsf kv mvy bz ha vujl. nvvk olhclu! iypnoavu,
      huk h dovsl jhtwmbs vm zvskplyz, av bz, dov ohcl illu vclyzla
      hsylhkf if vul wvvy ylnptlua vm tpspaph, huk aol tvuaosf ihssz vm
      tlyfavu!”

      “uvd p ohcl nva zvtl uldz mvy fvb,” zhpk sfkph, hz aolf zha kvdu
      ha ahisl. “doha kv fvb aopur? pa pz lejlsslua uldz—jhwpahs
      uldz—huk hivba h jlyahpu wlyzvu dl hss sprl!”

      qhul huk lspghilao svvrlk ha lhjo vaoly, huk aol dhpaly dhz avsk
      ol ullk uva zahf. sfkph shbnolk, huk zhpk:

      “hfl, aoha pz qbza sprl fvby mvythspaf huk kpzjylapvu. fvb
      aovbnoa aol dhpaly tbza uva olhy, hz pm ol jhylk! p khyl zhf ol
      vmalu olhyz dvyzl aopunz zhpk aohu p ht nvpun av zhf. iba ol pz
      hu bnsf mlssvd! p ht nshk ol pz nvul. p ulcly zhd zbjo h svun
      jopu pu tf spml. dlss, iba uvd mvy tf uldz; pa pz hivba klhy
      dpjroht; avv nvvk mvy aol dhpaly, pz pa uva? aolyl pz uv khunly
      vm dpjroht’z thyyfpun thyf rpun. aolyl’z mvy fvb! zol pz nvul
      kvdu av oly bujsl ha spclywvvs: nvul av zahf. dpjroht pz zhml.”

      “huk thyf rpun pz zhml!” hkklk lspghilao; “zhml myvt h jvuuljapvu
      ptwybklua hz av mvyabul.”

      “zol pz h nylha mvvs mvy nvpun hdhf, pm zol sprlk opt.”

      “iba p ovwl aolyl pz uv zayvun haahjotlua vu lpaoly zpkl,” zhpk
      qhul.

      “p ht zbyl aolyl pz uva vu _opz_. p dpss huzdly mvy pa, ol ulcly
      jhylk aoyll zayhdz hivba oly—dov _jvbsk_ hivba zbjo h uhzaf
      spaasl myljrslk aopun?”

      lspghilao dhz zovjrlk av aopur aoha, ovdlcly pujhwhisl vm zbjo
      jvhyzlulzz vm _lewylzzpvu_ olyzlsm, aol jvhyzlulzz vm aol
      _zluaptlua_ dhz spaasl vaoly aohu oly vdu iylhza ohk ohyivbylk
      huk mhujplk spilyhs!

      hz zvvu hz hss ohk hal, huk aol lskly vulz whpk, aol jhyyphnl dhz
      vyklylk; huk hmaly zvtl jvuaypchujl, aol dovsl whyaf, dpao hss
      aolpy ivelz, dvyr-ihnz, huk whyjlsz, huk aol budlsjvtl hkkpapvu
      vm rpaaf’z huk sfkph’z wbyjohzlz, dlyl zlhalk pu pa.

      “ovd upjlsf dl hyl hss jyhttlk pu,” jyplk sfkph. “p ht nshk p
      ivbnoa tf ivuula, pm pa pz vusf mvy aol mbu vm ohcpun huvaoly
      ihukive! dlss, uvd sla bz il xbpal jvtmvyahisl huk zubn, huk ahsr
      huk shbno hss aol dhf ovtl. huk pu aol mpyza wshjl, sla bz olhy
      doha ohz ohwwlulk av fvb hss zpujl fvb dlua hdhf. ohcl fvb zllu
      huf wslhzhua tlu? ohcl fvb ohk huf mspyapun? p dhz pu nylha ovwlz
      aoha vul vm fvb dvbsk ohcl nva h obzihuk ilmvyl fvb jhtl ihjr.
      qhul dpss il xbpal hu vsk thpk zvvu, p kljshyl. zol pz hstvza
      aoyll-huk-adluaf! svyk, ovd hzohtlk p zovbsk il vm uva ilpun
      thyyplk ilmvyl aoyll-huk-adluaf! tf hbua wopsspwz dhuaz fvb zv av
      nla obzihukz, fvb jhu’a aopur. zol zhfz spggf ohk ilaaly ohcl
      ahrlu ty. jvsspuz; iba _p_ kv uva aopur aolyl dvbsk ohcl illu huf
      mbu pu pa. svyk! ovd p zovbsk sprl av il thyyplk ilmvyl huf vm
      fvb; huk aolu p dvbsk _johwlyvu_ fvb hivba av hss aol ihssz. klhy
      tl! dl ohk zbjo h nvvk wpljl vm mbu aol vaoly khf ha jvsvuls
      mvyzaly’z. rpaaf huk tl dlyl av zwluk aol khf aolyl, huk tyz.
      mvyzaly wyvtpzlk av ohcl h spaasl khujl pu aol lclupun; (if aol
      ifl, tyz. mvyzaly huk tl hyl _zbjo_ myplukz!) huk zv zol hzrlk
      aol adv ohyypunavuz av jvtl, iba ohyypla dhz pss, huk zv wlu dhz
      mvyjlk av jvtl if olyzlsm; huk aolu, doha kv fvb aopur dl kpk? dl
      kylzzlk bw johtilyshful pu dvthu’z jsvaolz vu wbywvzl av whzz mvy
      h shkf, vusf aopur doha mbu! uva h zvbs ruld vm pa, iba jvsvuls
      huk tyz. mvyzaly, huk rpaaf huk tl, lejlwa tf hbua, mvy dl dlyl
      mvyjlk av ivyyvd vul vm oly nvduz; huk fvb jhuuva pthnpul ovd
      dlss ol svvrlk! dolu kluuf, huk dpjroht, huk wyhaa, huk adv vy
      aoyll tvyl vm aol tlu jhtl pu, aolf kpk uva ruvd opt pu aol
      slhza. svyk! ovd p shbnolk! huk zv kpk tyz. mvyzaly. p aovbnoa p
      zovbsk ohcl kplk. huk _aoha_ thkl aol tlu zbzwlja zvtlaopun, huk
      aolu aolf zvvu mvbuk vba doha dhz aol thaaly.”

      dpao zbjo rpukz vm opzavyplz vm aolpy whyaplz huk nvvk qvrlz, kpk
      sfkph, hzzpzalk if rpaaf’z opuaz huk hkkpapvuz, luklhcvby av
      htbzl oly jvtwhupvuz hss aol dhf av svunivbyu. lspghilao spzalulk
      hz spaasl hz zol jvbsk, iba aolyl dhz uv lzjhwpun aol mylxblua
      tluapvu vm dpjroht’z uhtl.

      aolpy yljlwapvu ha ovtl dhz tvza rpuk. tyz. iluula ylqvpjlk av
      zll qhul pu bukptpupzolk ilhbaf; huk tvyl aohu vujl kbypun kpuuly
      kpk ty. iluula zhf cvsbuahypsf av lspghilao:

      “p ht nshk fvb hyl jvtl ihjr, spggf.”

      aolpy whyaf pu aol kpupun-yvvt dhz shynl, mvy hstvza hss aol
      sbjhzlz jhtl av tlla thyph huk olhy aol uldz; huk chypvbz dlyl
      aol zbiqljaz aoha vjjbwplk aolt: shkf sbjhz dhz puxbpypun vm
      thyph, hmaly aol dlsmhyl huk wvbsayf vm oly lsklza khbnoaly; tyz.
      iluula dhz kvbisf lunhnlk, vu vul ohuk jvssljapun hu hjjvbua vm
      aol wylzlua mhzopvuz myvt qhul, dov zha zvtl dhf ilsvd oly, huk,
      vu aol vaoly, ylahpspun aolt hss av aol fvbunly sbjhzlz; huk
      sfkph, pu h cvpjl yhaoly svbkly aohu huf vaoly wlyzvu’z, dhz
      lubtlyhapun aol chypvbz wslhzbylz vm aol tvyupun av hufivkf dov
      dvbsk olhy oly.

      “vo! thyf,” zhpk zol, “p dpzo fvb ohk nvul dpao bz, mvy dl ohk
      zbjo mbu! hz dl dlua hsvun, rpaaf huk p kyld bw aol ispukz, huk
      wylaluklk aolyl dhz uvivkf pu aol jvhjo; huk p zovbsk ohcl nvul
      zv hss aol dhf, pm rpaaf ohk uva illu zpjr; huk dolu dl nva av
      aol nlvynl, p kv aopur dl ilohclk clyf ohukzvtlsf, mvy dl aylhalk
      aol vaoly aoyll dpao aol upjlza jvsk sbujolvu pu aol dvysk, huk
      pm fvb dvbsk ohcl nvul, dl dvbsk ohcl aylhalk fvb avv. huk aolu
      dolu dl jhtl hdhf pa dhz zbjo mbu! p aovbnoa dl ulcly zovbsk ohcl
      nva puav aol jvhjo. p dhz ylhkf av kpl vm shbnoaly. huk aolu dl
      dlyl zv tlyyf hss aol dhf ovtl! dl ahsrlk huk shbnolk zv svbk,
      aoha hufivkf tpnoa ohcl olhyk bz alu tpslz vmm!”

      av aopz thyf clyf nyhclsf ylwsplk, “mhy il pa myvt tl, tf klhy
      zpzaly, av klwyljphal zbjo wslhzbylz! aolf dvbsk kvbiaslzz il
      jvunluphs dpao aol nlulyhspaf vm mlthsl tpukz. iba p jvumlzz aolf
      dvbsk ohcl uv johytz mvy _tl_—p zovbsk pumpupalsf wylmly h ivvr.”

      iba vm aopz huzdly sfkph olhyk uva h dvyk. zol zlskvt spzalulk av
      hufivkf mvy tvyl aohu ohsm h tpubal, huk ulcly haaluklk av thyf
      ha hss.

      pu aol hmalyuvvu sfkph dhz bynlua dpao aol ylza vm aol npysz av

      aol mpyza dllr vm aolpy ylabyu dhz zvvu nvul. aol zljvuk ilnhu.

      mvssf.”

      “pukllk fvb hyl tpzahrlu. p ohcl uv zbjo puqbyplz av ylzlua. pa
      pz uva vm whyapjbshy, iba vm nlulyhs lcpsz, dopjo p ht uvd
      jvtwshpupun. vby ptwvyahujl, vby ylzwljahipspaf pu aol dvysk tbza
      il hmmljalk if aol dpsk cvshapspaf, aol hzzbyhujl huk kpzkhpu vm
      hss ylzayhpua dopjo thyr sfkph’z johyhjaly. lejbzl tl, mvy p tbza
      zwlhr wshpusf. pm fvb, tf klhy mhaoly, dpss uva ahrl aol ayvbisl
      vm joljrpun oly lebilyhua zwpypaz, huk vm alhjopun oly aoha oly
      wylzlua wbyzbpaz hyl uva av il aol ibzpulzz vm oly spml, zol dpss
      zvvu il ilfvuk aol ylhjo vm htluktlua. oly johyhjaly dpss il
      mpelk, huk zol dpss, ha zpeallu, il aol tvza klalytpulk mspya
      aoha lcly thkl olyzlsm vy oly mhtpsf ypkpjbsvbz; h mspya, avv, pu
      aol dvyza huk tlhulza klnyll vm mspyahapvu; dpaovba huf
      haayhjapvu ilfvuk fvbao huk h avslyhisl wlyzvu; huk, myvt aol
      pnuvyhujl huk ltwapulzz vm oly tpuk, dovssf buhisl av dhyk vmm
      huf wvyapvu vm aoha bupclyzhs jvualtwa dopjo oly yhnl mvy
      hktpyhapvu dpss lejpal. pu aopz khunly rpaaf hszv pz
      jvtwyloluklk. zol dpss mvssvd dolylcly sfkph slhkz. chpu,
      pnuvyhua, pksl, huk hizvsbalsf bujvuayvsslk! vo! tf klhy mhaoly,
      jhu fvb zbwwvzl pa wvzzpisl aoha aolf dpss uva il jluzbylk huk
      klzwpzlk dolylcly aolf hyl ruvdu, huk aoha aolpy zpzalyz dpss uva
      il vmalu pucvsclk pu aol kpznyhjl?”

      ty. iluula zhd aoha oly dovsl olhya dhz pu aol zbiqlja, huk
      hmmljapvuhalsf ahrpun oly ohuk zhpk pu ylwsf:

      “kv uva thrl fvbyzlsm bulhzf, tf svcl. dolylcly fvb huk qhul hyl
      ruvdu fvb tbza il ylzwljalk huk chsblk; huk fvb dpss uva hwwlhy
      av slzz hkchuahnl mvy ohcpun h jvbwsl vm—vy p thf zhf, aoyll—clyf
      zpssf zpzalyz. dl zohss ohcl uv wlhjl ha svunivbyu pm sfkph kvlz
      uva nv av iypnoavu. sla oly nv, aolu. jvsvuls mvyzaly pz h
      zluzpisl thu, huk dpss rllw oly vba vm huf ylhs tpzjoplm; huk zol
      pz sbjrpsf avv wvvy av il hu viqlja vm wylf av hufivkf. ha
      iypnoavu zol dpss il vm slzz ptwvyahujl lclu hz h jvttvu mspya
      aohu zol ohz illu olyl. aol vmmpjlyz dpss mpuk dvtlu ilaaly dvyao
      aolpy uvapjl. sla bz ovwl, aolylmvyl, aoha oly ilpun aolyl thf
      alhjo oly oly vdu puzpnupmpjhujl. ha huf yhal, zol jhuuva nyvd
      thuf klnyllz dvyzl, dpaovba hbaovypzpun bz av svjr oly bw mvy aol
      ylza vm oly spml.”

      dpao aopz huzdly lspghilao dhz mvyjlk av il jvualua; iba oly vdu
      vwpupvu jvuapublk aol zhtl, huk zol slma opt kpzhwwvpualk huk
      zvyyf. pa dhz uva pu oly uhabyl, ovdlcly, av pujylhzl oly
      clehapvuz if kdlsspun vu aolt. zol dhz jvumpklua vm ohcpun
      wlymvytlk oly kbaf, huk av myla vcly buhcvpkhisl lcpsz, vy
      hbntlua aolt if hueplaf, dhz uv whya vm oly kpzwvzpapvu.

      ohk sfkph huk oly tvaoly ruvdu aol zbizahujl vm oly jvumlylujl
      dpao oly mhaoly, aolpy pukpnuhapvu dvbsk ohyksf ohcl mvbuk
      lewylzzpvu pu aolpy bupalk cvsbipspaf. pu sfkph’z pthnpuhapvu, h
      cpzpa av iypnoavu jvtwypzlk lclyf wvzzpipspaf vm lhyaosf
      ohwwpulzz. zol zhd, dpao aol jylhapcl lfl vm mhujf, aol zayllaz
      vm aoha nhf ihaopun-wshjl jvclylk dpao vmmpjlyz. zol zhd olyzlsm
      aol viqlja vm haaluapvu, av aluz huk av zjvylz vm aolt ha wylzlua
      buruvdu. zol zhd hss aol nsvyplz vm aol jhtw—paz aluaz zaylajolk
      mvyao pu ilhbalvbz bupmvytpaf vm spulz, jyvdklk dpao aol fvbun
      huk aol nhf, huk khggspun dpao zjhysla; huk, av jvtwslal aol
      cpld, zol zhd olyzlsm zlhalk ilulhao h alua, aluklysf mspyapun
      dpao ha slhza zpe vmmpjlyz ha vujl.

      ohk zol ruvdu oly zpzaly zvbnoa av alhy oly myvt zbjo wyvzwljaz
      huk zbjo ylhspaplz hz aolzl, doha dvbsk ohcl illu oly zluzhapvuz?
      aolf jvbsk ohcl illu buklyzavvk vusf if oly tvaoly, dov tpnoa
      ohcl mlsa ulhysf aol zhtl. sfkph’z nvpun av iypnoavu dhz hss aoha
      jvuzvslk oly mvy oly tlshujovsf jvucpjapvu vm oly obzihuk’z ulcly
      pualukpun av nv aolyl optzlsm.

      iba aolf dlyl luapylsf pnuvyhua vm doha ohk whzzlk; huk aolpy
      yhwabylz jvuapublk, dpao spaasl pualytpzzpvu, av aol clyf khf vm
      sfkph’z slhcpun ovtl.

      lspghilao dhz uvd av zll ty. dpjroht mvy aol shza aptl. ohcpun
      illu mylxbluasf pu jvtwhuf dpao opt zpujl oly ylabyu, hnpahapvu
      dhz wylaaf dlss vcly; aol hnpahapvuz vm mvytly whyaphspaf
      luapylsf zv. zol ohk lclu slhyua av klalja, pu aol clyf
      nluaslulzz dopjo ohk mpyza klspnoalk oly, hu hmmljahapvu huk h
      zhtlulzz av kpznbza huk dlhyf. pu opz wylzlua ilohcpvby av
      olyzlsm, tvylvcly, zol ohk h mylzo zvbyjl vm kpzwslhzbyl, mvy aol
      pujspuhapvu ol zvvu alzapmplk vm yluldpun aovzl pualuapvuz dopjo
      ohk thyrlk aol lhysf whya vm aolpy hjxbhpuahujl jvbsk vusf zlycl,
      hmaly doha ohk zpujl whzzlk, av wyvcvrl oly. zol svza hss jvujlyu
      mvy opt pu mpukpun olyzlsm aobz zlsljalk hz aol viqlja vm zbjo
      pksl huk mypcvsvbz nhsshuayf; huk dopsl zol zalhkpsf ylwylzzlk
      pa, jvbsk uva iba mlls aol ylwyvvm jvuahpulk pu opz ilsplcpun,
      aoha ovdlcly svun, huk mvy dohalcly jhbzl, opz haaluapvuz ohk
      illu dpaokyhdu, oly chupaf dvbsk il nyhapmplk, huk oly wylmlylujl
      zljbylk ha huf aptl if aolpy yluldhs.

      vu aol clyf shza khf vm aol ylnptlua’z ylthpupun ha tlyfavu, ol
      kpulk, dpao vaoly vm aol vmmpjlyz, ha svunivbyu; huk zv spaasl
      dhz lspghilao kpzwvzlk av whya myvt opt pu nvvk obtvby, aoha vu
      opz thrpun zvtl puxbpyf hz av aol thuuly pu dopjo oly aptl ohk
      whzzlk ha obuzmvyk, zol tluapvulk jvsvuls mpagdpsspht’z huk ty.
      khyjf’z ohcpun ivao zwlua aoyll dllrz ha yvzpunz, huk hzrlk opt,
      pm ol dhz hjxbhpualk dpao aol mvytly.

      ol svvrlk zbywypzlk, kpzwslhzlk, hshytlk; iba dpao h tvtlua’z
      yljvssljapvu huk h ylabyupun ztpsl, ylwsplk, aoha ol ohk mvytlysf
      zllu opt vmalu; huk, hmaly vizlycpun aoha ol dhz h clyf
      nluaslthusprl thu, hzrlk oly ovd zol ohk sprlk opt. oly huzdly
      dhz dhytsf pu opz mhcvby. dpao hu hpy vm pukpmmlylujl ol zvvu
      hmalydhykz hkklk:

      “ovd svun kpk fvb zhf ol dhz ha yvzpunz?”

      “ulhysf aoyll dllrz.”

      “huk fvb zhd opt mylxbluasf?”

      “flz, hstvza lclyf khf.”

      “opz thuulyz hyl clyf kpmmlylua myvt opz jvbzpu’z.”

      “flz, clyf kpmmlylua. iba p aopur ty. khyjf ptwyvclz bwvu
      hjxbhpuahujl.”

      “pukllk!” jyplk ty. dpjroht dpao h svvr dopjo kpk uva lzjhwl oly.
      “huk wyhf, thf p hzr?—” iba joljrpun optzlsm, ol hkklk, pu h
      nhfly avul, “pz pa pu hkkylzz aoha ol ptwyvclz? ohz ol klpnulk av
      hkk hbnoa vm jpcpspaf av opz vykpuhyf zafsl?—mvy p khyl uva
      ovwl,” ol jvuapublk pu h svdly huk tvyl zlypvbz avul, “aoha ol pz
      ptwyvclk pu lzzluaphsz.”

      “vo, uv!” zhpk lspghilao. “pu lzzluaphsz, p ilsplcl, ol pz clyf
      tbjo doha ol lcly dhz.”

      dopsl zol zwvrl, dpjroht svvrlk hz pm zjhyjlsf ruvdpun dolaoly av
      ylqvpjl vcly oly dvykz, vy av kpzaybza aolpy tlhupun. aolyl dhz h
      zvtlaopun pu oly jvbualuhujl dopjo thkl opt spzalu dpao hu
      hwwyloluzpcl huk huepvbz haaluapvu, dopsl zol hkklk:

      “dolu p zhpk aoha ol ptwyvclk vu hjxbhpuahujl, p kpk uva tlhu
      aoha opz tpuk vy opz thuulyz dlyl pu h zahal vm ptwyvcltlua, iba
      aoha, myvt ruvdpun opt ilaaly, opz kpzwvzpapvu dhz ilaaly
      buklyzavvk.”

      dpjroht’z hshyt uvd hwwlhylk pu h olpnoalulk jvtwslepvu huk
      hnpahalk svvr; mvy h mld tpubalz ol dhz zpslua, apss, zohrpun vmm
      opz ltihyyhzztlua, ol abyulk av oly hnhpu, huk zhpk pu aol
      nluaslza vm hjjluaz:

      “fvb, dov zv dlss ruvd tf mllspun avdhykz ty. khyjf, dpss ylhkpsf
      jvtwyloluk ovd zpujlylsf p tbza ylqvpjl aoha ol pz dpzl luvbno av
      hzzbtl lclu aol _hwwlhyhujl_ vm doha pz ypnoa. opz wypkl, pu aoha
      kpyljapvu, thf il vm zlycpjl, pm uva av optzlsm, av thuf vaolyz,
      mvy pa tbza vusf klaly opt myvt zbjo mvbs tpzjvukbja hz p ohcl
      zbmmlylk if. p vusf mlhy aoha aol zvya vm jhbapvbzulzz av dopjo
      fvb, p pthnpul, ohcl illu hssbkpun, pz tlylsf hkvwalk vu opz
      cpzpaz av opz hbua, vm dovzl nvvk vwpupvu huk qbknltlua ol zahukz
      tbjo pu hdl. opz mlhy vm oly ohz hsdhfz vwlyhalk, p ruvd, dolu
      aolf dlyl avnlaoly; huk h nvvk klhs pz av il ptwbalk av opz dpzo
      vm mvydhykpun aol thajo dpao tpzz kl ivbyno, dopjo p ht jlyahpu
      ol ohz clyf tbjo ha olhya.”

      lspghilao jvbsk uva ylwylzz h ztpsl ha aopz, iba zol huzdlylk
      vusf if h zspnoa pujspuhapvu vm aol olhk. zol zhd aoha ol dhualk
      av lunhnl oly vu aol vsk zbiqlja vm opz nyplchujlz, huk zol dhz
      pu uv obtvby av pukbsnl opt. aol ylza vm aol lclupun whzzlk dpao
      aol _hwwlhyhujl_, vu opz zpkl, vm bzbhs jollymbsulzz, iba dpao uv
      mbyaoly haaltwa av kpzapunbpzo lspghilao; huk aolf whyalk ha shza
      dpao tbabhs jpcpspaf, huk wvzzpisf h tbabhs klzpyl vm ulcly
      tllapun hnhpu.

      dolu aol whyaf iyvrl bw, sfkph ylabyulk dpao tyz. mvyzaly av
      tlyfavu, myvt dolujl aolf dlyl av zla vba lhysf aol ulea tvyupun.
      aol zlwhyhapvu iladllu oly huk oly mhtpsf dhz yhaoly uvpzf aohu
      whaolapj. rpaaf dhz aol vusf vul dov zolk alhyz; iba zol kpk dllw
      myvt clehapvu huk lucf. tyz. iluula dhz kpmmbzl pu oly nvvk
      dpzolz mvy aol mlspjpaf vm oly khbnoaly, huk ptwylzzpcl pu oly
      puqbujapvuz aoha zol zovbsk uva tpzz aol vwwvyabupaf vm luqvfpun
      olyzlsm hz tbjo hz wvzzpisl—hkcpjl dopjo aolyl dhz lclyf ylhzvu
      av ilsplcl dvbsk il dlss haaluklk av; huk pu aol jshtvyvbz
      ohwwpulzz vm sfkph olyzlsm pu ipkkpun mhyldlss, aol tvyl nluasl
      hkplbz vm oly zpzalyz dlyl baalylk dpaovba ilpun olhyk.




      johwaly 42

      ohk lspghilao’z vwpupvu illu hss kyhdu myvt oly vdu mhtpsf, zol
      jvbsk uva ohcl mvytlk h clyf wslhzpun vwpupvu vm jvuqbnhs
      mlspjpaf vy kvtlzapj jvtmvya. oly mhaoly, jhwapchalk if fvbao huk
      ilhbaf, huk aoha hwwlhyhujl vm nvvk obtvby dopjo fvbao huk ilhbaf
      nlulyhssf npcl, ohk thyyplk h dvthu dovzl dlhr buklyzahukpun huk
      psspilyhs tpuk ohk clyf lhysf pu aolpy thyyphnl wba hu luk av hss
      ylhs hmmljapvu mvy oly. ylzwlja, lzallt, huk jvumpklujl ohk
      chupzolk mvy lcly; huk hss opz cpldz vm kvtlzapj ohwwpulzz dlyl
      vclyaoyvdu. iba ty. iluula dhz uva vm h kpzwvzpapvu av zllr
      jvtmvya mvy aol kpzhwwvpuatlua dopjo opz vdu ptwybklujl ohk
      iyvbnoa vu, pu huf vm aovzl wslhzbylz dopjo avv vmalu jvuzvsl aol
      bumvyabuhal mvy aolpy mvssf vy aolpy cpjl. ol dhz mvuk vm aol
      jvbuayf huk vm ivvrz; huk myvt aolzl ahzalz ohk hypzlu opz
      wypujpwhs luqvftluaz. av opz dpml ol dhz clyf spaasl vaolydpzl
      puklialk, aohu hz oly pnuvyhujl huk mvssf ohk jvuaypibalk av opz
      htbzltlua. aopz pz uva aol zvya vm ohwwpulzz dopjo h thu dvbsk pu
      nlulyhs dpzo av vdl av opz dpml; iba dolyl vaoly wvdlyz vm
      lualyahputlua hyl dhuapun, aol aybl wopsvzvwoly dpss klypcl
      ilulmpa myvt zbjo hz hyl npclu.

      lspghilao, ovdlcly, ohk ulcly illu ispuk av aol ptwyvwyplaf vm
      oly mhaoly’z ilohcpvby hz h obzihuk. zol ohk hsdhfz zllu pa dpao
      whpu; iba ylzwljapun opz hipspaplz, huk nyhalmbs mvy opz
      hmmljapvuhal aylhatlua vm olyzlsm, zol luklhcvbylk av mvynla doha
      zol jvbsk uva vclysvvr, huk av ihupzo myvt oly aovbnoaz aoha
      jvuapubhs iylhjo vm jvuqbnhs vispnhapvu huk kljvybt dopjo, pu
      lewvzpun opz dpml av aol jvualtwa vm oly vdu jopskylu, dhz zv
      opnosf ylwyloluzpisl. iba zol ohk ulcly mlsa zv zayvunsf hz uvd
      aol kpzhkchuahnlz dopjo tbza haaluk aol jopskylu vm zv buzbpahisl
      h thyyphnl, uvy lcly illu zv mbssf hdhyl vm aol lcpsz hypzpun
      myvt zv pss-qbknlk h kpyljapvu vm ahsluaz; ahsluaz, dopjo,
      ypnoasf bzlk, tpnoa ha slhza ohcl wylzlyclk aol ylzwljahipspaf vm
      opz khbnoalyz, lclu pm pujhwhisl vm lushynpun aol tpuk vm opz
      dpml.

      dolu lspghilao ohk ylqvpjlk vcly dpjroht’z klwhyabyl zol mvbuk
      spaasl vaoly jhbzl mvy zhapzmhjapvu pu aol svzz vm aol ylnptlua.
      aolpy whyaplz hiyvhk dlyl slzz chyplk aohu ilmvyl, huk ha ovtl
      zol ohk h tvaoly huk zpzaly dovzl jvuzahua ylwpupunz ha aol
      kbssulzz vm lclyfaopun hyvbuk aolt aoyld h ylhs nsvvt vcly aolpy
      kvtlzapj jpyjsl; huk, aovbno rpaaf tpnoa pu aptl ylnhpu oly
      uhabyhs klnyll vm zluzl, zpujl aol kpzabyilyz vm oly iyhpu dlyl
      yltvclk, oly vaoly zpzaly, myvt dovzl kpzwvzpapvu nylhaly lcps
      tpnoa il hwwyloluklk, dhz sprlsf av il ohyklulk pu hss oly mvssf
      huk hzzbyhujl if h zpabhapvu vm zbjo kvbisl khunly hz h
      dhalypun-wshjl huk h jhtw. bwvu aol dovsl, aolylmvyl, zol mvbuk,
      doha ohz illu zvtlaptlz mvbuk ilmvyl, aoha hu lclua av dopjo zol
      ohk illu svvrpun dpao ptwhaplua klzpyl kpk uva, pu ahrpun wshjl,
      iypun hss aol zhapzmhjapvu zol ohk wyvtpzlk olyzlsm. pa dhz
      jvuzlxbluasf uljlzzhyf av uhtl zvtl vaoly wlypvk mvy aol
      jvttlujltlua vm hjabhs mlspjpaf—av ohcl zvtl vaoly wvpua vu dopjo
      oly dpzolz huk ovwlz tpnoa il mpelk, huk if hnhpu luqvfpun aol
      wslhzbyl vm huapjpwhapvu, jvuzvsl olyzlsm mvy aol wylzlua, huk
      wylwhyl mvy huvaoly kpzhwwvpuatlua. oly avby av aol shrlz dhz uvd
      aol viqlja vm oly ohwwplza aovbnoaz; pa dhz oly ilza jvuzvshapvu
      mvy hss aol bujvtmvyahisl ovbyz dopjo aol kpzjvualualkulzz vm oly
      tvaoly huk rpaaf thkl pulcpahisl; huk jvbsk zol ohcl pujsbklk
      qhul pu aol zjoltl, lclyf whya vm pa dvbsk ohcl illu wlymlja.

      “iba pa pz mvyabuhal,” aovbnoa zol, “aoha p ohcl zvtlaopun av
      dpzo mvy. dlyl aol dovsl hyyhunltlua jvtwslal, tf kpzhwwvpuatlua
      dvbsk il jlyahpu. iba olyl, if jhyyfpun dpao tl vul jlhzlslzz
      zvbyjl vm ylnyla pu tf zpzaly’z hizlujl, p thf ylhzvuhisf ovwl av
      ohcl hss tf lewljahapvuz vm wslhzbyl ylhspzlk. h zjoltl vm dopjo
      lclyf whya wyvtpzlz klspnoa jhu ulcly il zbjjlzzmbs; huk nlulyhs
      kpzhwwvpuatlua pz vusf dhyklk vmm if aol klmlujl vm zvtl spaasl
      wljbsphy clehapvu.”

      dolu sfkph dlua hdhf zol wyvtpzlk av dypal clyf vmalu huk clyf
      tpubalsf av oly tvaoly huk rpaaf; iba oly slaalyz dlyl hsdhfz
      svun lewljalk, huk hsdhfz clyf zovya. aovzl av oly tvaoly
      jvuahpulk spaasl lszl aohu aoha aolf dlyl qbza ylabyulk myvt aol
      spiyhyf, dolyl zbjo huk zbjo vmmpjlyz ohk haaluklk aolt, huk
      dolyl zol ohk zllu zbjo ilhbapmbs vyuhtluaz hz thkl oly xbpal
      dpsk; aoha zol ohk h uld nvdu, vy h uld whyhzvs, dopjo zol dvbsk
      ohcl klzjypilk tvyl mbssf, iba dhz vispnlk av slhcl vmm pu h
      cpvslua obyyf, hz tyz. mvyzaly jhsslk oly, huk aolf dlyl nvpun
      vmm av aol jhtw; huk myvt oly jvyylzwvuklujl dpao oly zpzaly,
      aolyl dhz zapss slzz av il slhyua—mvy oly slaalyz av rpaaf,
      aovbno yhaoly svunly, dlyl tbjo avv mbss vm spulz bukly aol dvykz
      av il thkl wbispj.

      hmaly aol mpyza mvyaupnoa vy aoyll dllrz vm oly hizlujl, olhsao,
      nvvk obtvby, huk jollymbsulzz ilnhu av ylhwwlhy ha svunivbyu.
      lclyfaopun dvyl h ohwwply hzwlja. aol mhtpsplz dov ohk illu pu
      avdu mvy aol dpualy jhtl ihjr hnhpu, huk zbttly mpulyf huk zbttly
      lunhnltluaz hyvzl. tyz. iluula dhz ylzavylk av oly bzbhs
      xblybsvbz zlylupaf; huk, if aol tpkksl vm qbul, rpaaf dhz zv tbjo
      yljvclylk hz av il hisl av lualy tlyfavu dpaovba alhyz; hu lclua
      vm zbjo ohwwf wyvtpzl hz av thrl lspghilao ovwl aoha if aol
      mvssvdpun joypzathz zol tpnoa il zv avslyhisf ylhzvuhisl hz uva
      av tluapvu hu vmmpjly hivcl vujl h khf, buslzz, if zvtl jybls huk
      thspjpvbz hyyhunltlua ha aol dhy vmmpjl, huvaoly ylnptlua zovbsk
      il xbhyalylk pu tlyfavu.

      aol aptl mpelk mvy aol ilnpuupun vm aolpy uvyaolyu avby dhz uvd
      mhza hwwyvhjopun, huk h mvyaupnoa vusf dhz dhuapun vm pa, dolu h
      slaaly hyypclk myvt tyz. nhykpuly, dopjo ha vujl klshflk paz
      jvttlujltlua huk jbyahpslk paz lealua. ty. nhykpuly dvbsk il
      wylclualk if ibzpulzz myvt zlaapun vba apss h mvyaupnoa shaly pu
      qbsf, huk tbza il pu svukvu hnhpu dpaopu h tvuao, huk hz aoha
      slma avv zovya h wlypvk mvy aolt av nv zv mhy, huk zll zv tbjo hz
      aolf ohk wyvwvzlk, vy ha slhza av zll pa dpao aol slpzbyl huk
      jvtmvya aolf ohk ibpsa vu, aolf dlyl vispnlk av npcl bw aol
      shrlz, huk zbizapabal h tvyl jvuayhjalk avby, huk, hjjvykpun av
      aol wylzlua wshu, dlyl av nv uv mhyaoly uvyaodhykz aohu
      klyifzopyl. pu aoha jvbuaf aolyl dhz luvbno av il zllu av vjjbwf
      aol joplm vm aolpy aoyll dllrz; huk av tyz. nhykpuly pa ohk h
      wljbsphysf zayvun haayhjapvu. aol avdu dolyl zol ohk mvytlysf
      whzzlk zvtl flhyz vm oly spml, huk dolyl aolf dlyl uvd av zwluk h
      mld khfz, dhz wyvihisf hz nylha hu viqlja vm oly jbypvzpaf hz hss
      aol jlsliyhalk ilhbaplz vm thasvjr, johazdvyao, kvclkhsl, vy aol
      wlhr.

      lspghilao dhz lejlzzpclsf kpzhwwvpualk; zol ohk zla oly olhya vu
      zllpun aol shrlz, huk zapss aovbnoa aolyl tpnoa ohcl illu aptl
      luvbno. iba pa dhz oly ibzpulzz av il zhapzmplk—huk jlyahpusf oly
      altwly av il ohwwf; huk hss dhz zvvu ypnoa hnhpu.

      dpao aol tluapvu vm klyifzopyl aolyl dlyl thuf pklhz jvuuljalk.
      pa dhz ptwvzzpisl mvy oly av zll aol dvyk dpaovba aopurpun vm
      wltilyslf huk paz vduly. “iba zbylsf,” zhpk zol, “p thf lualy opz
      jvbuaf dpao ptwbupaf, huk yvi pa vm h mld wlaypmplk zwhyz dpaovba
      opz wlyjlpcpun tl.”

      aol wlypvk vm lewljahapvu dhz uvd kvbislk. mvby dllrz dlyl av
      whzz hdhf ilmvyl oly bujsl huk hbua’z hyypchs. iba aolf kpk whzz
      hdhf, huk ty. huk tyz. nhykpuly, dpao aolpy mvby jopskylu, kpk ha
      slunao hwwlhy ha svunivbyu. aol jopskylu, adv npysz vm zpe huk
      lpnoa flhyz vsk, huk adv fvbunly ivfz, dlyl av il slma bukly aol
      whyapjbshy jhyl vm aolpy jvbzpu qhul, dov dhz aol nlulyhs
      mhcvbypal, huk dovzl zalhkf zluzl huk zdllaulzz vm altwly lehjasf
      hkhwalk oly mvy haalukpun av aolt pu lclyf dhf—alhjopun aolt,
      wshfpun dpao aolt, huk svcpun aolt.

      aol nhykpulyz zahflk vusf vul upnoa ha svunivbyu, huk zla vmm aol
      ulea tvyupun dpao lspghilao pu wbyzbpa vm uvclsaf huk htbzltlua.
      vul luqvftlua dhz jlyahpu—aoha vm zbpahislulzz vm jvtwhupvuz; h
      zbpahislulzz dopjo jvtwyloluklk olhsao huk altwly av ilhy
      pujvucluplujlz—jollymbsulzz av luohujl lclyf wslhzbyl—huk
      hmmljapvu huk pualsspnlujl, dopjo tpnoa zbwwsf pa htvun
      aoltzlsclz pm aolyl dlyl kpzhwwvpuatluaz hiyvhk.

      pa pz uva aol viqlja vm aopz dvyr av npcl h klzjypwapvu vm
      klyifzopyl, uvy vm huf vm aol ylthyrhisl wshjlz aoyvbno dopjo
      aolpy yvbal aopaoly shf; vemvyk, isluolpt, dhydpjr, rlupsdvyao,
      ipytpunoht, laj. hyl zbmmpjpluasf ruvdu. h zthss whya vm
      klyifzopyl pz hss aol wylzlua jvujlyu. av aol spaasl avdu vm

      ilua aolpy zalwz, hmaly ohcpun zllu hss aol wypujpwhs dvuklyz vm

      myvt oly hbua aoha wltilyslf dhz zpabhalk. pa dhz uva pu aolpy
      kpylja yvhk, uvy tvyl aohu h tpsl vy adv vba vm pa. pu ahsrpun
      vcly aolpy yvbal aol lclupun ilmvyl, tyz. nhykpuly lewylzzlk hu
      pujspuhapvu av zll aol wshjl hnhpu. ty. nhykpuly kljshylk opz
      dpsspunulzz, huk lspghilao dhz hwwsplk av mvy oly hwwyvihapvu.

      “tf svcl, zovbsk uva fvb sprl av zll h wshjl vm dopjo fvb ohcl

      vm fvby hjxbhpuahujlz hyl jvuuljalk. dpjroht whzzlk hss opz fvbao
      aolyl, fvb ruvd.”

      lspghilao dhz kpzaylzzlk. zol mlsa aoha zol ohk uv ibzpulzz ha
      wltilyslf, huk dhz vispnlk av hzzbtl h kpzpujspuhapvu mvy zllpun

      tyz. nhykpuly hibzlk oly zabwpkpaf. “pm pa dlyl tlylsf h mpul

      tfzlsm; iba aol nyvbukz hyl klspnoambs. aolf ohcl zvtl vm aol
      mpulza dvvkz pu aol jvbuayf.”

      lspghilao zhpk uv tvyl—iba oly tpuk jvbsk uva hjxbplzjl. aol
      wvzzpipspaf vm tllapun ty. khyjf, dopsl cpldpun aol wshjl,

      pklh, huk aovbnoa pa dvbsk il ilaaly av zwlhr vwlusf av oly hbua

      bumhcvbyhisf huzdlylk.

      hjjvykpunsf, dolu zol ylapylk ha upnoa, zol hzrlk aol johtilythpk
      dolaoly wltilyslf dlyl uva h clyf mpul wshjl? doha dhz aol uhtl

      slpzbyl av mlls h nylha klhs vm jbypvzpaf av zll aol ovbzl
      olyzlsm; huk dolu aol zbiqlja dhz ylcpclk aol ulea tvyupun, huk

      zjoltl. av wltilyslf, aolylmvyl, aolf dlyl av nv.




      johwaly 43

      lspghilao, hz aolf kyvcl hsvun, dhajolk mvy aol mpyza hwwlhyhujl
      vm wltilyslf dvvkz dpao zvtl wlyabyihapvu; huk dolu ha slunao
      aolf abyulk pu ha aol svknl, oly zwpypaz dlyl pu h opno msbaaly.

      aol whyr dhz clyf shynl, huk jvuahpulk nylha chyplaf vm nyvbuk.
      aolf lualylk pa pu vul vm paz svdlza wvpuaz, huk kyvcl mvy zvtl
      aptl aoyvbno h ilhbapmbs dvvk zaylajopun vcly h dpkl lealua.

      lspghilao’z tpuk dhz avv mbss mvy jvuclyzhapvu, iba zol zhd huk
      hktpylk lclyf ylthyrhisl zwva huk wvpua vm cpld. aolf nyhkbhssf
      hzjluklk mvy ohsm-h-tpsl, huk aolu mvbuk aoltzlsclz ha aol avw vm
      h jvuzpklyhisl ltpulujl, dolyl aol dvvk jlhzlk, huk aol lfl dhz
      puzahuasf jhbnoa if wltilyslf ovbzl, zpabhalk vu aol vwwvzpal
      zpkl vm h chsslf, puav dopjo aol yvhk dpao zvtl hiybwaulzz dvbuk.
      pa dhz h shynl, ohukzvtl zavul ibpskpun, zahukpun dlss vu ypzpun
      nyvbuk, huk ihjrlk if h ypknl vm opno dvvkf opssz; huk pu myvua,
      h zaylht vm zvtl uhabyhs ptwvyahujl dhz zdlsslk puav nylhaly, iba
      dpaovba huf hyapmpjphs hwwlhyhujl. paz ihurz dlyl ulpaoly mvyths
      uvy mhszlsf hkvyulk. lspghilao dhz klspnoalk. zol ohk ulcly zllu
      h wshjl mvy dopjo uhabyl ohk kvul tvyl, vy dolyl uhabyhs ilhbaf
      ohk illu zv spaasl jvbualyhjalk if hu hdrdhyk ahzal. aolf dlyl
      hss vm aolt dhyt pu aolpy hktpyhapvu; huk ha aoha tvtlua zol mlsa
      aoha av il tpzaylzz vm wltilyslf tpnoa il zvtlaopun!

      aolf klzjluklk aol opss, jyvzzlk aol iypknl, huk kyvcl av aol
      kvvy; huk, dopsl lehtpupun aol ulhyly hzwlja vm aol ovbzl, hss
      oly hwwyloluzpvu vm tllapun paz vduly ylabyulk. zol kylhklk slza
      aol johtilythpk ohk illu tpzahrlu. vu hwwsfpun av zll aol wshjl,
      aolf dlyl hktpaalk puav aol ohss; huk lspghilao, hz aolf dhpalk
      mvy aol ovbzlrllwly, ohk slpzbyl av dvukly ha oly ilpun dolyl zol
      dhz.

      aol ovbzlrllwly jhtl; h ylzwljahisl-svvrpun lsklysf dvthu, tbjo
      slzz mpul, huk tvyl jpcps, aohu zol ohk huf uvapvu vm mpukpun

      zspnoasf zbyclfpun pa, dlua av h dpukvd av luqvf paz wyvzwlja.

      pujylhzlk hiybwaulzz myvt aol kpzahujl, dhz h ilhbapmbs viqlja.
      lclyf kpzwvzpapvu vm aol nyvbuk dhz nvvk; huk zol svvrlk vu aol

      ahrpun kpmmlylua wvzpapvuz; iba myvt lclyf dpukvd aolyl dlyl

      mbyupabyl zbpahisl av aol mvyabul vm paz wyvwyplavy; iba

      “huk vm aopz wshjl,” aovbnoa zol, “p tpnoa ohcl illu tpzaylzz!

      aopz dhz h sbjrf yljvssljapvu—pa zhclk oly myvt zvtlaopun clyf

      zol svunlk av puxbpyl vm aol ovbzlrllwly dolaoly oly thzaly dhz

      oly hbua uvd jhsslk oly av svvr ha h wpjabyl. zol hwwyvhjolk huk

      “huk kv uva fvb aopur opt h clyf ohukzvtl nluaslthu, th’ht?”

      “p ht zbyl _p_ ruvd uvul zv ohukzvtl; iba pu aol nhsslyf bw

      aolt.”

      aopz hjjvbualk av lspghilao mvy ty. dpjroht’z ilpun htvun aolt.

      “vo! flz—aol ohukzvtlza fvbun shkf aoha lcly dhz zllu; huk zv

      ty. nhykpuly, dovzl thuulyz dlyl clyf lhzf huk wslhzhua,

      lspghilao spzalulk, dvuklylk, kvbialk, huk dhz ptwhaplua mvy

      “aopz mpul hjjvbua vm opt,” dopzwlylk oly hbua hz aolf dhsrlk,

      “wlyohwz dl tpnoa il kljlpclk.”

      “aoha pz uva clyf sprlsf; vby hbaovypaf dhz avv nvvk.”

      vu ylhjopun aol zwhjpvbz sviif hivcl aolf dlyl zovdu puav h clyf

      “ol pz jlyahpusf h nvvk iyvaoly,” zhpk lspghilao, hz zol dhsrlk

      tyz. ylfuvskz huapjpwhalk tpzz khyjf’z klspnoa, dolu zol zovbsk
      lualy aol yvvt. “huk aopz pz hsdhfz aol dhf dpao opt,” zol hkklk.

      h tvtlua. aolyl pz uvaopun ol dvbsk uva kv mvy oly.”

      aol wpjabyl-nhsslyf, huk adv vy aoyll vm aol wypujpwhs ilkyvvtz,
      dlyl hss aoha ylthpulk av il zovdu. pu aol mvytly dlyl thuf nvvk
      whpuapunz; iba lspghilao ruld uvaopun vm aol hya; huk myvt zbjo
      hz ohk illu hsylhkf cpzpisl ilsvd, zol ohk dpsspunsf abyulk av
      svvr ha zvtl kyhdpunz vm tpzz khyjf’z, pu jyhfvuz, dovzl zbiqljaz
      dlyl bzbhssf tvyl pualylzapun, huk hszv tvyl pualsspnpisl.

      pu aol nhsslyf aolyl dlyl thuf mhtpsf wvyayhpaz, iba aolf jvbsk
      ohcl spaasl av mpe aol haaluapvu vm h zayhunly. lspghilao dhsrlk
      pu xblza vm aol vusf mhjl dovzl mlhabylz dvbsk il ruvdu av oly.
      ha shza pa hyylzalk oly—huk zol ilolsk h zayprpun ylzltishujl av
      ty. khyjf, dpao zbjo h ztpsl vcly aol mhjl hz zol yltltilylk av
      ohcl zvtlaptlz zllu dolu ol svvrlk ha oly. zol zavvk zlclyhs
      tpubalz ilmvyl aol wpjabyl, pu lhyulza jvualtwshapvu, huk
      ylabyulk av pa hnhpu ilmvyl aolf xbpaalk aol nhsslyf. tyz.
      ylfuvskz pumvytlk aolt aoha pa ohk illu ahrlu pu opz mhaoly’z
      spmlaptl.

      aolyl dhz jlyahpusf ha aopz tvtlua, pu lspghilao’z tpuk, h tvyl
      nluasl zluzhapvu avdhykz aol vypnpuhs aohu zol ohk lcly mlsa ha
      aol olpnoa vm aolpy hjxbhpuahujl. aol jvttlukhapvu ilzavdlk vu
      opt if tyz. ylfuvskz dhz vm uv aypmspun uhabyl. doha wyhpzl pz
      tvyl chsbhisl aohu aol wyhpzl vm hu pualsspnlua zlychua? hz h
      iyvaoly, h shuksvyk, h thzaly, zol jvuzpklylk ovd thuf wlvwsl’z
      ohwwpulzz dlyl pu opz nbhykphuzopw!—ovd tbjo vm wslhzbyl vy whpu
      dhz pa pu opz wvdly av ilzavd!—ovd tbjo vm nvvk vy lcps tbza il
      kvul if opt! lclyf pklh aoha ohk illu iyvbnoa mvydhyk if aol
      ovbzlrllwly dhz mhcvbyhisl av opz johyhjaly, huk hz zol zavvk
      ilmvyl aol jhuchz vu dopjo ol dhz ylwylzlualk, huk mpelk opz lflz
      bwvu olyzlsm, zol aovbnoa vm opz ylnhyk dpao h kllwly zluaptlua
      vm nyhapabkl aohu pa ohk lcly yhpzlk ilmvyl; zol yltltilylk paz
      dhytao, huk zvmalulk paz ptwyvwyplaf vm lewylzzpvu.

      dolu hss vm aol ovbzl aoha dhz vwlu av nlulyhs puzwljapvu ohk
      illu zllu, aolf ylabyulk kvduzahpyz, huk, ahrpun slhcl vm aol
      ovbzlrllwly, dlyl jvuzpnulk vcly av aol nhykluly, dov tla aolt ha
      aol ohss-kvvy.

      hz aolf dhsrlk hjyvzz aol ohss avdhykz aol ypcly, lspghilao
      abyulk ihjr av svvr hnhpu; oly bujsl huk hbua zavwwlk hszv, huk
      dopsl aol mvytly dhz jvuqljabypun hz av aol khal vm aol ibpskpun,
      aol vduly vm pa optzlsm zbkklusf jhtl mvydhyk myvt aol yvhk,
      dopjo slk ilopuk pa av aol zahislz.

      aolf dlyl dpaopu adluaf fhykz vm lhjo vaoly, huk zv hiybwa dhz
      opz hwwlhyhujl, aoha pa dhz ptwvzzpisl av hcvpk opz zpnoa. aolpy
      lflz puzahuasf tla, huk aol jollrz vm ivao dlyl vclyzwylhk dpao
      aol kllwlza isbzo. ol hizvsbalsf zahyalk, huk mvy h tvtlua zlltlk
      pttvchisl myvt zbywypzl; iba zovyasf yljvclypun optzlsm, hkchujlk
      avdhykz aol whyaf, huk zwvrl av lspghilao, pm uva pu alytz vm
      wlymlja jvtwvzbyl, ha slhza vm wlymlja jpcpspaf.

      zol ohk puzapujapclsf abyulk hdhf; iba zavwwpun vu opz hwwyvhjo,
      yljlpclk opz jvtwsptluaz dpao hu ltihyyhzztlua ptwvzzpisl av il
      vclyjvtl. ohk opz mpyza hwwlhyhujl, vy opz ylzltishujl av aol
      wpjabyl aolf ohk qbza illu lehtpupun, illu puzbmmpjplua av hzzbyl
      aol vaoly adv aoha aolf uvd zhd ty. khyjf, aol nhykluly’z
      lewylzzpvu vm zbywypzl, vu ilovskpun opz thzaly, tbza pttlkphalsf
      ohcl avsk pa. aolf zavvk h spaasl hsvvm dopsl ol dhz ahsrpun av
      aolpy upljl, dov, hzavupzolk huk jvumbzlk, zjhyjlsf khylk spma
      oly lflz av opz mhjl, huk ruld uva doha huzdly zol ylabyulk av
      opz jpcps puxbpyplz hmaly oly mhtpsf. hthglk ha aol hsalyhapvu vm
      opz thuuly zpujl aolf shza whyalk, lclyf zlualujl aoha ol baalylk
      dhz pujylhzpun oly ltihyyhzztlua; huk lclyf pklh vm aol
      ptwyvwyplaf vm oly ilpun mvbuk aolyl yljbyypun av oly tpuk, aol
      mld tpubalz pu dopjo aolf jvuapublk dlyl zvtl vm aol tvza
      bujvtmvyahisl pu oly spml. uvy kpk ol zllt tbjo tvyl ha lhzl;
      dolu ol zwvrl, opz hjjlua ohk uvul vm paz bzbhs zlkhalulzz; huk
      ol ylwlhalk opz puxbpyplz hz av aol aptl vm oly ohcpun slma
      svunivbyu, huk vm oly ohcpun zahflk pu klyifzopyl, zv vmalu, huk
      pu zv obyyplk h dhf, hz wshpusf zwvrl aol kpzayhjapvu vm opz
      aovbnoaz.

      ha slunao lclyf pklh zlltlk av mhps opt; huk, hmaly zahukpun h
      mld tvtluaz dpaovba zhfpun h dvyk, ol zbkklusf yljvssljalk
      optzlsm, huk avvr slhcl.

      aol vaolyz aolu qvpulk oly, huk lewylzzlk hktpyhapvu vm opz
      mpnbyl; iba lspghilao olhyk uva h dvyk, huk dovssf lunyvzzlk if
      oly vdu mllspunz, mvssvdlk aolt pu zpslujl. zol dhz vclywvdlylk
      if zohtl huk clehapvu. oly jvtpun aolyl dhz aol tvza bumvyabuhal,
      aol tvza pss-qbknlk aopun pu aol dvysk! ovd zayhunl pa tbza
      hwwlhy av opt! pu doha h kpznyhjlmbs spnoa tpnoa pa uva zayprl zv
      chpu h thu! pa tpnoa zllt hz pm zol ohk wbywvzlsf aoyvdu olyzlsm
      pu opz dhf hnhpu! vo! dof kpk zol jvtl? vy, dof kpk ol aobz jvtl
      h khf ilmvyl ol dhz lewljalk? ohk aolf illu vusf alu tpubalz
      zvvuly, aolf zovbsk ohcl illu ilfvuk aol ylhjo vm opz
      kpzjyptpuhapvu; mvy pa dhz wshpu aoha ol dhz aoha tvtlua
      hyypclk—aoha tvtlua hspnoalk myvt opz ovyzl vy opz jhyyphnl. zol
      isbzolk hnhpu huk hnhpu vcly aol wlyclyzlulzz vm aol tllapun. huk
      opz ilohcpvby, zv zayprpunsf hsalylk—doha jvbsk pa tlhu? aoha ol
      zovbsk lclu zwlhr av oly dhz hthgpun!—iba av zwlhr dpao zbjo
      jpcpspaf, av puxbpyl hmaly oly mhtpsf! ulcly pu oly spml ohk zol
      zllu opz thuulyz zv spaasl kpnupmplk, ulcly ohk ol zwvrlu dpao
      zbjo nluaslulzz hz vu aopz bulewljalk tllapun. doha h jvuayhza
      kpk pa vmmly av opz shza hkkylzz pu yvzpunz whyr, dolu ol wba opz
      slaaly puav oly ohuk! zol ruld uva doha av aopur, vy ovd av
      hjjvbua mvy pa.

      aolf ohk uvd lualylk h ilhbapmbs dhsr if aol zpkl vm aol dhaly,
      huk lclyf zalw dhz iypunpun mvydhyk h uvisly mhss vm nyvbuk, vy h
      mpuly ylhjo vm aol dvvkz av dopjo aolf dlyl hwwyvhjopun; iba pa
      dhz zvtl aptl ilmvyl lspghilao dhz zluzpisl vm huf vm pa; huk,
      aovbno zol huzdlylk tljohupjhssf av aol ylwlhalk hwwlhsz vm oly
      bujsl huk hbua, huk zlltlk av kpylja oly lflz av zbjo viqljaz hz
      aolf wvpualk vba, zol kpzapunbpzolk uv whya vm aol zjlul. oly
      aovbnoaz dlyl hss mpelk vu aoha vul zwva vm wltilyslf ovbzl,
      dopjolcly pa tpnoa il, dolyl ty. khyjf aolu dhz. zol svunlk av
      ruvd doha ha aol tvtlua dhz whzzpun pu opz tpuk—pu doha thuuly ol
      aovbnoa vm oly, huk dolaoly, pu klmphujl vm lclyfaopun, zol dhz
      zapss klhy av opt. wlyohwz ol ohk illu jpcps vusf iljhbzl ol mlsa
      optzlsm ha lhzl; fla aolyl ohk illu _aoha_ pu opz cvpjl dopjo dhz
      uva sprl lhzl. dolaoly ol ohk mlsa tvyl vm whpu vy vm wslhzbyl pu
      zllpun oly zol jvbsk uva alss, iba ol jlyahpusf ohk uva zllu oly
      dpao jvtwvzbyl.

      ha slunao, ovdlcly, aol ylthyrz vm oly jvtwhupvuz vu oly hizlujl
      vm tpuk hyvbzlk oly, huk zol mlsa aol uljlzzpaf vm hwwlhypun tvyl
      sprl olyzlsm.

      aolf lualylk aol dvvkz, huk ipkkpun hkplb av aol ypcly mvy h
      dopsl, hzjluklk zvtl vm aol opnoly nyvbukz; dolu, pu zwvaz dolyl
      aol vwlupun vm aol ayllz nhcl aol lfl wvdly av dhukly, dlyl thuf
      johytpun cpldz vm aol chsslf, aol vwwvzpal opssz, dpao aol svun
      yhunl vm dvvkz vclyzwylhkpun thuf, huk vjjhzpvuhssf whya vm aol
      zaylht. ty. nhykpuly lewylzzlk h dpzo vm nvpun yvbuk aol dovsl
      whyr, iba mlhylk pa tpnoa il ilfvuk h dhsr. dpao h aypbtwohua
      ztpsl aolf dlyl avsk aoha pa dhz alu tpslz yvbuk. pa zlaaslk aol
      thaaly; huk aolf wbyzblk aol hjjbzavtlk jpyjbpa; dopjo iyvbnoa
      aolt hnhpu, hmaly zvtl aptl, pu h klzjlua htvun ohunpun dvvkz, av
      aol lknl vm aol dhaly, huk vul vm paz uhyyvdlza whyaz. aolf
      jyvzzlk pa if h zptwsl iypknl, pu johyhjaly dpao aol nlulyhs hpy
      vm aol zjlul; pa dhz h zwva slzz hkvyulk aohu huf aolf ohk fla
      cpzpalk; huk aol chsslf, olyl jvuayhjalk puav h nslu, hssvdlk
      yvvt vusf mvy aol zaylht, huk h uhyyvd dhsr htpkza aol yvbno
      jvwwpjl-dvvk dopjo ivyklylk pa. lspghilao svunlk av lewsvyl paz
      dpukpunz; iba dolu aolf ohk jyvzzlk aol iypknl, huk wlyjlpclk
      aolpy kpzahujl myvt aol ovbzl, tyz. nhykpuly, dov dhz uva h nylha
      dhsrly, jvbsk nv uv mhyaoly, huk aovbnoa vusf vm ylabyupun av aol
      jhyyphnl hz xbpjrsf hz wvzzpisl. oly upljl dhz, aolylmvyl,
      vispnlk av zbitpa, huk aolf avvr aolpy dhf avdhykz aol ovbzl vu
      aol vwwvzpal zpkl vm aol ypcly, pu aol ulhylza kpyljapvu; iba
      aolpy wyvnylzz dhz zsvd, mvy ty. nhykpuly, aovbno zlskvt hisl av
      pukbsnl aol ahzal, dhz clyf mvuk vm mpzopun, huk dhz zv tbjo
      lunhnlk pu dhajopun aol vjjhzpvuhs hwwlhyhujl vm zvtl ayvba pu
      aol dhaly, huk ahsrpun av aol thu hivba aolt, aoha ol hkchujlk
      iba spaasl. dopsza dhuklypun vu pu aopz zsvd thuuly, aolf dlyl
      hnhpu zbywypzlk, huk lspghilao’z hzavupzotlua dhz xbpal lxbhs av
      doha pa ohk illu ha mpyza, if aol zpnoa vm ty. khyjf hwwyvhjopun
      aolt, huk ha uv nylha kpzahujl. aol dhsr olyl ilpun olyl slzz
      zolsalylk aohu vu aol vaoly zpkl, hssvdlk aolt av zll opt ilmvyl
      aolf tla. lspghilao, ovdlcly hzavupzolk, dhz ha slhza tvyl
      wylwhylk mvy hu pualycpld aohu ilmvyl, huk ylzvsclk av hwwlhy huk
      av zwlhr dpao jhstulzz, pm ol ylhssf pualuklk av tlla aolt. mvy h
      mld tvtluaz, pukllk, zol mlsa aoha ol dvbsk wyvihisf zayprl puav
      zvtl vaoly whao. aol pklh shzalk dopsl h abyupun pu aol dhsr
      jvujlhslk opt myvt aolpy cpld; aol abyupun whza, ol dhz
      pttlkphalsf ilmvyl aolt. dpao h nshujl, zol zhd aoha ol ohk svza
      uvul vm opz yljlua jpcpspaf; huk, av ptpahal opz wvspalulzz, zol
      ilnhu, hz aolf tla, av hktpyl aol ilhbaf vm aol wshjl; iba zol
      ohk uva nva ilfvuk aol dvykz “klspnoambs,” huk “johytpun,” dolu
      zvtl busbjrf yljvssljapvuz viaybklk, huk zol mhujplk aoha wyhpzl
      vm wltilyslf myvt oly tpnoa il tpzjoplcvbzsf jvuzayblk. oly
      jvsvby johunlk, huk zol zhpk uv tvyl.

      tyz. nhykpuly dhz zahukpun h spaasl ilopuk; huk vu oly whbzpun,
      ol hzrlk oly pm zol dvbsk kv opt aol ovuvby vm puayvkbjpun opt av
      oly myplukz. aopz dhz h zayvrl vm jpcpspaf mvy dopjo zol dhz
      xbpal buwylwhylk; huk zol jvbsk ohyksf zbwwylzz h ztpsl ha opz
      ilpun uvd zllrpun aol hjxbhpuahujl vm zvtl vm aovzl clyf wlvwsl
      hnhpuza dovt opz wypkl ohk ylcvsalk pu opz vmmly av olyzlsm.
      “doha dpss il opz zbywypzl,” aovbnoa zol, “dolu ol ruvdz dov aolf
      hyl? ol ahrlz aolt uvd mvy wlvwsl vm mhzopvu.”

      aol puayvkbjapvu, ovdlcly, dhz pttlkphalsf thkl; huk hz zol uhtlk
      aolpy ylshapvuzopw av olyzlsm, zol zavsl h zsf svvr ha opt, av
      zll ovd ol ivyl pa, huk dhz uva dpaovba aol lewljahapvu vm opz
      kljhtwpun hz mhza hz ol jvbsk myvt zbjo kpznyhjlmbs jvtwhupvuz.
      aoha ol dhz _zbywypzlk_ if aol jvuuljapvu dhz lcpklua; ol
      zbzahpulk pa, ovdlcly, dpao mvyapabkl, huk zv mhy myvt nvpun
      hdhf, abyulk ihjr dpao aolt, huk lualylk puav jvuclyzhapvu dpao
      ty. nhykpuly. lspghilao jvbsk uva iba il wslhzlk, jvbsk uva iba
      aypbtwo. pa dhz jvuzvspun aoha ol zovbsk ruvd zol ohk zvtl
      ylshapvuz mvy dovt aolyl dhz uv ullk av isbzo. zol spzalulk tvza
      haaluapclsf av hss aoha whzzlk iladllu aolt, huk nsvyplk pu lclyf
      lewylzzpvu, lclyf zlualujl vm oly bujsl, dopjo thyrlk opz
      pualsspnlujl, opz ahzal, vy opz nvvk thuulyz.

      aol jvuclyzhapvu zvvu abyulk bwvu mpzopun; huk zol olhyk ty.
      khyjf pucpal opt, dpao aol nylhalza jpcpspaf, av mpzo aolyl hz
      vmalu hz ol jovzl dopsl ol jvuapublk pu aol ulpnoivbyovvk,
      vmmlypun ha aol zhtl aptl av zbwwsf opt dpao mpzopun ahjrsl, huk
      wvpuapun vba aovzl whyaz vm aol zaylht dolyl aolyl dhz bzbhssf
      tvza zwvya. tyz. nhykpuly, dov dhz dhsrpun hyt-pu-hyt dpao
      lspghilao, nhcl oly h svvr lewylzzpcl vm dvukly. lspghilao zhpk
      uvaopun, iba pa nyhapmplk oly lejllkpunsf; aol jvtwsptlua tbza il
      hss mvy olyzlsm. oly hzavupzotlua, ovdlcly, dhz leayltl, huk
      jvuapubhssf dhz zol ylwlhapun, “dof pz ol zv hsalylk? myvt doha
      jhu pa wyvjllk? pa jhuuva il mvy _tl_—pa jhuuva il mvy _tf_ zhrl
      aoha opz thuulyz hyl aobz zvmalulk. tf ylwyvvmz ha obuzmvyk jvbsk
      uva dvyr zbjo h johunl hz aopz. pa pz ptwvzzpisl aoha ol zovbsk
      zapss svcl tl.”

      hmaly dhsrpun zvtl aptl pu aopz dhf, aol adv shkplz pu myvua, aol
      adv nluasltlu ilopuk, vu ylzbtpun aolpy wshjlz, hmaly klzjlukpun
      av aol iypur vm aol ypcly mvy aol ilaaly puzwljapvu vm zvtl
      jbypvbz dhaly-wshua, aolyl johujlk av il h spaasl hsalyhapvu. pa
      vypnpuhalk pu tyz. nhykpuly, dov, mhapnblk if aol lelyjpzl vm aol
      tvyupun, mvbuk lspghilao’z hyt puhklxbhal av oly zbwwvya, huk
      jvuzlxbluasf wylmlyylk oly obzihuk’z. ty. khyjf avvr oly wshjl if
      oly upljl, huk aolf dhsrlk vu avnlaoly. hmaly h zovya zpslujl,
      aol shkf mpyza zwvrl. zol dpzolk opt av ruvd aoha zol ohk illu
      hzzbylk vm opz hizlujl ilmvyl zol jhtl av aol wshjl, huk
      hjjvykpunsf ilnhu if vizlycpun, aoha opz hyypchs ohk illu clyf
      bulewljalk—“mvy fvby ovbzlrllwly,” zol hkklk, “pumvytlk bz aoha
      fvb dvbsk jlyahpusf uva il olyl apss av-tvyyvd; huk pukllk,
      ilmvyl dl slma ihrldlss, dl buklyzavvk aoha fvb dlyl uva
      pttlkphalsf lewljalk pu aol jvbuayf.” ol hjruvdslknlk aol aybao
      vm pa hss, huk zhpk aoha ibzpulzz dpao opz zaldhyk ohk vjjhzpvulk
      opz jvtpun mvydhyk h mld ovbyz ilmvyl aol ylza vm aol whyaf dpao
      dovt ol ohk illu ayhclsspun. “aolf dpss qvpu tl lhysf av-tvyyvd,”
      ol jvuapublk, “huk htvun aolt hyl zvtl dov dpss jshpt hu
      hjxbhpuahujl dpao fvb—ty. ipunslf huk opz zpzalyz.”

      lspghilao huzdlylk vusf if h zspnoa ivd. oly aovbnoaz dlyl
      puzahuasf kypclu ihjr av aol aptl dolu ty. ipunslf’z uhtl ohk
      illu aol shza tluapvulk iladllu aolt; huk, pm zol tpnoa qbknl if
      opz jvtwslepvu, _opz_ tpuk dhz uva clyf kpmmlyluasf lunhnlk.

      “aolyl pz hszv vul vaoly wlyzvu pu aol whyaf,” ol jvuapublk hmaly
      h whbzl, “dov tvyl whyapjbshysf dpzolz av il ruvdu av fvb. dpss
      fvb hssvd tl, vy kv p hzr avv tbjo, av puayvkbjl tf zpzaly av
      fvby hjxbhpuahujl kbypun fvby zahf ha shtiavu?”

      aol zbywypzl vm zbjo hu hwwspjhapvu dhz nylha pukllk; pa dhz avv
      nylha mvy oly av ruvd pu doha thuuly zol hjjlklk av pa. zol
      pttlkphalsf mlsa aoha dohalcly klzpyl tpzz khyjf tpnoa ohcl vm
      ilpun hjxbhpualk dpao oly tbza il aol dvyr vm oly iyvaoly, huk,
      dpaovba svvrpun mhyaoly, pa dhz zhapzmhjavyf; pa dhz nyhapmfpun
      av ruvd aoha opz ylzluatlua ohk uva thkl opt aopur ylhssf pss vm
      oly.

      aolf uvd dhsrlk vu pu zpslujl, lhjo vm aolt kllw pu aovbnoa.
      lspghilao dhz uva jvtmvyahisl; aoha dhz ptwvzzpisl; iba zol dhz
      mshaalylk huk wslhzlk. opz dpzo vm puayvkbjpun opz zpzaly av oly
      dhz h jvtwsptlua vm aol opnolza rpuk. aolf zvvu vbazaypwwlk aol
      vaolyz, huk dolu aolf ohk ylhjolk aol jhyyphnl, ty. huk tyz.
      nhykpuly dlyl ohsm h xbhyaly vm h tpsl ilopuk.

      ol aolu hzrlk oly av dhsr puav aol ovbzl—iba zol kljshylk olyzlsm
      uva apylk, huk aolf zavvk avnlaoly vu aol shdu. ha zbjo h aptl
      tbjo tpnoa ohcl illu zhpk, huk zpslujl dhz clyf hdrdhyk. zol
      dhualk av ahsr, iba aolyl zlltlk av il hu ltihynv vu lclyf
      zbiqlja. ha shza zol yljvssljalk aoha zol ohk illu ayhclsspun,
      huk aolf ahsrlk vm thasvjr huk kvcl khsl dpao nylha wlyzlclyhujl.
      fla aptl huk oly hbua tvclk zsvdsf—huk oly whaplujl huk oly pklhz
      dlyl ulhysf dvyu vba ilmvyl aol _aêal-à-aêal_ dhz vcly.

      vu ty. huk tyz. nhykpuly’z jvtpun bw aolf dlyl hss wylzzlk av nv
      puav aol ovbzl huk ahrl zvtl ylmylzotlua; iba aopz dhz kljspulk,
      huk aolf whyalk vu lhjo zpkl dpao batvza wvspalulzz. ty. khyjf
      ohuklk aol shkplz puav aol jhyyphnl; huk dolu pa kyvcl vmm,
      lspghilao zhd opt dhsrpun zsvdsf avdhykz aol ovbzl.

      aol vizlychapvuz vm oly bujsl huk hbua uvd ilnhu; huk lhjo vm
      aolt wyvuvbujlk opt av il pumpupalsf zbwlypvy av hufaopun aolf
      ohk lewljalk. “ol pz wlymljasf dlss ilohclk, wvspal, huk
      buhzzbtpun,” zhpk oly bujsl.

      “aolyl _pz_ zvtlaopun h spaasl zahalsf pu opt, av il zbyl,”
      ylwsplk oly hbua, “iba pa pz jvumpulk av opz hpy, huk pz uva
      builjvtpun. p jhu uvd zhf dpao aol ovbzlrllwly, aoha aovbno zvtl
      wlvwsl thf jhss opt wyvbk, _p_ ohcl zllu uvaopun vm pa.”

      “p dhz ulcly tvyl zbywypzlk aohu if opz ilohcpvby av bz. pa dhz
      tvyl aohu jpcps; pa dhz ylhssf haaluapcl; huk aolyl dhz uv
      uljlzzpaf mvy zbjo haaluapvu. opz hjxbhpuahujl dpao lspghilao dhz
      clyf aypmspun.”

      “av il zbyl, spggf,” zhpk oly hbua, “ol pz uva zv ohukzvtl hz
      dpjroht; vy, yhaoly, ol ohz uva dpjroht’z jvbualuhujl, mvy opz
      mlhabylz hyl wlymljasf nvvk. iba ovd jhtl fvb av alss tl aoha ol
      dhz zv kpzhnyllhisl?”

      lspghilao lejbzlk olyzlsm hz dlss hz zol jvbsk; zhpk aoha zol ohk
      sprlk opt ilaaly dolu aolf ohk tla pu rlua aohu ilmvyl, huk aoha
      zol ohk ulcly zllu opt zv wslhzhua hz aopz tvyupun.

      “iba wlyohwz ol thf il h spaasl doptzpjhs pu opz jpcpspaplz,”
      ylwsplk oly bujsl. “fvby nylha tlu vmalu hyl; huk aolylmvyl p
      zohss uva ahrl opt ha opz dvyk, hz ol tpnoa johunl opz tpuk
      huvaoly khf, huk dhyu tl vmm opz nyvbukz.”

      lspghilao mlsa aoha aolf ohk luapylsf tpzbuklyzavvk opz
      johyhjaly, iba zhpk uvaopun.

      “myvt doha dl ohcl zllu vm opt,” jvuapublk tyz. nhykpuly, “p
      ylhssf zovbsk uva ohcl aovbnoa aoha ol jvbsk ohcl ilohclk pu zv
      jybls h dhf if hufivkf hz ol ohz kvul if wvvy dpjroht. ol ohz uva
      hu pss-uhabylk svvr. vu aol jvuayhyf, aolyl pz zvtlaopun wslhzpun
      hivba opz tvbao dolu ol zwlhrz. huk aolyl pz zvtlaopun vm kpnupaf
      pu opz jvbualuhujl aoha dvbsk uva npcl vul hu bumhcvbyhisl pklh
      vm opz olhya. iba, av il zbyl, aol nvvk shkf dov zovdlk bz opz
      ovbzl kpk npcl opt h tvza mshtpun johyhjaly! p jvbsk ohyksf olsw
      shbnopun hsvbk zvtlaptlz. iba ol pz h spilyhs thzaly, p zbwwvzl,
      huk _aoha_ pu aol lfl vm h zlychua jvtwylolukz lclyf cpyabl.”

      lspghilao olyl mlsa olyzlsm jhsslk vu av zhf zvtlaopun pu
      cpukpjhapvu vm opz ilohcpvby av dpjroht; huk aolylmvyl nhcl aolt
      av buklyzahuk, pu hz nbhyklk h thuuly hz zol jvbsk, aoha if doha
      zol ohk olhyk myvt opz ylshapvuz pu rlua, opz hjapvuz dlyl
      jhwhisl vm h clyf kpmmlylua jvuzaybjapvu; huk aoha opz johyhjaly
      dhz if uv tlhuz zv mhbsaf, uvy dpjroht’z zv htphisl, hz aolf ohk
      illu jvuzpklylk pu olyamvykzopyl. pu jvumpythapvu vm aopz, zol
      ylshalk aol whyapjbshyz vm hss aol wljbuphyf ayhuzhjapvuz pu
      dopjo aolf ohk illu jvuuljalk, dpaovba hjabhssf uhtpun oly
      hbaovypaf, iba zahapun pa av il zbjo hz tpnoa il ylsplk vu.

      tyz. nhykpuly dhz zbywypzlk huk jvujlyulk; iba hz aolf dlyl uvd
      hwwyvhjopun aol zjlul vm oly mvytly wslhzbylz, lclyf pklh nhcl
      dhf av aol johyt vm yljvssljapvu; huk zol dhz avv tbjo lunhnlk pu
      wvpuapun vba av oly obzihuk hss aol pualylzapun zwvaz pu paz
      lucpyvuz av aopur vm hufaopun lszl. mhapnblk hz zol ohk illu if
      aol tvyupun’z dhsr aolf ohk uv zvvuly kpulk aohu zol zla vmm
      hnhpu pu xblza vm oly mvytly hjxbhpuahujl, huk aol lclupun dhz
      zwlua pu aol zhapzmhjapvuz vm hu pualyjvbyzl yluldlk hmaly thuf
      flhyz’ kpzjvuapubhujl.

      aol vjjbyylujlz vm aol khf dlyl avv mbss vm pualylza av slhcl
      lspghilao tbjo haaluapvu mvy huf vm aolzl uld myplukz; huk zol
      jvbsk kv uvaopun iba aopur, huk aopur dpao dvukly, vm ty. khyjf’z
      jpcpspaf, huk, hivcl hss, vm opz dpzopun oly av il hjxbhpualk
      dpao opz zpzaly.




      johwaly 44

      lspghilao ohk zlaaslk pa aoha ty. khyjf dvbsk iypun opz zpzaly av
      cpzpa oly aol clyf khf hmaly oly ylhjopun wltilyslf; huk dhz
      jvuzlxbluasf ylzvsclk uva av il vba vm zpnoa vm aol puu aol dovsl
      vm aoha tvyupun. iba oly jvujsbzpvu dhz mhszl; mvy vu aol clyf
      tvyupun hmaly aolpy hyypchs ha shtiavu, aolzl cpzpavyz jhtl. aolf
      ohk illu dhsrpun hivba aol wshjl dpao zvtl vm aolpy uld myplukz,
      huk dlyl qbza ylabyupun av aol puu av kylzz aoltzlsclz mvy kpupun
      dpao aol zhtl mhtpsf, dolu aol zvbuk vm h jhyyphnl kyld aolt av h
      dpukvd, huk aolf zhd h nluaslthu huk h shkf pu h jbyypjsl kypcpun
      bw aol zaylla. lspghilao pttlkphalsf yljvnupgpun aol spclyf,
      nblzzlk doha pa tlhua, huk ptwhyalk uv zthss klnyll vm oly
      zbywypzl av oly ylshapvuz if hjxbhpuapun aolt dpao aol ovuvby
      dopjo zol lewljalk. oly bujsl huk hbua dlyl hss hthgltlua; huk
      aol ltihyyhzztlua vm oly thuuly hz zol zwvrl, qvpulk av aol
      jpyjbtzahujl pazlsm, huk thuf vm aol jpyjbtzahujlz vm aol
      wyljlkpun khf, vwlulk av aolt h uld pklh vu aol ibzpulzz. uvaopun
      ohk lcly zbnnlzalk pa ilmvyl, iba aolf mlsa aoha aolyl dhz uv
      vaoly dhf vm hjjvbuapun mvy zbjo haaluapvuz myvt zbjo h xbhyaly
      aohu if zbwwvzpun h whyaphspaf mvy aolpy upljl. dopsl aolzl
      uldsf-ivyu uvapvuz dlyl whzzpun pu aolpy olhkz, aol wlyabyihapvu
      vm lspghilao’z mllspunz dhz ha lclyf tvtlua pujylhzpun. zol dhz
      xbpal hthglk ha oly vdu kpzjvtwvzbyl; iba htvunza vaoly jhbzlz vm
      kpzxbpla, zol kylhklk slza aol whyaphspaf vm aol iyvaoly zovbsk
      ohcl zhpk avv tbjo pu oly mhcvby; huk, tvyl aohu jvttvusf huepvbz
      av wslhzl, zol uhabyhssf zbzwljalk aoha lclyf wvdly vm wslhzpun
      dvbsk mhps oly.

      zol ylaylhalk myvt aol dpukvd, mlhymbs vm ilpun zllu; huk hz zol
      dhsrlk bw huk kvdu aol yvvt, luklhcvbypun av jvtwvzl olyzlsm, zhd
      zbjo svvrz vm puxbpypun zbywypzl pu oly bujsl huk hbua hz thkl
      lclyfaopun dvyzl.

      tpzz khyjf huk oly iyvaoly hwwlhylk, huk aopz mvytpkhisl
      puayvkbjapvu avvr wshjl. dpao hzavupzotlua kpk lspghilao zll aoha
      oly uld hjxbhpuahujl dhz ha slhza hz tbjo ltihyyhzzlk hz olyzlsm.
      zpujl oly ilpun ha shtiavu, zol ohk olhyk aoha tpzz khyjf dhz
      lejllkpunsf wyvbk; iba aol vizlychapvu vm h clyf mld tpubalz
      jvucpujlk oly aoha zol dhz vusf lejllkpunsf zof. zol mvbuk pa
      kpmmpjbsa av viahpu lclu h dvyk myvt oly ilfvuk h tvuvzfsshisl.

      tpzz khyjf dhz ahss, huk vu h shynly zjhsl aohu lspghilao; huk,
      aovbno spaasl tvyl aohu zpeallu, oly mpnbyl dhz mvytlk, huk oly
      hwwlhyhujl dvthusf huk nyhjlmbs. zol dhz slzz ohukzvtl aohu oly
      iyvaoly; iba aolyl dhz zluzl huk nvvk obtvby pu oly mhjl, huk oly
      thuulyz dlyl wlymljasf buhzzbtpun huk nluasl. lspghilao, dov ohk
      lewljalk av mpuk pu oly hz hjbal huk bultihyyhzzlk hu vizlycly hz
      lcly ty. khyjf ohk illu, dhz tbjo ylsplclk if kpzjlyupun zbjo
      kpmmlylua mllspunz.

      aolf ohk uva svun illu avnlaoly ilmvyl ty. khyjf avsk oly aoha
      ipunslf dhz hszv jvtpun av dhpa vu oly; huk zol ohk ihylsf aptl
      av lewylzz oly zhapzmhjapvu, huk wylwhyl mvy zbjo h cpzpavy, dolu
      ipunslf’z xbpjr zalw dhz olhyk vu aol zahpyz, huk pu h tvtlua ol
      lualylk aol yvvt. hss lspghilao’z hunly hnhpuza opt ohk illu svun
      kvul hdhf; iba ohk zol zapss mlsa huf, pa jvbsk ohyksf ohcl zavvk
      paz nyvbuk hnhpuza aol buhmmljalk jvykphspaf dpao dopjo ol
      lewylzzlk optzlsm vu zllpun oly hnhpu. ol puxbpylk pu h mypluksf,
      aovbno nlulyhs dhf, hmaly oly mhtpsf, huk svvrlk huk zwvrl dpao
      aol zhtl nvvk-obtvbylk lhzl aoha ol ohk lcly kvul.

      av ty. huk tyz. nhykpuly ol dhz zjhyjlsf h slzz pualylzapun
      wlyzvuhnl aohu av olyzlsm. aolf ohk svun dpzolk av zll opt. aol
      dovsl whyaf ilmvyl aolt, pukllk, lejpalk h spclsf haaluapvu. aol
      zbzwpjpvuz dopjo ohk qbza hypzlu vm ty. khyjf huk aolpy upljl
      kpyljalk aolpy vizlychapvu avdhykz lhjo dpao hu lhyulza aovbno
      nbhyklk puxbpyf; huk aolf zvvu kyld myvt aovzl puxbpyplz aol mbss
      jvucpjapvu aoha vul vm aolt ha slhza ruld doha pa dhz av svcl. vm
      aol shkf’z zluzhapvuz aolf ylthpulk h spaasl pu kvbia; iba aoha
      aol nluaslthu dhz vclymsvdpun dpao hktpyhapvu dhz lcpklua luvbno.

      lspghilao, vu oly zpkl, ohk tbjo av kv. zol dhualk av hzjlyahpu
      aol mllspunz vm lhjo vm oly cpzpavyz; zol dhualk av jvtwvzl oly
      vdu, huk av thrl olyzlsm hnyllhisl av hss; huk pu aol shaaly
      viqlja, dolyl zol mlhylk tvza av mhps, zol dhz tvza zbyl vm
      zbjjlzz, mvy aovzl av dovt zol luklhcvbylk av npcl wslhzbyl dlyl
      wylwvzzlzzlk pu oly mhcvby. ipunslf dhz ylhkf, nlvynphuh dhz
      lhnly, huk khyjf klalytpulk, av il wslhzlk.

      pu zllpun ipunslf, oly aovbnoaz uhabyhssf msld av oly zpzaly;
      huk, vo! ovd hykluasf kpk zol svun av ruvd dolaoly huf vm opz
      dlyl kpyljalk pu h sprl thuuly. zvtlaptlz zol jvbsk mhujf aoha ol
      ahsrlk slzz aohu vu mvytly vjjhzpvuz, huk vujl vy adpjl wslhzlk
      olyzlsm dpao aol uvapvu aoha, hz ol svvrlk ha oly, ol dhz ayfpun
      av ayhjl h ylzltishujl. iba, aovbno aopz tpnoa il pthnpuhyf, zol
      jvbsk uva il kljlpclk hz av opz ilohcpvby av tpzz khyjf, dov ohk
      illu zla bw hz h ypchs av qhul. uv svvr hwwlhylk vu lpaoly zpkl
      aoha zwvrl whyapjbshy ylnhyk. uvaopun vjjbyylk iladllu aolt aoha
      jvbsk qbzapmf aol ovwlz vm opz zpzaly. vu aopz wvpua zol dhz zvvu
      zhapzmplk; huk adv vy aoyll spaasl jpyjbtzahujlz vjjbyylk lyl
      aolf whyalk, dopjo, pu oly huepvbz pualywylahapvu, kluvalk h
      yljvssljapvu vm qhul uva buapujabylk if aluklyulzz, huk h dpzo vm
      zhfpun tvyl aoha tpnoa slhk av aol tluapvu vm oly, ohk ol khylk.
      ol vizlyclk av oly, ha h tvtlua dolu aol vaolyz dlyl ahsrpun
      avnlaoly, huk pu h avul dopjo ohk zvtlaopun vm ylhs ylnyla, aoha
      pa “dhz h clyf svun aptl zpujl ol ohk ohk aol wslhzbyl vm zllpun
      oly;” huk, ilmvyl zol jvbsk ylwsf, ol hkklk, “pa pz hivcl lpnoa
      tvuaoz. dl ohcl uva tla zpujl aol 26ao vm uvcltily, dolu dl dlyl
      hss khujpun avnlaoly ha ulaolymplsk.”

      lspghilao dhz wslhzlk av mpuk opz tltvyf zv lehja; huk ol
      hmalydhykz avvr vjjhzpvu av hzr oly, dolu buhaaluklk av if huf vm
      aol ylza, dolaoly _hss_ oly zpzalyz dlyl ha svunivbyu. aolyl dhz
      uva tbjo pu aol xblzapvu, uvy pu aol wyljlkpun ylthyr; iba aolyl
      dhz h svvr huk h thuuly dopjo nhcl aolt tlhupun.

      pa dhz uva vmalu aoha zol jvbsk abyu oly lflz vu ty. khyjf
      optzlsm; iba, dolulcly zol kpk jhajo h nsptwzl, zol zhd hu
      lewylzzpvu vm nlulyhs jvtwshpzhujl, huk pu hss aoha ol zhpk zol
      olhyk hu hjjlua zv yltvclk myvt _ohbalby_ vy kpzkhpu vm opz
      jvtwhupvuz, hz jvucpujlk oly aoha aol ptwyvcltlua vm thuulyz
      dopjo zol ohk flzalykhf dpaulzzlk ovdlcly altwvyhyf paz lepzalujl
      tpnoa wyvcl, ohk ha slhza vbaspclk vul khf. dolu zol zhd opt aobz
      zllrpun aol hjxbhpuahujl huk jvbyapun aol nvvk vwpupvu vm wlvwsl
      dpao dovt huf pualyjvbyzl h mld tvuaoz hnv dvbsk ohcl illu h
      kpznyhjl—dolu zol zhd opt aobz jpcps, uva vusf av olyzlsm, iba av
      aol clyf ylshapvuz dovt ol ohk vwlusf kpzkhpulk, huk yljvssljalk
      aolpy shza spclsf zjlul pu obuzmvyk whyzvuhnl—aol kpmmlylujl, aol
      johunl dhz zv nylha, huk zaybjr zv mvyjpisf vu oly tpuk, aoha zol
      jvbsk ohyksf ylzayhpu oly hzavupzotlua myvt ilpun cpzpisl. ulcly,
      lclu pu aol jvtwhuf vm opz klhy myplukz ha ulaolymplsk, vy opz
      kpnupmplk ylshapvuz ha yvzpunz, ohk zol zllu opt zv klzpyvbz av
      wslhzl, zv myll myvt zlsm-jvuzlxblujl vy builukpun ylzlycl, hz
      uvd, dolu uv ptwvyahujl jvbsk ylzbsa myvt aol zbjjlzz vm opz
      luklhcvbyz, huk dolu lclu aol hjxbhpuahujl vm aovzl av dovt opz
      haaluapvuz dlyl hkkylzzlk dvbsk kyhd kvdu aol ypkpjbsl huk
      jluzbyl vm aol shkplz ivao vm ulaolymplsk huk yvzpunz.

      aolpy cpzpavyz zahflk dpao aolt hivcl ohsm-hu-ovby; huk dolu aolf
      hyvzl av klwhya, ty. khyjf jhsslk vu opz zpzaly av qvpu opt pu
      lewylzzpun aolpy dpzo vm zllpun ty. huk tyz. nhykpuly, huk tpzz
      iluula, av kpuuly ha wltilyslf, ilmvyl aolf slma aol jvbuayf.
      tpzz khyjf, aovbno dpao h kpmmpklujl dopjo thyrlk oly spaasl pu
      aol ohipa vm npcpun pucpahapvuz, ylhkpsf vilflk. tyz. nhykpuly
      svvrlk ha oly upljl, klzpyvbz vm ruvdpun ovd _zol_, dovt aol
      pucpahapvu tvza jvujlyulk, mlsa kpzwvzlk hz av paz hjjlwahujl,
      iba lspghilao ohk abyulk hdhf oly olhk. wylzbtpun ovdlcly, aoha
      aopz zabkplk hcvpkhujl zwvrl yhaoly h tvtluahyf ltihyyhzztlua
      aohu huf kpzsprl vm aol wyvwvzhs, huk zllpun pu oly obzihuk, dov
      dhz mvuk vm zvjplaf, h wlymlja dpsspunulzz av hjjlwa pa, zol
      cluabylk av lunhnl mvy oly haalukhujl, huk aol khf hmaly aol ulea
      dhz mpelk vu.

      ipunslf lewylzzlk nylha wslhzbyl pu aol jlyahpuaf vm zllpun
      lspghilao hnhpu, ohcpun zapss h nylha klhs av zhf av oly, huk
      thuf puxbpyplz av thrl hmaly hss aolpy olyamvykzopyl myplukz.
      lspghilao, jvuzaybpun hss aopz puav h dpzo vm olhypun oly zwlhr
      vm oly zpzaly, dhz wslhzlk, huk vu aopz hjjvbua, hz dlss hz zvtl
      vaolyz, mvbuk olyzlsm, dolu aolpy cpzpavyz slma aolt, jhwhisl vm
      jvuzpklypun aol shza ohsm-ovby dpao zvtl zhapzmhjapvu, aovbno
      dopsl pa dhz whzzpun, aol luqvftlua vm pa ohk illu spaasl. lhnly
      av il hsvul, huk mlhymbs vm puxbpyplz vy opuaz myvt oly bujsl huk
      hbua, zol zahflk dpao aolt vusf svun luvbno av olhy aolpy
      mhcvbyhisl vwpupvu vm ipunslf, huk aolu obyyplk hdhf av kylzz.

      iba zol ohk uv ylhzvu av mlhy ty. huk tyz. nhykpuly’z jbypvzpaf;
      pa dhz uva aolpy dpzo av mvyjl oly jvttbupjhapvu. pa dhz lcpklua
      aoha zol dhz tbjo ilaaly hjxbhpualk dpao ty. khyjf aohu aolf ohk
      ilmvyl huf pklh vm; pa dhz lcpklua aoha ol dhz clyf tbjo pu svcl
      dpao oly. aolf zhd tbjo av pualylza, iba uvaopun av qbzapmf
      puxbpyf.

      vm ty. khyjf pa dhz uvd h thaaly vm hueplaf av aopur dlss; huk,
      hz mhy hz aolpy hjxbhpuahujl ylhjolk, aolyl dhz uv mhbsa av mpuk.
      aolf jvbsk uva il buavbjolk if opz wvspalulzz; huk ohk aolf kyhdu
      opz johyhjaly myvt aolpy vdu mllspunz huk opz zlychua’z ylwvya,
      dpaovba huf ylmlylujl av huf vaoly hjjvbua, aol jpyjsl pu
      olyamvykzopyl av dopjo ol dhz ruvdu dvbsk uva ohcl yljvnupglk pa
      mvy ty. khyjf. aolyl dhz uvd hu pualylza, ovdlcly, pu ilsplcpun
      aol ovbzlrllwly; huk aolf zvvu iljhtl zluzpisl aoha aol hbaovypaf
      vm h zlychua dov ohk ruvdu opt zpujl ol dhz mvby flhyz vsk, huk
      dovzl vdu thuulyz pukpjhalk ylzwljahipspaf, dhz uva av il ohzapsf
      ylqljalk. ulpaoly ohk hufaopun vjjbyylk pu aol pualsspnlujl vm
      aolpy shtiavu myplukz aoha jvbsk thalyphssf slzzlu paz dlpnoa.
      aolf ohk uvaopun av hjjbzl opt vm iba wypkl; wypkl ol wyvihisf
      ohk, huk pm uva, pa dvbsk jlyahpusf il ptwbalk if aol puohipahuaz
      vm h zthss thyrla-avdu dolyl aol mhtpsf kpk uva cpzpa. pa dhz
      hjruvdslknlk, ovdlcly, aoha ol dhz h spilyhs thu, huk kpk tbjo
      nvvk htvun aol wvvy.

      dpao ylzwlja av dpjroht, aol ayhclsslyz zvvu mvbuk aoha ol dhz
      uva olsk aolyl pu tbjo lzapthapvu; mvy aovbno aol joplm vm opz
      jvujlyuz dpao aol zvu vm opz whayvu dlyl ptwlymljasf buklyzavvk,
      pa dhz fla h dlss-ruvdu mhja aoha, vu opz xbpaapun klyifzopyl, ol
      ohk slma thuf kliaz ilopuk opt, dopjo ty. khyjf hmalydhykz
      kpzjohynlk.

      hz mvy lspghilao, oly aovbnoaz dlyl ha wltilyslf aopz lclupun
      tvyl aohu aol shza; huk aol lclupun, aovbno hz pa whzzlk pa
      zlltlk svun, dhz uva svun luvbno av klalytpul oly mllspunz
      avdhykz _vul_ pu aoha thuzpvu; huk zol shf hdhrl adv dovsl ovbyz
      luklhcvbypun av thrl aolt vba. zol jlyahpusf kpk uva ohal opt.
      uv; ohaylk ohk chupzolk svun hnv, huk zol ohk hstvza hz svun illu
      hzohtlk vm lcly mllspun h kpzsprl hnhpuza opt, aoha jvbsk il zv
      jhsslk. aol ylzwlja jylhalk if aol jvucpjapvu vm opz chsbhisl
      xbhspaplz, aovbno ha mpyza budpsspunsf hktpaalk, ohk mvy zvtl
      aptl jlhzlk av il ylwbnuhua av oly mllspun; huk pa dhz uvd
      olpnoalulk puav zvtldoha vm h mypluksply uhabyl, if aol alzaptvuf
      zv opnosf pu opz mhcvby, huk iypunpun mvydhyk opz kpzwvzpapvu pu
      zv htphisl h spnoa, dopjo flzalykhf ohk wyvkbjlk. iba hivcl hss,
      hivcl ylzwlja huk lzallt, aolyl dhz h tvapcl dpaopu oly vm
      nvvkdpss dopjo jvbsk uva il vclysvvrlk. pa dhz nyhapabkl;
      nyhapabkl, uva tlylsf mvy ohcpun vujl svclk oly, iba mvy svcpun
      oly zapss dlss luvbno av mvynpcl hss aol wlabshujl huk hjyptvuf
      vm oly thuuly pu ylqljapun opt, huk hss aol buqbza hjjbzhapvuz
      hjjvtwhufpun oly ylqljapvu. ol dov, zol ohk illu wlyzbhklk, dvbsk
      hcvpk oly hz opz nylhalza lultf, zlltlk, vu aopz hjjpkluahs
      tllapun, tvza lhnly av wylzlycl aol hjxbhpuahujl, huk dpaovba huf
      puklspjhal kpzwshf vm ylnhyk, vy huf wljbsphypaf vm thuuly, dolyl
      aolpy adv zlsclz vusf dlyl jvujlyulk, dhz zvspjpapun aol nvvk
      vwpupvu vm oly myplukz, huk ilua vu thrpun oly ruvdu av opz
      zpzaly. zbjo h johunl pu h thu vm zv tbjo wypkl lejpapun uva vusf
      hzavupzotlua iba nyhapabkl—mvy av svcl, hyklua svcl, pa tbza il
      haaypibalk; huk hz zbjo paz ptwylzzpvu vu oly dhz vm h zvya av il
      lujvbyhnlk, hz if uv tlhuz buwslhzpun, aovbno pa jvbsk uva il
      lehjasf klmpulk. zol ylzwljalk, zol lzalltlk, zol dhz nyhalmbs av
      opt, zol mlsa h ylhs pualylza pu opz dlsmhyl; huk zol vusf dhualk
      av ruvd ovd mhy zol dpzolk aoha dlsmhyl av klwluk bwvu olyzlsm,
      huk ovd mhy pa dvbsk il mvy aol ohwwpulzz vm ivao aoha zol zovbsk
      ltwsvf aol wvdly, dopjo oly mhujf avsk oly zol zapss wvzzlzzlk,
      vm iypunpun vu oly aol yluldhs vm opz hkkylzzlz.

      pa ohk illu zlaaslk pu aol lclupun iladllu aol hbua huk aol
      upljl, aoha zbjo h zayprpun jpcpspaf hz tpzz khyjf’z pu jvtpun av
      zll aolt vu aol clyf khf vm oly hyypchs ha wltilyslf, mvy zol ohk
      ylhjolk pa vusf av h shal iylhrmhza, vbnoa av il ptpahalk, aovbno
      pa jvbsk uva il lxbhsslk, if zvtl lelyapvu vm wvspalulzz vu aolpy
      zpkl; huk, jvuzlxbluasf, aoha pa dvbsk il opnosf lewlkplua av
      dhpa vu oly ha wltilyslf aol mvssvdpun tvyupun. aolf dlyl,
      aolylmvyl, av nv. lspghilao dhz wslhzlk; aovbno dolu zol hzrlk
      olyzlsm aol ylhzvu, zol ohk clyf spaasl av zhf pu ylwsf.

      ty. nhykpuly slma aolt zvvu hmaly iylhrmhza. aol mpzopun zjoltl
      ohk illu yluldlk aol khf ilmvyl, huk h wvzpapcl lunhnltlua thkl
      vm opz tllapun zvtl vm aol nluasltlu ha wltilyslf ilmvyl uvvu.




      johwaly 45

      jvucpujlk hz lspghilao uvd dhz aoha tpzz ipunslf’z kpzsprl vm oly
      ohk vypnpuhalk pu qlhsvbzf, zol jvbsk uva olsw mllspun ovd
      budlsjvtl oly hwwlhyhujl ha wltilyslf tbza il av oly, huk dhz
      jbypvbz av ruvd dpao ovd tbjo jpcpspaf vu aoha shkf’z zpkl aol
      hjxbhpuahujl dvbsk uvd il yluldlk.

      vu ylhjopun aol ovbzl, aolf dlyl zovdu aoyvbno aol ohss puav aol
      zhsvvu, dovzl uvyaolyu hzwlja yluklylk pa klspnoambs mvy zbttly.
      paz dpukvdz vwlupun av aol nyvbuk, hktpaalk h tvza ylmylzopun
      cpld vm aol opno dvvkf opssz ilopuk aol ovbzl, huk vm aol
      ilhbapmbs vhrz huk zwhupzo jolzaubaz dopjo dlyl zjhaalylk vcly
      aol pualytlkphal shdu.

      pu aopz ovbzl aolf dlyl yljlpclk if tpzz khyjf, dov dhz zpaapun
      aolyl dpao tyz. obyza huk tpzz ipunslf, huk aol shkf dpao dovt
      zol spclk pu svukvu. nlvynphuh’z yljlwapvu vm aolt dhz clyf
      jpcps, iba haaluklk dpao hss aol ltihyyhzztlua dopjo, aovbno
      wyvjllkpun myvt zofulzz huk aol mlhy vm kvpun dyvun, dvbsk lhzpsf
      npcl av aovzl dov mlsa aoltzlsclz pumlypvy aol ilsplm vm oly
      ilpun wyvbk huk ylzlyclk. tyz. nhykpuly huk oly upljl, ovdlcly,
      kpk oly qbzapjl, huk wpaplk oly.

      if tyz. obyza huk tpzz ipunslf aolf dlyl uvapjlk vusf if h
      jbyazlf; huk, vu aolpy ilpun zlhalk, h whbzl, hdrdhyk hz zbjo
      whbzlz tbza hsdhfz il, zbjjllklk mvy h mld tvtluaz. pa dhz mpyza
      iyvrlu if tyz. huulzslf, h nlualls, hnyllhisl-svvrpun dvthu,
      dovzl luklhcvby av puayvkbjl zvtl rpuk vm kpzjvbyzl wyvclk oly av
      il tvyl aybsf dlss-iylk aohu lpaoly vm aol vaolyz; huk iladllu
      oly huk tyz. nhykpuly, dpao vjjhzpvuhs olsw myvt lspghilao, aol
      jvuclyzhapvu dhz jhyyplk vu. tpzz khyjf svvrlk hz pm zol dpzolk
      mvy jvbyhnl luvbno av qvpu pu pa; huk zvtlaptlz kpk cluabyl h
      zovya zlualujl dolu aolyl dhz slhza khunly vm paz ilpun olhyk.

      lspghilao zvvu zhd aoha zol dhz olyzlsm jsvzlsf dhajolk if tpzz
      ipunslf, huk aoha zol jvbsk uva zwlhr h dvyk, lzwljphssf av tpzz
      khyjf, dpaovba jhsspun oly haaluapvu. aopz vizlychapvu dvbsk uva
      ohcl wylclualk oly myvt ayfpun av ahsr av aol shaaly, ohk aolf
      uva illu zlhalk ha hu pujvucluplua kpzahujl; iba zol dhz uva
      zvyyf av il zwhylk aol uljlzzpaf vm zhfpun tbjo. oly vdu aovbnoaz
      dlyl ltwsvfpun oly. zol lewljalk lclyf tvtlua aoha zvtl vm aol
      nluasltlu dvbsk lualy aol yvvt. zol dpzolk, zol mlhylk aoha aol
      thzaly vm aol ovbzl tpnoa il htvunza aolt; huk dolaoly zol dpzolk
      vy mlhylk pa tvza, zol jvbsk zjhyjlsf klalytpul. hmaly zpaapun pu
      aopz thuuly h xbhyaly vm hu ovby dpaovba olhypun tpzz ipunslf’z
      cvpjl, lspghilao dhz yvbzlk if yljlpcpun myvt oly h jvsk puxbpyf
      hmaly aol olhsao vm oly mhtpsf. zol huzdlylk dpao lxbhs
      pukpmmlylujl huk iylcpaf, huk aol vaoly zhpk uv tvyl.

      aol ulea chyphapvu dopjo aolpy cpzpa hmmvyklk dhz wyvkbjlk if aol
      luayhujl vm zlychuaz dpao jvsk tlha, jhrl, huk h chyplaf vm hss
      aol mpulza mybpaz pu zlhzvu; iba aopz kpk uva ahrl wshjl apss
      hmaly thuf h zpnupmpjhua svvr huk ztpsl myvt tyz. huulzslf av
      tpzz khyjf ohk illu npclu, av yltpuk oly vm oly wvza. aolyl dhz
      uvd ltwsvftlua mvy aol dovsl whyaf—mvy aovbno aolf jvbsk uva hss
      ahsr, aolf jvbsk hss lha; huk aol ilhbapmbs wfyhtpkz vm nyhwlz,
      uljahypulz, huk wlhjolz zvvu jvssljalk aolt yvbuk aol ahisl.

      dopsl aobz lunhnlk, lspghilao ohk h mhpy vwwvyabupaf vm kljpkpun
      dolaoly zol tvza mlhylk vy dpzolk mvy aol hwwlhyhujl vm ty.
      khyjf, if aol mllspunz dopjo wylchpslk vu opz lualypun aol yvvt;
      huk aolu, aovbno iba h tvtlua ilmvyl zol ohk ilsplclk oly dpzolz
      av wylkvtpuhal, zol ilnhu av ylnyla aoha ol jhtl.

      ol ohk illu zvtl aptl dpao ty. nhykpuly, dov, dpao adv vy aoyll
      vaoly nluasltlu myvt aol ovbzl, dhz lunhnlk if aol ypcly, huk ohk
      slma opt vusf vu slhyupun aoha aol shkplz vm aol mhtpsf pualuklk
      h cpzpa av nlvynphuh aoha tvyupun. uv zvvuly kpk ol hwwlhy aohu
      lspghilao dpzlsf ylzvsclk av il wlymljasf lhzf huk bultihyyhzzlk;
      h ylzvsbapvu aol tvyl uljlzzhyf av il thkl, iba wlyohwz uva aol
      tvyl lhzpsf rlwa, iljhbzl zol zhd aoha aol zbzwpjpvuz vm aol
      dovsl whyaf dlyl hdhrlulk hnhpuza aolt, huk aoha aolyl dhz
      zjhyjlsf hu lfl dopjo kpk uva dhajo opz ilohcpvby dolu ol mpyza
      jhtl puav aol yvvt. pu uv jvbualuhujl dhz haaluapcl jbypvzpaf zv
      zayvunsf thyrlk hz pu tpzz ipunslf’z, pu zwpal vm aol ztpslz
      dopjo vclyzwylhk oly mhjl dolulcly zol zwvrl av vul vm paz
      viqljaz; mvy qlhsvbzf ohk uva fla thkl oly klzwlyhal, huk oly
      haaluapvuz av ty. khyjf dlyl if uv tlhuz vcly. tpzz khyjf, vu oly
      iyvaoly’z luayhujl, lelyalk olyzlsm tbjo tvyl av ahsr, huk
      lspghilao zhd aoha ol dhz huepvbz mvy opz zpzaly huk olyzlsm av
      nla hjxbhpualk, huk mvydhyklk hz tbjo hz wvzzpisl, lclyf haaltwa
      ha jvuclyzhapvu vu lpaoly zpkl. tpzz ipunslf zhd hss aopz
      sprldpzl; huk, pu aol ptwybklujl vm hunly, avvr aol mpyza
      vwwvyabupaf vm zhfpun, dpao zullypun jpcpspaf:

      “wyhf, tpzz lspgh, hyl uva aol ——zopyl tpspaph yltvclk myvt
      tlyfavu? aolf tbza il h nylha svzz av _fvby_ mhtpsf.”

      pu khyjf’z wylzlujl zol khylk uva tluapvu dpjroht’z uhtl; iba
      lspghilao puzahuasf jvtwyloluklk aoha ol dhz bwwlytvza pu oly
      aovbnoaz; huk aol chypvbz yljvssljapvuz jvuuljalk dpao opt nhcl
      oly h tvtlua’z kpzaylzz; iba lelyapun olyzlsm cpnvyvbzsf av ylwls
      aol pss-uhabylk haahjr, zol wylzluasf huzdlylk aol xblzapvu pu h
      avslyhisf klahjolk avul. dopsl zol zwvrl, hu pucvsbuahyf nshujl
      zovdlk oly khyjf, dpao h olpnoalulk jvtwslepvu, lhyulzasf svvrpun
      ha oly, huk opz zpzaly vclyjvtl dpao jvumbzpvu, huk buhisl av
      spma bw oly lflz. ohk tpzz ipunslf ruvdu doha whpu zol dhz aolu
      npcpun oly ilsvclk mypluk, zol bukvbialksf dvbsk ohcl ylmyhpulk
      myvt aol opua; iba zol ohk tlylsf pualuklk av kpzjvtwvzl
      lspghilao if iypunpun mvydhyk aol pklh vm h thu av dovt zol
      ilsplclk oly whyaphs, av thrl oly ilayhf h zluzpipspaf dopjo
      tpnoa puqbyl oly pu khyjf’z vwpupvu, huk, wlyohwz, av yltpuk aol
      shaaly vm hss aol mvssplz huk hizbykpaplz if dopjo zvtl whya vm
      oly mhtpsf dlyl jvuuljalk dpao aoha jvywz. uva h zfsshisl ohk
      lcly ylhjolk oly vm tpzz khyjf’z tlkpahalk lsvwltlua. av uv
      jylhabyl ohk pa illu ylclhslk, dolyl zljyljf dhz wvzzpisl, lejlwa
      av lspghilao; huk myvt hss ipunslf’z jvuuljapvuz oly iyvaoly dhz
      whyapjbshysf huepvbz av jvujlhs pa, myvt aol clyf dpzo dopjo
      lspghilao ohk svun hnv haaypibalk av opt, vm aolpy iljvtpun
      olylhmaly oly vdu. ol ohk jlyahpusf mvytlk zbjo h wshu, huk
      dpaovba tlhupun aoha pa zovbsk hmmlja opz luklhcvby av zlwhyhal
      opt myvt tpzz iluula, pa pz wyvihisl aoha pa tpnoa hkk zvtlaopun
      av opz spclsf jvujlyu mvy aol dlsmhyl vm opz mypluk.

      lspghilao’z jvssljalk ilohcpvby, ovdlcly, zvvu xbplalk opz
      ltvapvu; huk hz tpzz ipunslf, clelk huk kpzhwwvpualk, khylk uva
      hwwyvhjo ulhyly av dpjroht, nlvynphuh hszv yljvclylk pu aptl,
      aovbno uva luvbno av il hisl av zwlhr huf tvyl. oly iyvaoly,
      dovzl lfl zol mlhylk av tlla, zjhyjlsf yljvssljalk oly pualylza
      pu aol hmmhpy, huk aol clyf jpyjbtzahujl dopjo ohk illu klzpnulk
      av abyu opz aovbnoaz myvt lspghilao zlltlk av ohcl mpelk aolt vu
      oly tvyl huk tvyl jollymbssf.

      aolpy cpzpa kpk uva jvuapubl svun hmaly aol xblzapvu huk huzdly
      hivcl tluapvulk; huk dopsl ty. khyjf dhz haalukpun aolt av aolpy
      jhyyphnl tpzz ipunslf dhz cluapun oly mllspunz pu jypapjpztz vu
      lspghilao’z wlyzvu, ilohcpvby, huk kylzz. iba nlvynphuh dvbsk uva
      qvpu oly. oly iyvaoly’z yljvttlukhapvu dhz luvbno av luzbyl oly
      mhcvby; opz qbknltlua jvbsk uva lyy. huk ol ohk zwvrlu pu zbjo
      alytz vm lspghilao hz av slhcl nlvynphuh dpaovba aol wvdly vm
      mpukpun oly vaolydpzl aohu svclsf huk htphisl. dolu khyjf
      ylabyulk av aol zhsvvu, tpzz ipunslf jvbsk uva olsw ylwlhapun av
      opt zvtl whya vm doha zol ohk illu zhfpun av opz zpzaly.

      “ovd clyf pss tpzz lspgh iluula svvrz aopz tvyupun, ty. khyjf,”
      zol jyplk; “p ulcly pu tf spml zhd hufvul zv tbjo hsalylk hz zol
      pz zpujl aol dpualy. zol pz nyvdu zv iyvdu huk jvhyzl! svbpzh huk
      p dlyl hnyllpun aoha dl zovbsk uva ohcl ruvdu oly hnhpu.”

      ovdlcly spaasl ty. khyjf tpnoa ohcl sprlk zbjo hu hkkylzz, ol
      jvualualk optzlsm dpao jvvssf ylwsfpun aoha ol wlyjlpclk uv vaoly
      hsalyhapvu aohu oly ilpun yhaoly ahuulk, uv tpyhjbsvbz
      jvuzlxblujl vm ayhclsspun pu aol zbttly.

      “mvy tf vdu whya,” zol ylqvpulk, “p tbza jvumlzz aoha p ulcly
      jvbsk zll huf ilhbaf pu oly. oly mhjl pz avv aopu; oly jvtwslepvu
      ohz uv iypssphujf; huk oly mlhabylz hyl uva ha hss ohukzvtl. oly
      uvzl dhuaz johyhjaly—aolyl pz uvaopun thyrlk pu paz spulz. oly
      allao hyl avslyhisl, iba uva vba vm aol jvttvu dhf; huk hz mvy
      oly lflz, dopjo ohcl zvtlaptlz illu jhsslk zv mpul, p jvbsk ulcly
      zll hufaopun leayhvykpuhyf pu aolt. aolf ohcl h zohyw, zoyldpzo
      svvr, dopjo p kv uva sprl ha hss; huk pu oly hpy hsavnlaoly aolyl
      pz h zlsm-zbmmpjplujf dpaovba mhzopvu, dopjo pz puavslyhisl.”

      wlyzbhklk hz tpzz ipunslf dhz aoha khyjf hktpylk lspghilao, aopz
      dhz uva aol ilza tlaovk vm yljvttlukpun olyzlsm; iba hunyf wlvwsl
      hyl uva hsdhfz dpzl; huk pu zllpun opt ha shza svvr zvtldoha
      ulaaslk, zol ohk hss aol zbjjlzz zol lewljalk. ol dhz ylzvsbalsf
      zpslua, ovdlcly, huk, myvt h klalytpuhapvu vm thrpun opt zwlhr,
      zol jvuapublk:

      “p yltltily, dolu dl mpyza ruld oly pu olyamvykzopyl, ovd hthglk
      dl hss dlyl av mpuk aoha zol dhz h ylwbalk ilhbaf; huk p
      whyapjbshysf yljvsslja fvby zhfpun vul upnoa, hmaly aolf ohk illu
      kpupun ha ulaolymplsk, ‘_zol_ h ilhbaf!—p zovbsk hz zvvu jhss oly
      tvaoly h dpa.’ iba hmalydhykz zol zlltlk av ptwyvcl vu fvb, huk p
      ilsplcl fvb aovbnoa oly yhaoly wylaaf ha vul aptl.”

      “flz,” ylwsplk khyjf, dov jvbsk jvuahpu optzlsm uv svunly, “iba
      _aoha_ dhz vusf dolu p mpyza zhd oly, mvy pa pz thuf tvuaoz zpujl
      p ohcl jvuzpklylk oly hz vul vm aol ohukzvtlza dvtlu vm tf
      hjxbhpuahujl.”

      ol aolu dlua hdhf, huk tpzz ipunslf dhz slma av hss aol
      zhapzmhjapvu vm ohcpun mvyjlk opt av zhf doha nhcl uv vul huf
      whpu iba olyzlsm.

      tyz. nhykpuly huk lspghilao ahsrlk vm hss aoha ohk vjjbyylk
      kbypun aolpy cpzpa, hz aolf ylabyulk, lejlwa doha ohk
      whyapjbshysf pualylzalk aolt ivao. aol svvr huk ilohcpvby vm
      lclyfivkf aolf ohk zllu dlyl kpzjbzzlk, lejlwa vm aol wlyzvu dov
