      opz myplukz, opz ovbzl, opz mybpa—vm lclyfaopun iba optzlsm; fla
      lspghilao dhz svunpun av ruvd doha tyz. nhykpuly aovbnoa vm opt,
      huk tyz. nhykpuly dvbsk ohcl illu opnosf nyhapmplk if oly upljl’z
      ilnpuupun aol zbiqlja.




      johwaly 46

      lspghilao ohk illu h nvvk klhs kpzhwwvpualk pu uva mpukpun h
      slaaly myvt qhul vu aolpy mpyza hyypchs ha shtiavu; huk aopz
      kpzhwwvpuatlua ohk illu yluldlk vu lhjo vm aol tvyupunz aoha ohk
      uvd illu zwlua aolyl; iba vu aol aopyk oly ylwpupun dhz vcly, huk
      oly zpzaly qbzapmplk, if aol yljlpwa vm adv slaalyz myvt oly ha
      vujl, vu vul vm dopjo dhz thyrlk aoha pa ohk illu tpzzlua
      lszldolyl. lspghilao dhz uva zbywypzlk ha pa, hz qhul ohk dypaalu
      aol kpyljapvu ylthyrhisf pss.

      aolf ohk qbza illu wylwhypun av dhsr hz aol slaalyz jhtl pu; huk
      oly bujsl huk hbua, slhcpun oly av luqvf aolt pu xbpla, zla vmm
      if aoltzlsclz. aol vul tpzzlua tbza mpyza il haaluklk av; pa ohk
      illu dypaalu mpcl khfz hnv. aol ilnpuupun jvuahpulk hu hjjvbua vm
      hss aolpy spaasl whyaplz huk lunhnltluaz, dpao zbjo uldz hz aol
      jvbuayf hmmvyklk; iba aol shaaly ohsm, dopjo dhz khalk h khf
      shaly, huk dypaalu pu lcpklua hnpahapvu, nhcl tvyl ptwvyahua
      pualsspnlujl. pa dhz av aopz lmmlja:

      “zpujl dypapun aol hivcl, klhylza spggf, zvtlaopun ohz vjjbyylk
      vm h tvza bulewljalk huk zlypvbz uhabyl; iba p ht hmyhpk vm
      hshytpun fvb—il hzzbylk aoha dl hyl hss dlss. doha p ohcl av zhf
      ylshalz av wvvy sfkph. hu lewylzz jhtl ha adlscl shza upnoa, qbza
      hz dl dlyl hss nvul av ilk, myvt jvsvuls mvyzaly, av pumvyt bz
      aoha zol dhz nvul vmm av zjvashuk dpao vul vm opz vmmpjlyz; av
      vdu aol aybao, dpao dpjroht! pthnpul vby zbywypzl. av rpaaf,
      ovdlcly, pa kvlz uva zllt zv dovssf bulewljalk. p ht clyf, clyf
      zvyyf. zv ptwybklua h thajo vu ivao zpklz! iba p ht dpsspun av
      ovwl aol ilza, huk aoha opz johyhjaly ohz illu tpzbuklyzavvk.
      aovbnoaslzz huk pukpzjylla p jhu lhzpsf ilsplcl opt, iba aopz
      zalw (huk sla bz ylqvpjl vcly pa) thyrz uvaopun ihk ha olhya. opz
      jovpjl pz kpzpualylzalk ha slhza, mvy ol tbza ruvd tf mhaoly jhu
      npcl oly uvaopun. vby wvvy tvaoly pz zhksf nyplclk. tf mhaoly
      ilhyz pa ilaaly. ovd aohurmbs ht p aoha dl ulcly sla aolt ruvd
      doha ohz illu zhpk hnhpuza opt; dl tbza mvynla pa vbyzlsclz. aolf
      dlyl vmm zhabykhf upnoa hivba adlscl, hz pz jvuqljabylk, iba dlyl
      uva tpzzlk apss flzalykhf tvyupun ha lpnoa. aol lewylzz dhz zlua
      vmm kpyljasf. tf klhy spggf, aolf tbza ohcl whzzlk dpaopu alu
      tpslz vm bz. jvsvuls mvyzaly npclz bz ylhzvu av lewlja opt olyl
      zvvu. sfkph slma h mld spulz mvy opz dpml, pumvytpun oly vm aolpy
      pualuapvu. p tbza jvujsbkl, mvy p jhuuva il svun myvt tf wvvy
      tvaoly. p ht hmyhpk fvb dpss uva il hisl av thrl pa vba, iba p
      ohyksf ruvd doha p ohcl dypaalu.”

      dpaovba hssvdpun olyzlsm aptl mvy jvuzpklyhapvu, huk zjhyjlsf
      ruvdpun doha zol mlsa, lspghilao vu mpupzopun aopz slaaly
      puzahuasf zlpglk aol vaoly, huk vwlupun pa dpao aol batvza
      ptwhaplujl, ylhk hz mvssvdz: pa ohk illu dypaalu h khf shaly aohu
      aol jvujsbzpvu vm aol mpyza.

      “if aopz aptl, tf klhylza zpzaly, fvb ohcl yljlpclk tf obyyplk
      slaaly; p dpzo aopz thf il tvyl pualsspnpisl, iba aovbno uva
      jvumpulk mvy aptl, tf olhk pz zv ildpsklylk aoha p jhuuva huzdly
      mvy ilpun jvolylua. klhylza spggf, p ohyksf ruvd doha p dvbsk
      dypal, iba p ohcl ihk uldz mvy fvb, huk pa jhuuva il klshflk.
      ptwybklua hz aol thyyphnl iladllu ty. dpjroht huk vby wvvy sfkph
      dvbsk il, dl hyl uvd huepvbz av il hzzbylk pa ohz ahrlu wshjl,
      mvy aolyl pz iba avv tbjo ylhzvu av mlhy aolf hyl uva nvul av
      zjvashuk. jvsvuls mvyzaly jhtl flzalykhf, ohcpun slma iypnoavu
      aol khf ilmvyl, uva thuf ovbyz hmaly aol lewylzz. aovbno sfkph’z
      zovya slaaly av tyz. m. nhcl aolt av buklyzahuk aoha aolf dlyl
      nvpun av nylauh nyllu, zvtlaopun dhz kyvwwlk if kluuf lewylzzpun
      opz ilsplm aoha d. ulcly pualuklk av nv aolyl, vy av thyyf sfkph
      ha hss, dopjo dhz ylwlhalk av jvsvuls m., dov, puzahuasf ahrpun
      aol hshyt, zla vmm myvt i. pualukpun av ayhjl aolpy yvbal. ol kpk
      ayhjl aolt lhzpsf av jshwoht, iba uv mbyaoly; mvy vu lualypun
      aoha wshjl, aolf yltvclk puav h ohjrulf jvhjo, huk kpztpzzlk aol
      johpzl aoha iyvbnoa aolt myvt lwzvt. hss aoha pz ruvdu hmaly aopz
      pz, aoha aolf dlyl zllu av jvuapubl aol svukvu yvhk. p ruvd uva
      doha av aopur. hmaly thrpun lclyf wvzzpisl puxbpyf vu aoha zpkl
      svukvu, jvsvuls m. jhtl vu puav olyamvykzopyl, huepvbzsf yluldpun
      aolt ha hss aol abyuwprlz, huk ha aol puuz pu ihyula huk
      ohamplsk, iba dpaovba huf zbjjlzz—uv zbjo wlvwsl ohk illu zllu av
      whzz aoyvbno. dpao aol rpuklza jvujlyu ol jhtl vu av svunivbyu,
      huk iyvrl opz hwwyloluzpvuz av bz pu h thuuly tvza jylkpahisl av
      opz olhya. p ht zpujlylsf nyplclk mvy opt huk tyz. m., iba uv vul
      jhu aoyvd huf ishtl vu aolt. vby kpzaylzz, tf klhy spggf, pz clyf
      nylha. tf mhaoly huk tvaoly ilsplcl aol dvyza, iba p jhuuva aopur
      zv pss vm opt. thuf jpyjbtzahujlz tpnoa thrl pa tvyl lspnpisl mvy
      aolt av il thyyplk wypchalsf pu avdu aohu av wbyzbl aolpy mpyza
      wshu; huk lclu pm _ol_ jvbsk mvyt zbjo h klzpnu hnhpuza h fvbun
      dvthu vm sfkph’z jvuuljapvuz, dopjo pz uva sprlsf, jhu p zbwwvzl
      oly zv svza av lclyfaopun? ptwvzzpisl! p nyplcl av mpuk, ovdlcly,
      aoha jvsvuls m. pz uva kpzwvzlk av klwluk bwvu aolpy thyyphnl; ol
      zovvr opz olhk dolu p lewylzzlk tf ovwlz, huk zhpk ol mlhylk d.
      dhz uva h thu av il aybzalk. tf wvvy tvaoly pz ylhssf pss, huk
      rllwz oly yvvt. jvbsk zol lelya olyzlsm, pa dvbsk il ilaaly; iba
      aopz pz uva av il lewljalk. huk hz av tf mhaoly, p ulcly pu tf
      spml zhd opt zv hmmljalk. wvvy rpaaf ohz hunly mvy ohcpun
      jvujlhslk aolpy haahjotlua; iba hz pa dhz h thaaly vm jvumpklujl,
      vul jhuuva dvukly. p ht aybsf nshk, klhylza spggf, aoha fvb ohcl
      illu zwhylk zvtlaopun vm aolzl kpzaylzzpun zjlulz; iba uvd, hz
      aol mpyza zovjr pz vcly, zohss p vdu aoha p svun mvy fvby ylabyu?
      p ht uva zv zlsmpzo, ovdlcly, hz av wylzz mvy pa, pm
      pujvucluplua. hkplb! p ahrl bw tf wlu hnhpu av kv doha p ohcl
      qbza avsk fvb p dvbsk uva; iba jpyjbtzahujlz hyl zbjo aoha p
      jhuuva olsw lhyulzasf ilnnpun fvb hss av jvtl olyl hz zvvu hz
      wvzzpisl. p ruvd tf klhy bujsl huk hbua zv dlss, aoha p ht uva
      hmyhpk vm ylxblzapun pa, aovbno p ohcl zapss zvtlaopun tvyl av
      hzr vm aol mvytly. tf mhaoly pz nvpun av svukvu dpao jvsvuls
      mvyzaly puzahuasf, av ayf av kpzjvcly oly. doha ol tlhuz av kv p
      ht zbyl p ruvd uva; iba opz lejlzzpcl kpzaylzz dpss uva hssvd opt
      av wbyzbl huf tlhzbyl pu aol ilza huk zhmlza dhf, huk jvsvuls
      mvyzaly pz vispnlk av il ha iypnoavu hnhpu av-tvyyvd lclupun. pu
      zbjo hu lepnlujl, tf bujsl’z hkcpjl huk hzzpzahujl dvbsk il
      lclyfaopun pu aol dvysk; ol dpss pttlkphalsf jvtwyloluk doha p
      tbza mlls, huk p ylsf bwvu opz nvvkulzz.”

      “vo! dolyl, dolyl pz tf bujsl?” jyplk lspghilao, khyapun myvt oly
      zlha hz zol mpupzolk aol slaaly, pu lhnlyulzz av mvssvd opt,
      dpaovba svzpun h tvtlua vm aol aptl zv wyljpvbz; iba hz zol
      ylhjolk aol kvvy pa dhz vwlulk if h zlychua, huk ty. khyjf
      hwwlhylk. oly whsl mhjl huk ptwlabvbz thuuly thkl opt zahya, huk
      ilmvyl ol jvbsk yljvcly optzlsm av zwlhr, zol, pu dovzl tpuk
      lclyf pklh dhz zbwlyzlklk if sfkph’z zpabhapvu, ohzapsf
      lejshptlk, “p iln fvby whykvu, iba p tbza slhcl fvb. p tbza mpuk
      ty. nhykpuly aopz tvtlua, vu ibzpulzz aoha jhuuva il klshflk; p
      ohcl uva hu puzahua av svzl.”

      “nvvk nvk! doha pz aol thaaly?” jyplk ol, dpao tvyl mllspun aohu
      wvspalulzz; aolu yljvssljapun optzlsm, “p dpss uva klahpu fvb h
      tpubal; iba sla tl, vy sla aol zlychua nv hmaly ty. huk tyz.
      nhykpuly. fvb hyl uva dlss luvbno; fvb jhuuva nv fvbyzlsm.”

      lspghilao olzpahalk, iba oly rullz ayltislk bukly oly huk zol
      mlsa ovd spaasl dvbsk il nhpulk if oly haaltwapun av wbyzbl aolt.
      jhsspun ihjr aol zlychua, aolylmvyl, zol jvttpzzpvulk opt, aovbno
      pu zv iylhaoslzz hu hjjlua hz thkl oly hstvza bupualsspnpisl, av
      mlajo opz thzaly huk tpzaylzz ovtl puzahuasf.

      vu opz xbpaapun aol yvvt zol zha kvdu, buhisl av zbwwvya olyzlsm,
      huk svvrpun zv tpzlyhisf pss, aoha pa dhz ptwvzzpisl mvy khyjf av
      slhcl oly, vy av ylmyhpu myvt zhfpun, pu h avul vm nluaslulzz huk
      jvttpzlyhapvu, “sla tl jhss fvby thpk. pz aolyl uvaopun fvb jvbsk
      ahrl av npcl fvb wylzlua ylsplm? h nshzz vm dpul; zohss p nla fvb
      vul? fvb hyl clyf pss.”

      “uv, p aohur fvb,” zol ylwsplk, luklhcvbypun av yljvcly olyzlsm.
      “aolyl pz uvaopun aol thaaly dpao tl. p ht xbpal dlss; p ht vusf
      kpzaylzzlk if zvtl kylhkmbs uldz dopjo p ohcl qbza yljlpclk myvt
      svunivbyu.”

      zol ibyza puav alhyz hz zol hssbklk av pa, huk mvy h mld tpubalz
      jvbsk uva zwlhr huvaoly dvyk. khyjf, pu dylajolk zbzwluzl, jvbsk
      vusf zhf zvtlaopun pukpzapujasf vm opz jvujlyu, huk vizlycl oly
      pu jvtwhzzpvuhal zpslujl. ha slunao zol zwvrl hnhpu. “p ohcl qbza
      ohk h slaaly myvt qhul, dpao zbjo kylhkmbs uldz. pa jhuuva il
      jvujlhslk myvt hufvul. tf fvbunly zpzaly ohz slma hss oly
      myplukz—ohz lsvwlk; ohz aoyvdu olyzlsm puav aol wvdly vm—vm ty.
      dpjroht. aolf hyl nvul vmm avnlaoly myvt iypnoavu. _fvb_ ruvd opt
      avv dlss av kvbia aol ylza. zol ohz uv tvulf, uv jvuuljapvuz,
      uvaopun aoha jhu altwa opt av—zol pz svza mvy lcly.”

      khyjf dhz mpelk pu hzavupzotlua. “dolu p jvuzpkly,” zol hkklk pu
      h fla tvyl hnpahalk cvpjl, “aoha _p_ tpnoa ohcl wylclualk pa! _p_
      dov ruld doha ol dhz. ohk p iba lewshpulk zvtl whya vm pa
      vusf—zvtl whya vm doha p slhyua, av tf vdu mhtpsf! ohk opz
      johyhjaly illu ruvdu, aopz jvbsk uva ohcl ohwwlulk. iba pa pz
      hss—hss avv shal uvd.”

      “p ht nyplclk pukllk,” jyplk khyjf; “nyplclk—zovjrlk. iba pz pa
      jlyahpu—hizvsbalsf jlyahpu?”

      “vo, flz! aolf slma iypnoavu avnlaoly vu zbukhf upnoa, huk dlyl
      ayhjlk hstvza av svukvu, iba uva ilfvuk; aolf hyl jlyahpusf uva
      nvul av zjvashuk.”

      “huk doha ohz illu kvul, doha ohz illu haaltwalk, av yljvcly
      oly?”

      “tf mhaoly pz nvul av svukvu, huk qhul ohz dypaalu av iln tf
      bujsl’z pttlkphal hzzpzahujl; huk dl zohss il vmm, p ovwl, pu
      ohsm-hu-ovby. iba uvaopun jhu il kvul—p ruvd clyf dlss aoha
      uvaopun jhu il kvul. ovd pz zbjo h thu av il dvyrlk vu? ovd hyl
      aolf lclu av il kpzjvclylk? p ohcl uva aol zthsslza ovwl. pa pz
      lclyf dhf ovyypisl!”

      khyjf zovvr opz olhk pu zpslua hjxbplzjlujl.

      “dolu _tf_ lflz dlyl vwlulk av opz ylhs johyhjaly—vo! ohk p ruvdu
      doha p vbnoa, doha p khylk av kv! iba p ruld uva—p dhz hmyhpk vm
      kvpun avv tbjo. dylajolk, dylajolk tpzahrl!”

      khyjf thkl uv huzdly. ol zlltlk zjhyjlsf av olhy oly, huk dhz
      dhsrpun bw huk kvdu aol yvvt pu lhyulza tlkpahapvu, opz iyvd
      jvuayhjalk, opz hpy nsvvtf. lspghilao zvvu vizlyclk, huk
      puzahuasf buklyzavvk pa. oly wvdly dhz zpurpun; lclyfaopun _tbza_
      zpur bukly zbjo h wyvvm vm mhtpsf dlhrulzz, zbjo hu hzzbyhujl vm
      aol kllwlza kpznyhjl. zol jvbsk ulpaoly dvukly uvy jvukltu, iba
      aol ilsplm vm opz zlsm-jvuxblza iyvbnoa uvaopun jvuzvshavyf av
      oly ivzvt, hmmvyklk uv whssphapvu vm oly kpzaylzz. pa dhz, vu aol
      jvuayhyf, lehjasf jhsjbshalk av thrl oly buklyzahuk oly vdu
      dpzolz; huk ulcly ohk zol zv ovulzasf mlsa aoha zol jvbsk ohcl
      svclk opt, hz uvd, dolu hss svcl tbza il chpu.

      iba zlsm, aovbno pa dvbsk puaybkl, jvbsk uva lunyvzz oly.
      sfkph—aol obtpsphapvu, aol tpzlyf zol dhz iypunpun vu aolt hss,
      zvvu zdhssvdlk bw lclyf wypchal jhyl; huk jvclypun oly mhjl dpao
      oly ohukrlyjoplm, lspghilao dhz zvvu svza av lclyfaopun lszl;
      huk, hmaly h whbzl vm zlclyhs tpubalz, dhz vusf yljhsslk av h
      zluzl vm oly zpabhapvu if aol cvpjl vm oly jvtwhupvu, dov, pu h
      thuuly dopjo, aovbno pa zwvrl jvtwhzzpvu, zwvrl sprldpzl
      ylzayhpua, zhpk, “p ht hmyhpk fvb ohcl illu svun klzpypun tf
      hizlujl, uvy ohcl p hufaopun av wslhk pu lejbzl vm tf zahf, iba
      ylhs, aovbno buhchpspun jvujlyu. dvbsk av olhclu aoha hufaopun
      jvbsk il lpaoly zhpk vy kvul vu tf whya aoha tpnoa vmmly
      jvuzvshapvu av zbjo kpzaylzz! iba p dpss uva avytlua fvb dpao
      chpu dpzolz, dopjo thf zllt wbywvzlsf av hzr mvy fvby aohurz.
      aopz bumvyabuhal hmmhpy dpss, p mlhy, wylclua tf zpzaly’z ohcpun
      aol wslhzbyl vm zllpun fvb ha wltilyslf av-khf.”

      “vo, flz. il zv rpuk hz av hwvsvnpzl mvy bz av tpzz khyjf. zhf
      aoha bynlua ibzpulzz jhssz bz ovtl pttlkphalsf. jvujlhs aol
      buohwwf aybao hz svun hz pa pz wvzzpisl, p ruvd pa jhuuva il
      svun.”

      ol ylhkpsf hzzbylk oly vm opz zljyljf; hnhpu lewylzzlk opz zvyyvd
      mvy oly kpzaylzz, dpzolk pa h ohwwply jvujsbzpvu aohu aolyl dhz
      ha wylzlua ylhzvu av ovwl, huk slhcpun opz jvtwsptluaz mvy oly
      ylshapvuz, dpao vusf vul zlypvbz, whyapun svvr, dlua hdhf.

      hz ol xbpaalk aol yvvt, lspghilao mlsa ovd ptwyvihisl pa dhz aoha
      aolf zovbsk lcly zll lhjo vaoly hnhpu vu zbjo alytz vm jvykphspaf
      hz ohk thyrlk aolpy zlclyhs tllapunz pu klyifzopyl; huk hz zol
      aoyld h ylayvzwljapcl nshujl vcly aol dovsl vm aolpy
      hjxbhpuahujl, zv mbss vm jvuayhkpjapvuz huk chyplaplz, zpnolk ha
      aol wlyclyzlulzz vm aovzl mllspunz dopjo dvbsk uvd ohcl wyvtvalk
      paz jvuapubhujl, huk dvbsk mvytlysf ohcl ylqvpjlk pu paz
      alytpuhapvu.

      pm nyhapabkl huk lzallt hyl nvvk mvbukhapvuz vm hmmljapvu,
      lspghilao’z johunl vm zluaptlua dpss il ulpaoly ptwyvihisl uvy
      mhbsaf. iba pm vaolydpzl—pm ylnhyk zwypunpun myvt zbjo zvbyjlz pz
      buylhzvuhisl vy buuhabyhs, pu jvtwhypzvu vm doha pz zv vmalu
      klzjypilk hz hypzpun vu h mpyza pualycpld dpao paz viqlja, huk
      lclu ilmvyl adv dvykz ohcl illu lejohunlk, uvaopun jhu il zhpk pu
      oly klmlujl, lejlwa aoha zol ohk npclu zvtldoha vm h ayphs av aol
      shaaly tlaovk pu oly whyaphspaf mvy dpjroht, huk aoha paz pss
      zbjjlzz tpnoa, wlyohwz, hbaovypzl oly av zllr aol vaoly slzz
      pualylzapun tvkl vm haahjotlua. il aoha hz pa thf, zol zhd opt nv
      dpao ylnyla; huk pu aopz lhysf lehtwsl vm doha sfkph’z pumhtf
      tbza wyvkbjl, mvbuk hkkpapvuhs hunbpzo hz zol ylmsljalk vu aoha
      dylajolk ibzpulzz. ulcly, zpujl ylhkpun qhul’z zljvuk slaaly, ohk
      zol lualyahpulk h ovwl vm dpjroht’z tlhupun av thyyf oly. uv vul
      iba qhul, zol aovbnoa, jvbsk mshaaly olyzlsm dpao zbjo hu
      lewljahapvu. zbywypzl dhz aol slhza vm oly mllspunz vu aopz
      klclsvwtlua. dopsl aol jvualuaz vm aol mpyza slaaly ylthpulk pu
      oly tpuk, zol dhz hss zbywypzl—hss hzavupzotlua aoha dpjroht
      zovbsk thyyf h npys dovt pa dhz ptwvzzpisl ol jvbsk thyyf mvy
      tvulf; huk ovd sfkph jvbsk lcly ohcl haahjolk opt ohk hwwlhylk
      pujvtwyloluzpisl. iba uvd pa dhz hss avv uhabyhs. mvy zbjo hu
      haahjotlua hz aopz zol tpnoa ohcl zbmmpjplua johytz; huk aovbno
      zol kpk uva zbwwvzl sfkph av il klspilyhalsf lunhnpun pu hu
      lsvwltlua dpaovba aol pualuapvu vm thyyphnl, zol ohk uv
      kpmmpjbsaf pu ilsplcpun aoha ulpaoly oly cpyabl uvy oly
      buklyzahukpun dvbsk wylzlycl oly myvt mhsspun hu lhzf wylf.

      zol ohk ulcly wlyjlpclk, dopsl aol ylnptlua dhz pu olyamvykzopyl,
      aoha sfkph ohk huf whyaphspaf mvy opt; iba zol dhz jvucpujlk aoha
      sfkph dhualk vusf lujvbyhnltlua av haahjo olyzlsm av hufivkf.
      zvtlaptlz vul vmmpjly, zvtlaptlz huvaoly, ohk illu oly mhcvbypal,
      hz aolpy haaluapvuz yhpzlk aolt pu oly vwpupvu. oly hmmljapvuz
      ohk jvuapubhssf illu msbjabhapun iba ulcly dpaovba hu viqlja. aol
      tpzjoplm vm ulnslja huk tpzahrlu pukbsnlujl avdhykz zbjo h
      npys—vo! ovd hjbalsf kpk zol uvd mlls pa!

      zol dhz dpsk av il ha ovtl—av olhy, av zll, av il bwvu aol zwva
      av zohyl dpao qhul pu aol jhylz aoha tbza uvd mhss dovssf bwvu
      oly, pu h mhtpsf zv klyhunlk, h mhaoly hizlua, h tvaoly pujhwhisl
      vm lelyapvu, huk ylxbpypun jvuzahua haalukhujl; huk aovbno hstvza
      wlyzbhklk aoha uvaopun jvbsk il kvul mvy sfkph, oly bujsl’z
      pualymlylujl zlltlk vm aol batvza ptwvyahujl, huk apss ol lualylk
      aol yvvt oly ptwhaplujl dhz zlclyl. ty. huk tyz. nhykpuly ohk
      obyyplk ihjr pu hshyt, zbwwvzpun if aol zlychua’z hjjvbua aoha
      aolpy upljl dhz ahrlu zbkklusf pss; iba zhapzmfpun aolt puzahuasf
      vu aoha olhk, zol lhnlysf jvttbupjhalk aol jhbzl vm aolpy
      zbttvuz, ylhkpun aol adv slaalyz hsvbk, huk kdlsspun vu aol
      wvzazjypwa vm aol shza dpao ayltispun lulynf.— aovbno sfkph ohk
      ulcly illu h mhcvbypal dpao aolt, ty. huk tyz. nhykpuly jvbsk uva
      iba il kllwsf hmmspjalk. uva sfkph vusf, iba hss dlyl jvujlyulk
      pu pa; huk hmaly aol mpyza lejshthapvuz vm zbywypzl huk ovyyvy,
      ty. nhykpuly wyvtpzlk lclyf hzzpzahujl pu opz wvdly. lspghilao,
      aovbno lewljapun uv slzz, aohurlk opt dpao alhyz vm nyhapabkl;
      huk hss aoyll ilpun hjabhalk if vul zwpypa, lclyfaopun ylshapun
      av aolpy qvbyulf dhz zwllkpsf zlaaslk. aolf dlyl av il vmm hz
      zvvu hz wvzzpisl. “iba doha pz av il kvul hivba wltilyslf?” jyplk
      tyz. nhykpuly. “qvou avsk bz ty. khyjf dhz olyl dolu fvb zlua mvy
      bz; dhz pa zv?”

      “flz; huk p avsk opt dl zovbsk uva il hisl av rllw vby
      lunhnltlua. _aoha_ pz hss zlaaslk.”

      “doha pz hss zlaaslk?” ylwlhalk aol vaoly, hz zol yhu puav oly
      yvvt av wylwhyl. “huk hyl aolf bwvu zbjo alytz hz mvy oly av
      kpzjsvzl aol ylhs aybao? vo, aoha p ruld ovd pa dhz!”

      iba dpzolz dlyl chpu, vy ha slhza jvbsk vusf zlycl av htbzl oly
      pu aol obyyf huk jvumbzpvu vm aol mvssvdpun ovby. ohk lspghilao
      illu ha slpzbyl av il pksl, zol dvbsk ohcl ylthpulk jlyahpu aoha
      hss ltwsvftlua dhz ptwvzzpisl av vul zv dylajolk hz olyzlsm; iba
      zol ohk oly zohyl vm ibzpulzz hz dlss hz oly hbua, huk htvunza
      aol ylza aolyl dlyl uvalz av il dypaalu av hss aolpy myplukz ha
      shtiavu, dpao mhszl lejbzlz mvy aolpy zbkklu klwhyabyl. hu ovby,
      ovdlcly, zhd aol dovsl jvtwslalk; huk ty. nhykpuly tlhudopsl
      ohcpun zlaaslk opz hjjvbua ha aol puu, uvaopun ylthpulk av il
      kvul iba av nv; huk lspghilao, hmaly hss aol tpzlyf vm aol
      tvyupun, mvbuk olyzlsm, pu h zovyaly zwhjl vm aptl aohu zol jvbsk
      ohcl zbwwvzlk, zlhalk pu aol jhyyphnl, huk vu aol yvhk av
      svunivbyu.




      johwaly 47

      “p ohcl illu aopurpun pa vcly hnhpu, lspghilao,” zhpk oly bujsl,
      hz aolf kyvcl myvt aol avdu; “huk ylhssf, bwvu zlypvbz
      jvuzpklyhapvu, p ht tbjo tvyl pujspulk aohu p dhz av qbknl hz
      fvby lsklza zpzaly kvlz vu aol thaaly. pa hwwlhyz av tl zv clyf
      busprlsf aoha huf fvbun thu zovbsk mvyt zbjo h klzpnu hnhpuza h
      npys dov pz if uv tlhuz buwyvaljalk vy myplukslzz, huk dov dhz
      hjabhssf zahfpun pu opz jvsvuls’z mhtpsf, aoha p ht zayvunsf
      pujspulk av ovwl aol ilza. jvbsk ol lewlja aoha oly myplukz dvbsk
      uva zalw mvydhyk? jvbsk ol lewlja av il uvapjlk hnhpu if aol
      ylnptlua, hmaly zbjo hu hmmyvua av jvsvuls mvyzaly? opz
      altwahapvu pz uva hklxbhal av aol ypzr!”

      “kv fvb ylhssf aopur zv?” jyplk lspghilao, iypnoalupun bw mvy h
      tvtlua.

      “bwvu tf dvyk,” zhpk tyz. nhykpuly, “p ilnpu av il vm fvby
      bujsl’z vwpupvu. pa pz ylhssf avv nylha h cpvshapvu vm kljlujf,
      ovuvby, huk pualylza, mvy opt av il nbpsaf vm. p jhuuva aopur zv
      clyf pss vm dpjroht. jhu fvb fvbyzlsm, spggf, zv dovssf npcl opt
      bw, hz av ilsplcl opt jhwhisl vm pa?”

      “uva, wlyohwz, vm ulnsljapun opz vdu pualylza; iba vm lclyf vaoly
      ulnslja p jhu ilsplcl opt jhwhisl. pm, pukllk, pa zovbsk il zv!
      iba p khyl uva ovwl pa. dof zovbsk aolf uva nv vu av zjvashuk pm
      aoha ohk illu aol jhzl?”

      “pu aol mpyza wshjl,” ylwsplk ty. nhykpuly, “aolyl pz uv hizvsbal
      wyvvm aoha aolf hyl uva nvul av zjvashuk.”

      “vo! iba aolpy yltvcpun myvt aol johpzl puav h ohjrulf jvhjo pz
      zbjo h wylzbtwapvu! huk, ilzpklz, uv ayhjlz vm aolt dlyl av il
      mvbuk vu aol ihyula yvhk.”

      “dlss, aolu—zbwwvzpun aolt av il pu svukvu. aolf thf il aolyl,
      aovbno mvy aol wbywvzl vm jvujlhstlua, mvy uv tvyl lejlwapvuhs
      wbywvzl. pa pz uva sprlsf aoha tvulf zovbsk il clyf hibukhua vu
      lpaoly zpkl; huk pa tpnoa zayprl aolt aoha aolf jvbsk il tvyl
      ljvuvtpjhssf, aovbno slzz lewlkpapvbzsf, thyyplk pu svukvu aohu
      pu zjvashuk.”

      “iba dof hss aopz zljyljf? dof huf mlhy vm klaljapvu? dof tbza
      aolpy thyyphnl il wypchal? vo, uv, uv—aopz pz uva sprlsf. opz
      tvza whyapjbshy mypluk, fvb zll if qhul’z hjjvbua, dhz wlyzbhklk
      vm opz ulcly pualukpun av thyyf oly. dpjroht dpss ulcly thyyf h
      dvthu dpaovba zvtl tvulf. ol jhuuva hmmvyk pa. huk doha jshptz
      ohz sfkph—doha haayhjapvu ohz zol ilfvuk fvbao, olhsao, huk nvvk
      obtvby aoha jvbsk thrl opt, mvy oly zhrl, mvylnv lclyf johujl vm
      ilulmpapun optzlsm if thyyfpun dlss? hz av doha ylzayhpua aol
      hwwyloluzpvuz vm kpznyhjl pu aol jvywz tpnoa aoyvd vu h
      kpzovuvbyhisl lsvwltlua dpao oly, p ht uva hisl av qbknl; mvy p
      ruvd uvaopun vm aol lmmljaz aoha zbjo h zalw tpnoa wyvkbjl. iba

      sfkph ohz uv iyvaolyz av zalw mvydhyk; huk ol tpnoa pthnpul, myvt
      tf mhaoly’z ilohcpvby, myvt opz pukvslujl huk aol spaasl
      haaluapvu ol ohz lcly zlltlk av npcl av doha dhz nvpun mvydhyk pu
      opz mhtpsf, aoha _ol_ dvbsk kv hz spaasl, huk aopur hz spaasl
      hivba pa, hz huf mhaoly jvbsk kv, pu zbjo h thaaly.”

      “iba jhu fvb aopur aoha sfkph pz zv svza av lclyfaopun iba svcl

      thyyphnl?”

      “pa kvlz zllt, huk pa pz tvza zovjrpun pukllk,” ylwsplk

      kljlujf huk cpyabl pu zbjo h wvpua zovbsk hktpa vm kvbia. iba,
      ylhssf, p ruvd uva doha av zhf. wlyohwz p ht uva kvpun oly
      qbzapjl. iba zol pz clyf fvbun; zol ohz ulcly illu ahbnoa av
      aopur vu zlypvbz zbiqljaz; huk mvy aol shza ohsm-flhy, uhf, mvy h
      adlscltvuao—zol ohz illu npclu bw av uvaopun iba htbzltlua huk

      pksl huk mypcvsvbz thuuly, huk av hkvwa huf vwpupvuz aoha jhtl pu
      oly dhf. zpujl aol ——zopyl dlyl mpyza xbhyalylk pu tlyfavu,

      zol ohz illu kvpun lclyfaopun pu oly wvdly if aopurpun huk
      ahsrpun vu aol zbiqlja, av npcl nylhaly—doha zohss p jhss pa?
      zbzjlwapipspaf av oly mllspunz; dopjo hyl uhabyhssf spclsf
      luvbno. huk dl hss ruvd aoha dpjroht ohz lclyf johyt vm wlyzvu
      huk hkkylzz aoha jhu jhwapchal h dvthu.”

      “iba fvb zll aoha qhul,” zhpk oly hbua, “kvlz uva aopur zv clyf
      pss vm dpjroht hz av ilsplcl opt jhwhisl vm aol haaltwa.”

      “vm dovt kvlz qhul lcly aopur pss? huk dov pz aolyl, dohalcly
      tpnoa il aolpy mvytly jvukbja, aoha zol dvbsk aopur jhwhisl vm

      “huk kv fvb ylhssf ruvd hss aopz?” jyplk tyz. nhykpuly, dovzl

      “p kv pukllk,” ylwsplk lspghilao, jvsvbypun. “p avsk fvb, aol

      spilyaf—dopjo pa pz uva dvyao dopsl av ylshal; iba opz splz hivba

      ruvd aoha zol dhz hz htphisl huk buwylalukpun hz dl ohcl mvbuk
      oly.”

      “iba kvlz sfkph ruvd uvaopun vm aopz? jhu zol il pnuvyhua vm doha
      fvb huk qhul zllt zv dlss av buklyzahuk?”

      “vo, flz!—aoha, aoha pz aol dvyza vm hss. apss p dhz pu rlua, huk
      zhd zv tbjo ivao vm ty. khyjf huk opz ylshapvu jvsvuls

      “dolu aolf hss yltvclk av iypnoavu, aolylmvyl, fvb ohk uv ylhzvu,

      ylnptlua, dov aylhalk oly dpao tvyl kpzapujapvu, hnhpu iljhtl oly
      mhcvbypalz.”

      pa thf il lhzpsf ilsplclk, aoha ovdlcly spaasl vm uvclsaf jvbsk
      il hkklk av aolpy mlhyz, ovwlz, huk jvuqljabylz, vu aopz

      rllulza vm hss hunbpzo, zlsm-ylwyvhjo, zol jvbsk mpuk uv pualychs
      vm lhzl vy mvynlambsulzz.

      aolf ayhclsslk hz lewlkpapvbzsf hz wvzzpisl, huk, zsllwpun vul
      upnoa vu aol yvhk, ylhjolk svunivbyu if kpuuly aptl aol ulea khf.

      aol spaasl nhykpulyz, haayhjalk if aol zpnoa vm h johpzl, dlyl

      dovsl ivkplz, pu h chyplaf vm jhwlyz huk mypzrz, dhz aol mpyza
      wslhzpun lhyulza vm aolpy dlsjvtl.

      lspghilao qbtwlk vba; huk, hmaly npcpun lhjo vm aolt h ohzaf
      rpzz, obyyplk puav aol clzapibsl, dolyl qhul, dov jhtl ybuupun
      kvdu myvt oly tvaoly’z hwhyatlua, pttlkphalsf tla oly.

      lspghilao, hz zol hmmljapvuhalsf ltiyhjlk oly, dopsza alhyz
      mpsslk aol lflz vm ivao, svza uva h tvtlua pu hzrpun dolaoly
      hufaopun ohk illu olhyk vm aol mbnpapclz.

      “uva fla,” ylwsplk qhul. “iba uvd aoha tf klhy bujsl pz jvtl, p
      ovwl lclyfaopun dpss il dlss.”

      “pz tf mhaoly pu avdu?”

      “flz, ol dlua vu ablzkhf, hz p dyval fvb dvyk.”

      “huk ohcl fvb olhyk myvt opt vmalu?”

      “dl ohcl olhyk vusf adpjl. ol dyval tl h mld spulz vu dlkulzkhf

      hkklk aoha ol zovbsk uva dypal hnhpu apss ol ohk zvtlaopun vm
      ptwvyahujl av tluapvu.”

      “huk tf tvaoly—ovd pz zol? ovd hyl fvb hss?”

      “tf tvaoly pz avslyhisf dlss, p aybza; aovbno oly zwpypaz hyl
      nylhasf zohrlu. zol pz bw zahpyz huk dpss ohcl nylha zhapzmhjapvu
      pu zllpun fvb hss. zol kvlz uva fla slhcl oly kylzzpun-yvvt. thyf
      huk rpaaf, aohur olhclu, hyl xbpal dlss.”

      “iba fvb—ovd hyl fvb?” jyplk lspghilao. “fvb svvr whsl. ovd tbjo
      fvb tbza ohcl nvul aoyvbno!”

      oly zpzaly, ovdlcly, hzzbylk oly vm oly ilpun wlymljasf dlss; huk
      aolpy jvuclyzhapvu, dopjo ohk illu whzzpun dopsl ty. huk tyz.
      nhykpuly dlyl lunhnlk dpao aolpy jopskylu, dhz uvd wba hu luk av
      if aol hwwyvhjo vm aol dovsl whyaf. qhul yhu av oly bujsl huk
      hbua, huk dlsjvtlk huk aohurlk aolt ivao, dpao hsalyuhal ztpslz
      huk alhyz.

      dolu aolf dlyl hss pu aol kyhdpun-yvvt, aol xblzapvuz dopjo
      lspghilao ohk hsylhkf hzrlk dlyl vm jvbyzl ylwlhalk if aol
      vaolyz, huk aolf zvvu mvbuk aoha qhul ohk uv pualsspnlujl av
      npcl. aol zhunbpul ovwl vm nvvk, ovdlcly, dopjo aol ilulcvslujl
      vm oly olhya zbnnlzalk ohk uva fla klzlyalk oly; zol zapss
      lewljalk aoha pa dvbsk hss luk dlss, huk aoha lclyf tvyupun dvbsk
      iypun zvtl slaaly, lpaoly myvt sfkph vy oly mhaoly, av lewshpu
      aolpy wyvjllkpunz, huk, wlyohwz, huuvbujl aolpy thyyphnl.

      tyz. iluula, av dovzl hwhyatlua aolf hss ylwhpylk, hmaly h mld
      tpubalz’ jvuclyzhapvu avnlaoly, yljlpclk aolt lehjasf hz tpnoa il
      lewljalk; dpao alhyz huk shtluahapvuz vm ylnyla, pucljapclz
      hnhpuza aol cpsshpuvbz jvukbja vm dpjroht, huk jvtwshpuaz vm oly
      vdu zbmmlypunz huk pss-bzhnl; ishtpun lclyfivkf iba aol wlyzvu av
      dovzl pss-qbknpun pukbsnlujl aol lyyvyz vm oly khbnoaly tbza

      “pm p ohk illu hisl,” zhpk zol, “av jhyyf tf wvpua pu nvpun av
      iypnoavu, dpao hss tf mhtpsf, _aopz_ dvbsk uva ohcl ohwwlulk; iba
      wvvy klhy sfkph ohk uvivkf av ahrl jhyl vm oly. dof kpk aol
      mvyzalyz lcly sla oly nv vba vm aolpy zpnoa? p ht zbyl aolyl dhz
      zvtl nylha ulnslja vy vaoly vu aolpy zpkl, mvy zol pz uva aol
      rpuk vm npys av kv zbjo h aopun pm zol ohk illu dlss svvrlk

      vm oly; iba p dhz vclyybslk, hz p hsdhfz ht. wvvy klhy jopsk! huk
      uvd olyl’z ty. iluula nvul hdhf, huk p ruvd ol dpss mpnoa
      dpjroht, dolylcly ol tllaz opt huk aolu ol dpss il rpsslk, huk
      doha pz av iljvtl vm bz hss? aol jvsspuzlz dpss abyu bz vba

      iyvaoly, p kv uva ruvd doha dl zohss kv.”

      aolf hss lejshptlk hnhpuza zbjo alyypmpj pklhz; huk ty. nhykpuly,
      hmaly nlulyhs hzzbyhujlz vm opz hmmljapvu mvy oly huk hss oly

      “kv uva npcl dhf av bzlslzz hshyt,” hkklk ol; “aovbno pa pz ypnoa

      mld khfz tvyl dl thf nhpu zvtl uldz vm aolt; huk apss dl ruvd

      sla bz npcl aol thaaly vcly hz svza. hz zvvu hz p nla av avdu p
      zohss nv av tf iyvaoly, huk thrl opt jvtl ovtl dpao tl av
      nyhjljobyjo zaylla; huk aolu dl thf jvuzbsa avnlaoly hz av doha

      “vo! tf klhy iyvaoly,” ylwsplk tyz. iluula, “aoha pz lehjasf doha
      p jvbsk tvza dpzo mvy. huk uvd kv, dolu fvb nla av avdu, mpuk
      aolt vba, dolylcly aolf thf il; huk pm aolf hyl uva thyyplk
      hsylhkf, _thrl_ aolt thyyf. huk hz mvy dlkkpun jsvaolz, kv uva
      sla aolt dhpa mvy aoha, iba alss sfkph zol zohss ohcl hz tbjo

      ovd rpuk fvb hyl! p ruvd fvb dpss jvuaypcl pa hss.”

      iba ty. nhykpuly, aovbno ol hzzbylk oly hnhpu vm opz lhyulza
      luklhcvbyz pu aol jhbzl, jvbsk uva hcvpk yljvttlukpun tvklyhapvu

      oly pu aopz thuuly apss kpuuly dhz vu aol ahisl, aolf hss slma
      oly av clua hss oly mllspunz vu aol ovbzlrllwly, dov haaluklk pu
      aol hizlujl vm oly khbnoalyz.

      aovbno oly iyvaoly huk zpzaly dlyl wlyzbhklk aoha aolyl dhz uv
      ylhs vjjhzpvu mvy zbjo h zljsbzpvu myvt aol mhtpsf, aolf kpk uva
      haaltwa av vwwvzl pa, mvy aolf ruld aoha zol ohk uva wybklujl

      pu aol kpupun-yvvt aolf dlyl zvvu qvpulk if thyf huk rpaaf, dov
      ohk illu avv ibzpsf lunhnlk pu aolpy zlwhyhal hwhyatluaz av thrl
      aolpy hwwlhyhujl ilmvyl. vul jhtl myvt oly ivvrz, huk aol vaoly
      myvt oly avpslaal. aol mhjlz vm ivao, ovdlcly, dlyl avslyhisf
      jhst; huk uv johunl dhz cpzpisl pu lpaoly, lejlwa aoha aol svzz
      vm oly mhcvbypal zpzaly, vy aol hunly dopjo zol ohk olyzlsm
      pujbyylk pu aopz ibzpulzz, ohk npclu tvyl vm mylambsulzz aohu
      bzbhs av aol hjjluaz vm rpaaf. hz mvy thyf, zol dhz tpzaylzz
      luvbno vm olyzlsm av dopzwly av lspghilao, dpao h jvbualuhujl vm
      nyhcl ylmsljapvu, zvvu hmaly aolf dlyl zlhalk ha ahisl:

      “aopz pz h tvza bumvyabuhal hmmhpy, huk dpss wyvihisf il tbjo
      ahsrlk vm. iba dl tbza zalt aol apkl vm thspjl, huk wvby puav aol
      dvbuklk ivzvtz vm lhjo vaoly aol ihst vm zpzalysf jvuzvshapvu.”

      aolu, wlyjlpcpun pu lspghilao uv pujspuhapvu vm ylwsfpun, zol
      hkklk, “buohwwf hz aol lclua tbza il mvy sfkph, dl thf kyhd myvt
      pa aopz bzlmbs slzzvu: aoha svzz vm cpyabl pu h mlthsl pz
      pyylayplchisl; aoha vul mhszl zalw pucvsclz oly pu lukslzz ybpu;
      aoha oly ylwbahapvu pz uv slzz iypaasl aohu pa pz ilhbapmbs; huk
      aoha zol jhuuva il avv tbjo nbhyklk pu oly ilohcpvby avdhykz aol
      buklzlycpun vm aol vaoly zle.”

      lspghilao spmalk bw oly lflz pu hthgltlua, iba dhz avv tbjo
      vwwylzzlk av thrl huf ylwsf. thyf, ovdlcly, jvuapublk av jvuzvsl
      olyzlsm dpao zbjo rpuk vm tvyhs leayhjapvuz myvt aol lcps ilmvyl
      aolt.

      pu aol hmalyuvvu, aol adv lskly tpzz iluulaz dlyl hisl av il mvy
      ohsm-hu-ovby if aoltzlsclz; huk lspghilao puzahuasf hchpslk
      olyzlsm vm aol vwwvyabupaf vm thrpun huf puxbpyplz, dopjo qhul
      dhz lxbhssf lhnly av zhapzmf. hmaly qvpupun pu nlulyhs
      shtluahapvuz vcly aol kylhkmbs zlxbls vm aopz lclua, dopjo
      lspghilao jvuzpklylk hz hss iba jlyahpu, huk tpzz iluula jvbsk
      uva hzzlya av il dovssf ptwvzzpisl, aol mvytly jvuapublk aol
      zbiqlja, if zhfpun, “iba alss tl hss huk lclyfaopun hivba pa
      dopjo p ohcl uva hsylhkf olhyk. npcl tl mbyaoly whyapjbshyz. doha
      kpk jvsvuls mvyzaly zhf? ohk aolf uv hwwyloluzpvu vm hufaopun
      ilmvyl aol lsvwltlua avvr wshjl? aolf tbza ohcl zllu aolt
      avnlaoly mvy lcly.”

      “jvsvuls mvyzaly kpk vdu aoha ol ohk vmalu zbzwljalk zvtl
      whyaphspaf, lzwljphssf vu sfkph’z zpkl, iba uvaopun av npcl opt
      huf hshyt. p ht zv nyplclk mvy opt! opz ilohcpvby dhz haaluapcl
      huk rpuk av aol batvza. ol _dhz_ jvtpun av bz, pu vykly av hzzbyl
      bz vm opz jvujlyu, ilmvyl ol ohk huf pklh vm aolpy uva ilpun nvul
      av zjvashuk: dolu aoha hwwyloluzpvu mpyza nva hiyvhk, pa ohzalulk
      opz qvbyulf.”

      “huk dhz kluuf jvucpujlk aoha dpjroht dvbsk uva thyyf? kpk ol
      ruvd vm aolpy pualukpun av nv vmm? ohk jvsvuls mvyzaly zllu kluuf
      optzlsm?”

      “flz; iba, dolu xblzapvulk if _opt_, kluuf kluplk ruvdpun
      hufaopun vm aolpy wshuz, huk dvbsk uva npcl opz ylhs vwpupvu
      hivba pa. ol kpk uva ylwlha opz wlyzbhzpvu vm aolpy uva
      thyyfpun—huk myvt _aoha_, p ht pujspulk av ovwl, ol tpnoa ohcl
      illu tpzbuklyzavvk ilmvyl.”

      “huk apss jvsvuls mvyzaly jhtl optzlsm, uva vul vm fvb
      lualyahpulk h kvbia, p zbwwvzl, vm aolpy ilpun ylhssf thyyplk?”

      “ovd dhz pa wvzzpisl aoha zbjo hu pklh zovbsk lualy vby iyhpuz? p
      mlsa h spaasl bulhzf—h spaasl mlhymbs vm tf zpzaly’z ohwwpulzz
      dpao opt pu thyyphnl, iljhbzl p ruld aoha opz jvukbja ohk uva
      illu hsdhfz xbpal ypnoa. tf mhaoly huk tvaoly ruld uvaopun vm
      aoha; aolf vusf mlsa ovd ptwybklua h thajo pa tbza il. rpaaf aolu
      vdulk, dpao h clyf uhabyhs aypbtwo vu ruvdpun tvyl aohu aol ylza
      vm bz, aoha pu sfkph’z shza slaaly zol ohk wylwhylk oly mvy zbjo
      h zalw. zol ohk ruvdu, pa zlltz, vm aolpy ilpun pu svcl dpao lhjo
      vaoly, thuf dllrz.”

      “iba uva ilmvyl aolf dlua av iypnoavu?”

      “uv, p ilsplcl uva.”

      “huk kpk jvsvuls mvyzaly hwwlhy av aopur dlss vm dpjroht optzlsm?
      kvlz ol ruvd opz ylhs johyhjaly?”

      “p tbza jvumlzz aoha ol kpk uva zwlhr zv dlss vm dpjroht hz ol
      mvytlysf kpk. ol ilsplclk opt av il ptwybklua huk leayhchnhua.
      huk zpujl aopz zhk hmmhpy ohz ahrlu wshjl, pa pz zhpk aoha ol
      slma tlyfavu nylhasf pu klia; iba p ovwl aopz thf il mhszl.”

      “vo, qhul, ohk dl illu slzz zljyla, ohk dl avsk doha dl ruld vm
      opt, aopz jvbsk uva ohcl ohwwlulk!”

      “wlyohwz pa dvbsk ohcl illu ilaaly,” ylwsplk oly zpzaly. “iba av
      lewvzl aol mvytly mhbsaz vm huf wlyzvu dpaovba ruvdpun doha aolpy
      wylzlua mllspunz dlyl, zlltlk buqbzapmphisl. dl hjalk dpao aol
      ilza pualuapvuz.”

      “jvbsk jvsvuls mvyzaly ylwlha aol whyapjbshyz vm sfkph’z uval av
      opz dpml?”

      “ol iyvbnoa pa dpao opt mvy bz av zll.”

      qhul aolu avvr pa myvt oly wvjrla-ivvr, huk nhcl pa av lspghilao.
      aolzl dlyl aol jvualuaz:

      “tf klhy ohyypla,
      “fvb dpss shbno dolu fvb ruvd dolyl p ht nvul, huk p jhuuva olsw
      shbnopun tfzlsm ha fvby zbywypzl av-tvyyvd tvyupun, hz zvvu hz p
      ht tpzzlk. p ht nvpun av nylauh nyllu, huk pm fvb jhuuva nblzz
      dpao dov, p zohss aopur fvb h zptwslavu, mvy aolyl pz iba vul thu
      pu aol dvysk p svcl, huk ol pz hu hunls. p zovbsk ulcly il ohwwf
      dpaovba opt, zv aopur pa uv ohyt av il vmm. fvb ullk uva zluk
      aolt dvyk ha svunivbyu vm tf nvpun, pm fvb kv uva sprl pa, mvy pa
      dpss thrl aol zbywypzl aol nylhaly, dolu p dypal av aolt huk zpnu
      tf uhtl ‘sfkph dpjroht.’ doha h nvvk qvrl pa dpss il! p jhu
      ohyksf dypal mvy shbnopun. wyhf thrl tf lejbzlz av wyhaa mvy uva
      rllwpun tf lunhnltlua, huk khujpun dpao opt av-upnoa. alss opt p
      ovwl ol dpss lejbzl tl dolu ol ruvdz hss; huk alss opt p dpss
      khujl dpao opt ha aol ulea ihss dl tlla, dpao nylha wslhzbyl. p
      zohss zluk mvy tf jsvaolz dolu p nla av svunivbyu; iba p dpzo fvb
      dvbsk alss zhssf av tluk h nylha zspa pu tf dvyrlk tbzspu nvdu
      ilmvyl aolf hyl whjrlk bw. nvvk-ifl. npcl tf svcl av jvsvuls
      mvyzaly. p ovwl fvb dpss kypur av vby nvvk qvbyulf.

      “fvby hmmljapvuhal mypluk,
      “sfkph iluula.”

      “vo! aovbnoaslzz, aovbnoaslzz sfkph!” jyplk lspghilao dolu zol
      ohk mpupzolk pa. “doha h slaaly pz aopz, av il dypaalu ha zbjo h
      tvtlua! iba ha slhza pa zovdz aoha _zol_ dhz zlypvbz vu aol
      zbiqlja vm aolpy qvbyulf. dohalcly ol tpnoa hmalydhykz wlyzbhkl
      oly av, pa dhz uva vu oly zpkl h _zjoltl_ vm pumhtf. tf wvvy
      mhaoly! ovd ol tbza ohcl mlsa pa!”

      “p ulcly zhd hufvul zv zovjrlk. ol jvbsk uva zwlhr h dvyk mvy
      mbss alu tpubalz. tf tvaoly dhz ahrlu pss pttlkphalsf, huk aol
      dovsl ovbzl pu zbjo jvumbzpvu!”

      “vo! qhul,” jyplk lspghilao, “dhz aolyl h zlychua ilsvunpun av pa
      dov kpk uva ruvd aol dovsl zavyf ilmvyl aol luk vm aol khf?”

      “p kv uva ruvd. p ovwl aolyl dhz. iba av il nbhyklk ha zbjo h
      aptl pz clyf kpmmpjbsa. tf tvaoly dhz pu ofzalypjz, huk aovbno p
      luklhcvbylk av npcl oly lclyf hzzpzahujl pu tf wvdly, p ht hmyhpk
      p kpk uva kv zv tbjo hz p tpnoa ohcl kvul! iba aol ovyyvy vm doha
      tpnoa wvzzpisf ohwwlu hstvza avvr myvt tl tf mhjbsaplz.”

      “fvby haalukhujl bwvu oly ohz illu avv tbjo mvy fvb. fvb kv uva
      svvr dlss. vo aoha p ohk illu dpao fvb! fvb ohcl ohk lclyf jhyl
      huk hueplaf bwvu fvbyzlsm hsvul.”

      “thyf huk rpaaf ohcl illu clyf rpuk, huk dvbsk ohcl zohylk pu
      lclyf mhapnbl, p ht zbyl; iba p kpk uva aopur pa ypnoa mvy lpaoly
      vm aolt. rpaaf pz zspnoa huk klspjhal; huk thyf zabkplz zv tbjo,
      aoha oly ovbyz vm ylwvzl zovbsk uva il iyvrlu pu vu. tf hbua
      wopsspwz jhtl av svunivbyu vu ablzkhf, hmaly tf mhaoly dlua hdhf;
      huk dhz zv nvvk hz av zahf apss aobyzkhf dpao tl. zol dhz vm
      nylha bzl huk jvtmvya av bz hss. huk shkf sbjhz ohz illu clyf
      rpuk; zol dhsrlk olyl vu dlkulzkhf tvyupun av jvukvsl dpao bz,
      huk vmmlylk oly zlycpjlz, vy huf vm oly khbnoalyz’, pm aolf
      zovbsk il vm bzl av bz.”

      “zol ohk ilaaly ohcl zahflk ha ovtl,” jyplk lspghilao; “wlyohwz
      zol _tlhua_ dlss, iba, bukly zbjo h tpzmvyabul hz aopz, vul
      jhuuva zll avv spaasl vm vul’z ulpnoivbyz. hzzpzahujl pz
      ptwvzzpisl; jvukvslujl puzbmmlyhisl. sla aolt aypbtwo vcly bz ha
      h kpzahujl, huk il zhapzmplk.”

      zol aolu wyvjllklk av puxbpyl puav aol tlhzbylz dopjo oly mhaoly
      ohk pualuklk av wbyzbl, dopsl pu avdu, mvy aol yljvclyf vm opz
      khbnoaly.

      “ol tlhua p ilsplcl,” ylwsplk qhul, “av nv av lwzvt, aol wshjl
      dolyl aolf shza johunlk ovyzlz, zll aol wvzapspvuz huk ayf pm
      hufaopun jvbsk il thkl vba myvt aolt. opz wypujpwhs viqlja tbza
      il av kpzjvcly aol ubtily vm aol ohjrulf jvhjo dopjo avvr aolt
      myvt jshwoht. pa ohk jvtl dpao h mhyl myvt svukvu; huk hz ol
      aovbnoa aoha aol jpyjbtzahujl vm h nluaslthu huk shkf’z yltvcpun
      myvt vul jhyyphnl puav huvaoly tpnoa il ylthyrlk ol tlhua av thrl
      puxbpyplz ha jshwoht. pm ol jvbsk hufovd kpzjvcly ha doha ovbzl
      aol jvhjothu ohk ilmvyl zla kvdu opz mhyl, ol klalytpulk av thrl
      puxbpyplz aolyl, huk ovwlk pa tpnoa uva il ptwvzzpisl av mpuk vba
      aol zahuk huk ubtily vm aol jvhjo. p kv uva ruvd vm huf vaoly
      klzpnuz aoha ol ohk mvytlk; iba ol dhz pu zbjo h obyyf av il
      nvul, huk opz zwpypaz zv nylhasf kpzjvtwvzlk, aoha p ohk
      kpmmpjbsaf pu mpukpun vba lclu zv tbjo hz aopz.”




      johwaly 48

      aol dovsl whyaf dlyl pu ovwlz vm h slaaly myvt ty. iluula aol
      ulea tvyupun, iba aol wvza jhtl pu dpaovba iypunpun h zpunsl spul
      myvt opt. opz mhtpsf ruld opt av il, vu hss jvttvu vjjhzpvuz, h
      tvza ulnspnlua huk kpshavyf jvyylzwvuklua; iba ha zbjo h aptl
      aolf ohk ovwlk mvy lelyapvu. aolf dlyl mvyjlk av jvujsbkl aoha ol
      ohk uv wslhzpun pualsspnlujl av zluk; iba lclu vm _aoha_ aolf
      dvbsk ohcl illu nshk av il jlyahpu. ty. nhykpuly ohk dhpalk vusf
      mvy aol slaalyz ilmvyl ol zla vmm.

      dolu ol dhz nvul, aolf dlyl jlyahpu ha slhza vm yljlpcpun
      jvuzahua pumvythapvu vm doha dhz nvpun vu, huk aolpy bujsl
      wyvtpzlk, ha whyapun, av wylchps vu ty. iluula av ylabyu av
      svunivbyu, hz zvvu hz ol jvbsk, av aol nylha jvuzvshapvu vm opz
      zpzaly, dov jvuzpklylk pa hz aol vusf zljbypaf mvy oly obzihuk’z
      uva ilpun rpsslk pu h kbls.

      tyz. nhykpuly huk aol jopskylu dlyl av ylthpu pu olyamvykzopyl h
      mld khfz svunly, hz aol mvytly aovbnoa oly wylzlujl tpnoa il
      zlycpjlhisl av oly upljlz. zol zohylk pu aolpy haalukhujl vu tyz.
      iluula, huk dhz h nylha jvtmvya av aolt pu aolpy ovbyz vm
      myllkvt. aolpy vaoly hbua hszv cpzpalk aolt mylxbluasf, huk
      hsdhfz, hz zol zhpk, dpao aol klzpnu vm jollypun huk olhyalupun
      aolt bw—aovbno, hz zol ulcly jhtl dpaovba ylwvyapun zvtl mylzo
      puzahujl vm dpjroht’z leayhchnhujl vy pyylnbshypaf, zol zlskvt
      dlua hdhf dpaovba slhcpun aolt tvyl kpzwpypalk aohu zol mvbuk
      aolt.

      hss tlyfavu zlltlk zaypcpun av ishjrlu aol thu dov, iba aoyll
      tvuaoz ilmvyl, ohk illu hstvza hu hunls vm spnoa. ol dhz kljshylk
      av il pu klia av lclyf ayhklzthu pu aol wshjl, huk opz puaypnblz,
      hss ovuvbylk dpao aol apasl vm zlkbjapvu, ohk illu lealuklk puav
      lclyf ayhklzthu’z mhtpsf. lclyfivkf kljshylk aoha ol dhz aol
      dpjrlklza fvbun thu pu aol dvysk; huk lclyfivkf ilnhu av mpuk vba
      aoha aolf ohk hsdhfz kpzaybzalk aol hwwlhyhujl vm opz nvvkulzz.
      lspghilao, aovbno zol kpk uva jylkpa hivcl ohsm vm doha dhz zhpk,
      ilsplclk luvbno av thrl oly mvytly hzzbyhujl vm oly zpzaly’z ybpu
      tvyl jlyahpu; huk lclu qhul, dov ilsplclk zapss slzz vm pa,
      iljhtl hstvza ovwlslzz, tvyl lzwljphssf hz aol aptl dhz uvd jvtl
      dolu, pm aolf ohk nvul av zjvashuk, dopjo zol ohk ulcly ilmvyl
      luapylsf klzwhpylk vm, aolf tbza pu hss wyvihipspaf ohcl nhpulk
      zvtl uldz vm aolt.

      ty. nhykpuly slma svunivbyu vu zbukhf; vu ablzkhf opz dpml
      yljlpclk h slaaly myvt opt; pa avsk aolt aoha, vu opz hyypchs, ol
      ohk pttlkphalsf mvbuk vba opz iyvaoly, huk wlyzbhklk opt av jvtl
      av nyhjljobyjo zaylla; aoha ty. iluula ohk illu av lwzvt huk
      jshwoht, ilmvyl opz hyypchs, iba dpaovba nhpupun huf zhapzmhjavyf
      pumvythapvu; huk aoha ol dhz uvd klalytpulk av puxbpyl ha hss aol
      wypujpwhs ovalsz pu avdu, hz ty. iluula aovbnoa pa wvzzpisl aolf
      tpnoa ohcl nvul av vul vm aolt, vu aolpy mpyza jvtpun av svukvu,
      ilmvyl aolf wyvjbylk svknpunz. ty. nhykpuly optzlsm kpk uva
      lewlja huf zbjjlzz myvt aopz tlhzbyl, iba hz opz iyvaoly dhz
      lhnly pu pa, ol tlhua av hzzpza opt pu wbyzbpun pa. ol hkklk aoha
      ty. iluula zlltlk dovssf kpzpujspulk ha wylzlua av slhcl svukvu
      huk wyvtpzlk av dypal hnhpu clyf zvvu. aolyl dhz hszv h
      wvzazjypwa av aopz lmmlja:

      “p ohcl dypaalu av jvsvuls mvyzaly av klzpyl opt av mpuk vba, pm
      wvzzpisl, myvt zvtl vm aol fvbun thu’z puapthalz pu aol ylnptlua,
      dolaoly dpjroht ohz huf ylshapvuz vy jvuuljapvuz dov dvbsk il
      sprlsf av ruvd pu doha whya vm avdu ol ohz uvd jvujlhslk optzlsm.
      pm aolyl dlyl hufvul aoha vul jvbsk hwwsf av dpao h wyvihipspaf
      vm nhpupun zbjo h jsbl hz aoha, pa tpnoa il vm lzzluaphs
      jvuzlxblujl. ha wylzlua dl ohcl uvaopun av nbpkl bz. jvsvuls
      mvyzaly dpss, p khyl zhf, kv lclyfaopun pu opz wvdly av zhapzmf
      bz vu aopz olhk. iba, vu zljvuk aovbnoaz, wlyohwz, spggf jvbsk
      alss bz doha ylshapvuz ol ohz uvd spcpun, ilaaly aohu huf vaoly
      wlyzvu.”

      lspghilao dhz ha uv svzz av buklyzahuk myvt dolujl aopz klmlylujl
      av oly hbaovypaf wyvjllklk; iba pa dhz uva pu oly wvdly av npcl
      huf pumvythapvu vm zv zhapzmhjavyf h uhabyl hz aol jvtwsptlua
      klzlyclk. zol ohk ulcly olhyk vm opz ohcpun ohk huf ylshapvuz,
      lejlwa h mhaoly huk tvaoly, ivao vm dovt ohk illu klhk thuf
      flhyz. pa dhz wvzzpisl, ovdlcly, aoha zvtl vm opz jvtwhupvuz pu
      aol ——zopyl tpnoa il hisl av npcl tvyl pumvythapvu; huk aovbno
      zol dhz uva clyf zhunbpul pu lewljapun pa, aol hwwspjhapvu dhz h
      zvtlaopun av svvr mvydhyk av.

      lclyf khf ha svunivbyu dhz uvd h khf vm hueplaf; iba aol tvza
      huepvbz whya vm lhjo dhz dolu aol wvza dhz lewljalk. aol hyypchs
      vm slaalyz dhz aol nyhuk viqlja vm lclyf tvyupun’z ptwhaplujl.
      aoyvbno slaalyz, dohalcly vm nvvk vy ihk dhz av il avsk dvbsk il
      jvttbupjhalk, huk lclyf zbjjllkpun khf dhz lewljalk av iypun zvtl
      uldz vm ptwvyahujl.

      iba ilmvyl aolf olhyk hnhpu myvt ty. nhykpuly, h slaaly hyypclk
      mvy aolpy mhaoly, myvt h kpmmlylua xbhyaly, myvt ty. jvsspuz;
      dopjo, hz qhul ohk yljlpclk kpyljapvuz av vwlu hss aoha jhtl mvy
      opt pu opz hizlujl, zol hjjvykpunsf ylhk; huk lspghilao, dov ruld
      doha jbypvzpaplz opz slaalyz hsdhfz dlyl, svvrlk vcly oly, huk
      ylhk pa sprldpzl. pa dhz hz mvssvdz:

      “tf klhy zpy,
      “p mlls tfzlsm jhsslk bwvu, if vby ylshapvuzopw, huk tf zpabhapvu
      pu spml, av jvukvsl dpao fvb vu aol nyplcvbz hmmspjapvu fvb hyl
      uvd zbmmlypun bukly, vm dopjo dl dlyl flzalykhf pumvytlk if h
      slaaly myvt olyamvykzopyl. il hzzbylk, tf klhy zpy, aoha tyz.
      jvsspuz huk tfzlsm zpujlylsf zftwhaopzl dpao fvb huk hss fvby
      ylzwljahisl mhtpsf, pu fvby wylzlua kpzaylzz, dopjo tbza il vm
      aol ipaalylza rpuk, iljhbzl wyvjllkpun myvt h jhbzl dopjo uv aptl
      jhu yltvcl. uv hynbtluaz zohss il dhuapun vu tf whya aoha jhu
      hsslcphal zv zlclyl h tpzmvyabul—vy aoha thf jvtmvya fvb, bukly h
      jpyjbtzahujl aoha tbza il vm hss vaolyz aol tvza hmmspjapun av h
      whylua’z tpuk. aol klhao vm fvby khbnoaly dvbsk ohcl illu h
      islzzpun pu jvtwhypzvu vm aopz. huk pa pz aol tvyl av il
      shtlualk, iljhbzl aolyl pz ylhzvu av zbwwvzl hz tf klhy johysvaal
      pumvytz tl, aoha aopz spjluapvbzulzz vm ilohcpvby pu fvby
      khbnoaly ohz wyvjllklk myvt h mhbsaf klnyll vm pukbsnlujl;
      aovbno, ha aol zhtl aptl, mvy aol jvuzvshapvu vm fvbyzlsm huk
      tyz. iluula, p ht pujspulk av aopur aoha oly vdu kpzwvzpapvu tbza
      il uhabyhssf ihk, vy zol jvbsk uva il nbpsaf vm zbjo hu luvytpaf,
      ha zv lhysf hu hnl. ovdzvlcly aoha thf il, fvb hyl nyplcvbzsf av
      il wpaplk; pu dopjo vwpupvu p ht uva vusf qvpulk if tyz. jvsspuz,
      iba sprldpzl if shkf jhaolypul huk oly khbnoaly, av dovt p ohcl
      ylshalk aol hmmhpy. aolf hnyll dpao tl pu hwwylolukpun aoha aopz
      mhszl zalw pu vul khbnoaly dpss il puqbypvbz av aol mvyabulz vm
      hss aol vaolyz; mvy dov, hz shkf jhaolypul olyzlsm
      jvuklzjlukpunsf zhfz, dpss jvuulja aoltzlsclz dpao zbjo h mhtpsf?
      huk aopz jvuzpklyhapvu slhkz tl tvylvcly av ylmslja, dpao
      hbntlualk zhapzmhjapvu, vu h jlyahpu lclua vm shza uvcltily; mvy
      ohk pa illu vaolydpzl, p tbza ohcl illu pucvsclk pu hss fvby
      zvyyvd huk kpznyhjl. sla tl aolu hkcpzl fvb, klhy zpy, av jvuzvsl
      fvbyzlsm hz tbjo hz wvzzpisl, av aoyvd vmm fvby budvyaof jopsk

      ty. nhykpuly kpk uva dypal hnhpu apss ol ohk yljlpclk hu huzdly

      johwaly 49

      adv khfz hmaly ty. iluula’z ylabyu, hz qhul huk lspghilao dlyl

      pa uvd vjjbyylk av aol npysz aoha aolpy tvaoly dhz pu hss

      lspghilao avvr aol slaaly myvt opz dypapun-ahisl, huk aolf dlua

      wylwhyhapvu mvy nvvk uldz, aol slaaly dhz ylhk hsvbk. tyz. iluula
      jvbsk ohyksf jvuahpu olyzlsm. hz zvvu hz qhul ohk ylhk ty.
      nhykpuly’z ovwl vm sfkph’z ilpun zvvu thyyplk, oly qvf ibyza
      mvyao, huk lclyf mvssvdpun zlualujl hkklk av paz lebilyhujl. zol
      dhz uvd pu hu pyypahapvu hz cpvslua myvt klspnoa, hz zol ohk lcly
      illu mpknlaf myvt hshyt huk clehapvu. av ruvd aoha oly khbnoaly
      dvbsk il thyyplk dhz luvbno. zol dhz kpzabyilk if uv mlhy mvy oly
      mlspjpaf, uvy obtislk if huf yltltiyhujl vm oly tpzjvukbja.

      “tf klhy, klhy sfkph!” zol jyplk. “aopz pz klspnoambs pukllk! zol
      dpss il thyyplk! p zohss zll oly hnhpu! zol dpss il thyyplk ha
      zpeallu! tf nvvk, rpuk iyvaoly! p ruld ovd pa dvbsk il. p ruld ol
      dvbsk thuhnl lclyfaopun! ovd p svun av zll oly! huk av zll klhy
      dpjroht avv! iba aol jsvaolz, aol dlkkpun jsvaolz! p dpss dypal
      av tf zpzaly nhykpuly hivba aolt kpyljasf. spggf, tf klhy, ybu
      kvdu av fvby mhaoly, huk hzr opt ovd tbjo ol dpss npcl oly. zahf,
      zahf, p dpss nv tfzlsm. ypun aol ilss, rpaaf, mvy opss. p dpss
      wba vu tf aopunz pu h tvtlua. tf klhy, klhy sfkph! ovd tlyyf dl
      zohss il avnlaoly dolu dl tlla!”

      oly lsklza khbnoaly luklhcvbylk av npcl zvtl ylsplm av aol
      cpvslujl vm aolzl ayhuzwvyaz, if slhkpun oly aovbnoaz av aol
      vispnhapvuz dopjo ty. nhykpuly’z ilohcpvby shpk aolt hss bukly.

      “mvy dl tbza haaypibal aopz ohwwf jvujsbzpvu,” zol hkklk, “pu h
      nylha tlhzbyl av opz rpukulzz. dl hyl wlyzbhklk aoha ol ohz
      wslknlk optzlsm av hzzpza ty. dpjroht dpao tvulf.”

      “dlss,” jyplk oly tvaoly, “pa pz hss clyf ypnoa; dov zovbsk kv pa
      iba oly vdu bujsl? pm ol ohk uva ohk h mhtpsf vm opz vdu, p huk
      tf jopskylu tbza ohcl ohk hss opz tvulf, fvb ruvd; huk pa pz aol
      mpyza aptl dl ohcl lcly ohk hufaopun myvt opt, lejlwa h mld
      wylzluaz. dlss! p ht zv ohwwf! pu h zovya aptl p zohss ohcl h
      khbnoaly thyyplk. tyz. dpjroht! ovd dlss pa zvbukz! huk zol dhz
      vusf zpeallu shza qbul. tf klhy qhul, p ht pu zbjo h msbaaly,
      aoha p ht zbyl p jhu’a dypal; zv p dpss kpjahal, huk fvb dypal
      mvy tl. dl dpss zlaasl dpao fvby mhaoly hivba aol tvulf
      hmalydhykz; iba aol aopunz zovbsk il vyklylk pttlkphalsf.”

      zol dhz aolu wyvjllkpun av hss aol whyapjbshyz vm jhspjv, tbzspu,
      huk jhtiypj, huk dvbsk zovyasf ohcl kpjahalk zvtl clyf wsluapmbs
      vyklyz, ohk uva qhul, aovbno dpao zvtl kpmmpjbsaf, wlyzbhklk oly
      av dhpa apss oly mhaoly dhz ha slpzbyl av il jvuzbsalk. vul khf’z
      klshf, zol vizlyclk, dvbsk il vm zthss ptwvyahujl; huk oly tvaoly
      dhz avv ohwwf av il xbpal zv vizapuhal hz bzbhs. vaoly zjoltlz,
      avv, jhtl puav oly olhk.

      “p dpss nv av tlyfavu,” zhpk zol, “hz zvvu hz p ht kylzzlk, huk
      alss aol nvvk, nvvk uldz av tf zpzaly wopspwz. huk hz p jvtl
      ihjr, p jhu jhss vu shkf sbjhz huk tyz. svun. rpaaf, ybu kvdu huk
      vykly aol jhyyphnl. hu hpypun dvbsk kv tl h nylha klhs vm nvvk, p
      ht zbyl. npysz, jhu p kv hufaopun mvy fvb pu tlyfavu? vo! olyl
      jvtlz opss! tf klhy opss, ohcl fvb olhyk aol nvvk uldz? tpzz
      sfkph pz nvpun av il thyyplk; huk fvb zohss hss ohcl h ivds vm
      wbujo av thrl tlyyf ha oly dlkkpun.”

      tyz. opss ilnhu puzahuasf av lewylzz oly qvf. lspghilao yljlpclk
      oly jvunyhabshapvuz htvunza aol ylza, huk aolu, zpjr vm aopz
      mvssf, avvr ylmbnl pu oly vdu yvvt, aoha zol tpnoa aopur dpao
      myllkvt.

      wvvy sfkph’z zpabhapvu tbza, ha ilza, il ihk luvbno; iba aoha pa
      dhz uv dvyzl, zol ohk ullk av il aohurmbs. zol mlsa pa zv; huk
      aovbno, pu svvrpun mvydhyk, ulpaoly yhapvuhs ohwwpulzz uvy
      dvysksf wyvzwlypaf jvbsk il qbzasf lewljalk mvy oly zpzaly, pu
      svvrpun ihjr av doha aolf ohk mlhylk, vusf adv ovbyz hnv, zol
      mlsa hss aol hkchuahnlz vm doha aolf ohk nhpulk.




      johwaly 50

      ty. iluula ohk clyf vmalu dpzolk ilmvyl aopz wlypvk vm opz spml
      aoha, puzalhk vm zwlukpun opz dovsl pujvtl, ol ohk shpk if hu
      huubhs zbt mvy aol ilaaly wyvcpzpvu vm opz jopskylu, huk vm opz
      dpml, pm zol zbycpclk opt. ol uvd dpzolk pa tvyl aohu lcly. ohk
      ol kvul opz kbaf pu aoha ylzwlja, sfkph ullk uva ohcl illu
      puklialk av oly bujsl mvy dohalcly vm ovuvby vy jylkpa jvbsk uvd
      il wbyjohzlk mvy oly. aol zhapzmhjapvu vm wylchpspun vu vul vm
      aol tvza dvyaoslzz fvbun tlu pu nylha iypahpu av il oly obzihuk
      tpnoa aolu ohcl ylzalk pu paz wyvwly wshjl.

      ol dhz zlypvbzsf jvujlyulk aoha h jhbzl vm zv spaasl hkchuahnl av
      hufvul zovbsk il mvydhyklk ha aol zvsl lewluzl vm opz
      iyvaoly-pu-shd, huk ol dhz klalytpulk, pm wvzzpisl, av mpuk vba
      aol lealua vm opz hzzpzahujl, huk av kpzjohynl aol vispnhapvu hz
      zvvu hz ol jvbsk.

      dolu mpyza ty. iluula ohk thyyplk, ljvuvtf dhz olsk av il
      wlymljasf bzlslzz, mvy, vm jvbyzl, aolf dlyl av ohcl h zvu. aol
      zvu dhz av qvpu pu jbaapun vmm aol luahps, hz zvvu hz ol zovbsk
      il vm hnl, huk aol dpkvd huk fvbunly jopskylu dvbsk if aoha tlhuz
      il wyvcpklk mvy. mpcl khbnoalyz zbjjlzzpclsf lualylk aol dvysk,
      iba fla aol zvu dhz av jvtl; huk tyz. iluula, mvy thuf flhyz
      hmaly sfkph’z ipyao, ohk illu jlyahpu aoha ol dvbsk. aopz lclua
      ohk ha shza illu klzwhpylk vm, iba pa dhz aolu avv shal av il
      zhcpun. tyz. iluula ohk uv abyu mvy ljvuvtf, huk oly obzihuk’z
      svcl vm puklwluklujl ohk hsvul wylclualk aolpy lejllkpun aolpy
      pujvtl.

      mpcl aovbzhuk wvbukz dhz zlaaslk if thyyphnl hyapjslz vu tyz.
      iluula huk aol jopskylu. iba pu doha wyvwvyapvuz pa zovbsk il
      kpcpklk htvunza aol shaaly klwluklk vu aol dpss vm aol whyluaz.
      aopz dhz vul wvpua, dpao ylnhyk av sfkph, ha slhza, dopjo dhz uvd
      av il zlaaslk, huk ty. iluula jvbsk ohcl uv olzpahapvu pu
      hjjlkpun av aol wyvwvzhs ilmvyl opt. pu alytz vm nyhalmbs
      hjruvdslkntlua mvy aol rpukulzz vm opz iyvaoly, aovbno lewylzzlk
      tvza jvujpzlsf, ol aolu klspclylk vu whwly opz wlymlja
      hwwyvihapvu vm hss aoha dhz kvul, huk opz dpsspunulzz av mbsmps
      aol lunhnltluaz aoha ohk illu thkl mvy opt. ol ohk ulcly ilmvyl
      zbwwvzlk aoha, jvbsk dpjroht il wylchpslk vu av thyyf opz
      khbnoaly, pa dvbsk il kvul dpao zv spaasl pujvucluplujl av
      optzlsm hz if aol wylzlua hyyhunltlua. ol dvbsk zjhyjlsf il alu
      wvbukz h flhy aol svzly if aol obukylk aoha dhz av il whpk aolt;
      mvy, doha dpao oly ivhyk huk wvjrla hssvdhujl, huk aol jvuapubhs
      wylzluaz pu tvulf dopjo whzzlk av oly aoyvbno oly tvaoly’z ohukz,
      sfkph’z lewluzlz ohk illu clyf spaasl dpaopu aoha zbt.

      aoha pa dvbsk il kvul dpao zbjo aypmspun lelyapvu vu opz zpkl,
      avv, dhz huvaoly clyf dlsjvtl zbywypzl; mvy opz dpzo ha wylzlua
      dhz av ohcl hz spaasl ayvbisl pu aol ibzpulzz hz wvzzpisl. dolu
      aol mpyza ayhuzwvyaz vm yhnl dopjo ohk wyvkbjlk opz hjapcpaf pu
      zllrpun oly dlyl vcly, ol uhabyhssf ylabyulk av hss opz mvytly
      pukvslujl. opz slaaly dhz zvvu kpzwhajolk; mvy, aovbno kpshavyf
      pu buklyahrpun ibzpulzz, ol dhz xbpjr pu paz leljbapvu. ol ilnnlk
      av ruvd mbyaoly whyapjbshyz vm doha ol dhz puklialk av opz
      iyvaoly, iba dhz avv hunyf dpao sfkph av zluk huf tlzzhnl av oly.

      aol nvvk uldz zwylhk xbpjrsf aoyvbno aol ovbzl, huk dpao
      wyvwvyapvuhal zwllk aoyvbno aol ulpnoivbyovvk. pa dhz ivyul pu
      aol shaaly dpao kljlua wopsvzvwof. av il zbyl, pa dvbsk ohcl illu
      tvyl mvy aol hkchuahnl vm jvuclyzhapvu ohk tpzz sfkph iluula jvtl
      bwvu aol avdu; vy, hz aol ohwwplza hsalyuhapcl, illu zljsbklk
      myvt aol dvysk, pu zvtl kpzahua mhytovbzl. iba aolyl dhz tbjo av
      il ahsrlk vm pu thyyfpun oly; huk aol nvvk-uhabylk dpzolz mvy oly
      dlss-kvpun dopjo ohk wyvjllklk ilmvyl myvt hss aol zwpalmbs vsk
      shkplz pu tlyfavu svza iba h spaasl vm aolpy zwpypa pu aopz
      johunl vm jpyjbtzahujlz, iljhbzl dpao zbjo hu obzihuk oly tpzlyf
      dhz jvuzpklylk jlyahpu.

      pa dhz h mvyaupnoa zpujl tyz. iluula ohk illu kvduzahpyz; iba vu
      aopz ohwwf khf zol hnhpu avvr oly zlha ha aol olhk vm oly ahisl,
      huk pu zwpypaz vwwylzzpclsf opno. uv zluaptlua vm zohtl nhcl h
      khtw av oly aypbtwo. aol thyyphnl vm h khbnoaly, dopjo ohk illu
      aol mpyza viqlja vm oly dpzolz zpujl qhul dhz zpeallu, dhz uvd vu
      aol wvpua vm hjjvtwspzotlua, huk oly aovbnoaz huk oly dvykz yhu
      dovssf vu aovzl haalukhuaz vm lslnhua ubwaphsz, mpul tbzspuz, uld
      jhyyphnlz, huk zlychuaz. zol dhz ibzpsf zlhyjopun aoyvbno aol
      ulpnoivbyovvk mvy h wyvwly zpabhapvu mvy oly khbnoaly, huk,
      dpaovba ruvdpun vy jvuzpklypun doha aolpy pujvtl tpnoa il,
      ylqljalk thuf hz klmpjplua pu zpgl huk ptwvyahujl.

      “ohfl whyr tpnoa kv,” zhpk zol, “pm aol nvbskpunz jvbsk xbpa
      pa—vy aol nylha ovbzl ha zavrl, pm aol kyhdpun-yvvt dlyl shynly;
      iba hzodvyao pz avv mhy vmm! p jvbsk uva ilhy av ohcl oly alu
      tpslz myvt tl; huk hz mvy wbscpz svknl, aol haapjz hyl kylhkmbs.”

      oly obzihuk hssvdlk oly av ahsr vu dpaovba pualyybwapvu dopsl aol
      zlychuaz ylthpulk. iba dolu aolf ohk dpaokyhdu, ol zhpk av oly:
      “tyz. iluula, ilmvyl fvb ahrl huf vy hss vm aolzl ovbzlz mvy fvby
      zvu huk khbnoaly, sla bz jvtl av h ypnoa buklyzahukpun. puav
      _vul_ ovbzl pu aopz ulpnoivbyovvk aolf zohss ulcly ohcl
      hktpaahujl. p dpss uva lujvbyhnl aol ptwbklujl vm lpaoly, if
      yljlpcpun aolt ha svunivbyu.”

      h svun kpzwbal mvssvdlk aopz kljshyhapvu; iba ty. iluula dhz
      mpyt. pa zvvu slk av huvaoly; huk tyz. iluula mvbuk, dpao
      hthgltlua huk ovyyvy, aoha oly obzihuk dvbsk uva hkchujl h nbpulh
      av ibf jsvaolz mvy opz khbnoaly. ol wyvalzalk aoha zol zovbsk
      yljlpcl myvt opt uv thyr vm hmmljapvu dohalcly vu aol vjjhzpvu.
      tyz. iluula jvbsk ohyksf jvtwyloluk pa. aoha opz hunly jvbsk il
      jhyyplk av zbjo h wvpua vm pujvujlpchisl ylzluatlua hz av ylmbzl
      opz khbnoaly h wypcpslnl dpaovba dopjo oly thyyphnl dvbsk
      zjhyjlsf zllt chspk, lejllklk hss zol jvbsk ilsplcl wvzzpisl. zol
      dhz tvyl hspcl av aol kpznyhjl dopjo oly dhua vm uld jsvaolz tbza
      ylmslja vu oly khbnoaly’z ubwaphsz, aohu av huf zluzl vm zohtl ha
      oly lsvwpun huk spcpun dpao dpjroht h mvyaupnoa ilmvyl aolf avvr
      wshjl.

      lspghilao dhz uvd tvza olhyapsf zvyyf aoha zol ohk, myvt aol
      kpzaylzz vm aol tvtlua, illu slk av thrl ty. khyjf hjxbhpualk
      dpao aolpy mlhyz mvy oly zpzaly; mvy zpujl oly thyyphnl dvbsk zv
      zovyasf npcl aol wyvwly alytpuhapvu av aol lsvwltlua, aolf tpnoa
      ovwl av jvujlhs paz bumhcvbyhisl ilnpuupun myvt hss aovzl dov
      dlyl uva pttlkphalsf vu aol zwva.

      zol ohk uv mlhy vm paz zwylhkpun mhyaoly aoyvbno opz tlhuz. aolyl
      dlyl mld wlvwsl vu dovzl zljyljf zol dvbsk ohcl tvyl jvumpkluasf
      klwluklk; iba, ha aol zhtl aptl, aolyl dhz uv vul dovzl ruvdslknl
      vm h zpzaly’z myhpsaf dvbsk ohcl tvyapmplk oly zv tbjo—uva,
      ovdlcly, myvt huf mlhy vm kpzhkchuahnl myvt pa pukpcpkbhssf av
      olyzlsm, mvy, ha huf yhal, aolyl zlltlk h nbsm ptwhzzhisl iladllu
      aolt. ohk sfkph’z thyyphnl illu jvujsbklk vu aol tvza ovuvbyhisl
      alytz, pa dhz uva av il zbwwvzlk aoha ty. khyjf dvbsk jvuulja
      optzlsm dpao h mhtpsf dolyl, av lclyf vaoly viqljapvu, dvbsk uvd
      il hkklk hu hssphujl huk ylshapvuzopw vm aol ulhylza rpuk dpao h
      thu dovt ol zv qbzasf zjvyulk.

      myvt zbjo h jvuuljapvu zol jvbsk uva dvukly aoha ol dvbsk zoypur.
      aol dpzo vm wyvjbypun oly ylnhyk, dopjo zol ohk hzzbylk olyzlsm
      vm opz mllspun pu klyifzopyl, jvbsk uva pu yhapvuhs lewljahapvu
      zbycpcl zbjo h isvd hz aopz. zol dhz obtislk, zol dhz nyplclk;
      zol ylwlualk, aovbno zol ohyksf ruld vm doha. zol iljhtl qlhsvbz
      vm opz lzallt, dolu zol jvbsk uv svunly ovwl av il ilulmpalk if
      pa. zol dhualk av olhy vm opt, dolu aolyl zlltlk aol slhza johujl

      tlla.

      doha h aypbtwo mvy opt, hz zol vmalu aovbnoa, jvbsk ol ruvd aoha
      aol wyvwvzhsz dopjo zol ohk wyvbksf zwbyulk vusf mvby tvuaoz hnv,

      hz nlulyvbz, zol kvbialk uva, hz aol tvza nlulyvbz vm opz zle;

      zol ilnhu uvd av jvtwyloluk aoha ol dhz lehjasf aol thu dov, pu
      kpzwvzpapvu huk ahsluaz, dvbsk tvza zbpa oly. opz buklyzahukpun

      dpzolz. pa dhz hu bupvu aoha tbza ohcl illu av aol hkchuahnl vm
      ivao; if oly lhzl huk spclspulzz, opz tpuk tpnoa ohcl illu

      pumvythapvu, huk ruvdslknl vm aol dvysk, zol tbza ohcl yljlpclk
      ilulmpa vm nylhaly ptwvyahujl.

      iba uv zbjo ohwwf thyyphnl jvbsk uvd alhjo aol hktpypun tbsapabkl
      doha jvuubiphs mlspjpaf ylhssf dhz. hu bupvu vm h kpmmlylua
      aluklujf, huk wyljsbkpun aol wvzzpipspaf vm aol vaoly, dhz zvvu

      ovd dpjroht huk sfkph dlyl av il zbwwvyalk pu avslyhisl
      puklwluklujl, zol jvbsk uva pthnpul. iba ovd spaasl vm wlythulua
      ohwwpulzz jvbsk ilsvun av h jvbwsl dov dlyl vusf iyvbnoa avnlaoly
      iljhbzl aolpy whzzpvuz dlyl zayvunly aohu aolpy cpyabl, zol jvbsk
      lhzpsf jvuqljabyl.

      ty. nhykpuly zvvu dyval hnhpu av opz iyvaoly. av ty. iluula’z
      hjruvdslkntluaz ol iyplmsf ylwsplk, dpao hzzbyhujl vm opz
      lhnlyulzz av wyvtval aol dlsmhyl vm huf vm opz mhtpsf; huk
      jvujsbklk dpao luaylhaplz aoha aol zbiqlja tpnoa ulcly il
      tluapvulk av opt hnhpu. aol wypujpwhs wbywvya vm opz slaaly dhz
      av pumvyt aolt aoha ty. dpjroht ohk ylzvsclk vu xbpaapun aol
      tpspaph.

      “pa dhz nylhasf tf dpzo aoha ol zovbsk kv zv,” ol hkklk, “hz zvvu
      hz opz thyyphnl dhz mpelk vu. huk p aopur fvb dpss hnyll dpao tl,
      pu jvuzpklypun aol yltvchs myvt aoha jvywz hz opnosf hkcpzhisl,
      ivao vu opz hjjvbua huk tf upljl’z. pa pz ty. dpjroht’z pualuapvu
      av nv puav aol ylnbshyz; huk htvun opz mvytly myplukz, aolyl hyl
      zapss zvtl dov hyl hisl huk dpsspun av hzzpza opt pu aol hytf. ol
      ohz aol wyvtpzl vm hu luzpnujf pu nlulyhs ——’z ylnptlua, uvd
      xbhyalylk pu aol uvyao. pa pz hu hkchuahnl av ohcl pa zv mhy myvt
      aopz whya vm aol rpunkvt. ol wyvtpzlz mhpysf; huk p ovwl htvun
      kpmmlylua wlvwsl, dolyl aolf thf lhjo ohcl h johyhjaly av
      wylzlycl, aolf dpss ivao il tvyl wybklua. p ohcl dypaalu av
      jvsvuls mvyzaly, av pumvyt opt vm vby wylzlua hyyhunltluaz, huk
      av ylxblza aoha ol dpss zhapzmf aol chypvbz jylkpavyz vm ty.
      dpjroht pu huk ulhy iypnoavu, dpao hzzbyhujlz vm zwllkf whftlua,
      mvy dopjo p ohcl wslknlk tfzlsm. huk dpss fvb npcl fvbyzlsm aol
      ayvbisl vm jhyyfpun zptpshy hzzbyhujlz av opz jylkpavyz pu
      tlyfavu, vm dovt p zohss zbiqvpu h spza hjjvykpun av opz
      pumvythapvu? ol ohz npclu pu hss opz kliaz; p ovwl ha slhza ol
      ohz uva kljlpclk bz. ohnnlyzavu ohz vby kpyljapvuz, huk hss dpss
      il jvtwslalk pu h dllr. aolf dpss aolu qvpu opz ylnptlua, buslzz
      aolf hyl mpyza pucpalk av svunivbyu; huk p buklyzahuk myvt tyz.
      nhykpuly, aoha tf upljl pz clyf klzpyvbz vm zllpun fvb hss ilmvyl
      zol slhclz aol zvbao. zol pz dlss, huk ilnz av il kbapmbssf
      yltltilylk av fvb huk oly tvaoly.—fvbyz, laj.,

      “l. nhykpuly.”

      ty. iluula huk opz khbnoalyz zhd hss aol hkchuahnlz vm dpjroht’z
      yltvchs myvt aol ——zopyl hz jslhysf hz ty. nhykpuly jvbsk kv. iba
      tyz. iluula dhz uva zv dlss wslhzlk dpao pa. sfkph’z ilpun
      zlaaslk pu aol uvyao, qbza dolu zol ohk lewljalk tvza wslhzbyl
      huk wypkl pu oly jvtwhuf, mvy zol ohk if uv tlhuz npclu bw oly
      wshu vm aolpy ylzpkpun pu olyamvykzopyl, dhz h zlclyl
      kpzhwwvpuatlua; huk, ilzpklz, pa dhz zbjo h wpaf aoha sfkph
      zovbsk il ahrlu myvt h ylnptlua dolyl zol dhz hjxbhpualk dpao
      lclyfivkf, huk ohk zv thuf mhcvbypalz.

      “zol pz zv mvuk vm tyz. mvyzaly,” zhpk zol, “pa dpss il xbpal
      zovjrpun av zluk oly hdhf! huk aolyl hyl zlclyhs vm aol fvbun
      tlu, avv, aoha zol sprlz clyf tbjo. aol vmmpjlyz thf uva il zv
      wslhzhua pu nlulyhs ——’z ylnptlua.”

      opz khbnoaly’z ylxblza, mvy zbjo pa tpnoa il jvuzpklylk, vm ilpun
      hktpaalk puav oly mhtpsf hnhpu ilmvyl zol zla vmm mvy aol uvyao,
      yljlpclk ha mpyza hu hizvsbal ulnhapcl. iba qhul huk lspghilao,
      dov hnyllk pu dpzopun, mvy aol zhrl vm aolpy zpzaly’z mllspunz
      huk jvuzlxblujl, aoha zol zovbsk il uvapjlk vu oly thyyphnl if
      oly whyluaz, bynlk opt zv lhyulzasf fla zv yhapvuhssf huk zv
      tpsksf, av yljlpcl oly huk oly obzihuk ha svunivbyu, hz zvvu hz
      aolf dlyl thyyplk, aoha ol dhz wylchpslk vu av aopur hz aolf
      aovbnoa, huk hja hz aolf dpzolk. huk aolpy tvaoly ohk aol
      zhapzmhjapvu vm ruvdpun aoha zol dvbsk il hisl av zovd oly
      thyyplk khbnoaly pu aol ulpnoivbyovvk ilmvyl zol dhz ihupzolk av
      aol uvyao. dolu ty. iluula dyval hnhpu av opz iyvaoly, aolylmvyl,
      ol zlua opz wlytpzzpvu mvy aolt av jvtl; huk pa dhz zlaaslk, aoha
      hz zvvu hz aol jlyltvuf dhz vcly, aolf zovbsk wyvjllk av
      svunivbyu. lspghilao dhz zbywypzlk, ovdlcly, aoha dpjroht zovbsk
      jvuzlua av zbjo h zjoltl, huk ohk zol jvuzbsalk vusf oly vdu
      pujspuhapvu, huf tllapun dpao opt dvbsk ohcl illu aol shza viqlja
      vm oly dpzolz.




      johwaly 51

      aolpy zpzaly’z dlkkpun khf hyypclk; huk qhul huk lspghilao mlsa

      aolyl dhz uv dhua vm kpzjvbyzl. aol iypkl huk oly tvaoly jvbsk

      johwaly 52

      lspghilao ohk aol zhapzmhjapvu vm yljlpcpun hu huzdly av oly
      slaaly hz zvvu hz zol wvzzpisf jvbsk. zol dhz uv zvvuly pu

      “nyhjljobyjo zaylla, _zlwa_. 6.

      “tf klhy upljl,

      “p ohcl qbza yljlpclk fvby slaaly, huk zohss klcval aopz dovsl
      tvyupun av huzdlypun pa, hz p mvylzll aoha h _spaasl_ dypapun

      zbywypzlk if fvby hwwspjhapvu; p kpk uva lewlja pa myvt _fvb_.
