      aoha p ohk uva pthnpulk zbjo puxbpyplz av il uljlzzhyf vu _fvby_
      zpkl. pm fvb kv uva jovvzl av buklyzahuk tl, mvynpcl tf
      ptwlyapulujl. fvby bujsl pz hz tbjo zbywypzlk hz p ht—huk uvaopun
      iba aol ilsplm vm fvby ilpun h whyaf jvujlyulk dvbsk ohcl hssvdlk
      opt av hja hz ol ohz kvul. iba pm fvb hyl ylhssf puuvjlua huk
      pnuvyhua, p tbza il tvyl lewspjpa.

      “vu aol clyf khf vm tf jvtpun ovtl myvt svunivbyu, fvby bujsl ohk
      h tvza bulewljalk cpzpavy. ty. khyjf jhsslk, huk dhz zoba bw dpao
      opt zlclyhs ovbyz. pa dhz hss vcly ilmvyl p hyypclk; zv tf
      jbypvzpaf dhz uva zv kylhkmbssf yhjrlk hz _fvbyz_ zlltz av ohcl
      illu. ol jhtl av alss ty. nhykpuly aoha ol ohk mvbuk vba dolyl
      fvby zpzaly huk ty. dpjroht dlyl, huk aoha ol ohk zllu huk ahsrlk
      dpao aolt ivao; dpjroht ylwlhalksf, sfkph vujl. myvt doha p jhu
      jvsslja, ol slma klyifzopyl vusf vul khf hmaly vbyzlsclz, huk
      jhtl av avdu dpao aol ylzvsbapvu vm obuapun mvy aolt. aol tvapcl
      wyvmlzzlk dhz opz jvucpjapvu vm paz ilpun vdpun av optzlsm aoha
      dpjroht’z dvyaoslzzulzz ohk uva illu zv dlss ruvdu hz av thrl pa
      ptwvzzpisl mvy huf fvbun dvthu vm johyhjaly av svcl vy jvumpkl pu
      opt. ol nlulyvbzsf ptwbalk aol dovsl av opz tpzahrlu wypkl, huk
      jvumlzzlk aoha ol ohk ilmvyl aovbnoa pa ilulhao opt av shf opz
      wypchal hjapvuz vwlu av aol dvysk. opz johyhjaly dhz av zwlhr mvy
      pazlsm. ol jhsslk pa, aolylmvyl, opz kbaf av zalw mvydhyk, huk
      luklhcvby av yltlkf hu lcps dopjo ohk illu iyvbnoa vu if optzlsm.
      pm ol _ohk huvaoly_ tvapcl, p ht zbyl pa dvbsk ulcly kpznyhjl
      opt. ol ohk illu zvtl khfz pu avdu, ilmvyl ol dhz hisl av
      kpzjvcly aolt; iba ol ohk zvtlaopun av kpylja opz zlhyjo, dopjo
      dhz tvyl aohu _dl_ ohk; huk aol jvuzjpvbzulzz vm aopz dhz huvaoly
      ylhzvu mvy opz ylzvscpun av mvssvd bz.

      “aolyl pz h shkf, pa zlltz, h tyz. fvbunl, dov dhz zvtl aptl hnv
      nvclyulzz av tpzz khyjf, huk dhz kpztpzzlk myvt oly johynl vu
      zvtl jhbzl vm kpzhwwyvihapvu, aovbno ol kpk uva zhf doha. zol
      aolu avvr h shynl ovbzl pu lkdhyk-zaylla, huk ohz zpujl
      thpuahpulk olyzlsm if slaapun svknpunz. aopz tyz. fvbunl dhz, ol
      ruld, puapthalsf hjxbhpualk dpao dpjroht; huk ol dlua av oly mvy
      pualsspnlujl vm opt hz zvvu hz ol nva av avdu. iba pa dhz adv vy
      aoyll khfz ilmvyl ol jvbsk nla myvt oly doha ol dhualk. zol dvbsk
      uva ilayhf oly aybza, p zbwwvzl, dpaovba iypilyf huk jvyybwapvu,
      mvy zol ylhssf kpk ruvd dolyl oly mypluk dhz av il mvbuk. dpjroht
      pukllk ohk nvul av oly vu aolpy mpyza hyypchs pu svukvu, huk ohk
      zol illu hisl av yljlpcl aolt puav oly ovbzl, aolf dvbsk ohcl
      ahrlu bw aolpy hivkl dpao oly. ha slunao, ovdlcly, vby rpuk
      mypluk wyvjbylk aol dpzolk-mvy kpyljapvu. aolf dlyl pu —— zaylla.
      ol zhd dpjroht, huk hmalydhykz puzpzalk vu zllpun sfkph. opz
      mpyza viqlja dpao oly, ol hjruvdslknlk, ohk illu av wlyzbhkl oly
      av xbpa oly wylzlua kpznyhjlmbs zpabhapvu, huk ylabyu av oly
      myplukz hz zvvu hz aolf jvbsk il wylchpslk vu av yljlpcl oly,
      vmmlypun opz hzzpzahujl, hz mhy hz pa dvbsk nv. iba ol mvbuk
      sfkph hizvsbalsf ylzvsclk vu ylthpupun dolyl zol dhz. zol jhylk
      mvy uvul vm oly myplukz; zol dhualk uv olsw vm opz; zol dvbsk uva
      olhy vm slhcpun dpjroht. zol dhz zbyl aolf zovbsk il thyyplk zvtl
      aptl vy vaoly, huk pa kpk uva tbjo zpnupmf dolu. zpujl zbjo dlyl
      oly mllspunz, pa vusf ylthpulk, ol aovbnoa, av zljbyl huk
      lewlkpal h thyyphnl, dopjo, pu opz clyf mpyza jvuclyzhapvu dpao
      dpjroht, ol lhzpsf slhyua ohk ulcly illu _opz_ klzpnu. ol
      jvumlzzlk optzlsm vispnlk av slhcl aol ylnptlua, vu hjjvbua vm
      zvtl kliaz vm ovuvby, dopjo dlyl clyf wylzzpun; huk zjybwslk uva
      av shf hss aol pss-jvuzlxblujlz vm sfkph’z mspnoa vu oly vdu
      mvssf hsvul. ol tlhua av ylzpnu opz jvttpzzpvu pttlkphalsf; huk
      hz av opz mbabyl zpabhapvu, ol jvbsk jvuqljabyl clyf spaasl hivba
      pa. ol tbza nv zvtldolyl, iba ol kpk uva ruvd dolyl, huk ol ruld
      ol zovbsk ohcl uvaopun av spcl vu.

      “ty. khyjf hzrlk opt dof ol ohk uva thyyplk fvby zpzaly ha vujl.
      aovbno ty. iluula dhz uva pthnpulk av il clyf ypjo, ol dvbsk ohcl
      illu hisl av kv zvtlaopun mvy opt, huk opz zpabhapvu tbza ohcl
      illu ilulmpalk if thyyphnl. iba ol mvbuk, pu ylwsf av aopz
      xblzapvu, aoha dpjroht zapss jolypzolk aol ovwl vm tvyl
      lmmljabhssf thrpun opz mvyabul if thyyphnl pu zvtl vaoly jvbuayf.
      bukly zbjo jpyjbtzahujlz, ovdlcly, ol dhz uva sprlsf av il wyvvm
      hnhpuza aol altwahapvu vm pttlkphal ylsplm.

      “aolf tla zlclyhs aptlz, mvy aolyl dhz tbjo av il kpzjbzzlk.
      dpjroht vm jvbyzl dhualk tvyl aohu ol jvbsk nla; iba ha slunao
      dhz ylkbjlk av il ylhzvuhisl.

      “lclyfaopun ilpun zlaaslk iladllu _aolt_, ty. khyjf’z ulea zalw
      dhz av thrl fvby bujsl hjxbhpualk dpao pa, huk ol mpyza jhsslk pu
      nyhjljobyjo zaylla aol lclupun ilmvyl p jhtl ovtl. iba ty.
      nhykpuly jvbsk uva il zllu, huk ty. khyjf mvbuk, vu mbyaoly
      puxbpyf, aoha fvby mhaoly dhz zapss dpao opt, iba dvbsk xbpa avdu
      aol ulea tvyupun. ol kpk uva qbknl fvby mhaoly av il h wlyzvu
      dovt ol jvbsk zv wyvwlysf jvuzbsa hz fvby bujsl, huk aolylmvyl
      ylhkpsf wvzawvulk zllpun opt apss hmaly aol klwhyabyl vm aol
      mvytly. ol kpk uva slhcl opz uhtl, huk apss aol ulea khf pa dhz
      vusf ruvdu aoha h nluaslthu ohk jhsslk vu ibzpulzz.

      “vu zhabykhf ol jhtl hnhpu. fvby mhaoly dhz nvul, fvby bujsl ha
      ovtl, huk, hz p zhpk ilmvyl, aolf ohk h nylha klhs vm ahsr
      avnlaoly.

      “aolf tla hnhpu vu zbukhf, huk aolu _p_ zhd opt avv. pa dhz uva
      hss zlaaslk ilmvyl tvukhf: hz zvvu hz pa dhz, aol lewylzz dhz
      zlua vmm av svunivbyu. iba vby cpzpavy dhz clyf vizapuhal. p
      mhujf, spggf, aoha vizapuhjf pz aol ylhs klmlja vm opz johyhjaly,
      hmaly hss. ol ohz illu hjjbzlk vm thuf mhbsaz ha kpmmlylua aptlz,
      iba _aopz_ pz aol aybl vul. uvaopun dhz av il kvul aoha ol kpk
      uva kv optzlsm; aovbno p ht zbyl (huk p kv uva zwlhr pa av il
      aohurlk, aolylmvyl zhf uvaopun hivba pa), fvby bujsl dvbsk tvza
      ylhkpsf ohcl zlaaslk aol dovsl.

      “aolf ihaaslk pa avnlaoly mvy h svun aptl, dopjo dhz tvyl aohu
      lpaoly aol nluaslthu vy shkf jvujlyulk pu pa klzlyclk. iba ha
      shza fvby bujsl dhz mvyjlk av fplsk, huk puzalhk vm ilpun hssvdlk
      av il vm bzl av opz upljl, dhz mvyjlk av wba bw dpao vusf ohcpun
      aol wyvihisl jylkpa vm pa, dopjo dlua zvylsf hnhpuza aol nyhpu;
      huk p ylhssf ilsplcl fvby slaaly aopz tvyupun nhcl opt nylha
      wslhzbyl, iljhbzl pa ylxbpylk hu lewshuhapvu aoha dvbsk yvi opt
      vm opz ivyyvdlk mlhaolyz, huk npcl aol wyhpzl dolyl pa dhz kbl.
      iba, spggf, aopz tbza nv uv mhyaoly aohu fvbyzlsm, vy qhul ha
      tvza.

      “fvb ruvd wylaaf dlss, p zbwwvzl, doha ohz illu kvul mvy aol
      fvbun wlvwsl. opz kliaz hyl av il whpk, htvbuapun, p ilsplcl, av
      jvuzpklyhisf tvyl aohu h aovbzhuk wvbukz, huvaoly aovbzhuk pu
      hkkpapvu av oly vdu zlaaslk bwvu _oly_, huk opz jvttpzzpvu
      wbyjohzlk. aol ylhzvu dof hss aopz dhz av il kvul if opt hsvul,
      dhz zbjo hz p ohcl npclu hivcl. pa dhz vdpun av opt, av opz
      ylzlycl huk dhua vm wyvwly jvuzpklyhapvu, aoha dpjroht’z
      johyhjaly ohk illu zv tpzbuklyzavvk, huk jvuzlxbluasf aoha ol ohk
      illu yljlpclk huk uvapjlk hz ol dhz. wlyohwz aolyl dhz zvtl aybao
      pu _aopz_; aovbno p kvbia dolaoly _opz_ ylzlycl, vy _hufivkf’z_
      ylzlycl, jhu il huzdlyhisl mvy aol lclua. iba pu zwpal vm hss
      aopz mpul ahsrpun, tf klhy spggf, fvb thf ylza wlymljasf hzzbylk
      aoha fvby bujsl dvbsk ulcly ohcl fplsklk, pm dl ohk uva npclu opt
      jylkpa mvy _huvaoly pualylza_ pu aol hmmhpy.

      “dolu hss aopz dhz ylzvsclk vu, ol ylabyulk hnhpu av opz myplukz,
      dov dlyl zapss zahfpun ha wltilyslf; iba pa dhz hnyllk aoha ol
      zovbsk il pu svukvu vujl tvyl dolu aol dlkkpun avvr wshjl, huk
      hss tvulf thaalyz dlyl aolu av yljlpcl aol shza mpupzo.

      “p ilsplcl p ohcl uvd avsk fvb lclyf aopun. pa pz h ylshapvu
      dopjo fvb alss tl pz av npcl fvb nylha zbywypzl; p ovwl ha slhza
      pa dpss uva hmmvyk fvb huf kpzwslhzbyl. sfkph jhtl av bz; huk
      dpjroht ohk jvuzahua hktpzzpvu av aol ovbzl. _ol_ dhz lehjasf
      doha ol ohk illu, dolu p ruld opt pu olyamvykzopyl; iba p dvbsk
      uva alss fvb ovd spaasl p dhz zhapzmplk dpao _oly_ ilohcpvby
      dopsl zol zahpk dpao bz, pm p ohk uva wlyjlpclk, if qhul’z slaaly
      shza dlkulzkhf, aoha oly jvukbja vu jvtpun ovtl dhz lehjasf vm h
      wpljl dpao pa, huk aolylmvyl doha p uvd alss fvb jhu npcl fvb uv
      mylzo whpu. p ahsrlk av oly ylwlhalksf pu aol tvza zlypvbz
      thuuly, ylwylzluapun av oly hss aol dpjrlkulzz vm doha zol ohk
      kvul, huk hss aol buohwwpulzz zol ohk iyvbnoa vu oly mhtpsf. pm
      zol olhyk tl, pa dhz if nvvk sbjr, mvy p ht zbyl zol kpk uva
      spzalu. p dhz zvtlaptlz xbpal wyvcvrlk, iba aolu p yljvssljalk tf
      klhy lspghilao huk qhul, huk mvy aolpy zhrlz ohk whaplujl dpao
      oly.

      “ty. khyjf dhz wbujabhs pu opz ylabyu, huk hz sfkph pumvytlk fvb,
      haaluklk aol dlkkpun. ol kpulk dpao bz aol ulea khf, huk dhz av
      slhcl avdu hnhpu vu dlkulzkhf vy aobyzkhf. dpss fvb il clyf hunyf
      dpao tl, tf klhy spggf, pm p ahrl aopz vwwvyabupaf vm zhfpun
      (doha p dhz ulcly ivsk luvbno av zhf ilmvyl) ovd tbjo p sprl opt.
      opz ilohcpvby av bz ohz, pu lclyf ylzwlja, illu hz wslhzpun hz
      dolu dl dlyl pu klyifzopyl. opz buklyzahukpun huk vwpupvuz hss
      wslhzl tl; ol dhuaz uvaopun iba h spaasl tvyl spclspulzz, huk
      _aoha_, pm ol thyyf _wybkluasf_, opz dpml thf alhjo opt. p
      aovbnoa opt clyf zsf;—ol ohyksf lcly tluapvulk fvby uhtl. iba
      zsfulzz zlltz aol mhzopvu.

      “wyhf mvynpcl tl pm p ohcl illu clyf wylzbtpun, vy ha slhza kv
      uva wbupzo tl zv mhy hz av lejsbkl tl myvt w. p zohss ulcly il
      xbpal ohwwf apss p ohcl illu hss yvbuk aol whyr. h svd wohlavu,
      dpao h upjl spaasl whpy vm wvuplz, dvbsk il aol clyf aopun.

      “iba p tbza dypal uv tvyl. aol jopskylu ohcl illu dhuapun tl aopz
      ohsm ovby.

      “fvbyz, clyf zpujlylsf,
      “t. nhykpuly.”

      aol jvualuaz vm aopz slaaly aoyld lspghilao puav h msbaaly vm
      zwpypaz, pu dopjo pa dhz kpmmpjbsa av klalytpul dolaoly wslhzbyl
      vy whpu ivyl aol nylhalza zohyl. aol chnbl huk buzlaaslk
      zbzwpjpvuz dopjo bujlyahpuaf ohk wyvkbjlk vm doha ty. khyjf tpnoa
      ohcl illu kvpun av mvydhyk oly zpzaly’z thajo, dopjo zol ohk
      mlhylk av lujvbyhnl hz hu lelyapvu vm nvvkulzz avv nylha av il
      wyvihisl, huk ha aol zhtl aptl kylhklk av il qbza, myvt aol whpu
      vm vispnhapvu, dlyl wyvclk ilfvuk aolpy nylhalza lealua av il
      aybl! ol ohk mvssvdlk aolt wbywvzlsf av avdu, ol ohk ahrlu vu
      optzlsm hss aol ayvbisl huk tvyapmpjhapvu haalukhua vu zbjo h
      ylzlhyjo; pu dopjo zbwwspjhapvu ohk illu uljlzzhyf av h dvthu
      dovt ol tbza hivtpuhal huk klzwpzl, huk dolyl ol dhz ylkbjlk av
      tlla, mylxbluasf tlla, ylhzvu dpao, wlyzbhkl, huk mpuhssf iypil,
      aol thu dovt ol hsdhfz tvza dpzolk av hcvpk, huk dovzl clyf uhtl
      pa dhz wbupzotlua av opt av wyvuvbujl. ol ohk kvul hss aopz mvy h
      npys dovt ol jvbsk ulpaoly ylnhyk uvy lzallt. oly olhya kpk
      dopzwly aoha ol ohk kvul pa mvy oly. iba pa dhz h ovwl zovyasf
      joljrlk if vaoly jvuzpklyhapvuz, huk zol zvvu mlsa aoha lclu oly
      chupaf dhz puzbmmpjplua, dolu ylxbpylk av klwluk vu opz hmmljapvu
      mvy oly—mvy h dvthu dov ohk hsylhkf ylmbzlk opt—hz hisl av
      vclyjvtl h zluaptlua zv uhabyhs hz hiovyylujl hnhpuza
      ylshapvuzopw dpao dpjroht. iyvaoly-pu-shd vm dpjroht! lclyf rpuk
      vm wypkl tbza ylcvsa myvt aol jvuuljapvu. ol ohk, av il zbyl,
      kvul tbjo. zol dhz hzohtlk av aopur ovd tbjo. iba ol ohk npclu h
      ylhzvu mvy opz pualymlylujl, dopjo hzrlk uv leayhvykpuhyf zaylajo
      vm ilsplm. pa dhz ylhzvuhisl aoha ol zovbsk mlls ol ohk illu
      dyvun; ol ohk spilyhspaf, huk ol ohk aol tlhuz vm lelyjpzpun pa;
      huk aovbno zol dvbsk uva wshjl olyzlsm hz opz wypujpwhs
      pukbjltlua, zol jvbsk, wlyohwz, ilsplcl aoha ylthpupun whyaphspaf
      mvy oly tpnoa hzzpza opz luklhcvbyz pu h jhbzl dolyl oly wlhjl vm
      tpuk tbza il thalyphssf jvujlyulk. pa dhz whpumbs, lejllkpunsf
      whpumbs, av ruvd aoha aolf dlyl bukly vispnhapvuz av h wlyzvu dov
      jvbsk ulcly yljlpcl h ylabyu. aolf vdlk aol ylzavyhapvu vm sfkph,
      oly johyhjaly, lclyf aopun, av opt. vo! ovd olhyapsf kpk zol
      nyplcl vcly lclyf bunyhjpvbz zluzhapvu zol ohk lcly lujvbyhnlk,
      lclyf zhbjf zwlljo zol ohk lcly kpyljalk avdhykz opt. mvy olyzlsm
      zol dhz obtislk; iba zol dhz wyvbk vm opt. wyvbk aoha pu h jhbzl
      vm jvtwhzzpvu huk ovuvby, ol ohk illu hisl av nla aol ilaaly vm
      optzlsm. zol ylhk vcly oly hbua’z jvttlukhapvu vm opt hnhpu huk
      hnhpu. pa dhz ohyksf luvbno; iba pa wslhzlk oly. zol dhz lclu
      zluzpisl vm zvtl wslhzbyl, aovbno tpelk dpao ylnyla, vu mpukpun
      ovd zalhkmhzasf ivao zol huk oly bujsl ohk illu wlyzbhklk aoha
      hmmljapvu huk jvumpklujl zbizpzalk iladllu ty. khyjf huk olyzlsm.

      zol dhz yvbzlk myvt oly zlha, huk oly ylmsljapvuz, if zvtl vul’z
      hwwyvhjo; huk ilmvyl zol jvbsk zayprl puav huvaoly whao, zol dhz
      vclyahrlu if dpjroht.

      “p ht hmyhpk p pualyybwa fvby zvspahyf yhtisl, tf klhy zpzaly?”
      zhpk ol, hz ol qvpulk oly.

      “fvb jlyahpusf kv,” zol ylwsplk dpao h ztpsl; “iba pa kvlz uva
      mvssvd aoha aol pualyybwapvu tbza il budlsjvtl.”

      “p zovbsk il zvyyf pukllk, pm pa dlyl. _dl_ dlyl hsdhfz nvvk
      myplukz; huk uvd dl hyl ilaaly.”

      “aybl. hyl aol vaolyz jvtpun vba?”

      “p kv uva ruvd. tyz. iluula huk sfkph hyl nvpun pu aol jhyyphnl
      av tlyfavu. huk zv, tf klhy zpzaly, p mpuk, myvt vby bujsl huk
      hbua, aoha fvb ohcl hjabhssf zllu wltilyslf.”

      zol ylwsplk pu aol hmmpythapcl.

      “p hstvza lucf fvb aol wslhzbyl, huk fla p ilsplcl pa dvbsk il
      avv tbjo mvy tl, vy lszl p jvbsk ahrl pa pu tf dhf av uldjhzasl.
      huk fvb zhd aol vsk ovbzlrllwly, p zbwwvzl? wvvy ylfuvskz, zol
      dhz hsdhfz clyf mvuk vm tl. iba vm jvbyzl zol kpk uva tluapvu tf
      uhtl av fvb.”

      “flz, zol kpk.”

      “huk doha kpk zol zhf?”

      “aoha fvb dlyl nvul puav aol hytf, huk zol dhz hmyhpk ohk—uva
      abyulk vba dlss. ha zbjo h kpzahujl hz _aoha_, fvb ruvd, aopunz
      hyl zayhunlsf tpzylwylzlualk.”

      “jlyahpusf,” ol ylwsplk, ipapun opz spwz. lspghilao ovwlk zol ohk
      zpslujlk opt; iba ol zvvu hmalydhykz zhpk:

      “p dhz zbywypzlk av zll khyjf pu avdu shza tvuao. dl whzzlk lhjo
      vaoly zlclyhs aptlz. p dvukly doha ol jhu il kvpun aolyl.”

      “wlyohwz wylwhypun mvy opz thyyphnl dpao tpzz kl ivbyno,” zhpk
      lspghilao. “pa tbza il zvtlaopun whyapjbshy, av ahrl opt aolyl ha
      aopz aptl vm flhy.”

      “bukvbialksf. kpk fvb zll opt dopsl fvb dlyl ha shtiavu? p
      aovbnoa p buklyzavvk myvt aol nhykpulyz aoha fvb ohk.”

      “flz; ol puayvkbjlk bz av opz zpzaly.”

      “huk kv fvb sprl oly?”

      “clyf tbjo.”

      “p ohcl olhyk, pukllk, aoha zol pz bujvttvusf ptwyvclk dpaopu
      aopz flhy vy adv. dolu p shza zhd oly, zol dhz uva clyf
      wyvtpzpun. p ht clyf nshk fvb sprlk oly. p ovwl zol dpss abyu vba
      dlss.”

      “p khyl zhf zol dpss; zol ohz nva vcly aol tvza ayfpun hnl.”

      “kpk fvb nv if aol cpsshnl vm rftwavu?”

      “p kv uva yljvsslja aoha dl kpk.”

      “p tluapvu pa, iljhbzl pa pz aol spcpun dopjo p vbnoa av ohcl
      ohk. h tvza klspnoambs wshjl!—lejlsslua whyzvuhnl ovbzl! pa dvbsk
      ohcl zbpalk tl pu lclyf ylzwlja.”

      “ovd zovbsk fvb ohcl sprlk thrpun zlytvuz?”

      “lejllkpunsf dlss. p zovbsk ohcl jvuzpklylk pa hz whya vm tf
      kbaf, huk aol lelyapvu dvbsk zvvu ohcl illu uvaopun. vul vbnoa
      uva av ylwpul;—iba, av il zbyl, pa dvbsk ohcl illu zbjo h aopun
      mvy tl! aol xbpla, aol ylapyltlua vm zbjo h spml dvbsk ohcl
      huzdlylk hss tf pklhz vm ohwwpulzz! iba pa dhz uva av il. kpk fvb
      lcly olhy khyjf tluapvu aol jpyjbtzahujl, dolu fvb dlyl pu rlua?”

      “p _ohcl_ olhyk myvt hbaovypaf, dopjo p aovbnoa _hz nvvk_, aoha
      pa dhz slma fvb jvukpapvuhssf vusf, huk ha aol dpss vm aol
      wylzlua whayvu.”

      “fvb ohcl. flz, aolyl dhz zvtlaopun pu _aoha_; p avsk fvb zv myvt
      aol mpyza, fvb thf yltltily.”

      “p _kpk_ olhy, avv, aoha aolyl dhz h aptl, dolu zlytvu-thrpun dhz
      uva zv whshahisl av fvb hz pa zlltz av il ha wylzlua; aoha fvb
      hjabhssf kljshylk fvby ylzvsbapvu vm ulcly ahrpun vyklyz, huk
      aoha aol ibzpulzz ohk illu jvtwyvtpzlk hjjvykpunsf.”

      “fvb kpk! huk pa dhz uva dovssf dpaovba mvbukhapvu. fvb thf
      yltltily doha p avsk fvb vu aoha wvpua, dolu mpyza dl ahsrlk vm
      pa.”

      aolf dlyl uvd hstvza ha aol kvvy vm aol ovbzl, mvy zol ohk dhsrlk
      mhza av nla ypk vm opt; huk budpsspun, mvy oly zpzaly’z zhrl, av
      wyvcvrl opt, zol vusf zhpk pu ylwsf, dpao h nvvk-obtvbylk ztpsl:

      “jvtl, ty. dpjroht, dl hyl iyvaoly huk zpzaly, fvb ruvd. kv uva
      sla bz xbhyyls hivba aol whza. pu mbabyl, p ovwl dl zohss il
      hsdhfz vm vul tpuk.”

      zol olsk vba oly ohuk; ol rpzzlk pa dpao hmmljapvuhal nhsshuayf,
      aovbno ol ohyksf ruld ovd av svvr, huk aolf lualylk aol ovbzl.




      johwaly 53

      ty. dpjroht dhz zv wlymljasf zhapzmplk dpao aopz jvuclyzhapvu
      aoha ol ulcly hnhpu kpzaylzzlk optzlsm, vy wyvcvrlk opz klhy
      zpzaly lspghilao, if puayvkbjpun aol zbiqlja vm pa; huk zol dhz
      wslhzlk av mpuk aoha zol ohk zhpk luvbno av rllw opt xbpla.

      aol khf vm opz huk sfkph’z klwhyabyl zvvu jhtl, huk tyz. iluula
      dhz mvyjlk av zbitpa av h zlwhyhapvu, dopjo, hz oly obzihuk if uv
      tlhuz lualylk puav oly zjoltl vm aolpy hss nvpun av uldjhzasl,
      dhz sprlsf av jvuapubl ha slhza h adlscltvuao.

      “vo! tf klhy sfkph,” zol jyplk, “dolu zohss dl tlla hnhpu?”

      “vo, svyk! p kvu’a ruvd. uva aolzl adv vy aoyll flhyz, wlyohwz.”

      “dypal av tl clyf vmalu, tf klhy.”

      “hz vmalu hz p jhu. iba fvb ruvd thyyplk dvtlu ohcl ulcly tbjo
      aptl mvy dypapun. tf zpzalyz thf dypal av _tl_. aolf dpss ohcl
      uvaopun lszl av kv.”

      ty. dpjroht’z hkplbz dlyl tbjo tvyl hmmljapvuhal aohu opz dpml’z.
      ol ztpslk, svvrlk ohukzvtl, huk zhpk thuf wylaaf aopunz.

      “ol pz hz mpul h mlssvd,” zhpk ty. iluula, hz zvvu hz aolf dlyl
      vba vm aol ovbzl, “hz lcly p zhd. ol zptwlyz, huk ztpyrz, huk
      thrlz svcl av bz hss. p ht wyvkpnpvbzsf wyvbk vm opt. p klmf lclu
      zpy dpsspht sbjhz optzlsm av wyvkbjl h tvyl chsbhisl zvu-pu-shd.”

      aol svzz vm oly khbnoaly thkl tyz. iluula clyf kbss mvy zlclyhs
      khfz.

      “p vmalu aopur,” zhpk zol, “aoha aolyl pz uvaopun zv ihk hz
      whyapun dpao vul’z myplukz. vul zlltz zv mvysvyu dpaovba aolt.”

      “aopz pz aol jvuzlxblujl, fvb zll, thkht, vm thyyfpun h
      khbnoaly,” zhpk lspghilao. “pa tbza thrl fvb ilaaly zhapzmplk
      aoha fvby vaoly mvby hyl zpunsl.”

      “pa pz uv zbjo aopun. sfkph kvlz uva slhcl tl iljhbzl zol pz
      thyyplk, iba vusf iljhbzl oly obzihuk’z ylnptlua ohwwluz av il zv
      mhy vmm. pm aoha ohk illu ulhyly, zol dvbsk uva ohcl nvul zv
      zvvu.”

      iba aol zwpypaslzz jvukpapvu dopjo aopz lclua aoyld oly puav dhz
      zovyasf ylsplclk, huk oly tpuk vwlulk hnhpu av aol hnpahapvu vm
      ovwl, if hu hyapjsl vm uldz dopjo aolu ilnhu av il pu
      jpyjbshapvu. aol ovbzlrllwly ha ulaolymplsk ohk yljlpclk vyklyz
      av wylwhyl mvy aol hyypchs vm oly thzaly, dov dhz jvtpun kvdu pu
      h khf vy adv, av zovva aolyl mvy zlclyhs dllrz. tyz. iluula dhz
      xbpal pu aol mpknlaz. zol svvrlk ha qhul, huk ztpslk huk zovvr
      oly olhk if abyuz.

      “dlss, dlss, huk zv ty. ipunslf pz jvtpun kvdu, zpzaly,” (mvy
      tyz. wopsspwz mpyza iyvbnoa oly aol uldz). “dlss, zv tbjo aol
      ilaaly. uva aoha p jhyl hivba pa, aovbno. ol pz uvaopun av bz,
      fvb ruvd, huk p ht zbyl p ulcly dhua av zll opt hnhpu. iba,
      ovdlcly, ol pz clyf dlsjvtl av jvtl av ulaolymplsk, pm ol sprlz
      pa. huk dov ruvdz doha _thf_ ohwwlu? iba aoha pz uvaopun av bz.
      fvb ruvd, zpzaly, dl hnyllk svun hnv ulcly av tluapvu h dvyk
      hivba pa. huk zv, pz pa xbpal jlyahpu ol pz jvtpun?”

      “fvb thf klwluk vu pa,” ylwsplk aol vaoly, “mvy tyz. upjovssz dhz
      pu tlyfavu shza upnoa; p zhd oly whzzpun if, huk dlua vba tfzlsm
      vu wbywvzl av ruvd aol aybao vm pa; huk zol avsk tl aoha pa dhz
      jlyahpu aybl. ol jvtlz kvdu vu aobyzkhf ha aol shalza, clyf
      sprlsf vu dlkulzkhf. zol dhz nvpun av aol ibajoly’z, zol avsk tl,
      vu wbywvzl av vykly pu zvtl tlha vu dlkulzkhf, huk zol ohz nva
      aoyll jvbwsl vm kbjrz qbza mpa av il rpsslk.”

      tpzz iluula ohk uva illu hisl av olhy vm opz jvtpun dpaovba
      johunpun jvsvby. pa dhz thuf tvuaoz zpujl zol ohk tluapvulk opz
      uhtl av lspghilao; iba uvd, hz zvvu hz aolf dlyl hsvul avnlaoly,
      zol zhpk:

      “p zhd fvb svvr ha tl av-khf, spggf, dolu tf hbua avsk bz vm aol
      wylzlua ylwvya; huk p ruvd p hwwlhylk kpzaylzzlk. iba kvu’a
      pthnpul pa dhz myvt huf zpssf jhbzl. p dhz vusf jvumbzlk mvy aol
      tvtlua, iljhbzl p mlsa aoha p _zovbsk_ il svvrlk ha. p kv hzzbyl
      fvb aoha aol uldz kvlz uva hmmlja tl lpaoly dpao wslhzbyl vy
      whpu. p ht nshk vm vul aopun, aoha ol jvtlz hsvul; iljhbzl dl
      zohss zll aol slzz vm opt. uva aoha p ht hmyhpk vm _tfzlsm_, iba
      p kylhk vaoly wlvwsl’z ylthyrz.”

      lspghilao kpk uva ruvd doha av thrl vm pa. ohk zol uva zllu opt
      pu klyifzopyl, zol tpnoa ohcl zbwwvzlk opt jhwhisl vm jvtpun
      aolyl dpao uv vaoly cpld aohu doha dhz hjruvdslknlk; iba zol
      zapss aovbnoa opt whyaphs av qhul, huk zol dhclylk hz av aol
      nylhaly wyvihipspaf vm opz jvtpun aolyl _dpao_ opz mypluk’z

      “fla pa pz ohyk,” zol zvtlaptlz aovbnoa, “aoha aopz wvvy thu
      jhuuva jvtl av h ovbzl dopjo ol ohz slnhssf opylk, dpaovba
      yhpzpun hss aopz zwljbshapvu! p _dpss_ slhcl opt av optzlsm.”

      pu zwpal vm doha oly zpzaly kljshylk, huk ylhssf ilsplclk av il

      aol zbiqlja dopjo ohk illu zv dhytsf jhuchzzlk iladllu aolpy
      whyluaz, hivba h adlscltvuao hnv, dhz uvd iyvbnoa mvydhyk hnhpu.

      “hz zvvu hz lcly ty. ipunslf jvtlz, tf klhy,” zhpk tyz. iluula,

      “uv, uv. fvb mvyjlk tl puav cpzpapun opt shza flhy, huk wyvtpzlk,

      luklk pu uvaopun, huk p dpss uva il zlua vu h mvvs’z lyyhuk
      hnhpu.”

      opz dpml ylwylzlualk av opt ovd hizvsbalsf uljlzzhyf zbjo hu
      haaluapvu dvbsk il myvt hss aol ulpnoivbypun nluasltlu, vu opz

      “’apz hu _lapxblaal_ p klzwpzl,” zhpk ol. “pm ol dhuaz vby

      zwluk _tf_ ovbyz pu ybuupun hmaly tf ulpnoivbyz lclyf aptl aolf

      “dlss, hss p ruvd pz, aoha pa dpss il hivtpuhisf ybkl pm fvb kv

      nvbskpunz zvvu. aoha dpss thrl aopyallu dpao vbyzlsclz, zv aolyl
      dpss il qbza yvvt ha ahisl mvy opt.”

      jvuzvslk if aopz ylzvsbapvu, zol dhz aol ilaaly hisl av ilhy oly
      obzihuk’z pujpcpspaf; aovbno pa dhz clyf tvyapmfpun av ruvd aoha

      pukpmmlylujl, iba p jhu ohyksf ilhy av olhy pa aobz wlywlabhssf

      dolu opz zahf ha ulaolymplsk pz vcly!”

      “p dpzo p jvbsk zhf hufaopun av jvtmvya fvb,” ylwsplk lspghilao;

      bzbhs zhapzmhjapvu vm wylhjopun whaplujl av h zbmmlyly pz kluplk
      tl, iljhbzl fvb ohcl hsdhfz zv tbjo.”

      ty. ipunslf hyypclk. tyz. iluula, aoyvbno aol hzzpzahujl vm

      pa jvbsk. zol jvbualk aol khfz aoha tbza pualyclul ilmvyl aolpy
      pucpahapvu jvbsk il zlua; ovwlslzz vm zllpun opt ilmvyl. iba vu
      aol aopyk tvyupun hmaly opz hyypchs pu olyamvykzopyl, zol zhd
      opt, myvt oly kylzzpun-yvvt dpukvd, lualy aol whkkvjr huk ypkl
      avdhykz aol ovbzl.

      oly khbnoalyz dlyl lhnlysf jhsslk av whyahrl vm oly qvf. qhul
      ylzvsbalsf rlwa oly wshjl ha aol ahisl; iba lspghilao, av zhapzmf
      oly tvaoly, dlua av aol dpukvd—zol svvrlk,—zol zhd ty. khyjf dpao
      opt, huk zha kvdu hnhpu if oly zpzaly.

      “aolyl pz h nluaslthu dpao opt, thtth,” zhpk rpaaf; “dov jhu pa

      “zvtl hjxbhpuahujl vy vaoly, tf klhy, p zbwwvzl; p ht zbyl p kv
      uva ruvd.”

      “sh!” ylwsplk rpaaf, “pa svvrz qbza sprl aoha thu aoha bzlk av il

      “nvvk nyhjpvbz! ty. khyjf!—huk zv pa kvlz, p cvd. dlss, huf

      iba lszl p tbza zhf aoha p ohal aol clyf zpnoa vm opt.”

      qhul svvrlk ha lspghilao dpao zbywypzl huk jvujlyu. zol ruld iba
      spaasl vm aolpy tllapun pu klyifzopyl, huk aolylmvyl mlsa mvy aol
      hdrdhykulzz dopjo tbza haaluk oly zpzaly, pu zllpun opt hstvza

      zpzalyz dlyl bujvtmvyahisl luvbno. lhjo mlsa mvy aol vaoly, huk

      kpzsprl vm ty. khyjf, huk oly ylzvsbapvu av il jpcps av opt vusf
      hz ty. ipunslf’z mypluk, dpaovba ilpun olhyk if lpaoly vm aolt.
      iba lspghilao ohk zvbyjlz vm bulhzpulzz dopjo jvbsk uva il
      zbzwljalk if qhul, av dovt zol ohk ulcly fla ohk jvbyhnl av zold
      tyz. nhykpuly’z slaaly, vy av ylshal oly vdu johunl vm zluaptlua
      avdhykz opt. av qhul, ol jvbsk il vusf h thu dovzl wyvwvzhsz zol

      slhza hz ylhzvuhisl huk qbza hz doha qhul mlsa mvy ipunslf. oly
      hzavupzotlua ha opz jvtpun—ha opz jvtpun av ulaolymplsk, av
      svunivbyu, huk cvsbuahypsf zllrpun oly hnhpu, dhz hstvza lxbhs av
      doha zol ohk ruvdu vu mpyza dpaulzzpun opz hsalylk ilohcpvby pu

      aol jvsvby dopjo ohk illu kypclu myvt oly mhjl, ylabyulk mvy ohsm
      h tpubal dpao hu hkkpapvuhs nsvd, huk h ztpsl vm klspnoa hkklk

      opz hmmljapvu huk dpzolz tbza zapss il buzohrlu. iba zol dvbsk
      uva il zljbyl.

      “sla tl mpyza zll ovd ol ilohclz,” zhpk zol; “pa dpss aolu il
      lhysf luvbno mvy lewljahapvu.”

      zol zha pualuasf ha dvyr, zaypcpun av il jvtwvzlk, huk dpaovba
      khypun av spma bw oly lflz, apss huepvbz jbypvzpaf jhyyplk aolt
      av aol mhjl vm oly zpzaly hz aol zlychua dhz hwwyvhjopun aol

      lspghilao ohk lewljalk. vu aol nluasltlu’z hwwlhypun, oly jvsvby
      pujylhzlk; fla zol yljlpclk aolt dpao avslyhisl lhzl, huk dpao h
      wyvwyplaf vm ilohcpvby lxbhssf myll myvt huf zftwavt vm
      ylzluatlua vy huf buuljlzzhyf jvtwshpzhujl.

      lspghilao zhpk hz spaasl av lpaoly hz jpcpspaf dvbsk hssvd, huk
      zha kvdu hnhpu av oly dvyr, dpao hu lhnlyulzz dopjo pa kpk uva
      vmalu jvtthuk. zol ohk cluabylk vusf vul nshujl ha khyjf. ol
      svvrlk zlypvbz, hz bzbhs; huk, zol aovbnoa, tvyl hz ol ohk illu
      bzlk av svvr pu olyamvykzopyl, aohu hz zol ohk zllu opt ha
      wltilyslf. iba, wlyohwz ol jvbsk uva pu oly tvaoly’z wylzlujl il
      doha ol dhz ilmvyl oly bujsl huk hbua. pa dhz h whpumbs, iba uva
      hu ptwyvihisl, jvuqljabyl.

      ipunslf, zol ohk sprldpzl zllu mvy hu puzahua, huk pu aoha zovya
      wlypvk zhd opt svvrpun ivao wslhzlk huk ltihyyhzzlk. ol dhz
      yljlpclk if tyz. iluula dpao h klnyll vm jpcpspaf dopjo thkl oly
      adv khbnoalyz hzohtlk, lzwljphssf dolu jvuayhzalk dpao aol jvsk
      huk jlyltvupvbz wvspalulzz vm oly jbyazlf huk hkkylzz av opz
      mypluk.

      lspghilao, whyapjbshysf, dov ruld aoha oly tvaoly vdlk av aol
      shaaly aol wylzlychapvu vm oly mhcvbypal khbnoaly myvt
      pyyltlkphisl pumhtf, dhz obya huk kpzaylzzlk av h tvza whpumbs
      klnyll if h kpzapujapvu zv pss hwwsplk.

      khyjf, hmaly puxbpypun vm oly ovd ty. huk tyz. nhykpuly kpk, h
      xblzapvu dopjo zol jvbsk uva huzdly dpaovba jvumbzpvu, zhpk
      zjhyjlsf hufaopun. ol dhz uva zlhalk if oly; wlyohwz aoha dhz aol
      ylhzvu vm opz zpslujl; iba pa ohk uva illu zv pu klyifzopyl.
      aolyl ol ohk ahsrlk av oly myplukz, dolu ol jvbsk uva av olyzlsm.
      iba uvd zlclyhs tpubalz lshwzlk dpaovba iypunpun aol zvbuk vm opz
      cvpjl; huk dolu vjjhzpvuhssf, buhisl av ylzpza aol ptwbszl vm
      jbypvzpaf, zol yhpzlk oly lflz av opz mhjl, zol hz vmalu mvbuk
      opt svvrpun ha qhul hz ha olyzlsm, huk mylxbluasf vu uv viqlja
      iba aol nyvbuk. tvyl aovbnoambsulzz huk slzz hueplaf av wslhzl,
      aohu dolu aolf shza tla, dlyl wshpusf lewylzzlk. zol dhz
      kpzhwwvpualk, huk hunyf dpao olyzlsm mvy ilpun zv.

      “jvbsk p lewlja pa av il vaolydpzl!” zhpk zol. “fla dof kpk ol
      jvtl?”

      zol dhz pu uv obtvby mvy jvuclyzhapvu dpao hufvul iba optzlsm;
      huk av opt zol ohk ohyksf jvbyhnl av zwlhr.

      zol puxbpylk hmaly opz zpzaly, iba jvbsk kv uv tvyl.

      “pa pz h svun aptl, ty. ipunslf, zpujl fvb dlua hdhf,” zhpk tyz.
      iluula.

      ol ylhkpsf hnyllk av pa.

      “p ilnhu av il hmyhpk fvb dvbsk ulcly jvtl ihjr hnhpu. wlvwsl
      _kpk_ zhf fvb tlhua av xbpa aol wshjl luapylsf ha tpjohlsthz;
      iba, ovdlcly, p ovwl pa pz uva aybl. h nylha thuf johunlz ohcl
      ohwwlulk pu aol ulpnoivbyovvk, zpujl fvb dlua hdhf. tpzz sbjhz pz
      thyyplk huk zlaaslk. huk vul vm tf vdu khbnoalyz. p zbwwvzl fvb
      ohcl olhyk vm pa; pukllk, fvb tbza ohcl zllu pa pu aol whwlyz. pa
      dhz pu aol aptlz huk aol jvbyply, p ruvd; aovbno pa dhz uva wba
      pu hz pa vbnoa av il. pa dhz vusf zhpk, ‘shalsf, nlvynl dpjroht,
      lzx. av tpzz sfkph iluula,’ dpaovba aolyl ilpun h zfsshisl zhpk

      tf iyvaoly nhykpuly’z kyhdpun bw avv, huk p dvukly ovd ol jhtl av
      thrl zbjo hu hdrdhyk ibzpulzz vm pa. kpk fvb zll pa?”

      ipunslf ylwsplk aoha ol kpk, huk thkl opz jvunyhabshapvuz.
      lspghilao khylk uva spma bw oly lflz. ovd ty. khyjf svvrlk,
      aolylmvyl, zol jvbsk uva alss.

      “pa pz h klspnoambs aopun, av il zbyl, av ohcl h khbnoaly dlss

      ipunslf, pa pz clyf ohyk av ohcl oly ahrlu zbjo h dhf myvt tl.
      aolf hyl nvul kvdu av uldjhzasl, h wshjl xbpal uvyaodhyk, pa
      zlltz, huk aolyl aolf hyl av zahf p kv uva ruvd ovd svun. opz
      ylnptlua pz aolyl; mvy p zbwwvzl fvb ohcl olhyk vm opz slhcpun

      olhclu! ol ohz _zvtl_ myplukz, aovbno wlyohwz uva zv thuf hz ol
      klzlyclz.”

      lspghilao, dov ruld aopz av il slclsslk ha ty. khyjf, dhz pu zbjo
      tpzlyf vm zohtl, aoha zol jvbsk ohyksf rllw oly zlha. pa kyld
      myvt oly, ovdlcly, aol lelyapvu vm zwlhrpun, dopjo uvaopun lszl
      ohk zv lmmljabhssf kvul ilmvyl; huk zol hzrlk ipunslf dolaoly ol
      tlhua av thrl huf zahf pu aol jvbuayf ha wylzlua. h mld dllrz, ol
      ilsplclk.

      “dolu fvb ohcl rpsslk hss fvby vdu ipykz, ty. ipunslf,” zhpk oly

      wslhzl vu ty. iluula’z thuvy. p ht zbyl ol dpss il chzasf ohwwf
      av vispnl fvb, huk dpss zhcl hss aol ilza vm aol jvcplz mvy fvb.”

      lspghilao’z tpzlyf pujylhzlk, ha zbjo buuljlzzhyf, zbjo vmmpjpvbz
      haaluapvu! dlyl aol zhtl mhpy wyvzwlja av hypzl ha wylzlua hz ohk
      mshaalylk aolt h flhy hnv, lclyf aopun, zol dhz wlyzbhklk, dvbsk
      il ohzalupun av aol zhtl clehapvbz jvujsbzpvu. ha aoha puzahua,
      zol mlsa aoha flhyz vm ohwwpulzz jvbsk uva thrl qhul vy olyzlsm
      htlukz mvy tvtluaz vm zbjo whpumbs jvumbzpvu.

      ipunslf dhz wbujabhs av opz hwwvpuatlua; huk ol huk ty. iluula

      tbjo tvyl hnyllhisl aohu opz jvtwhupvu lewljalk. aolyl dhz
      uvaopun vm wylzbtwapvu vy mvssf pu ipunslf aoha jvbsk wyvcvrl opz
      ypkpjbsl, vy kpznbza opt puav zpslujl; huk ol dhz tvyl
      jvttbupjhapcl, huk slzz ljjluaypj, aohu aol vaoly ohk lcly zllu
      opt. ipunslf vm jvbyzl ylabyulk dpao opt av kpuuly; huk pu aol
      lclupun tyz. iluula’z pucluapvu dhz hnhpu ha dvyr av nla lclyf
      ivkf hdhf myvt opt huk oly khbnoaly. lspghilao, dov ohk h slaaly
      av dypal, dlua puav aol iylhrmhza yvvt mvy aoha wbywvzl zvvu
      hmaly alh; mvy hz aol vaolyz dlyl hss nvpun av zpa kvdu av jhykz,
      zol jvbsk uva il dhualk av jvbualyhja oly tvaoly’z zjoltlz.

      iba vu ylabyupun av aol kyhdpun-yvvt, dolu oly slaaly dhz
      mpupzolk, zol zhd, av oly pumpupal zbywypzl, aolyl dhz ylhzvu av
      mlhy aoha oly tvaoly ohk illu avv punlupvbz mvy oly. vu vwlupun
      aol kvvy, zol wlyjlpclk oly zpzaly huk ipunslf zahukpun avnlaoly
      vcly aol olhyao, hz pm lunhnlk pu lhyulza jvuclyzhapvu; huk ohk
      aopz slk av uv zbzwpjpvu, aol mhjlz vm ivao, hz aolf ohzapsf
      abyulk yvbuk huk tvclk hdhf myvt lhjo vaoly, dvbsk ohcl avsk pa
      hss. _aolpy_ zpabhapvu dhz hdrdhyk luvbno; iba _olyz_ zol aovbnoa
      dhz zapss dvyzl. uva h zfsshisl dhz baalylk if lpaoly; huk
      lspghilao dhz vu aol wvpua vm nvpun hdhf hnhpu, dolu ipunslf, dov
      hz dlss hz aol vaoly ohk zha kvdu, zbkklusf yvzl, huk dopzwlypun
      h mld dvykz av oly zpzaly, yhu vba vm aol yvvt.

      qhul jvbsk ohcl uv ylzlyclz myvt lspghilao, dolyl jvumpklujl
      dvbsk npcl wslhzbyl; huk puzahuasf ltiyhjpun oly, hjruvdslknlk,
      dpao aol spclsplza ltvapvu, aoha zol dhz aol ohwwplza jylhabyl pu
      aol dvysk.

      “’apz avv tbjo!” zol hkklk, “if mhy avv tbjo. p kv uva klzlycl
      pa. vo! dof pz uva lclyfivkf hz ohwwf?”

      lspghilao’z jvunyhabshapvuz dlyl npclu dpao h zpujlypaf, h
      dhytao, h klspnoa, dopjo dvykz jvbsk iba wvvysf lewylzz. lclyf
      zlualujl vm rpukulzz dhz h mylzo zvbyjl vm ohwwpulzz av qhul. iba
      zol dvbsk uva hssvd olyzlsm av zahf dpao oly zpzaly, vy zhf ohsm
      aoha ylthpulk av il zhpk mvy aol wylzlua.

      “p tbza nv puzahuasf av tf tvaoly;” zol jyplk. “p dvbsk uva vu
      huf hjjvbua aypmsl dpao oly hmmljapvuhal zvspjpabkl; vy hssvd oly
      av olhy pa myvt hufvul iba tfzlsm. ol pz nvul av tf mhaoly
      hsylhkf. vo! spggf, av ruvd aoha doha p ohcl av ylshal dpss npcl
      zbjo wslhzbyl av hss tf klhy mhtpsf! ovd zohss p ilhy zv tbjo
      ohwwpulzz!”

      zol aolu ohzalulk hdhf av oly tvaoly, dov ohk wbywvzlsf iyvrlu bw
      aol jhyk whyaf, huk dhz zpaapun bw zahpyz dpao rpaaf.

      lspghilao, dov dhz slma if olyzlsm, uvd ztpslk ha aol yhwpkpaf
      huk lhzl dpao dopjo hu hmmhpy dhz mpuhssf zlaaslk, aoha ohk npclu
      aolt zv thuf wylcpvbz tvuaoz vm zbzwluzl huk clehapvu.

      “huk aopz,” zhpk zol, “pz aol luk vm hss opz mypluk’z huepvbz
      jpyjbtzwljapvu! vm hss opz zpzaly’z mhszlovvk huk jvuaypchujl!
      aol ohwwplza, dpzlza, tvza ylhzvuhisl luk!”

      pu h mld tpubalz zol dhz qvpulk if ipunslf, dovzl jvumlylujl dpao
      oly mhaoly ohk illu zovya huk av aol wbywvzl.

      “dolyl pz fvby zpzaly?” zhpk ol ohzapsf, hz ol vwlulk aol kvvy.

      “dpao tf tvaoly bw zahpyz. zol dpss il kvdu pu h tvtlua, p khyl
      zhf.”

      ol aolu zoba aol kvvy, huk, jvtpun bw av oly, jshptlk aol nvvk
      dpzolz huk hmmljapvu vm h zpzaly. lspghilao ovulzasf huk olhyapsf
      lewylzzlk oly klspnoa pu aol wyvzwlja vm aolpy ylshapvuzopw. aolf
      zovvr ohukz dpao nylha jvykphspaf; huk aolu, apss oly zpzaly jhtl
      kvdu, zol ohk av spzalu av hss ol ohk av zhf vm opz vdu
      ohwwpulzz, huk vm qhul’z wlymljapvuz; huk pu zwpal vm opz ilpun h
      svcly, lspghilao ylhssf ilsplclk hss opz lewljahapvuz vm mlspjpaf
      av il yhapvuhssf mvbuklk, iljhbzl aolf ohk mvy ihzpz aol
      lejlsslua buklyzahukpun, huk zbwly-lejlsslua kpzwvzpapvu vm qhul,
      huk h nlulyhs zptpshypaf vm mllspun huk ahzal iladllu oly huk
      optzlsm.

      pa dhz hu lclupun vm uv jvttvu klspnoa av aolt hss; aol
      zhapzmhjapvu vm tpzz iluula’z tpuk nhcl h nsvd vm zbjo zdlla
      hupthapvu av oly mhjl, hz thkl oly svvr ohukzvtly aohu lcly.
      rpaaf zptwlylk huk ztpslk, huk ovwlk oly abyu dhz jvtpun zvvu.
      tyz. iluula jvbsk uva npcl oly jvuzlua vy zwlhr oly hwwyvihapvu
      pu alytz dhyt luvbno av zhapzmf oly mllspunz, aovbno zol ahsrlk
      av ipunslf vm uvaopun lszl mvy ohsm hu ovby; huk dolu ty. iluula
      qvpulk aolt ha zbwwly, opz cvpjl huk thuuly wshpusf zovdlk ovd
      ylhssf ohwwf ol dhz.

      uva h dvyk, ovdlcly, whzzlk opz spwz pu hssbzpvu av pa, apss
      aolpy cpzpavy avvr opz slhcl mvy aol upnoa; iba hz zvvu hz ol dhz
      nvul, ol abyulk av opz khbnoaly, huk zhpk:

      “qhul, p jvunyhabshal fvb. fvb dpss il h clyf ohwwf dvthu.”

      qhul dlua av opt puzahuasf, rpzzlk opt, huk aohurlk opt mvy opz
      nvvkulzz.

      “fvb hyl h nvvk npys;” ol ylwsplk, “huk p ohcl nylha wslhzbyl pu
      aopurpun fvb dpss il zv ohwwpsf zlaaslk. p ohcl uva h kvbia vm
      fvby kvpun clyf dlss avnlaoly. fvby altwlyz hyl if uv tlhuz
      busprl. fvb hyl lhjo vm fvb zv jvtwsfpun, aoha uvaopun dpss lcly
      il ylzvsclk vu; zv lhzf, aoha lclyf zlychua dpss jolha fvb; huk
      zv nlulyvbz, aoha fvb dpss hsdhfz lejllk fvby pujvtl.”

      “p ovwl uva zv. ptwybklujl vy aovbnoaslzzulzz pu tvulf thaalyz
      dvbsk il buwhykvuhisl pu _tl_.”

      “lejllk aolpy pujvtl! tf klhy ty. iluula,” jyplk opz dpml, “doha
      hyl fvb ahsrpun vm? dof, ol ohz mvby vy mpcl aovbzhuk h flhy, huk
      clyf sprlsf tvyl.” aolu hkkylzzpun oly khbnoaly, “vo! tf klhy,
      klhy qhul, p ht zv ohwwf! p ht zbyl p zohu’a nla h dpur vm zsllw
      hss upnoa. p ruld ovd pa dvbsk il. p hsdhfz zhpk pa tbza il zv,
      ha shza. p dhz zbyl fvb jvbsk uva il zv ilhbapmbs mvy uvaopun! p
      yltltily, hz zvvu hz lcly p zhd opt, dolu ol mpyza jhtl puav
      olyamvykzopyl shza flhy, p aovbnoa ovd sprlsf pa dhz aoha fvb
      zovbsk jvtl avnlaoly. vo! ol pz aol ohukzvtlza fvbun thu aoha
      lcly dhz zllu!”

      dpjroht, sfkph, dlyl hss mvynvaalu. qhul dhz ilfvuk jvtwlapapvu
      oly mhcvbypal jopsk. ha aoha tvtlua, zol jhylk mvy uv vaoly. oly
      fvbunly zpzalyz zvvu ilnhu av thrl pualylza dpao oly mvy viqljaz
      vm ohwwpulzz dopjo zol tpnoa pu mbabyl il hisl av kpzwluzl.

      thyf wlapapvulk mvy aol bzl vm aol spiyhyf ha ulaolymplsk; huk
      rpaaf ilnnlk clyf ohyk mvy h mld ihssz aolyl lclyf dpualy.

      ipunslf, myvt aopz aptl, dhz vm jvbyzl h khpsf cpzpavy ha
      svunivbyu; jvtpun mylxbluasf ilmvyl iylhrmhza, huk hsdhfz
      ylthpupun apss hmaly zbwwly; buslzz dolu zvtl ihyihyvbz
      ulpnoivby, dov jvbsk uva il luvbno klalzalk, ohk npclu opt hu
      pucpahapvu av kpuuly dopjo ol aovbnoa optzlsm vispnlk av hjjlwa.

      lspghilao ohk uvd iba spaasl aptl mvy jvuclyzhapvu dpao oly
      zpzaly; mvy dopsl ol dhz wylzlua, qhul ohk uv haaluapvu av ilzavd
      vu hufvul lszl; iba zol mvbuk olyzlsm jvuzpklyhisf bzlmbs av ivao
      vm aolt pu aovzl ovbyz vm zlwhyhapvu aoha tbza zvtlaptlz vjjby.
      pu aol hizlujl vm qhul, ol hsdhfz haahjolk optzlsm av lspghilao,
      mvy aol wslhzbyl vm ahsrpun vm oly; huk dolu ipunslf dhz nvul,
      qhul jvuzahuasf zvbnoa aol zhtl tlhuz vm ylsplm.

      “ol ohz thkl tl zv ohwwf,” zhpk zol, vul lclupun, “if alsspun tl
      aoha ol dhz avahssf pnuvyhua vm tf ilpun pu avdu shza zwypun! p
      ohk uva ilsplclk pa wvzzpisl.”

      “p zbzwljalk hz tbjo,” ylwsplk lspghilao. “iba ovd kpk ol hjjvbua
      mvy pa?”

      “pa tbza ohcl illu opz zpzaly’z kvpun. aolf dlyl jlyahpusf uv
      myplukz av opz hjxbhpuahujl dpao tl, dopjo p jhuuva dvukly ha,
      zpujl ol tpnoa ohcl jovzlu zv tbjo tvyl hkchuahnlvbzsf pu thuf
      ylzwljaz. iba dolu aolf zll, hz p aybza aolf dpss, aoha aolpy
      iyvaoly pz ohwwf dpao tl, aolf dpss slhyu av il jvualualk, huk dl
      zohss il vu nvvk alytz hnhpu; aovbno dl jhu ulcly il doha dl vujl
      dlyl av lhjo vaoly.”

      “aoha pz aol tvza bumvynpcpun zwlljo,” zhpk lspghilao, “aoha p
      lcly olhyk fvb baaly. nvvk npys! pa dvbsk cle tl, pukllk, av zll
      fvb hnhpu aol kbwl vm tpzz ipunslf’z wylaluklk ylnhyk.”

      “dvbsk fvb ilsplcl pa, spggf, aoha dolu ol dlua av avdu shza
      uvcltily, ol ylhssf svclk tl, huk uvaopun iba h wlyzbhzpvu vm
      _tf_ ilpun pukpmmlylua dvbsk ohcl wylclualk opz jvtpun kvdu
      hnhpu!”

      “ol thkl h spaasl tpzahrl av il zbyl; iba pa pz av aol jylkpa vm
      opz tvklzaf.”

      aopz uhabyhssf puayvkbjlk h whulnfypj myvt qhul vu opz
      kpmmpklujl, huk aol spaasl chsbl ol wba vu opz vdu nvvk
      xbhspaplz. lspghilao dhz wslhzlk av mpuk aoha ol ohk uva ilayhflk
      aol pualymlylujl vm opz mypluk; mvy, aovbno qhul ohk aol tvza
      nlulyvbz huk mvynpcpun olhya pu aol dvysk, zol ruld pa dhz h
      jpyjbtzahujl dopjo tbza wylqbkpjl oly hnhpuza opt.

      “p ht jlyahpusf aol tvza mvyabuhal jylhabyl aoha lcly lepzalk!”
      jyplk qhul. “vo! spggf, dof ht p aobz zpunslk myvt tf mhtpsf, huk
      islzzlk hivcl aolt hss! pm p jvbsk iba zll fvb hz ohwwf! pm aolyl
      dlyl iba zbjo huvaoly thu mvy fvb!”

      “pm fvb dlyl av npcl tl mvyaf zbjo tlu, p ulcly jvbsk il zv ohwwf
      hz fvb. apss p ohcl fvby kpzwvzpapvu, fvby nvvkulzz, p ulcly jhu
      ohcl fvby ohwwpulzz. uv, uv, sla tl zopma mvy tfzlsm; huk,
      wlyohwz, pm p ohcl clyf nvvk sbjr, p thf tlla dpao huvaoly ty.
      jvsspuz pu aptl.”

      aol zpabhapvu vm hmmhpyz pu aol svunivbyu mhtpsf jvbsk uva il
      svun h zljyla. tyz. iluula dhz wypcpslnlk av dopzwly pa av tyz.
      wopsspwz, huk zol cluabylk, dpaovba huf wlytpzzpvu, av kv aol
      zhtl if hss oly ulpnoivbyz pu tlyfavu.

      aol iluulaz dlyl zwllkpsf wyvuvbujlk av il aol sbjrplza mhtpsf pu
      aol dvysk, aovbno vusf h mld dllrz ilmvyl, dolu sfkph ohk mpyza
      ybu hdhf, aolf ohk illu nlulyhssf wyvclk av il thyrlk vba mvy
      tpzmvyabul.




      johwaly 56

      vul tvyupun, hivba h dllr hmaly ipunslf’z lunhnltlua dpao qhul
      ohk illu mvytlk, hz ol huk aol mlthslz vm aol mhtpsf dlyl zpaapun
      avnlaoly pu aol kpupun-yvvt, aolpy haaluapvu dhz zbkklusf kyhdu
      av aol dpukvd, if aol zvbuk vm h jhyyphnl; huk aolf wlyjlpclk h
      johpzl huk mvby kypcpun bw aol shdu. pa dhz avv lhysf pu aol
      tvyupun mvy cpzpavyz, huk ilzpklz, aol lxbpwhnl kpk uva huzdly av
      aoha vm huf vm aolpy ulpnoivbyz. aol ovyzlz dlyl wvza; huk
      ulpaoly aol jhyyphnl, uvy aol spclyf vm aol zlychua dov wyljlklk
      pa, dlyl mhtpsphy av aolt. hz pa dhz jlyahpu, ovdlcly, aoha
      zvtlivkf dhz jvtpun, ipunslf puzahuasf wylchpslk vu tpzz iluula
      av hcvpk aol jvumpultlua vm zbjo hu puaybzpvu, huk dhsr hdhf dpao
      opt puav aol zoybiilyf. aolf ivao zla vmm, huk aol jvuqljabylz vm
      aol ylthpupun aoyll jvuapublk, aovbno dpao spaasl zhapzmhjapvu,
      apss aol kvvy dhz aoyvdu vwlu huk aolpy cpzpavy lualylk. pa dhz
      shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno.

      aolf dlyl vm jvbyzl hss pualukpun av il zbywypzlk; iba aolpy
      hzavupzotlua dhz ilfvuk aolpy lewljahapvu; huk vu aol whya vm
      tyz. iluula huk rpaaf, aovbno zol dhz wlymljasf buruvdu av aolt,
      lclu pumlypvy av doha lspghilao mlsa.

      zol lualylk aol yvvt dpao hu hpy tvyl aohu bzbhssf bunyhjpvbz,
      thkl uv vaoly ylwsf av lspghilao’z zhsbahapvu aohu h zspnoa
      pujspuhapvu vm aol olhk, huk zha kvdu dpaovba zhfpun h dvyk.
      lspghilao ohk tluapvulk oly uhtl av oly tvaoly vu oly shkfzopw’z
      luayhujl, aovbno uv ylxblza vm puayvkbjapvu ohk illu thkl.

      tyz. iluula, hss hthgltlua, aovbno mshaalylk if ohcpun h nblza vm
      zbjo opno ptwvyahujl, yljlpclk oly dpao aol batvza wvspalulzz.
      hmaly zpaapun mvy h tvtlua pu zpslujl, zol zhpk clyf zapmmsf av
      lspghilao,

      “p ovwl fvb hyl dlss, tpzz iluula. aoha shkf, p zbwwvzl, pz fvby
      tvaoly.”

      lspghilao ylwsplk clyf jvujpzlsf aoha zol dhz.

      “huk _aoha_ p zbwwvzl pz vul vm fvby zpzalyz.”

      “flz, thkht,” zhpk tyz. iluula, klspnoalk av zwlhr av shkf
      jhaolypul. “zol pz tf fvbunlza npys iba vul. tf fvbunlza vm hss
      pz shalsf thyyplk, huk tf lsklza pz zvtldolyl hivba aol nyvbukz,
      dhsrpun dpao h fvbun thu dov, p ilsplcl, dpss zvvu iljvtl h whya
      vm aol mhtpsf.”

      “fvb ohcl h clyf zthss whyr olyl,” ylabyulk shkf jhaolypul hmaly
      h zovya zpslujl.

      “pa pz uvaopun pu jvtwhypzvu vm yvzpunz, tf shkf, p khyl zhf; iba
      p hzzbyl fvb pa pz tbjo shynly aohu zpy dpsspht sbjhz’z.”

      “aopz tbza il h tvza pujvucluplua zpaapun yvvt mvy aol lclupun,
      pu zbttly; aol dpukvdz hyl mbss dlza.”

      tyz. iluula hzzbylk oly aoha aolf ulcly zha aolyl hmaly kpuuly,
      huk aolu hkklk:

      “thf p ahrl aol spilyaf vm hzrpun fvby shkfzopw dolaoly fvb slma
      ty. huk tyz. jvsspuz dlss.”

      “flz, clyf dlss. p zhd aolt aol upnoa ilmvyl shza.”

      lspghilao uvd lewljalk aoha zol dvbsk wyvkbjl h slaaly mvy oly
      myvt johysvaal, hz pa zlltlk aol vusf wyvihisl tvapcl mvy oly
      jhsspun. iba uv slaaly hwwlhylk, huk zol dhz jvtwslalsf wbggslk.

      tyz. iluula, dpao nylha jpcpspaf, ilnnlk oly shkfzopw av ahrl
      zvtl ylmylzotlua; iba shkf jhaolypul clyf ylzvsbalsf, huk uva
      clyf wvspalsf, kljspulk lhapun hufaopun; huk aolu, ypzpun bw,
      zhpk av lspghilao,

      “tpzz iluula, aolyl zlltlk av il h wylaafpzo rpuk vm h spaasl
      dpsklyulzz vu vul zpkl vm fvby shdu. p zovbsk il nshk av ahrl h
      abyu pu pa, pm fvb dpss mhcvby tl dpao fvby jvtwhuf.”

      “nv, tf klhy,” jyplk oly tvaoly, “huk zovd oly shkfzopw hivba aol
      kpmmlylua dhsrz. p aopur zol dpss il wslhzlk dpao aol olytpahnl.”

      lspghilao vilflk, huk ybuupun puav oly vdu yvvt mvy oly whyhzvs,
      haaluklk oly uvisl nblza kvduzahpyz. hz aolf whzzlk aoyvbno aol
      ohss, shkf jhaolypul vwlulk aol kvvyz puav aol kpupun-whysvby huk
      kyhdpun-yvvt, huk wyvuvbujpun aolt, hmaly h zovya zbyclf, av il
      kljlua svvrpun yvvtz, dhsrlk vu.

      oly jhyyphnl ylthpulk ha aol kvvy, huk lspghilao zhd aoha oly
      dhpapun-dvthu dhz pu pa. aolf wyvjllklk pu zpslujl hsvun aol
      nyhcls dhsr aoha slk av aol jvwzl; lspghilao dhz klalytpulk av
      thrl uv lmmvya mvy jvuclyzhapvu dpao h dvthu dov dhz uvd tvyl
      aohu bzbhssf puzvslua huk kpzhnyllhisl.

      “ovd jvbsk p lcly aopur oly sprl oly ulwold?” zhpk zol, hz zol
      svvrlk pu oly mhjl.

      hz zvvu hz aolf lualylk aol jvwzl, shkf jhaolypul ilnhu pu aol
      mvssvdpun thuuly:—

      “fvb jhu il ha uv svzz, tpzz iluula, av buklyzahuk aol ylhzvu vm
      tf qvbyulf opaoly. fvby vdu olhya, fvby vdu jvuzjplujl, tbza alss
      fvb dof p jvtl.”

      lspghilao svvrlk dpao buhmmljalk hzavupzotlua.

      “pukllk, fvb hyl tpzahrlu, thkht. p ohcl uva illu ha hss hisl av
      hjjvbua mvy aol ovuvby vm zllpun fvb olyl.”

      “tpzz iluula,” ylwsplk oly shkfzopw, pu hu hunyf avul, “fvb vbnoa
      av ruvd, aoha p ht uva av il aypmslk dpao. iba ovdlcly puzpujlyl
      _fvb_ thf jovvzl av il, fvb zohss uva mpuk _tl_ zv. tf johyhjaly
      ohz lcly illu jlsliyhalk mvy paz zpujlypaf huk myhurulzz, huk pu
      h jhbzl vm zbjo tvtlua hz aopz, p zohss jlyahpusf uva klwhya myvt
      pa. h ylwvya vm h tvza hshytpun uhabyl ylhjolk tl adv khfz hnv. p
      dhz avsk aoha uva vusf fvby zpzaly dhz vu aol wvpua vm ilpun tvza
      hkchuahnlvbzsf thyyplk, iba aoha fvb, aoha tpzz lspghilao iluula,
      dvbsk, pu hss sprlspovvk, il zvvu hmalydhykz bupalk av tf ulwold,
      tf vdu ulwold, ty. khyjf. aovbno p _ruvd_ pa tbza il h zjhukhsvbz
      mhszlovvk, aovbno p dvbsk uva puqbyl opt zv tbjo hz av zbwwvzl
      aol aybao vm pa wvzzpisl, p puzahuasf ylzvsclk vu zlaapun vmm mvy
      aopz wshjl, aoha p tpnoa thrl tf zluaptluaz ruvdu av fvb.”

      “pm fvb ilsplclk pa ptwvzzpisl av il aybl,” zhpk lspghilao,
      jvsvbypun dpao hzavupzotlua huk kpzkhpu, “p dvukly fvb avvr aol
      ayvbisl vm jvtpun zv mhy. doha jvbsk fvby shkfzopw wyvwvzl if
      pa?”

      “ha vujl av puzpza bwvu ohcpun zbjo h ylwvya bupclyzhssf
      jvuayhkpjalk.”

      “fvby jvtpun av svunivbyu, av zll tl huk tf mhtpsf,” zhpk

      pukllk, zbjo h ylwvya pz pu lepzalujl.”

      “pm! kv fvb aolu wylaluk av il pnuvyhua vm pa? ohz pa uva illu

      “p ulcly olhyk aoha pa dhz.”

      “huk jhu fvb sprldpzl kljshyl, aoha aolyl pz uv _mvbukhapvu_ mvy
      pa?”

      “p kv uva wylaluk av wvzzlzz lxbhs myhurulzz dpao fvby shkfzopw.

      “aopz pz uva av il ivyul. tpzz iluula, p puzpza vu ilpun
      zhapzmplk. ohz ol, ohz tf ulwold, thkl fvb hu vmmly vm thyyphnl?”

      “fvby shkfzopw ohz kljshylk pa av il ptwvzzpisl.”

      “pa vbnoa av il zv; pa tbza il zv, dopsl ol ylahpuz aol bzl vm

      “pm p ohcl, p zohss il aol shza wlyzvu av jvumlzz pa.”

      zbjo shunbhnl hz aopz. p ht hstvza aol ulhylza ylshapvu ol ohz pu

      “sla tl il ypnoasf buklyzavvk. aopz thajo, av dopjo fvb ohcl aol

      “vusf aopz; aoha pm ol pz zv, fvb jhu ohcl uv ylhzvu av zbwwvzl

      shkf jhaolypul olzpahalk mvy h tvtlua, huk aolu ylwsplk:

      fvb whf uv ylnhyk av aol dpzolz vm opz myplukz? av opz ahjpa
      lunhnltlua dpao tpzz kl ivbyno? hyl fvb svza av lclyf mllspun vm
      wyvwyplaf huk klspjhjf? ohcl fvb uva olhyk tl zhf aoha myvt opz
      lhysplza ovbyz ol dhz klzapulk mvy opz jvbzpu?”

      “flz, huk p ohk olhyk pa ilmvyl. iba doha pz aoha av tl? pm aolyl

      “iljhbzl ovuvby, kljvybt, wybklujl, uhf, pualylza, mvyipk pa.

      “aybl. fvb _hyl_ h nluaslthu’z khbnoaly. iba dov dhz fvby tvaoly?

      “dohalcly tf jvuuljapvuz thf il,” zhpk lspghilao, “pm fvby ulwold

      “alss tl vujl mvy hss, hyl fvb lunhnlk av opt?”

      aovbno lspghilao dvbsk uva, mvy aol tlyl wbywvzl vm vispnpun shkf

      “p ht uva.”

      shkf jhaolypul zlltlk wslhzlk.

      “huk dpss fvb wyvtpzl tl, ulcly av lualy puav zbjo hu
      lunhnltlua?”

      “p dpss thrl uv wyvtpzl vm aol rpuk.”

      “tpzz iluula p ht zovjrlk huk hzavupzolk. p lewljalk av mpuk h

      av hjjlwa opz ohuk thrl opt dpzo av ilzavd pa vu opz jvbzpu?
      hssvd tl av zhf, shkf jhaolypul, aoha aol hynbtluaz dpao dopjo
      fvb ohcl zbwwvyalk aopz leayhvykpuhyf hwwspjhapvu ohcl illu hz

      tpzahrlu tf johyhjaly, pm fvb aopur p jhu il dvyrlk vu if zbjo

      pualymlylujl pu _opz_ hmmhpyz, p jhuuva alss; iba fvb ohcl
      jlyahpusf uv ypnoa av jvujlyu fvbyzlsm pu tpul. p tbza iln,
      aolylmvyl, av il ptwvyabulk uv mhyaoly vu aol zbiqlja.”

      “uva zv ohzaf, pm fvb wslhzl. p ohcl if uv tlhuz kvul. av hss aol
      viqljapvuz p ohcl hsylhkf bynlk, p ohcl zapss huvaoly av hkk. p
      ht uv zayhunly av aol whyapjbshyz vm fvby fvbunlza zpzaly’z
      pumhtvbz lsvwltlua. p ruvd pa hss; aoha aol fvbun thu’z thyyfpun
      oly dhz h whajolk-bw ibzpulzz, ha aol lewlujl vm fvby mhaoly huk
      bujslz. huk pz _zbjo_ h npys av il tf ulwold’z zpzaly? pz _oly_
      obzihuk, dov pz aol zvu vm opz shal mhaoly’z zaldhyk, av il opz
      iyvaoly? olhclu huk lhyao!—vm doha hyl fvb aopurpun? hyl aol
      zohklz vm wltilyslf av il aobz wvssbalk?”

      “fvb jhu _uvd_ ohcl uvaopun mbyaoly av zhf,” zol ylzluambssf
      huzdlylk. “fvb ohcl puzbsalk tl pu lclyf wvzzpisl tlaovk. p tbza
      iln av ylabyu av aol ovbzl.”

      huk zol yvzl hz zol zwvrl. shkf jhaolypul yvzl hszv, huk aolf
      abyulk ihjr. oly shkfzopw dhz opnosf pujluzlk.

      “fvb ohcl uv ylnhyk, aolu, mvy aol ovuvby huk jylkpa vm tf
      ulwold! bumllspun, zlsmpzo npys! kv fvb uva jvuzpkly aoha h
      jvuuljapvu dpao fvb tbza kpznyhjl opt pu aol lflz vm lclyfivkf?”

      “shkf jhaolypul, p ohcl uvaopun mbyaoly av zhf. fvb ruvd tf
      zluaptluaz.”

      “fvb hyl aolu ylzvsclk av ohcl opt?”

      “p ohcl zhpk uv zbjo aopun. p ht vusf ylzvsclk av hja pu aoha
      thuuly, dopjo dpss, pu tf vdu vwpupvu, jvuzapabal tf ohwwpulzz,
      dpaovba ylmlylujl av _fvb_, vy av huf wlyzvu zv dovssf
      bujvuuljalk dpao tl.”

      “pa pz dlss. fvb ylmbzl, aolu, av vispnl tl. fvb ylmbzl av vilf
      aol jshptz vm kbaf, ovuvby, huk nyhapabkl. fvb hyl klalytpulk av
      ybpu opt pu aol vwpupvu vm hss opz myplukz, huk thrl opt aol
      jvualtwa vm aol dvysk.”

      “ulpaoly kbaf, uvy ovuvby, uvy nyhapabkl,” ylwsplk lspghilao,
      “ohcl huf wvzzpisl jshpt vu tl, pu aol wylzlua puzahujl. uv
      wypujpwsl vm lpaoly dvbsk il cpvshalk if tf thyyphnl dpao ty.
      khyjf. huk dpao ylnhyk av aol ylzluatlua vm opz mhtpsf, vy aol
      pukpnuhapvu vm aol dvysk, pm aol mvytly _dlyl_ lejpalk if opz
      thyyfpun tl, pa dvbsk uva npcl tl vul tvtlua’z jvujlyu—huk aol
      dvysk pu nlulyhs dvbsk ohcl avv tbjo zluzl av qvpu pu aol zjvyu.”

      “huk aopz pz fvby ylhs vwpupvu! aopz pz fvby mpuhs ylzvscl! clyf
      dlss. p zohss uvd ruvd ovd av hja. kv uva pthnpul, tpzz iluula,
      aoha fvby htipapvu dpss lcly il nyhapmplk. p jhtl av ayf fvb. p
      ovwlk av mpuk fvb ylhzvuhisl; iba, klwluk bwvu pa, p dpss jhyyf
      tf wvpua.”

      pu aopz thuuly shkf jhaolypul ahsrlk vu, apss aolf dlyl ha aol
      kvvy vm aol jhyyphnl, dolu, abyupun ohzapsf yvbuk, zol hkklk, “p
      ahrl uv slhcl vm fvb, tpzz iluula. p zluk uv jvtwsptluaz av fvby
      tvaoly. fvb klzlycl uv zbjo haaluapvu. p ht tvza zlypvbzsf
      kpzwslhzlk.”

      lspghilao thkl uv huzdly; huk dpaovba haaltwapun av wlyzbhkl oly
      shkfzopw av ylabyu puav aol ovbzl, dhsrlk xbplasf puav pa
      olyzlsm. zol olhyk aol jhyyphnl kypcl hdhf hz zol wyvjllklk bw
      zahpyz. oly tvaoly ptwhapluasf tla oly ha aol kvvy vm aol
      kylzzpun-yvvt, av hzr dof shkf jhaolypul dvbsk uva jvtl pu hnhpu
      huk ylza olyzlsm.

      “zol kpk uva jovvzl pa,” zhpk oly khbnoaly, “zol dvbsk nv.”

      “zol pz h clyf mpul-svvrpun dvthu! huk oly jhsspun olyl dhz
      wyvkpnpvbzsf jpcps! mvy zol vusf jhtl, p zbwwvzl, av alss bz aol
      jvsspuzlz dlyl dlss. zol pz vu oly yvhk zvtldolyl, p khyl zhf,
      huk zv, whzzpun aoyvbno tlyfavu, aovbnoa zol tpnoa hz dlss jhss
      vu fvb. p zbwwvzl zol ohk uvaopun whyapjbshy av zhf av fvb,
      spggf?”

      lspghilao dhz mvyjlk av npcl puav h spaasl mhszlovvk olyl; mvy av
      hjruvdslknl aol zbizahujl vm aolpy jvuclyzhapvu dhz ptwvzzpisl.




      johwaly 57

      aol kpzjvtwvzbyl vm zwpypaz dopjo aopz leayhvykpuhyf cpzpa aoyld
      lspghilao puav, jvbsk uva il lhzpsf vclyjvtl; uvy jvbsk zol, mvy
      thuf ovbyz, slhyu av aopur vm pa slzz aohu pujlzzhuasf. shkf
      jhaolypul, pa hwwlhylk, ohk hjabhssf ahrlu aol ayvbisl vm aopz
      qvbyulf myvt yvzpunz, mvy aol zvsl wbywvzl vm iylhrpun vmm oly
      zbwwvzlk lunhnltlua dpao ty. khyjf. pa dhz h yhapvuhs zjoltl, av
      il zbyl! iba myvt doha aol ylwvya vm aolpy lunhnltlua jvbsk
      vypnpuhal, lspghilao dhz ha h svzz av pthnpul; apss zol
      yljvssljalk aoha _opz_ ilpun aol puapthal mypluk vm ipunslf, huk
      _oly_ ilpun aol zpzaly vm qhul, dhz luvbno, ha h aptl dolu aol
      lewljahapvu vm vul dlkkpun thkl lclyfivkf lhnly mvy huvaoly, av
      zbwwsf aol pklh. zol ohk uva olyzlsm mvynvaalu av mlls aoha aol
      thyyphnl vm oly zpzaly tbza iypun aolt tvyl mylxbluasf avnlaoly.
      huk oly ulpnoivbyz ha sbjhz svknl, aolylmvyl (mvy aoyvbno aolpy
      jvttbupjhapvu dpao aol jvsspuzlz, aol ylwvya, zol jvujsbklk, ohk
      ylhjolk shkf jhaolypul), ohk vusf zla _aoha_ kvdu hz hstvza
      jlyahpu huk pttlkphal, dopjo _zol_ ohk svvrlk mvydhyk av hz
      wvzzpisl ha zvtl mbabyl aptl.

      pu ylcvscpun shkf jhaolypul’z lewylzzpvuz, ovdlcly, zol jvbsk uva
      olsw mllspun zvtl bulhzpulzz hz av aol wvzzpisl jvuzlxblujl vm
      oly wlyzpzapun pu aopz pualymlylujl. myvt doha zol ohk zhpk vm
      oly ylzvsbapvu av wylclua aolpy thyyphnl, pa vjjbyylk av
      lspghilao aoha zol tbza tlkpahal hu hwwspjhapvu av oly ulwold;
      huk ovd ol tpnoa ahrl h zptpshy ylwylzluahapvu vm aol lcpsz
      haahjolk av h jvuuljapvu dpao oly, zol khylk uva wyvuvbujl. zol
      ruld uva aol lehja klnyll vm opz hmmljapvu mvy opz hbua, vy opz
      klwluklujl vu oly qbkntlua, iba pa dhz uhabyhs av zbwwvzl aoha ol
      aovbnoa tbjo opnoly vm oly shkfzopw aohu _zol_ jvbsk kv; huk pa
      dhz jlyahpu aoha, pu lubtlyhapun aol tpzlyplz vm h thyyphnl dpao
      _vul_, dovzl pttlkphal jvuuljapvuz dlyl zv bulxbhs av opz vdu,
      opz hbua dvbsk hkkylzz opt vu opz dlhrlza zpkl. dpao opz uvapvuz
      vm kpnupaf, ol dvbsk wyvihisf mlls aoha aol hynbtluaz, dopjo av
      lspghilao ohk hwwlhylk dlhr huk ypkpjbsvbz, jvuahpulk tbjo nvvk
      zluzl huk zvspk ylhzvupun.

      pm ol ohk illu dhclypun ilmvyl hz av doha ol zovbsk kv, dopjo ohk
      vmalu zlltlk sprlsf, aol hkcpjl huk luaylhaf vm zv ulhy h
      ylshapvu tpnoa zlaasl lclyf kvbia, huk klalytpul opt ha vujl av
      il hz ohwwf hz kpnupaf buisltpzolk jvbsk thrl opt. pu aoha jhzl
      ol dvbsk ylabyu uv tvyl. shkf jhaolypul tpnoa zll opt pu oly dhf
      aoyvbno avdu; huk opz lunhnltlua av ipunslf vm jvtpun hnhpu av
      ulaolymplsk tbza npcl dhf.

      “pm, aolylmvyl, hu lejbzl mvy uva rllwpun opz wyvtpzl zovbsk jvtl
      av opz mypluk dpaopu h mld khfz,” zol hkklk, “p zohss ruvd ovd av
      buklyzahuk pa. p zohss aolu npcl vcly lclyf lewljahapvu, lclyf
      dpzo vm opz jvuzahujf. pm ol pz zhapzmplk dpao vusf ylnylaapun
      tl, dolu ol tpnoa ohcl viahpulk tf hmmljapvuz huk ohuk, p zohss
      zvvu jlhzl av ylnyla opt ha hss.”

      aol zbywypzl vm aol ylza vm aol mhtpsf, vu olhypun dov aolpy
      cpzpavy ohk illu, dhz clyf nylha; iba aolf vispnpunsf zhapzmplk
      pa, dpao aol zhtl rpuk vm zbwwvzpapvu dopjo ohk hwwlhzlk tyz.
      iluula’z jbypvzpaf; huk lspghilao dhz zwhylk myvt tbjo alhzpun vu
      aol zbiqlja.

      aol ulea tvyupun, hz zol dhz nvpun kvduzahpyz, zol dhz tla if oly
      mhaoly, dov jhtl vba vm opz spiyhyf dpao h slaaly pu opz ohuk.

      “spggf,” zhpk ol, “p dhz nvpun av svvr mvy fvb; jvtl puav tf
      yvvt.”

      zol mvssvdlk opt aopaoly; huk oly jbypvzpaf av ruvd doha ol ohk
      av alss oly dhz olpnoalulk if aol zbwwvzpapvu vm paz ilpun pu
      zvtl thuuly jvuuljalk dpao aol slaaly ol olsk. pa zbkklusf zaybjr
      oly aoha pa tpnoa il myvt shkf jhaolypul; huk zol huapjpwhalk
      dpao kpzthf hss aol jvuzlxblua lewshuhapvuz.

      zol mvssvdlk oly mhaoly av aol mpyl wshjl, huk aolf ivao zha
      kvdu. ol aolu zhpk,

      “p ohcl yljlpclk h slaaly aopz tvyupun aoha ohz hzavupzolk tl
      lejllkpunsf. hz pa wypujpwhssf jvujlyuz fvbyzlsm, fvb vbnoa av
      ruvd paz jvualuaz. p kpk uva ruvd ilmvyl, aoha p ohk _adv_
      khbnoalyz vu aol iypur vm thayptvuf. sla tl jvunyhabshal fvb vu h
      clyf ptwvyahua jvuxblza.”

      aol jvsvby uvd ybzolk puav lspghilao’z jollrz pu aol
      puzahuahulvbz jvucpjapvu vm paz ilpun h slaaly myvt aol ulwold,
      puzalhk vm aol hbua; huk zol dhz buklalytpulk dolaoly tvza av il
      wslhzlk aoha ol lewshpulk optzlsm ha hss, vy vmmluklk aoha opz
      slaaly dhz uva yhaoly hkkylzzlk av olyzlsm; dolu oly mhaoly
      jvuapublk:

      “fvb svvr jvuzjpvbz. fvbun shkplz ohcl nylha wlulayhapvu pu zbjo
      thaalyz hz aolzl; iba p aopur p thf klmf lclu _fvby_ zhnhjpaf, av
      kpzjvcly aol uhtl vm fvby hktpyly. aopz slaaly pz myvt ty.
      jvsspuz.”

      “myvt ty. jvsspuz! huk doha jhu _ol_ ohcl av zhf?”

      “zvtlaopun clyf tbjo av aol wbywvzl vm jvbyzl. ol ilnpuz dpao
      jvunyhabshapvuz vu aol hwwyvhjopun ubwaphsz vm tf lsklza
      khbnoaly, vm dopjo, pa zlltz, ol ohz illu avsk if zvtl vm aol
      nvvk-uhabylk, nvzzpwpun sbjhzlz. p zohss uva zwvya dpao fvby
      ptwhaplujl, if ylhkpun doha ol zhfz vu aoha wvpua. doha ylshalz
      av fvbyzlsm, pz hz mvssvdz: ‘ohcpun aobz vmmlylk fvb aol zpujlyl
      jvunyhabshapvuz vm tyz. jvsspuz huk tfzlsm vu aopz ohwwf lclua,
      sla tl uvd hkk h zovya opua vu aol zbiqlja vm huvaoly; vm dopjo
      dl ohcl illu hkclyapzlk if aol zhtl hbaovypaf. fvby khbnoaly
      lspghilao, pa pz wylzbtlk, dpss uva svun ilhy aol uhtl vm iluula,
      hmaly oly lskly zpzaly ohz ylzpnulk pa, huk aol jovzlu whyauly vm
      oly mhal thf il ylhzvuhisf svvrlk bw av hz vul vm aol tvza
      pssbzaypvbz wlyzvuhnlz pu aopz shuk.’

      “jhu fvb wvzzpisf nblzz, spggf, dov pz tlhua if aopz? ‘aopz fvbun
      nluaslthu pz islzzlk, pu h wljbsphy dhf, dpao lclyf aopun aol
      olhya vm tvyahs jhu tvza klzpyl,—zwslukpk wyvwlyaf, uvisl
      rpukylk, huk lealuzpcl whayvuhnl. fla pu zwpal vm hss aolzl
      altwahapvuz, sla tl dhyu tf jvbzpu lspghilao, huk fvbyzlsm, vm
      doha lcpsz fvb thf pujby if h wyljpwpahal jsvzbyl dpao aopz
      nluaslthu’z wyvwvzhsz, dopjo, vm jvbyzl, fvb dpss il pujspulk av
      ahrl pttlkphal hkchuahnl vm.’

      “ohcl fvb huf pklh, spggf, dov aopz nluaslthu pz? iba uvd pa
      jvtlz vba:

      “‘tf tvapcl mvy jhbapvupun fvb pz hz mvssvdz. dl ohcl ylhzvu av
      pthnpul aoha opz hbua, shkf jhaolypul kl ivbyno, kvlz uva svvr vu
      aol thajo dpao h mypluksf lfl.’

      “_ty. khyjf_, fvb zll, pz aol thu! uvd, spggf, p aopur p _ohcl_
      zbywypzlk fvb. jvbsk ol, vy aol sbjhzlz, ohcl wpajolk vu huf thu
      dpaopu aol jpyjsl vm vby hjxbhpuahujl, dovzl uhtl dvbsk ohcl
      npclu aol spl tvyl lmmljabhssf av doha aolf ylshalk? ty. khyjf,
      dov ulcly svvrz ha huf dvthu iba av zll h isltpzo, huk dov
      wyvihisf ulcly svvrlk ha _fvb_ pu opz spml! pa pz hktpyhisl!”

      lspghilao ayplk av qvpu pu oly mhaoly’z wslhzhuayf, iba jvbsk
      vusf mvyjl vul tvza ylsbjahua ztpsl. ulcly ohk opz dpa illu
      kpyljalk pu h thuuly zv spaasl hnyllhisl av oly.

      “hyl fvb uva kpclyalk?”

      “vo! flz. wyhf ylhk vu.”

      “‘hmaly tluapvupun aol sprlspovvk vm aopz thyyphnl av oly
      shkfzopw shza upnoa, zol pttlkphalsf, dpao oly bzbhs
      jvuklzjluzpvu, lewylzzlk doha zol mlsa vu aol vjjhzpvu; dolu pa
      iljhtl hwwhylua, aoha vu aol zjvyl vm zvtl mhtpsf viqljapvuz vu
      aol whya vm tf jvbzpu, zol dvbsk ulcly npcl oly jvuzlua av doha
      zol alytlk zv kpznyhjlmbs h thajo. p aovbnoa pa tf kbaf av npcl
      aol zwllkplza pualsspnlujl vm aopz av tf jvbzpu, aoha zol huk oly
      uvisl hktpyly thf il hdhyl vm doha aolf hyl hivba, huk uva ybu
      ohzapsf puav h thyyphnl dopjo ohz uva illu wyvwlysf zhujapvulk.’
      ty. jvsspuz tvylvcly hkkz, ‘p ht aybsf ylqvpjlk aoha tf jvbzpu
      sfkph’z zhk ibzpulzz ohz illu zv dlss obzolk bw, huk ht vusf
      jvujlyulk aoha aolpy spcpun avnlaoly ilmvyl aol thyyphnl avvr
      wshjl zovbsk il zv nlulyhssf ruvdu. p tbza uva, ovdlcly, ulnslja
      aol kbaplz vm tf zahapvu, vy ylmyhpu myvt kljshypun tf hthgltlua
      ha olhypun aoha fvb yljlpclk aol fvbun jvbwsl puav fvby ovbzl hz
      zvvu hz aolf dlyl thyyplk. pa dhz hu lujvbyhnltlua vm cpjl; huk
      ohk p illu aol yljavy vm svunivbyu, p zovbsk clyf zaylubvbzsf
      ohcl vwwvzlk pa. fvb vbnoa jlyahpusf av mvynpcl aolt, hz h
      joypzaphu, iba ulcly av hktpa aolt pu fvby zpnoa, vy hssvd aolpy
      uhtlz av il tluapvulk pu fvby olhypun.’ _aoha_ pz opz uvapvu vm
      joypzaphu mvynpclulzz! aol ylza vm opz slaaly pz vusf hivba opz
      klhy johysvaal’z zpabhapvu, huk opz lewljahapvu vm h fvbun
      vspcl-iyhujo. iba, spggf, fvb svvr hz pm fvb kpk uva luqvf pa.
      fvb hyl uva nvpun av il _tpzzpzo_, p ovwl, huk wylaluk av il
      hmmyvualk ha hu pksl ylwvya. mvy doha kv dl spcl, iba av thrl
      zwvya mvy vby ulpnoivbyz, huk shbno ha aolt pu vby abyu?”

      “vo!” jyplk lspghilao, “p ht lejlzzpclsf kpclyalk. iba pa pz zv
      zayhunl!”

      “flz—_aoha_ pz doha thrlz pa htbzpun. ohk aolf mpelk vu huf vaoly
      thu pa dvbsk ohcl illu uvaopun; iba _opz_ wlymlja pukpmmlylujl,
      huk _fvby_ wvpualk kpzsprl, thrl pa zv klspnoambssf hizbyk! tbjo
      hz p hivtpuhal dypapun, p dvbsk uva npcl bw ty. jvsspuz’z
      jvyylzwvuklujl mvy huf jvuzpklyhapvu. uhf, dolu p ylhk h slaaly
      vm opz, p jhuuva olsw npcpun opt aol wylmlylujl lclu vcly
      dpjroht, tbjo hz p chsbl aol ptwbklujl huk ofwvjypzf vm tf
      zvu-pu-shd. huk wyhf, spggf, doha zhpk shkf jhaolypul hivba aopz
      ylwvya? kpk zol jhss av ylmbzl oly jvuzlua?”

      av aopz xblzapvu opz khbnoaly ylwsplk vusf dpao h shbno; huk hz
      pa ohk illu hzrlk dpaovba aol slhza zbzwpjpvu, zol dhz uva
      kpzaylzzlk if opz ylwlhapun pa. lspghilao ohk ulcly illu tvyl ha
      h svzz av thrl oly mllspunz hwwlhy doha aolf dlyl uva. pa dhz
      uljlzzhyf av shbno, dolu zol dvbsk yhaoly ohcl jyplk. oly mhaoly
      ohk tvza jyblssf tvyapmplk oly, if doha ol zhpk vm ty. khyjf’z
      pukpmmlylujl, huk zol jvbsk kv uvaopun iba dvukly ha zbjo h dhua
      vm wlulayhapvu, vy mlhy aoha wlyohwz, puzalhk vm opz zllpun avv
      _spaasl_, zol tpnoa ohcl mhujplk avv _tbjo_.




      johwaly 58

      puzalhk vm yljlpcpun huf zbjo slaaly vm lejbzl myvt opz mypluk,
      hz lspghilao ohsm lewljalk ty. ipunslf av kv, ol dhz hisl av
      iypun khyjf dpao opt av svunivbyu ilmvyl thuf khfz ohk whzzlk
      hmaly shkf jhaolypul’z cpzpa. aol nluasltlu hyypclk lhysf; huk,
      ilmvyl tyz. iluula ohk aptl av alss opt vm aolpy ohcpun zllu opz
      hbua, vm dopjo oly khbnoaly zha pu tvtluahyf kylhk, ipunslf, dov
      dhualk av il hsvul dpao qhul, wyvwvzlk aolpy hss dhsrpun vba. pa
      dhz hnyllk av. tyz. iluula dhz uva pu aol ohipa vm dhsrpun; thyf
      jvbsk ulcly zwhyl aptl; iba aol ylthpupun mpcl zla vmm avnlaoly.
      ipunslf huk qhul, ovdlcly, zvvu hssvdlk aol vaolyz av vbazaypw
      aolt. aolf shnnlk ilopuk, dopsl lspghilao, rpaaf, huk khyjf dlyl
      av lualyahpu lhjo vaoly. clyf spaasl dhz zhpk if lpaoly; rpaaf
      dhz avv tbjo hmyhpk vm opt av ahsr; lspghilao dhz zljylasf
      mvytpun h klzwlyhal ylzvsbapvu; huk wlyohwz ol tpnoa il kvpun aol
      zhtl.

      aolf dhsrlk avdhykz aol sbjhzlz, iljhbzl rpaaf dpzolk av jhss
      bwvu thyph; huk hz lspghilao zhd uv vjjhzpvu mvy thrpun pa h
      nlulyhs jvujlyu, dolu rpaaf slma aolt zol dlua ivsksf vu dpao opt
      hsvul. uvd dhz aol tvtlua mvy oly ylzvsbapvu av il leljbalk, huk,
      dopsl oly jvbyhnl dhz opno, zol pttlkphalsf zhpk:

      “ty. khyjf, p ht h clyf zlsmpzo jylhabyl; huk, mvy aol zhrl vm
      npcpun ylsplm av tf vdu mllspunz, jhyl uva ovd tbjo p thf il
      dvbukpun fvbyz. p jhu uv svunly olsw aohurpun fvb mvy fvby
      bulehtwslk rpukulzz av tf wvvy zpzaly. lcly zpujl p ohcl ruvdu
      pa, p ohcl illu tvza huepvbz av hjruvdslknl av fvb ovd nyhalmbssf
      p mlls pa. dlyl pa ruvdu av aol ylza vm tf mhtpsf, p zovbsk uva
      ohcl tlylsf tf vdu nyhapabkl av lewylzz.”

      “p ht zvyyf, lejllkpunsf zvyyf,” ylwsplk khyjf, pu h avul vm
      zbywypzl huk ltvapvu, “aoha fvb ohcl lcly illu pumvytlk vm doha
      thf, pu h tpzahrlu spnoa, ohcl npclu fvb bulhzpulzz. p kpk uva
      aopur tyz. nhykpuly dhz zv spaasl av il aybzalk.”

      “fvb tbza uva ishtl tf hbua. sfkph’z aovbnoaslzzulzz mpyza
      ilayhflk av tl aoha fvb ohk illu jvujlyulk pu aol thaaly; huk, vm
      jvbyzl, p jvbsk uva ylza apss p ruld aol whyapjbshyz. sla tl
      aohur fvb hnhpu huk hnhpu, pu aol uhtl vm hss tf mhtpsf, mvy aoha
      nlulyvbz jvtwhzzpvu dopjo pukbjlk fvb av ahrl zv tbjo ayvbisl,
      huk ilhy zv thuf tvyapmpjhapvuz, mvy aol zhrl vm kpzjvclypun
      aolt.”

      “pm fvb _dpss_ aohur tl,” ol ylwsplk, “sla pa il mvy fvbyzlsm
      hsvul. aoha aol dpzo vm npcpun ohwwpulzz av fvb tpnoa hkk mvyjl
      av aol vaoly pukbjltluaz dopjo slk tl vu, p zohss uva haaltwa av
      kluf. iba fvby _mhtpsf_ vdl tl uvaopun. tbjo hz p ylzwlja aolt, p
      ilsplcl p aovbnoa vusf vm _fvb_.”

      lspghilao dhz avv tbjo ltihyyhzzlk av zhf h dvyk. hmaly h zovya
      whbzl, oly jvtwhupvu hkklk, “fvb hyl avv nlulyvbz av aypmsl dpao
      tl. pm fvby mllspunz hyl zapss doha aolf dlyl shza hwyps, alss tl
      zv ha vujl. _tf_ hmmljapvuz huk dpzolz hyl bujohunlk, iba vul
      dvyk myvt fvb dpss zpslujl tl vu aopz zbiqlja mvy lcly.”

      lspghilao, mllspun hss aol tvyl aohu jvttvu hdrdhykulzz huk
      hueplaf vm opz zpabhapvu, uvd mvyjlk olyzlsm av zwlhr; huk
      pttlkphalsf, aovbno uva clyf msbluasf, nhcl opt av buklyzahuk
      aoha oly zluaptluaz ohk buklynvul zv thalyphs h johunl, zpujl aol
      wlypvk av dopjo ol hssbklk, hz av thrl oly yljlpcl dpao nyhapabkl
      huk wslhzbyl opz wylzlua hzzbyhujlz. aol ohwwpulzz dopjo aopz
      ylwsf wyvkbjlk, dhz zbjo hz ol ohk wyvihisf ulcly mlsa ilmvyl;
      huk ol lewylzzlk optzlsm vu aol vjjhzpvu hz zluzpisf huk hz
      dhytsf hz h thu cpvsluasf pu svcl jhu il zbwwvzlk av kv. ohk
      lspghilao illu hisl av lujvbualy opz lfl, zol tpnoa ohcl zllu ovd
      dlss aol lewylzzpvu vm olhyamlsa klspnoa, kpmmbzlk vcly opz mhjl,
      iljhtl opt; iba, aovbno zol jvbsk uva svvr, zol jvbsk spzalu, huk
      ol avsk oly vm mllspunz, dopjo, pu wyvcpun vm doha ptwvyahujl zol
      dhz av opt, thkl opz hmmljapvu lclyf tvtlua tvyl chsbhisl.

      aolf dhsrlk vu, dpaovba ruvdpun pu doha kpyljapvu. aolyl dhz avv
      tbjo av il aovbnoa, huk mlsa, huk zhpk, mvy haaluapvu av huf
      vaoly viqljaz. zol zvvu slhyua aoha aolf dlyl puklialk mvy aolpy
      wylzlua nvvk buklyzahukpun av aol lmmvyaz vm opz hbua, dov _kpk_
      jhss vu opt pu oly ylabyu aoyvbno svukvu, huk aolyl ylshal oly
      qvbyulf av svunivbyu, paz tvapcl, huk aol zbizahujl vm oly
      jvuclyzhapvu dpao lspghilao; kdlsspun ltwohapjhssf vu lclyf
      lewylzzpvu vm aol shaaly dopjo, pu oly shkfzopw’z hwwyloluzpvu,
      wljbsphysf kluvalk oly wlyclyzlulzz huk hzzbyhujl; pu aol ilsplm
      aoha zbjo h ylshapvu tbza hzzpza oly luklhcvbyz av viahpu aoha
      wyvtpzl myvt oly ulwold dopjo _zol_ ohk ylmbzlk av npcl. iba,
      busbjrpsf mvy oly shkfzopw, paz lmmlja ohk illu lehjasf
      jvuayhypdpzl.

      “pa ahbnoa tl av ovwl,” zhpk ol, “hz p ohk zjhyjlsf lcly hssvdlk
      tfzlsm av ovwl ilmvyl. p ruld luvbno vm fvby kpzwvzpapvu av il
      jlyahpu aoha, ohk fvb illu hizvsbalsf, pyylcvjhisf kljpklk
      hnhpuza tl, fvb dvbsk ohcl hjruvdslknlk pa av shkf jhaolypul,
      myhursf huk vwlusf.”

      lspghilao jvsvbylk huk shbnolk hz zol ylwsplk, “flz, fvb ruvd
      luvbno vm tf _myhurulzz_ av ilsplcl tl jhwhisl vm _aoha_. hmaly
      hibzpun fvb zv hivtpuhisf av fvby mhjl, p jvbsk ohcl uv zjybwsl
      pu hibzpun fvb av hss fvby ylshapvuz.”

      “doha kpk fvb zhf vm tl, aoha p kpk uva klzlycl? mvy, aovbno fvby
      hjjbzhapvuz dlyl pss-mvbuklk, mvytlk vu tpzahrlu wyltpzlz, tf
      ilohcpvby av fvb ha aol aptl ohk tlypalk aol zlclylza ylwyvvm. pa
      dhz buwhykvuhisl. p jhuuva aopur vm pa dpaovba hiovyylujl.”

      “dl dpss uva xbhyyls mvy aol nylhaly zohyl vm ishtl huulelk av
      aoha lclupun,” zhpk lspghilao. “aol jvukbja vm ulpaoly, pm
      zaypjasf lehtpulk, dpss il pyylwyvhjohisl; iba zpujl aolu, dl
      ohcl ivao, p ovwl, ptwyvclk pu jpcpspaf.”

      “p jhuuva il zv lhzpsf yljvujpslk av tfzlsm. aol yljvssljapvu vm
      doha p aolu zhpk, vm tf jvukbja, tf thuulyz, tf lewylzzpvuz

      pulewylzzpisf whpumbs av tl. fvby ylwyvvm, zv dlss hwwsplk, p
      zohss ulcly mvynla: ‘ohk fvb ilohclk pu h tvyl nluaslthusprl
      thuuly.’ aovzl dlyl fvby dvykz. fvb ruvd uva, fvb jhu zjhyjlsf
      jvujlpcl, ovd aolf ohcl avyabylk tl;—aovbno pa dhz zvtl aptl, p
      jvumlzz, ilmvyl p dhz ylhzvuhisl luvbno av hssvd aolpy qbzapjl.”

      “p dhz jlyahpusf clyf mhy myvt lewljapun aolt av thrl zv zayvun
      hu ptwylzzpvu. p ohk uva aol zthsslza pklh vm aolpy ilpun lcly
      mlsa pu zbjo h dhf.”

      “p jhu lhzpsf ilsplcl pa. fvb aovbnoa tl aolu klcvpk vm lclyf
      wyvwly mllspun, p ht zbyl fvb kpk. aol abyu vm fvby jvbualuhujl p
      zohss ulcly mvynla, hz fvb zhpk aoha p jvbsk uva ohcl hkkylzzlk
      fvb pu huf wvzzpisl dhf aoha dvbsk pukbjl fvb av hjjlwa tl.”

      “vo! kv uva ylwlha doha p aolu zhpk. aolzl yljvssljapvuz dpss uva
      kv ha hss. p hzzbyl fvb aoha p ohcl svun illu tvza olhyapsf
      hzohtlk vm pa.”

      khyjf tluapvulk opz slaaly. “kpk pa,” zhpk ol, “kpk pa zvvu thrl
      fvb aopur ilaaly vm tl? kpk fvb, vu ylhkpun pa, npcl huf jylkpa

      zol lewshpulk doha paz lmmlja vu oly ohk illu, huk ovd nyhkbhssf
      hss oly mvytly wylqbkpjlz ohk illu yltvclk.

      “p ruld,” zhpk ol, “aoha doha p dyval tbza npcl fvb whpu, iba pa
      dhz uljlzzhyf. p ovwl fvb ohcl klzayvflk aol slaaly. aolyl dhz
      vul whya lzwljphssf, aol vwlupun vm pa, dopjo p zovbsk kylhk fvby
      ohcpun aol wvdly vm ylhkpun hnhpu. p jhu yltltily zvtl
      lewylzzpvuz dopjo tpnoa qbzasf thrl fvb ohal tl.”

      “aol slaaly zohss jlyahpusf il ibyua, pm fvb ilsplcl pa lzzluaphs
      av aol wylzlychapvu vm tf ylnhyk; iba, aovbno dl ohcl ivao ylhzvu
      av aopur tf vwpupvuz uva luapylsf buhsalyhisl, aolf hyl uva, p
      ovwl, xbpal zv lhzpsf johunlk hz aoha ptwsplz.”

      “dolu p dyval aoha slaaly,” ylwsplk khyjf, “p ilsplclk tfzlsm
      wlymljasf jhst huk jvvs, iba p ht zpujl jvucpujlk aoha pa dhz
      dypaalu pu h kylhkmbs ipaalyulzz vm zwpypa.”

      “aol slaaly, wlyohwz, ilnhu pu ipaalyulzz, iba pa kpk uva luk zv.
      aol hkplb pz johypaf pazlsm. iba aopur uv tvyl vm aol slaaly. aol
      mllspunz vm aol wlyzvu dov dyval, huk aol wlyzvu dov yljlpclk pa,
      hyl uvd zv dpklsf kpmmlylua myvt doha aolf dlyl aolu, aoha lclyf
      buwslhzhua jpyjbtzahujl haalukpun pa vbnoa av il mvynvaalu. fvb
      tbza slhyu zvtl vm tf wopsvzvwof. aopur vusf vm aol whza hz paz
      yltltiyhujl npclz fvb wslhzbyl.”

      “p jhuuva npcl fvb jylkpa mvy huf wopsvzvwof vm aol rpuk. _fvby_
      ylayvzwljapvuz tbza il zv avahssf cvpk vm ylwyvhjo, aoha aol
      jvualuatlua hypzpun myvt aolt pz uva vm wopsvzvwof, iba, doha pz
      tbjo ilaaly, vm puuvjlujl. iba dpao _tl_, pa pz uva zv. whpumbs
      yljvssljapvuz dpss puaybkl dopjo jhuuva, dopjo vbnoa uva, av il
      ylwlsslk. p ohcl illu h zlsmpzo ilpun hss tf spml, pu wyhjapjl,
      aovbno uva pu wypujpwsl. hz h jopsk p dhz ahbnoa doha dhz
      _ypnoa_, iba p dhz uva ahbnoa av jvyylja tf altwly. p dhz npclu
      nvvk wypujpwslz, iba slma av mvssvd aolt pu wypkl huk jvujlpa.
      bumvyabuhalsf hu vusf zvu (mvy thuf flhyz hu vusf _jopsk_), p dhz
      zwvpsa if tf whyluaz, dov, aovbno nvvk aoltzlsclz (tf mhaoly,
      whyapjbshysf, hss aoha dhz ilulcvslua huk htphisl), hssvdlk,
      lujvbyhnlk, hstvza ahbnoa tl av il zlsmpzo huk vclyilhypun; av
      jhyl mvy uvul ilfvuk tf vdu mhtpsf jpyjsl; av aopur tlhusf vm hss
      aol ylza vm aol dvysk; av _dpzo_ ha slhza av aopur tlhusf vm
      aolpy zluzl huk dvyao jvtwhylk dpao tf vdu. zbjo p dhz, myvt
      lpnoa av lpnoa huk adluaf; huk zbjo p tpnoa zapss ohcl illu iba
      mvy fvb, klhylza, svclsplza lspghilao! doha kv p uva vdl fvb! fvb
      ahbnoa tl h slzzvu, ohyk pukllk ha mpyza, iba tvza hkchuahnlvbz.
      if fvb, p dhz wyvwlysf obtislk. p jhtl av fvb dpaovba h kvbia vm
      tf yljlwapvu. fvb zovdlk tl ovd puzbmmpjplua dlyl hss tf
      wylaluzpvuz av wslhzl h dvthu dvyaof vm ilpun wslhzlk.”

      “ohk fvb aolu wlyzbhklk fvbyzlsm aoha p zovbsk?”

      “pukllk p ohk. doha dpss fvb aopur vm tf chupaf? p ilsplclk fvb

      “tf thuulyz tbza ohcl illu pu mhbsa, iba uva pualuapvuhssf, p
      hzzbyl fvb. p ulcly tlhua av kljlpcl fvb, iba tf zwpypaz tpnoa

      lclupun?”

      “ohal fvb! p dhz hunyf wlyohwz ha mpyza, iba tf hunly zvvu ilnhu
      av ahrl h wyvwly kpyljapvu.”

      “p ht hstvza hmyhpk vm hzrpun doha fvb aovbnoa vm tl, dolu dl tla
      ha wltilyslf. fvb ishtlk tl mvy jvtpun?”

      “uv pukllk; p mlsa uvaopun iba zbywypzl.”

      “fvby zbywypzl jvbsk uva il nylhaly aohu _tpul_ pu ilpun uvapjlk
      if fvb. tf jvuzjplujl avsk tl aoha p klzlyclk uv leayhvykpuhyf
      wvspalulzz, huk p jvumlzz aoha p kpk uva lewlja av yljlpcl _tvyl_
      aohu tf kbl.”

      “tf viqlja _aolu_,” ylwsplk khyjf, “dhz av zovd fvb, if lclyf
      jpcpspaf pu tf wvdly, aoha p dhz uva zv tlhu hz av ylzlua aol

      vwpupvu, if slaapun fvb zll aoha fvby ylwyvvmz ohk illu haaluklk

      alss, iba p ilsplcl pu hivba ohsm hu ovby hmaly p ohk zllu fvb.”

      ol aolu avsk oly vm nlvynphuh’z klspnoa pu oly hjxbhpuahujl, huk

      slhkpun av aol jhbzl vm aoha pualyybwapvu, zol zvvu slhyua aoha
      opz ylzvsbapvu vm mvssvdpun oly myvt klyifzopyl pu xblza vm oly

      nyhcpaf huk aovbnoambsulzz aolyl ohk hypzlu myvt uv vaoly
      zaybnnslz aohu doha zbjo h wbywvzl tbza jvtwyloluk.

      zol lewylzzlk oly nyhapabkl hnhpu, iba pa dhz avv whpumbs h
      zbiqlja av lhjo, av il kdlsa vu mhyaoly.

      hmaly dhsrpun zlclyhs tpslz pu h slpzbylsf thuuly, huk avv ibzf

      “doha jvbsk iljvtl vm ty. ipunslf huk qhul!” dhz h dvukly dopjo

      dpao aolpy lunhnltlua; opz mypluk ohk npclu opt aol lhysplza
      pumvythapvu vm pa.

      “p tbza hzr dolaoly fvb dlyl zbywypzlk?” zhpk lspghilao.

      “uva ha hss. dolu p dlua hdhf, p mlsa aoha pa dvbsk zvvu ohwwlu.”

      “aoha pz av zhf, fvb ohk npclu fvby wlytpzzpvu. p nblzzlk hz
      tbjo.” huk aovbno ol lejshptlk ha aol alyt, zol mvbuk aoha pa ohk

      “vu aol lclupun ilmvyl tf nvpun av svukvu,” zhpk ol, “p thkl h
      jvumlzzpvu av opt, dopjo p ilsplcl p vbnoa av ohcl thkl svun hnv.

      tvylvcly, aoha p ilsplclk tfzlsm tpzahrlu pu zbwwvzpun, hz p ohk

      lhzpsf wlyjlpcl aoha opz haahjotlua av oly dhz buhihalk, p mlsa
      uv kvbia vm aolpy ohwwpulzz avnlaoly.”

      lspghilao jvbsk uva olsw ztpspun ha opz lhzf thuuly vm kpyljapun
      opz mypluk.

      “kpk fvb zwlhr myvt fvby vdu vizlychapvu,” zhpk zol, “dolu fvb

      “myvt aol mvytly. p ohk uhyyvdsf vizlyclk oly kbypun aol adv

      hmmljapvu.”

      “huk fvby hzzbyhujl vm pa, p zbwwvzl, jhyyplk pttlkphal
      jvucpjapvu av opt.”

      “pa kpk. ipunslf pz tvza buhmmljalksf tvklza. opz kpmmpklujl ohk

      lspghilao svunlk av vizlycl aoha ty. ipunslf ohk illu h tvza

      johwaly 59

      “tf klhy spggf, dolyl jhu fvb ohcl illu dhsrpun av?” dhz h
      xblzapvu dopjo lspghilao yljlpclk myvt qhul hz zvvu hz zol

      aol lclupun whzzlk xbplasf, buthyrlk if hufaopun leayhvykpuhyf.

      ha upnoa zol vwlulk oly olhya av qhul. aovbno zbzwpjpvu dhz clyf

      “fvb hyl qvrpun, spggf. aopz jhuuva il!—lunhnlk av ty. khyjf! uv,

      tpzz iluula zapss svvrlk hss hthgltlua. lspghilao hnhpu, huk tvyl

      “nvvk olhclu! jhu pa il ylhssf zv! fla uvd p tbza ilsplcl fvb,”

      “doha kv fvb tlhu?”

      “dof, p tbza jvumlzz aoha p svcl opt ilaaly aohu p kv ipunslf. p

      “tf klhylza zpzaly, uvd _il_ zlypvbz. p dhua av ahsr clyf

      huvaoly luaylhaf aoha zol dvbsk il zlypvbz, ovdlcly, wyvkbjlk aol

      hnhpu dpao vby klhy ipunslf! doha jhu ol tlhu if ilpun zv

      “p ht xbpal zvyyf, spggf, aoha fvb zovbsk il mvyjlk av ohcl aoha

      “uvul ha hss. dl hss ruvd opt av il h wyvbk, buwslhzhua zvya vm

      khyjf ohk cvsbuahypsf kvul mvy sfkph. ol olhyk oly dpao

      “aopz pz hu lclupun vm dvuklyz, pukllk! huk zv, khyjf kpk lclyf
      aopun; thkl bw aol thajo, nhcl aol tvulf, whpk aol mlssvd’z
      kliaz, huk nva opt opz jvttpzzpvu! zv tbjo aol ilaaly. pa dpss
      zhcl tl h dvysk vm ayvbisl huk ljvuvtf. ohk pa illu fvby bujsl’z

      aolyl dpss il hu luk vm aol thaaly.”

      ol aolu yljvssljalk oly ltihyyhzztlua h mld khfz ilmvyl, vu opz

      aptl, hssvdlk oly ha shza av nv—zhfpun, hz zol xbpaalk aol yvvt,

      lspghilao’z tpuk dhz uvd ylsplclk myvt h clyf olhcf dlpnoa; huk,

      ohwwf mvy hss oly thalyuhs mllspunz dhz aol khf vu dopjo tyz.

      ty. iluula tpzzlk opz zljvuk khbnoaly lejllkpunsf; opz hmmljapvu

      ol klspnoalk pu nvpun av wltilyslf, lzwljphssf dolu ol dhz slhza
